/ /AshtsarYoratnasyakoShasakaleShTasamudAyanAmadzambUdwIpadiguttaramunermahAyubarAdzAshrImAMbhUmipaNDarakaShyabaMshatantroratnAnAMyathAbhUtanIyAnAMbimokShobidzahAraM/// /'dzam
gling byang phyogs kyi thub pa'i rgyal tshab chen po dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che ji ltar byon pa'i tshul gyi rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar rin po che'i
bang mdzod dgos 'dod kun 'byung zhes bya ba bzhugs so//

/ /rgya gar skad du/ shrI wAM bhU mi paNDo ssanggu ru dharma sya swa mI sarba satwA nAM shAstA nutta re bhyoà¾… nu sA ri ka ma yA bhIkShNa pra na mA mi/ bod skad du/ dpal ldan
sa skya pa'i bla ma dam pa chos kyi rje sems can thams cad kyi ston pa bla na med pa rnams la rjes su 'brang ba bdag yang yang phyag bgyi'o/ /mtha' yas shes bya'i gnas
kun kun tu gzigs pa'i gzigs pa sgrib med rab mnga' ba/ /bgrang yas ma lus lus can kun la brtse ba'i brtse bas rtag tu thugs brlan zhing / /dpag yas lhag pa'i bdud dpung dpung
'joms mdzad pa'i mdzad pa rmad du byung ba can/ /bsam yas 'jam dbyangs dbyangs can la sogs lha yi lhar gyur dbyer med bla ma rgyal/ /thub pa dbang po'i bstan 'dzin mchog
ces mchog tu grags pa gsal ldan gang / /gang zhig byang phyogs 'gro ba'i skyabs gyur skyabs mchog mkhyen

brtse nus pa'i phul/ /phul byung rigs gsum mgon po'i rnam 'phrul yang dang yang du byon pa'i brgyud/ /brgyud pa dri med rim bzhin byon la dad cing dad pas bdag phyag 'tshal/
/lha mchog zur phud lnga pa'i utpal sngo ldan 'od gsal gyi/ /lha rigs sprul nas byon pa'i 'chi med dbang po mched gsum dang / /lha sras rnam pa bzhi dang gzhan yang ma
bzang spun bdun sogs/ /lha yi gdung rabs sprul pa'i gar mkhan de rnams bsngags par 'os/ /nang ltar ma rig la 'khon 'khon gyi mtshan 'chang rdo rje 'dzin/ /phyi ltar srin
po la 'khon 'khon zhes 'gro la rab grags pa'i/ /mtshan mchog don ldan 'khon ston 'khon gyi dri med gdung 'dzin pa'i/ /gsang sngags grub pa 'khon rje 'khon gyi skyes mchog
rnams la 'dud/ /sa skya'i dbyig 'dzin ri bo'i ngos nas legs 'ongs

pa'i/ /sa skya'i 'phrin las rta bdun rgyal po'i 'od zer ltar/ /sa skya pa zhes snyan grags kun tu rab gsal ba/ /sa skya pa yi rje btsun rnams la snying nas dad/ /de lta'i skyes
chen rnams kyi zhabs padmo/ /de dag stobs ldan rgyal pos nyer bsten nas/ /de tshe mkha' la nyi zla rnam gnyis ltar/ /de bzhin sa la mchod yon gnyis zhes grags/ /'on
kyang bar skabs yid srub rtsa lag 'gas/ /mi bsrun ngan pa'i spyod pa sna tshogs kyis/ /sa skya'i bstan dang bstan 'dzin dgon gnas bcas/ /dus ngan mtshan gyi lhag mar nye
bar byas/ /e ma de tshe sngags 'chang sprul pa'i sku/ /e ma mthu stobs rdzu 'phrul bsam yas des/ /e ma bdud rigs bcom nas dpal sa skya'i/ /e ma bstan pa'i me ro rmang nas
bslangs/ /de lta'i bka' drin gzhal du ma mchis pa'i/ /sngags 'chang bla ma kun dga' rin chen

dang / /gang de'i thugs sras 'jam dbyangs sku mched la/ /snying nas thal sbyar gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /khyad par sngags 'chang rgyal ba'i rgyal tshab mchog /'dzam gling mdzes
pa'i rgyan gcig sems dpa' che/ rgyal ba rab 'byams ma lus bskyed pa'i yab/ /mnyam med bka' drin can la gus btud nas/ /'dzam gling byang phyogs thub pa'i rgyal tshab
mchog /sa skya pa yi gdung rabs byon tshul gyi/ /rnam thar ngo mtshar rin chen bang mdzod 'di/ /'chad par 'gyur gyis don gnyer dga' bas nyon/ /ces mchod par brjod cing bshad
par dam bcas nas nyan par gdams te/ 'dir 'dzam gling byang phyogs kyi thub pa'i rgyal tshab chen po dpal ldan sa skya pa'i gdung rabs rin po che ji ltar byon pa'i tshul
gyi rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar rin po che'i bang mdzod dgos 'dod kun 'byung

zhes bya ba 'di 'chad pa la don lnga ste/ 'od gsal lha'i gdung rabs bshad pa/ dri med 'khon gyi gdung rabs bshad pa/ lha rigs 'khon sa skya pa'i gdung rabs bshad pa/ de las
gyes pa'i bla brang rnam bzhi'i gdung rabs bshad pa/ skabs su babs pa'i don gzhan bshad pa'o/ /de'i dang po 'od gsal lha'i gdung rabs bshad pa la yang tshigs bcad kyi sgo
nas mdor bstan pa dang / de'i don rgyas par bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ /mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i sa skya pa'i gdung rabs ya rabs kha
rgyan las/ /'jam dbyangs sprul pa dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /gdung gi thog ma 'od gsal lha yul du/ /spyi ring g.yu ring g.yu se mched gsum byon/ /g.yu ses mi rje mdzad nas
sras bzhi bskrun/ /de yi grogs su gcen po g.yu ring byon/ /g.yu ring dang ni dmu bza' ldem bu'i sras/ /ma bzang spun bdud byon pa'i gcen po drug /yab dang bcas pa lha yi
yul du gshegs/ /bdun gyi tha chung ma bzang spyi rje dang / /thog lcam 'ur mo'i sras ni dpa' bo stag /de dang klu lcam bra ma gnyis kyi sras/ /klu tsha stag po 'od can
zhes pa byung / /klu tsha dang ni mon bza' mtsho mo rgyal/ /lhan cig bzhugs pa'i rigs sras g.ya' spang gi /mtshams su 'khrungs pas mtshan yang g.ya' spang skyes/ /zhes grags
gzhan gyis mi thub dpa' bo byon/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa de'i don rgyas par bshad pa la/ de la spyir bod kha ba can gyi ljongs 'dir rigs gsum mgon po'i rnam sprul chos rgyal
byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rgyal ba'i bstan pa sngar med gsar du btsugs/ gtsang g.yo dmar gsum/ bla chen mkhan brgyud rnams kyis sngar yod nyams pa gsos/ lha btsun
khu dbon/ jo bo yab sras/ 'brog 'gos mar gsum/ pa tshab rngog khyung / ra 'bro la sogs pas shin tu dar ba mdzad mod kyi/ phal cher mdo dang sngags kyi phyogs re ba tsam
du zad la/ dus phyis rgyal ba thams cad kyi ye shes gcig tu bsdus pa rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid 'khon gyi gdung brgyud kyi tshul bzung nas/ phyi nang mdo sngags bshad
sgrub kyi bstan pa mtha' dag 'dzin skyong spel gsum gyi sgo nas ches shin tu rgyas par mdzad de/ shar phyogs rgya mtsho'i mthas gtugs pa'i 'dzam gling byang phyogs kyi
skye dgu thams cad chos dang zang zing gi dpal 'byor bzang pos legs par bskyangs pa ni ngo mtshar zhing bka' drin shin tu che bar gyur pa yin pas/ de lta bu'i skyes bu
bzang po rim par byon pa de rnams kyi byon tshul dang / rnam par thar pa 'chad pa dang nyan pa la 'bad par bya ba ni don chen po dang ldan pa nyid du rig par bya'o/ /de
la 'di'i rigs ni bod du bram ze'i rigs su gsal ba ma byung bas/ rgyal rigs/ rje'u rigs/ dmangs rigs gsum las/ zhang blon rje'u rigs yin te/ 'di nyid kyi mi'i gdung rabs kyi
thog ma dkon pa rje gung stag tu grags pa de nyid nas 'dzin par bshad pa'i phyir ro/ /rus ni bod kyi rus chen bzhi dang / mi'u rigs drug tu grags pa sogs las chad pa ma
yin gyi/ gdung rus gtsang ma lha las babs pa yin te/ de yang nges pa'i don du 'jam

pa'i dbyangs nyid gdul bya gzhan gyi ngor 'od gsal gyi lha'i rigs su sprul pa ni/ gnam lha spyi ring g.yu ring g.yu se ste mched gsum du grags pa mi yul du babs pa la mi'i
rje zhus pas/ gnam lha chung ba g.yu ses mi rje mdzad pas/ /sras se byi li spun bzhir grags pa byung / de dag gis ldong rus chen bco brgyad dang 'thab/ de'i grogs la gnam
lha bar pa g.yu ring gis byon te ldong btul nas bran du byas/ bar pa g.yu ring 'dis dmu'i bu mo dmu za ldem bu khab tu bzhes pas sras ma bzang spun bdun du grags pa byung
zhing / de ltar bdun gyi gcen drug yab dang bcas pa lha yul du gshegs/ bdun pa ma sang spyi rje bya ba des mi yul du bzhugs nas thog lha 'od can gyi bu mo thog lcam 'ur
mo khab tu bzhes pa la sras thog tsha dpa' bo stag tu grags pa 'khrungs te/ des klu'i bu mo klu lcam bra ma khab tu bzhes pas klu tsha stag po 'od can bya ba sras su byung
/ de yan chad bar snang la bzhugs par bshad cing klu tsha des mon bza' mtsho mo rgyal khab tu bzhes pa la sras gcig g.ya' dang spang gi mtshams su skyes shing / 'di 'dra
re re tsam yin zhes grags pas mtshan yang g.ya' spang skyes gcig tu btags/ 'di nyid kyis g.yas ru shangs kyi nub byang na byang ri kun las mtho zhing mdzes pa cig yod
pa'i ri de la gnas bcas pas ri de la yang g.ya' spang du grags so zhes pa de rnams kyis lha'i gdung rabs bstan zin to/ /'dir smras pa/ lha yi mchog rje btsun 'jam dpal gyis/
/gzhan ngor gzhan don dbang gis sprul pa'i skur/ /legs byon legs par bshad

pa'i ngo mtshar gtam/ /'di 'dra 'di zhes gang gis smras de mdzes/ /bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa'o// //spyi don gnyis pa dri med 'khon gyi gdung rabs bshad pa la yang tshigs
bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang / de'i don rgyas par bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ sa skya pa'i gdung rabs ya rabs kha rgyan las/ gong du drangs pa'i g.ya' spang
skyes byon pa'i tshul bshad pa'i rjes de ma thag par/ gang des srin po skya rengs khrag med ni/ /bsad nas chung ma g.ya' 'brum si li ma/ /phrogs te nyid kyi khab tu bzhes
pa las/ /sras gcig byung ba 'khon par skyes zhes grags/ /de dang btsan bza' lcam bu sgron gyi sras/ /gzugs mdzes blo ldan mi yul dkon pa 'khrungs/ /de la dkon pa rje gung
stag ces btags/ /'khon ston dpal po cher grags gnyan rtser byon/ /dpal po che dang glang bza' ne chung sras/ /khri mdzes lha legs tshe lha dbang phyug dang / /mkhas mchog
klu yi dbang po tshe 'dzin bzhi/gdung rabs ya rabs kha rgyan 'dir bshad pa ltar/ 'khon dpal po che la sras bzhi byung pa'i lugs dang / klu'i dbang po dang rdo rje rin
chen te sras gnyis byung ba'i lugs srol mi 'dra ba las/ kho bo ni phyi ma'i rjes su 'brangs pa ste rgyas bshad 'og nas 'byung ngo / /tshe 'dzin sras ni rdo rje dkon mchog
lhun grub kyi gdung rabs tshigs bcad ma 'di sogs gdung rabs 'ga' zhig las/ 'khon rdo rje rin chen tshe 'dzin gyi sras su 'dod pa ni/ rje btsun rin po ches sa skya pa chen
po'i rnam thar du yi ge pas ma dag pa'i skyon byung ba bzhin gyi rjes su 'brang ba yin la/ rdo rje rin chen klu'i dbang po'i gcung du 'dod pa rnams ni/ rje btsun gyis
mdzad pa'i 'khon gyi gdung rabs dang / ga ring rgyal po'i rtsis bsdur gyi yi ge

sogs khungs thub kyi yig cha dag pa du ma'i rjes su 'brangs pa yin te/ kho bo cag ni rjes 'brangs phyi ma nyid gtso bor bzung ngo / rin po che/ /gang de'i btsun mo 'bro bza'
g.ya' lon skyid/ /de la 'bro tsha mched bdun byon pa las/ /gzhan rnams yul phyogs so sor 'gro don mdzad/ mtha' ltag shes rab yon tan grom par byon/ /de nas yon tan 'byung
gnas tshul khrims rgyal/ /gtsug tor shes rab dge skyabs dge mthong dang / /'khon ston bal po shAkya blo gros rnams/ /rim bzhin snga ma'i rigs sras phyi ma yin/ /shAkya
blo gros sras gnyis che ba'i mtshan/ /shes rab tshul khrims dkon mchog rgyal po gcung / /gcen po yan chad gsang sngags snga 'gyur mdzad/ /ces so/ /gnyis pa de'i don rgyas
par bshad pa la/ g.ya' spang skyes zhes grags pa'i dpa' bo chen po des/ srin po skya rengs khrag med ces bya ba la chung ma g.ya' 'brum si li ma zhes bya ba shin tu mtshar
ba cig yod pas/ srin po dang 'thab rol byas/ khyo bsad/ chung ma khab tu bzhes pa la sras gcig 'khrungs pa/ lha dang srin par 'khon pa'i bar du byung bas g.ya' phrug
'khon bar skyes su btags/ gdung brgyud 'di la 'khon gyi mtshan yang de nas byung ste shAka rigs bzhin no/ /yum sras de gnyis gnas pa'i g.ya' spang gi nub byang na gangs ri'i
phreng ba chen po'i nang na shin tu mdzes shing mtho ba shel tsha rgyal mo'i gangs su grags pa dang / g.ya' spang gi lho 'gram na sa skya pa'i bla mtsho yang yod do/
/thog mar 'od gsal gyi lha mi yul du babs pa'i tshe yang shel tsha rgyal mo'i gangs de nyid kyi rtse mor babs pa

yin ces/ /sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung rgyun bdag gi bla ma 'jam dbyangs sku mched las dngos su thos so/ /gdung rabs kha cig las/ yul mtho zhing sa gtsang ba mnga'
ris stod kyi sa'i char babs par bshad do/ /lha phrug 'khon bar skyes des btsan bza' lcam bu sgron khab tu bzhes pa la mi'i mchog gcig 'khrungs pa ni/ mthu stobs dang rdzu
'phrul che ba/ blo dang rig par ldan pa/ gzugs dang lang tshor 'dzom pa/ kun gyi yid 'phrog pa zhig byung bas 'di 'dra mi yul du 'byung ba dkon byas nas mtshan dkon pa
rje gung stag ces btags/ 'di yul tshol du btang bas bsam yas la yul gyi dge 'am yon tan bcu ga tshang ste rgyal pos bzung tshar ba dang / la stod gnyen rtse thar gyi ya
chang la yul gyi dge brgyad tshang bar gzigs nas bzung ste/ de yang dge brgyad ni sa'i dge zhing thang chen thang chung ni khang sa dang zhing sar bzang / chu'i dge mtsho
chen mtsho mo ni 'thung chu dang zhing chu ru bzang / shing gi dge nags dgun tha dang dgun smug ni khang shing dang bud shing du bzang / rtswa'i dge thar gyi ya chad ni
gam 'brog dang rgyad 'brog tu bzang ba'o/ /dge bcu la stag tshang lo tsA bas/ gong gi brgyad po'i steng du kha cig phu na la sgo/ mda' na gru sgo yod pa zer mod kyang /
de gnyis bcud kyi yon tan yin pas mi 'thad kyi/ gzhan brgyad snod kyi yon tan yin pa bzhin du/ rdo'i dge khang rdo dang 'thag rdo zhes bya la/ gnyis tshan nang phan tshun
tshogs pa shin tu 'gal bas/ gcig yod sa na cig shos yod pa shin tu dkon

pas dge bcu tshang ba dka' ba yin no zhes bshad do/ /rje 'dis bsam yas kyi chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan gyi thugs zin pas nang blon bcol/ dpal 'byor shin tu 'phel bas
'khon dpal bo che zhes bya bar grags shing 'khon gyi mtshan grags de de nas byung ngo / /'dis glang khams pa lo tsA ba'i lcam mo glang bza' ne chung ma khab tu bzhes pa la
sras gnyis 'khrungs pa'i che ba la/ 'khon lo tsA ba klu'i dbang po bsrung ba/ chung ba 'khon rdo rje rin po che zhes bya zhing / 'dir rje btsun chen po'i sa chen gyi rnam
thar las/ sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba sad mi mi bdun zhes bya ba las/ gzhon gsum gyi nang nas mkhas par byed pa 'khon klu'i dbang po zhes bya ba yin no/ /de'i gcung phal
pa zhig la sras yon tan gyis phyug pa rdo rje rin po che zhes bya ba byung ngo zhes gsungs pa'i rjes su 'brangs nas/ ya rabs kha rgyan sogs nyi lde/ mus srad pa/ ngo mtshar
snang ba sogs gdung rabs kha cig tu/ khri mdzes lha legs/ tshe lha dbang phyug klu'i dbang po/ tshe 'dzin dang bzhi byung bar bshad pa dang / yang kha cig tshe 'dzin
dang rdo rje rin chen gcig nyi lde gdung rabs las bshad par 'dod pa dang / de gnyis ya rabs kha rgyan dang /ngo mtshar snang ba/ gtsang byams pa'i gdung rabs rnams las yab
sras su bshad/ yab sras su 'dod pa sogs mang du snang yang / rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa'i 'khon gyi gdung rabs las/ 'khon klu'i dbang po bsrungs pa zhes bya ba ni sad
mi mi bdun gyi yab gcig lags/ de'i gcung po 'khon rdo rje rin po che slob dpon padma 'byung gnas kyi slob ma bsten sngags par bzhugs pa yin zhes

dang / kun mkhyen chen po'i gsung rab dgongs gsal las/ lho pa kun mkhyen dang / bde ba can pa ye shes mgon po gnyis kyis kyang rdo rje rin po che klu'i dbang po'i gcung du
bzhed par bshad pa dang / gzhan yang gdung rabs che stag tshang gdung rabs dang bla ma dam pa'i dngos slob shes rab rdo rjes mdzad pa'i gdung rabs sogs phran mang po zhig
mthun par de ltar du 'byung zhing / rje btsun gyi bla ma sa chen gyi rnam thar las/ de'i gcung phal pa zhig la zhes pa'i don rdo rje rin chen klu'i dbang po'i gcung gi sras
su bshad pa ltar na tshe 'dzin phal pa dang / de'i sras phal pa ma yin pa lta bu zhig bstan dgos la de ltar na yab sras gnyis po de phal pa yin min gyi khyad par 'byed
dgos pa las/ de ni shin tu dka' bar snang bas des na de'i gcung phal pa zhig la zhes pa ni yi ge ma dag pa'am/ yang na klu'i dbang po de'i gcung po ni yum phal pa zhig
la 'khrungs pa'i sras yon tan gyis phyug pa/ mtshan rdo rje rin chen zhes bya ba de nyid yin zhes pa'i don yin te/ rje btsun gyi 'khon gyi gdung rabs dang / ga ring rgyal
po la rtsis bsdur du gnang ba'i yi ge gnyis ka las/ rdo rje rin chen klu'i dbang po'i gcung du bshad pas/ rje btsun gyi gsung rab la nang 'gal mi srid pa'i phyir/ des na
gcung du 'dod pa de bzhin 'thad pa yin zhes sa lo chen po'i gsung las 'byung ba ltar sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po yab sras rnams kyang bzhed pa lags/ de yang klu'i dbang
po bsrungs pa ni rgya gar shar phyogs za hor gyi mkhas grub chen po gangs can gyi dpal mgon mkhan chen zhi ba

'tshos bod la rab byung rung mi rung nyams sad pas/ rung bar gzigs nas gnang pa'i bod kyi rab byung gi thog ma sad mi mi bdun du drags pa lo tsA ba khyad par can sprul pa'i
gang zag bdun la/ rgan gsum/ gzhon gsum/ bar pa gcig rnams byung ba'i gzhon gsum gyi bar pa 'khon nA gendra rakShi ta zhes bya ste/ bod skad du klu'i dbang po bsrungs pa'o/
/kha cig 'di khong rang gi zhang po las rab tu byung zhes zer ba ni sad mir 'dod pa dang 'gal te/ sad mi bdun la sad mi zhes pa'i rgyu mtshan/ mkhan chen zhi ba 'tshos
bod la rab byung rung mi rung nyams sad pa na rung bar dgongs nas/ de'i drung du rab tu byung zhing bod du rab byung gi thog ma yin pas na de skad ces bya la/ glang khams
pa lo tsA ba ni sad mi mi bdun gyi bar pa bde gshegs go cha bsrungs pa zhes grags pa de nyid yin pas/ de'i drung du rab tu byung na 'khon 'di sad mi ma yin par 'gyur te/
'di'i thog mar bod kyi rab byung byung bar khas len dgos pas so/ /rgyu mtshan de'i phyir na mkhan chen gyis sdom phrug tu bshad pa 'di nyid 'thad pa yin no/ /des na mkhan
chen dang zhang po la chos mang du bslab/ lo tsA legs par mkhyen/ slob dpon chen po padma las kyang gdams ngag nod/ yer pa'i brag la sgrub pa mdzad pas grub pa thob/
mkhas grub kyi grags pa cher byung bas 'khon chos kyi che ba'i thog ma yin no/ /gcung rdo rje rin po ches kyang slob dpon padma las gsang sngags rnying ma'i chos mang du
gsan zhing bslab/ grub pa yang ci rigs thob/ mtshan grags thon/ 'di'i yab yul du 'bro dgra

'dul gyi bu mo 'bro bza' g.yang lon skyid khab tu bzhes pa la sras bdun byung zhing / zhang po de bod kyi gyad pa'i brgyud yin pas zhang rigs kyi sku rtsal shin tu che bar
byung / de'i tshe 'brog gnyan rtser ltad mo nyi ma gsum byung ba la sku mched bdun pos rta dang lus chas nyin re bzhin re re spos te/ de yang nyi ma dang po la rta dkar ber
dkar/ gnyis pa la rta dmar ber dmar/ gsum pa la rta nag ber nag tu byas te rta rgyugs tshab 'gran byas pas/ khrom thog chod pa byung ba na zhang po la 'gras 'dzugs par
go nas zhang pos dmag bsags 'thab mo byed zer byung ba la/ khong rnams kyis gcig par zhang po yin/ gnyis par khyim mtshes yun ring 'grogs nas/ rgyal khams yangs po la dog
'tsher byed don med zer nas/ che ba mnga' ris mang yul du byon/ de 'og mnga' ris gung thang / de 'og srad/ de 'og gnyal lo ro/ /de 'og nyang shab tu byon te yul so sor
bzung bas/ de rnams las gyes pa'i 'khon tsho mang du 'phel te grags chen ma byung / chung bas pha yul rang du bzhugs/ 'bro dang 'khrug pa yang sprad/ de las gyes pa gnyan
rtse rang na ma khrigs sde gsum du grags pa byung ngo / /drug pa shes rab yon tan gyi grom pa g.ya' lung du bzhugs/ de la sras gnyis byung ba'i chung ba khab so stag thog
tu byon/ de las gyes pa la stod byang gi 'khon tsho rnams yin/ che ba yon tan 'byung gnas kyis yab mes kyi chos brgyud bzung la/ de la sras gsum byung ba'i tshul khrims
rgyal pos grom par bzhugs nas chos kyis gdul bya

bskyangs shing / de la sras gsum byung ba'i bar pa brdal chang tshang du byon/ che ba gtsug tor shes rab dang / chung ba g.ya' lung du bzhugs/ gtsug tor shes rab la sras bdun
'khrungs/ de bdun nu bo dang bcas pa la 'khon tsho brgyad du grags shing / bdun po'i lnga pa 'khon dge skyabs kyis phyis shab tu byon/ de la sras gnyis byung ba'i chung
ba la shab stod kyi 'khon mi rnams gyes par grags/ che ba dge mthong la sras gcig byung ba la 'khon ston bal po zhes bya ba tsha mo rong gi brag la yang phur gyi sgrub
pa mdzad pas grub pa brnyes shing bstan ma bcu gnyis bran du 'khol/ de la sras shAkya blo gros/ 'dis bya ru lung pa dang / shab stod smad bzung zhing 'phrin las kyang che
bar byung bar grags la/ sku tshe smad la yab mes kyi yul g.ya' lung mkhar stabs bzung / sras gnyis byung ba'i che ba 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims/ chung ba 'khon dkon
mchog rgyal po'o/ /gcen gyis lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug gi mkhan bu zhu ston brtson 'grus drung du gzhon nu nas gau mi'i dge bsnyen mdzad/ tshangs spyod shin tu btsun pas
sras med/ yab mes kyi chos la mkhas/ rdo rje phur pa'i grub pa thob/ mthu dang rdzu 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab par grags so/ /de ltar shes rab tshul khrims yan rnams kyis
phar phyin sogs mtshan nyid kyi skor ci rigs pa dang / sngags la gsar ma sde drug snga 'gyur lnga/ phyi 'gyur bcu gsum/ phyi mo nyi shu rtsa gcig la sogs pa'i gsang sngags
snga 'gyur la shin tu mkhas shing / yang dag dang phur pa la thugs dam gyi mthil mdzad pas grub pa

brnyes/ chos skyong dkar mo nyi zla dang bdud mgon la mdzad pas nus pa thon pa sha stag go zhes pa de rnams kyis dri med 'khon gyi gdung rabs byon tshul bstan zin to/ /'dir
smras pa/ ma rig la 'khon 'khon ston mthu rtsal can/ /rim bzhin legs byon byon tshul 'di mthong na/ /gdung brgyud brgyud pa rin chen phreng ba 'di/ /ngo mtshar mtshar ba'i
yul du cis mi rtogs/ /bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa'o// //spyi don gsum pa lha rigs 'khon sa skya pa'i gdung rabs bshad pa la yang tshigs bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan
pa dang / de'i don rgyas par bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ sa skya pa'i gdung rabs ya rabs kha rgyan las/ 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims sku mched gnyis byon pa'i/ gcen
po yan chad gsang sngags snga 'gyur mdzad pa'i tshul bshad pa'i rjes de ma thag par/ gcung gis gsar 'gyur srol bskyangs sa skya btab/ /de dang zhang mo bsod nams skyid
kyi sras/ /sa skya'i bla chen kun dga' snying por grags/ /bla chen de yi btsun mo tsha rong ma/ /jo lcam phur mo'i sras ni kun dga' 'bar/ /btsun mo gnyis pa jo lcam 'od
sgron sras/ /slob dpon rtse mo rje btsun grags pa dang / /dpal chen 'od po zhes bya rnam gsum yin/ /dpal chen 'od po'i btsun mo gar phu ma/ /nyi khri lcam la sa skya paN
chen dang / /zangs tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan rnam gnyis 'khrungs/ /zangs tsha'i btsun mo mdog stod tsha sna ma/ /ma gcig kun skyid sras po 'phags pa dang / /'gro mgon phyag
na rdo rje mched gnyis

byon/ /btsun mo gnyis pa sa skya'i chu mdo ma/ /jo 'bro'i sras po slob dpon rin rgyal te/ /gsum pa ma gcig rdo rje ldan gyi sras/ /slob dpon chen po ye shes 'byung gnas so/
/phyag na'i btsun mo ma gcig zhwa lu ma/ /mkha' 'gro 'bum sras dharma pA la yin/ /dharma pA la'i btsun mo stag 'bum sras/ /ratna bha dra gzhon nu'i dus su gshegs/ /ye 'byung
btsun mo ma gcig khab smad ma/ /chos srin skyid la bdag nyid chen po 'khrungs/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa de'i don rgyas par bshad pa la/ 'khon rog shes rab tshul khrims kyi
gcung po dkon mchog rgyal po ni 'khon sa skya pa zhes grags pa'i thog ma rang yin te/ shing pho khyi la sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu nas yab dang gcen la dbang bshad man ngag
mang du gsan/ yab mes kyi chos la mkhas par sbyangs/ gsang sngags gsar 'gyur la yang mos pa yod pa'i skabs su 'bro'i lung ston chen mo cig byung sar byon pas/ ltad mo sna
tshogs 'dug pa'i nang nas sngags pa mang pos dbang phyug ma nyi shu rtsa brgyad kyi mgo brnyan gyon/ phyag mtshan so sor khyer/ ma mo ral pa can gyis rnga stabs dang bcas
nas 'chams kyin 'dug pas/ ltad mo yang de kha che/ khrom thog kyang des chod song / de'i rgyu mtshan rnams gcen la zhus pas/ da gsang sngags 'chol par spyod pa zhes bya
ba'i dus byung bas/ da phyin chad rnying ma ba la grub thob mtshan nyid pa dkon pa yin pas/ rang la yod pa rnams rang nyid dbang che ba yin pas nga rang gi dpe cha rten
gsum rnams gter du sbed gsungs nas sbas pas/ yang phur gnyis chos

skyong gnyan nas sbed ma thub pas/ phyis kyi gdung brgyud rnams kyis kyang 'di gnyis la thugs dam mdzad/ chos skyong dkar mo nyi zla lcam sring la dus gtor ma chag pa 'di byung
ba yin no/ /de nas gcen gyi zhal nas/ nga ni rgas 'dug /khyod gzhon pa yin pas gsang sngags gsar 'gyur slob/ de yang da lta 'brog mi shAkya ye shes mkhas pas der rgyug
gsungs pa la der mthon/ 'khyin lo tsA ba la kye rdo rje'i dbang zhus/ rgyud gsan/ rgyud cung ma rdzogs pa la 'khyin lo grongs/ chos 'phro 'brog mi'i drung du zhus gsungs
pa ltar zhur byon pas/ khyod kyi pha shi nas mes po snyegs pa lags sam gsungs nas dgyes/ phyis yul zhing 'ga' btsongs nas rta bcu bdun dang / rtswa rin nor bu'i phreng
ba dang bcas pa phul/ gsung ngag rin po che zhus pas lam skor cha lag 'ga' re gnang / khyad par rgyud gsum gyi bshad pa rgyas par gnang nas/ bshad bka' 'dzin pa'i bu chen
lnga'i nang nas mchog tu gyur/ gzhan yang 'gos lo tsA ba la gsang 'dus kyi skor gsan/ o rgyan gyi paNDi ta shes rab gsang ba la thig le lnga'i skor/ rma lo tsA ba la bde
mchog dang grub snying gi skor la sogs pa gsan/ gzhan yang mal lo tsA ba/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ spu hrang lo tsA ba/ gnam kha'u pa sku mched/ 'khon sgyi chu ba/ skyu ra a seng
la sogs pa bla ma dam pa mang po la sems bskyed/ dbang bshad man ngag mtha' yas pa gsan nas sngags gsar rnying mtha' dag gi bdag por gyur/ de nas zhang yul 'jag gshong
du yab dang gcen gyi

phyi rten bzhengs/ de'i nang du seng ldeng gi phur pa byin rlabs can cig bzhugs su bcug bra bo lung par dgon chung cig btab nas lo 'ga' bzhugs pas de la sa skya gog por grags
so/ /de'i tshe dpon slob rnams kyis skyo sangs la byon te ri kha nas gzigs pas/ dpon po ri glang po che nyal ba 'dra ba'i mkhal khung g.yas pa'i thad nas dkar zhing snum
pa/ chu g.yas su 'bab pa la sogs pa bkra shis dang dge mtshan du ma dang ldan par gzigs nas/ 'dir dgon pa gcig btab na bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa rgya chen po 'byung
ba 'dug snyam du dgongs te/ de skor gyi sa cha spyi'i bdag po jo bo gdong nag pa bya ba yod pa de la zhus pas kyang gnang / sgos kyi bdag po zhang gzhung gu ra ba dang
/ bande grong bzhi/ lha mi grong bdun bya ba yod pa de rnams la/ nga 'dir dgon pa cig byed 'dod pas khyed rnams la 'gal ba mi 'ong na khyed rnams la rin cig kyang 'jal
bas sa cha 'di nga la byin na ji ltar legs gsungs pas/ rin ye mi 'tshal cis kyang mdzad par zhu zer nas phul ba la/ bla mas 'on kyang phyi rabs tshun chad la 'thad pa yong
gsungs nas rgod ma dkar mo gcig nor bu'i phreng ba/ mo gos gcig la sogs pa gnang nas/ mon grog man nas 'bal grog yan bla ma bdag par byas nas/ bla ma 'di dgung lo bzhi
bcu bzhes pa sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa lnga brgya pa phrag bcur gnas pa'i nang nas/ phrag bdun pa mngon pa'i dus kyi lnga brgya'i steng nas lo nyis brgya dang bdun lon pa
chu mo glang gi lo khrums kyi zla ba'i yar tshes la bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan sa

skya'i gtsug lag khang btab/ 'di man chad nas gdung brgyud rnams la lha rigs 'khon sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud du grags/ de'i sras jo bo lha gcig gi bande byang chub sems dpa'
'am/ sbyin pa dpal gyi bar srid spyan ras gzigs kha sar pA Ni'i tshul du yod pa la/ gnam kha'u pas dkon mchog rgyal po'i btsun mo snga ma rdo rje phyug mo la 'khon gyi
sras ma byung bar brten/ ma gcig zhang mo la rten 'brel 'grig par mkhyen nas/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po la de bzhin gyi thabs lam 'grig pa'i bka' stsal gnang ba thog tu khel
ba'i legs lam la brten gong gi spyan ras gzigs bar srid kyi tshul du yod pa/ ma gcig zhang mo'i lhums su zhugs pa las rje btsun sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po
zhes kha ba can gyi rdo rje 'dzin pa kun gyi gtsug rgyan dam par gyur pa de nyid byon pa yin te/ de yang gnam kha'u pa chen pos 'khon dkon mchog rgyal por gdung sras 'byung
ba'i rten 'brel sgrig bar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ de'i dus su kha'u skyed lhas kyi dgon pa na rje btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug chos kyi rgyal mtshan de nyid kyi 'od gsal la
rtse gcig tu zhugs pa'i gzigs snang la dkar gong lung gi nam mkha'i thad 'ja' 'od gur khang 'khyil ba'i dbus na bar srid kyi tshul la/ rnam pa spyan ras gzigs kha sar pA
Ni zhal gcig phyag gnyis kyi g.yas mchog sbyin dang / g.yon utpal mtheb srin gyis 'dzin pa/ dar dang rin po ches brgyan pa/ zhabs gnyis mnyam pa'i stabs kyis bzhengs nas
bzhugs pa zhig mngon sum lta bur gzigs nas de la brtag

dpyad mdzad pa na/ spyan ras gzigs kyi rnam sprul zhig 'byon par dgongs nas/ de nas rje btsun kha'u pas rten 'brel 'grig pa'i slad du dkon mchog rgyal po sa skyar bzhugs pa
la yang yang du byon gsungs nas lan mang du byon pa'i phal cher nyin 'khor mdzad pa la/ skabs shig gi tshe nyi ma ma rgas tsam gyi bar gsung gleng mdzad de 'gor/ de nas
phud rin nas shig gnang nas/ do nub 'dis phud tshod gcig 'jal la dkar gong lung du nges par bzhugs shig gsungs pa'i tshe/ 'khon gyi thugs dgongs la de ring 'di 'dra'i phyi
ba la sdod kyang mi gsungs pa snyam nas thugs yi chad de ba cig la byon te/ phru ma'i gdong phyogs de nas skyed lhas phyogs la phyi mig zhig gzigs nas/ rgan po brdzangs
nas bla ma thugs rje chung / /zhes gsungs shing yi chad de ba zhig gi ngang nas byon pas/ ri gdong de la thugs rje gdong dang / 'phrang de la yi chad 'phrang zhes kyang
grags so/ /de nas 'on kyang bla ma ci gsungs bya snyam du dal bus byon pas nyi ma ma rgas par dkar gong lung du phebs pa dang / de dang dus mnyam du ma gcig dkar gong lung
ma'i chu zhig bcus nas g.yas skor du byon pa gnyis ma bsgrigs rang 'grig tu rten 'brel 'grigs nas/ 'khon gyis do nub nga la gnas tshang zhig thongs gsungs pas/ ma gcig
gis kyang shin tu gus pas nang du gdan drangs/ de nas bla mas chang zhig tshong gsungs pas/ phud ro mchog dang ldan zhing snod kyang gas chag med pa zhig drung du khyer byung
bas rten 'brel bzang snyam du bzhes te/ de nub bla ma'i bka' bzhin gnas

der bzhugs pas rten 'brel phun sum tshogs pa 'grigs shing / de rjes rim gyis zla grangs tshang ba na/ rje btsun kha'u pa nyid kyi bka' lung la/ da ni 'di phyogs su gdan drongs
shig bkur sti rim gro gang drag nga rang gis byed pa yin no gsungs nas yum gyi phru mar phebs shing / de nas re zhig song ba na yab dkon mchog rgyal po dgung lo nga dgur
phebs ba na/ anggir zhes pa chu pho spre'u'i lo ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po nyid da lta phru ma'i bdud 'dul mchod rten dus
'khor nas bshad pa bzhin sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos gsar bzhengs gnang ba bzhugs pa'i sa 'dir 'khrungs pa yin no/ /de la dgongs nas bar skabs su phyogs 'di na shag
sa nyor zhig las gzhan med pa la/ dus phyis phru ma'i dgon gnas ngo mtshar can 'di yang sngags 'chang bla ma de nyid kyis gsar du 'debs par mdzad pa yin la/ de nas jo sras
'khrungs ma thag gnam kha'u pas sku pang du bzhes shing bsngags pa ches cher mdzad de/ /'di ni nges par spyan ras gzigs sam/ byang chub sems dpa' sbyin pa dpal nyid yin
la/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug nyid du'ang mi 'gal ba yin no zhes gsungs shing / de nas sku skyed shin tu che bas kun gyis mthong na dga' zhing yid du 'ong ba zhig byung bas
mtshan yang kun dga' snying por gsol zhing / re zhig rdo rje phyug mo la gsang ba las/ skabs shig na khong gi shes nas de ma thag 'khon ston chen po la/ nyid kyi brgyud
'di chad du phongs pa yin pas/ zhang mo la sras yod pa de

bdag la gsang ba ma legs/ nga nyid la sras yod pas chog bdag la nor mi dgos/ sras kyi yum la nor dgos pa yin zhus nas/ sa skya'i mdun gyi mchod zhing ma gtogs gzhis tsho thams
cad zhang mo yum sras la gtad do/ /'di'i mchod zhing la bya phra ma yin zer ba dang / smad zhing yin pa'i tshul gdung rabs dag na mi 'dra bar snang ngo / /rje sa chen
gyi yum gyi yul gyi ming la yang mkhar sgo lung ma dag la dkar gong lung zhes pa dag pa yin te/ de'i rgyu mtshan lung pa 'di nyid na gser kha yod pas/ de'i kha bun la dkar
gong 'byung bas de'i lung par grags pa yin pas so zhes kyang yig tshang rnying pa 'ga' zhig las 'byung ba yin no/ /de ltar spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa rje sa skya pa
chen po sogs rigs gsum mgon po'i sprul pa'i gang zag sa phyogs 'dir rgyun mi chad pa 'byon pa dang / de dag gi bsti gnas gdan sa chen po bstan srung dang bcas pa 'byung tshul
jo bo rje dang / slob dpon padma sogs kyis lung bstan pa'i tshul ni/ de yang jo bo rje dpal ldan a ti sha bod du byon nas mnga' ris stod sogs su lo gsum bzhugs/ 'brom
ston pas spyan drangs te dbus su phebs pa'i mar lam 'brong ngu la'i rtser phebs pa dang / dpon po ri gzigs pas/ de'i ngos la 'brong chen po gnyis rtswa bza' zhing yod pa
gzigs/ 'khor rnams la 'di ltar 'dug gsungs/ de ci'i ltas lags zhus pas/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su ma hA kA la gnyis der 'phrin las mdzad pa'i ltas su 'dug gsungs/ de sa skya
pa'i chos skyong gur zhal rnam gnyis la byed pa 'di lung

bstan/ de nas phyag 'tshal sgang du phebs pa dang chibs pa babs nas 'khor rnams la mchod pa shom gsungs nas sa dkar logs la phyag mchod rgyas par mdzad pa la/ 'khor rnams kyis
de ltar mdzad pa ci lags zhus pas/ khyed rnams kyis ma mthong ba yin nam/ sa dkar po pha gi logs la dhIHyig bdun dang / hrIHyig gcig hU~M yig gcig rnams 'dug pa la phyag
mchod byas pa yin gsungs/ de ci'i ltas lags zhus pas/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul pa bdun/ spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul pa gcig phyag na rdo rje'i sprul
pa gcig ste dgu thog mar 'byon zhing / gzhan yang rigs gsum mgon pa'i sprul pa rgyun mi chad pa gnas pha gir byon nas 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa'i rtags su 'dug gsungs pa dang
/ gzhan yang slob dpon padmas klong gsal mkha' 'gro snyan brgyud kyi lung bstan las/ kun dga' snying po sa skya lo tsA dang / /bsod nams rtse mo grags pa rgyal mtshan zhes/
/rigs gsum mgon po'i sprul pa gtsang du 'byung / /zhes dang / sa skyar lo tsA kun dga'i ming / /'phags pa'i ming can gnyis byung nas/ /bod 'bangs sems can bde la phan/
/sangs rgyas bstan pa lnga bcu 'dzin/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sprul pa yin/ /zhes gsungs/ de dag gi don slob dpon rin po ches sa chen la bstod par/ mgon khyod nges par
rdo rje 'chang dbang dang / /'jam pa'i dpal las gzhan du yod ma mchis/ /zhes dang / rje btsun chen pos/ 'jam pa'i dpal yang mi yi gzugs

'dzin cing / /zhes dang / rdo rje 'chang dang 'jam mgon dbyer med pa'i/ /bla ma mchog dang dam pa khyod nyid la/ /khyad par 'ga' yang bdag gis yod ma shes/ /zhes gsungs pa
ltar ro/ /de ltar rje sa chen gyi yab 'khon dkon mchog rgyal pos dpal ldan sa skya btab/ gdan sa yun ring du mdzad de bla ma 'brog mi nas brgyud pa'i rgyud kyi bshad pa shin
tu dar bar mdzad/ gdul bya mang po smin grol la bkod/ bstan pa'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad nas chu pho rta'i lo dgung lo drug cu re dgu bzhes pa'i tshe ngo mtshar ba'i ltas
du ma dang bcas nas sgo rum du bde bar gshegs so/ /gshegs khar zhal chems la/ sa skya 'di klu'i pho brang gi steng na brtsigs yod cing / dus phyis 'byor pa rgyas/ /spyod
pa rtsing pas klu'i gnod pa byung nyen yod pas/ grog po mdung tshugs kyi steng du nga'i pur 'di ma nyams pa ril por mchod rten gyi nang du bzhugs su chug gsungs pa'i
zhal ta byas pa bzhin/ da lta 'khon sku 'bum du grags pa 'di yin no/ /bla ma des gong du bstan pa ltar btsun mo gnyis khab tu bzhes pa las/ chen ma rdo rje phyug mo la sras
ma byung zhing / btsun mo chung ba yul kha'u'i mdo dkar gong lung ma/ pha ming zhang gzhung gu ra ba/ ma ming ma gcig zhang mo/ de la sras gcig 'khrungs pa sa skya pa
chen po kun dga' snying po ste de nyid 'khrungs pa'i tshul ni rgyas par gong du bshad pa ltar yin la/ skyes chen dam pa 'di nyid bltams pa nas brtsams te rim gyis longs spyod
dang dbang phyug phun sum tshogs par gyur nas mtho ris yon tan bdun la mnga' mdzad pa yin

no/ /de lta bu'i bla ma chen po de nyid la lung dang rtogs pa'i yon tan ji ltar mnga' ba gnyis kyi/ dang po la gnyis las/ thun mong gi yon tan ji ltar mnga' ba ni/ dang po
nyid nas klog yig rtsis la sogs pa la byang zhing lugs kyi bstan bcos rnams dang / skyes pa/ bud med/ dud 'gro/ nor bu brtag pa/ sgyu rtsal/ sman dpyad/ sgra/ snyan ngag
sdeb sbyor la sogs pa la mkhas par gyur pa'i tshul de dag gi sgo nas 'jig rten pa kun gyi yid tshim par mdzad pa yin no/ /gnyis pa thun mong ma yin pa'i yon tan la gnyis
kyi/ spyir gsan sbyong mdzad tshul ni/ thog ma kho nar yab las kye rdo rje'i dbang zhus te/ de'i thugs su chud pa'i chos rnams ci rigs par gsan no/ /de nas dgung lo bcu gcig
lon pa na yab bde bar gshegs te rtsis byas pas/ gshegs rdzong byed pa/ phyi rten gyi 'gram 'ding ba/ gdan sa ba tshud pa rnams nyin gcig la grub na shul du phun sum tshogs
pa yong zer bas/ yum na re/ /nyid kyi yab kyang lo tsA ba dang 'brel shin tu che zhing chos 'di brdzun chung zer nas mnyes te/ yab kyi slob dpon yang lo tsA ba yin
pas nyid kyang lo tsA ba cig la chos slob dgos shing / nyid chung bas 'o cag gi dgon pa mi zin/ gdan sa yang ba ri lo tsA ba la gtad pa drag zer nas/ ba ri ba g.yu mkhar
mo na yod pa spyan drangs te 'phrang brag dmar gnyis bsags nas chos 'khor byed pa/ phyi rten gyi 'gram 'ding ba/ ba ri ba gdan sa ston pa rnams nyin gcig la byas te/ zhing
mo che ma gtogs pa'i gzhis tsho bla ma ba ri

lo tsA ba la gtad do/ /bla ma'i zhal nas khyod pha jo sras kyi bu la slob gnyer byed dgos pa yin/ de la shes rab dgos pas de'i lha 'phags pa 'jam dpal yin zhing / a ra pa tsa
na 'di sgrubs gsungs nas bsgrubs pas/ res 'ga' dung gi mi chen po cig yong / res 'ga' seng ge chen po byung ba bla ma la zhus pas/ 'byung po dpe dkar kho bar chad bya
'dod pas/ bar der jo bo mi g.yo ba'i sgom bzlas gyis gsungs nas/ de'i rjes gnang dang chu'i srung ba sgrub thabs yan lag dang bcas pa rdzogs par gnang ste/ de ltar mdzad
pas bar chad zhi nas zla ba drug nas 'grub ste 'jam dpal gyis zhal gzigs shing / de'i sgrub khang 'jam dpal brag khung du grags pa bla brang shar gyi dkyil na yod do/ /de
ltar 'jam dbyangs kyis mngon sum du zhal bstan nas zhen pa bzhi bral gyi gdams pa stsal zhing / 'jam dbyangs kyi thugs ka nas ral gri mu 'brel ba bdun bla ma nyid kyi thugs
kar thim pa'i snang ba bstan pa ni/ gdung brgyud rnams kyang 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul pa sha stag dang / khyad par 'jam dbyangs gdung brgyud 'byon pa'i rten 'brel yin par
bshad cing / de ltar yi dam gyi lhas dngos su byin gyis brlabs pas shes bya phal mo che 'bad med du thugs su chud mod kyang / dam pa'i spyod pa dang mthun par bstan pa
dang / phyi rabs kyi gang zag rnams kyi bsam ngo dang bstun nas thos pa mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ de nas dgung lo bcu gnyis bzhes pa'i dus su da jo sras 'di slob gnyer cig la
gtong dgos pas gang du gtang ba drag gros byas pas/ chos kyi bshad

gzhi che bar 'dug pas mngon pa cig slob tu gtang ba drag zer te/ rong ngur smrig tu byon pas brang ti ba'i grwa pa rnams rdzogs nas brang khang med pas/ srang kha phug rdugs
cig tu char ba'i yol bas bcad nas bzhugs/ khang tshes na yar 'brog khob le pa'i grwa ba cig la 'brum bu sme ba nag po byung ba la/ nad g.yogs med pas ma bzod nas/ bla ma
'dis grwa pa de la g.yog mdzad pas phan te/ bla ma la 'gos nas 'brum bu'i nad kyis bsnyungs te/ de dus sa skya na a pho phag ston bya ba mig mthong mkhan cig yod pa des
snga dro nyi ma la 'thon nas bsdad tsa na/ shar phyogs bra chung gong kha na yar rta bra bo la zhon/ zhwa thang thebs can phod kha chen po gyon pa cig lcag g.yab kyin sa
skya'i thad kar rta kha bsgyur nas/ kun dga' snying po na yin yod khyed sa skya pa tshos ci mno ba yin zer ba cig byung / 'di bdud rgyal thod phreng can yin par grags/ de'i
lo rgyus bsnyad pas/ mi rnams kyis a pho zer ba bzhin yong ba cig yod phal cher bden las che zer te/ de'i dgongs mo bang chen pa slebs pa dang / ma gcig gis kun dga'
snying po ma shi na rung / shi na nga la'ang sa sbyar 'khor rgyu med bsam nas tshong 'phrul byas te gser la sogs pa mang po khyer nas byon pas/ yum sras mjal dus bla ma 'di
sku na gzhon pa dang / thag ring du bsnyung ba'i stabs nas yum gyi drung du bshum pas/ yum na re/ pha jo sras kyi bu bya ba la snying rus dgos pa yin/ snying rus kyis
tshugs dang / khyod dge 'dun rgya mtsho lta bu 'di'i gseb tu shi na rang legs

pa yin te zer nas she bcad skad/ de dus yum dang mjal khar bla chen gyi sku'i rjes brag la gsal por byung ba da lta yang yod ces grags so/ /de nas sku bsnyung ba las gdangs
nas ngur smrig pa brang ti dar ma snying po la mngon pa tshar gcig gsan nas ma lus pa thugs su chud pas kun gyis ngo mtshar du 'dzin par byung / de nas dge bshes brang ti
sku gshegs te zur chos pa byang chad pa khyung la sa sde lnga dang / sdom rnam gnyis dang bcas pa gsan cing / de'i rjes su nyang stod du khyung rin chen grags la rnam nges
dang rigs thig la sogs pa gsan/ de'i dus kyi zur chos pa me dig pa yin no/ /de tsa na sa skya pa'i gzhis pas 'phrin bskur te/ tshad ma phyis gsan pas chog bla ma ba ri
ba bgres pas phyis gsan long mi yong bas yar 'byon par zhu zhes zhus pas bla mas kyang yar byon nas/ bla ma ba ri ba la pha rol tu phyin pa'i gzhung lugs dang / 'phags
pa dkon mchog brtsegs pa dang / sangs rgyas phal po che las gzhung rab tu dbye ba dang / de'i man ngag dag kyang gsan/ bya ba'i rgyud las rgyud sde dum bu nyis brgya tsam
yan lag dang bcas pa man ngag phra mos brgyan pa gsan cing / spyod rgyud la gshin rje gshed/ khro bo rnam par rgyal ba yan lag dang bcas pa gsan/ rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud
la dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rtsa ba dang bshad pa'i rgyud lnga/ slob dpon 'phags pa yab sras kyi dgongs pa 'grel pa yan lag phra mo dang bcas pa/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs
kyi dgongs pa 'grel pa yan lag phra mo dang bcas pa rnams dang / gshin rje

gshed dgra nag po'i rgyud gsum/ dpal 'dzin gyi 'grel pa yan lag dang bcas pa rnams dang / dpal rdo rje gdan bzhi'i 'grel pa yan lag dang bcas pa dang / sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor
gyi 'grel pa yan lag dang bcas pa rnams dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang / man ngag phra mo brjod kyis mi long ba gsan zhing khong du chud par mdzad do/ /de ltar bla
ma ba ri bas gdan sa lo brgyad bzung zhing / de'i bar la rgya gar gyi gnas byin rlabs can du ma'i sa dang / byang chub kyi shing dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dang / paN grub
du ma'i ring bsrel dang gdung / khyad par du sangs rgyas 'od srung gi snam sbyar bzhugs pa'i rnam rgyal mchod rten/ bstan pa'i gzhi rten du 'gyur pa'i rten 'brel du ma
dang bcas pa bzhengs te/ rnam rgyal gyi gzungs 'bum ther gsum dang khri tsho bdun bzhugs shing / rab gnas kyi don du'ang rnam rgyal gyi cho ga stong phrag gnyis mdzad pa'i
tshes brgyad kyi nyin me tog gtor ba na/ mchod rten gyi bum pa las 'phros pa'i 'od ser po/ la la la gser btso ma'i 'od 'khyud pas mig gis mthong tshad kyi sa gzhi dang
nam mkha' khengs shing dril bu'i sgra lta bu 'khrol ba dang / legs so bya ba'i sgra mi che ba lan bzhi kun gyis mthong thos su gyur pas thams cad ya mtshan du gyur/ de nas
bzung ste phyogs dus kun du bkra shis pa'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ba yin no zhes slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo'i gsung rab ba ri ba'i rnam thar las bshad do/ /gzhan
yang mgon po'i bka' babs bzhi'i nang tshan gyi sku'i

bka' babs rdo mgon yid bzhin gyi nor bu yang bla ma 'di nyid kyis rje sa chen la gnang ba yin no/ /de nas bla ma sa chen la gdan sa gtad de yun mi ring ba na ba ri lo tsA ba
bar phug tu sku gshegs so/ /de nas bla mas grom pa g.yu rtse 'byid phur/ me lhang tsher la rnam nges/ rigs thig brgya 'grel bam po bco lnga pa dang / dbu ma rang rgyud
shar gsum du grags pa gsan zhing khongs su chud par mdzad do/ /de nas bla ma gnam kha'u pa'i drung du byon nas/ bya ba'i rgyud la rig pa mchog gi rgyud legs par grub pa/
dpung pa bzang po/ phyag rdor dbang bskur ba'i rgyud/ gsang ba spyi rgyud/ bsam gtan phyi ma/ dam tshig gsum bkod pa la sogs pa'i rgyud/ de'i 'grel pa yan lag dang bcas pa/
spyod rgyud la rnam snang mngon byang rgyud 'grel pa phran dang bcas pa/ rnal 'byor gyi rgyud de nyid 'dus pa/ de'i 'grel pa de nyid snang ba/ ko sa la'i rgyan/ dpal mchog
dang po'i rgyud/ de'i 'grel pa stong phrag nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ rdo rje rtse mo/ khams gsum rnam rgyal/ mgon po kun snang / ngan song sbyong rgyud/ thams cad gsang
ba rgyud 'grel dang bcas pa/ yang de nyid 'dus pa'i don 'grel a wa ta ra/ bsnyen sgrub kyi gzhung rdo rje 'byung ba/ khams gsum rnam rgyal/ gtsug dgu la sogs pa gzhung phra
mo du ma dang bcas pa dang / rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud la slob dpon 'phags pa yab sras kyi dgongs 'grel sgron gsal/ rim lnga mdo bsre dang / ArYa de wa'i spyod bsdus/
bdag byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa/ sems kyi sgrib sbyong / klu'i bshes gnyen

gyi sgrub thabs kyi rnam gzhag dkyil chog nyi shu pa/ zla grags kyi rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs kun bzang 'grel pa
gsum dang bcas pa/ don 'grel dza yanta dang / tha ka na dang / snyim pa'i me tog che chung gnyis/ dkyil chog bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa rtsa 'grel/ mi bskyod rdo rje bya ba'i
sgrub thabs bstan pa'i nor rjas/ de'i 'grel pa bsod snyoms pas mdzad pa che ba/ de'i don bsdus ka hi ka zhes bya ba dang / sgeg pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i 'jam dpal gyi 'grel
pa bar par grags pa dang / de'i rgyud zla gsang dpal gyis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa/ rnam rtog bde ba zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa/ 'grel pa gong ma de dag gi yan lag gi phra mo
rnams kyang gsan no/ /mtshan nyid kyi phyogs la mngon rtogs rgyan ma gtogs pa'i byams pa'i chos bzhi/ bslab btus/ spyod 'jug mdo kun las btus dang / spyod phyogs phra mo
mang du gsan te thugs su chud par mdzad do/ /de nas bgres po rnams bgros te/ da pha chos shig rtsad gcod par 'thad par 'dug pa las/ pu hrang pa gsal snying mkhas te ni gshegs/
de'i slob ma 'khon sgyi chu ba dgra lha 'bar mkhas kyang zer/ gdung rus kyang gcig pas khong can byon pa drag zer nas byon pas/ dbang bskur zhus pas sta gon gyis nub
mo mnal lam du srid pa'i rgya mtsho yin zer ba'i chu bo chen po dmar mer ba cig la zam pa gsum 'dug pa'i chu 'gram na bsgral rgyu'i mi mang po 'dug pas/ nga sgrol bar
zhu nga sgrol bar zhu zer nas de la bsgral

bas/ zam pa phyi ma la mi gsum/ bar pa la bdun/ nye shos la mang po cig bsgral ba rmis/ cung zad bsnyel te nyi ma gcig la bsnyel gso ba snyam byed tsa na mnal sad nas/ nang
par sgyi chu bas bla ma 'di la rmi lam dris pa na 'di ltar byung zhus pas/ bla ma sgyi chu ba'i zhal nas/ khyod kyi 'khos kyis mi gsum las ga la sgrol nus zhes zhal kyal
yang gsungs zhes grags so/ /de nas sngar yab la gsan pa'i kye rdo rje'i rgyud rgyas pa gsum/ 'grel pa ku mu ti yan lag phra mo man ngag dang bcas pa/ bram ze nag po'i srol
gyi dges rdor/ rnal 'byor sbyor phreng zhes bya ba'i 'grel pa yan lag du ma dang bcas pa/ snying po'i skor gyi grub pa sde bco brgyad/ grub pa'i khongs su gtogs pa dang
snying po'i skor phra mo nyi shu rtsa lnga yan lag dang bcas pa shin tu zab pa'i man ngag gis brgyan pa dang / bla ma 'brog mi'i bshad srol gyi mahA mA yA 'grel pa gnyis
yan lag dang bcas pa dang / zla gsang thig le dang sangs rgyas thod pa 'grel pa yan lag dang bcas pa dang / mar pa lo tsA ba'i bshad srol gyi gur brtag gdan bzhi/ mahA
mA ya rgyud rkyang pa dang bzhi'i bshad pa man ngag dang bcas pa/ bla ma mnga' ris pa'i bshad srol/ rang rgyud shar gsum/ bslab btus/ spyod 'jug dang bcas pa rnams gsan zhing
khong du chud par mdzad do/ /de'i dus su khong la grwa pa brgyad cu tsam yod pa'i nang nas/ sa chen 'di nyid kyis lung dang rig pa phyin ci ma log par mkhyen pa dang
/ 'jam dpal gyis rjes su bzung ba'i stobs kyis chos gsan pa kun tshar re la mkhyen te/ bla ma

sgyi chu ba yang rje 'di la thugs gtsigs che skad do/ /de tsa na mdog stod du chos 'khor cig la bla ma se byon zer ba thos pas/ bla chen de ltad mo la sogs pa la mi dges kyang
bla ma se bzang po yin pa dang / chos dbar yin pas sgyi chu ba'i slob ma ban chung 'ga' dang 'grogs te der byon pas/ bla ma se gral mgo na bzhugs 'ad 'ud mang po gsung
gin 'dug pa dang mjal ba na/ bla ma se mkhar chung pa'i rje'i grogs po tsho la re re nas jo sras nyid yul gang yin/ yon tan ci shes/ bshad pa mno 'am/ bsgrub pa bya mno
gsungs shing / de nas bla chen la jo sras khyed gang nas yin gsungs pas/ bla ma 'di'i bdag grom phug pha gi ba cig lags zhus pas/ /de'i yab gang na yod gsungs pa la/ sa
skya na bdog byas pas/ se ston gyi zhal nas 'o na de na nga'i bla ma cig yod pa yin te sku ni gshegs yod par 'dug nga la khral 'dod pa cig kyang ma byung / da ni ba ri ba
yam bya ba cig gis bzung 'dug zer ba thos pas 'gro snying yang ma 'dod/ da de'i shul na ji ltar yod gsungs pas/ rje 'dis de'i bu'i dod cig ka bdag cag lags byas pas/ bla
ma na re/ jo sras kyi brdzun ma zer/ nga'i bla ma la sras mi mnga' ba yin gsungs pa dang / rdo rje phyug mo la med pas bla chen gyis lan 'debs ma nus pa la/ grogs kun gyis
rgyu mtshan bshad de/ rdo rje phyug mo la med kyang logs su zhang mo bya ba la 'di ltar byon pa lags byas pas/ bla ma'i zhal nas mi gson shi mi 'phrad zer te 'phrad pa'i
dus byung gsungs nas/ bla chen

pang du bzhes spyan chab phyung nas rgad po gog po 'di'i nang na chos yod pas khyod la ster ba yin pas myur du shog ga le yong snyam na sang phod nga ni 'chi ba yin gsungs
nas bla chen gyis der zhag gcig bzhugs/ de'i bar la bla ma ses lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa 'di la dkyus su bshad pa 'di tsam zhig yod/ de la 'phros dang gegs sel la sogs pa
'di ltar yod kyi rkang grangs lam me ba cig gsungs/ de nas yar byon nas mkhar chung du bzhud dgongs te khres po tshun chod grab yod tsa na/ khong gi grwa rogs ston pa rdo
rje 'od dang / zhang btsun ra tsa bya ba gnyis na re/ bla ma 'dis grwa pa 'di tsam gyi nang nas khyod kho na la thugs la 'dogs par 'dug spyir yang gsang sngags pa bya ba
gang yang bla ma la zhu dgos pa yin pas/ bla ma la zhus la song zer bas bden snyam nas sgyi chu ba la zhus pas/ bla ma'i zhal nas khyod ci la 'gro gsungs/ gdams ngag cig
zhu ba lags byas pa la/ khyod tshod ma chung / de ni se lce la re bya ba yin gdams ngag ci yang med/ nga'i bla ma mnga' ris pa'i chos kyi gral grul 'dra bsgrugs nas 'chad
pa yin gsungs nas 'gror ma gnang / der bla mas ma gnang bar 'gro ba'i cha ma yin te/ 'on kyang sang phod 'gro snyam tsa na se gsungs pa bden te sku 'das pa dang / thugs
'gyod de bya thabs ni med/ de nas dus ring zhig na bla ma sgyi chu ba sa skyar gdan drangs nas chos 'khor bya dgongs te/ nas khal sum brgya tsam dang / gzhan yang cha rkyen
mang du bsgrubs/ slob ma 'ga' yang bsdus nas yod tsa na/ bla ma sgyi chu ba bsnyungs pas bla

chen la shog gsungs pa byung nas byon pas sgyi chu ba gshegs nas ma mjal ba dang / bla mas khyod rab tu byung la 'khon tsho'i sde 'di skyong gsungs pa'i gsung bzhag pa'i zhal
chems de bzhin du sgyi chu ba'i gdan sa bla chen la gtad/ de'i rjes kyi bya ba rnams tshar nas sa skyar byon te/ bla ma'i gsung bsgrub pa'i ched du rab tu byung dgongs
nas na bza' ser chas bsgrubs pas/ bla ma gnam kha'u pas gsan te shog gsungs byon pas/ khyod ser chas bsgrubs nas ci byed gsungs/ rab tu byung ba lags byas pas ma byed gsungs/
bla ma sgyi chu ba'i gsung yin zhus pas/ bla ma mnyam po la khong gshin po'i kha chems pas/ nga gson po'i ngag la nyon/ rab tu ma byung ba bstan pa dang sems can la
phan che ba cig yong gsungs nas ma gnang / rab tu byung ba ma gnang yang 'khon tsho'i dpon ni mdzad de/ /de nas bla chen 'di'i bla ma sgyi chu ba de bla ma mal gyi slob
ma yin pas sgyi chu ba'i bde mchog gi phyag dpe rnams bsnams nas gung thang na la rtse gnas gsar du byon te/ bla ma mal la bde mchog rtsa ba dang bshad pa'i rgyud/ rdo rje
mkha' 'gro/ /a bhi dha na/ he ru ka mngon 'byung / kun spyod/ sambu Ta/ rnal 'byor ma bzhi kha sbyor/ mkha' 'gro ma mngon 'byung / rdo rje mkha' 'gro dang kun spyod gnyis
kyi 'grel pa lo hi pa'i yan lag phra mo dang bcas pa/ dril bu yan lag dang bcas pa/ nag po chos drug nA ro mkha' spyod/ rtsa dbu ma'i man ngag phra mo dang bcas pa dang
/ gshin rje gshed nag po rgyud gsum 'grel pa dang bcas pa

dang / rgyud kyi bshad pa lugs gnyis man ngag phra mo dang bcas pa dang / nA ro ta pa'i gur dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'grel pa gsum yan lag dang bcas pa rnams dang / jo
bo rin chen bzang po nas brgyud pa'i bde mchog rtsa rgyud/ slob dpon ko ka na rgyal ba bzang po'i skor/ 'grel pa gsum/ dkyil chog sgrub thabs bstod pa dang bcas pa dang /
jo bo rje las brgyud pa'i bde mchog rtsa rgyud/ 'grel pa/ sgrub thabs kyi gleng gzhi dang bcas pa dang / a bhi dha na la sogs pa'i yan lag rnams dang / mi g.yo ba dang /
phyag na rdo rje la sogs pa dang / sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs yan lag du ma dang bcas pa dang / yang bde mchog sdom 'byung / kha che rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs
yan lag du ma dang bcas pa dang / dbu ma rigs tshogs dang / mdo kun las btus dang / bstod pa'i tshogs rnams kyi rtsa ba dang 'grel pa phra mo rnams kyang gsan nas khongs
su chud par mdzad do/ /de'i tshe bla mas chos rnams tshar re la mkhyen pa dang / mal gyis thugs su ma tshud pa'i tshul mdzad de/ la las ni mi tshe phyid pa'i chos la la
las tshar res shes su re ba gsungs nas bkyon skad/ lan cig bla chen 'di med par mal lo dpon slob tshos rtog bdun gyi sngags shig thu yin 'dug pa dang / slob ma tshos ma shes
ba la/ bla chen gyis der byon nas de la tshegs med 'di ltar byas na mchi byas pas bla ma kyag gis bzhengs nas/ shes na dga' ba tshos mi shes/ ma shes na dga' ba tshos
shes 'dug gsungs nas gshegs song ba dang / der bla ma 'di

thugs cung zad steng gin logs shig na bsam mno byed cing bzhugs tsa na/ yang khong tsho 'tshogs nas sngags thu yin yod pa dang / lhag pas shog bu khyer ba bla chen gyi gam
du byung nas/ de khyer te 'di na gda' zhus pas/ de rten 'brel bzang chos kyis phan thogs pa yong ba yin gsungs nas bla ma mal mnyes/ de nas sa chen mar 'byon khar bla ma
na re/ nga'i chos 'di nges par sangs rgya ba'i chos yin pas/ mi nyid kyis rigs kyi dbang bskur re byed zer nas ra tshang cig tu phub go gcig gi steng du padma 'dab brgyad
cig byas/ blu gu cig gi ske la bal cig dkris byed pa'i nyen yod do/ /de 'dra ma byed gsungs pas/ bla ma'i chos la de 'dra ga nas byed byas te mar byon/ g.yas ru na mar dbang
bskur sems bskyed 'dra mdzad pas/ gser srang bcu bdun 'bul ba la byung ste/ de rnams sngags pa cig la bskur nas bla ma la 'bul du btang bas/ bla ma ston mo byed pa cig
gi gral mgo na bzhugs pa la/ sa skya nas 'ong ba cig gis mjal bar zhu yin gda'o byas te zhus pas/ za 'dod 'dra yin nam byin gsungs nas ma mjal/ yar lon mar lon mang ba
cig byas nas/ sa skya nas 'ong ba'i 'bul ba cig bdog pas mjal byas pas/ 'phral thugs col chung 'dra ba cig yod pas khong rang byon nas/ 'bul ba ci yod gsungs gser cig bdog
zhus pas zho du yod gsungs/ srang bcu bdun tsam bdog byas pas mnyes nas khong rang gi khug ma nas kyang srang gang bton nas 'di yang de'i steng du bsnon la srang bco brgyad
yod

gyis la tshogs su phul gsungs/ de ltar byas pas khong dam tshig pa bsam gyis mi khyab par 'dug pa la/ ngas de ltar cung ma go da nga'i gam du kho da lo lan cig cis kyang shog
chos kyi lhag ma da rung yod pas khyod la ster ba yin gyis shig gsungs/ der bande des mar 'ongs nas bla ma la 'phrin byas/ bla chen gyis kyang yar byon te sbyong rgyud
dang / rab gnas kyi rgyud yan lag bdun pa dang bcas pa dang / rdo rje sems dpa'i sgrub thabs che chung / yan lag brgyad pa la sogs pa sman dpyad kyi gzhung dang / khyad
par du mgon po'i sgrub thabs rjes gnang dang bcas pa gnang nas/ de'i rten du dar nag dang lcags kyi rdo rje rtse dgu pa cig dang bcas te/ mahA kA la'i sku'i bka' babs bzhi'i
nang nas mchog tu gyur pa mgon po'i 'chams sku bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes la mi la mis zer ba ltar da nga rgas pas khyod mi dgos/ khyod rang 'khon sa skya pa'i rjes la
song la sa skya pa brgyud pa dang bcas pa'i bka' bzhin sgrubs shig zer nas brdzangs/ de rnams bsnams nas mar byon/ lho stod du pu hrang lo chung la bal po bha danta'i lugs
kyi bde mchog skor dang / ha du'i dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i arghaM la sogs pa'i chos skor gsum dang / dus kyi 'khor lo yan lag dang bcas pa dang / bya rgyud kyi phyogs
'ga' gsan nas thugs su chud par mdzad cing / bram ze mchog sred kyi pur sol la rang 'byon du 'khrungs pa'i shing mgon yid bzhin gyi nor bu 'di yang lo tsA ba 'dis bla ma
chen po la gnang ba yin no/ /gzhan yang mdo khams nas 'bri khung pa'i skyu ra

a skyabs bya ba de sa skyar gdan drangs nas/ gsang 'dus 'phags pa yab sras kyi dgongs pa lha rdo rje snying po zhes bya ba'i lugs dang / sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyi brgyud
pa sman pa'i zhabs zhes bya ba'i skor la/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi zhal lung dang / ye shes zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i lung dang mthun pa'i chos bcu bdun dang / rgyud kyi 'grel
pa rin po che'i ljon shing dang / zhal lung dang / mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa'i dkyil chog rnams la/ sman pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa re re dang / slob dpon
de nyid kyi dgongs pa dngos grub 'byung ba'i gter zhes bya ba rnams gsan nas thugs su chud par mdzad do/ /rdo rje gdan pa la bha wa pa'i 'grel pa yan lag dang bcas pa
dang / mahA mA yA'i 'grel pa lugs gnyis yan lag dang bcas pa dang / rdo rje bdud rtsi'i rgyud dang 'grel pa yan lag dang bcas pa dang / sems 'dzin brgyad bcu pa zhes bya
ba rnams gsan no/ /bal po paNDi ta padma shrI la/ mtshan brjod/ dus 'khor dang / man ngag du ma gsan no/ /bal po dznyA na badzra la rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i chos du ma gsan
no/ /rgya gar gyi rnal 'byor pa bha dra rA hu la la man ngag du ma nos so/ /dge bshes rngog ces bya ba la sher phyin jo bo'i lugs/ nyi khri snang ba rtsa 'grel/ brgyad
stong rtsa 'grel/ mngon rtogs rgyan rtsa 'grel/ sdud pa rtsa 'grel/ brgyad stong don bsdus rtsa 'grel/ shAnti pa'i gzhung lugs tshan cig rnams gsan nas thugs su chud par
mdzad do/ /gnyis pa khyad par gsung

ngag nod pa'i tshul ni/ de nas gsung ngag mnyan par bzhed de/ se'i slob ma su drag dris pas/ 'ga' zhig zha ma drag zer/ rgyus ma rnams na re/ de la gdams ngag rdzogs pa med
pas zhang ston mched gnyis drag de'ang gcung po ni grongs/ gcen po bzhugs pas de mkhas zer/ der bzhud par dgongs nas bla ma gnam la 'gro bar zhus pas/ sgom chen 'di brdzun
che ba yin/ gdams pa ci yang med de mchi/ dad pa yod na gsang 'dus kyi sgrub thabs bstan pa'i nor rdzas bsgom gsungs nas ma gnang ba la/ bdag la yid ches gcig bdog zhus
pas/ 'o na rgyug gsungs nas byon/ sag thang du phebs pa dang / thags mkhan tsho gcig 'dug pa la zhang dgon pa ba la mjal gyis dang byas pas/ pha ki ka yin zer nas bltas
pas/ mi mang po cig gi gseb na sham thabs shig gsol/ sha 'gag med par ra thul cig phyir klog tu gyon nas yo ga byed cing gtam chal chol mang po gsung gin 'dug pa dang /
der drung du phyin nas phyag byas pas khyed ni ga shed kyi mi chen cig 'dra na/ de nas kyang gsar ma pa cig 'dra na nor ba ma yin nam gsungs pa la/ ma nor lags gsung ngag
rin po che zhu ba lags byas te khrab cig phyag rten du phul bas/ bla ma zhang gi zhal nas/ da ci ru nor byas te ngas de 'dra mi shes/ de'i ming yang da res las ma thos/
ngas rdzogs chen tsa mun ti dang bram ze'i skor 'dra bshad pa yin/ de kun nyan pa la khyed gsar ma ba bya ba rtog pa che bas rtog pa mi byed dam gsungs/ bskyar nas zhus pas
kyang de 'dra'i gdams ngag

med gsungs pa dang / bla chen gyi dgongs pa la 'o na spyod lam gyi lugs 'di dang byas pas gdams ngag med pa 'dra/ nga rang nor ba yin nam snyam nas log pa dang / jo sras 'od
mchog gi pha des bla ma zhang la 'o skol rang mkhar chung na yod tsa na/ sgyi chu ba'i grwa ba cig la nga'i bla ma'i sras po yin nas pang du len pa de 'dra na ldog pas
cang mchi'am zhus pas/ 'o na dam tshig nyes par 'gro nyen yod pas bos gsungs nas ldog ste lo rgyus zhib tu mdzad pas/ sa skya pa'i sras yin par thugs yid ches nas/ ngas da
ci ngo ma shes par brdzun byas/ man ngag yod de sngar ma bshad pas bsam mno 'dra bya dgos/ spyir yang da lta dor ka mdo bya ba 'di na se ston rdor 'byung gis paN chen dang
paN chung dang / lo paN dpon slob mang po la chos 'khor byed pa'i rtsar/ rnal 'byor pa rgan po cig gis bshad nyan byas kyang mi mdzes pas/ dpyid so byon chos tsho tshar
ba bgyid gsungs/ phyis sa chen gyi zhal nas/ 'od mchog gi pha 'di nged la drin che/ rta brgya phul ba bas dga' gsungs/ de nas dpyid ka byon te slebs pa'i nub mo chos kyi
gleng gleng mang du mdzad pas/ rje bla ma nyid rgyud gsum thugs la shin tu byang bar bzhugs pas lan btab pas/ bla ma zhang gis 'or che shin tu go chod nas 'dug gsungs
nas mnyes skad/ yang rje'i zhal nas/ rgyud las rtsa sum cu rtsa gnyis gsungs pa 'di kun sgrub pa po'i lam du khyer na ci tshugs byed gsungs nas/ gdams ngag gi gnad 'drir
byung ba la lan ma thebs nas/ gdams ngag

zab mo yod par 'dug dgongs nas shin tu thugs ches gsungs/ de nas dbang dang gdams ngag zhus te sngon 'gro'i khrid tshar nas/ nang par nas gsung ngag gsungs pa'i nub mo rje'i
ljags skrangs te bsnyungs nas chos gsungs pa ma byung bas/ rje'i zhal nas 'o skol gnyis kyi bar na dam tshig gi nyes pa cig yod par 'dug pas maNDal phul/ yi ge brgya pa
grongs shig gsungs pa dang / bla chen gyi thugs dgongs la gzhan yong ba med/ kha sing gdams ngag med pa yin nam snyam pa cig byung ba des yin nam snyam ste/ de la dmigs
nas maNDal phul/ yi ge brgya pa mang du bgrangs pas phan gsungs/ man ngag kyang khong gis gnang ba la/ jo mos khong la gdams ngag myur du byin mdzod byas pas khong thugs
zab pas/ ci zer gdams ngag zab mo la khyi dang glo ba 'phrad pa bzhin ci thod thod du gtong ngam gsungs nas rim gyis gnang / der dbyar dgun bzhi lhag tsam bzhugs te gdams
ngag zhus pas/ bla ma dkon mchog rgyal po bla ma se'i slob dpon yin pas brgyud pa'i dam tshig dgongs nas gsung ngag rin po che ma lus par gnang / mdor na lam skor dgu/ phra
mo nyi shu rtsa lnga/ de re re la yang yan lag du ma dang bcas pa dang / gsung ngag gi rgyab rten kye rdo rje rgyud rkyang gi bshad pa shin tu zab pa'i lugs dang / gsang
'dus rtsa rgyud/ mnyam sbyor rtsa rgyud/ kye rdo rje'i rtsa rgyud/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud/ gdan bzhi rtsa rgyud/ mahA mA yA dang / mtshan brjod shin tu zab pa'i bshad srol
rnams kyang gsan nas thugs su chud par mdzad do/ /

gdams ngag rdzogs te sgrub pa lung sbyin pa'i dus su/ lo bco brgyad kyi bar du chos 'di gzhan la lung sbyin pa dang ston pa lta zhog 'di 'dra yod pa dang shes pa'i ming tsam
yang ma 'don/ yi ger yang ma 'bri/ de nas gzhan la 'chad dam/ yi ger 'bri'am gang byed kyang khyed rang chos kyi bdag po yin gsungs nas bka' rgyas btab/ spyir khyed kyis
sgrub pa gtso bor byas na tshe 'di nyid la phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob/ nyan bshad byas na gdul bya dpag tu med pa'i don du 'gyur zhing / khyad par du lus
ma spangs par phyag rgya chen po mchog grub pa gsum/ bzod pa thob pa bdun/ rtogs pa dang ldan pa brgyad cu tsam 'byung zhes lung bstan no/ /der bla mas lo bco brgyad du
bsnyel gyis dogs pas zla ba re la gsung ngag ma lus pa bshad pa'i bsam mno tshar re/ nyin zhag re la rdo rje'i tshig rkang drug gam bdun 'don pa'i dam bca' mdzad nas byon/
de ltar bla chen gyi sku tshe'i stod yan chad du bka' rgya ma tshang ba'i stobs kyis yi ge med pas gsung ngag rin po che 'di snyan brgyud 'ba' zhig tu bzhugs pa yin no/
/de nas bka' rgya lo bco brgyad thim pa dang / bla ma a seng gis lam 'bras khungs chod nas/ nyid la gsung ngag rin po che mnga' ba gda' ba la sngar yod kyang mi gsung
pa 'dug da res tshar gcig gsungs pa dang yi ge zhib pa cig kyang mdzad pa zhu zhus pas/ der bka' rgya thim pa dang khong gis zhus pa 'dzom pas/ bla mas rten 'brel bsgrigs
pa yin dgongs nas bla ma a seng la tshar gcig

gsungs/ lam 'bras don bsdus ma de mdzad nas gnang / de nas rim gyis zhu ba po so so'i ngor/ sga theng ma/ zhu byas ma/ klog skya ma la sogs pa 'grel ba bcu gcig tsam mdzad
pa las/ dge bshes snyags kyi ngor mdzad pa 'di tshig nyung don rgyas sdeb legs par dgongs nas ding sang gi bar du 'di phyag dpe mdzad do/ /de dag gi bar skabs kyi gsal byed
yi ge la/ kun gzhi rgyu rgyud/ gdan sogs lus dkyil/ 'chi ltas brtag pa 'chi bslu dang bcas pa/ 'da' kha ma'i gdams ngag thig le'i rnal 'byor/ phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid/
yi ges sgo dgag pa'i man ngag bar do bzhi/ lam dus kyi dbang / tshad ma bzhi/ gdams ngag drug rten 'brel lnga/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin sreg grib ma khrus kyis sel ba/
tsha tshas sel ba/ thig le bsrung ba/ yig brgya 'don thabs/ rlung sbyor bdun gyi lam khrid pa/ bha ga'i yi ge bcu bzhi/ 'khor bzhi'i rgya/ sa bcu gsum pa'i sa phyed kyi
mngon rtogs/ don bsdus pa'i tshigs bcad rnams dang / de rnams kyi 'phros la 'khor 'das dbyer med rtsa 'grel gnyis/ dbang bzhi'i cho ga'i gnad/ mchog dbang gsum gyi yi ge
phyi bskyed rim gyi gdams ngag bdud rtsi ril bu'i sgrub thabs/ 'phrang bdun bsal ba'i man ngag byung rgyal du mi gtong ba'i gnad bzhi/ 'byung ba lus 'khrugs rlung dang spyod
lam gyis bsal ba/ phrin las so gnyis/ lam 'bring po/ lam bsdus pa/ gzhung ji lta ba bzhin du bkri ba/ gnad drug gis bkri ba/ gnad bcu gcig gis bkri ba/ dbang po

rab 'bring gsum gyis bkri ba/ lam 'jug ldog phyag rgya 'jug ldog shes pas phan 'dogs pa'i man ngag bdun/ lam sra ba 'gros dang bcas pa/ phyi nang gi mdzad pa bcu gnyis/ bla
ma'i rnal 'byor/ bla ma bod kyi lo rgyus/ rgya gar ba'i lo rgyus/ birWa pa'i glu dang bcas pa/ de thams cad kyi dkar chag lam skor gzhan gyi gdams ngag la/ tog tse pa'i
bsam mi khyab la man ngag lnga/ mtsho skyes kyi rnam thar/ mtsho skyes kyi zab pa'i tshul dgu/ Dombi pa'i man ngag la/ man ngag tshan pa bzhi/ nag po pa'i gtum mo lam rdzogs/
ngag dbang grags pa'i yi ge med pa/ klu sgrub kyi mchod rten drung thob/ yon po bsrang ba'i man ngag indra bhU ti'i man ngag rnams te/ de ltar gsung ngag rin po che
lam skor phyi ma dang bcas pa'i gsal byed kyi yi ge de rnams sa chen nyid kyi gsung kho nar ma nges kyang / bla ma chen po yab sras kyis mdzad pa'i lam 'bras sogs man ngag
phyogs kyi bstan bcos zab mo rnams brjod bde ba'i phyir phyogs gcig tu bkod pa yin la/ dpal brtse ba chen po rang nyid kyis bstan pa'i rgyun la dgongs pa'i legs bshad gsar
du mdzad pa ni/ rgyud sde spyi'i rnam gzhag brtag gnyis kyi bsdus don/ brtag gnyis kyi dka' 'grel/ gur gyi tho yig zer ba'i rgyud kyi don bsdus/ klu'i bshad pa/ rtsa'i
mngon rtogs/ gur gyi bshad pa'i chings/ rdo rje snying 'grel gyi yig sna/ sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi don 'grel/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi le 'grel/ rtsa rgyud kyi sa bcad/
bde mchog nag po

pa'i dkyil chog gi tho yig ras bris la brten pa'i dkyil chog gsang ba'i de kho na nyid kyi don gyi cha gsungs bzhin bris pa/ de'i sa bcad/ o la pa ti'i don bsdus/ bde mchog
gi rnal 'byor pa'i ro sreg pa'i cho ga o la pa ti dang dpyid thig gi man ngag o la pa ti'i 'grel pa/ de'i sa bcad/ gsang ba'i de kho na nyid kyi tshig don bsdus pa'i go
'byed/ 'jigs byed rtogs bdun gyi TIka sgrol ma bcu bdun ma'i dkyil chog man ngag gces bsdus/ bha ya na'i srung 'khor/ bla ma skyu ra a skyabs la zhu yig bum gter gzhug tshul
gyi man ngag sgrub thabs mtsho skyes kyi sa bcad/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi TI ka mu tig gi phreng ba/ bde mchog lU yi pa'i mngon rtogs kyi TI ka la sogs pa mdzad de/
bla ma nyid kyis mdzad pa'i bstan bcos rnams ni yi ge'i 'jog gtsang ba/ phal cher dbu na mchod brjod dang / mjug na bsngo ba dang mdzad pa po'i mtshan la sogs pa smos pa'o/
/yang bla chen 'dis mchan dang 'khor lo'i dpe bris mdzad pa la kye rdor rgyud gsum/ nag 'jigs skor gsum gyi rgyud/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro /a bhi dha na'i 'grel pa ku mu ta'i
mchan dang / bde mchog nyung ngu / sampu Ta/ tshogs bdag 'dod rgyal rnams kyi dpe bris mdzad do/ /gnyis pa rtogs pa'i yon tan ni/ sdom pa gsum dang 'gal ba'i nyes pa phra
zhing phra bas kyang ma gos shing / byams pa dang thugs rjes rgyud brlan pa/ dngos po gang la'ang mi chags la dad pa dang sgrub pa'i sgo nas bla ma rnams mnyes par mdzad
de/ nang du rten 'brel thams cad bsgrigs

pas yi dam lha'i zhal gzigs pa dang / chos thams cad la mnga' brnyes pa dang mngon shes dang rdzu 'phrul la sogs pa la thogs pa mi mnga' ba yin no/ /de yang gong du bshad pa
ltar 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyis dngos su rjes su bzung ba'i skabs der 'phags pa mi g.yo ba dang / rje btsun ma sgrol ma gnyis kyis kyang zhal gzigs shing bar chad bsal ba dang
/ gzhan yang mahA lo tsA ba sku gshegs nas gung thang du byon nas bsnyung ba'i tshe/ zo mo tsi tsis sman drangs gdams ngag byin pas sku khams gdangs/ de nas g.yas ru'i
grong chung dgon par byon pas dug ro langs nas zla ba gnyis tsam bsnyung bas/ chos thams cad brjed nas gcig kyang med par song ste/ grogs gcig la dri sa yang med/ rgya
gar du phyin yang rgya gar na yang ji 'dra yod cha med snyam nas thugs ma bde ste/ sa skyar byon nas brang khang rnying par sku mtshams bcad nas/ bla ma dkon mchog la gsol
ba btab pas tshul 'ga' re dran pa byung / de nas rje dgon pa ba mnal lam du byon nas chos gsungs pas ma lus pa dran pa byung / slar yang dges spro dang bcas gsol ba drag
tu btab pas/ skabs shig tho rangs ka rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa zhabs skyil krung phyag chos 'khor gyi phyag rgya mdzad pa/ g.yas su shar phyogs nag po pa zhabs skyil
krung / g.yas ba men gyi rwa dung / g.yon thod pa bdud rtsis gang ba 'dzin pa/ g.yon du ga ya dha ra na bza' dkar po lding gon mdzad nas rdor dril thugs kar bsnol ba/
rgyab tu ko Ta li pa pus mo btsugs nas gdugs

'dzin pa/ mdun du bi na sa ste nags khrod pa thal mo sbyar nas bdud rtsi 'bul ba ste/ gtso 'khor lnga sa dkar po rgyab yol du mdzad/ ya gi mon grog nas ma gi 'bal grog gi bar
skyil krung gis khyab par mdzad nas/ 'di rnams thams cad nga dbang gsungs shing dngos su byon nas zhal bstan pas/ thugs la rnam par mi rtog pa'i ting nge 'dzin bsam gyis
mi khyab pa 'khrungs shing / ting nge 'dzin de las bzhengs nas a la la ste zhes sogs kyi bstod pa yang mdzad/ de nas zla ba gcig gi bar du 'tsho ba zur nas blangs shing
sku mtshams bsdams nas gtso 'khor ci rigs par byon zhing / bla med kyi rgyud sde bdun cu rtsa gnyis sam/ /bla med dang 'brel ba'i dbang byin rlabs sogs kyi chos sna bdun
cu rtsa gnyis/ khyad par du lcags ri phyir mi 'da' ba'i zab chos bzhi la sogs pa gsan cing thugs su chud pa dang / yang dge bshes snyag gis bzang rgyud 'brog pa'i gseb
tu byon tsa na/ mgrin pa yan chad thig les brtan pa'i rtags shar ba cig mthong nas/ su'i slob ma yin dris pas/ bla chen gyi tshar khar bzhugs tsa na khrid lo gsum bskyangs
pa'i slob ma yin zer/ bgres po kun la bla chen tshar khar nam byon dris pas/ gung thang yan chad du byon pa ye med zer te/ de lta bu'i sku'i bkod pa bstan nas sgom chen
sum cu tsam re la khrid skyong ba dang / sa skyar bzhugs nas lam 'bras gsungs shing bla ma gong ma'i dgongs pa rdzogs thabs mdzad pa dang / gung thang du mal gyi nye gnas
mdzad nas dril bu pa'i chos skor zhus pa dang / 'bring mtshams su mgron la lcam

lha khang du 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' dri med kyi dkyil 'khor bzhengs nas rab gnas mdzad pa/ zangs sdong 'brog pa'i gseb tu gsung ngag gsungs pa/ shab sgo lngar chos 'khor bskor
ba rnams lo zla tshes grangs gcig par 'dug pa la/ phyis sku gshegs nas slob ma rnams gsung gleng mdzad pa ma gtogs sus kyang rtogs pa mi 'dug pas/ de ni dus gcig la sku'i
bkod pa drug bstan pa yin par grags so/ /yang mthu rtsal gyi sgo nas bstan dgra gdug pa can rnams tshar bcad pa'i tshul ni/ bdud sprul sngags nag bla chen stag tsha
dang / bon nag re ba 'dzu gu zhes bya ba gnyis kyis bstan 'dzin rnams la shin tu phrag dog pa'i sgo nas/ brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po nyid la yang bar chad mtho 'tshams
byed snyam ste/ stag tsha'i slob ma khams kyi ldan ma nas 'ong ba'i ming rdor rgyal zer ba cig gser gyis slad nas bla chen bkrong du btang bas/ khams pa des kyang khas
blangs nas sa skyar 'ong ba'i tshe/ brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying po de sgo rum gzims spyil dkar por bzhugs yod pa la/ khams pa des mjal kha zhus pa na de 'phral sku
gzhogs su gnang ba'i tshe/ khams pa na re/ bdag skyes sa khams kyi ldan ma yin/ zhing stod kyi phyogs su phyin nas lo du ma song / de nas bla chen khyed kyi snyan pa thos
nas dad pa chen pos mjal du 'ong ba lags/ da re zhig khyed kyi zhabs drung du bsdad chog par zhu ba la de bzhin du gnang zhing / gzhan yang 'phral du khams pa des gus
gus ltar gyi thabs ci 'dra zhig byas nas bkrong ba drag

gam snyam du sems pa'i tshe/ bla chen nyid kyis mkhyen bzhin pa'i ngang nas nyin gcig gi tshe/ bla chen nyid kyi skyu bem gyi nang du rje btsun sku mched rnams dang yab sras
lhan cig tu bzhugs pa na/ de nyid khams pas mthong ba'i tshe 'jig rten phal pa lta bu'i pha bu sdod lugs 'di 'dra dang bcas bla ma lta ci/ chos pa tsam du yang mi 'dug
snyam log lta cher skyes pa'i tshe/ de nyid bla ma chen pos ye shes kyi gzigs pas legs par dgongs te/ khams pa la zhabs drung du shog gsungs nas/ khyod la rnam rtog ngan
pa med mchis sam zhes gsungs pas/ khams pa nyid shin tu skrag ste tsab tsob tu gyur pa na/ bla chen gyi zhal nas gsang sngags pa'i rdo rje slob dpon la log lta byed pa shin
tu 'khrul pa yin gsungs nas/ zhabs gnyis shad kyis rkyong par mdzad pa'i zhabs mthil g.yas g.yon la kye rdo rje dang 'khor lo bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor bris pa las kyang
gsal ba gnyis khams pa la bstan pas/ rdor rgyal nyid shin tu 'gyod par gyur te sngar byas rnams bshags pa dang / phyin chad bla chen gyi ched du lus ngag yid gsum gtong
ba'i dam bca' phul/ de nas khams pa des bla chen stag tsha'i drung du phyin te/ sa chen bkrongs grub pa lta bu'i tshul smras pas/ bla chen stag tshas de nyid bden par bsam
ste mgo bo 'khor te rdor rgyal la nye gnas bcol zhing / nged kyi mal sa dang phreng ba 'di la tho reg med cing shin tu gtsang ba rang dus rgyun du bya dgos so zer ba sogs
kyi bslab bya mang du byas pa la khams pas bsams bzhin du mal sa yang yang du bshig bcos byed pa dang / phreng

ba'i mdud pa bkrol te spyod lam du 'dor ba sogs mi mtshungs pa sna tshogs byas shing / de bzhin du bon nag la yang byas pas/ khong gnyis kyi ngan sngags kyi tshogs rnams shin
tu 'khrugs par gyur to/ /de nas de'i skabs der nus mthu'i mnga' bdag bla chen kun dga' snying po de nyid kyis chos skyong mthu rtsal can rnams bran du bkol te/ drag po
mngon spyod kyi las la bskul ba'i tshe/ sngags bon gnyis 'dug pa'i gnas der sngar nas med pa'i g.yag rgod rog po gnyis rwa brdar la sogs pa drag po'i spyod pa zil dang ldan
pa du ma byed pa zhig byung zhing / gzhan yang bya nag khyi nag ce spyang sogs chos skyong gi sprul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'ang de'i dus byung zhes grags la/ de dang
dus mtshungs par dam tshig ldan pa'i khams pa rdor rgyal des/ sngags nag dang bon nag gnyis kyi slob 'khor rnams phyogs gzhan du byer ba'i thabs byas nas/ de nas khong rang
gcig pus zhag bcu phrag gsum gyi bar du sngags bon gnyis kyi zhabs tog la ches cher brtson par ltar byas nas/ zhag sum cu lon pa nyer dgu'i nub/ bla ma dang bstan pa'i
ched du sngags nag dang bon nag gnyis srog bral gyi cho ga yang dag pa la sbyar nas/ khong gnyis kyi phung po gnyis chos skyong gi sprul pa'i g.yag rgod la bkal te gdan
sar 'ong bas/ mtshan lam gcig la nyin lam drug chod ces grags shing / de nas khams pas bla chen gyi drung du phung po gnyis phul bas shin tu dges shing bya dga' chen po
gnang zhing / khyad par tshe gcig lus gcig la sangs rgya nges pa'i

gdams pa'i nying khu rnams gnang ste/ rdor rgyal gyis kyang khams su phyin te bsgoms pas grub rtags chen po phyogs med du ston pa'i rnal 'byor pa bar dor phyag chen mchog gi
dngos grub thob nges pa zhig byung bar grags so/ /de nas bla chen gyis sngags nag gi snying phyung ste hom khung gi nang mdze thod kha sbyor gyi nang du bcug nas bse mgon
chen po'i zhal gdong du 'jog par mdzad de/ mngon spyod kyi 'phrin las ci bsam 'grub pa'i bka' bsgo mdzad pa yin la/ dus phyis bstan pa'i nyi ma sngags 'chang chos kyi
rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyis kyang bse 'bag gi zhal gdong gi hom khung kha phye nas mdze thod kyi nang gi snying la nyams pa'i dgra bo lha gnas gnyis sogs la
dmigs pa'i dgug gzhug lha dbye bden bdar sogs mdzad pas/ dam nyams rnams gtan brlag tu thod pa 'di bzhin byung ba yin zhes bdag gi bla ma 'jam dbyangs sku mched kyi gsung
las yang yang du thos shing / da dung yang sa skya pa'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa la gnod pa'i bstan dgra mi bsrun pa dag la shin tu myur ba'i las sbyor dgos
pa byung ba'i tshe bsam pa rnam par dag pas kun nas bslangs te bla ma gong ma de rnams kyi phyag len ltar bgyis na rtags mtshan 'byung ba la the tshom mi dgos sam snyam
du kho bo sems so/ /sngags nag gi phung po bying sgo rum mgon khang gi them 'og tu bla chen nyid kyis mnan pa mdzad pa bzhin da lta yang dbu rtse'i bskor lam nas phung
po'i snod kyi rkyal pa kun gyis mthong sar yod do/ /bon nag re ba 'dzu gu'i phung po ni chos khri thang mo che'i

nub sgo'i 'khris kyi chu 'gram na mchod rten gyi tshul du mnan pa mdzad pa yin pas/ 'di la ched gtad kyi bskor ba mi bya zhing / gal te byed kyang mgon po'i rtsa sngags dang
bzlog bsad kyi sngags rnams bzla zhing bskor ba g.yon skor du bya ba yin par gsungs so/ /'dir skabs kyi rje sa chen gyi dngos slob khams pa rdor rgyal dang / bde gshegs
khams pa rdor rgyal gnyis ming zur 'dra yang ngo bo mi gcig ste/ phag gru'i mtshan la rdo rje rgyal mtshan zhes bya zhing / 'di'i ming la rdo rje rgyal po zhes zer ro/ /de
lta bu'i sngags nag dang bon nag gi lo rgyus 'di rnams ni sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i gsung rgyun yin zhes sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyi
bka' phebs ji ltar gnang ba bzhin 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched gnyis ka'i gsung las thos pa dang / lhag par 'jam dbyangs bsod nams dbang pos sa skya'i gnas bshad gsung
rtsom gnang 'phro thor bur yod pa rnams las ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin la/ gzhan yang bla ma de nyid kyis rdzu 'phrul bstan pa'i tshul ni/ skabs shig tu khams pa
cig gis khyed spyan ras gzigs yin pa'i rtags mngon sum du mi ston na kho bo 'di nyid du 'gum mo zhes gri snying gar btsugs pas/ de btsugs mi dgos 'di la ltos gsungs nas
phyag mthil nas spyan bstan pa sogs mtha' yas so/ /de lta bu'i bla ma chen po de nyid la slob ma'i mchog ji ltar byung snyam na/ kun gyi mchog ni slob dpon dpal ldan rtse
mo zhabs te chos dang rigs kyi sras su gyur

pa/ sa dang po gzhon nu'i sa la bzhugs shing sku'i bkod pa gnyis kyi sgo nas bde ba can du gshegs pa de yin la/ gzhan yang rje dgon pa bas lung bstan pa dang / sgyi chu ba
la dbang zhus pa'i sta gon gyi mnal lam dang mthun par tshe 'di nyid la phyag rgya chen po 'grub pa gsum ni/ singga la'i gling nas a tsa ra gcig byang chub sems dpa' stag
sgom pa skyi 'bar ba dang gsum mo/ /bzod pa thob pa bdun ni/ rje btsun rin po che/ zhu byas/ dga' ston rdo rje grags/ nags sgom bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ tshar kha'i rnal
'byor pa/ sgom pa 'od grags/ mang chung ma'o/ /gzhan yang mkhas pa dang / nus pa dang ldan pa dang / ting nge 'dzin mchog dang ldan pa ku sa li'i tshul du sbas te bzhugs
pa dpag tu med pa byung ngo / 'di dag gi rnam thar rgyas pa ni kho bos byas pa'i gsung ngag gi chos 'byung chen mo legs bshad 'dus pa'i rgya mtsho sogs su blta bar bya zhing
/ gzhan yang gzhung bshad gces par 'dzin pa'i thugs sras bcu gcig tshig rkang rnam par 'grel pa'i thugs sras bdun/ phyogs kyi mkhas grub chen po bzhi sogs byung ba yin
te/ zhu byas kyis bsdebs pa'i bstod pa las/ zab don yongs su rdzogs pa'i slob ma ni/ pho brgyad mo gsum dag la yi ger gdams/ /zhes pa ltar/ khams pa a seng / lho pa zhu
byas/ klog skya jo sras chos grags/ thugs sras gnyan phul chung ba/ gtsug tor rgyal po/ mtshan dngos bsod nams rdo rje/ spyan ras gzigs kyi rnam sprul byang sems zla ba
rgyal mtshan/ zangs ri phug

pa/ khams pa sga theng / snyag bzhi dar ma dbang phyug rgyal mtshan te pho brgyad/ rang sras kun dga' 'bar gyi yum jo lcam phur mo/ /g.ya' lung gi jo mo 'a 'u ma/ mang mkhar
gyi jo mo mang chung ma ste mo gsum/ rnam 'grel bcu gcig ces grags pa ni gang zag 'di bcu gcig la gdams pa yin gyis gzhan du yid g.yo bar ma byed cig gnyis pa ni gzhung
bshad mdzad pa'i dngos slob sna ro bande/ stong sgom byang chub shes rab/ mi nyag pradznyA dzwa la/ zhu brag dmar ba/ 'u yug gi g.yar sbu ba/ phag mo grub pa'o/ /phyogs
kyi mkhas grub bzhi ni/ la stod pa dkon mchog mkhar/ khams pa rgwa lo/ ne tshe sbal ston/ gshen rdo rje bzang po dang bzhi rnams so/ /yang bla chen de nyid las slob ma 'phel
tshul rnams gzhan gyis rtogs sla ba'i phyir tshigs bcad du bsdebs pa ni/ rje sa chen gyi bstod pa zhu byas kyis mdzad pa'i kha skong paN chen mi nyag grags rdor gyis
mdzad pa las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ gdul bya mtha' dag smin par mdzad pa la/ /zhang dgon sgyi chu ba yi lung bstan ltar/ /tshe 'dir phyag chen thob pa rnam pa gsum/ /singga
gling gi rnal 'byor byang sems stag /sgom pa skyi 'bar gsum du gsal bar grags/ /bzod pa thob pa bdun du grags pa ni/ /rje btsun chen po zhus byas dngos grub dang / /nags
sgom bsod rgyal tshar kha'i rnal 'byor pa/ /sgom pa 'od grags dga' ston mang chung ma/ /gzhon nu'i sa la gnas pa'i slob ma ni/ /mkha' spyod dbang po bsod nams rtse mor grags/
/gzhan yang bdag nyid

che de'i slob ma ni/ /brtul zhugs grub pa dpal chen rgwa lo'i zhabs/ /byang chub sems dpa' zla ba rgyal mtshan dang / /dpal ldan phag mo grub pa chen po dang / /sgom pa rta
rgan rnal 'byor phag ston sogs/ /grub pa brnyes pa'i skyes chen du ma dang / /rta nag 'khrungs pa'i rgyal tsha tal phug pa/ /'u yug 'khrungs pa'i dbyar ston sbu ma ba/ /g.yor
ston byon pa'i gshen ston rdor seng dang / /yar lung 'khrungs pa'i gshen ston dgon dkar ba/ /'on du byon pa'i zhang ston gsum thog pa/ /brag dmar zhu dang zhang ston
spe'i dmar pa/ /skyu ra a skyabs de sras a seng dang / /gnam du byon pa'i ne tshe sbal ston dang / /lha brag dkar ston lcags kyi rdo rje dang / /gsang phu'i mkhas pa mdzangs
ston mdza' ne dang / /thugs sras dam pa bsod nams gnyan phul chung bar grags pa rdo rje dang / /snyag ston dbang rgyal rgya sgom tshul khrims grags/ /mi nyag ston pa
pradznyA dzwa la dang / khams pa sga theng 'a 'u ma la sogs/ /rmi lam na yang 'dod la ma chags shing / /rgyud sde'i snying po rim gnyis lhur len pa'i/ /mkhas grub dam pa
mu mtha' 'brel pa yis/ /rgya mtsho'i gos can dpal dang ldan par byas/ /rgwa lo'i slob ma g.yu brag pa la sogs/ /zla rgyal slob ma nyin phug pa la sogs/ /phag gru'i slob
ma 'bri stag gling gsum sogs/ /rgyal tsha'i slob ma ri ma lce bsgom sogs/ /a seng slob ma phyag gtsang nyang ran sogs/ /rje pa'i slob ma sa skya paN chen dang / /grags pa'i
mtha' can brgyad la sogs pa ste/ /shar phyogs rgya mtsho'i mtha' klas dam pa rnams/ /

thugs rje che ldan de yi slob rgyud lags/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /de lta bu'i bla ma chen po 'di nyid kyis dgung lo nyi shu nas drug cu rtsa bdun gyi bar gdan sa lo zhe brgyad
bzung nas/ sa pho stag gi lo tha skar gyi zla ba'i dkar phyogs kyi tshes bcu bzhi'i tshe dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs kyis bsus te g.yas ru skya bo kha gdong
du zhi bar gshegs la/ de'i tshe skye bo thams cad kyi mthun snang du grub par rol mo dang dri zhim pa'i tshogs dang / 'ja' tshon gyi 'od kyis gang bar byas shing / sku'i
bkod pa bzhir bstan te/ gcig ni bde ba can/ gnyis pa ni po ta la/ gsum pa ni o rgyan/ bzhi pa ni byang phyogs kyi 'jig rten gyi khams gser mdog can du gshegs par spyan snga
