che'i phreng ba'i blo gsal zhing yid gzhungs pa'i ded dpon dga' ba bskyed pa'i phyir dang / chos rje nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor gyis skye dgu rnams kyi mi shes pa'i mun pa bsal
ba'i phyir dang / rta mchog 'gro ba'i tshe na shes/ /glang chen g.yul ngor shes 'gyur te/ /gser dngul bzhu na shes par 'gyur/ /mkhas pa legs bshad brtsams na shes/ /zhes
pa ltar rang nyid kyi thugs kyi rnam par thar pa rmad du byung ba yang bstan pa'i phyir du dri ma med pa'i bstan bcos du ma mdzad pa yin no/ /'di la gnyis las/ spyir bstan
bcos mdzad pa'i rnam grangs ni/ 'jig rten gyi chos lugs bzang po ston pa'i thabs kyis dam pa'i chos kyi lam ston pa/ legs par bshad pa rin po che'i gter zhes bya ba
phyi nang gi slob dpon rnams kyis bstan bcos

mtha' dag gi don bsdus pa dang / sgra'i bstan bcos mkhas pa 'jug pa'i sgo dang / shes rab 'phro ba dang / shes rab la 'jug pa dang / sgra nyer bsdu zhes bya ba bzhi dang /
tshad ma'i bstan bcos sde bdun gyi snying po rig pa'i gter 'grel pa dang bcas pa dang / bzo'i bstan bcos/ sku gzugs kyi bstan bcos dang / sa brtag pa dang / bstan pa rin
po che'i rtsis dang / sman dpyad kyi bstan bcos yan lag brgyad pa'i bsdus don dang / nang rig pa la gsung rab spyi'i don gsal bar byed pa la sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa'
la zhu ba'i 'phrin yig grub mtha' rnam 'byed dang / pha rol phyin pa'i gzhung lugs spyi'i tshogs chos chen mo dang / gsang sngags la rje btsun pas mdzad pa'i bdag med
ma'i bstod pa'i 'grel pa/ rdo rje theg pa'i man ngag rten 'brel lnga'i yi ge lam sbas bshad dang bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ khrid kyi dkar chag la sogs pa du ma dang / rig pa'i
gnas chung bar grags pa la/ sdeb sbyor me tog gi chun po dang / de'i ngal gso'i dpe tsam ston pa bde bar gshegs pa'i thugs rje la bskul ba dang / snyan ngag mkhas pa'i
kha rgyan dang / mngon brjod tshig gi gter dang / zlos gar rab dga'i 'jug pa dang / de'i rol mo dbyangs 'dren pa'i phyogs tsam ston pa rol mo'i bstan bcos dang / gzhan de
dus na chos rje nyid gangs can gyi khrod na lung rigs man ngag thams cad la the tshom za ba thams cad kyis 'dri ba'i gnas yin pas/ zhang lo/ chag lo/ glo bo lo tsA ba gsum
la sogs bsngags pa dang / dge slong rdo rje seng ge sogs bka'

gdams pa dang / snye mo sgom chen pa sogs sgom chen pa mang pos zhus pa'i lan mdzad pa mang po dang / thub pa dang 'jam dbyangs sogs la bstod pa la sogs pa mang po mdzad do/
/de lta bu'i rtsom pa rnams kyang 'bad rtsol la mi ltos par 'byung ba dang / tshig nyung ngus kyang don rgya chen po ston pa dang / blun pos bltas na go sla bas don gsal
ba dang / tshig gi rgyan bzang pos mkhas pa rnams yid 'phrog par byed pa dang / mkhas par rlom pa brgya'i blo gros phyogs gcig tu bsdoms pas kyang dpyod par mi nus pa'i
don zab mo ston pa yin te/ 'phags pas/ rtsom pa 'di 'dra myur 'jug pa/ /glog 'gyu bas kyang ches myur zhing / /rtsol ba med par 'byung ba ni/ /mtsho ltar ngang gis lhun
grub lags/ /de don phun sum tshogs gyur pa/ /rlom chen blo yi dbang po mchog /'gas kyang sngon chad ma dpyad pa/ /dpyod ldan gang gis rnam dpyad pa/ /yid gsal bgyid pa gangs
ri'i rtser/ /nyi ma shar ba lta bu ste/ /kun nas dga' ba bskyed pa ni/ /bsam gtan ro myong lta bur mchis/ /zhes pa ltar ro/ /'on kyang bdag nyid chen po 'dis byis pa
bde blag tu 'jug pa dang / bstod pa rgyud gsum 'khor lo'i 'grel pa sogs 'ga' zhig las gzhan gyis byas pa'i bstan bcos dang / rgyud kyi 'grel pa tshig re re nas 'byed pa ni
ma mdzad cing / 'jam dbyangs/ rnam 'joms bir lugs/ khro bo dme brtsegs sgrub thabs nyung ngu cung zad ma gtogs dkyil 'khor chen po'i sgrub thabs dang / de'i cho ga sogs
rgya cher ma

mdzad pa ni/ rje btsun gong ma rdo rje 'chang dang gnyis su ma mchis pa'i gzhung lugs rnams mi nyams pa'i phyir kho na yin no/ /gsung rab de dag gi rnam grangs mdo tsam zhig
gong du brjod zin yang 'dir zhib tu brjod na/ sgra'i phyogs la shes rab 'phro ba/ sgra la 'jug pa/ smra sgo'i bsdus don/ byis pa bde 'jug gi 'grel pa/ yi ge'i sbyor ba/
sgra nye bar bsdu ba rnams mdzad la/ tshad ma la rig pa'i gter rtsa 'grel/ snyan ngag la mkhas pa'i kha rgyan bde bar gshegs pa'i thugs rje la bskul ba mdzad/ sdeb sbyor
la sdeb sbyor me tog gi chun po/ mngon brjod la tshig gi gter/ zlos gar la rab dga'i 'jug pa dang rol mo'i bstan bcos/ bzo rig pa la sku gzugs kyi bstan bcos dang sa brtag
pa'i rab byed/ gso ba rig pa la yan lag brgyad pa'i don bsdus/ nang rig pa la bstod pa'i skor la/ sangs rgyas kyi bstod pa/ thub pa'i bstod pa/ spyan ras gzigs kyi bstod
pa gnyis/ 'jam dbyangs kyi phyag mtshan ri mo la bstod pa/ bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i gnas chen la bstod pa/ 'jam dbyangs kyi bstod pa'i rnam bshad rnams mdzad/ theg
pa thun mong la/ grub mtha'i rnam 'byed/ thub pa dgongs gsal/ sdom gsum rab dbye/ sems bskyed chen mo lung sbyor dang bcas pa/ chos nyams su blang ba'i rim pa/ chos spyod
bcu pa/ zhen pa bzhi bral/ theg pa chen po'i lam gyi rnam gzhag mdor bsdus pa/ bsngo ba'i yon bshad rnams mdzad/ gzhung lugs spyi la mkho ba mkhas pa 'jug pa'i sgo/ gzhung
lugs legs dpyad/ lugs

kyi bstan bcos la legs bshad/ thor bu ba la 'phrog byed dga' bo pham par byas pa'i tshigs bcad/ ba go ra zhes bya ba'i sgra las drangs pa'i tshigs bcad/ blo gsal ba'i skyes
bu rnams la ji ltar dri ba'i tshigs bcad/ bdag nyid kyi rnam thar nga brgyad ma rtsa 'grel rnams mdzad/ 'phrin yig dang zhus lan gyi skor la/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dang
byang chub sems dpa' la zhu ba'i 'phrin yig skyes bu dam pa rnams la springs yig bstan pa la dga' ba'i lha rnams la springs yig shing kun na bzhugs pa'i dge 'dun rnams
la springs yig nyi ma la springs yig glo bo lo tsA ba la springs yig zhang lo tsA ba la gdams pa/ 'od 'jo ba'i dge bshes la springs yig snye mo sgom chen la springs yig
do gor ba'i zhus lan/ chag lo tsA ba'i zhus lan rnams mdzad/ theg pa thun mong ma yin pa'i skor la/ 'jam dpal gyi sgrub thabs kyi gsal byed/ sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs/ gza'
yum gyi mchod pa'i cho ga zhi ba 'tsho las brgyud pa'i gza' yum gyi sgrub thabs/ zung 'jug gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga snang ba mtha' yas kyi bsgom don/ 'chi kha ma'i
gdams ngag rnams mdzad/ bla med kyi skor la/ bla ma'i bstod pa gnyis/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi bstod pa/ bde mchog brgyud pa'i bstod pa/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor chen mo/ phyi
nang gsang gsum gyi maNDal/ lam 'bras kyi khrid kyi dkar chag sgrub pa lung sbyin/ rten 'brel lngas lam yongs su rdzogs pa/ lam sbas bshad rtsa ba yan lag dang bcas

pa/ grub chen bcu phra mo brgyad dang bcas pa/ aShTa'i gzhi bshad/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo'i yi ge bdag med ma'i bstod pa'i 'grel pa/ rigs drug gi mtshan don dang ye shes bsre
ba'i bshad pa/ bde mchog lhan skyes kyi byin rlabs/ rnam 'joms bir lugs kyi bshad pa/ sampu Ta/ rdo rje rnam 'joms kyi rgyud/ sdom gsum rab dbye la sogs pa dri ma med pa'i
bstan bcos mang du mdzad de bstan pa gsal bar mdzad pa yin no/ /gsum pa rtsod pa rdo rje'i shugs kyis lta ngan gyi brag ri bshig pa'i tshul ni/ 'di nyid rigs pa'i dbang
phyug gam chen por gyur par grags pa'i 'od dkar rgya mtsho'i mthas klas pa'i sa'i dkyil 'khor kun tu 'phro bar gyur pa na thub pa chen po ser skya dang / drang srong rgyas
pa dang / gzegs zan la sogs pa'i rjes su 'brangs pa'i grangs can dang / rig byed dang / rigs pa can pa zhes grags shing dbang phyug dang / tshangs pa dang / nyin mo long
pa dang / nor lha'i bu dang / byin za la sogs pa cher mgu ba dang / lho phyogs kyi rgyud du rgyu zhing rnam par 'phyan pa 'phrog byed dga' bo la sogs pa'i phyi rol pa'i
ston pa drug gis dam bcas pa/ kho bo cag kha ba can gyi ljongs su song la/ de na gnas pa'i skye bo gau ta ma'i dge slong du khas 'che ba/ bud med kyi brtul zhugs 'dzin
cing lta ba dang spyod pa ngan pa la zhen pa de bzlog par bya'o zhes gleng ste mthar song pa dang / bdag cag gi bla ma rgol ba ngan pa'i khyu mchog gi spyi gtsug rnam par
gnon pa'i seng ge 'di byang chub kyi snying po rdo rje gdan las byang phyogs su dpag tshad bcu phrag drug

bgrod pa/ mang yul skyid grong 'phags pa wa ti'i gtsug lag khang dang 'dab 'byor ba'i tshong 'dus na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ sngar smos pa'i ston pa drug po der lhag pa na chos rje
nyid dang / bde bar gshegs pa'i rten la phyag mi 'tshal bar/ bde legs dang bsngags par 'os pa'i tshigs su bcad pa re re tsam brjod nas gral la 'khod pa na 'di skad smras
te/ nged kyi rigs thams cad ni bla ma tshangs pa nas brtsams te deng sang gi bar du gau ta ma'i bstan pa la mi ltos/ dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro ma myong bas drang
srong gi rigs rnam par dag pa kho bo cag yin no zhes dregs shing smra bar byed do/ /de'i dus chos kyi rje 'dis gsungs pa ni/ ci tshangs pa ni ston pa la shin tu gus pa
yin na/ 'on kyang de gti mug che bas gnyid kyis non pa min nam/ ji skad du/ rab mchog lag pa bzhi pa bcu drug phyed phyed phyogs kyi gdong pa can/ /bzlas dang nges pa'i
cho ga shes shing nges brjod rig byed 'don pa po/ /dri med padma'i skye gnas tshangs pa de yang gnyid log gyur/ /zhes dang / kho bo'i ston pa stobs bcu mnga' ba de ni rtag
tu rab tu snga ba nyid du nam langs pa'o zhes gsungs pas/ de dag shin tu ma bzod cing ma rangs pas 'bel ba'i gtam gyi skabs rnyed de/ rgol ba ngan pa de thams cad re re
nas sun phyung zhing pham par mdzad de mi smra ba'i brtul zhugs la bkod nas/ slar yang de thams cad kyi lta ba ngan pa'i snyems pa'i dri ma med par mdzad de/ ral pa'i khur
dregs nas nyid kyi thad du rab tu byung ste/ nges par 'byung ba rin po

che'i 'byor pa dang ldan par mdzad pa'i skabs su/ /shAkya'i rgyal po de'i bstan pa la rma 'byin pa gang dag byung ba na/ slar yang de bzhin du gdul bar bya'o snyam du dgongs
nas 'di gsungs pa/ rgya mtsho'i gos can rgya mtsho'i mthas klas sa chen 'di na lha chen po/ /'phrog byed bran byed de dag lhar byed thub pa drang srong karka sogs/ /rgyas
pa grog mkhar ba dang gzegs zan rkang mig ser skya'i rjes 'jug pa/ /thor gtsug shing shun lo ma'i gos can thal ba dbyug gu ku sha thogs/ /ral pa'i khur 'dzin munydzas
legs dkris ri dwags g.yang gzhi'i stod g.yogs can/ /so ris gsum mtshan rtse mo can mchod tshangs skud mchod phyir thogs pa 'chang / /rig byed kun sbyangs nges brjod 'don
mkhas sgra dang sdeb sbyor mthar son pa/ /bdag tu lta ba'i lta ba la lta rgyun du dka' spyod nga rgyal can/ /de lta'i tshul can mu stegs glang chen rab tu myos pa'i klad
'gems pa/ /dpal ldan smra ba'i seng ge blo gros stobs ldan rigs pa'i mche ba can/ brda sprod byed gzhung yan lag rab rdzogs bde gshegs bstan pa'i ral pas brjid/ /legs sbyar
nga ro gtan tshigs gad rgyangs rtag brjod sun 'byin mig bgrad pa/ /de lta'i ri dwags rgyal po de/ /dpal ldan sa skya'i gangs rir gnas/ /blo gsal rnams kyi ri dwags skyong
/ rgol ba ngan pa'i wa tshogs 'joms/ /da dung du yang mu stegs byed/ /thams cad chos kyis pham byas nas/ /bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa'i tshul/ /kun dga'i rgyal mtshan
'dzin par shog /ces gsungs te/ de dag gi ral pa dpal ldan sa skya'i dbu

rtse rnying ma na da lta yang yod do/ /des na bod kyi paNDi tas phyi rol mu stegs kyi rgol ba bzlog pa ni chos rje 'di kho nar zad do/ /gnyis pa 'phrin las sna tshogs pas gzhan
gyi don mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ spyir ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par thar pa bsam gyis mi khyab mod/ phyogs tsam zhig brjod na/bdag nyid chen po 'dis dgung lo bco brgyad bzhes
pa'i dus/ dpal ldan sa skya'i a phyi'i 'bum pa'i drung du/ sangs rgyas gnyis pa slob dpon dbyig gnyen yin zer ba'i paNDi ta sngo sangs sku sha ha cang zhum pa ma yin pa
zhig bzhugs pa la chos mngon pa mdzod zla ba gcig gi bar du gsan pa rmis shing / mnal sad pa na mdzod kyi tshig don ma lus pa thugs su chud de/ phyis kha che paN chen la
gsan dus sngar las khyad par che ba ma byung gsungs so/ /de ltar slob dpon dbyig gnyen dang chos rje sa skya paNDi ta nas rim pa bzhin du brgyud pa'i bshad srol yang 'jam
pa'i dbyangs shes rab rgya mtshos gsan no zhes de nyid kyi gsan yig las 'byung ngo / /gzhan yang mnal lam ngo mtshar can ni/ kha che paN chen bod du ma byon pa na/ de nyid
kyis chos zab mo rdo rje'i glu ru len pa gsan pa rmis te/ mnal sad pa na tshig don ma brjed par snang zhing / phyis de bod du byon dus don de nyid zhus pas/ de nub kho
bo la'ang rmi lam de lta bu byung zhes gsungs par grags la/ de ltar yang / chos kyi ma mo ma bslabs thugs su chud/ /gzhon nu'i dus na yon tan thams cad rdzogs/ mkhas pa
du ma'i tshogs kyi dbus na bstod/ /blo ldan khyod la spyi bos phyag

'tshal lo/ /zhes pa dang / srid pa kun tu legs par sbyangs pa'i phyir/ /mnal lam du yang chos kyi sgo rnams kun/ /dge ba'i bshes kyis mngon sum gdams par mdzad/ /rnam dag khyod
la spyi bos phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes so/ /gzhan yang nub cig bdag nyid chen po la khyed slob dpon chen po dpal phyogs kyi glang po'i gdan sar bsko bas gshegs par zhu zer
zhing / phyogs kyi glang po'i ri phug yin zer ba'i brag bug sgo glegs dang bcas pa/ ngos rnams la glegs bam mang po yod pa zhig gi lde mig gtad pa rmis te/ de nas tshad
ma'i bstan bcos rnams 'bad mi dgos par mkhyen no zhes gsungs pa dang / yang skyid grong du byon tshe nub gcig mnal lam du de'i jo bo la/ dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad
kyi/ /mkhyen brtse gcig tu bsdus pa'i dngos/ /de mtshan thugs rje che zhes bgyi/ /spyan ras gzigs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes sogs bstod pa mdzad pa la/ mnal sad pa na tshigs
su bcad pa dang po bzhi las/ gzhan rnams ni mi dran gsungs so/ /yang skabs shig gi tshe mnal lam du tshogs chen po zhig la tshad ma rnam 'grel gyi mchod brjod saM skri
ta'i skad du gsungs pas/ phrag gong gnyis nas nyi zla dus gcig la shar te song ba rmis pa na/ de nyid rje btsun chen po la zhus pas/ de lta bu thub par dka' gsungs nas tshogs
pa lnga stong tsam la mang ja bskol zhes thos so/ /yang dpal bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang du chos 'khor la btsad pos spyan drangs nas chos 'khor mdzad
pa na/ rgyud kyi brtag pa phyi ma'i le'u lnga pa yan

song / lam 'bras phal cher song nas srin po ri pas dge 'dun gyi ston mo mdzad pa'i tshogs dpon la spyan 'dren du byung nas nang par 'byon pa'i do nub dmigs pa dang / byin rlabs
dang / bka' bgros zhu ba mang po zhig gis thugs g.yengs nas tho rangs bar du mnal rgyu ma byung / de nas cung zad mnal ba na mi skya shar ba tshan cig byung nas phyag
dang phyag rten phul te/ chos rje pa sems can thams cad skye rga na 'chi'i chu bo chen po 'dis shin tu nyam thag par mi gda' lags sam zer ba la/ de tsug 'dug gsungs pas/
de las thar pa'i gsol 'debs gcig zhu zer ba la/ skye ba skye ba med pa'i don rtogs kyang / /da dung skye ba'i 'dam las grol ma gyur/ /skye ba kun tu skye bor skye 'gyur
ba'i/ /skye ngan bdag gi skye ba'i skyabs mdzod cig /gyis la gsol ba thob gsungs pas/ rgas pa la sogs pa gzhan gsum la'ang de sbyar du rung ngam zer ba la/ rung zhes gsungs
pa la/ phyag btsal nas bka' drin che'o zhes zer nas song pa rmi zhing / mnal sad pa na de gtsug lag khang gi bka' srung rgyal po yin pa 'dug snyam du dgongs so zhes zer
ba thos so/ /gzhan yang rgyud yongs su dag pa'i gdul bya 'ga' zhig la rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid kyi sku dngos su bstan nas don mdzad do zhes 'byung ste/ bo dong
rin po che brtson 'grus rdo rjes de lta bur gzigs so zhes bstod pa byed pas kyang / bsam pa dag pa'i gdul bya 'ga' zhig gis/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs su mig gis mthong gyur cing
/ /'phags pa'i yul na'ang

gtam du de ltar grags/ /zhes gsungs so/ /yang gtsang nags phug pa 'jam dbyangs shes rab 'od zer gyi rnam thar las kyang / khong gi rmi lam zin nas nam mkhar 'phur nas shar
phyogs su phyin pas/ rgya'i ri bo rtse lnga yin zer ba'i spang ri bzang po shin tu yid du 'ong ba cig gi steng na gnas gzhi bzang po lta bu'i khang bzang cig snang / rje
btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi pho brang yin snyam nas mtha' mar bskor zhing gsol ba btab pas yun ring du sgo ma rnyed/ mthar shar phyogs nas sgo gcig phye nas nang du phyin
par snang nas gtsug lag khang shin tu bzang ba cig 'dug de'i dbus na rin po che'i khri chen po gcig gi steng na bla ma chos rje sa skya pa zhal byang du bstan nas bzhugs
'dug 'di nyid rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs nyid yin snyam nas phyag dang bskor ba mang du byas shing gsol ba btab pas/ gsung ni ma byon/ dar gyi na bza' mang po zhig gis
dril ba'i glegs bam gcig gnang nas bltas pas gser gyi mtshan brjod cig 'dug pa rmis/ de nas yun ring du nyin par stong nyid kyi don la blo gros 'jug pa dang / mtshan mo rmi
lam bzang po mang du byung zhes dris te ngo mtshar ba'i rnam 'phrul lo/ /gzhan yang chos kyi rje dbus su chos 'khor cig la gdan drangs nas bzhugs pa dang / nye ba'i lho
rong cig na dge bshes g.yag sde bsod nams bzang po zhes bya ba sgrub pa mdzad kyin yod pas/ srod kyi cha la rang gis yi dam kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs mthong
ba'i rjes su ci yin ma shes nas tho rangs snga mor langs nas chos rje la zhu ru yong ba dang / srod la

chos rje gtor ma mdzad pa'i drung du slebs nas phyag 'tshal ba'i rjes thogs su chos rje'i zhal snga nas dge bshes yong ngam gsungs/ mchis lags zhus pas ci la yong gsungs/ zhu
rgyu cig bdog ces smras pas/ mdang gi de ma yin nam/ rgyal po dpe dkar kho cho 'phrul cig ston gyin 'dug pa yin te/ da nga dang 'phrad pas btub par yong / 'on kyang na
tsha drag po cig yong dogs yod ces gsungs pa la de lo g.yag sde pa la bsnyung gzhi drag po 'grongs la khad pa cig byung nas de dngas pa tshun chad/ sgrub pa 'phel zhing
bsod nams chen po byung ba la brten te/ g.yag sde ba na re/ de man chad chos rje sangs rgyas dngos yin snyam pa'i mi phyed pa'i dad pa yod ces gsungs par grags shing / dngos
slob gzhan dag la yang 'di ni nges par 'jam dbyangs nyid do zhes shin tu thugs ches par snang ba yin no zhes bya ba gnyan stod 'dul ba seng ges bsgrigs pa'i gsung ngag
gi rnam par thar pa las 'byung ngo / /gzhan yang dbu ma pa shes rab 'bum gyis gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras zhus te bsgoms pas khams 'dus byung nas chos rje pa'i drung
du phyin te/ khams 'dus 'di lta bu byung bas gegs sel gnang dgos zhes zhus pas/ gzhan ci yang mi gsung bar shes rab yod na khams 'dus rgyu med ces gsungs/ de nas de ka'i
don la zhib tu bsam pas ting nge 'dzin gyi mchog rgyud la skyes so zhes kyang rnam thar las 'byung ste gzhan don mdzad pa'i rnam par thar pa phul du byung ba'o/ /gzhan
yang lam 'bras nas

bshad pa'i rgyas pa'i 'chi ltas ni gang zag 'ga' tsam la mi 'byung zhing / byung ba'i tshe na ni dus nges pa can yin no zhes bshad la/ shar pa shes rab 'byung gnas la de lta
bu'i ltas byung ba'i tshe/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'ba' zhig thugs dam du mdzad cing gsol ba btab pas rgyas pa'i 'chi ltas las kyang grol te/ /yun ring du bzhugs so zhes kyang
rnam thar las gsungs so/ /gzhan yang 'di nyid gang na bzhugs pa'i sa phyogs su 'byung po'i gdon gyis byas pa'i rims nad dang / phyi nang gi 'khrug long dang lo nyes la
sogs pa mi 'byung zhing / rgya lam zhig na byung na yang nyid kyi mthus myur du zhi ba dang / spyod yul gyi 'gro ba rnams kyang phan tshun byams pa'i sems dang ldan pa
yin no/ /des na 'di nyid ji srid bzhugs pa de srid du yul 'dir hor la sogs pa pha rol gyi dmag dang / nang gi 'khrug pa la sogs pa gtan nas ma byung ngo / /rgyas pa'i 'phrin
las kyang chos dang 'jig rten gyi dpal 'byor phun sum tshogs pa grangs med pa zhig byung ste/ bshad sgrub kyi bstan pa'i pad tshal shin tu rgyas par gyur nas/ mkhas pa
dang grub pa'i yon tan brnyes pa'i slob ma'i tshogs grangs med pa bskrun zhing / rang dang dus mtshungs pa'i mkhas pa'i skye bo ches che ba dag gis kyang zhabs kyi padmo
spyi bo'i gtsug tu gus pas blangs te mchod par byas so zhes thos te/ dper na/ de dus kyi 'chad nyan smar zhing mkhas par grags pa smyal zhig 'jam pa'i rdo rje dpon slob
rnams yin pa las/ chos rje pa'i snyan grags shin tu ma bzod nas/ bu dgu'i rig pa bzang shos 'u yug pa

rig pa'i seng ge yin pa chos rje la rtsod du btang nas chos rar zhag shas bsdad nas 'gal du bsgugs pas ma rnyed cing / rtsod par cung zad kyang ma nus kyi steng nas mi phyed
pa'i dad pa thob ste zhabs pad yun ring du bsten pas bu chen du gyur pa lta bu'o/ /slob ma'i mchog ji ltar byung pa'i rnam grangs ni mdo tsam 'og nas kyang 'chad par 'gyur
la/ zhib tu ni rnam thar rgyas pa logs su 'byung ba rnams las shes par bya'o/ /yang dbus kyi phyogs su bsam yas kyi btsan po shAkya mgon gyis gdan drangs te byon pa'i
dus su yang / chos 'khor de nyid kyi 'khor sa bar ma la 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi phyag mtshan ri mo dang / sngon gyi chos rgyal byang chub sems dpa' rnams la bsngags pa'i
tshigs su bcad pa mdzad cing chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor nas/ slar yang tshigs su bcad pa mdzad pa dang / de la ched du brjod pa chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa ni/
sgra dang tshad ma'i mig gnyis dang ldan pas/ /shes bya'i dkyil 'khor blta ba'i blo gros can/ /mang du thos shing legs par sbyangs pa po/ /skad gnyis smra ba dpal ldan sa
skya pas/ /nam mkha'i mtha' dang mnyam pa'i sems can rnams/ /kun mkhyen rgyal po'i go 'phang thob phyir dang / /'gro ba'i bla ma de dag mnyes bya'i phyir/ /dam chos dkon
mchog sgron ma gsal bar bshad/ /'gro ba'i bla ma yon tan rin chen gter/ /phyogs rnams kun tu snyan pa'i dris khyab pa'i/ /bstan pa 'jig rten khams 'dir gsal bya'i phyir/
/sde snod 'dzin pa dpal ldan sa skya pas/ /bsam yas

lhun gyis grub pa'i gnas chen 'dir/ /zab cing rgya che'i chos rnams bshad pa las/ /byung ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba gang yod des/ /'gro ba srid pa'i mtsho las grol bar shog /ri
bong 'dzin pa bsil ba'i 'od zer can/ /mtshan mo sa dang nam mkha' gsal byed pa/ /log blo'i rgyu skar tshogs rnams zil mnan nas/ /me tog kunda'i tshogs rnams kha 'byed byed/
/tshigs su bcad pa 'di rnams bla ma chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta chen pos bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang chen por/ mkhas pa rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bu slob
dpon chen po kA ma la shI la'i chos kyi gdan seng ge'i khri bshams pa ga la ba der bzhugs nas/ zab pa dang rgya che ba'i gdams pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor zhing / bstan
pa rin po che'i byi dor dang / skye dgu'i tshogs rab tu mang po'i don mdzad pa nyid kyis thugs cung zad rangs par gyur cing / sngon gyi dam pa de dag gi rnam par thar
pa dang rmad du byung ba'i 'phrin las dgongs shing mngon sum du gzigs la/ dus kyi 'gyur bas skye dgu'i tshogs ma rungs par gyur par mkhyen pa'i dbang gis thugs cung zad gdung
bar gyur yang / slad nas 'jig rten gyi chos kyis skye dgu'i bde legs su gyur cig snyam du dgongs te/ gtsug lag khang gi 'khor sa'i ngos ji ltar rigs pa'i gzhi dag la/
nyid kyi phyag g.yas pa rin po che mngon par brkyangs nas/ yi ge'i 'du byed mngon par 'du mdzad nas phyag rgya'i dbyibs las ri mo'i gzugs brnyan gyi tshul gyi rgyud de
dag gi sug tu gsal bar phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa ni gang gis mthong

ba dang / kha don du byed pa de dag gi rgyud la mdzad pa po'i ye shes gzigs pa'i dam pa 'jug par gyur cig ces dge slong 'phags pas smras so zhes bya ba legs par bkod do/ /gnyis
pa byang phyogs hor gyi yul du bstan pa'i bya ba ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ bod kyi yul 'dir bdag nyid chen pos thub pa'i bstan pa la mdzad pa rgya che ba grub pa'i
skabs su/ hor zhes bya ba'i skye bo gdug pa can blang dor gyi gnas la dud 'gro bas rmongs shing / snying rje ni las kyi gshin rje bas kyang chung / lus kyi rtsal ni gnod
sbyin bas kyang che/ lha ma yin gyi dpung tshogs ltar grangs mang zhing 'jigs su rung ba zhig gis thog mar rgya'i yul dang / de nas mi nyag gi yul la sogs pa byang phyogs
kyi rgyud mtha' dag bdag gir bzung nas/ khyim pa dang rab tu byung ba'i rnam dbye med par thams cad dmag khral las gsum gyi khyur bcug nas/ bstan pa'i ming tsam yang med
par byas te rang gzhan thams cad phung bar 'gyur bar gzigs te/ de dag la bzod glags med pa'i snying rjes hor rnams kyi sems chos kyi lam la drangs te 'dul ba'i smon lam
btab pa dus la babs par gzigs shing / nyid kyi mkhan po paN chen shAkya shrI singga la'i gling du byon pa na/ de la lha gnam the'u dkar pos hor gyi yul du 'byon par zhus
pa na/ sgrol ma la gsol ba btab pas khyod kyis phyin kyang phan pa med/ khyod kyi slob ma zhig bod na yod des phyin na phan par 'gyur bas lung ston cig gsungs te paN chen
gyis de ltar lung bstan cing / yang bla ma rje btsun chen pos

gshegs khar khyod kyi tshe mjug tu hor gyi 'bod mi yong / phyin na bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa rgya chen po yong bas ci nas song shig ces lung bstan pas/ chos rje nyid
kyis dgung lo drug cu re gcig la sngon 'gro'i chos 'khor chen po mdzad/ re gnyis pa la stobs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po jing gir gan gyi sras po tho lo no yon zhes
bya ba'i sras e chen go dan zhes pas spyan 'dren gyi pho nya mngags te/ de dus hor gyis phul ba'i 'ja' sa gdan 'dren ma las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ tshe ring gnam gyi shed
mong la bsod nams chen po'i dpal la brten nas rgyal po nged kyi lung / sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po la go bar byed pa'i gtam/ nged pha ma dang gnam
sa'i drin lan 'jal ba'i phyir/ lam gyi blang dor ma nor ba ston shes pa'i bla ma gcig dgos pa brtag pa byas dus khyod du 'dug pas/ lam gyi dka' tshegs la ma blta bar
yong dgos/ gal te na so rgas zer na sngon thub pa'i dbang pos sems can gyi don du lus grangs med sbyin par gtong ba ji tsam/ khyod kyis chos go ba'i dam bca' dang e 'gal/
ngas mtha'i khrims ra blangs dmag dpung chen pos brda ded byas nas sems can mang po la gnod pa byas na mi skrag pa e yin/ des na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang sems can mang
po la soms la khyod mgyogs par shog nyi ma nub phyogs kyi bande rnams khyod shes su 'jug pa yin/ gnang sbyin la dngul bre chen lnga/ gos chen gyi chos gos mu tig gi tshom
bu can la mu tig stong phrag drug dang nyis brgya/ gos lu hang gi ring

'gag lhwam 'bob dang bcas pa/ kha ti kha tshang ma yug gnyis/ thon ti kha tshang ma yug gnyis/ gos chen sna lnga yug nyi shu rnams yod/ 'di'i lon la rdor sri mgon dang / dbon
jo dar ma gnyis gtang ba yin/ 'brug lo zla ba brgyad pa'i gnam gang la bris zhes pa'i zhu yig dang bcas pa hor gyi gdan 'dren pa rnams slebs pa na/ sku na bgres na'ang
sngar bshad pa'i rgyu mtshan rnams dgongs te/ sku srog la yang phongs pa med par byon/ drug cu re gsum la mi nyag gi yul byang ngos su phebs/ de'i tshe mdo khams kyi ston
pa blo gros rab gsal zhes bya bas chos kyi dri ba zhus pa la lan 'di ltar gnang nas/ gzhung lugs kyi don gsal bar mdzad de/ dris lan dngos ni/ ston pa blo gros rab gsal
gyis/ /dri ba 'dri dar rten bcas pa/ /bdag gi sug par 'phrod gyur bas/ /de la dga' ba rab tu 'phel/ /khyed kyi dri ba dang po rig gter las/ /gang yod de 'jig bum pa bzhin/
/sgra yang yod ces rang bzhin rtags/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / sdom gsum rab dbye las/ chos dbyings yod pa'ang ma yin te/ /yod tsam mi rtag gis khyab par/ /chos kyi grags
pas gsal bar gsungs/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don sgra ji bzhin pa lags sam zhes pa ni/ dpal chos kyi grags pas rtog ge pa'i skabs su/ don dam don byed nus pa gang / /de 'dir don
dam yod pa ste/ /gzhan ni kun rdzob yod pa yin/ /de dag rang spyi'i mtshan nyid bshad/ /ces don byed nus pa la don dam du yod pa dang / don byed mi nus pa

kun rdzob tu yod pa'i rnam gzhag mdzad/ yang / 'jig la 'bras dang yod nyid bzhin/ /zhes sgra 'jig par bsgrub pa la/ 'bras bu rtags su bkod pa dang / don gyi yod pa nyid rtags
su 'god par mdzad/ de phyir dngos po med rten can/ /phyi rol rten ni sgra don la/ /brten nas 'dir ni bsgrub pa dang / /dgag pa thams cad 'dod pa yin/ /de yang sgra 'jug
pa nyid las/ /yod ces tha snyad bstan par 'dod/ /ces dang / de nyid med pa ma yin sgra don phyir/ /zhes sgra don la yod pa'i tha snyad mdzad pa dang / yang / de la dmigs
rung rnams kyis ni/ /yod pa dmigs pa las gzhan min/ /zhes tshad mas dmigs pa yod pa'i mtshan nyid du gsungs/ de dag gi don yang 'di yin te/ 'dir ni yod pa rnam gnyis te/
/don dang tha snyad dag gis so/ /don gyi yod pas bya ba byed/ /tha snyad yod pas dgag sgrub rten/ /zhes pa'o/ /dri ba gnyis pa chos kyi dbyings shes bya ma yin lags sam
zhes pa'i lan ni/ rdo rje gcod pa las/ sangs rgyas rnams ni chos kyi sku/ /'dren pa rnams ni chos nyid lta/ /chos nyid shes bya ma yin te/ /de ni shes par nus ma yin/ /zhes
gsungs pa dang / spyod 'jug las/ don dam blo yi spyod yul min/ /blo ni kun rdzob yin par 'dod/ /ces gsungs pa'i don chos dbyings rang ngos nas shes brjod kyi yul las
'das mod/ gzhan sel gyi sgo nas shes byar tha snyad mdzad de/ rgyud bla ma las/ gal te sangs rgyas khams med na/ /sdug la skyo bar mi 'gyur zhing / /mya ngan 'das par 'dod
pa dang / /don gnyer smon

pa'ang med par 'gyur/ /zhes dang / dbus mtha' las/ de bzhin nyid dang yang dag mtha'/ /mtshan ma med dang don dam dang / /chos kyi dbyings ni rnam grangs so/ /gzhan min phyin
ci log pa ni/ /de 'gag 'phags pa'i spyod yul dang / /'phags pa'i chos kyi rgyu yi phyir/ /rnam grangs don de go rim bzhin/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / chos mngon pa'i mdzod
las/ thog ma med pa'i dus kyi dbyings/ /chos rnams kun gyi gnas yin te/ /de yod pas ni 'gro kun gyis/ /mya ngan 'das pa thob par 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs so/ /de dag gi don yang
'di yin te/ don dam mtha' bzhi spros pa bral/ /kun rdzob yod med la sogs pa'i/ /gzhan sel phan tshun dngos 'gal gcod/ /yod pa min la med par gsungs/ /zhes pa'o/ /de'ang
rnam 'grel las/ sgrub dang dgag pa ma gtogs pa/ /sgra las byung ba'i tha snyad gzhan/ /yod min de phyir med pa la/ /med phyir 'di ni mi smra thob/ /ces gsungs so/ /dri
ba gsum pa 'gog bden ma byas pa'i dge ba lags sam zhes pa ni/ 'gog bden ma byas pa yin mod/ /dge ba mtshan nyid par mi bzhed de/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi rtsa she las/ ci
ste las rnams ma byas na/ /ma byas pa dang 'phrad 'jig 'gyur/ /tshangs spyod gnas pa ma yin pa/ /de la skyon du thal bar 'gyur/ /tha snyad thams cad nyid dang yang / /'gal
bar 'gyur na the tshom med/ /bsod nams dang ni sdig byed pa'i/ /rnam par dbye ba'ang 'thad mi 'gyur/ /gal te de ni rnam smin na/ /yang dang

yang du rnam smin 'gyur/ /zhes ma byas pa'i dge sdig mtshan nyid pa yod pa bkag par shes par bya'o/ /blo gros ldan pa'i blo gros kyis/ tshul bzhin dris pa'i dri ba kun/ /kun
dga'i ming gis kun mkhyen ltar/ /legs par phye la legs par gzigs/ /mdo smad kyi ston pa blo gros rab gsal gyi dris lan bi ji rin chen grags kyis gling khar bris pa'o zhes
pa'o/ /yang mdo smad kyi lam du rnal 'byor pa phru ma pa zhes pa'i dris lan gsungs pa ni/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam 'phrul chos rje sa skya paNDi ta hor yul
du chag phebs pa'i mdo smad kyi lam khar chibs gong du byon nas lam la gshegs pa'i tshe/ rnal 'byor pa phru ma pa zhes bya ba'i sgom chen pa bzang po cig gis chos rje pa
la gos phyi nang gcig phul nas/ chos rje pa khyed kyi chos dang chos ma yin pa rnam par 'byed pa'i bstan bcos las/ blun pos phyag rgya che bsgoms pa/ /phal cher dud 'gro'i
rgyu ru gsungs/ /min na gzugs med khams su skye/ /yang na nyan thos 'gog par lhung / /gal te de ni bsgom legs kyang / /dbu ma'i bsgom las 'da' ba med/ /dbu ma'i bsgom
de bzang mod kyi/ /'on kyang 'grub pa shin tu dka'/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don ci lags zhu yin 'dug pa la/ chos rje pa'i zhal nas 'di skad gsungs par gda'o/ /btsan thabs su ci
yang yid la mi sems par sems lteng rgyun du gnas shing gnyid rmugs 'dren pa'o/rnam rtog kha tshom zhi gnas dang / /stong pa rgyal po indra bhU tis/ rmongs pa'i bsgom pa
gang yin pa/ /rmongs pas rmongs pa thob par 'gyur/ ces gsungs/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis/ stong pa nyid la blta nyes na/ /

shes rab chung rnams phung bar 'gyur/ /so sor rtog pa'i shes rab kyis/ /ma dpyad par snang zhen gyi chos/ /ci yang med par 'dzin pa dang / /mthong yul 'gag pa'i stong nyams
shar ba'o/ /zhes gsungs so/ thal byung lhag mthong gnyis/ /ngan 'gror ltung ba'i rgyu chen te/ /legs 'dod rnams kyis spangs na legs/ /sems rgyu mi gsal zhi gnas dang /sems
kyi rgyu ba mi gsal bar lhag mthong shas che ba'i stobs kyis ngang gis dmigs pa la gnas pa'o/ /'di'i don mngon pa la sogs par gsal ma dpyad par chos thams cad nam mkha'
dang sems ci yang med pa dang yod min med min ngo 'phrod nas nyams shar ba'o//gzugs snang bkag pa'i lhag mthong gnyis/ /gzugs med skye ba'i rgyu chen te/ /thar 'dod gzugs
med du skye ba'i mi g.yo ba'i las bsog pa'o/ rnams kyis spangs na legs/ ting nge 'dzin bsgom pa'i tshe ci yang mi dran par yun ring du gnas pa'o//dran tshor med pa'i zhi
gnas dang / mig la sogs pa'i rnam shes tshogs drug rgyu ba mi gsal ba'o//tshogs drug bkag pa'i lhag mthong gnyis/ /nyan thos 'gog pa cha mthun te/'gog pa'i snyoms 'jug
dang 'dra ba'i nyams skyes pa'o/ /mchog 'dod rnams kyis spangs na legs/ /shin sbyangs bde ldan zhi gnas dang /mdo sde rgyan las/ des na de yi lus dang sems/ /shin tu sbyangs
pa ches gang nas/ /yid la byed pa can zhes bya/ /zhes gsungs so/ spros kun nyer zhi'i lhag mthong gnyis/ArYa de wa'i zhal snga nas/ yod min med min yod med min/ /gnyis
ka'i bdag nyid min pa'ang min/ /mtha' bzhi las grol don gyi mchog /de ni dbu ma pa yi lugs/ /zhes gsungs so/ /phar phyin theg pa'i lam chen te/ /rgyal sras rnams kyis
bsgrubs na legs/ /mtshan rtog sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs kyis/ tha mal kun rtog rgyu ni ma gtogs

pa/ /srid pa'i 'ching ba gzhan ci yod min te/ /de dang rnam par 'gal bar gyur pa'i sems/ /gang yin de ni kun tu rtogs mi 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs so/ /nyer zhi'i zhi gnas dang /
/bde stong zung 'jug lhag mthong gnyis/spyan ras gzigs pad dkar gyis/ /phra rab rdul gyi chos nyid 'das/ pra phab pa yi rnam pa can/ /rnam pa kun gyi mchog ldan pa/ /phyag
rgya chen po mi 'gyur bde/ /zhes gsungs so/ /gsang sngags phyag chen lam mchog ste/ /tshe 'dir grol 'dod bsgrubs na legs/ /tshigs su bcad pa lnga po 'di'i don khongs su
chud na phyag rgya chen po dag pa dang ma dag pa shes par 'gyur bas 'di la dpyod mdzod gsung gin 'dug rnal 'byor pa phru ma pa la gdams pa'i tshigs su bcad pa lnga pa bi
jis mdo khams smad gling khar bris pa'o/ /dris lan gyi rim pa gsum po 'di sngon chad dar bar ma byung yang / mdo khams nas rdo rje 'chang kun dga' dbang phyug gi phyag
tu byung ba la bris pa yin no/ /zhes gsungs so/ /mchan bu 'di yang chos rje pa'i gsung ji lta ba bzhin bi jis bris pa'o zhes 'byung zhing / yang mdo srang du phebs pa'i tshe
mi cig gis dar nag po gcig la gser gyi thig le mang po byas pa zhig phyag rten la byung ba de lha rje bi ji la gnang nas/ 'di khyod rang tshags gyis/ nam mkha' dwangs
pa la skar ma bkra ba lta bu'i bstan pa cig 'u cag la yong ba yin gsungs/ sa skya pas ring bsrel bkag zer ba yod pa la/ de yang / ring bsrel phal cher gdon las byung / dkar
po'i phyogs kyis byas pa'ang srid/ 'byung bzhi dag gis bskyed pa'ang yod/ /'phags pa gsum gyi ring bsrel ni/ /yon tan stobs kyis 'byung ba ste/ /'byung khungs nas byung
rin chen 'dra/ /de la

grangs ni brtsi rgyu med/ /mi 'grib 'phel ba'i ring bsrel yin/ /zhes bya ba yin la/ nga la rten 'byon na grangs brtsi rgyu med pa cig 'byon pa yin pas khyed rang tshags gyis
la/ dar 'di de'i na bza' gyis zhes gsungs shing / yang ngas ku re byas pa yin mi la ma zlo sdig pa gsog pa'i rgyu yin gsungs zhes kyang gsungs so/ /de nas rim gyis 'gro
ba'i mgon po chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che dang / chos kyi rgyal po se chen gan yon mchod du 'brel te/ rgyal po 'di'i 'og gi skad rigs mi gcig pa'i rgyal khams
dkon mchog gsum gyi sgra mi grag pa'i phyogs rnams su yang dkon mchog la dad pa skyes nas las 'bras la blang dor byed pa dang / hor rnams kyang theg pa chen po'i sems bskyed
dang dbang bskur zhu ba dang / dkon mchog mchod cing sems can la phan pa bsgrub pa dang / sdig to mi dge ba'i las lam cha shas kyi spangs nas lam bzang po la 'jug pa
dang / khyad par bod dang / yu gur dang / mi nyag sman rtse la sogs pa rang rang gi mnga' 'og na yod pa'i rab tu byung ba dang / sngags pa sogs yon tan can gyi mi rnams la
dmag khral las gsum gyi 'tshe ba med cing / bza' ba dang / btung ba dang / bgo ba dang / gser dngul/ gos dar la sogs pa'i dbul ba bzang zhing grangs mang ba yang nas yang
du 'bul ba dang / gug shrI sogs kyi ming bzang po byin nas bkur sti rgya chen po byas te/ rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che rnyed pa dang bkur sti bcas te yun ring du gnas
pa dang / gzhan yang hor gyi

rgyal khams 'di mi tshan che ba dang / shes pa 'char che bas ngo log byas kyis dogs nas/ lo skor re zhing skyes pa lo dgu yan chad re re nas bsad kyis mi 'dang bas/ khyu 'ded
byas te phyi'i rgya mtshor 'debs pa las/ de dag la lhag par brtse bas rgyal po la bka' nan che bar stsal te/ des kyang dbang zhus pa'i yon du phul nas de phyin chad chad
pa yin no zhes grags so/ /des na deng sang byang phyogs kyi rgyud 'dir bde skyid cung zad yod pa ni chos rje khu dbon gyi bka' drin thun mong ma yin pa yin te/ deng sang
gi phal pa lta ci smos/ dge bshes su khas 'che ba rnams dang / de dag las kyang rig pa dang mi rig pa dpyod pa'i blo shin tu gsal zhing / bstan pa dang sems can gyi don
gyi 'khur khyer bar grags pa dag kyang de ltar mi sems pa ni thugs mi ched pa'am thugs rtsing par zad do/ /des na khu dbon 'di gnyis kyis sems can la dngos su phan par
mdzad pa 'di lta bu ni bod kyi dge bshes sus kyang byas pa med do/ /de la 'ga' zhig sa skya pa lha'i bu'i bdud kyis g.yengs pas hor dang 'brel lo zhes zer ba'ang mi rigs
te/ hor gyi ngor rab tu byung ba yang hor dang spyod pa bstun pa cung zad byung yang / gal te sa skya pas de'i blo dang ma bstun na de chos la 'jug par mi nus te/ thub pas
kyang 'jig rten gzhug pa'i don du 'jig rten mthun 'jug mdzad pa lta bu'o/ /de chos la ma zhugs na sngar bshad pa'i nyes dmigs rnams yong bas dgag bya bas dgos pa che ba
yin no/ /'di ni byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi rmad du byung ba'i rnam par thar pa

yin te/ blo dman rnams ni mos par dka'o/ /don 'di la dgongs nas chos rje pas nyid kyi sku tshe'i 'du byed gtong ba'i tshe'ang / mgon po khyod kyi gsung rab mchog /nan tan gyis
ni bka' stsal pa/ /'bad pas ci nus bsgrub pa'i tshe/ /bar du gcod pa'i chos de sgrol/ /de nas ji skad gsungs pa yi/ /bka' stsal de dag bcings pa bzhin/ /rnam pa kun tu
thog tu babs/ /bden gsungs khyed la bdag skyabs mchi/ /zhes gsungs so/ /des na byang ngos su byon pa la yang gzhan gyi snang ngor 'byon pa mi spro pa'i tshul bstan pa sogs
rnam par thar pa 'ga' zhig tu 'byung mod kyi/ don ni gzhan don rgya che ba'i rten 'brel zab mo mkhyen bzhin du byon pa ste/ do skor ba'i dris lan las/ bdag kyang sngon
gyi byed pa 'ga' yi rgyus/ /bstan pa'i nyi ma shar gyi phyogs su shar/ /thos bsam sgom pa yid bzhin nor bu des/ /dad ldan dbus gtsang re ba myur du rdzogs/ /zhes gsungs
pa'i phyir ro/ /de nas dgung lo drug cu rtsa lnga bzhes pa'i dus su me pho rta'i lo zla ba brgyad pa la byang phyogs ling chur gdan phebs te/ de'i dus su rgyal po go dan/
go yug gan rgyal sar ston pa la hor yul du bzhud nas tshur byon pa dang lug lo zla ba dang po la mjal/ rgyal po yang shin tu mnyes nas chos dang 'jig rten lugs kyi gsung
gleng mang po mdzad par gda'/ de'i gong du rgyal po'i drung du bod kyi bande 'ga' 'dug pa la/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi yon tan gyi khyad par gang yang bskyed par ma nus
so/ /smon lam 'debs pa la dbang bar khas len pa la

'tshogs pa'i dus su e ka 'un dang / hor gyi lha pa gral mgor 'jog pa yod pa 'dug de nas rgyal po dang bla ma chos rje pa chos kyi gsung gleng mang po mdzad pa la/ mgo ba'i
skabs su yu gur gyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen mkhas pa mang pos kyang mtshams sbyor byas nas chos kyi don thams cad legs par gor bcug pas/ rgyal po yang shin tu mnyes par gyur
nas/ de ring phyin e ka 'un dang lha pa tsho bande'i gral mgor ma sdod/ thams cad kyi gral mgor bla ma chos rje pa bzhugs la smon lam 'debs pa'i dus su/ sngon la bandes
smon lam thob gsungs pa'i lung byung nas hor gyi rgyal khams su rab tu byung ba'i dbu 'phang bstod de/ de nas rgyal po go dan la sha khra'i nad cung zad byung ba'i rim gror
chab gtor 'jam dpal ma mang du mdzad pas/ lug lo zla ba gsum pa'i tshes bcu gcig gi tho rangs mnal lam du mi 'theng po lus la rma dang shu bas gang ba cig byung ba la/
khyod su yin dris pas/ nga la dpon po gcig yod pa na re/ sa skya pas 'bod cing 'dug pas khyod song la ci zer nyon/ nga'i lus po na nas 'gro mi nus pa 'dug zer nas yong ba
yin zer/ de nas chos rje pas/ go dan gyi gser yig pa btang nas nged thag ring po nas bos/ da 'di la phan pa cig dgos pa byung bas nad 'di'i rgyu ci yin/ da thabs ci byas
na phan zhes dris pas/ mi de na re/ yul phyogs de rnams sus kyang ma bdag pa'i dus su nga'i dpon po des bdag byas pa yin/ de'i tshe go dan 'di'i shAkya mu ne la bsod nams
bsags pa'i rgyal po cig tu skyes/ de nas tshe 'phos te mi

nyag gi rgyal po cig tu skyes/ rgyal po des nga'i khang pa'i steng du mkhar las byas nas/ mi nyag gi rgyal po des bande rnams la nga mkhar las byed pas sa gzhi slong zer/ bande
rnams dbyangs 'dra byed pa dang / rol mo 'dra 'khrol ba dang / gtor ma 'dra gtong gin 'dug ste/ sa chog mi shes par 'dug pas sa gzhi ma byin/ der rgyal pos mkhar las
byas pas nged dpon g.yog ris non pa bzhin song / de nas mi'i bsod nams ma thub par byang ngos 'dir 'ongs nas yul legs par bzung / der yang rgyal po de 'ongs nas nged kyi
steng du me btang / sa brkos/ gzhan yang gnod pa mang du byas/ der yang sdod sa ma byung / de nas nga'i dpon po de khros nas yul phyogs kyi lha 'dre thams cad bsdus nas/
rgyal po 'dis nga'i yul lan gnyis phyung bas/ da 'di la gnod pa cig byed pas khyed rnams kyis grogs gyis byas pas/ lha 'dre rnams na re/ rgyal po 'dis shAkya mu ne la bsod
nams bsags pa yin pas 'di'i stobs mi thub kyis khyod skam sar ma sdod par chu mig dang 'dam rdzab yod sar yul bzung zer nas der bsdad pa'i dus su/ rgyal po des rgyal po
snga ma kun gyi bande rnams la rgyugs byin pa'i yi ge bltas pas/ sngar gyi rgyugs ches zer nas phri/ de'i tshe shAkya mu ne 'di gser yin nam/ shing yin nam/ rdo yin blta
zer nas zhabs la gzong gis brkos pa dang / de nas lha 'dre rnams na re/ da 'di'i bsod nams kyi cha nyams pas bar chad bya ba'i dus la babs zer nas lha 'dre rnams 'tshogs
pa dang / 'di

bsod nams can yin pas gzhan sus kyang brlag par mi nus pas/ nang gi blon po dang rgyal po la phra ma gzhug zer nas phra ma bcug pas der blon pos bsad/ rgyal po des 'chi khar
smon lam btab ste nga tshe phyi ma rgyal po gcig gi bur skyes nas khyed rnams la gnod pa skyel zhing / khyed rnams bran bzhin du 'khol bar shog cig ces smon lam btab pas
jing gir rgyal po'i tsha bor skyes nas go dan 'di yin/ des byang ngos 'dir 'ongs nas nged kyi sdod sar chu dang 'dam rdzab kyi steng du rta rgyugs/ der rta bsad/ rta khrag
gar song sar nged la la na/ la la shi nga'i lus la yod pa'i sbal lcong 'di rnams kyang shi la khad pa la/ nga'i lus kyi drod kyis ma shi ba yin zer nas lus la sbal pa
dang lcong mo phyed skam pa dang / shi la khad pa yod pa la de rnams bstan nas gong gi bande rnams kyis go dan la smon lam 'dra 'debs pa las/ nged klu la phan pa ci yang
ma byung / da khyed sa skya pas sman dang bza' rgyu byin pas nged klu la phan par byung / nga gar yang 'gro mi nus pa da res cung zad phan pa yin/ nga'i dpon de shi la khad
yod/ de shi na go dan yang 'chi/ nga'i dpon sos na go dan yang sos pas/ rim gro yang chung chung gis mi phan mi sos pas/ khyed kyis nga'i dpon dang go dan gso ba'i 'bad
pa chen po gyis/ nga'i dpon sos na go dan yang sos/ de sos na khyed kyang bzang por 'gro zer/ de nas chos rje pa'i thugs dgongs la da 'di la thabs ci byas na phan snyam
pa la/ bar chad cung zad cig gis de yal song gsungs so/ /de nas rgyal po'i don du 'phags pa

seng ge sgra'i cho ga mdzad pas/ rgyal po nad las thar bas shin tu dad de theg pa chen po'i sems bskyed la sogs pa zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos mang du zhus/ mchod gnas rnams
kyi phud du bkur/ de nas bzung ste skad rigs mi gcig pa'i gdul bya chos la mi dad pa rnams chos la dad par byas/ dad pa rnams theg pa chen por bcug mdor na gdul bya
dpag tu med pa smin cing grol bar mdzad pas bstan pa'i dar rgyas phul du phyin pa mdzad do/ /gzhan yang rgya nag ri bo rtse lngar byon nas/ de na gnas pa'i rtogs ldan rgyan
po zhes bya ba la/ bcom ldan 'das kyai rdo rje Dombi lugs kyi dkyil 'khor du mngon par dbang bskur ba sngon du 'gro ba can gyi rje btsun bdag med ma'i sindhu ra'i dkyil
'khor du byin gyis brlabs pa dang / de'i rjes su rdzogs rim zab mo bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i man ngag byin te/ phyag rgya chen po'i ye shes ngo sprod par byed pa'i gdams
pa zab mo gnang nas rgyud grol bar mdzad pa yin te/ gdams pa de nyid las/ rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam 'phrul chos rje sa skya paNDi ta chen po rgya nag ri bo rtse
ldar phebs nas bzhugs pa'i tshe/ de na sgom chen cig gnas pa'i rtogs ldan rgyan po zhes bya ba zhig gis chos rje pa la bskor ba dang phyag mang po byed cing 'dug pa la/
chos rje pa'i zhal nas/ rtogs ldan pa bskor phyag kyang ngo mtshar che ste/ gnas 'di 'dra na 'dug pa la gdams ngag bzang po la brten pa'i sgom sgrub cig dgos pa yin te ang
gsung gi 'dug rtogs ldan pa des bsam mno zhig btang ste rang gi gnas

nas dar yug dkar po gcig blangs te chos rje ba la phul nas/ chos rje ba lta ba phyag rgya chen po 'di theg pa thams cad kyi sgom du bzhed dam/ phyag rgya chen po 'di rang ji
lta bu lags/ ci'i phyir phyag rgya chen po zhes bya/ 'di skye tshul dang / sa lam bgrod tshul gyi rnam pa ci lta bu lags/ bdag la phyag rgya chen po'i gdams ngag zab mo
zhig gnang ba zhu zhu yin 'dug pa la chos rje pa thugs dgyes te/ Dombi pa'i kye rdo rje'i dbang bskur mdzad nas/ phyag rgya chen po lhan cig skyes grub dang / tog tse ba'i
bsam mi khyab kyi gdams ngag tshang ma cig gnang nas/ nged kyi lugs kyi phyag rgya chen po'i khrid lugs 'di ltar yin/ grub thob ma snga bar rtse gcig tu sgrub pa mdzod
dang mi bslu ba yong / khyod kyis dris pa'i don mdor bsdus pa 'di rnams thugs la zhog gsungs nas/ spyir pha rol tu phyin pa'i theg pa'i lugs la lta ba dka' rtags kyi phyag
rgya bzhis rgyas 'debs/ rgyud sde 'og ma gsum gyi lugs la zab gsal gnyis med kyi rgyas 'debs par bshad kyang / phyag rgya chen po'i tha snyad ma gsungs shing de dag gi
lugs la mchog gi dngos grub bshad kyang phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub ma bshad pas lta ba phyag rgya chen po mtshan nyid par bsgom par mi 'dod do/ /de dag gi lugs
la rtogs bya stong pa nyid zab mo bshad kyang / rtogs byed thabs lam zab mo ma bshad pas phyag rgya chen po mtshan nyid pa mi 'thad pa yin/ dper na nyan thos lugs la sbyin
pa dang tshul khrims la sogs pa bshad kyang / grogs thabs shes khyad par can ma bshad pas sbyin pa'i pha rol tu

phyin pa la sogs pa mi 'thad pa bzhin/ mi blun po la ba glang du 'dogs pa ltar/ de dag gis lta ba'i sgom la phyag rgya chen por 'dogs na ming tsam la mi rtsod/ phyag rgya chen
po'i rang bzhin ni/ /phyag rgya chen po mi 'gyur bde/ /gzung dang 'dzin pa dbyibs dag dang / /rtog dang brjod pa rnam par spangs/ /dri za'i grong khyer lta bu dang /
/pra phab pa yi rang bzhin can/ /rnal 'byor thabs dang shes rab bdag /e waM yi ge de la 'dud/ /phra rab rdul gyi chos nyid 'das/ /pra phab pa yi rnam pa can/ /rnam pa kun
gyi mchog ldan pa/ /phyag rgya chen po de la 'dud/ /ces gsungs pa ltar rtogs bya chos nyid gnyug ma zhes bya ba rnam pa kun gyi mchog dang ldan pa'i stong pa nyid do/ /rtogs
tshul smra bsam brjod med kyi nyams pra phab pa'i rnam pa can gyi sgo nas rtogs bya'i ngo bor rnal 'byor zung 'jug gi ye shes/ de yang snang stong zung 'jug rig stong
zung 'jug bde stong zung 'jug bde chen zung 'jug lhan skyes ye shes/ rang byung ye shes/ rang rig ye shes/ so sor rtog pa'i ye shes zhes bya ba la sogs pa mtshan gyi rnam
grangs du ma dang ldan pa de rtogs pa'i thabs bshad rgyud rdo rje phreng ba las/ bla ma legs par mnyes byas te/ /yang dag dbang bskur rab mnos nas/ /de nyid don ni rab
tu dbye/ /zhes pa dang / brtag gnyis las/ phyi nas de nyid rab tu dbye/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar smin byed kyi dbang bskur mtshan nyid pa dang / grol byed kyi rim gnyis yan
lag dang bcas pa tshul bzhin du bsgoms pa las 'byung ba yin

te/ 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis/ sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos bstan pa/ rim pa gnyis la yang dag brten/ /gcig ni bskyed pa'i rim pa ste/ /gzhan ni rdzogs pa'i rim pa yin/ /zhes
gsang sngags bla med kyi ye shes 'dren pa'i thabs thams cad rim pa gnyis su bsdus nas bshad pa'i gnad yin no/ /phyag rgya chen po zhes bya ba'i sgra don ni/ legs sbyar gyi
skad la ma sbyangs pa dag phyag ni stong pa'i ye shes te/ /rgya ni 'khor ba'i rgya las grol/ /zhes gsang snying dang / phyag rgya chen po thig le sogs las 'byung zhes smra
ba ni 'khrul pa ste/ legs sbyar gyi skad la mahA mu dra zhes pa ni/ bod skad du mahA chen po/ mu dra rgya dang / rtags dang / mtshan ma dang / gug skyed la sogs pa la
'jug pa las/ 'dir rgya ru bsgyur ba yin no/ /don ni a wa dhU tI pas/ rgyas gdab phyir na rgya zhes te/ /srid gsum ro gcig phyag chen po/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar 'khor 'das
kyi chos thams cad bde stong zung 'jug gi ngang du rgyas btab nas nyams su len pa'i don gyis lta ba phyag rgya chen po zhes bya ba yin no/ /skye tshul gyi rim pa ni/ gang
zag skal bzang 'ga' zhig la dbang gi ye shes 'bebs pa'i dus nas phyag rgya chen po'i ye shes mtshan nyid pa skye ba yang yod mod/ phal che ba ni thabs bsgom pa sogs la ltos
shing / thog mar phyag rgya chen po ltar snang skyes nas/ phyis phyag rgya chen po mtshan nyid pa skye bar 'gyur ba yin/ phyag rgya chen po ltar snang zhes bya ba yang
cha mthun pa dug can dang / 'ba' zhig pa skyon can gnyis 'byung ba yin/ dug can ni thos bsam gyis

bsdus pa go rtogs dang / bsgom byung gis bsdus pa rnam rtog gi rba rlabs ma yal bzhin du zung 'jug gi nyams span spun skyes pa yin/ 'ba' zhig pa ni gnas pa 'ba' zhig pa dang
/ so sor rtog pa 'ba' zhig tu gyur pa dang / snang phyogs 'ba' zhig tu gyur pa dang / stong phyogs 'ba' zhig tu gyur pa dang / lus la bde drod dang / 'phar g.yo dang /
ngag la nges med kyi smra brjod dang / sems la nges pa med pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi nyams snang sna tshogs pa ste sgo gsum gyi nyams 'ba' zhig tu gyur pa dang / brgyal ba
dang tshogs drug 'gags pa la sogs pa'i nyi tshe ba 'ba' zhig tu gyur pa rnams yin/ sa lam bgrod tshul ni/ byang chub tu gnyer ba'i smin byed dbang bskur nas brtsams te nyams
skyon can rnams rdzogs pa yan chad theg pa thun mong ba ltar na tshogs lam zhes bya ba yin/ brtag gnyis las/ kun mkhyen ye shes de lta bu/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ bde stong
zung 'jug gi ye shes mtshan nyid pa rgyud la skyes shing rnam par mi rtog pa'i nyams rgyun chags su 'byung yang / rnam par rtog pa'i bag chags phra mo dang bcas pa nam
langs pa la nyi ma shar ba lta bus dpe'i ye shes rgyud la skyes pa ni sbyor ba'i lam zhes bya ba yin te/ mtshan brjod las/ rnam par shes pa'i chos nyid 'das/ /ye shes
gnyis med tshul 'chang ba/ /rnam par rtog med lhun gyis grub/ /ces gsungs pa ltar/ rnam pa kun gyi mchog dang ldan pa'i stong nyid mngon sum du rtogs pa rnam par mi rtog
pa'i ye shes mtshan nyid pa phyag rgya chen po don gyi ye

shes thog mar skyes pa'i tshe na mthong ba'i lam thob pa zhes bya ba yin/ des na rgyun chags su goms shing gong nas gong du bgrod de sa bcu gnyis pa'i bar du phyin pa ni bsgom
pa'i lam zhes bya ba yin/ de nas sa bcu gsum mngon du byas pa na sku bzhi ye shes lnga la sogs pa yon tan rgya mtsho lta bu thob pa ni mi slob lam mngon sum du byas pa'o/
/de yang thun mong ba ltar na sbyor lam/ thun mong ma yin pa ltar na phyag rgya chen po dpe'i ye shes mtshan nyid pa rgyud la skyes nas don gyi ye shes mngon du byas
pa dang / zung 'jug rdo rje 'chang gi go 'phang tshe 'dir mngon du byed par 'dod na/ rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i spyod pa dang / nye rgyu sogs tshul bzhin du nyams len byas
na/ rgya gar gyi grub thob rnams ltar 'dir 'grub pa las 'os ci yong / dpe'i ye shes mtshan nyid pa rgyud la skyes nas spyod pa ma 'grub na 'da' kha ma dang / bar do'i gdams
ngag gis 'grub par bshad/ 'ga' zhig gis/ phyag rgya chen po chig chod la/ /sa lam brtsi ba'i rmongs pa 'khrul/ /zhes bya ba ni 'khrul pa ste/ mtshan brjod las/ mgon po
sa bcu'i dbang phyug ste/ /zhes bya ba dang / a bhi dha na las/ rab tu dga' dang dri ma med/ /de bzhin 'od byed 'od 'phro dang / /shin tu sbyang dka' mngon du gyur/ /ring
du song dang mi g.yo ba/ /legs pa'i blo gros chos kyi sprin/ /dpe med pa dang ye shes che/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa bcu gsum sa/ /zhes sogs rgyud sde dang grub pa'i slob dpon
rnams kyis sa lam gyi rnam gzhag rgya cher mdzad pa'i phyir ro/ /mtshan brjod las/ skad cig gcig

gis rdzogs sangs rgyas/ /zhes gsungs pa ni/ sa lam bgrod pa'i tha ma la mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba'i tshul yin/ 'da' ka ye shes las/ sems rtog na sangs rgyas yin
pas sangs rgyas gzhan du mi 'tshol ba'i 'du shes bsgom par bya'o zhes gsungs pa ni/ sa ra has/ sems nyid gcig pu kun gyi sa bon te/ /gang la srid dang mya ngan 'das 'phro
ba/ /'dod pa'i 'bras bu ster bar byed pa yi/ /yid bzhin nor 'dra'i sems la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ sems kun gzhi'i rnam par shes pa'i kun rdzob dang / don
dam pa'i gnas tshul mngon du gyur pa'i sgo nas sa lam bgrod de 'tshang rgya ba la dgongs pa yin/ ji skad du/ rin chen sems las phyir gyur pa'i/ /sangs rgyas med cing sems
can med/ /rnam par shes pa'i gnas don nam/ /phyi rol gyur pa yod ma yin/ /zhes pa dang / rnam dag ye shes gzugs can dang / /'khor ba rnam par rtog pa la/ /khyad par cung
zad yod ma yin/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ 'khor 'das kyi snang ba thams cad sems su ro gcig pa'i gnad kyis yin/ rtogs ldan khyed kyis 'di dag thugs la zhog la sgrub pa mdzod
dang phan thogs pa chen po cig 'ong gsungs nas ched gnyer mdzad cing 'dug rtogs ldan rgyan po la gdams pa phyag rgya chen po'i mig thur zhes bya ba chos rje pa'i gsung
la yang yang nan chags byas nas bi jis ri bo rtse lngar bris pa'o zhes gsungs so/ /gzhan yang ling chu rtse khab tu bzhugs te chos gsungs pa'i tshe mi mang po zhig ri bo
rtse

lnga la mchod pa la phyin pas thams cad kyi rmi lam du da lta ri bo rtse lnga na 'jam dpal mi bzhugs/ ling chu rtse khab na chos gsung gin yod zer ba mthun par rmi ste/ sad
pa na mi rnams kyis the tshom med par ling chur 'ong pas/ chos rje nyid byang chub kyi mchog tu sems bskyed pa gsungs pa dang mjal te chos thob bo zhes yongs su grags so/
/yang chos rje nyid dang / hor rgyal po go dan gnyis 'bel ba'i bka' mchid mang du byung ba'i 'phros shig la/ mdo sde gser 'od dam pa'i lung gis/ rus sbal la spu mi 'byung
ba'i tshul bsnyad pas/ de sun dbyung ba'i phyir rgyal pos/ chos rje pa la pags pa 'dom skor tsam la spu ring po 'ja' tshon gyi ri mo yod pa zhig gzigs phul bas/ bdag nyid
chen pos gsung gis/ 'di ni rus sbal gyi pags pa ga la yin/ 'di ni chu la gnas pa'i sems can gyi don bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa' rus sbal 'dra ba'i gzugs can
gyis 'byon par gsung rab las bshad pa gang yin pa de nyid kyi pags pa yin/ de'i rgyu mtshan ston shes kyis bstan nas blta shes kyis bltas na pags pa 'di'i ngos la sangs rgyas
stong dang byang sems nye ba'i sras brgyad kyi sku brnyan gsal bar yod gsungs nas de dag bstan pas/ der lhags pa'i skye bo kun ngo mtshar du gyur cing / rgyal po cung
zad skyengs te lan zhig bya dgos snyam nas blon po rnams la bka' bgros te/ sgyu ma mkhan rnams rdzas sngags kyis sgyu ma sprul du bcug pas/ sngar med pa'i yul yid du 'ong
ba zhig na gtsug lag khang sogs dgon pa'i rnam pa ngo mtshar can

zhig sprul thub pa dang / rgyal po'i lung gis chos rje nyid la/ khyod ngas mchod gnas la bos pa mkhas par 'dug cing / yon tan ya mtshan can mang po mthong bas spro bar gyur/
da ni gnas dben pa zhig na dgon pa phun sum tshogs pa zhig yod pas khyod la ster bas der 'gro gsungs nas/ bdag nyid chen po dpon slob rnams dang / rgyal po 'khor dang bcas
pas kyang byon/ de'i tshe chos rje nyid kyis phyogs de gzigs ma thag nas sgyu ma sprul pa yin par mngon par mkhyen pas dgongs te/ sgo srung 'jigs su rung ba mang po 'dug
pa de rnams la bka' bsgo dang / gnas brtan gzhan rnams la rab gnas kyi me tog 'thor ba mdzad pas/ sgyu ma bshig ma thub par dus da lta yang mngon sum du yod cing / sprul
pa sde zhes bya bar ming yang grags pa yin no/ /de ltar ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa du ma'i sgo nas rgya'i yul du bstan pa dar rgyas phul du phyin pa mdzad nas/ de nas chos
rje nyid bod du 'byon pa bas byang ngos su bzhugs na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la phan che bar gzigs nas gnas de nyid du thugs phab/ bod kyi grwa slob rnams la gnang sbyin
dang 'bul ba mang po bskur/ chos kyi skyes su byang chub sems dpa'i lam la 'jug pa'i rim pa thub pa'i dgongs pa gsal ba zhes bya ba bskur nas tshogs chos 'di dbus gtsang
khams gsum du bshad pa yin pas/ nga'i slob ma thams cad kyis lung thob pa yin pas yi ge 'di la ltos la shod/ 'di bzhin du nyams su long gsungs pa'i gsung 'phrin dang
bcas bu slob rnams la bka' shog

'di ltar gnang ba yin te/ oM swa sti siddhaM/ bla ma dang mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /dpal ldan sa skya paNDi tas/ dbus gtsang mnga' ris dang bcas pa'i dge
ba'i bshes gnyen yon mchod rnams la springs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang / sems can spyi dang / sgos bod skad smra ba thams cad la phan par bsam nas hor nang du 'ong
/ nged 'bod mkhan la yon bdag chen po shin tu dges/ 'phags pa spun 'di 'dra ba'i chung ba nas khrid nas 'khor dang bcas pa 'ong ba de nged la bsam pa yin/ khyed mgos
ngo bltas pa yin/ gzhan tsho rkang pas ngo bltas pa yin/ khyod ngas bos pa yin/ gzhan tsho skrag nas 'ong ba yin/ de ngas mi shes pa e yin/ 'phags pa spun gyis sngar yang
bod kyi chos ni shes par 'dug da dung yang 'phags pas bod chos slob/ phyag na rdo rjes hor yig dang hor skad slob/ ngas mi chos kyis bskyangs/ khyed kyis lha chos kyis bskyangs
na shAkya mu ne'i bstan pa yang phyi'i rgya mtsho'i mtha' tshun chad khyab par mi 'gro ba e yin gsungs so/ /rgyal po byang chub sems dpa' 'di spyir sangs rgyas kyi
bstan pa dang / sgos dkon mchog gsum la shin tu gus khrims lugs bzang pos 'khor thams cad legs par skyong zhing / khyad par du yang nged la gzhan las lhag pa'i thugs la
'dogs par byung / khong gi zhal nas khyod rang blo bde bar chos shod/ khyed la gang dgos ngas ster ba yin/ khyod bzang po gtong ba ngas shes/ ngas bzang por e gtong gnam
shes gsungs/ khyad par 'phags pa spun la thugs

'dogs che bar 'dug rang shes khrims lugs 'khur shes na/ rgyal khams thams cad la phan par bya snyam pa'i thugs dgongs bzang po cig 'dug sgos khyed rang gi mi sde bod rnams
la khrims lugs legs par slobs/ skyid du 'jug pa ngas shes gsungs pa dang / rgyal po dang rgyal brgyud rnams tshe ring ba'i smon lam rim gro pa thams cad kyis 'bad par zhu/
skabs don hor 'di'i dmag sde grangs las 'das/ 'dzam bu'i gling thams cad khong gi mnga' ris su 'dug snyam pa'i bsam pa cig 'dug khong rang dang mthun pa tsho skyid sdug
khong rang dang mnyam par byed/ khong la zhe thag pas gang zer la ma nyan na ngo bltas pa yin zer ba'i ming gis mi chog pa/ rting brlag par byed pa cig 'dug yu gur gyi rgyal
khams 'di yang ma brlag par gong du phan/ mi nor rnams khong gis blangs nas/ yig mkhan/ nor gnyer ba/ bu dga' thams cad khong gis byed/ rgya/ mi nyag sog po la sogs
pa ma brlag gong du hor 'dra btang yang ci zer ma nyan pas/ brlag pa'i rting la 'gro sa ma rnyed nas ngo blta dgos byung / 'on kyang de rting ci zer nyan pas da lta thad
thad so so na bu dga' nor gnyer/ dmag dpon/ yig mkhan la sogs pa khong rang gi mi chen re bskos pa mang / 'o skol mi sde ngan la gyong pas thabs sna tshogs kyi sgo nas bros
pas thar du re/ thag ring bas mi yong du re/ 'thab thub tu re nas/ g.yo sgyu zol gsum byas pas brlag kyang brlag tha thad so so nas ngo bltas pa'i tsho mang / bod ngan
la

gyong pa'i stobs kyis bran dang g.yog gi bye brag ma gtogs pa/ dpon por bskos pa brgya la re 'ga' tsam las ma mthong / bod ngo bltas pa mang yang 'dab nor nyung ba'i stabs
kyis mi chen tsho rting nas ma mgu ba'i gnad cig gda'/ na ning ni lo 'ga' la stod du dmag song ba med/ ngas bi ri khrid nas ngo bltas/ 'dir shin tu ngo blta legs pas/ stod
mnga' ris/ dbus gtsang ba rnams ngo bltas/ bi ri tha thad tsho yang ngo blta bar yod byas pas/ da bar la dmag ma song ba des phan pa yin te/ stod kyi mi rnams de tsho mi
shes te mchis/ de skabs su 'di na mar ngo bltas pa yin kyang 'dab nor legs po ma byas pa dang / blo ma gtad pa kun la dmag rgyab nas mi nor thams cad gtor ba de khyed rnams
kyis thos te mchis/ dmag rgyab pa de tsho yul btsan/ mi dpa'/ dmag mang / go cha sra zhing mda' mkhas pa rnams kyis thub tu re byas pas brlag 'dug mi rnams kyi bsam
pa la/ hor kho rang 'u lag dang dmag khral chung / gzhan tsho 'u lag dang dmag khral che bsam ste/ gzhan tsho bas hor rang 'u lag dang dmag khral che/ de dang sbyar na gzhan
tsho chung bar gda'/ da dung yang ci zer gyi ngag la nyan na khyed rnams kyi yul/ sa phyogs kyi mi sde/ so so'i dpon gang yod pa de dpon du bskos/ sa skya pa'i gser yig
pa dang dngul yig pa bos la/ nged kyi dar kha che 'di bskos na 'thad pa yin zer ba'i ngo sprod gyis la phar 'gro tshur 'gro'i bang chen pa go chod pa tshud/ de nas dpon
gyi ming / mi sde'i grangs/ 'dab nor gyi tshad yi

ge legs po gsum gyis la/ gcig nged la bskur/ gcig sa skyar zhog gcig rang rang gi dpon gyis bzung / yang ngo bltas pa 'di yin/ ma bltas pa 'di yin zer ba'i sa ris legs po gyis/
shan ma phyed na ngo ma bltas pa'i zhor la bltas pa tsho yang brlag dogs yod/ sa skya pa'i gser yig pas yul gang yin pa'i dpon dang gros gyis la/ sems can la yang phan
par gyis la rang tshod dbang che ma byed/ yul dpon gyis kyang sa skya pa'i gser yig pa dang gros ma byas par rang tshod ma byed/ gros ma byas par rang tshod byed pa khrims
la med/ nyes pa la thug na 'di na zhu ba dka'/ der thams cad blo mthun par gyis/ hor gyi khrims lugs byas na legs po 'ong / gser yig pa bsu bskyel dang zhabs tog legs
por gyis/ 'di yang gser yig pa yong ba kun la gzhan 'dri ba'i sngon la ma bros sam 'thab bam/ gser yig pa tsho nya ra legs por byas sam/ 'u lag byung ngam/ ngo bltas pa
rnams brtan nam byas pa de tsho sngon la 'dri bar 'dug gser yig pa de ma mgu na gnod thub pa'i gtam gtong bar nges/ mgu na phan thogs nus pa cig gda'/ gser yig pa'i ngag
la ma nyan na byas kyang dka' bar mthong / 'dir mi gang drag pa dang 'dab nor khyer nas 'ong ba tsho bzang por gtong bar gda'/ rang re tsho yang bzang po bya snyam pa'i
bsam pa yod na/ nged rang gi dpon po kun 'dab nor bzang po bzung la sa skya pa'i mi dang 'grogs la byon/ 'dab nor 'di tsam gcig 'dab zer ba'i gros gyis/ 'dir ngas

kyang gros byed/ de nas rang yul 'ongs nas rang gzhan thams cad la phan par 'ong / spyir ngas kyang na ning nas mi btang nas 'di ltar byas na legs byas nas gros bstan pa/ khyed
rang rnams kyis kyang de bzhin byed pa'i rigs su med pa 'dug brlag pa'i rjes la khyed tha dad tsho ci zer nyan pa cig 'dod pa yin nam/ ci zer ba yin yang ma go /phyis
sa skya pa hor gseb tu song ba yin te nged la ma phan zer ba de mi gsung bar zhu/ ngas bdag pas gzhan gces pa'i bsam pa byas nas/ bod skad smra ba thams cad la phan pa'i
phyir du hor gseb tu 'ong ba yin te/ nga ci zer la nyan na phan par 'dug khyed rnams kyis 'di'i snang tshul ma mthong / thos pa rnams la yid ches pa shin tu dka'/ de'i
stobs kyis da dung btub par 'ong snyam ste/ bde ba'i 'phro la glo bur du 'dres mnan pa lta bu'i 'thib gnon cig byung nas dbus gtsang gi bu tsha dang mi la sogs pa hor gseb
tu song gis dogs/ nged ni legs nyes ci byung yang nga la 'gyod pa med/ bla ma dkon mchog gi byin rlabs dang bka' drin gyis da dung legs po 'ong ba'ang srid/ khyed rang
rnams kyang dkon mchog la gsol ba thob/ rgyal pos nged la su dang yang mi 'dra ba'i thugs la btags/ de'i stobs kyis rgya bod/ yu gur/ mi nyag la sogs pa'i dge bshes mi chen/
yul mi gcig pa thams cad kyis ngo mtshar che snyam nas chos nyan pa dang gus pa che ba 'dug nged 'dir 'ong ba rnams la hor gyis ci 'dra byed snyam pa'i dogs pa mi dgos/
thams cad kyi thugs la btags nas bzang por yod

pas/ nged kyi phyogs nas thams cad blo bde bar bzhugs pas chog 'dab nor la gser/ dngul/ glang po che'i mche ba/ mu tig rdog po che ba/ mtshal/ btsod/ ru rta/ gi wang / stag
gzig gung gsum/ sram/ bod snam/ dbus phrug bzang po/ 'di na de tsho dga' bar 'dug spyir nor la 'dir gtsigs chung yang rang rang gi yul na gang bzang gi nor rdzas 'ong bas
chog pa yin/ gser yod na gang 'dod 'ong bar 'dug pas dgongs mdzod/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa phyogs mtha' dag tu rgyas par gyur cig mangga laM zhes zhes pa'i gsung shog
gnang ba dbus gtsang gi grwa bu slob sbyin bdag dang bcas pa sogs skye bo thams cad kyis mthong bas so sor dga' mgu yi rang zhing yid spro ba mchog tu thob par mdzad pa yin
no/ /de lta bu'i bla ma rtsod pa'i dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa gnyis pa de dgung lo bdun cu'i bar du rgyal ba'i bstan pa dang / sems can dpag tu med pa smin cing grol
bar mdzad nas/ mthar gzugs kyi sku'i bkod pa ji ltar bsdu ba'i tshul slob dpon bi ji ba'i gsung ltar brjod na/ lcags mo phag gi dus su gzhan don la bzhud pa'i dus su tha
skar gyi zla ba la ltas chen po bco brgyad byung / tha skar gyi tshes brgyad kyi nyin par sa g.yos chen po byung / bdag bi ji lha rjes rgyu mtshan zhus pas/ rgyal ba'i sras
su gyur pa chen po rnams gzhan don la 'gro ba'i ltas yin/ 'u cag kyang de'i rjes su 'jug pa 'dra gsungs/ nyi shu dgu'i nam phyed na longs sku'i cha lugs sgra dbyangs mi
zad pa sgrog pa'i rgyal po

mngon sum du byon/ sku mdog dkar po zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa byon nas/ khyed kyis spos phul gsungs nas bdag gis spos phul/ tho rangs kyi dus su spyan ras gzigs dbang zhal bcu
gcig pas byin rlabs mdzad pa'i snang ba byung / spos phul gsungs pas bdag gis phul/ smin drug gi zla ba'i yar tshes drug gi nyin sgra sna tshogs bsgrags/ bdag drung na
yod pas/ lha khang gi nang na rnam rgyal mchod pa byed mi rnams yin nam zhus pas/ lha khang na rnam rgyal byed pa la bltar song gsungs/ de ltar phyin bas khong rnams kyis
kyang sgra thos zin ci yin nam khyed zhur song zer bdag gis zhus pas/ lha'i bsu ba mang po byung mchod pa gyis/ da rang gzhan gyi don la 'gro dgos pa yin gsungs/ me tog
gi char yang sa la 'bab rgyu med pa nam mkha' la mang po byung / tshes bcu gsum gyi nyin par gdugs la bzhugs pa'i dus su nyi ma yod 'phro la sprin dkar po legs pa cig nar
gyis byung / nam mkha' la phyag mdzub gtad nas bzhad cig mdzad nas/ khyod kyis e mthong gsungs/ bdag gis ma mthong shin tu sems dga' ba cig byung zhus pas/ sdig shas chung
bar 'dug ste/ 'on kyang sdig pa dri ma 'dra bas sdig sbyong gyis gsungs/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das seng ge'i khri la 'khor nyan thos dang bcas pa bzhugs pa'i snang ba
byung bas spos phul gsungs/ de nas spos phul/ bcu bzhi'i nyin par phyi dro gdugs la bzhugs pa'i dus su sprin sngar gyi de 'dra ba cig byung / dpal kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor
gsal por gzigs pas spos phul gsungs nas

spos phul/ bco lnga'i snga dro yang phyi na bzhugs pa'i dus su sprin sngar gyi de 'dra ba cig byung / 'jam dbyangs lan gsum gzigs/ yang spos phul/ spos lan gsum phul ba'i rting
ma nga la gzigs nas bzhad cig mdzad/ ci lags zhus pas/ 'jam dbyangs dang byams pa gnyis bgro gleng mdzad kyin 'dug gsungs/ de'i tshig kyang gsungs pas brjed/ de'i phyis
de nyin bskor ba mdzad dus su/ mchog sbyin dpal gyi bzhugs khri cog tse chung chung cig dang / bzhugs 'bol cig bzung nas sngon la 'gro/ bdag gi dpung pa g.yon la phyag
gis brten nas bzhugs/ mchod khang thad sor byon pa dang bzhugs khri de la bzhugs nas/ mchog sbyin dpal khyod ja skol du song gsungs/ bdag la khyod song la spos shig sbyor
la shog gsungs/ spos khyer yong ba dang a yu tA ra gsungs/ sgrol ma zhal gzigs par 'dug tshes bcu bdun gyi nam gung tsam la/ bdag drung na tsog ge yod pas gzims pa de
tsog ge bzhengs nas khyod kyis ci yang ma mthong ngam/ glu dbyangs rol mo'i sgra thos gsungs/ slob dpon jo gdan dang nged mang rab yod pas rol mo'i sgra thos/ gzhan ci yang
ma mthong zhus pas bdag la gzigs te/ bde mchog gis gtso byas pa'i dkyil 'khor bcu gsum gyi snang ba byung gsungs/ dpa' bo dang dpa' mo thams cad kyis glu dang gar mdzad
cing 'dug gsungs/ tshigs bcad mang po cig gsung ba bdag gis ma zin/ slob dpon jo gdan gyis mang rab cig zin snang ba 'dir ma bris/ gzhan la ma

bshad sdig pa gsog pa'i rgyu ru 'gro gsungs/ ju gur me mar na dge bshes rdo rang zer ba cig na gin yod pa/ bdag gi slob ma rin chen rgyal mtshan bltar btang bas/ bshang gci
thams cad mal du btang / g.yog po med/ sdug par snang ba'i lo rgyus zlo zhing snang ba dang / chos rje'i zhal nas/ sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyang
mkhyen bzhin du thugs rjes mi gzigs pa gsungs/ de'i nub mo tho rangs bla ma rje btsun pa dang / slob dpon birWa pa dang / nag po pa gsum byon nas khyod de la yi ma chad/
zag bcas kyi lus 'di la skye rga na 'chi'i chu bo bzhi yod pa yin gsungs/ birWa pas 'dzum pa mdzad/ nag po pas de yin gsungs/ birWa pas thod pa'i bdud rtsi la srin lag gis
reg nas khyod kyi ljags rkyongs gsungs nas/ ljags la thig le byas pa'i snang ba byung gsungs/ de'i dus su rtog pa dang rtog med mtha' las 'das pa/ bde gsal mi rtog pa rgyal
ba rnams kyi thugs la'ang 'di las lhag pa med snyam pa'i snang ba byung / de nas bla ma rje btsun pas 'di nas gzhan don la 'gro ba'i dus su/ shar phyogs kyi 'jig rten
gyi khams du ma brgal ba'i pha rol du mkha' la gnas pa'i rig pa 'dzin par gyur nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa du ma mnyes par byas shing / sangs rgyas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa
dang / sems can du ma yongs su smin par byas nas sa dang lam phal cher bgrod de/ skye ba gsum pa la 'dzam bu'i gling 'di nyid kyi rgya gar shar lho mu mu nir zhes bya bar
rgyal po nyi ma'i stobs 'phel zhes bya ba'i bur 'khrungs nas gzhon

nu la rtsom pa dang / 'chad pa mang po mdzad/ mngon par shes pas 'jig rten thams cad gzigs nas/ 'khor dad ldan 'bum phrag du ma grol bar byas nas/ de'i dus su ngas dbang bskur
ba dang chos 'brel byas pa tsam thams cad nga'i 'khor du 'ong bar 'dug gsungs pa'i tshig kyang yod/ sku tshe'i tshad kyang yod pa brjed zin/ de nas sku tshe 'phos nas
sangs rgyas dri ma med pa'i dpal zhes bya bar sku skye ba bzhes nas sems can gyi don mdzad par 'dug gsungs/ rje btsun pas birWa pa la de ltar lags sam gsungs/ slob dpon
gyis de yin gsungs/ nag po pas kyang de yin gsungs nas mthun 'gyur mdzad/ de nas bdag la tshogs kyi mchod pa shoms shig gsungs nas bsham mo/ /de nas zab mo'i lam la nan tan
du mdzad pa'i stobs kyis gsang ba'i gnas bltar mi mngon pa dang / dbu'i gtsug tor gsal por 'phags pa dang / smin mtshams kyi mdzod spu dung ltar 'khyil ba la sogs pa'i
sku yon tan dang ldan par gyur to/ /zla ba bcu gcig pa'i yar tshes bdun la sprul pa'i lha khang na 'tshogs tshad kyis thos pa'i sgra sna tshogs pa'i rol mo grag kho bos
rgyu mtshan ci lags zhus pas/ khyed thams cad gsol ba 'debs pa la brtson par gyis gsungs/ lam pha rol tu phyin pa'i lugs la mgo dang rkang lag bdog pa thams cad btang bas
kyang / dbang bskur ba mchog thob pa'i bla ma la mos gus dang zhabs tog skad cig tsam byas pa bsod nams che gsungs/ yod tshad bla ma rang la phul bas de'i dus bdag la

'bul rgyu med pas/ sngon gnas brtan rkang pa bcos pa'i yon du byin pa'i zhwa phrug gi phyam tshe dmar po so ma legs pa gcig yod pa de'i phud phul nas/ chos rje rang gis bsnams
nas yod pas/ de 'bul dgos snyam pa cig byung bas zhal 'dzum pa cig mdzad nas/ de nga la 'bul mi dgos de sngar ngas gyon pa de phul ba yin/ kho bos byang chub dam pa brnyes
pa'i dus su a ru ra lag mthil du bzhag pa bzhin du/ khyod slob ma rnams kyis zhabs tog ci byas pa thams cad gzigs pa yin/ de'i dbang bskur sems bskyed zhabs tog ci
byas pa thams cad dang / kho bo mthong zhing rjes su dran pa thams cad dang / reg pa dang / gtam byas pa dang / 'brel pa byas pa thams cad don med par mi 'gyur bar ngan 'gro'i
sdug bsngal las grol ba yin/ des na khyod kyang nga'i zhabs tog mang po byas pas dga' ba sgoms shig gsungs/ bdag gis nub gcig srod nas tho rangs kyi cha tshun chad
la res sku'i rgyab nas brten/ res sku sta zur nas brten pas/ 'dul ba rgyal mtshan la shog gsungs nas/ dpon mo zo rog tas phul ba'i phyam tshe de khyer la shog gsungs nas/
bdag la 'di khyod gon/ 'u cag gnyis tshe snga ma nas 'brel pa mang po yod pa yin gsungs/ khyod dang po nga'i ja 'dren pa byas/ de nas mi nyag 'ga' ru jo 'bum gug shrI'i
rtsar brdzangs/ der hor gyi ded pa la ma shi bas da lta nga'i zhabs tog mang du byas/ phyi ma la nga'i drung du mi skye kha med yin gsungs/ smal po zla ba'i yar tshes bcu
bzhi'i tho rangs kyi cha la sna tshogs rgyal mtshan dang / rol

mo'i sgra dang / glu mchod pa sna tshogs dang / sa g.yo ba dang bcas pas zhi bar gshegs pa gyur to/ /nyi shu lnga'i nyin par gdung bzhus pa'i dud pa thams cad kyang 'ja'i rnam
par gyur/ rol mo'i sgra mang po yang skye bo'i tshogs thams cad kyis thos so/ /gdung yang phal che ba ring bsrel dang lha sku sogs rang byon bsam gyis mi khyab par gyur
te/ sems can gyi don mdzad pa ni yar lung pa grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i rnam thar bstod pa las/ gtsug tor mchog dbus kye yi rdo rje dang / /'jam pa'i dbyangs
sku dri med gsal bar byon/ /dpral ba'i dbyings su 'khor lo sdom pa'i tshogs/ /ltag pa'i cha la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das/ /phrag pa'i gdung la kha sar pA Ni dang / /rkang
gi sbubs su spyan ras gzigs dbang dang / /sgal bu'i cha la gsang ba'i yum bzhi byon/ /sgrol ma mi g.yo pus gtsug rnam pa gnyis/ /phyag sor g.yas pa klu shing ljon pa'i
steng / /byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo'i phyag rgya can/ /sprul pa rnam bcu sku yi rten du byon/ /tshangs pa'i gsung dbyangs stong nyid seng ge'i sgra/ /skye med don ston
a yig 'bur du dod/ /snyan gong gnyis la rnam rgyal mchod rten re/ /dam tshig rdo rje lta bar hU~M gis mtshan/ /thugs dgongs rnam dag rang byung chos skur shar/ /gzhan yang
ring bsrel sna tshogs dpag med byon/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar yin no/ /bdag nyid chen po 'di'i gdan sa che 'bring chung gsum las/ che ba dpal ldan sa skya/ byang phyogs ling
chu rtser khab/ bar pa bsam yas/ nyang stod rkyang

thur/ shangs sreg shing / chung ba khams gtsang dbus gsum na shin tu mang ba'i bdag gnyer mdzad nas/ spyir mdo sngags/ khyad par rnam 'grel sogs mtshan nyid kyi bshad srol
la chos rje pa 'di kho nas 'phrin las kyi rgyun bzang ba yin te/ zhal bzhugs pa'i dus kyang hor yul la 'byon pa'i tshe/ sa skyar mtshan nyid tshogs dpon 'u yug pa rig pa'i
seng ge sngags kyi tshogs dpon zhang btsun mdo sde dpal/ spyi dpon nye gnas su dge bshes shAkya bzang po bskos nas byon pas/ sa skyar rigs chen pa rang la yang cha brgyad
cu tsam byung bar grags pa dang / chos rje nyid mya ngan las 'das pa'i rjes su yang tshad ma sogs rang gi mtshan nyid kyi grub mtha' srol 'dzin gyi grangs 'phel ba yang
/ nA lendra/ gser mdog can/ skyid tshal/ thub bstan rnam rgyal/ thub bstan yangs can/ dbus rtses thang / byang ngam ring / dpal sa skya'i thub bstan lha chen sogs shin
tu dar rgyas su gyur pa dang / de bzhin du sngags phyogs kyi rang gi grub mtha' srol 'dzin gyi dgon gnas kyang che phran mang po zhig 'phel rgyas su gyur pa 'di ni/ gzhan
las rmad du byung ba'i rnam par thar pa ste/ rtsod dus gdul bya nyams dma' ba'i dus su 'phrin las rnam dag gi rgyun tshugs pa rnam thar gyi mchog yin gyi/ nyid kyis sangs
rgyas byang sems mang po gzigs pa sogs ni byis pa mtshar bskyed du zad do zhes mkhas pa rnams kyi gsung rab las 'byung ba bzhin don la gnas par shes par bya'o/ /'dir smras
pa/ de ltar gnas lnga rigs pa chos kyi rje/ /thub dbang gnyis pa

sa skya paN chen gyi/ /rnam thar cha shas mthong bas kho bo cag /gzhon nu'i tshe na'ang mi phyed dad pa thob/ /grangs med skye bar sbyangs pa'i paNDi ta/ /shes bya ma lus gzigs
pa'i thams cad mkhyen/ /da lta dri med dpal du sangs rgyas pa'i/ /don gnyis mthar phyin de la skyabs su mchi/ /khyed kyi mkhyen pas 'jam dbyangs zil gnon zhing / /brtse
bas rgyal sras khyod kyi dgung gi lo/ /mtha' ru son kyang bod khams bde ba'i thabs/ /gcig tu dgongs nas hor gyi rgyal khams byon/ /gang gi nus pas rje btsun sa skya pa'i/
/bstan pas 'dzam gling khyab 'di ma legs sam/ /de 'dra'i bka' drin gzhal du med pa'i tshul/ /sngon byon skyes bu kun gyi thugs la gsal/ /kye ma deng sang dus ngan skabs
'di na/ /de 'dra'i tshul lugs ji bzhin ma rig pas/ /gang gi grub mtha' rtsod bral khungs thub las/ /gsar byung 'ga' zhig mchog tu 'dzin 'di mtshar/ /kyi hud chos nyams
med pa'i blun po rnams/ /dregs pa'i rjes su 'brangs pa dngos po'i gshis/ /de phyir bdag gi bstan pa spel ba'i grogs/ /chos rje chos kyi rgyal pos dbyings nas mdzod/ /ces
pa 'di yang rang babs su byung ba'i gsol 'debs lags so/ /de lta bu'i bla ma de'i gcung bsod nams rgyal mtshan ni/ yab dgung lo so lnga pa/ yum nyer gsum ma shing pho 'brug
gi lo la skya'o kha gdangs su 'khrungs/ yab mes kyi chos mtha' dag la sbyangs/ kye rdo rje dang phur pa gnyis la thugs dam gyi mthil mdzad/ chos skyong lcam dral 'khor
bcas bran du 'khol

zhing / mdzad pa'i 'phrin las kyang dbu rtse rnying ma bzhengs pa dang / dgon pa la lcags ri mdzad/ de'i dus su mon grog 'bal grog sa dkar logs rnams rgyab yol du tshud pa'i
lcags ri mdzad gsungs pa la/ bgres po kun gyis zhus pas/ zhing mo che nas rgyab pas mda' rgyang gang gis lcags ri 'di mdzad/ zi thang sogs su tshong 'dus dang mi dmangs
kyi grong 'dzugs pa/ grom stod/ grom smad/ stag thog mang mkhar dril chen/ gtsang bar phug shab stod smad/ rta nag sogs su gzhis 'dings pa/ byang gcung / khab so/ kom 'dre/
gar phug sogs su 'brog sde mang du 'cha' ba/ ra sa sogs su rta khyu 'cha' ba/ bstan 'dzin du ma bsten nas zhabs tog 'tsho sbyor mdzad pa/ sku gsung thugs kyi rten bzhengs
pa/ mchod pa rgyun par 'bul ba/ bla ma gong ma'i dus mchod kyi rgyun 'dzugs pa sogs tshad med pa mdzad/ phyi ma'i skye ba gzigs pa'i mngon shes kyang mnga' ste/ mya
ngan las 'da' ba'i dus su da skye ba phyi ma la lho phyogs kyi rgyud du spang ri chen po cig gi 'dabs su gdul bya 'ga' re la dbang bskur zhing / sbas pa'i rnal 'byor gyi
lam zab mo nyams su len pa gcig tu skye bar 'dug gsungs shing / 'di na bza' brag phug pa yin pa'i snyan brgyud kyang yod la/ de lta bu'i bla ma de dgung lo nga drug bzhes
pas sa mo phag rgyal gyi zla ba'i nyi shu gnyis la dag pa'i snang ba mang po gzigs shing / bla ma dang yi dam dbyer med pa'i dgongs pa mdzad nas/ khyed rnams chos rje pa
'di sangs rgyas dngos su 'dug pas the tshom ma byed par

mos gus gyis gsungs te/ la stod byang gi mdog stod ros kyi dpal rir sku gshegs so/ /nga'i rus pa 'di pha gi shod kyi steng der sregs shig nga'i bu tsha brgyud kyis rgyal khams
dbang du 'du pa'i rten 'brel yod gsungs nas de bzhin du byas so/ /kha cig na re/ zangs tsha'i yum yul rta re rong / brgyud bzang ba/ pha ming zangs kyi jo sras/ de la
sras gcung zangs tsha bsod nams rgyal mtshan 'khrungs pa yin pas chos rje sku mched yum gcig par 'dod pa ni nor ba ste/ chos rje ni zangs tsha ma yin pa'i phyir zer kyang
/ rje btsun gyis ga ring rgyal po la rtsis bsdur du btang ba'i yi ge las/ yum tha dad ma gsungs pas/ yum gcig pa nyid don la gnas pa yin no/ /bla ma des btsun mo lnga khab
tu bzhes pa'i dang po de yul mdog gi tsha sna'i 'dab/ pha ming zur khang gi brgya tsho/ zhang rgyal ba dpal/ ming ma gcig kun skyid/ de la sras gcen 'gro ba'i mgon po
chos rgyal 'phags pa/ yab dgung lo nga gnyis bzhes pa shing mo lug gi lo zla ba gsum pa'i tshes drug la g.yas ru ngam ring gi klu khung du sku 'khrungs/ yum gyi lhums su
zhugs pa dang bltams pa'i dus su ngo mtshar gyi ltas dang bcas shing / chung ngu nas 'bri klog la sogs pa rig pa'i gnas lnga 'ga' zhig ma bslabs par mkhyen/ 'ga' zhig dka'
tshegs med par mkhyen/ sngon gyi gnas dran pa'i mngon shes kyang mnga' ste/ 'di'i snga ma'i skye ba spyan ras gzigs dang gsung gleng mdzad par grags pa'i sa ston ri pa
yin zer bas de brtag pa'i phyir du/ sa ston ri

pa'i slob ma gnyis kyis bltar 'ong ba dang / bla ma 'di byis pa'i khrod na rtse zhing bzhugs pas mkhyen nas khyed 'ong ngam gsungs pas/ khong gnyis pos khyed kyis ngo mkhyen
nam zhus pas shes te/ nga'i slob ma 'di dang 'di'o zhes gsungs pas dad nas lus thams cad kyis 'dud par gyur to/ /de ltar 'ong ba'i rgyu mtshan ni/ de yang yab zangs tshas
tshogs bdag bsgrubs pas/ tshogs bdag gi glang po che'i sna rtser 'khur nas ri rab kyi rtser bskyal te ltos shig zer bas/ zangs tsha skrag nas ring zhig blta ba'i nus pa
ma byung / de nas dbus gtsang khams gsum sogs bod kyi gzhung tal tsam cig gzigs pas/ khyod rang gis gang mthong dbang du 'du ba yin pa la/ dbus gtsang khams gsum sogs khyod
kyi bu'am tsha brgyud kyi dbang du 'du ba cig 'byung / myur du ma mthong bas khyod rang la ni dbang thang med zer/ de nas kyang zangs tsha la sras yun ring du ma byung
bas thugs zid thung nas/ tshogs bdag gnad la dbab pa'i sbyor ba mdzad pas/ skabs shig gi tshe gung thang du sa ston ri pa'i rtsar tshogs bdag byung nas/ zangs tshas nga
la dbus gtsang khams gsum 'du ba gcig dgos zer nas rgyab tshags mig ltar song song bskul ba yin pas/ khong rang la ni dbang rigs mi 'dug kho'i bur skye ba la byang chub
sems dpa' srid pa tha ma yin pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya chen po dbang du 'du ba'i smon lam btab pa zhig dgos rgyu la/ khyed la de tshang nas 'dug pas/ zangs tsha'i bur
khyed kyi skye ba bzhes na dbus gtsang khams gsum sogs bod yul phal cher

dbang du 'du ba 'dug pas bsam bzhin skye ba blang dgos zer nas de bzhin mdzad pa yin la/ de nas re zhig na chos rje'i chag phyir skyid grong du byon pa'i tshe glang ri pa'i
dge 'dun rnams kyis mjal ba dang / btsun pa bgres po cig la nga'i nye gnas bkra shis don grub byung gsungs pas/ des kyang bla mar shes zhabs la 'jus te mchi ma phyung ngo
zhes grags so/ /de nas dgung lo gsum pa la sgrub thabs mtsho skyes la sogs pa thugs las gsungs pas kun gyis ya mtshan du 'dzin te 'di ni nges par 'phags pa'o zhes phyogs
kun tu grags pas de phyin chad 'phags pa zhes mtshan yongs su grags so/ /brgyad pa la skyes rabs thugs las gsungs/ dgu pa la chos rje pa'i sngon 'gro'i chos 'khor mdzad
dus brtag gnyis gsungs/ tshogs kyi gtam bshad mdzad pas thams cad ngo mtshar te mkhas pa thams cad kyi nga rgyal bcag cing snyan pas khyab par mdzad par gyur to/ /bcu pa
la rje'i chag phyir byang ngos su byon pa'i lam du dbus su chos rje pas mkhan po zul phu ba'i na bza' 'phred gsol gyi slob dpon mdzad nas rab tu byung / skyor mo lung pa'i
