mkhan po shes rab sengge la dge tshul gyi bslab bya gsan/ de nas bcu bdun pa la chos rje pa la mnga' ba'i yon tan thams cad rdzogs pas chos rje pa thugs shin tu mnyes
te/ bstan pa'i khur bzod par dgongs nas chos dung dang lhung bzed la sogs pa gnang / slob ma'i tshogs rnams gtad nas bstan pa'i bya ba dang sems can mang po'i don bya ba'i
dus la babs pas sngon gyi dam bcas pa dran

par gyis shig pa'i bka' bsgos nas bstan pa gtad do/ /de nas glang lo la se chen gan gyis gdan drangs pa nas pho brang du byon te/ rgyal pos gzhan gyis dris pa'i lan ma thebs
pa'i the tshom mang po dris pa'i lan rgyu mtshan dang bcas pa gsungs pas mnyes pa yin te/ de yang rgyal pos khyed bod kyi yul na mi che ba su 'dra byung gsungs pa la/ 'phags
pa rin po che'i zhal nas/ nged bod kyi yul du mi che ba chos rgyal mes dbon rnam gsum byon pa lags gsungs pas/ de gsum mi che ba'i rgyu mtshan ci yin gsungs pa la/
srong btsan sgam po thugs rje chen po'i sprul pa/ khri srong lde'u btsan 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul pa/ khri ral pa can phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa lags pas mi che ba lags zhus
pas/ khyed bod yul du pho rgod pa su byung gsungs pa la/ pho rgod po mi la ras pa zhes bya ba byung gsungs pas de ci yin gsungs/ tshe stod la dgra brtul/ tshe gzhug la
chos byas grub pa thob pa lags zhus pas/ khyod kyi yul du mi yon tan che ba su byung gsungs pa la/ yon tan che ba bdag gi bla ma rje sa skya pa lta bu byung zhus pas/ bla
ma chos rje pa'i mkhyen pa de ci tsam yin/ de la khyed rang gis ci tsam bslab gsungs pas/ bla ma chos rje pa'i mkhyen pa de rgya mtsho dang 'dra/ de nas bdag gis chu phul
gang blangs pa tsam bslab zhus so/ /de nas rgyal po'i zhal nas bod la dmag khral 'gel ba dang / nor sdud la gtong gsungs pa la/ rgyal po la 'phags pa rin po ches zhu ba
tshan cher zhu bar mdzad de/ bod mtha' khob yul chung / sa rgya dang 'byor pa med pas dmag mi

thegs pa zhu ba zhus na'ang rgyal pos ma gnang bar/ dgongs pa ma 'grub par thugs ma bde nas/ de ltar na bod kyi bande 'dir 'ongs nas bsdad pa la dgos pa mi 'dug pas rang yul
la 'gro bar zhu zhus pas/ 'o na byon pas chog ces rgyal pos gsungs pa la/ dpon mo cha bus rgyal po la 'di 'dra'i bande dkon/ sngar gyi tshal pa la sogs pa'i bande rgan
po 'di rnams la 'di'i yon tan gyi cha shas sngon gyi gtam rgyus tsam yang mi 'dug pas bod la ma btang bar/ da dung yon mchod gsung gleng dang chos kyi dri ba 'dra mdzad na
zhus par/ rgyal pos gsan nas yon mchod gsung gleng mang du mdzad pa'i dus su/ 'phags pas thugs rgyal che ba ltar mdzad pa las/ rgyal pos khyed de tsam du nga rgyal che
ba ci yin/ khyed la gong ci yod gsungs pa las/ 'phags pas de la lan du nged la gshed ci yang med/ nged sngon nas rgya mi nyag rgya gar/ mon/ bod rgyal po la sogs pa'i bla
mchod byas pas zhu ba dpangs mtho tsam byung ba yin zhus pas/ rgyal po na re/ bod kyi rgyal po nam byas/ rgyal po su yis bkur zhing dbang su yis zhus/ bande bod dang mi
mthun pa'i brdzun zer ba cig 'dug gsungs pa la/ 'phags pas bod kyi rgyal po byas rgya dang dmag 'thab pas/ bod rgyal bas 'dzam bu gling gi sum gnyis 'og tu chug der rjes
rgya bod gnyen byas/ kong jo dang yi dam jo bo byon tshul rnams zhus pas/ de bzhin bden na rgyal thogs med na yi ger bris yod pas ltos gsungs pas/ rgya'i sngon gyi yig tshangs
rnams la

bltas pas/ 'phags pas ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin byung bas rgyal po thugs dgyes/ de nas 'phags pas der yang ma zad pa'i snga rol lo bye ba'i gong du 'dzam bu gling du khrag gi
char pa zhag bdun babs yod gsungs pas/ rgya'i yig tshangs na btab 'dug pas rgyal po shin tu yid ches shing / yang 'phags pas spyir nged kyi pha mes la mi nyag rgyal pos
gos chen gyi bla bre sha ba'i rwa co nas bzung thub pa phul yod gsungs pas/ rgyal pos sa skyar bltar btang bas 'dug zer bas rgyal po yab sras mos par gyur to/ /de nas dpon
mos rgyal po la 'phags pa bod la ma btang bas legs 'dug sa skya pa la gsang sngags zab mo'i dbang bskur gzhan la med pa'i khyad chos cig yod par 'dug de zhus pa 'thad zhus
pas/ rgyal po na re sngon la khyod kyis zhus/ a'u tse ba 'dug na nga yang zhu gsungs pas/ dpon mos kye rdo rje'i dbang zhus shin tu mos par gyur/ de'i dus su dpon mos
dbang yon ci 'tshal zhus pas/ 'phags pa'i zhal nas/ rang gi lus longs spyod kha rje dbang thang thams cad 'bul ba yin/ khyad par rang gang la chags shing gtsigs che ba de
'bul ba yin gsungs pas/ btsun mos nga khyo sa la yong dus pha mas byin pa'i gtsigs che shos yin zer nas rna rgyan gyi steng na mu tig rdog po cig 'dug pa de phul bas/ sog
po gcig la btsongs pas gser bre chen gang dang / dngul bre chen stong byung bas yar slebs/ gtsang chu mig gi chos 'khor dang sa skya'i gser thog chen mo'i gzhi byas zer/
de nas rgyal po la dpon mos/ chos gzhan las

khyad par 'phags pa cig 'dug pas gsan pa drag zhus pas/ rgyal pos de bzhin byed gsungs nas bla ma la zhus pas/ /spyir yang khyed kyis chos zhu ba'i dam tshig mi thub cing /
da res lo tsA ba mkhas pa'ang med pas phyis byed par zhu gsungs pas/ rgyal po na re/ dam tshig ci bsrung dgos gsungs pas/ dbang bskur zhus nas bla ma gral mgor bzhugs/ lus
kyis phyag 'tshal/ ngag gis ci gsungs nyan/ yid kyis thugs dang ma 'gal ba bya dgos pa yin/ de mi yong gsungs pas/ dpon mos 'chams pa zhus pa la chos zhu ba dang / mi
nyung dus bla ma gung la bzhugs/ rgyal brgyud/ mag pa/ mi dpon/ mi dmangs tshogs dus mi gnon dgos pas rgyal po gung la bzhugs/ bod phyogs kyi bya ba la bla ma ci gsung dang
du long / bla ma la ma zhus par rgyal pos lung mi gnang / bya ba che chung gzhan la bla ma snying rje che bas zhu ngo 'chol du 'ong na rgyal khams mi non pas/ bla ma'i
gsung dang zhal 'jug ma mdzad ces zhus pas/ bla ma'i gsung gis/ de ltar gyi tshe na khyed hor la gshed mong yun du ma 'thab pa'i gog sa chen po la mi 'jug pa bzhin/ nged
kyang bsnyen sgrub ma byas par dbang bskur na mi yong bas/ bsnyen sgrub kyi grabs kyis gsungs nas/ bsnyen sgrub kyi bar la lo tsA ba gser yig pas mgyogs par bos nas/ rgyal
pos dbu mdzad pa'i dbang pa nyi shu rtsa lnga la lan gsum gyi bar du sa skya pa'i khyad chos dpal kye rdo rje'i dbang yongs su rdzogs par bskur ba las/ hor gyi rgyal khams
su rdo rje

theg pa'i dbu bsnyes pa yin zhing / de'i dbang yon dang po la khri skor bcu gsum phul ba yin par bshad pas/ de yang khri skor re la lha sde bzhi stong dang / mi sde drug stong
yong ba yin no/ /dbang yon bar ma la chos dung dkar po rgyang grags kyis gtsos pa'i bod phyogs kha gsum gyi bande dang / mi sde sogs thams cad phul ba yin pas phyogs
kha gsum la zhing gcig tu brtsis pa yin par bshad de/ /de yang stod mnga' ris skor gsum nas sog la skya bo yan dam pa chos kyi phyogs kha/ sog la skya bo man nas rma chu
khug pa yan mgo nag mi'i phyogs kha/ rma chu khug pa man nas rgya mchod rten dkar po yan chad gyad gling rta'i phyogs kha zhes grags shing / zhing zhes pa'i tha snyad kyang
khang pa ka ba drug gi sa yod pa/ mi bza' mi gnyis/ bu pho mo gnyis/ g.yog pho mo gnyis te drug phyugs rta bong gnyis/ ba glang ra lug rnams dang / zhing hor son khal
bcu gnyis kyi sa yod pa rnams la hor dud chung gcig zer ba yin te/ de 'dra nyi shu rtsa lnga la dud chen gcig de gnyis la rta mgo gcig zer/ de gnyis la brgya skor gcig de
bcu la stong skor gcig de bcu la khri skor gcig de bcu la klu gcig de bcu la zhing gcig zhes bya ba yin cing / hor se chen rgyal po'i mnga' 'og tu zhing bcu gcig yod cing
/ phyogs kha gsum la zhing gcig cung ma longs kyang / bla ma bzhugs sa yin pa dang bstan pa dar sa yin pa nas zhing gcig tu brtsis nas phul ba yin no/ /dbang yon rting
ma la bla ma'i bka' bzhin rgya'i mi yur chen po phul bas shin tu mnyes nas/ bla ma

'phags pas bsngo ba 'di ltar mdzad de/ nam mkha'i khams ni khrag gi mdog ltar dmar/ /rkang leb ro yis phyi yi rgya mtsho khengs/ /'di 'dra bcad pa'i dge ba gang de yis/ /mkhyen
rab dbang phyug thugs dgongs rdzogs pa'i phyir/ /phan bde'i bstan pa rab tu rgyas pa dang / /mi dbang sku tshe yun du brtan phyir bsngo/ /zhes gsungs pa yin zhing /
der skabs dbang yon bar ma'i skabs su phul ba'i chos dung dkar po rgyang grags kyi lo rgyus ni/ dpal ldan sa skya la bsngags pa snyan ngag dbang po'i nyer mtsho las/ klu
dbang dbang po'i dpal yon las 'ongs pa'i/ /dung dkar dkar po rgyang grags tshangs dbyangs can/ /thub dbang dbang pos chos 'khor bskor ba'i tshe/ /lha dbang dbang pos phul
te 'di legs drangs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyis chos 'khor bskor ba'i dus kyi chos dung 'khrul med byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar ba
'di nyid ni/ sa skya pa'i phyag tu rgya nag nas 'byung ba'i gong rol du rgya nag tu byung tshul ji ltar yin zhe na/ rgya gar rgyal po dharmA pha la dang / rgya nag rgyal
po de wa rA dza gnyis mthong ma myong 'phrad ma myong ba'i grogs po byas te/ rgya gar rgyal po dharmA pha la'i ring la mu stegs pa'i dmag gis shrI nA lendra bcom/ bstan pa
bsnub pa'i dus su rgya nag rgyal po de wa rA dza la dpung grogs dgos pa'i 'phrin bskur bas/ nged kyi dmag mi thon/ skyel gyi nor rdzas bzang po bskur gyis de la brten nas
phyi pa thul/ bstan pa ma 'grib pa gyis shig zer nas/ gos lu hang gi ber srub

med pa ri mos spras shing sra ba/ mtshon dang gzong gis mi phigs pa/ thugs ka ru nor bu dpal be'u phung phung yong ba cig gis mgo byas skyel bzang po thang gnyis bskur/ gros
dang bslab bya legs par byas btang ba'i mthu dang rten 'brel 'grig pas mu stegs pa'i dpung tshogs pham par byas te/ nang pa'i bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal bar byung bas/
rgya gar rgyal blon thams cad dga' bar gyur te/ 'di lta bu'i bstan pa 'byung pa 'di rgya nag rgyal po khyed kyis sems brtse ba'i bslab bya dang / skyel bzang po rim par bskur
byung ba'i stobs dang nus pa yin pas khyed drin che ba yod/ skyel lan la ci 'dod pa bskur bas lan srings shig byas pas/ rgya nag rgyal po na re/ khyed de ltar sems na
sangs rgyas dgung lo brgyad pa'i sku tshad dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos dung / chu klung gi mdo/ rgyan stug po bkod pa'i mdo/ 'dul ba ko sha dang / za ma tog bkod pa'i mdo
dang bzhi/ dge slong sdom brtson ldan pa bzhi sde dang bcas pa bskur cig zer byung ba nas/ rgyal po dharmA pha la na re/ nged kyi yi dam gyi lha shAkya mu ne sogs gzhan
du 'byon pa sems kyis thong ba med na'ang khyed drin che ba yin pas gdan drongs la 'gro ba mang po'i don rgyas par mdzod cig gsungs nas mchod rdzas kyi bye brag du ma dang
/ skyel bsu'i bshom rgyas par byas nas jo bo dang chos dung 'di nyid sogs rgya nag tu spyan drangs pa yin cing / rgya nag nas sa skya pa'i phyag tu byung tshul ni/ gong
du brjod pa bzhin chos rgyal 'phags pa la se chen gyis phul ba nyid yongs grags yin mod kyang / yang

lugs gcig la chos kyi rje sa skya paNDi ta la rgyal po go dan gyis phul/ sa paN gyis 'phags pa la gnang bar bshad pa'i lugs gcig kyang 'dug cing / gang ltar sa paN gyi chos
dung kyang yin te/ hor gyi yul skad rigs mi gcig pa'i rgyal khams du ma sangs rgyas kyi bstan pas khyab par mdzad cing / chos 'khor bsam gyis mi khyab pa bskor ba'i dus
kyi chos dung yin par gsungs pas so/ /de lta bu'i yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos dung khyad par du 'phags pa 'di ni dpal ldan sa skya nyid du 'gro ba'i mgon
po chos rgyal 'phags pa rgya nag nas phebs dus bsnams nas 'gro ba ma lus pa'i skyabs mgon dam par bzhugs su gsol ba yin no/ /chos dung 'di lta bu'i che ba'i yon tan ni
zhib par brjod kyis ga la lang / rags pa tsam brjod na/ gdul bya snod ldan gyis bltas pa de'i tshe 'di nyid la rnam bcu dbang ldan la sogs pa khyad par du 'phags pa'i rang
byon bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod cing / 'di'i gsung thos pa tsam gyis bskal pa bye ba dpag tu med pa nas bsags pa'i sdig sgrib 'dag cing / ngan song du skye ba'i sgo bkag
ste/ mtho ris dang thar pa'i bde ba la 'god par mdzad cing / gzhan yang sems can la bde skyid 'byung ba'i 'bru'i tshogs rnams la sde brgyad gdug pa can rnams kyis mtho 'tshams
pa'i ser ba la sogs pa byung tshe/ 'di'i gsung thos pa tsam gyis de ma thag tu rang zhi la 'gro ba dang / sa'i bcud 'phel te sems can la bde skyid phun sum tshogs
pa 'byung ba yin no/ /bar skabs su sngags

'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyi sku ring la bstan dgra lha sa rdzong pa sogs bdud sprul 'ga' zhig gis byed pas lha khang chen mo la bslus rgyab/ mchod
rdzas bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang chos dung 'di nyid sogs khyer dus/ sdig spyod kyi yul der bzhugs pa'i gnas ma yin pa dang / slar yang rnal 'byor dbang phyug gis byin
gyis brlabs pa'i gnas gdan sa chen po 'dir 'byon par dgongs te/ chos dung gi nang thams cad 'bus gang ba dang / mchod pa'i gral la bzhag pas 'bud mkhan med par mi shis
pa'i rtags mtshan gyis rang skad 'don pa sogs mngon sum du mi dge ba'i ltas sna tshogs bstan pa la brten nas/ de 'phral nyid du gdan sa chen po 'di nyid du bshags pa dang
bcas te phul ba yin zhing / 'di lta bu'i chos dung 'di ni dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i yid bzhin gyi nor bu dang khyad par med de/ 'di'i drung du gnas skabs dang / mthar thug gi
'dod pa'i 'bras bu 'byung ba'i smon lam ci btab pa rnams gang yid la bsam pa'i don rnams thogs pa med par stsol bar mdzad pa myong grub yin no/ /de ltar chos kyi rgyal
po 'phags pa rin po che de nyid rgyal po chen po'i ti shrIr gyur pa'i rjes su/ skyes mchog karma pakShi chen pos rdzu 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan pa'i dus su/ rang
re'i bla ma chen po de bzhin gshegs pa snang ba mtha' yas gnyis snang mi'i gzugs su byon pa la/ rdzu 'phrul che chung gi dbye ba med na'ang 'phral snang gi rdzu 'phrul dang
rtog pa rtogs ldan rgya bo 'di rang mtho ba 'dug ces se chen gyi btsun mo

blon po sogs kyis 'khor gyi nang du gsungs pa'i rkyen byas/ btsun mo cha bu des bla ma de nyid la mi phyed pa'i dad pa dang / sa skya pa'i bstan pa la gus zhen gzhan las mchog
tu che ba zhig yod 'dug pas 'phags pa rin po che'i spyan sngar byon te/ sngar gyi rgyal blon rnams kyi gnas tshul rnams snyan du gsol nas/ bla mas kyang dad pa chen po'i
gzhi mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul ma bstan na/ rgyal po'i re ba yang mi khengs shing thugs la 'gyur ba yang byung dogs 'dug ces gsol ba btab pas/ chos kyi rgyal po'i zhal
snga nas/ pakShi chen po rdzu 'phrul spyir gdul bya dus la babs pa dang / lhag par khong gi rdzu 'phrul yang don la nged kyi yin/ 'on kyang rgyal po dad pa dang dam tshig
can gyi sems kyi re ba ma khengs na mi nyan zhing / rdo rje theg pa'i gzhung las kyang nyes pa che bar bshad pas na/ nged kyis kyang de lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul bstan chog
pas/ btsun mo rang ral gri rnon po cig khyer shog gsungs nas/ gri phul bas/ nged kyi yan lag rnams rgyal ba rigs lngar byin gyis rlobs pas/ khyed rang rgyal blon rnams kyang
rigs lnga'i zhing khams gang mos su skye bar gsol ba thob dang yid ches pa'i phyir du gzims khri'i nang na yang lus ril bur yod pas/ de la mjal ba mdzod gsungs pa'i
bka' gnang ste/ de bzhin du dbu rnam par snang mdzad/ phyag zhabs bzhi rigs bzhir byin gyis brlabs te rgyal ba rigs lnga la/ rgyal po btsun mo blon po'i bka' 'khor dang bcas
pas lus kyis phyag dang bskor ba/ yid kyis smon lam gya nom pa btab ste

sku gzugs bum la mjal bas gzims khri'i nang na mtshal khrag gi sa cung zad tshos pa rgyal blon rnams kyis mthong ba dang / bzod glags med par skad shugs chen pos gsol ba btab
kyang / rgyun ring por rdzu 'phrul bstan pa ma bshig par/ de nas btsun mo cha bus 'jig rten gyi mgon po da myur du rdzu 'phrul shig cig ma yin na rgyal po snying gas nas
'chi ba 'dug go zhes gsol ba btab pas rdzu 'phrul de las bzhengs/ de phyin rgyal po'i spyan sngar mkhas grub du ma zhig byon nas mtha' yas pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi sgo bstan
kyang / 'gro ba'i don du 'di lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul ngo mtshar snyam pa ma gtogs/ spangs rtogs kyi yon tan nged kyi bla ma'i gong du 'gro ba 'dug bsam pa cung zad tsam yang
thugs la ma shar ba yin ces kyang grags so/ /de ltar na chos rgyal 'phags pa dgung lo bcu dgu pa chu mo glang gi lo gsar la se chen gan gyis dbang zhus/ ti shrI'i mtshan
gsol/ g.yang kri'u las byas pa'i ri mo la yi ge sa dang rin po che yod pa'i dam kha phul/ gzhan yang gser dang mu tig gi snam sbyar/ sku chos/ phyam tshe/ dbu zhwa/ chag
lhwam/ bzhugs gdan/ gser gyi khri/ gdugs/ gsol zhal/ gsol sder la sogs pa tshang ma rnga mo dang chibs dre'u/ gser gyi sga 'khor tshang ma/ khyad par gong du bshad pa'i
khri skor dang / chos dung sogs dbang yon gyi gtso bo rnams phul ba yin no/ /de'i phyi lo stag lo de la bande shed bskyed bod yig tu bris pa dang / dngul bre chen lnga
bcu rtsa drug ja sigs nyis brgya/ gos yug brgyad cu dang / dar yug stong dang brgya phul

lo/ /de dus chos rgyal 'phags pas bka' gnang nas/ bande'i khang par gser yig pas 'tsher mi 'bab pa dang / 'u lag mi bskul ba dang / khral mi 'ded pa rnams ji ltar dgongs pa
la bzhed pa ltar rgyal pos zhal gyis bzhes shing / gzhan yang rgyal po'i lung gis/ nyi ma nub kyi bande rnams ji ltar bya ba'i mgo lung sa skya pa shes su chug bya ba'i
lung gnang zhing / yang rgyal po'i gsung gis bod thams cad la sa skya pa'i chos lugs las gzhan byed dbang med pa'i lung 'bud gsungs pa la/ chos rgyal 'phags pas rang rang
gi chos lugs gang yong skyong du 'jug pa cis kyang dgos gsungs nas/ yon mchod gnyis ka'i 'ja' sa thams cad la rang rang gi chos lugs la 'bad pa thon gsungs pa sha stag yod
pas/ de ltar na mchod yon gnyis ka dbang spus bzang zhing thugs rje shin tu che ba yin la/ de ltar chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po ches gzhal du med pa'i bka' drin
gyis 'dzam bu'i gling byang phyogs 'di nyid rdzogs ldan gyi bde ba la 'god par mdzad pa'i bka' drin shes pa'i ched du hor gyis phul ba'i 'ja' sa mu tig ma dang / bande shed
bskyed ma'am/ 'ja' sa bod yig mar grags pa gnyis 'dir bri bar bya ste/ de yang 'ja' sa mu tig ma las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ tshe ring gnam gyi shed mong las/ bsod nams chen
po'i dpal la brten nas/ rgyal po nged kyi lung / dge 'dun rnams dang / mi sde mang po la zlo ba/ 'jig rten 'di'i phun sum tshogs pa/ jim gir rgyal po'i khrims lugs bzhin
spyad na 'byung

yang / phyi ma phan chod chos kyi lugs la brten dgos par gnang ba'i don la legs par brtags nas/ sangs rgyas shAkya mu ne'i lam 'di yang dag par mthong zhing / de yang rang
gis legs par rtogs nas gzhan la phyin ci ma log par ston pa slob dpon 'phags par 'dug pa'i don la dbang bskur ba zhus shing / gug shrI'i las ka phul nas/ dge 'dun 'dus pa
thams cad kyi mgon gnyer la bskos pa yin pas/ slob dpon gyis kyang spyir sangs rgyas bstan pa'i zhabs tog dang / dge 'dun gyi mgon gnyer dang / chos bshad pa dang / nyan
pa dang / sgrub pa'i mgo lung legs par gyis/ dge 'dun rnams kyis kyang / slob dpon gyi lung las log pa ma byed par/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i rtsa ba yin pas/ chos kyi
lugs legs par shes pa rnams kyis shod/ gzhon pa blo brtan pa rnams kyis slob/ chos kyi don legs par shes pa dang / bshad nyan mi nus pa rnams kyis tshul bzhin du bsgom/ de
ltar byas na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa yang de yin mod/ nged yon bdag gi tshogs rdzogs pa dang / dkon mchog gsum gyi zhabs tog byas pa yang don yod pa yin/ khyed dge 'dun
rnams kyis bshad pa dang / nyan pa dang / sgrub pa tshul bzhin du ma byas na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i bya ba de gang yin/ sangs rgyas kyis kyang / nga'i bstan pa 'di
ri dwags kyi rgyal po seng ge dang 'dra/ rang gi lus kyi nang nas gnod pa ma byung na phyi rol gang gis kyang gzhig par mi nus zhes gsungs pa yin mod/ nged lam chen po la
bsdad nas nged kyi lung

gi lugs bzhin bsgrubs nas chos kyi lung legs par shes pa byung na phyogs ris med par bkur bsti dang zhabs tog legs par byed pa yin/ de ltar lugs bzhin byed pa'i dge 'dun rnams
la gzhan dmag dpon dang / dmag mi/ mkhar dpon/ dar kha che/ gser yig pa la gtogs pa gang gis kyang ri rgyu ma byed/ dmag khral las gsum gang yang ma bkod par/ shAkya
mu ne'i lam gyi lugs las log pa mi byed cing gnam mchod pa dang / nged kyis smon lam 'debs kyin sdod chug 'das nas 'dzin rgyu'i 'ja' sa byin pa yin/ dge 'dun rnams lha khang
dang khang par gser yig pa ma babs su chug za ma 'u lag ma len du chug lha khang la gtogs pa'i sa cha dang / chu dang / chu thags la sogs pa ci yin pa thams cad ma 'phrogs
ma 'then chug lugs med pa'i gshed ma tshong chug dge 'dun rnams kyis kyang 'ja' sa yod pa yin zer nas shAkya mu ne'i lugs las log pa byed pa gar 'thad/ nged kyi lugs
kyi byi ba lo'i dbyar zla 'bring po'i tshes gcig la gshong thor bris/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa chos kyi gru/ /'khor ba rgya mtsho'i pha rol myur sgrol ba'i/ /mnyen
pa mkhas pa 'phags pa'i mtshan can la/ /brten nas gzhan la phan pa'i gtam 'di byas/ /dge ba 'di yis ma lus 'gro ba kun/ /rgyal ba'i yon tan rin chen gling zhugs te/ /'phrin
las 'od rdzogs dge ba rab mnyes pas/ /yid kyi mun pa ma lus sel gyur cig /ces pa 'di se chen rgyal po'i 'ja' sa mu tig ma'o/ /de rnams kyis

'ja' sa mu tig ma bstan zin nas/ da ni 'ja' sa bod yig ma'am/ bande gshed bskyed ma las 'byung tshul bshad par bya ste/ de yang / /oM swasti siddhaM/ bkra shis dang dge legs
thams cad kyi 'byung gnas lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten thams cad kyi skyabs dkon mchog gsum la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bsod nams rin chen las grub ye shes dkyil 'khor rab rgyas
mtshan dang dpe byad kun nas 'bar ba'i sku/ /brtse ba'i rlung gis chos dbyings mkha' la rab bskyod legs bshad gsung zer tsha zer bye ba'i 'od 'phros pas/ /bdud sde rgyu
skar zil gnon gzhung lugs ngan pa'i mun sel sna tshogs kun 'jug gdul bya'i 'jig rten gyi/ /blo gros padmo rab tu rgyas mdzad rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas skye dgu'i sgron me
de la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de yi legs gsung kun nas rnam dag gsal zhing ma 'dres pa/ /srid pa'i gdung ba rab tu sel bar byed pa'i bsil zer can/ /rnam par rtog pa'i rab rib
'joms mdzad bdud rtsi'i dkyil 'khor mchog /spros pa rab zhi dam chos zla ba de la kun nas 'dud/ /kun gzhi'i sa gzhir lhag bsam sa bon dad pa'i chu gter dang / /sangs rgyas
nyi ma'i gsung zer gyis bskyed dge legs lo 'dab can/ /nyes pa'i 'dam gyis ma gos mkhyen pa'i snying po rab rgyas pa/ /gzhan don sbrang rtsi'i bcud ldan dge 'dun pad tshal
rgyas gyur cig /mchog gi sprul sku brnyes kyang mtha' yas gdul bya'i ngor/ /sprul pas tha mal lus bzung dgung lo bcu gnyis la/ /'jam dbyangs zhal gzigs mkhyen brtse'i
chos rnams ston mdzad pa/ /snying po'i mtha'

can khyod zhabs lha brgya'i gtsug gis mchod/ /rnam dag chos dbyings mkha' la thugs rje'i sprin 'dus te/ /shes rab glog phreng snyan pa'i 'brug sgra dar dir can/ /legs bshad
char gyis rnam grol 'bras bu smin mdzad pa/ /klu dbang grags pa 'gro ba'i spyi gtsug rgyan bzhugs gsol/ /bsod nams gangs rir bslab gsum g.yu ral yon tan rgyas/ /rnam dpyod
rtsal ldan bdag med stong pa'i sgra bsgrags shing / /mkhyen brtse'i mche bas phas rgol ri dwags skrag mdzad pa/ /mi yi seng ge'i zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal lo/'di yan
'phags pa rin po ches mdzad/ /bla ma sangs rgyas thugs las 'khrungs pa'i sras thu bo/ /'jig rten kun la khyad 'phags 'phags pa zhes grags 'di/ /bsod nams stobs chen dang
po lhums nas bltams ma thag /rigs gzugs 'byor pa dbang phyug phun tshogs lha dbang bzhin/ /sku tshe snga mar yang yang paNDi ta'i/ /rigs su skyes nas rgyal dang rgyal
sras kyi/ /gsung rab gsung la 'bad pa mdzad ces gsungs/ /de tshe dpal khyod dpal ldan kun gyis mchod/ /de nas dgung lo gsum bzhi bzhes pa'i tshe/ /bdag med rtogs kyang bdag
'dzin yod yong skad/ /bdag gi 'khor zhes bdag bzung 'ga' re la/ /'khor 'das las sgrol 'jam dbyangs sgrol ma gsungs/ /sde snod 'dzin pa brgya phrag bco brgyad la/ /lo brgyad
bzhes tshe rgyud dang skyes rabs gsungs/ /spobs pa thogs med tshangs pa gdong bzhi 'dra/ /rnam 'phrul bsam mi khyab la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bcu gnyis bzhes tshe

chos rje'i zhal snga nas/ /bla chen rin chen rje btsun chen po bzhin/ /bcu bdun lon tshe yon tan rdzogs 'gyur gsungs/ /de tshe de rnams 'phrin las gcig par khums/ /'khor ba'i
rgya mtsho gting mtha' med pa'i sdug bsngal can/ /gson nam gzigs tshe mchi mas gdong khengs gdungs pa yis/ /phyogs bcu'i rgyal ba sras dang bcas la gsol 'debs pas/ /thugs
rje che mnga' khyod ni mgon po spyan ras gzigs/ /thub pa chen po'i gsung rnams lan res thugs chud nas/ /bsdu dngos 'phrin las rnam 'phrul da lta 'di 'dra na/ /byang chub
sangs rgyas gyur tshe phan mdzad smos ci dgos/ /shes rab mtshungs med 'jam dbyangs khyod la phyag 'tshal lo/'di yan 'phags pa'i slob ma cig gis mdzad/ /gang gi sngon
dus bsod nams dpag med rab bsags pas/ /rigs gzugs 'byor pa phun sum tshogs pa brnyes gyur nas/ /lha yi dbang pos mi yi dbang por dbang bskur ba'i/ /jim gir rgyal po 'gro
kun nyi ma ji bzhin gsal/ /mi dbang de yi bsod nams las grub sras kyi mchog /mi mchog kun gyis gtsug gi rgyan ltar rab bkur zhing / /tshar bcad rjes 'dzin las kyis 'gro kun
legs skyong ba'i/ /sa bdag de ni phyogs rnams kun las rnam par rgyal/ /de gcung bsod nams mtha' yas brtse ba'i yid ldan zhing / /mchod 'os rgyal po sri zhu'i sgo nas mnyes
byas nas/ /'gro ba gzhan la sna tshogs thabs kyis phan brtson pa'i/ /blo ldan de ni skye dgu kun gyi rtsa lag mchog /de sras thu bo bsod nams dpal gyis rab tu brjid/
rtag tu gzhan la bu gcig

ma ltar byams sems ldan/ /'phrin las lhun grub rgya mtsho'i mthas gtugs 'gro bas mchod/ /mong gor rgyal po 'jig rten 'di yan 'phags pa rin po ches mdzad/ kun gyi dpal du shar/
/de ltar bla ma dkon mchog rnams kyi byin rlabs dang / /gnam gyis bskos pa'i rgyal po jing gir gan ji dang / /ye ga rgyal po mong gor rgyal po'i bsod nams kyis/ /sangs
rgyas bstan la phan phyir go pe la yi gtam/ /yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa mi 'phrogs pa'i mkhyen rab dang / dmigs pa med pa'i thugs rje dang ldan
pa/ zla ba nya gang ba ltar bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs pa dang / nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor ltar ma rig pa'i mun pa 'khor dang bcas pa bcom pa/ ri dwags
kyi rgyal po seng ge ltar bdud dang mu stegs thams cad las rgyal ba ste/ de'i yon tan dang / 'phrin las dang / bstan pa la/ nga dang cha bu ga bstun yid ches pa'i stobs
kyis/ de snga yin na'ang bstan pa dang dge 'dun gyi bdag po byas/ da lta yin na'ang chos kyi rje sa skya pa dang / slob dpon 'phags pa la dad pa thob/ chos la yid ches nas
chu mo glang gi lo la dbang bskur zhus/ chos kyang mang du thob pa dang / lhag par yang bstan pa dang dge 'dun gyi bdag po bya snyam pa yin/ de'i rgyu mtshan gyis slob
dpon 'phags pa'i ngo la gtsang gi rgyal khams kyi dkon mchog gi rten dang / dge 'dun gyi sde la gnod pa bsrung ba'i 'ja' sa bzang po 'di chos kyi 'bul bar byin pa yin/ gzhan
yang slob dpon la na bza' gser

dang mu tig gis spras pa'i snam sbyar/ rin po ches brgyan pa'i phyam tshe/ chos gos/ rin po che'i zhwa/ lhwam/ stan la sogs pa phul/ yang yo byad la gser gyi gdugs/ gser gyi
khri'u/ gser gyi phor pa/ dngul gyi ja 'o rin po che'i yu ba can gyi gri la sogs pa phul/ yang nor sna la/ gser bre chen gcig dngul bre chen bzhi/ rnga mo'i chibs pa gsar
ma/ dre'u/ gser gyi sga stan srab gsum dang bcas pa phul ba yin/ stag gi lo 'di yang rten gyi rgyu dngul bre chen lnga bcu rtsa drug gsol ja rtse lnga sigs nyis brgya/
gos chen yug brgya dang bcu tham pa/ mdor na 'ja' sa dang longs spyod 'di rnams thams cad chos kyi yon du phul ba yin/ khyed gtsang gi bande rnams kyis kyang de shes par
gyis/ de ma yin na 'ja' sa ci la bskur/ khyed bande rnams kyang dpon mgo ma rtsod/ dpon mang na mi bzang ba yin/ 'ja' sa yod pas kyang gzhan la rung rung ma byed/ khyed
bande rnams dmag dang 'thab 'khrug ma byed par shAkya mu ne'i lugs bzhin du chos shes pas shod/ mi shes pas nyon/ chos 'bri klog dang sgom sgrub la 'bad pa gyis/ gnam mchod
cing nged la smon lam thob/ la la na re bslab mi dgos bsgom pa yin zer ba ma bslabs pa ci bsgom/ go nas bsgom mod/ bande rgan pa rnams kyis gzhon pa la kha ta gyis la
chos slob/ gzhon pas kyang rgan pa la nyon/ khyod bande rnams la dmag khral las gsum med pa 'di bla ma dkon mchog gi bka' drin yin pa de khyed kyis mi shes sam/ khyed kyis
shAkya mu ne'i lugs bzhin ma byas na hor

gyis kyang shAkya mu ne'i lugs 'di e yin zer/ khyod la skyon 'dzin du mi yong ba e yin/ hor gyis ci yang mi shes snyam du ma sems/ lan gcig gnyis ma shes kyang de nas shes
pa yin/ khyod bande rnams spyod pa ngan pa ma byed/ nga mi la ngo tshar ma bcug khyed chos dang mthun par gyis/ gnam mchod cing smon lam thob dang khyed kyi yon bdag ngas
byed pa yin/ rgyal po'i 'ja' sa dngos yin/ bsod nams mthu yis rigs gzugs 'byor par ldan/ /dad dang blo gros brtse ba'i thugs mnga' zhing / /drang pos sa skyong bstan pa'i
rtsa lag mchog /rgyal ba'i sras po go pe la dang ni/ /bsod nams las grub bud med rin po che/ /mdzes ma'i gzugs 'dzin 'dzum pa'i mdangs ldan zhing / /dpal gyis rab brgyan
byams pa'i blo mnga' ba/ /cha bu ga bstun sras dang bcas pa yis/ /dngos su 'byor dang yid kyis sprul pa yi/ /mchod pa sna tshogs rab 'byams dpag med kyis/ /dus gsum gshegs
pa'i rgyal ba rgya mtsho la/ /gus pas phul ba'i bsod nams gang yin dang / /dbyig gi tshogs dang bzhon pa dam pa dang / /sna tshogs tshon spras gos kyi rigs rnams dang
/ /skom pa'i gdung sel re mchog ldan pa'i ja/ /chos kyi don du gus pas phul ba dang / /bstan pa spel phyir dam chos 'dzin pa yi/ /dge 'dun rnams la 'jigs pa med pa yi/ /bka'
lung byin pa'i bsod nams rgya chen dang / /de las gzhan pa'i bsod nams gang yod pa/ /mong gor rgyal po mi dbang go pe la/ /sras dang btsun mo nad med tshe ring

zhing / /rgyal khams bde skyid dge 'dun mthun pa dang / /sangs rgyas bstan pa phyogs bcur rgyas par shog /bsod nams 'di yis srid pa thams cad du/ /dal 'byor rnyed cing rigs
gzugs longs spyod ldan/ /sangs rgyas mthong zhing dam chos nyan pa dang / /lus can rnams la phan pa byed par shog /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal rgya mtshor bying ba yi/ /lus can
thams cad legs par bsgral nas kyang / /chos rnams ma lus mngon sum mkhyen pa yi/ /rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas myur du thob par shog /bstan la phan pa'i bka' lung bzang po
'di/ /thog ma nyid du bstod 'os bsngags pa dang / /yongs su bsngo ba rjes su bgyis pa 'di/ /mi yi dbang pos dang bas bskul nas ni/ /dkon mchog gsum dang rgyal po'i bstod
pa rnams/ /srid zhi kun nas 'phags pa thob phyir mdzad/ /sangs rgyas ngo bo bla ma'i yon tan rnams/ /lung rigs don dang mi 'gal bdag gis sbyar/ /yongs su bsngo ba'i tshigs
bcad gang yin pa/ /rnam dag theg chen lung bzhin kho bos bsdebs/ /shing pho stag gi dbyar 'bring tshes dgu la/ /rgya bod mtshams kyi lung pa shar du bris/ /zhes hor rgyal
po'i 'ja' sa bod yig mar grags pa da lta'i bar du gdan sa chen po rang na bzhugs pa las zhal bshus pa yin no/ /de ltar na spyir 'dzam bu gling dang / bye brag dbus gtsang
khams gsum gyi 'gro ba rnams la bde skyid 'byung ba'i byed pa po dam par gyur pa chos kyi rgyal po dpal ldan 'phags pa'i zhabs de nyid kyis skad rigs mi gcig pa du ma
la chos kyi brda dang tha snyad du ma

gsal bar mdzad de/ slob dpon padma 'byung gnas kyis rgyal po khri srong lde'u btsan la ma 'ongs pa lung bstan pa las/ lo tsA ska ba dpal brtsegs khyed/ /dkar nag rgya ru 'gro
don byed/ /de nas u rgyan gha na ru/ /padma nga dang gros bstun nas/ /gtsang gi grom pa zhes bya bar/ /'khon gyi rigs gyur lug lo pa/ /de yis sde snod bstan pa 'dzin/
/'phags pa'i mtshan can gsang sngags skyong / /mtha' mi de yis 'dul bar gyur/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar mngon du mdzad do/ /de'i phyi lo rgyal pos ljang yul du dmag la byon dus/
bla ma 'phags pa byang ngos su byon te chos rje pa'i sku 'bum la rab gnas mdzad/Ordination of 'Phags padbus gtsang du byon te chos rje pa'i gsung bzhin du 'u yug pa la
bsnyen rdzogs zhu ba dang / sngar ma gsan pa'i chos gsan par dgongs nas mdo khams bar byon pa dang / 'u yug pa glang lo la sku gshegs zhes phyogs kyi 'grul pa las thos nas
phyir log ste/ rgyal po tshur byon pa dang lhan cig tu rgya yul du byon nas/ rgya dang hor yul gyi mtshams the le zhes bya bar chu bo chen po'i 'gram/ 'u thor dgung lo
nyer gcig pa shing mo yos kyi lo zla ba lnga pa'i tshes bco lnga'i nyin/ mkhan po snye thang pa grags pa seng ge la zhus nas bsnyen rdzogs mdzad pa yin te/ de dus chos rje
grags pa seng ge spyan 'dren gyi yi ge 'phags pa nyid kyis mdzad pa las 'di ltar 'byung ste/oM swasti siddhaM/ bla ma dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs la phyag 'tshal lo/ /bla ma
dam pa dus gsum gyi bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugs gnyis su med pa'i ye

shes kyi ngo bor gyur pa chos kyi rje'i zhabs la gus pas phyag 'tshal lo/ /lhag pa'i bsam pa rnam par dag pa'i mthus 'phrin du zhu ba'i yi ge 'di bri bar bya'o/ /bsod nams
dang ye shes kyi tshogs phul du byung ba bsags pas che ba'i yon tan bdun gyi khyad par 'phags pa'i rten rnam par dag par sku 'khrungs nas/ sngon gyi smon lam las grub pa'i
mthus bslab pa gsum gyi lus yongs su rdzogs pas yang dag pa'i bla ma rgya mtsho'i gling du blo gros mi zad pa'i gru bo cher brtson pa'i ded dpon gyis brtan par bzhugs nas
legs par dpyad pa'i nor bu'i tshogs yang dag par blang ste/ yon tan rin po che'i rgyan gyis spras pas mkhas pa skye bo'i tshogs zil gyis mnan nas/ de dag gi yid rab tu
'phrog par mdzad pa'i skyes bu chen po/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi ston pa grags pa seng ge'i spyan sngar/ shAkya'i dge tshul rdo rje 'dzin pa blo gros rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang pos mngon pa'i nga rgyal spangs te gus pa'i yid kyis gsol pa/ 'dir bla ma chos kyi rje dmigs pa med pa'i thugs rje dang mkhyen rab tu ldan pa de'ang 'jig rten
gyi khams gzhan du sems can gyi don rgya che ba la gzigs nas de bzhin gshegs pa dri ma med pa'i dpal zhes bya bar mngon par rdzogs pa 'tshang rgya bar zhal gyis bzhes te
rnam par sprul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i cho 'phrul gyis yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa'i tshul bstan to/ /'on kyang chos kyi rje nyid kyi zhal gyis da dung khyed rnams
gang gi sgo nas kyang legs par 'ong zhes bka' gnang ba dang / rgyal po so zin rgyal khams bde bar yod/ skabs

don la da res rgyal pos thugs la btags nas bande dang / bon po la sogs pa bla mchod pa thams cad la dmag khral med par bde bar sdod/ de'i mgo gnyer dang bande thams cad sa
skya pa shes su chug gsungs pa'i lung byon/ de'i 'ja' sa skyel ba dang / mi brtsi ba dang / slob dpon pa gdan 'dren pa'i don sdom la 'brug mngags pa yin/ 'dir chos kyi rje
bzhugs pa'i tshe na'ang rgyal bu'i drung du yang 'byon dgos pa dang / 'phral gyi bsod nams kyi g.yeng bas nged rang gi yid tshim pa'i chos kyi bshad nyan gyi long ma byung
bas khyed la chos kyi lung mang du len pa dang / bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan slob kyi ya ba zhu ba'i don du spyan 'dren pa'i gros byas pas/ chos rje pas kyang de 'thad gsungs
nas bka' yig kyang bskur/ nged kyis kyang zhu yig nan can bskur ba yin pa la byon ma nyan/ chos rje pa zhal bzhugs pa'i tshe byon na chos rje pa'ang mnyes par 'duggal
te sku gshegs na'ang khyed bzhugs na blo bde snyam nas gdan drangs pa la rkyen ci yin ma shes khyed ma byon pa de yin/ de la cung zad nged kyang yid chad par gyur/da dung
yang chos kyi rje ni mi bzhugs/ gzhan slob dpon med pas khyed la re zhing mchis/ 'dul ba/ phar phyin/ tshad ma la sogs pa'i lung mang du len pa dang / chos rje pa nyid
sku gshegs khar khyed dge slong cig ma grub pa de blo ma bde/ gzhan blo mi bde ba mi snang gsungs/ der nged spyan snga na yod pa rnams kyis de skad mi gsung bar yun ring
du bzhugs pa'i rten 'brel zhig bsgrig par zhu byas pas/ de shin tu

dka' gsungs nas ma gnang / 'o na gal te chos kyi rje pa mi bzhugs na mkhan po su la zhu byas pas/ deng sang dbus gtsang khams gsum na slob dpon grags pa seng ge bas mkhas btsun
'dzom pa med/ khos shAnti pa'i dod pher ba yin gsungs nas chos rje pas thugs kyis dgongs 'dug pas chos rje pa'i thugs dgongs rdzogs pa'i don du 'byon par zhu/ gal te
khyed ma byon na nga'i mkhan po'i 'os gzhan mi snang bas nga tshe 'di la bsnyen rdzogs mi 'grub par snang / chos mang po'i lung yang mi thob par 'dug ste de khyed la rag
las pa yin/ da chos rje pa ni mi bzhugs/ khyed kho na re che zhing ltos pa yin pas thugs la thogs/ khyod byon na chos rje dang khyad par med pa'i 'du shes yod pa yin pas
dam tshig la dgongs/ ngas zhus pa'i tshig 'di rnams la bcos ma dang mi bden pa'i tshig gcig yod na'ang rdo rje 'dzin pa'i ye shes kyi rdo rje 'bar bas bdag gi snying tshal
pa brgyar 'gas pa yin/ bla ma sangs rgyas ye shes kyi spyan dang ldan pa rnams dpang du bzhugs pa yin/ gzhan yang zhu ba'i tshig 'ga' zhig tshigs su bcad de snyan du gsol
pa/bdag gi bla ma mya ngan 'das//sprul pa'i dkyil 'khor dbyings su zhi//ye shes nyi ma nub par gyur//thugs rje sprin gyi phung po dengs//dam tshig char gyi rgyun yang
chad//kye ma bdag ni skal ba dman//dman pa'i dbang gis de ltar snang //snang bas khyed la gsol ba 'debs//khyed kyi thugs rjes ma gzigs na//da ni bdag gi ston pa su//de ltar
'phrin du zhus pa'i tshe//bla ma'i yon tan dran pa dang //khyed

kyang yul gyis bskal pa yi//nyes pa dran nas mchi ma lhung //bla ma'i bka' drin stobs dang ni//khyed nyid kyi ni thugs rje dang //bdag gi 'dun pa'i dbang gis ni//gsol ba'i
don de 'grub par mdzod//de ltar zhus la'ang mi dgongs na//ngo tsha gang yin khrel gang yin//dam tshig gang yin snying rje gang //ngus shing bos shing gsol btab na//'brel
med kyis kyang phan thogs pa//khyed kyi thugs rje cis mi 'jug/'phrin yig 'di ni gzigs tsam gyis//khyed sku rta mchog snying rje yi//lcag gis bskul nas brtson pa'i stobs//rlung
gi shugs kyis 'dir gshegs shig/nged rang de nar 'ong / sa skyar phyag re tsam 'tshal ba dang / bsnyen rdzogs shig gi ched du 'ong bar spro ba la 'u cag gi 'dun ma'i
rtsa ba 'di nas bsgrub dgos par snang bas ma 'ongs pa yin/ da khyed kyis nged la phyogs mtha' dag la sems par zhu/ lam yang rgyal srid 'jags pas bgrod sla bar yod/ mdo khams
sgang hril po'ang rang ra'i slob ma sha stag yin/ de thugs la yod pa gyis/ de'i rkyen skam mchu ba la yang mngags yod pas khos kyang zhabs tog tu ci 'gyur byed de mchis/
yi ge'i rten dang 'dir 'byon pa'i mthun rkyen la rgyal po'i gan nas byung ba'i dngul bre chen srang lnga bcu rtsa gsum byas pa cig mchis/ rgya cher ma 'dzom/ slad ma
khyed 'dir byon nas rang re thams cad chos dang zang zing gi longs spyod kha na ma tho ba med pa la 'tshogs pa dang shin tu bkra shis par smon/ chu pho byi ba'i lo dpyid
zla 'bring po'i yar gyi tshes gsum la

ling chu rtser khab kyi gtsug lag khang du bris pa bde legs su gyur cigces pa'i zhu yig dang bcas pa'i pho nya mngags techos rje grags pa seng ge ba spyan drangs te/ mkhan
po chos kyi rje nyid dang / slob dpon jo gdan byang pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ gsang ste ba yar lung pa byang chub rgyal mtshan/ dad dge chos rje dbu rgan/ mang ra ba mkhan
po spro dang / gnam phar ba tshul rin la sogs pa nyi shu'i dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs nas/ mkhan po la phar phyin tshig gsal sogs dang / slob dpon las so thar mdo rtsa
sogs dang / gsang ston las sde bdun la sogs pa mang du gsan te dpyis phyin par mdzad/nyer gsum la ldong gis gdan drangs nas rtse lngar byon te/ gshin rje gshed brda bzhi/
mahA mA yA/ rdor dbyings/ dus 'khor sogs rgyud 'grel pa cha lag dang bcas pa gsan/ gzhan yang rigs tshogs/ bstod tshogs mngon pa sogs mang du gsan no/ /lo de nyid kyi zla
ba bzhi pa'i tshes bcu gsum gyi mtshan mo chos rje gsal bar byon nas/ khyod 'di nas bzung ste lo 'bum phrag gcig dang stong 'das pa'i rjes su phyag rgya chen po mchog gi
dngos grub thob ces lung bstan zhing dbugs phyung ba'i rjes su/ srid par sdug bsngal du ma yis/ /yun ring dus su dub pa dag /legs par gsungs pa'i dbugs 'byin pa/ /thugs
rje'i dbang phyug mkhyen pa'i gtso/ /chos kyi rje la phyag 'tshal bstod/ /ces bstod pa mdzad ces gsungs shing / thos pa rgya mtsho ma yang de dus mdzad par grags la/ de
nas hor la yi ge med pa la

hor yig gsar brtsams/ de'i phud la bande gshed bskyed thags grub ma phul/ de nas rgyal po'i pho brang du byon nas chos 'khor bskor ba'i tshe/ tha shang la gyin zhes bya ba'i
rjes su 'brangs nas/ zin shing gi rab byung mang po yod pa lta ba ngan pa la zhen pa dag rang gzhan la gnod par gzigs nas/ rgyal po'i bkas bskul te/ zin shing gi ston pa
ring du sbyangs pa rang gi gzhung lugs mthar son pa bcu bdun rigs pas pham par mdzad nas rab tu byung ste/ yang dag pa'i lta ba 'dzin du bcug go /de nas dgung lo nyer brgyad
pa'i dus su yar cha rkyen mang du bskur nas dpon chen shAkya bzang pos dbu rtse rnying ma'i nub tu gser thog chen mo bzhengs/ de nas so gcig pa shing mo glang gi lo
la dpal ldan sa skyar phebs/ gser thog chen mor rdor dbyings kyi lha tshogs bzhugs pa'i bkra shis sgo mang rin po che du mas brgyan pa dang / rje btsun gong ma rnams kyi
phyi rten sku 'bum bdun la gdugs/ chos 'khor gser zangs las grub pa dang / khyad par sku 'bum la gser thog rnams mdzad/ mdo rgyud dang sher phyogs sogs rgyal ba'i bka' gser
gyi po ti nyis brgya lhag pa bzhengs/ chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen bskor nas 'gro ba mang po smin grol gyi lam la bkod/ bdag nyid chen po 'di nyid thos pa mthar phyin
nas chos kyi mnga' bdag yin yang / nga rgyal med cing chos la gus pa brtan pa'i phyir/ chos kyi don du bshes gnyen du ma bsten te/ kha che'i paNDi ta chen po shrI ta thA
ga ta bha dra/ bla ma rdo rje 'dzin pa glo bo lo tsA ba shes

rab rin chen dang / snar thang pa'i mkhan po mchims nam mkha' grags dang / gsang ba gnyan 'od srung mgon po dang / grub thob chen mo che ras par grags pa slob dpon yon tan
dpal/ sgyer bu ba tshogs sgom kun dga' dpal/ zhang zhung pa rdo rje 'od zer dang / rin po che skyob pa dpal dang / rang dben dmar pa rnal 'byor dbang phyug rgwa lo dang /
chag lo tsA ba'i dpon po nyi ma dpal dang / e pa zhang mngon pa ba rin chen rdo rje dang / brag phug pa dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'bum pa 'od zer dang / mdog glo ba 'dul 'dzin
shAkya byang chub dang / rong pa mkhan po seng ge zil gnon dang / chos rje'i slob ma mngon pa ba dbang phyug brtson 'grus dang / rong ri lung phug pa'i gsang sngags pa
chos kyi mgon po dang / rdzil bu ba'i dge bshes stag ston shes rab 'od zer dang / dbus sde pa slob dpon sangs rgyas 'bum dang / dge bshes 'bras khud pa dang / lha rje dar
ma seng ge la sogs pa mang du bsten nas/ 'ga' zhig la theg pa chung ngu dang / 'ga' zhig la theg pa chen po phar phyin/ 'ga' zhig la gsang sngags sogs mdor na rigs pa'i
gnas lnga/ sde snod gsum/ rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i bstan bcos/ mdo rgyud dbang byin rlabs/ man ngag cha lag dang bcas pa bod na yod pa phal che ba gsan pa yin no/ /de
ltar dam pa'i chos gsan pa'i ched du dka' ba dpag tu med pa mdzad pa ni/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa mi nub par gyur cig snyam du dgongs nas gzhan don 'ba' zhig gi phyir
mdzad pa yin no/ /de nas dgung lo sum cu rtsa gsum pa me mo

yos la/ rgyal po chen pos gdan 'dren gyi gser yig pa nan che bas gong la phebs/ de'i dus su las tshan bcu gsum gyi grwa sgrig mdzad nas byon pas/ bcom ldan ral gris/ sangs
rgyas bstan pa bka' chag sprin gyis sgrib/ /sems can bde skyid mi dpon lag tu shor/ /snyigs dus dge sbyong dpon po'i cha lugs 'dzin/ /'di gsum ma gtogs 'phags pa min par
go /zhes zur za'i tshig phul ba la/ chos kyi rgyal po nyid kyis de'i lan du/ bstan la 'phel 'grib yong ba rgyal bas gsungs/ /sems can bde skyid rang rang las la rag /gang
la gang 'dul de la de ston byed/ /'di gsum ma gtogs mkhas pa min par go /zhes gsungs par grags so/ /de la las tshan bcu gsum ni/ gdung rabs ya rabs kha rgyan las/ zhar las
byung ba phyi nang las tshan ni/ /gsol gzims mchod gsum/ mjal yig mdzod gsum/ thab 'dren gdan gsum skya rta mdzo khyi bzhi/ /chen po la 'os las tshan bcu gsum ste/ /'di
rnams chos kyi rgyal po sa skya pa/ /dpal ldan 'phags pa'i ring la dar ba yin/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar/ gsum tshan gsum dang nyis tshan gnyis zhes bya ste/ de la gsum tshan
gsum ni/ gsol gzims mchod gsum/ mjal yig mdzod gsum/ thab 'dren gdan gsum/ nyis tshan gnyis ni/ skya rta gnyis/ mdzo khyi gnyis zhes grags so/ /ding sang ni rang rang gi
blos btags pa'i bgrang lugs mi 'dra ba rab tu mang yang / 'dir bkod pa ni yi ge khungs thub rnams las

btus pa'o/ /de ltar 'phags pa dgung lo so gsum pa yos lo hor yul la byon pa'i bar lam du/ bka' gdams pa nam mkha' 'bum dgung lo drug cu re gcig pa dang mjal nas/ chos kyi rgyal
po nyid dang dri ba dris lan mang du mdzad pas/ chos rje bka' gdams pa nyid mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob par gyur te/ de dus nam mkha' 'bum nyid kyis mdzad pa'i chos kyi
rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che'i ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa'i cha shas rnams bkod pa'i rnam thar tshan pa gnyis su byas pa zhig 'byung ba'i/ de'i tshan pa dang po las 'di
ltar 'byung ste/ oM swasti siddhaM/ na mo gu ru manydzu gho ShA ya/ chos kyi rje/ chos kyi 'byung gnas/ /chos kyi bdag po/ chos kyi blo gros/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ chos
kyi dpal mgon/ chos kyi bzang khungs/ chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa la sgo gsum dang bas phyag 'tshal lo/ /skyes mchog 'di'i dbang du bgyis na/ sngon skye ba dpag tu med pa'i
gong rol nas tshogs bsags shing chos la sbyangs pa byas pa'i rtags su/ lo bdun la skye ba lnga drug dran pa zhal nas shar te byung ba/ chos rje nyid kyis bkag pas/ de
nas gsung du mi snang ba lags skad/ de'i dus na thams cad kyis 'di tha mal du mi 'dug /'phags par 'dug go zhes 'phags par thogs pa lags skad/ gtam de ni bla ma nyid kyi slob
ma gcig gi ngag las thos so/ /de nas lo bcu gsum pa la rab tu byung / nyi shu pa la bsnyen par rdzogs/ bco brgyad pa la chos rje 'das nas tshogs bsdus/ sum cu tham pa
la dbus gtsang du byon/ lug lo sum cu so gsum

pa/ sa skya pa'i rtsis kyi lugs kyi lo ma 'phos par 'dod pa'i me mo yos bu'i lo'i smin drug zla ba'i tshes lnga'i nyin par 'dam du byon/ nyer drug gi nyin par 'dam nas gshegs/
de tsa na bdag nam mkha' 'bum yos lo pa yin/ drug cu re gcig gi cha/ de phan chod kyi grangs la rang gi go rig dang / bka' gdams pa'i sna rgyus la brten nas jo bo 'das
nas lo nyis brgya nyi shu rtsa dgu song / ston pa 'das nas lo nyis brgya bcu dgu/ po to ba 'das nas dgu bcu rtsa lnga/ sha ra ba brgya dang nyi shu rtsa dgu/ stabs kha
bas dgu bcu rtsa drug zhang ston gyis brgyad cu rtsa gsum/ slob dpon dgon chen po 'das nas sum cu so dgu song ngo / /de rnams jo bo yab sras kyi bka' srol chig brgyud bya
ba yin/ jo bo bod du byon nas nyis brgya bzhi bcu rtsa bdun song / rwa sgreng rmang bting nas lo nyis brgya nyi shu rtsa brgyad song ngo / /de las gzhan pa'i bka' gdams
pa gong ma rnams dang / bstan pa'i babs la sogs pa dus rtsis phal che ba la/ bdag gi blo cung zad spro bar nus te/ mang bas brjod kyis mi lang ba la dgos pa'i gnad chung
ba'i phyir 'dir re zhig gzhag par bya'o/ /de dag ni zhar la 'ong ba brjod pa yin no/ /slad ma skabs don dngos la/ bla ma chos kyi rgyal po 'dam du zhag bcu gcig bzhugs pa
la bdag dang zhag bdun du mjal ba'i dang po chag phebs pa'i dgongs ka nas/ bdag bla ma la mjal du 'ongs nas yod/ nyin mo mi la 'tsher/ mtshams yun ring bas tsho mi thub
par gda' bas/ phyi nang gi 'grul chod pa'i nub mo brda sbyar

gyin mjal ba zhu dgos bya ba'i rgyu mtshan yi ge mang ba gcig bris nas 'jam ser skyel du btang bas/ yi ge la gzigs nas/ 'dir 'ong tshad rang 'dod kyis 'ong ba yin/ chos la
dmigs pa kho las med gsungs skad/ de nas 'jam ser la nang mo theg chen gsal ba'i yig sna dang / lung bsdu ba gnyis khong la skyol la gzigs su chug khong bzhugs sa dang 'o
mi brgyal bar e snang ltos gsungs pas/ nang mo nged kyi drung du 'jam ser dar kha gang thogs nas byung bas/ bla mas gzhan dang mi 'dra bar thugs la 'dogs par 'dug gis gsungs
nas gsung gleng mang du byung ngo / /bla ma byon ba'i phyi nub tshes bcu drug gi nub mo 'jam ser 'bod du btang nas byung bas/ nged dpon g.yog gsum gyis phyin/ spyan
sngar mjal/ phyag rten phul/ ja drangs gsung gleng mang du byung ngo / /de nas de nub ci zhu gsungs pas/ bka' gdams pa'i chos kyi mthil lags pas sems bskyed zab pa cig zhu
dgos/ sngags kyi yang nged kyi dam tshig ni thub/ rgyud ni mi thos par gda'/ sgor zhugs su btub mi btub gzigs nas/ btub na zhugs par zhu bya ba la sogs pa'i zhu ba mang
po cig snyan du gsol bas/ khyed lta bu la rgyud thos mi 'tshal/ nged kyi chos kyi mthil lags pas sngags shig gi yang sgor zhugs 'tshal/ do nub sems bskyed bgyi bas rten
khrom/ mchod pa shom gsungs nas mchod pa bzang po bsham mo/ /de nas tshur nud gsungs nas bla ma'i drung du bzhag ste/ me long gi maNDal chen mo gcig gi steng du chu blugs/
bdag gi lag pa bla

ma'i phyag gis bzung gin bsam bsgom dang rjes zlos bya rgyu mang po yang dag pa gda' pa rnams mdzad nas/ 'dir maNDal gyi cho ga yongs su rdzogs pa bya ba gal che ba yin gsungs
nas mdzad do/ /mchod rdzas rnams kyang bdag gi lag tu re re nas btang gin/ bsam bsgom dang rjes zlos byed du gzhug go /de bzhin du yan lag bdun pa thams cad la gdams
ngag cho ga rgyas po mdzad nas/ dngos gzhi'i skabs su 'di dkon mchog sgron ma na bzhugs/ mdo 'di bod du ma 'gyur gsungs nas chos rje pas cho ga rgyas pa lan gsum mdzad/ 'di
klu sgrub kyi byang chub sems 'grel na bzhugs gsungs nas/ gang phyir sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dang gsungs pa de lan gsum mdzad/ 'di zhi ba lha'i spyod 'jug na bzhugs
gsungs nas/ ji ltar sngon gyi bde gshegs kyi/ /gsungs pa de lan gsum mdzad do/ /de rnams zlos pa'i skyon du mi 'gyur ram snyam na/ grub mtha' gcig la zlos pa'i skyon du
mi 'gyur ba'i lung gcig drangs/ de nas rjes kyi cho ga rnams kyang shin tu rgyas pa mdzad/ de rnams kyi mtshams rnams su yang gdams ngag gi yod sgo mang du mdzad do/ /de'i
rjes la phung po gsum pa'i sgrub thabs dang 'don thabs gcig snang ba mtha' yas kyi 'chi ka'i rnal 'byor/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs/ de'i nyal ba'i rnal 'byor/ de'i blo
'phel/ mtshan brjod/ 'don thabs rnams gnang bas nam phyed yol du song ngo / /de nas bcu bdun gyi nub mo yang 'bod mi btang byung bas phying gur chen po cig tu me chen
po

btang / ja mang po drangs nas/ bka' gdams pa'i jo bo yab sras/ rnal 'byor pa rnam pa rnams sku mched gsum/ glang thang ba/ shar pa/ sne zur ba/ bya yul ba/ stod lung pa la
sogs pa'i bka' gdams pa gong ma rnams kyi mdzad spyod/ rnam thar/ yon tan/ dgung lo du la 'das pa/ mtshan dang rus ci yin pa/ tshogs pa ji tsam 'dus pa la sogs pa ma bzlugs
bar la 'dri ba cig gda' bas/ de rnams bdag la zhib mo yod pas shin tu mnyes nas/ de rnams kyi mtshan kun phal cher yi ger bris so/ /de'i skabs su bdag gi ston pa dkon
mchog seng ge la bskur ba'i zhu yig de rnams la lan legs pa cig ma byung na kho bo yi chad par yod pas/ bla mas sngar ma grub kyang mar la gdan drangs nas ma gir mdzad nas
yar bskur ba'am/ yang na sa skya lta bur zhu yig dang gsung 'phrin bsdebs nas bskur na lan yong ba'i rigs e yod ces zhus pas/ sa skya na 'di rnams kyi lan 'ong ba yod na
nga kho na dga' ste med/ khyod kyi yi ge rnams ngas tshags byas yod gsungs nas/ chos khug nas zhu yig gi yi ge rnams byung / mar me'i 'od la bla ma nyid kyis re re nas
bklags/ 'di la khyod ji ltar 'dod zer ba re re bris/ de rnams kyi lan 'di ltar 'ong ba yin gsungs nas mtshan yal der de rnams kyi lan gsungs/ zhu dag mdzad nas 'jam ser 'di
rnams khyod kyis tshags gyis shig 'di rnams la lung rigs thams cad 'dzom pa'i lan legs pa khong mnyes pa cig ma gir byas slar yar bskur ba yin gsungs nas zhu yig de rnams

khong la gtad nas mdang gi sems bskyed de rnams la gegs sel la sogs pa'i chos mang po yang gsungs/ chab tsha drangs nas gong gi gsung gleng 'phro mang du byung ngo / /de nas
tshes bco brgyad kyi snga dro 'jam ser bdag 'dug sar btang nas byung nas bla ma'i zhal nas/ khyed rang de ring sang gnyis maNDal 'bul gyin gsol ba thob/ dbang de khyed
rang gcig pu la dril bu ba lta bu zhig logs su bya'am/ gnang nub 'khor dge bshes bzang po sha stag mang po cig sgyu ma chen mo'i dbang nub gnyis pa gcig zhu bar yod/ grogs
po ni bzang po sha stag yod/ de gnyis gang 'thad kho rang la zhus la shog khong gang dgyes byed dgos gsungs skad/ der bdag gis 'jam ser la ngas cang mi shes/ gang ltar
'thad yas tshod che zhus pas/ khong gi zhal nas dus thug bya ba mang nas 'dug pas yas rang gcig pur song na/ bla ma la bag gzan nas 'ong / 'di tsho'i khyur zhugs na khong
bag mnyes te 'ong / khyed rang gang dges thugs la 'dogs par gnang gsungs pas/ de bden bla ma la gzan na mi yong / zla bo bzang tsa na de rnams kyi khyur bzhugs dgos/ ston
gzhon dang dge slong dang / khyed yongs song la dbang gnyer ba la khral dang thams cad gtan la phob cig bgyis nas khong rnams btang / bla ma la de tsho bshad pas dgyes
par gda'/ de nas de'i nub mo stag lung pa'i dbon po la sogs pa mang po gcig la dbang mdzad/ de nas bcu dgu'i nub mo mar 'gro'i dge bshes dang / mi dpon thams cad bsags nas
bsnyen

bkur byas nas mar gyi 'gro stabs dang / za ma'i bza' lugs dang / dge bshes tshan gcig la rim gro'i gnyer gtad la sogs pa'i bslab bya dang bcas pa'i khrims mang po mdzad skad/
de nas nyi shu'i nub mo sgyu ma chen mo'i sta gon/ nyer gcig gi nub mo dngos gzhi mdzad pa la/ bla ma gser khri mthon po gcig la bzhugs/ de'i g.yas phyogs na rten mang
po bkram/ mdun na mchod pa bzang po mang po bshams/ g.yon phyogs kyi khri'i rtsa na mngon pa bas dbu byas nas dge bshes dang mi chen sha stag gral rim byas nas sgor gyis
bskor bas g.yas kyi mchod pa'i drung yan chad nyi shu rtsa bzhis 'khor ba/ de'i rgyab na phar la dbang gtad pa mang po/ de'i nang 'khor na nye gnas pa dang mchod g.yog pa
mang po/ de rnams kyi dbus na bla ma'i khri'i drung rang du gdan bzang po bting ba'i steng du bdag bzhag nas bsnyen bkur thams cad kyang sngon la 'dren/ bla ma'i dbang
gi cho ga thams cad kyang sngon la bdag la gzhan pas yun ring ba re mdzad/ tha na dung dang 'khor lo dang mda' gzhu lag tu gtong pa yan chad dbang gi bya ba gang yin pa de
thams cad bdag la 'khor gyis byed ma myong / thams cad bla mas mdzad/ gzhan phal cher 'khor la gnyer gyin 'khor gyis mdzad par gda'/ mtshams mtshams su gdams ngag mang
po dang rjes zlos mang po dgos pa bdag la gsung sprad kyin bdag gcig pu la mdzad pa bzhin du bgyis so/ /rjes kyi cho ga yan chod tshar ba'i rjes la/ sang dro thon tsam na
khyed rang thams cad gur 'di'i mtha' skor du tshogs shig gsungs nas gyes

so/ /de nas nyer gnyis kyi dro thon pa la kun der 'tshogs nas yod tsa na/ bla ma stag lung pa'i dbon po de kun la chos gsung gin yod pa gda'/ de nas gur gyi phyir byon tsa
na/ gur gyi rgyab phyogs der chab bsil ba ston gzhon gyi chab de'i hub gcig e myong na snyam de'i tho phyir phyin pas/ phya ru ba nga'i 'chad dka' ba yod dam gsungs skad/
yod lags byas nas brgyugs pas chab hub gang myong nas/ bdag pha tshad na yod pa sbran nas phyin pas kun 'tshangs zin nas phyis las ma slebs pa dang / bla ma'i zhal nas khong
yar thongs gsungs nas khri'i drung du bzhag nas/ bka' gdams pa 'di de nas rgyud mi thos pa gda' bas/ rgyud chung du 'di dang sgrub thabs 'di kun la lung thob tsam gyi
bshad pa gcig byed dgos gsungs nas/ sngon du rgyud de bklags kyin bshad pa mdzad/ de nas sgrub thabs de gsungs/ las tshogs 'ga' yang gsungs/ de'i 'phro la nor bu phreng
ba zhu zer ba gcig gnyis byung / bdag la bos nas khyod la 'di'i dpe e yod gsungs/ yod lags bgyis pas/ nye gnas pa gcig la 'di'i dpe khyer la shog cig bshad do gsungs nas/
mar me'i 'od la bklags kyin de'i 'jig rten pa'i le'u de gsungs so/ /gzhan rnams gyes nas yang gsung gleng en cig mdzad do/ /de nas nyer gsum gyi nub mo nor bu'i phreng
ba'i chos 'phro de gsungs nas/ khyod kyi da de shes par e snang gsungs pas/ shes par 'dug bgyis/ rgyud de la'ang nan tan dang ljags bshad cig mdzad do/ /gzhan gyes nas

bdag gis ngan song sbyong ba gnyis dang / bka' gdams lha bzhi dang / sman bla dang / tshogs bdag dang / chos skyong dang / yi ge brgya pa dang / yi ge gcig ma dang / de lta
bu mang ba gcig la bdag la lung yang yod/ lag len yang byed pa yin te/ byin rlabs myur du re ba lags pas de thams cad la yang lung re zhu bgyis pas gnang ngo / /de nas nyer
bzhi'i nub mo mar 'gro rnams kyi kha ba ches pas mi rta yo gro nas cha/ bla mas rwa sgreng lta bu gcig tu chos gsungs/ gzhan rnams zhag shas rta gso dgos byas nas zhus
pas ma gnang skad/ nad pa gnyis kyi rtsar yang byon dgos par byung nas gda'/ de nas nyer lnga'i nub mo dpon gyi drung du bzhag dro drangs/ bla ma pa dang nged kyi lo rgyus
zhib par byung gsungs nas/ 'ja' sa legs pa gcig gnang nas yig mkhan 'di la gser zho re dgos pa yin te/ khyed dge sbyong bar gda' bas mi zhu ba lags gsungs nas thugs la
btags so/ /de'i dgongs mo shog gsungs nas phyin/ nyi ma mdung gang tsam gyi dus yin/ de tsam na bka' gdams pa la sogs pa phal gyi zin pa la phying gur chen mo gcig gi nang
du mi chen nyis brgya tsam pa gcig la theg pa spyi'i babs ji ltar yin pa dang / bye brag grub mtha' so so'i bzhed lugs dang / khyad par bstan pa 'di'i snying po sngags
yin lugs dang / pha rol tu phyin pa drug po'i bshad pa'ang sngags kho na mang lugs dang / phar phyin drug dang / mtshan nyid gsum dang / bden pa gnyis dang lam rim pa gnyis
rnams go na khyad par med lugs

dang / snyigs ma'i dus na sngags kho na bsngags pa'i bsngags lugs dang / rgya gar gyi grub thob rnams kyang sngags la brten nas grub pa thob pa yin lugs la sogs pa sngags kyi
zhal zin ches che ba'i chos thun chen po gcig gsungs nas kun gyes so/ /bdag gis sngar nas bla ma'i rnal 'byor zhu dgos bgyis nas bdog pas/ khyed rang der bzhugs shig gsungs
nas/ bla ma khri'i 'og tu gdan gcig gi steng du byon/ mchod pa legs par bsham/ bka' gdams pa 'di bla ma'i rnal 'byor zhu bar gda' bas/ khyed rnam pa gnyis zhur 'jug
pa lags/ 'di gnyis sne'u thog pa'i dge bshes lags gsungs tsa na/ dge bshes de gnyis mdun du bzhugs/ bdag 'bol gcig gi khar khyed 'dir bzhugs gsungs nas de la rjes zlos bya
rgyu cig kyang gda'/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor la rgyas bsdus gsum yod pa'i 'di rgyas shos yin no gsungs nas bshad pa mang po mdzad do/ /de thon ma thog phyag gru mo 'bur 'bur
'dug tsa na sku lus la chos gos phud nas khyed 'di gsol cig 'di'i bla ma'i rnal 'byor 'grub par byed pa yin gsungs nas bdag la gnang nas/ khyed gnyis la nged la med sems
pa srid de/ khyed rang gnyis kyis sgrub pa ma byas pas lan pa yin gsungs nas zhal skyal yang mdzad do/ /skabs der ston pa chos mgon der byung bas yas der bzhud par byas
min nam byas/ 'gro bar byas lags zer/ de 'thad/ mi chos la gtad pa med/ bla mas gnang ba byung yang gnang / nga gsha' ma min/ bla ma 'di 'dra'i

zla la 'gror yod pa 'tsheng ba yin/ yas dug yod zer ba'ang ma yin te/ po to ba'i zhal nas mi yas se ba phyo re ba gcig rta bzang po zhon/ gro brgyags bzang po blo la btags/
grogs bzang po dang 'grogs nas sna bstad bzang po'i sar 'gro ba lam ji tsam thag ring bas dga' ba yin lo byas pas/ gtam rgyud de da dung skyor cig gsungs nas dpe don zhib
par bshad do/ /de nas bdag nye gnas pa gcig la gtad nas dpe 'di jo gdan de'i yin pas bskur bas mi yong ba yod/ khong nga'i gzims gur du gdan drongs snag shog tshol la mar
me'i 'od la gsol 'debs 'di 'brir chug cig nga dpon chen pa'i der 'gro dgos par snang gsungs nas bla ma bzhud do/ /bdag nye gnas gcig gis gzims gur du khrid nas yig dpe
bshus tsam cig bris zin/ nam phyed tsam song tsa na bla ma rgyang ste byon pas/ bka' gdams pa nga'i gzims gur 'dir 'gro ba min nam gsungs/ 'gro lags bgyis/ de nas mngon
pa ba/ sne'u thog pa gnyis/ 'dul 'dzin chos mgon/ bdag dang lnga la khyed rnams gal che shos yin 'di ma byas na dpon slob sha mi phebs pa yin gsungs nas tshogs 'khor rgyas
pa cig mdzad/ de la'ang cho ga dang gdams ngag mang po gda'/ de'i ring la yang gsung gleng mang po mdzad/ bdag la khyed rang de kho nar gzims shig gsungs nas/ bla ma'i
gzims mal la yol ba btang nas de rang du nyal ba yin te/ rten dang bla ma thag nyes pas bsdams pa ltar song nas gnyid ye ma byung / nam langs nas khrus la phyin pa'i

shul du/ bla mas chos gos so ma gcig gsol nas khyod zhing dag par snang / mdang khyod la chos gos phul bas/ da nang gro gong 'di 'bul ba byung ba yin gsungs/ de nas khong gi
'khor rnams la nang chen du tsha ba drongs/ khong la nga'i drung du drongs gsungs nas/ bla ma nyid kyi gsol zas ci yin pa de'i sum cha tsam shugs nas bdag la drangs/ gzhan
gur nang der bca' bcu gcig la zan dron re dang sha dum re drangs/ de nas phyi phyag pa byung bas/ phyag rten dar kha re la yang zad pa med/ de'i skabs su khong gdan drongs
la rta phyag tu thongs shig gsungs nas/ bdag la rta bzang de nye gnas pa kun 'bul du bcug bdag gi rta 'khor kun la gtad/ khong rnams sngon la btang / ston gzhon gyis
bdag bsgug par byas nas/ nang du bdud rtsi ril bu zhur phyin pas gnang ba'i zhor la gser gcig kyang gnang / khyod kyis dus rtag tu nga'i rim gro gyis shig gsungs nas byin
rlabs yun ring du mdzad de spyan bye 'dzum med bzhin du gzigs pas/ bdag gis 'bral mi phod bzhin du phyir 'ong bas mchi ma ma thub bo/ /de'i gong skabs skabs su 'jam ser
dang / kun dga' grags dang / chos mgon la sogs pa chos 'brel bdog pa mang po byung / de thams cad la yang gang la gang dgos 'dra bshad pas kun mgu ba skad zer yin dga'
yin song ngo / /lar 'di rnams kun zur zlum nas dran tshod bris pa yin/ zhib par bris na brdzun dang sgro btags su go cha bar rtog gong bzhugs ring / de'i snga dro la sogs
pa'ang chu mig pa

la mdzod rtsa ba gsungs zer/ yang mang ba gcig la mkhas pa 'jug pa'i sgo gsungs/ sems bskyed kyang skabs skabs su mdzad/ sgos chos zhu ba la sogs pa mdor na nyin mtshan med
par chos kyi bya ba dang / gsung gleng dang / gzhan la ci phan na snyam pa dang / ji ltar byas na dngos dang brgyud pas gzhan gyi don du 'gyur na snyam pa ma gtogs pa/ rang
'dod dam chos brgyad la sogs pa tshe 'di'i rnam par rtog pa yid la 'gyu mi srid pa/ sems dang chos gnyis dkrug ste 'dres pa'i rten gyi gang zag cig gda'/ 'di la 'brel
thogs pa rnams don dang bcas/ thar zin pa dang 'dra snyam pa zhig bdag gi blo la yang yang skye yin gda'/ rgyu mtshan bshad na brjod kyis mi lang ngo / /skye ba dang srid
pa thams cad du da lta bzhin du thugs mnyes te bla ma'i zhabs drung du skye bar gyur cig 'khor 'dus pa dang po thob par gyur cig rnam par thar pa mtha' dag la rdzogs par
slob par gyur cig de ltar bslabs pa'i 'bras bus bdag gis sems can thams cad mthar bla na med pa'i byang chub rin po che la 'god par gyur cig ces pa de yan gyis chos kyi
rgyal po 'phags pa nyid kyi ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par thar pa bka' gdams pa nam mkha' 'bum gyis mdzad pa'i tshan pa gnyis kyi dang po bstan zin nas/ yang de nyid kyis mdzad
pa'i chos kyi rgyal po'i rnam thar tshan pa gnyis pa las 'byung tshul bshad par bya ste/ de yang 'di ltar/ bla ma dang 'jam pa'i dbyangs la sgo gsum dwang ba'i sgo nas
gus par phyag 'tshal lo/ /sdig sgrib dang 'khon yon tan skye ba'i rten/ /sa gzhi

ltar gyur ma rig sel ba la/ /skya rengs bzhin du 'dzin gsal mdzad pa yi/ /'khor du grags pa'i sa skya pa la 'dud/ /mkhyen dang brtse bas blo gros mchog tu gyur/ /chos kyi rgyal
mtshan 'gro ba'i dpal du shar/ /'phrin las bzang pos gzhan don mdzad pa yi/ /chos rgyal 'phags pa'i sku la skyabs su mchi/ /rus dang gnas dang mtshan dang gsum la mchod
kyis bstod/ /nam mkha' 'bum la skyob mdzod 'chad kha thugs kyis bzung / /sngon gyi las dang smon lam gyis/ /khyod dang 'phrad nas zhag bdun du/ /chos dang zang zing longs
spyod kyi/ /brtse bas ma bu 'phrad bzhin bskyangs/ /de yis bdag gi spobs bskyang nas/ /'dril bu rtag la mi 'jigs pas/ /dri ba bral grul cal col rnams/ /tha mal mi la
lab lab bgyis/ /de la bla ma slar dgyes te/ /mi rigs che ba kun bor nas/ /zhal gyi mdangs ston spyan gzigs te/ /thugs kyi dkyil nas 'di rnams gsungs/ /lags/ chos rje'i gsung
la/ sems bskyed mdzad pa'i rjes la phan yon gyi gnas skabs na/ gang zag gis sems bskyed btang yang / sems bskyed kyis gang zag mi gtong gsung ba de la/ dbu ru byang
phyogs na de'i tha snyad bsgyur nas sa skya pa la sems bskyed ci byas kyang mi 'chor ba ci yod zer yin/ ma go ba phal gyi sdig gsog par gda'/ de'i dgongs pa ji ltar lags
zhus pas/ gang zag gang yang rung ba gcig gis ngas chos rje pa lta bu la sems bskyed kyi cho ga byas nas bslab bya ji lta ba bzhin bsrungs na sangs rgyas

mod/ bslab bya ma bsrungs/ mi dge ba ma spangs na gang zag gis sems bskyed btang ba yin pas/ sdig pa'i rnam smin ngan song du skye ste/ skyes kyang de nas nam zhig thar ba'i
tshe/ da ltar gyi sems bskyed byas pa'i sa bon de kun gzhi'i thog tu bag chags bzhag pas/ des sems bskyed phyi ma skye ba'i rgyu byed pas/ sems bskyed kyis gang zag ma
btang zhes bya/ de ltar 'ong ba'i rgyu mtshan/ theg pa chen po'i byin rlabs dang / che ba dang / brten 'brel yin no/ /rgyu mtshan gnyis pa 'jam dpal gyis/ bdud dkar po la
dga' ba dang nag po la dga' ba'i rigs gnyis yod pa la sems bskyed gyis byas pas/ bdud thams cad ci byas kyang mnyan/ der 'jam dpal gyis se gol gcig brdabs pas/ bdud thams
cad rgan pa dang / rgud pa dang / mi mdzes pa'i mtshan ma mtha' dag dang ldan par gyur pas/ da 'di las thar pa'i thabs su la yod ces gleng pas/ thar pa'i thabs shAkya thub
pa la yod/ 'jam dpal nyid la yod/ gzhan su la'ang med ces 'cham/ 'jam dpal 'o skol gyi dgra yin zhu ba mi yong / shAkya thub pa la 'di dag las sgrol bar mdzad du gsol
zhes zhus pas/ nga lta bu de bzhin gshegs pa ganggA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyis kyang 'jam dpal gyis bcings pa byas pa las sgrol bar mi nus gsungs nas ma gnang / der dkar
po la dga' ba rnams na re/ da lta'i 'dug song na 'o skol rnams las gyong che ba med pas 'jam dpal rang la sgrol bar zhu dgos byas pas/ nag po la dga' ba rnams na re/ 'di
bas shi bar song na

yang 'jam dpal la mi zhu/ khos sems bskyed byed du 'ong zer ba la/ der bdud g.yo can gcig na re/ da thabs yod 'jam dpal la bcings pa 'di las sgrol bar zhus la/ 'di las grol
tsam na khos sems bskyed byed du 'ong ste/ sems bskyed kyi lan mo byas nas btang nas ma bsrungs pas chog zer bas/ de la bdud thams cad khos des 'thad par 'dug zer nas de
la 'cham nas/ 'jam dpal la/ bcings pa 'di dag las bdag cag rnams dgrol bar zhu zhes zhus pas/ bcings pa las bkrol tsam na khyed sems bskyed byed dam gsungs/ byed byas nas
dam bcas pa dang / 'jam dpal gyis se gol gcig brdabs pas gzugs sngar bas bzang zhing mdzes pa phun sum tshogs par gyur pa dang / de'i rjes kho na la 'jam dpal gyis sems
bskyed mdzad pas/ bdud thams cad kyis lan mo byas/ de nas sems bskyed lkog tu btang snyam tsan/ sems bskyed gzugs can ma yin pas/ sems bskyed dang sems nyid 'dres nas btang
ma shes/ gtong ma shes pa de phyi ma gtong snying mi 'dod pa'i rgyur song nas/ thams cad sems bskyed dang ldan nas grol bas/ der sems bskyed kyis gang zag ma btang ba
yin gsungs nas de'i thog tu lung drangs rgyu gcig kyang gda'/ sa bon gsar 'jog dang rnying 'jog gnyis ji ltar lags zhus pas/ de gang zag la rigs gnyis yod/ snga ma sems
bskyed ma byas pa de sa bon gsar/ sngar byed ma myong ba la byas pa de sa bon rnying par cha ba yin gsungs/ mngon

par shes pa myur bul ji ltar lags zhus pas/ ji ltar rnam gnas yid la byed pa las/ /mthu grub pa yi dam pa thob par 'gyur/ /bya ba yin pas/ rnam gnas zhi gnas yin/ mthu mngon
shes yin/ zhi gnas med pa'i mngon shes mi yong / zhi gnas shas che ba las byung ba de bul/ zung 'jug shas che ba las byung ba de myur ba yin gsungs/ smon 'jug gnyis la
dbye ba ji ltar bgyid zhus pas/ chos rje pa'i bzhed pa smon pa'i sems/ smon pa sems bskyed pa/ smon pa khyad par du 'gro ba gsum/ 'jug pa'i sems/ 'jug pa sems bskyed pa/
'jug pa khyad par du 'gro ba gsum dang drug tu byed gsungs nas bshad pa zhib mo mdzad do/ /smon pa'i thun tshod de nyin mtshan gyi sum cha la byed pa de mthun par gda'/ 'jug
pa de dang mnyam mam ring zhus pas/ de bas bag ring / lar 'di dag par 'jog pa yin/ gsal bar byed na nyin zhag phrugs gcig rang la byed de/ dkon mchog gsum la gsum mi
mchod na nyes pa bya ba/ nyin zhag phrugs gcig la mchod pa theng gcig ma byas na nyes pa bskyed de/ 'di'i thun tshod du 'ong ba'i shes byed du yod gsungs/ yul byang chub
sems dpa' la zhe sdang gis tshigs su bcad pa ma yin pa brjod pa des byang chub sems dpa' de'i tshad ji lta bu gcig yin/ zhe sdang gi tshad gang yin/ tshigs su bcad pa ma
yin pa'i tshad gang yin zhus pas/ byang chub sems dpa' dang po sems bskyed kyi cho ga byas nas/ da lta sdom pa yod rung med rung / shi rung gson rung rang gi sdom pa yod
par go

ba gcig la nyes pa bskyed/ zhe sdang gi tshad nang du ma ran pa'am phrag dog la sogs pa nyon mongs pa gcig gi kun slong gi sgo nas ku re'am rjes zlos lta bu la dngos gzhi mi
bskyed/ tshigs su bcad pa ma yin pa la nyams pa rnam pa bzhi bskyed pa cig dgos/ shes chung dang gzugs ngan zer ba tsam la dngos gzhi mi bskyed nyes pa tsam 'ong gsungs/
skyabs 'gro la mkha' ru ba thun tshod bzhed la/ po to ba mi bzhed/ don la thun tshod e mchis zhus pas/ thun mong ba la mi yong / khyad par can la rtsi ba cig 'ong ba yin
gsungs/ de gnyis min pa'i skyabs 'gro la dbye ba e bdog zhus pas/ chos rje pa'i bzhed kyis bzhir byed/ 'jig rten pa dang / 'das pa gnyis/ 'jig rten pa la 'phags pa dang
mchog gnyis/ 'das pa la thun mong ba dang khyad par can gnyis yin/ de la 'jig rten pa'i skyabs 'gro phal pa de/ 'jig rten pa nyag gcig gis skyabs su 'gro 'jig rten pa'i
mchog de 'jigs pa'ang yod mod/ de 'dod pa nyag gcig gis 'gro 'das pa'i thun mong ba la de gnyis kyang yod mod de/ dad pa nyag gcig gis 'gro khyad par can la 'jigs pa dang
/ 'dod pa dang / dad pa gsum ka yod mod de/ snying rje nyag gcig gis skyabs su 'gro ba yin gsungs/ theg pa chen po pa dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro bar mtshungs par
gda' ba la/ gtso che chung e yod zhus pas/ de yod byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyis gtso byas pa'i dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro/ rang

rgyal ba chos kyis gtso byas pa'i dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro/ nyan thos dge 'dun gyis gtso byas pa'i dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro ba yin gsungs nas/ de gsum la
lung re'ang drangs te/ yang dag par ni 'gro ba yi/ /zhes sogs gsungs so/ /skyabs 'gro gsum po 'di bka' gdams pa'i chos kyi mthil yin/ sngon bka' gdams pa la ming yang skyabs
'gro bar grags/ bdag kyang e 'dra bgyid/ de la bsam bsgom ji ltar zhus pas/ spyir theg pa chen po'i chos thams cad sbyor ba byang chub kyi sems kyis kun nas blangs/ dngos
gzhi mi dmigs pa zin/ rjes gzhan don du bsngo ba yin mod/ khyad par sangs rgyas la skyabs su mchi'o byas pas dngos po gzugs can thams cad rang bzhin med par bsgom/ chos
la skyabs su mchi'o byas pas gzugs can ma yin pa thams cad rang bzhin med par bsgom/ dge 'dun la skyabs su mchi'o byas pas/ de thams cad dang po'am gdod ma nas rang bzhin
med par bsgom zhing bgyid pa lags shig gsungs/ nged kha ton kho na la mos pa lags/ kha ton dang dge sbyor bzlas pa gnyis gang lhag zhus pas/ dbang ma thob pa la kha
ton rang lhag par mchi yis gsungs/ kha ton byed pa la sdud pa dang mngon rtogs gnyis bsod nams gang che zhus pas/ sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yi/ /thugs rgyud khyad
par gang yin pa/ /de dag gi ni mdzad pa yis/ /tshig la'ang bsod nams khyad de 'byung / /bstan bcos mkhan po'ang thugs rgyud gang mtho mthos mdzad pa de bsod

nams che ba lags gsungs/ sdud pa lta bu klog pa la rin po che dang snag tsha gnyis la bsod nams khyad e mchi zhus pas/ bri ba rgyu'i khyad par/ klog pa tshig gi khyad par/
bsgom pa don gyi khyad par bgyi ba/ klog pa la tshig dag pa dang / bzang ba gang yin bsod nams che ba lags/ dpes khyad par du ma byas/ 'on kyang rin po ches bris/ sku rags
na bza' yan chod legs pa dang bzang po yod na gus pa dang gces spras che bar 'ong / de las bzlog na gus pa dang gces spras chung / de tsam gyi cha nas bsod nams che chung
bag tsam cig 'ong ba'ang srid pa lags gsungs/ sdud pa lta bu 'don pa la thams cad blo la med pas sdud pa bying po dpe la bklags/ byang chub sems dpa' sbyin pas yid btags
sogs gsham gyi tshig kha yar po de blo la yod nas blo las bton na/ gcig gis ni klog par 'dug gcig kha ton du 'dug pas/ de gnyis chos spyod 'dres pa'i nyes pa e mchis zhus
pas/ de mi yong chos spyod bcu po re re'i sar bcu ka'i cha mthun 'dres kyang 'dod pa yin gsungs/ 'o na klog pa dang kha ton gnyis la bsod nams khyad e yod zhus pas/ chos
spyod bcu dang phar phyin drug la sogs pa 'di thams cad/ snga ma la brten phyi ma bskyed/ /dman dang mchog tu gnas phyir dang / /rags pa'i phyir dang phra ba'i phyir/
/de dag rim par bstan pa yin/ /bgyi ba lags pas snga ma la brten nas phyi ma skye/ snga ma snga ma dman/ phyi ma phyi ma mchog lags pas kha ton lhag chos 'chad pa bas kyang
kha ton lhag kha ton

pas lhag pa sems pa/ de bas lhag pa bsgom pa/ kha ton gyi gong na chos spyod bcu las lhag par bsam bsgom gnyis las med/ khyed mos pa dang mdzad pa de kha ton kho na lhag pa
dang / bsod nams che ba gda' yis gsungs/ 'o na 'jam dpal sdud pa lta bu la bsod nams khyad e che zhus pas/ de mi yong so so gang mos pa bsod nams che gsungs/ sdig pa sbyong
ba la gnyen po kun tu spyod pa'i stobs gang kho na lhag zhus pas/ de bzhin yin/ spyir chos 'di thams cad sdig pa'i gnyen po kun tu spyod pa yin pa bgyi ba dang / khyad
par du gang byas pa'i gnyen po de bsten pa sdig pa'i gnyen po kun tu spyod pa yin pa bgyi ba dang / chos nas bsod nams gang che zer ba byed pa sdig pa'i gnyen po kun tu
spyod pa yin pa bgyi ba dang / rang gang mos pa byed pa'i sdig pa'i gnyen po kun tu spyod pa yin pa bgyi ba dang bzhi lags gsungs/ stobs bzhi po la gal gang che zhus pas/
de sdig pa 'dag par byed pa la bzhi ka tshang dgos/ gal sor chud pa bya ba sdig pa phyi ma mi byed par 'phro chod pa 'di kho na gal che gsungs nas gal che lugs kyi bshad
pa mang du gsungs so/ /yang chos kyi spun/ rdo rje'i spun/ nye ba'i spun bgyi ba gsum gda' ba de ji ltar lags zhus pas/ skyabs su 'gro ba nas rigs 'dzin gyi bar dang /
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pas bsdus tshad de la chos kyi spun zer/ bla ma tha dad kyis dkyil 'khor tha dad du slob ma tha dad la dbang bskur ba la rdo rje spun zer/ bla ma gcig
gis dkyil 'khor gcig tu slob ma tha dad la dbang bskur ba la nye ba'i

spun zer ba yin gsungs/ bla ma lnga bcu pa 'di la bka' gdams pa kun kyang blta rtog dang lung 'dren 'dra byed par gda' ba/ 'di rgyud gang la brten nas brtsams zhus pas/ 'di
rtsa ltung bcu bzhi pa'i rtsa ltung dang po/ gang phyir rdo rje 'dzin pa yis/ /zhes pa'i tshig bzhi pa de'i 'grel pa shlo ka lnga bcu pa 'di yin gsungs so/ /srog gi dbang
po 'gags nas zhag gsum rnam shes brgyal ba bzhin du cha zer ba dang / skye ba snga ma'i 'du shes 'ong bya ba dang gnyis gda' ba de ji ltar lags zhus pas/ de zhag phyed
brgyal ba bzhin du 'gyur/ zhag phyed dang gsum skye ba snga ma'i 'du shes 'ong / zhag phyed dang bzhi na shi bar nges pa yin gsungs/ bar do la zhag bdun las ring ba e mchis
zhus pas/ yun snang ba la zhag pas tshogs ma bsags pa la bar do yun ring po yong ba'ang srid/ tshogs bsags pa la skad cig gi yun las kyang med/ bdun tsho bdun kun shas
che ba la btags pa yin gsungs/ bar do'i sems can de byis pa lo lnga lon pa la tshad byas pa de nges sam zhus pas/ de'ang shas che ba la btags pa yin te 'ong / /ma nges gsungs/
yang bar do'i sems can de sa rdo ri brag ci la yang thogs rdugs mi yong ba lags sam zhus pas/ ma'i mngal dang rdo rje'i gdan gnyis po ma gtogs thogs med 'gro/ bgyi
ba de gnyis la thogs/ gzhan ci la yang thogs rdugs med gsungs/ de'i rgyu mtshan ji ltar lags zhus pas/ bsgrubs pa'i rdzu 'phrul ma yin te/ /las kyi shugs kyi rdzu 'phrul
gyis/ /stong gsum dar cig

gis bskor nus/ /las kyi shugs kyis de ltar 'ong ba yin gsungs/ bar do gsum gyi sems can gang mang zhus pas/ de srid pa bar do mang gsungs nas rgyu mtshan/ ri bo mchog rab sha'i
phung por song yang zhag shas nas 'bu ru chags gsungs so/ /gson gyi las gshin la smin nam mi smin zhus pas/ 'di la bshad pa mang / smin pa'i khung dang mi smin pa'i
khung gnyis ka yod de/ bdag rkyen byas pa'i tshul gyis smin la/ rgyu rkyen byas pa'i tshul gyis mi smin pas/ gnyis ka ltar mi 'gal gsungs/ so so skye bo'i mtshan nyid dang
nges tshig gang lags zhus pas/ chos nyid dngos su ma mthong ba thams cad so so skye bo yin pa las rang rang gi las mi 'dra ba so so las skyes pas so so skye bo zhes thogs
pa yin gsungs/ 'phags pa'i mtshan nyid dang nges tshig zhus pas/ chos nyid dngos su mthong / las dang nyon mongs pa gnyis ka las ring du 'phags pas 'phags pa yin gsungs/
dam tshig gi nges tshig gang lags zhus pas/ dam tshig dag gi nges tshig ni/ /'da' bar dka' bas dam pa dang / /'das na tshig pas tshig ces bya/ /des na 'da' zhes legs par
bsrungs/ /bya ba yin gsungs/ spyir las rnam smin dang rgyu mthun gnyis gcig yin pa la/ rnam smin 'byor pa can la rgyu mthun ser sna can dang / rnam smin tshe phril gyi
dbul po la rgyu mthun chags zhen ye med pa'ang yong zer ba gda' ba/ de las ci 'dra ba cig las 'byung zhus pas/ de gnyis gcig pa shas che ba yin/ mi gcig pa'i las de/ ngas
nga'i rgyal po ma

gi la khyod kyis tshe snga ma la tshe phril le la ser sna sha stag byas/ tshe gzhug 'chi khar yul byang chub sems dpa' gcig la bsam pa dad nas dngos po rnam dag gcig phul nas
'dug byas pas/ de'i rtags su bla mchod nga 'dra ba dang 'phrad/ longs spyod 'byor ba phun sum tshogs pa 'di lta bu yod kyang / khyod snga ma ser sna la goms pas da dung
gtong ye mi nus pa 'di byung ba yin te/ de las 'dres ma las gyur pa'i dpe de 'dra ba cig lags gsungs/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa sprul mkhan gyi rnam par snang mdzad
chen po de dang / rigs lnga'i rnam par snang mdzad 'di gnyis e gcig zhus pas/ de mi gcig rigs lnga brda'i sangs rgyas bya ba yin pas/ sangs rgyas su sangs mi rgya na mi
rgya/ rgya phan chod rigs lnga'i bdag nyid du sangs rgya ba yin pas/ sangs rgyas de'i sku la rnam par snang mdzad zer/ gsung la snang ba mtha' yas/ thugs la rdo rje sems
dpa'/ yon tan la rin chen 'byung ldan/ 'phrin las la don yod grub pa zer ba yin/ sangs rgyas so so'i 'dul ngo la lnga po de gtso che chung yod/ lnga ka dang mi ldan pa'i
sangs rgyas mi srid/ rnam par snang mdzad gang chen mtsho bya ba de/ zhi sku dpag bsam shing ltar gsal gyur cing / /yid bzhin nor bu ji bzhin rnam mi rtog /'gro grol bar
du 'jig rten 'byor slad rtag /de ni spros dang bral las snang bar 'gyur/ /bya ba sa bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snang ba la 'char ba lags gsungs/ shAkya thub pa
lta bu sprul pa'i sku zhal mthong ba la tshogs lam

thob pa gcig dgos par gda' ba la/ 'o na sangs rgyas zhal bzhugs pa'i dus na'ang sangs rgyas mthong tshad tshogs lam par 'ong ngam 'on te 'das nas mthong ba tshogs lam par 'ong
zhus pas/ de gzhan stobs kyis mthong ba dang / rang stobs kyis mthong ba gnyis lags/ gzhan stobs kyis mthong ba bya ba/ nga'i rgyal po blta bar 'dod pa la/ rgyal po dbus
gtsang lta bu gcig tu khong yar 'ongs nas khong blta ba la dka' thub gang yang mi dgos/ mig yod pa tsam gyis khong mthong nas 'ong / de bzhin du sangs rgyas zhal bzhugs
pa'i dus na sangs rgyas mthong ba la tshogs lam thob mi dgos/ tha mal pa yan chod thams cad kyis mthong nas yong / rang stobs kyis mthong ba bya ba ma gi lta bur phyin
nas rgyal po blta bar 'dod na thag ring po yod/ dka' thub chen po byas nas ma gir slebs tsa na rgyal po mthong ste 'ong / de bzhin du sangs rgyas 'das nas sprul sku zhal
mthong ba la tshogs lam thob dgos pa yin gsungs/ tshogs lam pa ngan song du skye ba srid par gda' ba/ de la ngan song du skye ba la mi dge ba stobs can dgos pa 'dug tshogs
lam thob pa la ni dge ba stobs can cig dgos par 'dug pas/ tshogs lam pa des tshogs lam thob pa'i dus de rang na'ang ngan song du skye ba'i rgyu las/ de sa bon gyi tshul
du kho'i sems rgyud la yod dam/ 'on te kho je dman je dman gyur nas ngan song du skye rgyu'i las de gzhi nas gsog pa yin zhus pas/ de spyir tshogs lam pa phal che ba ngan
song du mi skye/ bsod nams kyi tshogs gtso bor gsog pa

yin/ srid pa de sems rgyud la las ngan pa btul te ma zad pas sa bon bag tsam cig kyang yod/ des gzhi byas nas ngan song du skye rgyu'i las de gzhi nas gsog tsa na gdod skye
ba yin/ gong gi sa bon rkyang pa des skye mi nus/ sa bon de med na'ang las ngan pa bsags pa'i gzhi med pas gnyis ka 'tshogs dgos pa lags gsungs/ 'o na nyan rang gi theg
pa chen po ril por spangs pa la ngan song du mi skye ba de ji ltar lags zhus pas/ theg pa chen po spangs pas ngan song du skye ba de dang po theg pa chen po chos yin pa shes
pa la/ phyi nas nyon mongs pa 'ga' zhig gis kun nas blangs/ mi dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis zin nas log lta skyes te ril po spangs pas ngan song du skye ba yin la/ nyan
rang kho rang gi grub mtha' brtan pa dang nges par bya ba'i phyir/ theg pa chen po sun 'byin pa yin/ theg pa chen po pa rang gis kyang sems tsam pas dbu ma sun 'byin/ dbu
ma pas sems tsam pa sun 'byin te/ rang gi grub mtha' nges par bya ba'i phyir/ grub mtha' gong 'og sun 'byin pa la nges pa med pa yin gsungs/ nyan thos kho rang sangs rgyas
cig kyang ma bral bar 'grogs pa la/ theg pa chen po bya ba tshig cig kyang gsungs par nyan rang gi bsngags pa dang che ba gcig pu brjod pa kho rang la nges 'thad nas yod
pa yin gsungs/ bla ma la rtog dpyod ye mi byed par dang po nas sangs rgyas su bsgom pa de legs sam/ rtog dpyod byas nas bsgom du btub na bsgom pa de legs zhus pas/ rtog
dpyod ye ma byas par sangs rgyas su bsgom pa de

gang zag dad pa'i rjes 'brang bya ba yin te mi bzang / shes rab kyi dgos pa rtog dpyod yin/ bla ma rang sde snod gsum shes pa'i blo gzu bor gnas pa gcig gi drung du bsdad nas
skyon btsal yang mi rnyed pa/ sangs rgyas kyi 'du shes ma bsgoms kyang skye ba gcig la bsgoms pas shugs kyis byin rlabs 'jug yon tan skye ba yin gsungs/ yon tan skye ba
la bla ma'i byin rlabs dang / slob ma'i mos gus gnyis stobs gang che zhus pas/ thun mong gi yon tan la slob ma'i mos gus stobs che ba'i skabs kyang yod/ mchog gi yon tan
la bla ma/ slob ma/ gdams ngag gsum ka'i stobs rab tu 'dzom dgos te/ dper na me rdo/ me lcags/ spra ba skyon med gsum la me 'byung ba ltar/ bla ma byin rlabs kyi bka' brgyud
ma chad pa/ slob ma mos gus kyi rten 'brel ma 'chugs pa/ gdams ngag bsre bslad kyi tshig gis ma spags pa gsum 'dzom tsam na yon tan la 'bad rtsol mi dgos par ngang
