shing /sras de gnyis dang lcam mo che ba phyag rdor 'bum bya ba dang / chung ba dge ma ste bzhi po de ni bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyi sras lcam sring bzhi po yin
la/ de ltar bzhi'i nang nas 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba des rje btsun sa skya pa'i dpon chen gyi brgyud pa khro mda' ba'i sras mo ma gcig dpal 'byung
rgyal mo zhes bya ba de khab tu bzhes pa la/ sras slob dpon ma bsod nams dpal 'dzom/ nam mkha' 'bum/ nam mkha' bzang mo/ slob dpon ma mkha' 'gro 'dzom ste lcam mo bzhi
dang / bdag nyid chen po rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan dang / mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug blo gros rgyal mtshan dang lcam sring drug 'khrungs te/de rnams kyi nang nas rgya
dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba ni me pho 'brug la sku 'khrungs shing / skyes stobs kyi thugs rab shin tu che ba dang / bshes gnyen dam pa mang po
bsten nas yab chos la sbyangs pas phul du phyin pa dgongs nas/ rtsom pa yang ci rigs pa mdzad cing / dgung lo nyer bdun tsam bzhes pa stag lo zla ba dgu pa'i nyer lnga la
gdan sa chen po nas gdan bteg ste khams kyi phyogs la phebs te/ bon khyung po stod bya bar 'byor pa na yul

de'i 'gro ba mang po smin grol la bkod cing / de nas nyi ma gnyis tsam gyi bar du dpon slob rnams la lam nor cung zad zhig byung ba'i tshul bstan te/ hor ser yod pa'i sa cha
zhig tu phebs pa na/ yul de'i mi rnams kyi cha byad kyang lha 'dre'i cha lugs lta bu yid du mi 'ong pa 'ba' zhig byas pa shin tu 'jigs su rung ba 'ba' zhig 'dug pa gzigs
pas slob 'khor rnams cung zad thugs ma bde ba na/ de'i gseb nas hor bod skad cung zad shes pa cig byung nas/ khyed rnams ci 'dra zhig yin zhes 'dri ba la/ rje nyid kyi
gsung gis/ gnas sa skya zhes bya ba nas 'ong zhing / rigs 'phags pa'i dpon po yin pa'i tshul gsungs pas/ de ltar yin nges na sngon bla ma 'phags pa bya ba dang nged hor gnyis
yon mchod yin zhes zer zhing / bdag nyid chen po la phyag dang bskor ba mang po zhig byas song nas/ de'i nang par hor gyi dpon blon thams cad phyag 'bul zhing byin rlabs
zhu ba dang bsnyen bkur rgya chen po 'bul ba la byung ste/ chos kyi sems dang bral zhing sdig pa'i las la dga' ba'i shin tu rtsub sems dang ldan pa rnams kyang gus par
gyur to/ de nas kyang rim gyis phebs te grub rdza bya ba'i yul mthon po zhig tu chu gtan nas med par khal ma rnams dang / drung na gnas pa thams cad shin tu skom pas nyen
pa na bdag nyid chen po 'dis brag la phur pa btab nas skom sar chu bton te thams cad skom pa'i 'jigs pa las bsgral ba dang / yang skabs shig tu kha ba chen po babs te/
la chen po zhig la lam thams cad kha bas non nas ci bya

gtol med du gyur pa na/ bla ma 'dis dkon mchog dang chos skyong srung ma la gsol ba btab bden bdar brjod nas nang par byon pa'i tshe/ 'brong gi rmig rjes shar gyis dod pa cig
'dug pa'i rjes bcad nas phebs pas/ 'brong sum cu tsam zhig la thog tu byung ste gangs rnams phar gshags tshur gshags nas song ba na/ de dag gi rjes bcad nas bdag nyid
chen po slob tshogs rnams kyis kyang byon pas lam bde bar bgrod de skyon med du 'thon zhes grags pa dang / gzhan yang lam nor cung zad byung ba'i tshul rnams la yang ri dwags
rkyang dang sha ba la sogs pas lam sna bstan pa sogs ngo mtshar mtha' yas shing / gzhan yang bod kyi sa'i cha dbus gtsang du phebs nas yang khang pa 'jig nges pa kha
cig tshon skud kyis bcings pas g.yo med du gnas pa dang / ma rungs pa dag gis chus bskor ba na na bza'i g.yab mo brdabs pas rdzing chen po phyogs med du ral ba dang / ngan
pa 'ga' zhig gis bdag nyid chen po 'di bzhugs pa'i bla brang la dmag gis bskor nas rung ba ma yin pa'i las byas pa na/ bla ma 'dis chos skyong la 'phrin las drag tu bcol
bas dpal ldan lha mo 'dod pa khams kyi dbang phyug ma'i sku brnyan bla ma 'di'i thugs dam mdzad pa'i rten cig yod pa des sgar gyi mthar nyul te lha mo'i sku las rdul 'thon
pa byung zhing / de nas ngan pa de'i sgar du nad chen po byung ste mi mang po shi ba na/ lha mo'i sku brnyan de la de nas bzung ste lha mo rdul ris ma zhes grags te/
deng sang yang dge sdings mgon khang na bzhugs pa 'di nyid yin no zhes kyang grag go /de ltar mthu

dang nus pas grub pa'i mtshan ma phyogs med du bstan te/ mthar shing pho stag gi lo'i zla ba gsum pa'i tshes bco lnga la shab dge sdings su sku'i bkod pa chos dbyings su bsdu
bar mdzad pa yin la/ de'i tshe na yang ngo mtshar ba'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung bar grags so/ /de lta bu'i bdag nyid chen po rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan du
grags pa de'i gcung blo gros rgyal mtshan du grags pa ni/ yab 'jam dbyangs chen po dgung lo bzhi bcu zhe brgyad bzhes pa mig dmar zhes bya ba shing pho byi ba'i lo la/ bod
chol kha gsum las bar gyi cha/ dbus gtsang ru bzhi las g.yas ru gtsang gi sa'i thig le/ shab sgo lnga gzhung gsum zhes bya ba'i yul gyi dbus sa gzhi lag mthil ltar snyoms
shing / phyogs dang phyogs mtshams kyi yul gru chen po dag na/ ljongs dang / yul 'khor dang / grong khyer dang / skye bo'i mdun sa dang / sman ljongs dang / ne'u gsing
yid du 'ong ba la me tog sna tshogs ched du bkram pa bzhin yod pa/ ljon shing gi ra ba 'khrigs pa'i yal ga dang / lo ma dag la brten pa'i bya sna tshogs skad snyan par
sgrog pa/ 'bru bcud dang lo thog phun sum tshogs pas skye dgu thams cad bde bar 'tsho ba/ chu klung chen po rlabs kyi phreng ba cung zad dang bcas pas dkyil 'khor gyi mdun
ngos su babs pa/ byams mgon gyi rnam 'phrul khro lo chen po'i gtsug lag khang dang khad nye ba'i sa phyogs/ rje btsun gong ma dag gi zhabs kyis bcags shing bdag gir mdzad
pa'i gnas/ shab dge sdings kyi sa'i cha lcam mo g.yang glong

zhes bya bar sku 'khrungs par gyur te/ de'i tshe yum gyi gzigs snang la/ mdun na rgya nag gi shing khri bkod pa shin tu legs pa cig gi steng na bud med dmar mo gser gyi dbu
rgyan can rus pa'i rgyan drug dang rin po che'i rgyan du mas spras pas khro 'dzum gyi rnam pa can zhig khyel byas pa'i lag pa gnyis na zangs gzhong padma dmar pos phyur
bur khengs pa bzung nas 'dug pa cig gzigs shing / 'khrungs ma thag nas dbu gdugs kyi rnam pa dang / dpral ba'i dbyes mtho ba sogs mthong na mi mthun pa med pa/ nor bu chu
shel dri ma med pa ltar sku lus dkar zhing 'od 'phro ba/ zhi zhing des pa'i ngang tshul 'dzum dang ldan pa zhig byung nas/ mtshan mkhan la bstan te ji ltar lung bstan pa
ltar gshin rje tshe bdag gi thang sku'i sku lus cung zad 'dril ba dang / ra dkar mo'i nu zho blud pa sogs byas shing / gzhon nu nyid nas tha mal pa'i byis pa'i spyod pa
las 'das pas tho co'i spyod pa spangs nas dul zhing yid gzhungs la chos dang mthun pa'i rtse dgas dus 'da' ba dang / rang bzhin gyi brkam chags chung zhing chos la thugs
'gro ba/ dben pa 'ba' zhig bsten pas bag chags ched du sad pas/ g.ya' ri gangs ri sogs mtho zhing sprin dang na bun gyis gtibs pa gzigs pa na dges tshor chen po mdzad pa
dang / nga ya gir cis kyang 'gro gsung ba sogs dang / gzhan yang bu rdzis rgyab tu spyan drangs pa na mi nag khyi nag 'di ltar 'dug gsung ba mang du byung bas/ rje btsun
yab la zhus pa na/ nged kyi brgyud pa rnams la chung ngu nas chos skyong gi rnam 'phrul mang po mthong ba

zhig yong gin yod pas de ltar yin gsung ba dang / dus cig gi tshe yab yum gnyis la rje 'dis bdag ming sring rnams de ring rtsed mo la phyi rol du cis kyang gtong bar zhu zhes
nan gyis zhus pas/ yab kyis kyang mtshams dam par yod na'ang gang yin mi shes pas de ltar gyis gsungs nas gnang / der phyi rol du lcam sring rnams phebs rjes sa g.yos
shin tu che ba zhig byung nas sngar gyi gzims khang de nyid rdibs pas/ kun gyis mngon mkhyen thogs med du mnga' ba mthun grub cing / 'khrungs ma thag pa'i dus su thang sku'i
sku dril ba sogs kyang phyis shin tu gsal bar dran pa byung zhes grags te/ de nas dgung lo gnyis gsum nas drug gi bar du yab yum gyi drung kho nar bzhugs te/ de'i skabs
su bla brang gung pa'i dge bshes cig gis 'dri klog sogs brda tsam phul bas thogs med du phul du phyin pa mkhyen cing / rje btsun yab nyid la gsung ngag rin po che yang
phur/ dkar bdud/ dmar po skor gsum/ chos skyong che chung gnyis rnams kyi chos skor dang / dur khrod bdag po'i chos skor/ las mkhan pu tra ming sring gi rjes gnang / tshe
dpag med lha dgu'i dbang / sgrol dkar gyi rjes gnang sogs dbang lung byin rlabs/ rjes gnang man ngag gzhan yang dbyangs rol gar 'chams la sogs pa'i phyag len phra mo tshun
chad zhib cha dang bcas pa sku chung ngu nyid nas legs par gsan cing / khyad par yab nyid kyis sras dang slob ma gzhan su la yang ma gnang ba'i dpal ldan sa skya pa'i
bstan srung rnam pa gnyis kyi thun mong ma

yin pa'i chos skor sogs gdung brgyud kho na la chig brgyud du bzhugs pa'i gdams pa rnams yongs su rdzogs par gnang bar chos skor 'di dag gi mnga' bdag chen por bzhugs pa ni/
bdag nyid chen po rang gi gsung las/ bod yul bstan pa'i mnga' bdag mchog /sa skya'i rje btsun las brgyud pa'i/ /nag po chen po'i man ngag la/ /nga mkhas zer ba mang na
yang / /ji bzhin rtogs pa kho bo tsam/ /zhes gsungs pa 'di nyid kyis rtogs par nus pa yin no/ /des na bdag nyid chen po 'dis 'khor ba'i khyim thab ni 'jigs shing nyam nga
ba'i sdug bsngal gyi rtsa bar gzigs nas/ mtho ris dang byang chub bsgrub pas med du mi rung ba'i gzhi chen po lhag pa'i tshul khrims kyi bslab pa kho nar dgongs te/ nges
par 'byung ba'i thugs kyi bsam pa ston gyi zla ba ltar dkar zhing dri ma med pas kun nas bslangs te/ dgung lo bdun pa rab myos zhes bya ba lcags pho rta'i lo la byang phyogs
shambha la'i rigs ldan grags pa gangs ri'i khrod 'dir ngur smrig gi bla gos kyi rnam par rol pa'i 'jam pa'i dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po zhes mtshan yongs su grags pa'i
nges don rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag chen po de nyid dge sdings bla brang du spyan drangs pa'i drung du khyim pa'i rtags mtha' dag bzhi mdo'i rtswa ltar dor zhing / ngur smrig
gi rgyal mtshan sogs rab tu byung ba'i rtags yang dag par bzhes pa'i sgo nas bar ma rab byung du bsgrub ste/ blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan gsol/ de
nas dam pa de nyid kyi zhabs phyir 'brangs te nyang stod dpal 'khor bde chen gyi chos sde chen

por phebs pa'i tshe/ bla ma yang rtse ba zer ba'i dpal mgon zhal gyi grub thob tu grags pa zhig gi gang zag gcig la zhal gyi rjes gnang byas pas/ 'khu ldog gi rnam pas khong
pa zhal lkugs te ci bya gtol med du gyur nas rje 'di'i drung du thogs med du byon byung ba na/ mgo thog tu spyan drongs zer ba'i brda byed kyin 'dug pa na/ slob dpon dpal
mchog pas rje 'di nyid pang du blangs nas khong gi dbu thog tu bzhag de ka'i mod la gsung khrol byung ba dang / mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob par gyur ces grags la/ de nas
dgung lo brgyad pa'i dus su rje btsun gcen dang lhan cig tu dpal ldan sa skya'i chos grwa chen por che 'don legs par mdzad/ tshangs pa'i dbyangs lta bu'i gsung gis dam pa'i
chos kyi bka' drin rtsal pas/ blo gsal mkhas pa'i tshogs rnams ngo mtshar zhing mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob par gyur/ de las gzhan pa'i skye bo rnams ni zhal mthong gsung
thos pa'i bag chags khyad par can rgyud la bzhag cing / zang zing gi sbyin pas yid rab tu tshim par mdzad la/ slar yang dgung lo dgu pa nas bcu gsum pa'i bar du 'jam dbyangs
chos rje de nyid kyi chag phyir nyang stod phyogs su phebs shing / slob dpon dpal mchog par grags pas kyang zur slob kyi tshul gyis zhabs tog mdzad/ rje de nyid kyi
drung du rgyas pa'i bstan bcos tshad ma rnam 'grel dang / de'i dgongs 'grel gyi bstan bcos tshad ma rigs gter/ rgyal sras lam bzang / sdom pa gsum gyi rab tu dbye ba/ dbu
ma rtsa ba shes rab la sogs pa gzhung lugs du ma zhig gsan

nas tshig don gyi cha la sgro 'dogs mtha' dag chod cing thugs su chud pa mdzad pa yin no/ /gzhan yang theg pa chen po'i sems bskyed/ gsung ngag rin po che cha tshang / rgyab
chos pod nag ma'i lung / lam skor phyi ma brgyad/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ birWa pa'i byin rlabs srung ba dang bcas pa/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang dang / sbyor drug gi khrid/
gsang 'dus 'phags lugs kyi dbang / rigs lnga'i smar khrid/ gzhan yang gshed dmar lha lnga/ phyag rdor 'khor chen/ tshe dpag med bu lugs la sogs pa dbang gi rigs du
ma dang / dam pa sangs rgyas kyi bka' 'bum gyi lung la sogs pa mdor na rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i chos tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gsan cing / de'i tshe dpal ldan
sa skya nas bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug pas gzhi thog gi gdan sar 'byon dgos pa'i zhal ta phebs/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po dang / rgyal rtse bas kyang bskor yang
mthun sbyor yang dag mdzad de/ dgung lo bcu bzhi pa me mo glang gi lo la yab 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dang / bdag chen grags pa rgyal mtshan pa khams nas byon
pa dang lhan cig tu gdan sa chen por chag phebs te/ rje btsun kun dga' dbang phyug nyid rab tu dges pa'i gsung gis/ rje 'di chos kyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal tshab
dam par dbang bskur/ de'i tshe rje btsun de nyid kyi drung du dpal kye rdo rje'i bka' babs bzhi'i dbang bskur ba sogs gsan cing / gzhan yang snga phyir bdag med ma'i dbang
/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi byin rlabs/ ku ru kulle'i byin

rlabs/ 'dod rgyal gyi rjes gnang / de gnyis dang 'brel ba'i yi ge ngor lugs mar grags pa cha tshang gi lung / nag po chen po lha brgyad/ dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa/ pu tra ming
sring rnams kyi rjes gnang / de dag dang rjes su 'brel ba'i yi ge'i lung rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po nas brgyud pa cha tshang / bdag chen kun rin pa nas brgyud pa'i
thun mong ma yin pa'i man ngag 'ga' zhig dang bcas pa gsan te/ de'i skabs su rje btsun kun dga' dbang phyug pa des rje 'di la khyed kyis gdan sa'i 'dzin skyong tshul bzhin
du mdzad de sde 'di la gang phan dang / khyad par rje sems dpa' chen po'i drung du ngor lugs kyi lam 'bras sogs gsan nas bstan pa la phan pa rgya che ba zhig mdzad dgos/
de bzhin ma mdzad na nga'i blo kha mi rdzogs pa yod do gsungs pa sogs lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas thugs brtse bas skyong bar mdzad cing / de nas dgung lo bco lnga pa sa pho
stag gi lo mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan zhes mtshan yongs la grags pa de nyid/ e waM gyi gdan sa 'phrod nas mus la phebs pa'i lam zhor la/ grub pa
mchog gi gnas bar sdings zhes bya bar gdan drangs te/ mkhan po 'dul ba 'bum sde'i mnga' bdag ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa yongs kyi gtsug gi nor bu sems dpa' chen
po de nyid dang / rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa'i dpal gyi rnam par rol pa/ bdag chen chos kyi rje gzhi thog pa kun dga' dbang
phyug pas las kyi slob dpon/ 'dul ba 'dzin pa sangs

rgyas dpal grub kyis grib tshod pa/ mkhan chen dkon blo ba la sogs pa rnams kyis grogs dan dang kha skong mdzad nas/ smin drug zla ba'i tshes bcu'i nyi ma gung gi cha la dge
tshul gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa bzhes te/ de nas bzung dge tshul gyi bslab pa'i gzhi bcu char gtogs dang bcas pa thams cad mig gi 'bras bu ltar gces par srung bar mdzad
cing / yang dgung lo bcu drug pa sa mo yos kyi lo la rje 'di nyid kyi thugs dgongs la sde snod kyi phyogs la mkhas grags thon pa zhig cis kyang mdzad dgongs pa shar nas
mtshan nyid phyogs kyi gzhung mang du gzigs rtog mdzad pa'i tshe/ rje kun dga' dbang phyug pa'i zhal nas/ deng sang khyed la bar chad kyi ltas cung zad 'dug pas re zhig
la gzigs rtog 'di 'then la/ dges pa rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen cig cis kyang mdzad pa 'thad gsungs pa ltar/ dpon slob gnyis kyis gzims khang dmar mor sku mtshams mdzad pas/ zla
ba gcig tsam song ba'i tshe/ rje 'di sku khams bde rgyu med tsam dang thugs yul du bde dog che rab byung ba'i skabs su thugs dam la rtse gcig tu 'bad pas/ lan cig nyi
ma snga dro'i cha'i gzigs snang la phyag g.yas g.yon gyi gru mo nas sbrul nag po 'dom re tsam re mngon sum du 'thon pas/ de 'phral sku khams shin tu dwangs pa dang thugs
dam gyi bogs kyang gzhan dang mi 'dra ba byung ste/ gzhi bsnyen kha skong gi sbyin sreg tshun chad kyang grub par mdzad/ de'i ring la rje sems dpa' chen po ngor la phebs
pa'i zhor la rje 'di'i bu sgo'i 'gag tu phebs nas byin rlabs dang zhal bkod mang du

mdzad/ khyad par kha skong gi sbyin sreg gi tshe lha sngags kyi grangs gtso che bas de cis kyang ma chad pa cig mdzod ces gsung ba phebs/ de nas slob dpon chen po sangs rgyas
dpal grub pas thub pa dgongs gsal/ rigs gter rang 'grel/ dag ljon skor gsum/ kye rdor/ gsang 'dus la sogs pa'i phyag khrid sogs phul zhes grags la/ nyi lder chos rje ngag
dbang grags pa'i drung du yang bde mchog gi dbang / bsam mi khyab kyi byin rlabs la sogs pa dbang lung man ngag byin rlabs la sogs pa du ma gsan cing / de nas dgung lo
bcu dgu bzhes pa chu pho rta'i lo bdag chen kun dga' dbang phyug pa zhing gzhan du gshegs pa dang / de ma thag rje nyid kyis dge sdings nas phebs te rje btsun pa'i thugs
dgongs rdzogs thabs kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa sgrub par mdzad cing / gdan sa chen po'i rtsis bzhes kyang gnang ste/ de ltar dgung lo nyi shu'i bar du gdan sa chen po
dge sdings/ bar sdings sogs gang dges su gsan sbyong thugs dam sogs mdor na thos bsam sgom gsum dus gcig tu nyams su bzhes par mdzad pa yin no/ /de nas rje btsun kun dga'
dbang phyug pa'i zhal chem las ji ltar byung ba bzhin/ dgung lo nyer gcig bzhes pa shing pho spre'u'i lo mus la phebs par bzhed pa na/ ma rungs pa 'ga' zhig gis phyogs lhung
gi dbang gis bzhed don la bar chad bya dogs pas/ thog mar skyed lhas su sku mtshams la phebs pa'i tshul mdzad/ de khog nas dpon slob nyung shas gdong dga' bar du zhabs

thang du srod la gsang thabs su phebs pas/ mtsho por phebs pa dang / mtsho po nang pa bsod nams dpal 'byor bya bas chibs pa dang 'phral kyi sku chas 'dra yang phul/ de nas
rim gyis phebs pas mus su mus chen sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan gyi drung du gegs med du mjal/ mjal ma thag tu thugs kyi dad pa tshad med pa 'khrungs shing /
rje sems dpa' chen pos kyang bsu ba ser phreng sogs bkur sti dpag tu med pa gnang zhing / de nas bdag nyid chen po 'di rten rnams kyi nang nas dge slong gi rten nyid mdo
rgyud mang po nas lan cig ma yin par yang yang bsngags pa rgya cher brjod cing mchog tu gsungs pa rnams kyis thugs yid 'phrogs te/ lo de'i tha skar zla ba'i tshes bcu'i
nyin mkhas grub du mas zhabs kyis bcags pa'i gnas mchog ya ma bde ldan chos rdzong gi ri khrod du mkhan po yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i mnga' bdag rje sems dpa' chen po nyid dang
/ las kyi slob dpon zha lu ba chos rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / gsang ste ston pa'i slob dpon sle lung mkhan po dkon mchog blo gros pa/ 'dul ba 'dzin pa chen po blo gros
rin chen pas grib tshod pa mdzad de dad pa'i dge 'dun 'khor 'dul ba 'dzin pa bcu gnyis dang bcas pa'i dbus su sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la zhugs la yongs su rdzogs pa
bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i dge slong gi dngos por bsgrubs te ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan 'dzin pa kun gyi gtsug gi nor bur gyur nas/ de nas bzung ltung ba sde lnga char gtogs
dang bcas pa'i dri ma mtha' dag dang bral zhing / khrims nyis brgya lnga bcu rtsa

gsum la g.yel ba med par gces spras su mdzad pa yin la/ dam pa 'di nyid kyi drung du rdo rje theg pa'i gsang ba zab mo'i bka' drin nos pa'i tshul ni/ zhabs drung du phebs ma
thag tu thog mar gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang / byin rlabs/ bskyed rdzogs kyi nyams khrid/ de la nye bar mkho ba'i lus sbyong 'phrul 'khor/ bskyed rdzogs kyi gzhung la sogs
pa gsan cing / gzhan yang blo sbyong don bdun mar grags pa'i nyams khrid dang / rgyal sras thogs med pas mdzad pa'i rtsa tshig gi lung la sogs pa blo sbyong skor du ma
dang / gzhan yang rgyud gsum gyi bshad bka' dang / 'khor lo bde mchog gi dbang lung man ngag du ma dang / nA ro mkha' spyod kyi chos skor/ rje rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang
po'i bka' 'bum thog gcig rje nyid kyi bka' 'bum yongs rdzogs kyi lung la sogs pa du ma zhig gsan te/ de'i skabs su bdag nyid chen po 'dis rje sems dpa' chen po la ni
gu chos drug spyod khrid sogs chos sna mang po zhig thor bkod nas 'di rnams gnang dgos tshul zhus pas/ rje sa chen gyi rnam thar gnang nas/ khyed rang gi chos rnams 'di
na yod pas 'di la gzigs/ 'di nang gi nged rang gis thob pa rnams 'bul gsung ba byung ba dang / de mthun dus gsum gyi rgyal ba thams cad kyi bgrod pa gcig pa'i lam po che/
rnal 'byor dbang phyug birWa pa'i gsung gi man ngag rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras rnams la snyan brgyud bzhi bar ma chad par byon pa'i gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu
dang bcas pa'i gdams pa zab mo gsan

par mdzad de/ de yang snang gsum gyi khrid rnams dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po dang lhan cig tu gsan cing / sngags lam tshugs nas dpon slob nyung shas la tshogs bshad zab khrid
kyi tshul du gnang / de nas gsol ja lta bu re'i bar la thun mong ma yin pa'i slob bshad snyan brgyud du bzhugs pa rnams rje 'di nyid kho na la chig brgyud du gnang ste/
de ltar lam 'bras yongs su rdzogs pa zhar byung dang bcas pa dang / kye rdo rje'i rgyu lam gyi dbang dang / gzhan yang 'di dang 'brel ba'i byin rlabs dang / yig cha'i
lung la sogs pa chos kyi sgo du ma gsan cing / gsung ngag rin po che'i bstan pa rje 'di la gtad par mdzad pa dang / de'i sras kyi thu bo zha lu ba sangs rgyas dpal bzang
dang / grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ chos rje blo gros rin chen/ chos rje dpal ldan rgyal po rnams la yang dbang dang byin rlabs/ rjes gnang / lung man ngag mang po zhig
gsan te thos pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son par gyur to/ /de nas mus su bzhugs pa'i skabs der/ a gro dge grags bya ba cig dang / dbon po chos dge phan la sogs pa khams pa'i
grwa pa 'ga' zhig gis khams phyogs la skor cig phebs na bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa rgya chen po 'grub tshul sogs rgyu mtshan nan gyis phul bas zhal gyis bzhes
te/ de bzhin gyi rgyu mtshan sems dpa' chen po la phul ba na/ de bzhin gnang na legs pa 'ong gsung ba'i bka' lung gnang sbyin rdzong ba dang bcas pa gnang ste/ de nas spre'u'i
lo de'i ston sa skya ru phebs nas/ de nas dpon slob nyung shas shig khams phyogs su

phebs pa'i chibs kha bsgyur te/ lam bar rnams su yang gdul bya dpag tu med pa smin grol la bkod cing rim gyis phebs pa na/ sngar gcen rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan gyis khams
phyogs la phebs pa'i dus su btab pa'i dgon pa don grub gling zhes bya bar spyan drangs te phebs pa'i tshe/ dus phyis sa phyogs der sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud sogs 'byon
bzhud nyung ba'i stabs kyis mi bdag bdag tu re ba'i rlom sems can/ yul de nas pha tshad phyin pa na karma pa'i sgar pa dpon slob tshan gcig yod pa rnams kyis/ rje nyid
der phebs pa la phrag dog gis kun nas bslangs pa'i skur zhus sogs mi dad pa'i rnam 'gyur mang po byas pa dang / der gnas pa'i grwa pa rnams kyis ma bzod de/ sa skya pa mthu'i
bdag po yin pas da lan bstan pa la dgongs nas 'di rnams la mthu'i rtags thon pa cig cis kyang mdzad dgos/ de bzhin ma mdzad na phyin chad phyogs 'dir sa skya pa'i sgra
tsam mi grag pa cig yong zhes yang yang nan bskyed nas zhus pa la brten nas/ khong rnams la zhag bdun gyi dus btab nas dpon slob bdun gyis pu tra la brten pa'i las sbyor
zhig mdzad pa na/ zhag gsum song ba'i nub mo sgrub khang du 'od 'khyug pa dang / thog 'tsheg pa dang / 'brub khung du lingga skad ngan 'don pa sogs nang rtags kyi cho
'phrul sna tshogs zhig byung zhing / /de dus karma pa'i sgar de'i dpon 'og ma bka' bgros pa/ rje nyid la skur zhus byed pa'i gtso bo gcig yod pa de rgyu ma rul nas nyam
thag pa'i skad 'don zhing tshe'i dus byas/ de ltar drag po'i las kyi

rtags mngon sum du mthong ba la brten nas snyan pa'i grags pas sa steng khyab par gyur ces kyang khums so/ /yang lan cig rma khams phyogs la thegs pa'i rma chu gtsang po zhes
bya ba'i chu klung shin tu che ba zhig gi rtsar sgar pa sngon ma rnams slebs nas der sdod pa'i grabs byas pa na/ rje nyid rjes su phebs nas da lta chu la 'gro ba'i grabs
kyis phebs pa na/ chag phyi ba rnams kyis mgrin gcig tu do nub thang yang chad/ nyi ma yang phyi mor song 'dug pas 'di khar bzhugs na legs pa 'dra zhes nan gyis zhus kyang
ma gsan par mchod g.yog pa nam shes la mgon po'i gtor ma gcig da lta 'chos la chu 'di la rgyob gsungs pa'i bka' lung mdzad pa na/ khong gis kyang de bzhin byas pas chu
la che chung du mngon pa gang yang ma byung / der rjes rje nyid kyis gtor ma gcig chu la gnang ba na/ lcags kyi tho lum me 'bar ba chur 'phangs pa ltar sgra 'jigs su rung
ba byung zhing / chu de yang de ma thag sum gnyis dri ba tsam song / der rje rang gis chu de la sngon la phebs shing / der rjes gzhan rnams kyang bar chad med par pha
rol tu sleb pa tsam na/ chu de sngar bas kyang bcu 'gyur gyis che ba tsam du song bas/ thams cad ngo mtshar zhing blo bde bar gyur/ de nas rje'i gsung gis mgon po la gtang
rag gi mchod gtor phul thams cad bde bar sdod gsungs/ de'i rgyu mtshan yul phyogs de na gnas pa'i skye bo rnams kyis thos pa na/ sngar rma chu gtsang po la sus kyang rab
ma 'thon pa la da lan 'di 'dra ba'i rab 'don pa 'di lta bu su zhig yin nam zhes thams cad 'jigs shing ha las nas

ngo mtshar ba'i gtam du gleng bar byed do/ /de nas yang yul phyogs gzhan zhig tu byon pa na/ bon po gdug pa can 'ga' zhig gis sngar gyi lo rgyus rnams thos pas zhe 'jigs kyang
phrag dog gi dbang gis/ dpon slob rnams la sngar thog lam rgyun par yod pa'i sa shin tu gnyan pa/ su yang sdod mi nus pa zhig tu sgar khung bstan te der bzhugs pa na/
srod thum pa nas sprin nag 'dus 'brug sgra shin tu drag po dang / glog phreng rgyun ma chad par tho rangs kyi bar du byung zhing / mi ma yin gyi cho 'phrul sbal pa nag po
shin tu che ba 'jigs su rung ba gcig cha ther gyi nang du byung ba la/ rje nyid kyis khro bcu'i srung 'khor dang / bde mchog gi go cha drug la brten pa'i srung 'khor gdug
rtsub ma zhi'i bar du mdzad cing / de nas zhag 'ga' yar gyi bar gang phebs par sprin nag po bya ra byed pa'i rnam pa byung ba de je 'gyangs je 'gyangs su song zhing thog
la sogs pa bar chad kyi rnam pa gang yang ma byung bas/ der gnas pa'i mi kun gyis gnas 'dir bzhugs tshugs pa 'di pa dpon slob las ma byung zer zhing / thams cad ha las
pas thun mong ma yin pa'i dad pa thob par gyur pa la sogs pa mthu stobs nus pa bsam gyis mi khyab cing gdul bya gang la gang 'dod la chos kyi dga' ston stsol bzhin par khams
kyi stod smad bar gsum du lo gsum yar mar lo gnyis te kun dril bas lo lnga'i bar du khams phyogs kyi 'gro ba rnams thar pa'i lam la 'god par mdzad pa yin zhes bshad
la/ de nas khams phyogs kyi dad pa dang ldan pa'i skye bo rnams kyis

'bul pa'i dngos po bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ba rnams dang bcas gdan sa chen por gegs med du phebs/ rje btsun 'jam dbyangs chen po yab sras kyis gtso mdzad gdan sa chen por
bzhugs pa rnams la 'bul ba'i dngos po tshad las 'das pa phul zhing rten so so la yang snyan dar la sogs pa mchod pa rgya chen po mdzad de/ de nas chu pho 'brug gi lo la
yab 'jam dbyangs chen po sku gshegs pa'i gshegs rdzong rgya chen po bsgrubs/ gzhi thog bla brang chos gzhis dang bcas pa thams cad gcen la phul te/ bdag nyid bya bral kho
na la thugs gtad nas/ 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang po'i drung du slar yang nges don gyi nying khu zab lam rdo rje'i rnal 'byor sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i bka' drin gsan
cing / lo de'i hor zla bcu pa la rgyal mkhar rtse nas spyan drangs te nor bu khyung rtser phebs nas/ dpon blon rnams la gsung chos kyi bka' drin stsal/ de nas slar yang
mus su phebs nas rje sems dpa' chen po'i sku gdung mjal ba dang / rje sangs rgyas dpal bzang / grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ chos rje blo rin pa rnams la rgyud sde bzhi
dang 'brel ba'i chos skor du ma zhig gsan pa dang / rje nyid kyis kyang dam pa de dag la gsung chos kyi bdud rtsi ci yang zhig stsal zhing / yang bar skabs su rje btsun
gcen gyi drung dang / theg chen chos rje'i zhal slob chos rje dpal ldan legs pa'i zhabs dang / rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug la sogs pa rnams la yang chos kyi
sgo du ma gsan nas thugs su chud par mdzad cing / gsan pa de dag kyang tshig don la sgro

'dogs legs par bcad de nyams su bzhes par mdzad pa yin te/ dus rgyun du nyin zhag re re nyams bzhes kyi rim pa'ang / lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ kye rdo rje'i bskyed pa'i
rim pa lam dus kyi dbang blang ba dang bcas pa bzlas brjod kyis mtha' brgyan pa/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi rnal 'byor bzlas pa dang bcas pa/ bir srung thun mong dang thun
mong ma yin pa/ lU nag dril gsum gyi bskyed rdzogs bzlas pa dang bcas pa/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i bskyed rim/ rdzogs rim spros med kyi rnal 'byor dang bcas pa/ 'jigs byed bskyed
rim bzlas bcas thun bzhi'am gnyis gang rung re dang / gzhan yang tshe dpag med la sogs pa lha'i rnal 'byor phra mo du ma dang / maNDal sgrub mchod sngon du 'gro ba'i
sgo nas bstan srung rnams la mchod gtor 'bul ba/ bskang gso'i rim pa dang bcas pa ma chag pa mdzad cing / de dag gi mtshams su bzlas pa/ gtor ma/ klog pa/ tsha tsha 'debs
pa/ bskor ba mdzad pa/ snod ldan la chos 'khor bskor ba sogs mdor na chos spyod bcus dus 'da' ba dang / de dag kyang lta ba'i rtsis zin par mdzad pa zhig go /de lta bu'i
bdag nyid chen po 'di ni rje sa skya pa chen po nyid slar yang rang gi rigs su rnam par sprul pa'i gar gyi rol par snang ste/ gong du smos pa ltar sems dpa' chen pos sa
chen gyi rnam thar rje 'di la gnang nas/ khyed rang gi chos 'di na yod gsungs pa dang / bse 'bag dang lhan cig tu rgya gar nas byung ba'i bse'i ga'u'i nang na yod pa'i
sgrub thabs sogs kyi yi ge deng sang ga na

yod dkar chag sogs su mi gsal ba la/ rje 'di'i gsung las/ sa chen zer ba'i bgres po des gter du sbas pa yin pa 'dug gsungs pa dang / sgo rum dpe khang sogs kyi rje sa chen
gyi phyag bris gang yin thogs med du mkhyen pa la/ rje btsun rdo ring pa chen pos/ 'di ltar mkhyen pa'i rgyu mtshan gang lags zhus pas/ de'i rgyu mtshan shin tu che ba gcig
yod/ de tsam gyis chog gzhan la sgros ye ma btang gsungs pa sogs rgyu mtshan mang du snang zhing / gzhan yang 'di'i ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar ni kha'u'i chu tshan du thugs
dam la 'byams pa'i dus su/ lus dkyil gyi lha brgya lnga bcu rtsa bdun mngon sum du gzigs shing / de'i nang nas gsang gnas kyi lha tshogs cung zad mi gsal ba dang / snying
ga'i lha tshogs shin tu gsal zhing 'od zer 'phro ba zhig 'dug pa la/ nged rang la 'phrin las kyi brgyud 'dzin ha cang mi mang / gang yod nges don la blo kha phyogs
pa kho na yong ba 'dug ces gsung bar grags la/ gzhan yang 'di ni mthu stobs kyi dbang phyug chen po grub pa'i mtshan ma phyogs med du ston pa zhig ste skyed lhas su 'jigs
byed drug cu pa'i phyag len gyi 'grig gnang dus/ rdo ring kun spangs pa sogs slob ma kha cig gis zhal ras kyi mdangs mthing nag tu 'gyur ba gzigs pa dang / lum pa chos mdzad
pas dbu la rwa sngo seng seng 'dug pa mthong ba dang / gzhan yang 'phan yul du gtor ma la me 'bar ba kun gyis mthong ba dang / rgyal rtser rje 'di'i zhabs sa la ma reg
par bar snang la phebs par 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog bzang pos gzigs

shing / yang skabs shig tu gzhi thog gi mkhas btsun chen pos thugs dam 'chams mgon gyi drung du gsung bsnyen zhig mdzad pa'i tshe/ mgon po zhal mngon sum du gzigs pa'i phyag
dpung g.yon gyi steng du me 'bar ba dang / gri gug gi rdo rje'i phyogs bzhi'i ra med pa dbus ma la me 'bar ba gzigs snang la byung ba dang / gzhan yang dpal ldan lha mos
a gro'i dgon pa don grub gling du zhal gzigs nas/ 'khor gyi tshul bzung ba'i dam nyams gcig 'dug pa ngas sgrol/ nga la yang bskang gso cig rtsoms gsungs pa la brten nas
lha mo'i bskang gso khyad par can zhig kyang mdzad/ dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa ni phod kha sngon po bzhes pa can gcig tu yang yang gzigs pa dang / yang lan cig skyed lhas su
mgon po 'di bram ze dkar po'i rnam pa/ dar dkar po'i na bza' can phyag g.yas na rtse gsum dang snying 'dzin pa/ g.yon na thod khrag 'dzin pa/ yum bzhi dang bcas pa mngon
sum du gzigs te/ de phyin chad mgon khang der phebs res kyi de 'dra'i tshul gyis bsu ba la yang mgon po 'di nyid 'byon zhes grags la/ yang dam can pu tra ming sring rnams
ni rgyun du bran ltar 'khol ba ste/ sa skyar bzhugs pa'i skabs shig rje rang gi gsung gis/ mdang pu tra 'dis mi mgo dar gyis dril ba cig khyer nas 'ur sgra dang bcas sgo
rum la song zhes gsungs pa dang / yang lan cig skyed lhas su sde dpon zhig gi gtor gsos zhig byung dus/ sum cu rtsa gsum bya ba'i sgrub khang gi steng du sngags pa nag
po thod phreng can zhig gis ma Ni bskul

ba'i 'chams gdangs byas pa na/ kha'u'i lung pa thams cad 'dar ling ling 'ong gin 'dug gsung ba dang / skyed lhas rgyal po 'di mgon po'i 'khor gyi ru 'dren cig yin pa 'dra/
lha 'dre gzhan 'di tsho skyed lhas mgon khang gi nang du ye yong mi nus 'dug na'ang / 'di thal mar yong gin 'dug gsung ba dang / skyed lhas kyi shing phung re re'i rtsa ba
na'ang mgon po'i 'khor du gtogs pa'i lha 'dre gdug pa can re re gnas pa yin gsung ba sogs 'od gsal gyi ngang nas thams cad thogs med du gzigs shing / yang lan cig skyed
lhas mgon khang du sku mtshams bdun phrag gcig mdzad pa na/ yum chen bzhi khrag gi ral pa shin tu ring ba dang bcas phebs nas gtang rag dgos zer yus pa'i tshul gyis ral
pa sprugs pa'i khrag gi zegs ma rje rang gi sku la yang thor thor yong ba dang / de nas ma tshad na byad ma mgo la gser gyi dbu rgyan gon pa/ byad mdangs med cing cung zad
ser ba/ ngo nongs pa'i tshul gyis 'dug pa gzigs pa dang / yang gal che ba cig gi tshe mgon po 'khor bcas las la bskul ba na/ las de mthar phyin par grub pa'i tshe rje'i
gzigs snang la/ lung pa shin tu yangs pa cig gi dkyil na tshur mgon po nyid mi dpon chen po'i tshul gyis rta nag po gcig la chibs/ phyag g.yas pas mdung bskor mdzad kyin
mdun ma len na 'di bzhin len pa yin gsungs nas zhal pho 'don pa'i rnam pa mdzad cing 'byon pa gzigs pa dang / yang skyed lhas su sku mtshams dam par mdzad pa'i skabs shig
na/ 'byung po chen po dge bshes kyi chas su byas snam sbyar ber thul

sogs brtsegs ma mang rab gyon/ lag tu gtor ma khyer 'khor stobs che ba dang bcas kha'u'i gzhung lam la zhugs/ phyag 'tshal sgang du slebs pa na 'phags pa brag khung gi 'debs
la dpal mgon chen po'i sku bram gzugs rje rang gi phyag bris ma cig bkram yod pa las/ 'od zer sngo nag phyogs mtshams kun tu 'phro ba dang dus mnyam du mi rkang gi gling
bu'i sgra skad shin tu che ba grag pa cig bus byung bas/ skad cig de nyid la bar snang la sprin nag po 'khrigs 'byung po yod pa'i sa der thog ser shin tu drag pa cig babs
song bas/ 'byung po 'khor bcas gar song cha med du song ba byung ba dang / yang lan cig nor bu khyung rtser phebs pa'i tshe/ chos rje rkyang 'dur ba dpon slob dang gzims
khang steng 'og mdzad nas bzhugs/ rje dpon slob rnams kyis tshoms 'og tu chos skyong rnams las la bskul ba'i rol mo drag brdungs mdzad pa na/ steng du chos rje rkyang
'dur ba'i dgongs pa la/ mtshan nyid rgan po'i skyon gyis bslad pas/ rnga brdungs 'di rang la 'byung chen po med dam snyam pa byung / de nas cung zad song ba'i dus chos rje
rkyang 'dur ba'i gzigs snang la/ sprul pa'i mi nag khyi nag bya nag sogs pho nya mang pos 'byung po chen po snam sbyar ta hun gser ma thang theb gyon pa dang bcas pa'i
ske nas zhags pas bzung lag pa bsdams pa cig dkar khung gi mthongs ka nas tshoms chen 'og ma'i 'brub khung nang du thogs med du khrid song ba gzigs/ zhag gcig song rjes phyir
shor song ba dang / dgongs thun gyi thugs dam gyi tshe slar yang

gong bzhin khrid nas mthu dang stobs med par dam la thogs pa gzigs te/ mi phyed pa'i dad pa thob cing de phyin chad rnga brdungs la yid gang yod ches pa cig byung zhes grags
pa dang / gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po 'di ni mthu dang nus pa'i mnga' bdag tu gyur pa'i stobs kyis 'dis sgrig par mdzad pa'i po ti me 'bar mar grags pa de/ gzims dpon
nam shes grogs mched kyis rgyal rtse nas blang ste sa skyar khyer 'ong ba'i lam zhong nga'i mdar chom rkun pa 'ga' zhig gis phrogs te khyer nas khong rnams kyi yul du phyin
pa na/ yul der mi 'dod pa'i ltas sna tshogs byung zhing / khyad par phyag dpe gang du bzhag sar me 'bar bas khong rnams kyis nyer tshags ma nus par ra sa rdzong pa'i lag
tu byung / der yang cho 'phrul sna tshogs byung ste rnam rtog gi ngang du yod pa na/ re zhig nas sman grong drung rdor bas der byon dus de bzhin gyi gsung gleng byung
bas rje'i phyag dpe yin par nges te/ rdzong pa dngos kyis 'bul ma nus par drung rdor ba brgyud nas phul/ de phyin mgon pod 'di nyid la deng sang gi bar gyi bu phyi yang phyi
dang bcas pa kun la mgon pod me 'bar mar grags pa 'di byung zhing / de ltar bu'i ma phye bdag chen rang gi phyag dpe dngos de ni rgyal mkhar rtse ba'i zhal ngo rnams
kyi sku srung du bzhugs pa/ dus phyis drung 'phags pa tshul khrims pa'i phyag brgyud de sa skya pa sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' bsod nams bdag gi lag tu rtsol med du
byung ba deng sang skal ldan rnams kyi mchod pa'i yul du gdan sa 'di nyid na bzhugs pa 'di yin no/ /yang skabs shig gi tshe

gnas gsar pa'i gzhis rin chen sgang du phebs pa'i dus khong rnams kyis rtsis mgon gyi lha mo la bskang mdos phul ba'i tshe/ rje'i zhal nas khyed kyis lha mo la bskang mdos
yang yang dgos pa 'di 'dra lkog pa la gsungs pas/ lha mo cung zad ma mnyes par/ de nub tho rangs rje thugs dam la bzhugs pa'i mdun du shin tu 'jigs pa'i cha lugs su bstan
nas byung ba na/ bar chad bya bar ni ma nus/ rnal 'byor ba lta ba la sbyangs 'dug gsung zhal 'dzum pa dang bcas de nyid du mi snang bar gyur ces kyang grags la/ gzhan yang
'od gsal gyi ngang la thogs bcas kyi dngos po sgrib mi nus par ji lta ba bzhin gzigs par snang ste/ lan cig gdan sa'i bla brang shar na gsung chos gnang ba'i dus/ rgya
'dre dpon g.yog mang po sa skya'i nye skor na sgar rgyab/ skabs su dpon po de'i mgo thog tu gdugs nyi 'og tu slebs pa tsam byas/ sa skya la bskor ba phyin phyi log theng
re byas dus/ gdan sa 'dir rgya 'dre mi bsad sogs yong ba cig 'dug pa la/ rje 'di'i thugs dam lta ba'i ngang nas me dmigs mang du gnang bas/ zhag 'ga' nas gsung chos pa rnams
phyir 'gro ba dang mnyam du mi sog po'i rnam pa can 'jigs su rung ba lus po kun la mes tshig pa'i ri mo yod pa gcig rje'i drung du thogs med du byung nas zhabs dbang
cig dgos zhu ba la/ khyod su yin gsungs pas/ bdag rgya 'dre'i dpon 'og ma cig yin/ kha sang nas khyed kyis dmigs pa mdzad pa des nged thams cad tshig da lan dpon po na drags
sku mdun la yong ma thub/ da

nged rnams 'gro bas thugs dam lhod dgos zer/ 'di la zhabs dbang mi dga' 'am dgongs tsa na/ khos zhabs 'og tu mgo bcug nas khyed kyi slob ma brgyud 'dzin dang bcas pa la mi
gnod pa'i dam bca' 'bul/ khyed nam sangs rgyas pa'i dus nga 'khor gyi thog mar skye bar shog zer nas 'ja' yal ba ltar song ba dang / de nas rgya 'dre rnams kyang gnas 'dir
med par gyur to zhes grags pa la sogs pa mdor na gsang ba las kyang ches gsang ba'i rnam par thar pa mtha' yas pa zhig mnga' ba yin no/ /de nas dgung lo so drug bzhes pa
sa mo phag gi lo la rgyal mkhar rtse nas chos rgyal bkra shis rab brtan dpal bzang po yab sras rnams kyis slar yang spyan drangs te/ der slob dpon grwa rigs sogs brgya
dang lnga bcu tsam la gsung ngag rin po che'i gdams pa zab mo legs par stsal zhing / der ye shes mgon po dngos su bzhugs nges pa'i mgon khang khyad par du 'phags pa zhig
kyang bzhengs pa mdzad/ slar skyed lhas su phebs nas dam tshig dang ldan pa'i skye bo rnams la thugs brtse bar dgongs te/ mdzes byed ces bya ba chu mo yos kyi lo dam rdzas
'chi med ril bu sgrub par mdzad pas/ grom pa'i lung nang thams cad dri bzang gis khyab pa dang / me tog gi char 'bab pa dang / lhag par gong bu'i sgrub pa tshugs nas ril
bu'i sgrub pa mthar ma phyin gyi bar la/ thog mtha' bar gsum du shin tu gsal ba'i sgras ril bu khar song ba'i sems can thams cad skye ba bcu gnyis tshun chad la nges par
sangs rgya ba yod do zer ba'i mkha' 'gro'i lung bstan khyad par can

brnyes pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i rtags du ma byung zhing / de nas rong ston thams cad mkhyen pas 'debs par mdzad pa'i chos grwa chen po dpal nA lendra'i gtsug lag khang
de nyid du rong ston nyid nas gdan sa rim pa bdun song ba'i mtshams su/ gzhan phyogs kyi bstan 'dzin gyi gzugs su rlom pa'i ma rungs pa'i sems can 'ga' zhig gis grub mtha'i
kun slong ngan pa zhe la bzhag nas/ chos grwa der bzhugs pa'i bla ma/ slob dpon/ mi sna drag gtogs/ mdor na khang khyim tshun chad ma rung par byas te nyam thag pa'i
tshe/ rje 'di dang rdo rings kun spangs pa gnyis kyis gsang thabs su phebs te/ mkhas grub chen po mkhyen rab rin chen mchog grub dpal bzang po rong ston chen po'i rgyal tshab
tu mnga' gsol/ lhag par de'i skabs su phrag dog gis rang nyid shin tu myos shing rang dbang mi thub pa'i gzhan phyogs kyi bshes gnyen du khas 'che ba'i chos rje smon
lam pa bya ba des/ ngan g.yo'i sbyor ba mngon mtshan can 'ga' byas shing / rje 'di la yang deng sang nA lendra na sa skya pa'i btsun chung tshe zad cig sleb yod pa 'dug
zer ba sogs rlom sems kyi tshig ngan 'brug ltar bsgrags pa'i tshe/ de dag la thugs brtse bas nye bar dgongs te/ rje nyid kyis gnas der ched du gtad pa'i thugs dam mdzad cing
/ dro sa'i phug ser du mgon po'i gtor chen mdzad pa'i tshe nub gcig mnal lam du/ phug pa'i rtsa bar nged 'di lta bu'i mi drag pa rang bcu gnyis shi zer ba'i dud mo'i
sgra lhang lhang ba byung zhing / rje 'di nyid kyi thugs dam

gyi nyams snang la mgon po'i las mkhan rnams kyis gser gyi mchod rten chen po 'od 'bar ba zhig dum bur gtubs kyin 'dug pas nang thams cad sol ba dang lham krad kyis brgyang
'dug pa gcig byung ste/ de'i tshe dgun shin tu grang ba'i dus yin kyang / nam phyed zin la khad pa tsam gyi tshod la dpal ldan sa skya'i bstan srung dbang po rnams kyi cho
'phrul gyi sprin nag po shin tu 'jigs su rung ba dpag tu med pa glo bur du nam mkha' la 'dus te/ skyid 'phan gnyis char du tshor ba'i 'brug gi sgra shin tu grag pa dang
/ glog gi 'od 'khyug pa dang bcas rbod gtong byed pa'i byad ma de'i mgo la gnam lcags kyi thog chen po mi bzad pa babs pa nas/ las ngan pa'i sbyor ba byed pa'i lus dang
phral nas/ sems nyid dag pa'i zhing du skad cig de nyid la spor bar mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang chos grwa chen po de nyid du zab rgyas chos kyi sgron me sbar te/ rong ston
thams cad mkhyen pas bstan pa'i srog shing 'dzugs par mdzad do/ /de ltar mthu dang nus pa'i sgo nas grub pa'i mtshan ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig bstan cing / gzhan yang
mkhas pa'i bya ba rnam pa gsum gyi sgo nas kyang bstan pa rin po che ches cher gsal bar mdzad pa zhig ste/ de yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis snga phyir gsung ngag rin po
che'i tshogs bshad dang / slob bshad 'dres pa'i tshar nyi shu rtsa grangs tsam gyis thog drangs/ sde snod gsum dang rgyud sde rin po che bzhi dang 'brel ba'i chos kyi sgo
mtha' yas pa stsal nas 'gro ba mang po smin cing grol bar mdzad pas bka' drin thob pa'i zhal slob kyang sa chen po'i rdul tsam

bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod pa rnams zhib tu bgrang bar ga la nus/ rags pa tsam dper mtshon na/ chos rje zha lu pa sangs rgyas dpal bzang / grub chen dkon mchog blo gros/ chos
rje blo gros rin chen/ paN chen dpal ldan rgyal po ste phan tshun bka' drin rjes su nos pa'i dam pa bzhi/ yang paNDi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan dri med legs pa'i blo
gros/ mdo sngags chos kyi mnga' bdag kun mkhyen bstan pa'i nyi ma bsod nams seng ge mi nyag paNDi ta grags pa rdo rje/ mkhas pa chen po zhu ba bsod nams rin chen/ rtse thang
rab 'byams pa sangs rgyas lhun grub ste 'dzam gling yongs su grags pa'i mkhas mchog chen po lnga/ 'khon gyi gdung brgyud bdag chen bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ shar pa 'jam
dbyangs chen po'i gdung brgyud slob dpon chen po kun dga' bkra shis pa ste gangs can chen por grags pa'i skyes bu gnyis dang / gzhan yang dpal 'khor bde chen gyi mkhan
po bde ba'i 'byung gnas/ rkyang 'dur chos rje dkon mchog dpal ba/ mkhas pa'i dbang po bsod nams blo gros/ rab 'byams dbang po dkon mchog tshul khrims/ chos rje chos skyong
rgyal mtshan/ yang dgon chos rje dpal ldan bkra shis pa/ sgo rum pa kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros/ gser mdog can gyi gdan sa pa chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa ste gsung
ngag gi gsang ba 'dzin pa'i dam pa brgyad/ yongs rdzogs snyan brgyud zab mo'i rgya mtsho 'gran zla kun dang bral ba'i thugs sras rje btsun rdo ring pa chen po kun spangs
chos kyi nyi ma la sogs pa

bsam gyis khyab pa zhig bskrun nas rgyal ba'i bstan pa rin po che phyogs dus kun du ches cher gsal bar mdzad pa yin la/ rtsod pa dngos stobs kyi rigs pas log smra sun dbyung
ba'i tshul ni/ gsung ngag lam 'bras kyi brgyud 'dzin rdzong lugs pa 'ga' zhig gi bzhed pa/ snang gsum khrid kyi sngon du rgyu dus kyi dbang nges par 'gro dgos pa rnal 'byor
dbang phyug brgyud pa dang bcas pa mtha' gcig tu bzhed pa yin zhes smra ba dang / kha cig gis mngon par rtogs pa tshul bco lnga po ngos 'dzin pa'i skabs su/ le'u brgyad
pa nas gsungs pa'i yum gyi mngon rtogs de 'dren pa rnams la dngos stobs kyi rigs pa phul du byung ba dang / de'i rgyab brten du rje btsun chen po'i gsung rnams yid ches
kyi lung du mdzad de/ mdor na lan gyis bzlog par mi nus pa'i lung rigs rnams kyis sgo nas grub mtha' mi 'dra ba rnams sun byung nas/ bstan pa'i snying po gsal bar mdzad
pa yin cing / yang rtsom pa mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ bdag nyid chen po sa paN gyis rang gi brjod pa bde zhing gzhan gyis rtogs par sla ba/ gnyis ka'i rna bar snyan pa zhig
sdeb sbyor gyi gtsug lag shes pa las 'byung bas zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi don rnams yongs su tshang ba'i gsung rab kyi tshogs kyang / sems dpa' chen po'i bstod pa/ yab 'jam
dbyangs chen po la bstod pa la sogs pa bstod pa dang gsol 'debs kyi skor du ma dang / gsung ngag gi khrid yig brda don gsal ba'i khrid yig dam tshig gi rnam bshad 'khrul
spangs rab gsal la sogs pa khrid yig dang rnam bshad kyi skor mang po

dang / gzhan yang sgrub thabs/ dkyil chog byin rlabs kyi yi ge sogs dang / 'jigs byed/ bde mchog kye rdor/ dmar po skor gsum rnams kyi chos skor bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang
/ khyad par chos skyong skor gyi 'khu ldog spong ba'i yi ge bsnyen pa'i yi ge spogs chog gi yi ge bka' bsgo/ bkra shis/ mchod gtor 'bul tshul gyi yi ge sogs shin tu zab cing
rgya che ba bgrang ba las 'das pa zhig mdzad nas gsang chen zab mo'i bstan pa mchog tu gsal bar mdzad pa ni ches ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par thar par snang ngo / /de ltar
dam pa 'dis bstan 'gro'i don so skye'i blos dpag par dka' ba zhig mdzad nas zhing 'di nyid kyi gdul bya'i don rgya chen po grub par dgongs te/ zhing khams gzhan du 'byon
pa dang nye ba'i ston gyi dus su skyed lhas kyi se 'bru rnams kyang cher ma skyes shing / skyes pa rnams kyang de ma thag skam 'gro ba dang / de'i dgun shin tu grang ba'i
dus su grom pa'i chu cher rgyas nas bla brang zam 'og tu ma shong bar tshogs chen por lud pa dang / sa chen po 'di yang nas yang du g.yos/ dus ma yin pa'i sgra grag pa
dang / 'od 'khyug pa la sogs pa'i ltas du ma byung bas skye bo gzhan rnams the tshom du gyur te/ de skabs su sku khams cung zad ma bde ba na/ rje'i gsung gis dge slong don
rgyal la/ btsun pa shi ba'i shul du nor mang po lus pa 'di don du'ang mi 'gyur zhing / 'jig rten pa rnams kyis kyang 'phyar ka'i gnas su byed pas/ dngos po thams cad dge
'dun gyi zhabs tog la thong gsung ba'i zhal ta

gnang / de nas skyed lhas nas gdan sa chen po 'dir phebs te/ gdan sa bka' bgros pa rnams kyis sku rim rgya chen po bsgrubs shing / sman dpyad la sogs pa rje'i zhabs tog rgya
chen po bsgrubs/ de dag gi skabs su rje nyid ni thugs bde nyams shin tu che zhing / nang du zag med kyi ye shes thugs rgyud la 'khrungs pa'i rtags su ha ha hi hi la sogs
pa nyams mnan pas mi non pa phyi rol nas thos pa byung ba dang / gzhan yang bla ma yi dam chos skyong la sogs pa dag pa'i gzigs snang mang pos dus 'da' ba byung zhing /
lhag par lan cig gi tshe yun ring por spyan nam mkha' la cher gzigs nas/ 'o mi rnams kyis nga la kho chos kyi rgyal po la mi mos zer e bden par 'dug chos kyi rgyal pos nga
la thugs rjes 'dzin par nges/ da lta rang rje btsun chen po dang / chos kyi rgyal po dang / rje btsun 'jam dbyangs chen po rnams sku 'od mer mer nam mkha'i mthongs na
bzhugs 'dug gsung ba dang / lan cig chag phyi ba du ma dang tsha mda' nas kyi 'tsho byed de drung na yod pa'i skabs su nub phyogs pha gi na 'od 'khyil le ba cig 'dug khyed
rnams kyis e mthong gsung ba dang / yang lan cig 'tsho byed de la/ 'tsho byed khyed kyi yid la mkha' 'gro ma 'di rnams kyis da lta rang gdan 'dren pa 'dra bsam pa e 'dug
de 'dra mi dgos ga le byas nas gdan drangs te 'gro yis gsung ba la sogs pa bla ma yi dam dpa' bo mkha' 'gro sogs gzigs pa'i nyams kyi gsung 'ba' zhig gsungs shing / de
ltar ngo mtshar ba'i rnam 'phrul du ma zhig gzigs

te/ de nas sku drang por bsrangs zhal lhor phyogs pa'i ngang nas rgyud sde rin po che nas gsungs pa'i 'da' kha ma'i rnal 'byor zab mos gsal btab ste dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa
gnyis pa shing mo yos kyi lo zla ba bzhi pa'i nyi ma shar dros tsam la gzhi thog bla brang du gzugs kyi sku'i dkyil 'khor chos kyi dbyings bde ba chen po'i ngang du bsdu
bar mdzad do/ /de ltar dgongs pa yongs su mya ngan las 'das nas kyang yun ring po'i bar du nam mkha' la 'ja' tshon dang lha'i spos kyi dri ngad khyad par can ldan pa dang
/ me tog gi char chen po 'bab pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung zhing / de nas lo 'ga' zhig gi bar du sku gdung rin po che mchod rten gyi snying
por bzhugs su gsol nas/ slar yab 'jam dbyangs chen po'i sku gdung dang rje 'di'i sku gdung lhan cig tu bzhu la phul te/ de'i tshe'ang nam mkha' la 'ja' dang / me tog
gi char la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba du ma byung zhing / khyad par gdung khang zhal phye ba na/ yab kyi gdung rnams ni gtso bor gdung log 'ba' zhig tu song zhing / lha sku ring
bsrel yang thor bur byon/ rje btsun rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid kyi gdung khang gi logs la rdo rje 'chang gi sku mi tshad tsam dang / de'i dpung zur g.yon pa'i 'og tsam
du stobs 'phrog nag po'i sku bram gzugs rkang gang tsam rgyan dang skye mched thams cad shin tu gsal ba dung ris las 'khrungs shing / sku gdung rnams la yang lha sku ring
bsrel bsam gyis mi khyab pa byon zhes grags so/ /'di dag ni bdag chen rdo rje 'chang chen po blo gros rgyal

mtshan nyid kyi rnam par thar pa rags pa tsam zhig rje de nyid kyi slob brgyud 'dzin cing snyan brgyud gdams pa'i mnga' bdag tshar pa chos rje blo gsal rgya mtsho zhes bya
ba'i grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po des mdzad pa'i rnam thar las logs su blangs nas bris pa yin la/ rgyas pa ni rnam thar de nyid dang / gzhan yang bdag chen nyid kyi dngos
slob du mas rnam par thar pa mang po zhig 'byung bas de dag tu bltas la khong du chud par bya'o/grags pa rgyal mtshan//yang bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyi sras/ mthu
stobs dbang phyug bsod nams rgyal mtshan zhes bya bas yul ldan ma/ ming ma gcig kun dga' 'bum bya ba khab tu bzhes pa la/ sras slob dpon chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan zhes
bya ba chu mo glang la 'khrungs shing / 'dis kyang khams phyogs su phebs nas bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen po bsgrubs nas/ dgung lo zhe gnyis pa shing pho rta'i lo la sku
gshegs so/ /de rnams kyis lha rigs 'khon sa skya pa ste mtshan mchog gsum dang ldan pa'i gdung rabs byon tshul las/ gdan sa chen po'i bla brang so sor dbang bsgyur ba'i
gdung rabs kyi nang nas/ rin chen sgang bla brang ba'i gdung rabs rin po che byon tshul legs par bstan zin to// //'dir smras pa/ rin chen gter gyis bltams pa'i sa 'dzin
rtser/ /rin chen khang brtsegs rmad byung nyams dga' bar/ /rin chen 'phreng pa bzhin du legs byon pa'i/ /rin chen sgang pa'i gdung rabs bsngags par 'os/ /khyad par byang
chub sems dpa' zhi ba 'tsho'i/ /rnam 'phrul 'gro mgon bsod nams rgyal mtshan zhes/ /snyigs dus thub pa'i

bstan la thub dbang ltar/ /rab grags kun gyi 'gran bral de la 'dud/ /gzhan yang mthu stobs rdzu 'phrul nus pa'i gter/ /ngo mtshar rnam thar gang la bsams gyur kyang / /phan
tshun 'gran pa bzhin du rim byon pa/ /kun la gsol ba 'debs so byin gyis rlobs/ /bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa'o// //spyi don gsum pa lha khang bla brang pa'i gdung rabs
bshad pa la yang / tshigs bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang / de'i don rgyas par bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs ya rabs kha rgyan las/
rin chen sgang pa'i gdung rabs byon tshul bshad zin ma thag pa'i mjug tu/ bdag nyid chen po'i btsun mo ra lung ma/ /kun dga' nam mkha'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya'i sras/
/ti shrI kun dga' legs 'byung zhes bya dang / /gcung po ti shrI kun dga' rgyal mtshan gnyis/ /kun rgyal btsun mo stag sde kha phyar ma/ /dpal ldan bzang mo'i sras ni chos
rgyal mtshan/ /btsun mo gnyis pa stag sde ra lung ma/ /bsod nams dpal la ta dben blo rgyal 'khrungs/ /ta dben chos rgyal btsun mo chu mdo ma/ /rgyal mo mtsho sras theg chen
chos rje yin/ /btsun mo gnyis pa nyang stod sras skyabs la/ /dharmA dhwa dza rdo rje rin chen gnyis/ /btsun mo gsum pa dpon mo sras pa la/ /slob dpon chen po bsod nams
bkra shis 'khrungs/ /bsod bkra'i btsun mo stag sde ra lung ma/ /nam pa'i sras po bde legs bkra shis yin/ /bde legs bkra shis btsun mo gcig bzhes pa/ /gang de'i sras po
bsod nams

rgyal mtshan dang / /shAkya seng ge don grub rgyal mtshan dang / /bsam grub rgyal mtshan zhes bya rnam bzhi 'o/ /shAka seng btsun mo gcung pa dpon mo'i sras/ /kun dga' bkra
shis kun dga' rgyal mtshan dang / kun dga' snying po zhes bya rnam pa gsum/ /btsun mo gnyis pa ma gcig yum pa'i sras/ /rin chen rgyal mtshan lha khang gdung rabs yin/ /zhes
so/ /gnyis pa de'i don rgyas par bshad pa ni/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po bzang po dpal zhes yongs su grags pa de'i btsun mo spyi grangs kyi lnga pa/ lung phebs nas khab
tu bzhes pa'i btsun mo bzhi pa yul sha la zug pa stag sde ra lung pa/ ming kun dga' nam mkha'i rgyal mtshan zhes pa la sras gnyis 'khrungs pa'i gcen nilha khang bla brang
/ti shrI kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnasti shrI kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba yab bdag nyid chen po dgung lo zhe bdun pa sa pho spre'u'i
lo la dus mchod pa'i gdung brgyud dbang kun dga' legs pa dang dgung mnyam du 'khrungs te/ bla ma 'di ni gzhon nu nyid nas rab tu byung zhing yab chos rnams la gsan
sbyong mdzad pas legs par thugs su chud de/ dgung lo nyer gcig pa'i dus gong nas spyan 'dren pa'i pho nya mngags pa la brten nas mdo khams su phebs/ rgyal po chen po'i
ti shrI dang gzhan yang bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen po zhig bsgrubs nas/ dgung lo sum cu so bzhi pa yos kyi lo la me tog ra bar sku gshegs pa'i tshul bstan zhes mus srad
pa'i gdung rabs las bshad la/ yang nyi lde pa'i gdung rabs las/ rgyal po'i ti shrI lo gsum mdzad nas nyer gsum pa rta'i lo la

gshegs zhes kyang 'byung bas brtag par bya'o/ /bla ma de'i gcungti shrI kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ti shrI kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni yab dgung lo zhe dgu pa lcags pho
khyi'i lo la shal zug bya bar sku 'khrungs te gzhon nu nas yab chos rnams la sbyangs pa phul du phyin pa mdzad cing / khyad par stag thog pa tshul khrims dpal la sogs
pa mkhas pa mang du bsten nas/ rnam 'grel sogs rigs pa'i gzhung lugs rnams la sbyangs pas shin tu mkhas shing smra ba'i mchog tu grags te/ gdan sa chen por dbyar chos dgun
chos ma chag par mdzad pas snyan pa'i grags pas sa'i steng ma lus pa khyab pa la brten nas/ gong nas rgyal po chen po'i chang gu'i gung gu shrI'i mtshan dang / gser gyi
dam kha sogs phul zhing / phyis gong nas gdan 'dren gser yig pa byung nas dgung lo nyer gnyis pa'i dus gong du phebs te/ lo nyi shu rtsa bdun gyi bar du rgyal po chen po'i
ti shrI mdzad pas/ rgyal pos kyang thub pa'i rgyal tshab chen por mnga' gsol zhing / bdag nyid chen po 'dis rgyal khams chen po der bstan pa'i bya ba 'chad rtsod rtsom
gsum dar rgyas su mdzad de/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal bar mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang sa phyogs der bar skabs bar skabs su phyi'i rgya mtsho chen po
lud nas gnod pa chen po yongs kyi yod pa la/ bla ma 'dis gtor chen dang bla gos bsdebs pa la sogs mdzad pas rgya mtsho phyir log pa dang / yang ngo log gi dmag gi rnam 'phrul
mang pos rdzu 'phrul gyis rta dmag gi mtshon cha 'phen pa sogs kyis rang phyogs

pham par byed pa byung ba la/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis dkon mchog la gsol ba btab chos skyong la 'phrin las drag tu bcol bas/ ser ba chen po babs te bar snang gi dmag thams cad
sa la lhung nas/ rang phyogs rgyal bar mdzad pa sogs nus pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' ba zhig ste/ de ltar mdzad pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad nas/ dgung lo zhe dgu
pa sa pho khyi'i lo la me tog ra bar ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te mya ngan las 'das par bshad cing / bla ma 'dis bsnyen par ma rdzogs gong btsun mo gnyis khab
tu bzhes pa'i dang po yul rta ste kha phyar pa/ ming ma gcig dpal ldan bzang mo bya ba la srasda dbon chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ta dben chos kyi rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes
bya ba/ yab dgung lo nyer gsum pa chu pho spre'u'i lo la g.yas ru ngam ring du sku 'khrungs te/ yab mes kyi chos la sbyangs pa phul phyin dang / khyad par tshad ma'i
skor la gsan sbyong mdzad pas rnam 'grel sogs sde bdun phyin ci ma log par mkhyen cing / tshogs chen por rnam 'grel dang rigs gter sogs tshad ma'i gzhung lugs du ma lan mang
du gsungs nas tshad ma'i gzhung lugs dar bar mdzad/ gzhan yang bu ston rin po che spyan drangs nas lha khang chen mor rdor dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor blos bslang dang /
sman bla'i pho brang chen po bzhengs pa sogs bya ba rgya chen po mdzad/ gong nas kyang chang gu'i gung gug shrI'i mtshan dang gser dam chen mo gnang zhing / phyis gang nas
gdan 'dren pa byung nas dgung lo nyer lnga bzhes pa spre'u'i lo la rgya yul du phebs te/ rgyal po A yu pri ta ra zhes bya ba'i sgos kyi

mchod gnas mdzad pas rgyal pos kyang tho ling te ho/ ta dben gu shrI'i mtshan dang shel gyi dam kha tho shu dang bcas pa phul/ rgyal po 'khor bcas smin grol la bkod pa sogs
bstan 'gro'i don rgya chen po zhig mdzad nas/ dgung lo nyer brgyad pa sa mo phag gi lo rgya yul du bde bar gshegs shing /ta dben blo gros rgyal mtshan/de'i gcung ta dben
blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po bya ba ni/ yab ti shrI kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyi btsun mo gnyis pa yul rta ste ra lung ma/ pha ming kun spangs chos grags kyi lcam mo/
ming ma gcig bsod nams dpal bya ba la/ chu pho spre'u lo zla grangs 'ga' zhig gi khyad tsam ma gtogs gcen chos kyi rgyal mtshan 'khrungs pa'i lo de nyid la shal zug tu
'khrungs pa yin te/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis chos rje bla ma dam pa dang / kun mkhyen jo nang pa dang / bu ston kha che/ sa bzang ma ti sogs mkhas grub kyi bshes gnyen khyad
par can mang du bsten nas dam pa'i chos spyi dang / bye brag tu yab mes kyi chos thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa gsan nas thugs su chud par mdzad cing / khyad par rgyas pa'i
bstan bcos tshad ma rnam 'grel la bdag nyid chen po sa paN dang / 'u yug pa rig pa'i seng ge gnyis kyi 'og nas bla ma 'di las rtsod pa bzang ba ma byung bar grags la/
bla ma 'dis gzhi thog gdan sa mdzad nas lo bco brgyad kyi bar du gdan sa chen po'i tshogs chos gsungs/ de'i ring la ta dben gu shrI'i mtshan dang dam kha phul/ phyis su gong
nas gser yig pa mngags nas gdan 'dren byung ba la/ zhing gzhan gyi gdul bya la

dgongs nas dgung lo so gsum pa shing pho 'brug gi lo la lha khang bla brang gi gzims khang byang mar bde bar gshegs so/ /sku mched 'di gnyis chu pho spre'u lo pa dgung mnyam
yin par gtsang byams pa'i gdung rabs dang / bla ma dam pa'i dngos slob shes rab rdo rjes mdzad pa'i gdung rabs las bshad pa ltar 'dir yang bkod pa yin la/ nyi lde ba dang
stag tshang lo tsA ba gnyis kyis/ gcen lcags mo lug lo pa dang / gcung chu pho spre'u lo pa yin par bshad nas/ 'das lo yang 'dir bshad pa dang cung zad mi mthun yang gang
dag dpyad par bya'o/ /kun dga' bkra shis/de ltar sku mched gnyis kyi nang nas gcen po ta dben chos kyi rgyal mtshan pa bsnyen rdzogs ma mdzad gong btsun mo gsum khab
tu bzhes pa'i dang po yul chu mdo ma/ nye gnas nam mkha' bag shi'i dbon mo/ ming ma gcig rgyal mo mtsho bya ba la sras theg chen chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba yab dgung lo bco brgyad pa'i dus mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sprul pa bar ma chad pa 'byon pa'i gnas mchog dpal sa skya'i lha khang chen
mo'i shar du sa mo glang gi lo bkra shis pa'i dge mtshan du ma dang bcas te 'khrungs shing / 'khrungs ma thag nas byis pa'i spyod pa las 'das te ya rab kyi spyod pa du
ma dang ldan pa zhig yin la/ khyad par bdag nyid chen po sa paN gyis spyir nged kyi mi brgyud rnams la 'od gsal cung zad re rgyun mi chad du yong ba yin zhes gsungs pa
dang mthun par/ bdag nyid chen po 'di la yang gzhon nu nyid nas 'od gsal rgyun mi chad pa mnga' ba ste/ smra mkhyen

nas dgung lo drug bdun tsam gyi bar du mnal du song ba'i ngang nas pha rol po dag gis ci smras pa dang / bya byed rnams thogs med du mkhyen te gsung bas kun ngo mtshar du 'dzin
pa byung zhes grags shing / gzhan yang gzhon nu'i dus su mi rtag pa dang nges 'byung thugs las 'khrungs pa'i dbang gis gzigs snang la za zi ban bun mang po 'byung gin
yod pa rnams rje 'di nyid kyi sku zhang dge ba'i bshes gnyen bzang po cig yod pa de'i drung du thugs rje chen po'i dmar khrid gsan pas/ sngar gyi nyams snang phal cher
'od gsal zin pa'i ltas su ngo 'phrod pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i yon tan gyi khyad par du ma gzhon nu nyid nas mnga' zhing / de nas rim gyis rgya bod kyi yi ge dang / klog
dang rtsis la sogs 'jig rten pa dang thun mong gi rigs pa rnams ni brda sprad pa tsam gyis thogs pa med par mkhyen pa'i blo gros dang ldan pa zhig yin mod/ de lta na
yang bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa rab tu byung bas 'dzin par dgongs nas/ dgung lo bcu drug bzhes pa shing pho 'brug gi lo/ ta dben gzhi thog pa kun dga' rin chen dang / sa
bzang ma ti gnyis kyi drung du rab tu byung nas/ mtshan kun dga' bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes gsol te/ de nas slob dpon chos kyi sengge nye bar bsten nas/
bka' spyi'i dgongs 'grel gyi bstan bcos rnam 'grel sogs tshad ma'i gzhung lugs rnams la gsan sbyong mdzad pa na/ skyes stobs kyi thugs rab phul du byung ba dang / /sbyor
byung gi brtson 'grus phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan zhing / yi

dam lhas rjes su bzung ba la brten nas sde bdun mdo dang bcas pa'i tshig don la ma rmongs shing mkhas pa'i phul du phyin par gyur to/ /de nas chu pho byi ba'i lo rje nyid dgung
lo nyi shu rtsa gcig bzhes pa'i dus chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos mkhan po dang / las kyi slob dpon gnas lnga rigs pa'i paNDi ta
chen po ma ti dhwa dza dang / gsang ste ston pa'i slob dpon lo chen byang chub rtse mos mdzad de/ phun sum tshogs pa'i dad pa'i dge 'dun bcu phrag zung dang bcas pa'i dbus
su gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas bsnyen par rdzogs par mdzad nas/ ngur smrig 'dzin pa rnams kyi gtsug gi nor bur gyur to/ /gzhan
yang bdag nyid chen po'i drung du theg pa chen po dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed dang / rdo rje phur pa sa lugs kyi dbang dang / gshed dmar lha bcu gsum ma'i dbang la sogs
pa dang / dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud 'grel gyi bshad pa chos rje bla ma rang gis mdzad pa'i 'grel chen gyi steng nas mdor bsdus lnga pa man dang / gzhan yang dag ljon
spyi gsum/ chos rje bla ma rang gis mdzad pa'i brtag gnyis kyi 'grel pa'i lung sogs dang / sgrub thabs kyi gzhung dang / gzhan yang man ngag las tshogs sogs ston pa'i
rgya gzhung bod gzhung / de dag gi rgyab brten bde bar gshegs pa'i bka' dri ma med pa rgyud kyi lung la sogs pa mdor na dbang lung man ngag rjes gnang la sogs pa chos kyi
sgo du ma gsan nas thugs su chud par mdzad cing / khyad par rin chen sgang bla brang du

gshed dmar lha bcu gsum ma'i dbang gsan pa'i dus su/ chos kyi rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nyid bcom ldan 'das gshin rje gshed dmar po mtshan nyid thams cad yongs su rdzogs
pa'i skur mngon sum du yun ring du gzigs nas/ chos rje bla ma dam pa nyid la sangs rgyas dngos kyi dad gus mdzad pa yin no zhes bshad pa yin/ gzhan yang rje rang nyid kyis
yab ta dben chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla chen bsod nams blo gros/ bdag chen gzhi thog pa kun dga' rin chen/ bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ chos rje ma ti paN chen/ mkhyen
rab kyi dbang phyug sa skya bu ston/ mkhas grub 'phags pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rin chen rdo rje/ 'jag chen byams pa dpal/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ bla ma khyung
po lhas pa/ chos lung mkhan chen rgyal ba bzang po la sogs pa mkhas shing grub pa brnyes pa'i bshes gnyen bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gus pa chen pos bsten nas/ rje
btsun rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug birWa pa nas rje sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po la legs par brgyud pa'i gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa
zab mo cha lag dang bcas pa sogs/ dpal dges pa rdo rje'i chos skor yongs su rdzogs pa rnams dang / slob dpon chen po lU hi pa/ rdo rje dril bu pa/ nag po spyod pa'i rdo
rje ste grub chen de gsum nas rim pa bzhin du brgyud pa'i 'khor lo bde mchog lU nag dril gsum du grags pa'i chos skor yongs rdzogs/ paNDi ta btsun mo can/ mngon shes can/
nag po dam tshig rdo rje gsum gyis 'gos

lo tsA ba bsod nams rtse mo la stsal ba'i gsang ba 'dus pa 'gos lugs su grags pa'i chos skor rnams dang / yang grub chen ti lo pa nas nA ro pa dang mar pa la legs par brgyud
pa'i gsang 'dus mar lugs su grags pa dang / yang 'gos lo nas rngog pa rnams la brgyud pa'i gsang 'dus rngog lugs la sogs pa 'gos rngog mar gsum du grags pa rnams dang /
gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po sa paN la kha che paNDi ta chen po shAkya shrI bha dra zhes bya ba nyid kyis legs par stsal ba'i gsang ba 'dus pa'i dbang bskur ba gsar mar
grags pa la sogs pa mdor na gsang ba 'dus pa'i chos skor bod du yod do cog ma lus pa dang / gzhan yang rwa lugs/ sa lugs/ 'bro lugs/ skyo lugs la sogs pa rdo rje 'jigs byed
kyi chos skor ma lus pa dang / dgra nag gdong drug gshed dmar te dgra gdong 'jigs gsum dang / dmar nag 'jigs gsum du grags pa'i pha rgyud gshin rje gshed kyi chos skor
rnams dang / yang rgya che ba gnyis med kyi rgyud la brten nas dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang / khrid lung man ngag la sogs pa mdor na rnal 'byor chen po bla na med pa'i
rgyud sde nas gsungs pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs phal mo che dang / gzhan yang kun rigs rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba la sogs pa sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis
kyi dbang dang / de dag gi rgyab brten ngan song yongs su sbyong ba'i rgyud la sogs pa rgyud dang rgya gzhung bod gzhung la sogs pa mdor na yo ga rnal 'byor rgyud kyi chos
skor bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dang / bya rgyud spyod rgyud

sogs rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i gdams pa zab mo mang po zhig gsan nas thugs su tshud par mdzad de/ de ltar bla ma dam pa rnams las thugs bzhed kyi chos rnams gsan cing
sgro 'dogs chod par mdzad nas/ nang du rim gnyis kyi rnal 'byor zab mo las ma g.yos bzhin du dpal dges pa rdo rje'i rgyud gsum gyi bshad bka' la sogs pa rgyud kyi bshad bka'
du ma dang / gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa zab mo la sogs pa khrid bka' du ma dang / gzhan yang lung rjes gnang byin rlabs/ dbang bskur ba
la sogs pa chos kyi rnam grangs tshad med pas 'os su gyur pa'i gdul bya rnams smin grol la bkod cing / khyad par rtsom pa nor bu'i phreng bas dngos dang brgyud pa'i gdul
bya rnams kyi bsam pa tshim par mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ dpal dges pa rdo rje'i rtsa rgyud kyi TI ka dag ldan snye ma dang / de'i dka' 'grel snye ma/ spros med rdo rje'i tshig
gi rnam bshad sogs rnam bshad kyi tshogs mang po dang / dus 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor yongs rdzogs/ thugs dkyil/ lhan skyes rnams kyi mngon rtogs/ 'khor lo sdom chen/ gsang
'dus mi bskyod pa/ gsang 'dus 'jam rdor/ kye rdor nas gling ma/ kye rdor rgyud lugs/ bde mchog lU hi pa/ gshin rje gshed/ dgra nag gdong drug gshed dmar/ a ra pa tsa na
lha lnga rnams kyi mngon rtogs la sogs pa/ sgrub thabs dang dkyil chog gi tshogs mang po zhig dang / dmar khrid kyi khrid yig bsam mi khyab kyi khrid yid sogs

khrid yig gi tshogs du ma dang / gzhan yang yi dam chos skyong gi gtor chog bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ dka' ba'i gnad kyi dris lan/ slob ma la springs yig dang / gdams
pa'i skor la sogs pa tshig brjod bde zhing kun gyi rna bar snyan pa/ don yid la 'bab cing bka' mdo rgyud kyi dgongs pa dang 'brel ba'i gsung rab bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig
mdzad cing / yang tshul khrims kyi bslab pa'i sgo nas kyang 'gro ba'i don rgya chen po mdzad de/ bdag nyid chen po 'di'i drung du dge bsnyen dang / dge tshul dang / dge
slong gi sdom pa nod pa yang stong phrag brgal zhing / de rnams las brgyud pa'i rab tu byung ba mang pos phyogs thams cad kun tu khyab pa dang / yul phyogs so so'i skye
bo'i tshogs khri phrag mang po la rje btsun sa skya pa'i bka' srol bzhin theg pa chen po dbu ma pa'i lugs kyi sems bskyed phog nas 'khor ba mtha' can du mdzad pa sogs smos
kyis mi lang ba ste mdor na pha rol du phyin pa drug dang / bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi'i sgo nas sems can gyi don dpag tu med pa mdzad pa zhig go /de ltar gzhan don rgya chen
po zhig mdzad nas/ de nas chos rje sa skya paN chen gyis/ thog mar shes bya kun la mkhas par sbyangs/ /bar du mkhas pa'i tshogs su legs par bshad/ /tha mar 'dris pa'i
don la brtson pas bsgom/ /dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyi bzhed gzhung yin/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / mdo las kyang / mang du thos pa nags kyi nang dag tu/ /lang tsho yol ba rnams
kyis gnas pa bde/ /zhes gsungs pa'i don phyag len la btab ste/ mnga'

rigs 'khor longs spyod la sogs pa 'jig rten gyi phun sum tshogs pa thams cad rgyang ring du bor nas kun spangs kyi spyod pas sa phyogs dben pa kho na la thugs gzhol bar gyur
te/ sku tshe dang sgrub pa mnyam pa lta bu'i dam bca' brtan par mdzad nas thugs dam 'ba' zhig la rtse gcig tu gnas par mdzad ces bshad de/ de yang rnal 'byor dbang phyug
gis byin gyis brlabs pa'i gnas mchog dpal ldan sa skya'i dbu rtse rnying mar lo gsum phyogs gsum gyi sku mtshams dang / gzhan yang jo mo nang la sogs pa'i bsgrub gnas khyad
par can rnams su nyin mtshan thams cad du bskyed rdzogs zung du 'brel ba'i mnyam gzhag gis dus 'da' bas ting nge 'dzin gong 'phel du mdzad nas/ nyams dang rtogs pa'i
yon tan rnams kyang dbyar gyi chu mtsho ltar 'phel zhing rgyas par gyur to/ /de dus sgrub pa tshugs nyams len bzang bas su dang yang kun spyod mi mthun pas kun gyis thugs
gshis gyod par byed ces grag cing / rje nyid kyi gsung las kyang / sgo gsum gnad la bor/ rig pa jur mig nas bton/ tshe 'di'i re ltos thag rbad kyis bcad la bsgom 'tshal
lo/ ma bsgoms pa'i chos de go yul lam/ yid smon la las pa lags so zhes gsungs pa ltar mdzad cing / de yang jo nang du zla ba drug tsam sku mtshams dam po la bzhugs pa'i
tshe/ lan cig lam 'bras kyi dbang gsum pa dang bzhi pa'i 'khrul 'khor la gnad du bsnun pas rlung stod 'tshangs kyi snyung ba thu mo rang cig byung ba la/ slar yang dmigs
pa dang 'khrul 'khor sogs

gdams ngag gis gcun pas/ snyung ba de dang po thu ru song / de nas ji zhig na bem pa tsam byung / de'i rjes nas sngar bsnyung ba'i dmigs rnams su bde drod cher skyes te sangs
kyis phan/ phyis ye nas bsnyung ba ma byung zhes dang / yang de'i dus na ting nge 'dzin la zhag bdun tsam 'byams pa byung zhes rje rang nyid kyis gsungs zhes grag go /de
ltar ched du gtad pa'i bcad rgya lta bu ma yin par rgyun gyi thugs dam chag med mdzad pa'i rim pa yang / nub mo nyal ba'i rnal 'byor gyis gzims nas/ nang par tho rangs
kyi tshe ldang ba'i rnal 'byor gyi ngang nas bzhengs te/ de nas thog mar lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ de rjes bir srung / tshe dpag med grub rgyal ma sogs kyi tshe sgrub/
srog rtsol la sogs pa'i rlung sbyor/ 'phrin las so gnyis la sogs pa'i 'khrul 'khor/ mtha' bral gyi lta ba skyong ba la sogs pa thugs dam gyi rim pas nyi ma snga phyed bar
du su dang yang mi mjal/ de nas phyag mchod la sogs pa'i yan lag bdun pa dang smon 'jug gi sems bskyed bzhes te/ tsha gong du gong ma'i phyag len dkar gtor cha bzhi/ sgrol
ma nyer gcig gzungs gtor dang cha gsum/ 'bul gtor/ gshed dmar gyi drug cu pa/ lan chags gtor ma brgya rtsa dang chu sbyin sogs kyi rjes su mdo sgrub tshar bdun nam nyer
cig gzhan yang bde mchog gshed dmar/ a ra pa tsa na/ rnam rgyal 'joms/ sme brtsegs/ sha ba rI/ 'od zer can/ spyan ras gzigs rnams kyi mngon rtogs/ bzlas pa/ sgrol ma
maNDal bzhi pa/ mtshan brjod la sogs pa'i zhal

'don skabs gang yin la mdzad cing / de nas dgongs mo kye rdor gyi bdag bskyed/ lam dus kyi dbang / mdun bskyed sgrub mchod gtor bsngo'i bar dang / chos skyong gi snying po
dang rtsa sngags brgya rtsa re/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi bsgom bzlas/ srod la'ang srung bzlog gi rigs du ma'i thugs dam gyis nam phyed yol bar du dus 'da'/ de nas phyag mchod
smon lam la sogs pa mdzad de/ gzims mal du'ang gtso cher sgom thag bsnams nas/ sku rnam snang gi chos bdun ldan gyi sgo nas thugs rnam par mi rtog pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi
ngang la bzhugs shing / cung zad mnal mdzad pa de dag kyang thugs dam las mi 'da' ba ste/ nyin mtshan thams cad du chu bo'i rgyun lta bu'i rnal 'byor bcus dus 'da' ba
ma gtogs/ sgo gsum tha mal dang / ma bsdams pa'i kun spyod dang snyom las su bzhugs pa'i skabs skad cig kyang mi mnga' ste/ rje de nyid kyi gsung sgros las/ sgrub pa 'phel
na gnas gcig tu/ /dam bca' bsring ba mchog yin gyi/ /mi 'phel gnas dang grogs longs spyod/ /bdud las spong ba dam pa'i lugs/ /rang sems chos dang mthun gyur na/ /rtag tu
sgrub pa yin mod kyi/ /rnam g.yeng le los dus 'da' ba'i/ /lus dben pa la snying po med/ /de phyir dge ba gang yin pa/ /thun bzhir nges pa'i dam bca' dang / /rtag tu 'chi
ba bsam pa dang / /bla ma'i mos gus bden med dang / /byang sems bsngo ba rgyas 'debs 'tshal/ /mi rtog ting 'dzin lam gyi mchog /'phel na rgyun du bsgrub par bya/ /mi 'phel
rtsol

bcas thun du bcad/ /kun gyi rtsa ba zhen log yin/ /mthun 'jug thams cad spang 'tshal lo/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar phyag len la khel ba mdzad ces grags so/ /de nas yang gnas mchog
rnams su sgrub pa la phebs te ngo mtshar ba'i ltas ji ltar byung ba'i tshul ni/ lan cig gi tshe kha rag thod bur sgrub pa la phebs te/ der phebs su nye ba na sa phyogs
de'i bar snang la rgyan du mas brgyan pa'i bud med kyi rta pa gsum phar rgyug tshur rgyug byed pa mngon sum du gzigs te/ kha rag khyung btsun ma mo dga' nas bsu ba byed
pa yin 'dug ces gsungs shing / de'i rjes thogs la skyes pa gcig gis zho rdza gcig khyer/ bu mo skran khyer ma gcig khyer nas byin rlabs zhu ba yin zer ba zhig byung ba la/
de gzhi bdag gi cho 'phrul yin par dgongs nas 'bul ba blang byin rlabs mdzad pas/ de 'phral la mo'i na zug zhi zhing / de nas der bzhugs sa dam pa phug bya ba rje dam pa
sangs rgyas kyi bzhugs gnas yin pa gcig yod pa der mdzad pas/ re zhig na sngags pa bag dron skra dpung pa gnyis su nyi le ba byas pa gcig dngos su byung nas/ bdag nyid
chen po la/ khyod 'dir ci la yong zer ba la/ bla ma 'dis nged gnas bskor du 'ong gsungs pas/ yang de na re/ gnas bskor nas ci byed zer ba dang / bdag nyid chen pos gnas bskor
nas rig pa'i rtsal sbyangs pa yin gsungs pas/ sngags pa de 'dzum dmul byas phyag cig btsal nas gar song cha med la song ba zhig byung ste/ de yang gzhi bdag gi cho 'phrul
du 'dug ces gsung bar bshad la/ de nas kha rag tu zla ba lnga'i bar

du sku mtshams la dam par bzhugs pa'i bar skabs su sgrub pa po rin chen sogs 'khor rnams na re/ deng sang mi nyung dus 'dir lha sar jo bo mjal du phebs pa drag zhus pa na/
bdag nyid chen po 'di rang thugs dam dge sbyor shin tu 'phel ba yod pas de kar bzhugs 'dod pa zhig yod kyang / sku 'khor rnams kyis zhu nan che bar brten lha sar phebs par
chas pa'i dus bud med mdzes ma cig byung nas/ phyag 'tshal zhing bla ma khyed gnas 'dir cis kyang bzhugs par zhu 'bul zhing / phebs lam du zhugs nas kyang zhu 'bul bshol
'debs yang yang byas nas/ bshol ma thebs pa dang a'u tsi a'u tsi zer nas mgo gug pa cig byas nas song ba bdag nyid chen pos gzigs pa ltar/ sgrub pa po rgya mtsho bya bas
kyang mthong bar grags shing / de'i dus su bdag nyid chen po 'di la mdzo mo gsum yod pa'i bzang shos de rbab tu shor nas shi ste/ de nyid gzhi bdag ma de bdag nyid chen
po 'di der ma bzhugs pa la ma dga' ba'i ltas su 'dug ces bdag nyid chen po rang nyid gsungs so zhes kyang bshad do/ /de nas lha sar phebs te jo bo'i drung du mchod pa dang
smon lam rgya chen po btab ste/ de rjes bstan 'dzin skyes bu du mas bsten pa'i gnas byang rwa sgreng rgyal ba'i dben gnas su chag phebs nas der zla ba lnga tsam gyi bar
du thugs dam gyi rim pa la gtso bor bzhugs shing / de nyid du 'dus pa'i gdul bya rnams la dbang khrid sogs dam pa'i chos zab mo du ma'i bka' drin stsal te/ de dus chos
skyong gi bsnyen pa mdzad pa'i tshe thugs kyi nyams snang

la/ mi nag po gcig gis ras phyam la gtum pa'i khur po gcig khur byung nas/ de ci yin nam snyam du dgongs tsa na/ mi ro gcig 'dug pa gtor ma'i gral du bzhag ste song ba dang
/ de la ched du gtad nas gzigs pa na mtho gang tsam du 'gro/ ched gtad ma gzigs par rang gar bzhag pa na mi dang bong mnyam par 'dug pa gzigs pas/ de'i nyin par rwa sgreng
gi phu na 'bri khung pa yin pa'i bla ma phyug po cig yod pa mjal ba la byung nas/ phyag rten du rten khebs gcig phul nas/ gnam gzer la phan pa'i gdams ngag cig gnang ba
zhu zhu ba la/ de dus bdag nyid chen po 'di 'phral chas thung nges las med pa dang / sgrub mchod kyi chas rkyen ma 'grigs par yod pas chos skyong gis 'tsho chas kyi rten
'brel bsgrig par gnang mod kyang / bdag nyid chen po 'dis dge sbyor la gnod dam snyam du dgongs nas de la gdams ngag de ma gnang / de dus gdams ngag de byas na rang gzhan
gnyis ka la phan par 'dug pas zhes gsungs zhes kyang grags shing / yang de skabs su gshed dmar gyi lus dkyil 'god lugs kun kyang thugs kyi nyams snang la gsal bar byung
ba phyis slob dpon dpal 'dzin gyi gzhung la gzigs pas sngar thugs kyi nyams snang la shar ba dang / gzhung nas bshad pa gnyis ji lta ba bzhin mthun par 'dug pas/ da lta
'di'i byin rlabs byed tsa na nga la nges shes 'drongs pa gcig yod pa yin gsungs zhes pa la sogs pa gzigs snang khyad par ba du ma byung zhing / de nas nyan po dgon pa/ zho
lung mtsho kha/ gro sa dgon pa/ rgya ma

gnas/ skyid shod kyi pha bong kha/ chos rdzong la sogs pa rnams su yang bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen sde snod 'dzin pa la sogs pa dge 'dun dang skye bo'i tshogs bgrang ba las
'das pa la zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi 'khor lo du ma bskor ba mdzad/ de nas slar gtsang phyogs su phebs nas gdan sa chen po dang / ngam ring dga' ldan byams pa'i
gling sogs su dam pa'i chos kyi dga' ston zab mo dang / zang zing gi sbyin pa la sogs pa lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas skye 'gro rnams kyi yid rab tu tshim par mdzad pa'i tshul
brjod par mi nus pa lta bu zhig mdzad pa dang / khyad par gdan sa chen por rje btsun gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum bzhengs pa dang / dpal 'khor lo bde mchog dges pa rdo rje/
bcom ldan 'das kun rig rnams kyi dkyil 'khor rin po che sna tshogs las grub pa'i blos bslang sogs dang / gzhan yang dbus su gshed dmar gyi blos bslang khyad par can dang
/ gos dar sna tshogs pa las grub pa'i chos skyong gi sku ngo mtshar ba la sogs pa sku gsung thugs kyi rten bsam gyis mi khyab pa bzhengs te/ rab tu gnas pa rgyud sde nas
ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin mdzad pa na/ de'i dus su me tog gi char chen po bab cing / gzhan yang phyag nas gtor ba rnams kyang phyag zhabs sogs kyis yun ring du bzung ba/ mchod
pa'i dkar me yun ring du gsal bar 'bar kyang dma' ru ma song ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung zhes kyang grag go /de ltar gdan sa chen
pos thog drangs dbus gtsang gi sa'i cha la gnas pa'i

skye bo rnams thar pa bla na med pa'i 'bras bu la bkod de/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che nyin mo ltar gsal bar mdzad pas snyan grags lha'i rnga bo che phyogs
kun tu bsgrags pa la brten/ byang phyogs kyi rgyal khams chen po nas stobs kyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po gong ma ta'i ming chen po/ thugs kyi dad pa chen po mngon
du phyogs par gyur te gdan 'dren gyi gser yig pa lan grangs gnyis kyi bar du byung ba'i stobs dang / khyad par du rgyal po chen po de dang sngon gyi smon lam gyi 'brel pas
der phebs na bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa rgya chen po 'byung bar dgongs nas/ rje 'di dgung lo drug cu bzhes pa 'brug lo zla ba bzhi pa la gdan sa chen po nas gdan
bteg ste/ de'i dus su gdan sa pa rnams kyi bsam pa la sngar rgyal pos ti shrI mdzad pa rnams kyang 'dir slar phebs ma thub par shas che bar byung ba dang sa thag ring zhing
/ bdag nyid chen po 'di sku nas kyang mthon por phebs pas slar gdan sa chen por phebs ma thub dogs mya ngan chen po skyes te/ kha cig gis sme sngags la sogs pa bton
pa na/ rje'i gsung gis nged khyed rnams gnyid ma sad par slebs yong / khams shin tu bzang ba'i mu nas khyed rnams dang 'phrad par 'dug gi mya ngan bya mi dgos zhes sogs kyi
zhal ta mang du mdzad/ de nas lam bar rnams su yang skal ldan rnams la chos sbyin gnang ba/ dkon mchog la mchod pa 'bul ba/ dbul phongs rnams la zang zing gi sbyin pa
la sogs pa mdor na chos dang mthun pa'i mdzad 'phrin kho nas bstan 'gro'i don mdzad kyin rim pas

phebs/ sbrul lo zla ba gnyis pa'i tshe pho brang chen po rnam thang du phebs/ gong ma chos rgyal chen po dang mjal nas chos kyi gsung gleng mang du mdzad pas/ rgyal po chen
po de slar yang dad pa'i spu long ches cher g.yos te gsang sngags zab mo'i lam gyi smin grol stsol bar gsol ba btab pa na/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis thog mar dpal dges pa rdo
rje'i dkyil 'khor du smin byed kyi dbang bskur ba zab mo stsal te rgyud smin par mdzad cing / gzhan yang bstan srung nag po chen po'i rjes gnang la sogs pa zab chos du
mas thugs tshim par mdzad de/ de nas gru gzings la sogs pa bkod pa khyad par can gyi chu 'jam las gdan drangs te/ pho brang chen po ta'i tu zhes bya bar phebs nas der skabs
bzhugs gnas la ha phin se zhes bya ba'i sde chen po gsar du bzhengs par mdzad cing / rgyal po chen pos sngon bcom ldan 'das la khyim bdag mgon med zas sbyin gyis bsnyen
bkur ba dang tshul mtshungs par chos rje nyid la gus pa chen po'i zhabs tog tshul bzhin du bsgrubs/ mchod gnas thams cad kyi phud du khur/ khyad par sngar sa skya pa brgyud
pa nas brgyud par bcas pas mdo sngags kyi bstan pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i bdag nyid chen po mdzad nas/ sems can mang po smin cing grol bar mdzad pa'i lugs bzhin khyed
kyis mdzad dgos zer nas/ bdag nyid chen po 'di la kun mkhyen yang dag par rig pa/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ nub phyogs kyi mchog tu dge ba/ rdo rje kun khyab/ 'od zer
chen po'i sangs rgyas khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang dbang la
