sogs par mtshan gsol nas/ bstan pa bstan 'dzin dang bcas pa rnams la shes su bcug pa yin pas/ shAkya mu ni'i ring lugs yang dag skyong gsung ba'i lung bkod pa'i gser gyi 'ja'
sa dam kha khyad par can dang / gser gyi 'khor lo stong dang ldan pa rin po che sna tshogs kyi 'phra'i bkod pa phul du phyin pa yod pa sogs zang zing gi dngos spyad bsam
gyis mi khyab pa zhig phul zhing / de nas rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs bzhugs pa'i gnas chen ri bo rtse lngar phebs te/ der gnas rnams mjal bar phebs pa'i tshe/ nam mkha'
ser bu dang chu 'dzin sogs kyi dri ma dang bral te shin tu dwangs pa la 'ja' 'od kha dog dang dbyibs sna tshogs pas phyogs kun tu khyab pa dang / de dag gi dbus dang mtha'
rnams su khye'u gzhon nu dang phyag mtshan la sogs pa'i gzigs snang dpag tu med pa byung zhing / gzhan yang a su ra'i brag phug nas 'od kha dog dkar po shin tu dwangs
shing gsal ba cig byung nas/ shar gyi phyogs su zla ba'i 'od zer bzhin song ste/ 'od de'i rtse mo tshur gug pa rje nyid kyi gzims gur gyi steng du gdugs phub pa bzhin 'khyil
bar gyur pa dang / yang de'i dus su gnas der yan lag brgyad dang ldan pa'i chu rdol nas 'khor dang bcas pas gsol zhing ci dgar rol pa las/ phyis su 'ga' zhig gis gnas
blta ba dang / chu de 'tshol ba la phyin pas ma rnyed ces grags shing / de nas slar yang pho brang chen por phebs te rgyal po chen po de dbang dang man ngag byin rlabs
lung rjes gnang la sogs pa chos kyi bka' du mas thugs tshim par mdzad/ khrims phog

pa'i nyes pa can khri phrag du ma yang rgyal po la bka' gnang nas khrims las thar bar mdzad de/ de'i skabs su yang dngul gyi kye rdor lha dgu sher shing gi 'jigs byed/ gur
lcam dral/ rdo rje phur pa'i lha tshogs la sogs pa rten gsum bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dang / gzhan yang mchod cha/ dbu zhwa/ na bza' la sogs pa dang / rin po che'i rigs
mi 'dra ba du ma dang / gzhan yang gser spyad/ dngul spyad/ gos dar/ gzims gur che chung / ja dkar nag mdzo rta dre'u sogs 'byor pa'i khyad par grangs dang rtsis las 'das
pa phul zhing / de ltar skad rigs mi gcig pa'i rgyal khams chen po der rgyal blon 'bangs dang bcas pa thar pa bla na med pa'i sa la bkod nas/ de nas rta'i lo pho brang
chen po nas gdan bteg ste/ lam la gnas pa'i skye bo'i tshogs thams cad chos dang zang zing gis yid tshim par mdzad cing rim gyis gangs can gyi ljongs chos 'khor lha sa zhes
bya ba'i gtsug lag khang chen por chag phebs nas/ jo bo chen pos thog drangs rten gsum khyad par can rnams kyi drung du gser chab dang / snyan dar/ rin po che sna tshogs
las grub pa'i maNDal sum cu so bdun ma'i bkod pa ngo mtshar ba la sogs pa mchod pa'i khyad par bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig phul zhing / rang gzhan gyi don du smon lam rgya
chen po 'debs par mdzad/ de nas rim gyis gdan bteg nas rta lo zla ba bcu gnyis pa la dpal sa skya'i chos grwa chen por phebs te/ der 'dus pa rgya mtsho'i tshogs dang
/ skye bo'i tshogs dpag tu med pa la zang zing gi

sbyin gtong rgya chen po dang / gzhan yang gdan sa chen po'i rten gsum rnams la dkar me/ snyan dar/ rin po che las grub pa'i mchod cha sogs mchod pa'i khyad par tshad las 'das
pa phul zhing / de nas lo de'i phyi lo gdan sa chen po na bzhugs pa'i bla ma/ slob dpon phyogs nas byon pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen sogs gzhi byes kyi tshogs pa dpag tu
med pa la gsung ngag rin po che cha lag dang bcas pas thog drangs chos kyi dga' ston mtha' yas pa zhig gsungs te/ de'i bar la lha'i me tog gi char chen po nyin re bzhin
rgyun ma chad par babs zhes kyang bshad la/ de ltar sku ji srid bzhugs kyi bar du chos kyi 'khor lo bar ma chad par bskor ba'i 'phrin las rlabs po ches smin cing grol ba'i
slob ma'i tshogs kyang / rin chen sgang pa bla chen kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ gzhi thog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan sku mched/ 'bri khung rin po che/ thel spyan snga ba/ stag
lung chos rje/ chos rje ratna ka ra/ 'tshal pa rin po che la sogs pa rigs rus dang yon tan gyis che zhing / mkhas btsun bzang gsum dang ldan pa'i slob ma'i tshogs mang po
zhig dang / gzhan yang karma byams chos pa/ bka' bzhi pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ rtse chen chos rje/ sgo mo rin po che/ rtsib ri jo gdan pa sogs nyams rtogs dang ldan pa
du ma zhig dang / chos sde so so'i bla ma slob dpon/ gzhan yang bskyed rdzogs la brtan pa thob pa'i ku sa li'i brtul zhugs la gnas pa sogs bgrang ba'i yul las 'das pa lta
bu zhig bskrun par mdzad nas sa chen po 'di yongs su khyab par gyur to/ /de nas yang skabs

shig tu bdag nyid chen po 'di la bsnyung gzhi drag po gcig byung ste sku khams cung zad ma bde ba na/ rje nyid kyis thabs lam gyi rnal 'byor la gnad du bsnun nas bcad rgya
zhig mdzad pas bsnyung ba las grol zhing / de'i phyi lo bdag nyid chen po 'di'i drung du spyan snga kun dga' rgyal mtshan gyis byon pas/ gsung gleng gi 'phros shig la snga
gong rgya yul du phyin pa'i dus rgya'i mi dpyad mkhan zhig gis nged la bla ma khyed rus sbal gyi rigs yin pas lo brgyad cu tsam thub zer ba gcig byung ste/ na ning shi
na kho la kha skyang zhig yong ba 'dug gsung ba sogs kyi zhal kur mdzad pa ltar dang / khyad par rje 'di bskyed rdzogs kyi don la brtan pa thob/ rtsa rlung byang sems la
dbang 'byor/ ting nge 'dzin zab mo gnad du song bas sku na shin tu bgres par gyur skabs kyang gzhon sha rab tu rgyas shing / skra dkar dang gnyer ma mi mnga'/ gzhan gang
las kyang gzi mdangs che/ sku ldang yang zhing phyag zhabs la sogs pa mnyen cing dri ma mi chags pa rdo rje'i skyil krung la sogs pa sku rnam snang gi chos bdun ldan gyis
nyin mtshan khor yug tu bzhugs pa la'ang ngal dub gtan mi mnga'/ sku la tshul khrims kyi dri zhim po'i ngad pa 'phro ba dang / de bzhin du na bza' dang bzhugs pa'i gzims
khang la sogs pa la'ang dri bzang yun ring po'i bar du mi yal ba 'byung zhes grags shing / gzhan yang rje 'di la rims dang / dug dang / 'byung ba'i gnod pa la sogs pa rkyen
glo bur ba gang gis kyang mi tshugs pa dang / pha rol gyis byas pa'i byad kha rbod gtong la sogs

pa'i bar chad thams cad kyang rang zhir 'gro ba la sogs pa byin rlabs dang nus mthu'i khyad par bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig mnga' ba yin la/ gzhan yang khams gsum chos kyi rgyal
po 'di nyid phyi rol du mkhas pa'i bya ba rgyun mi chad pa mdzad kyang / nang du gsang sngags kyi kun spyod khyad par can la g.yel ba cung zad kyang mi mnga' bas bla
ma dang yi dam gyi lha'i zhal gzigs shing lung bstan pa dang / mkha' 'gro chos skyong rnams kyis dgos pa khyad par can gyi tshe bka' nod pa dang / bsams na shes pa'i mngon
shes mnga' ba la sogs pa yon tan dpag tu med pa mnga' ste/ de yang skabs shig lha khang bla brang du bzhugs pa'i tshe/ bsnyen sgrub kyi thugs rdo rje'i rnal 'byor gyi
rten 'brel sogs la nyams bzhes mdzad pas/ 'dzag pa'i gegs phran bu byung nas thugs cung zad ma bde ba'i tshe nam langs khar mnal lam du dam pa sangs rgyas yin zer ba'i a
tsa ra gzi mdangs can phrug dkar po'i na bza' gsol ba cig byon nas/ 'di bzhin gyis gsungs pa'i brdar khong gi zhabs g.yon pa'i rting pas 'og sgo gnyis kyi bar bsdams/ g.yas
ri khrod lo ma gyon ma'i bzhugs steng gi rten byas byung bas byang chub kyi sems steng du rtsol med du 'drongs 'ong gis 'dug pa bzhin mdzad pas gegs las grol zhing / yang
sa skya'i dbu rtse rnying mar sku mtshams la bzhugs tsa na skabs shig tho rangs kha mnal lam du/ rje sa skya pa chen po dang mjal ba'i ngang la rje sa chen bdag nyid
chen po rang gi thugs kar thim par gyur te de'i mod la mnal sad tsa na/ dang

po sku khams bde zhing thugs rig shin tu dwangs pa la/ de nas yun du ma zhig song tsa na sku lus thams cad zi ber langs nas/ yang mnal du song tsa na bsnyung gzhi med par sngar
bas kyang sku khams bde zhing / ting nge 'dzin dpag tu med pa thugs la 'khrungs/ des rkyen byas nas rje btsun gong ma'i bka' 'bum bzhengs pa'i 'dun pa byung ba yin zhes
gsungs zhes kyang grags la/ yang gnas de nyid du sku mtshams la bzhugs pa'i skabs shig mnal lam du/ g.yabs chen gyi rje btsun chen po'i chos khri de'i steng na rje sa
chen dang / rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan te yab sras gnyis ka bzhugs 'dug pa dang mjal nas phyag dang mchod pa phul te/ de'i skabs su thigs khang byang ma'i
sgo nang de nas khye'u gzhon nu shin tu mdzes shing yid 'phrog pa rgyan du mas brgyan pa lus las 'od zer 'phro ba zhig byung ba na/ rje sa chen gyi zhal nas 'di 'u cag
gi mi yin pas ngo shes pa gyis shig ces ngo sprod byed pa cig byung ste/ khye'u de ni 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul pa yin nges su 'dug ces rje nyid gsung bar bshad pa dang / yang
lan cig rwa sgreng du sku mtshams mdzad dus tho rangs mnal lam du/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi gzims khang yin zer ba'i khang bzang dbu rtse
rnying ma'i skor las cung che ba zhal ba mdog ser po shin tu legs pa byas pa cig na rje thams cad mkhyen pa'ang bzhugs te/ de'i zhal nas khang pa 'di'i bdag po khyed la
bsko ba yin gsungs nas gnang ba cig byung nas de'i mod la mnal sad pa

na/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis bla ma'i rnal 'byor bsgom zhing gsol ba btab pas/ rje thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan de nyid na bza' jus dur kha'i zla gam gsol ba/ dbu
zhwa ltebs zhwa mdzad pa gsal po mngon sum du byon nas/ chos kyi sgo du ma ston pa la sogs pa byin rlabs kyi 'jug sgo ngo mtshar ba 'ga' zhig byung zhes gsungs shing /
de'i nyin par nyan po ba'i gdan 'dren byung ba la/ mnal lam gyi rten 'brel sogs kyis phebs pa'i zhal bzhes gnang ba yin zhes gsungs shing / yang phyis lha chen du bzhugs
pa'i dus gcig sa skya pa chen po mngon sum du phebs pa la rje 'dis mos gus tshad med pa 'khrungs te/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sgo nas phyag dang mchod pa phul nas zhabs drung
du 'byon par gsol ba btab pas/ rje sa chen zhal 'dzum pa cig mdzad nas ci yang mi gsung bar rgyang je ring je ring la bzhud de mthar mi snang bar gyur ces kyang grags so/
/yang lhag pa'i lhas zhal gzigs pa'i tshul ni/ lha khang bla brang du bzhugs pa'i skabs shig mnal lam du/ 'khor lo bde mchog sku mdog sngon po zhal gsum phyag drug pa/ zhabs
g.yas brkyang du bzhugs pa shin tu dwangs pa cig gzigs nas/ de la mos gus chen por phyag 'tshal zhing yod pa na/ de'i 'khor bud med dmar tshal ma cig rje 'di la bltas
nas/ ka ra ka ra la sogs pa'i gsang sngags bzla ba dang / yang de'i khrod nas bud med gzhon nu lha'i gos sna tshogs kyis bklubs pa cig gis gar sna mi gcig pa mtha' yas
pa bsgyur zhing / kha cig gis shin tu snyan pa'i gdangs

dbyangs bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas glu len pa dang / kha cig gis pi waM la sogs pa rol mo'i sgra snyan sna tshogs pas yid 'phrog par byed pa dang / bu mo cig gis me 'bud
cing 'dug pa sogs yun ring po'i bar du gzigs te/ de ni 'khor lo bde mchog mkha' 'gro'i tshogs kyis bskor ba mngon sum du gyur pa yin zhes bshad cing / yang lan cig kha
rag thod du bzhugs skabs/ gnas de'i brag ri chen po cig gi dkyil na brag dkar po tshes bco lnga'i zla ba 'dra ba/ de'i mdun na gdengs ka legs po byas pa cig 'dug pa der
snga dro tshogs mchod kyi gnas mdzad pas lan cig mdun bskyed sgrub pa'i skabs su thugs nyams 'ur nas thog mar thugs dran gyi 'dzin dgos pa byung zhing / de nas gsal stong
gi ting nge 'dzin shugs chen po tshad las 'das pa 'khrungs te/ de'i mdo la mdun gyi nam mkha' thams cad khengs pa'i kye rdo rje lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor shin tu gsal ba zhig
mngon sum du yun ring po'i bar du gzigs pa dang / gzhan yang dbu rtse rnying mar sku mtshams la bzhugs nas/ a ra pa tsa na'i bye bsnyen zhig mdzad pa na/ de'i dus su nam
mkha' la dkyil 'khor rigs mi gcig pa mang po yang nas yang du gzigs pa dang / ngam ring du mgon po 'jam dbyangs la gsung bsnyen 'gyur po zhig mdzad pas/ rje btsun 'jam
dbyangs mngon sum du gzigs te thugs rab kyi rtsal thogs pa med pa nang nas 'khrungs shing / de'i dus su mgon po 'jam pa'i dbyangs la bstod pa yang mdzad ces grags la/ yang
lan cig jo nang du

gshed dmar gyi sgrub mchod mdzad skabs gshed dmar gyi dkyil 'khor mngon sum du gzigs shing / nang mchod byin rlabs kyi tshe/ nang mchod kyi ka pA li la me dngos su 'bar ba
zhabs drung na yod pa kun gyis mthong ste ngo mtshar du gyur pa na/ rje'i gsung las/ 'di ye shes kyi me yin mod gsung ba la sogs pa gzigs snang khyad par can dpag tu med
pa byung zhes thos la/ yang mkha' 'gro chos skyong gis bka' nod pa'i tshul ni/ dbu rtser bzhugs dus mnal lam du gtsug lag khang gi khyams mthil du gur gyi mgon po'i rnam
pa gsal zhing mtshan nyid thams cad yongs su rdzogs pa cig dang por gzigs/ de nas de res 'ga' phyag drug pa'i rnam pa/ res 'ga' phyag bzhi pa'i rnam pa sogs rnam 'gyur mi
'dra ba mang du ston pa cig byung ba na/ de gsum ngo bo gcig yin zer ba'i brdar 'dug snyam pa'i nges shes thugs la 'khrungs pa dang / yang lan cig ngam ring du 'jam dkar
la gsung bsnyen mdzad pas nyi ma shar tsam na/ dpal ldan lha mo 'dod khams ma dpon g.yog gnyis dre'u nag po la chibs nas bar snang la sha ra ra byung ba gzigs pa dang /
lha khang bla brang na bzhugs skabs shig kyang dpon po ri'i rtse la shar phyogs nas rgyang gis byung ba gzigs pa sogs lan mang du gzigs snang la byung bar rje nyid kyis gsungs
so zhes bshad la/ yang dbu rtser bzhugs skabs dur khrod bdag po yab yum gnyis mdun nas gar stabs ling ling mdzad pa sogs rnam 'gyur khyad par ba du ma mdzad kyin phebs
pa mngon sum gzigs pa dang / gzhan yang

bdag nyid chen po rang gi zhal nas/ skabs shig pu tra 'di deng sang cha lugs 'gyur 'dug gsung ba sogs mdor na mkha' 'gro chos skyong mi ma yin sogs thams cad bran du khol zhing
las bsgrub pa zhig go /yang mngon par shes pa'i yon tan ni/ gdul bya 'ga' zhig la khyod kyi tshe tshad 'di'o zhes gsungs pa thams cad kyang ji lta ba bzhin thog tu khel
ba byung ba dang / kha cig gi bsam pa dang spyod pa'i 'gro ldog la sogs pa'i gnas tshul thams cad kyang ji ltar yod pa ltar dgongs te dngos su gsung byon pa dang / 'ga'
zhig gi yid the tshom du gyur pa dri ba zhu ma nus pa yod pa rnams la/ chos gsung ba sogs kyi 'phros la zhal ta gsal por gnang ba la sogs pa mtha' yas shing / yang lan
cig nyi shar dpon chen gyi sras rje btsun par grags pa dang / rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa gnyis kyis rje 'di'i sku mdun du 'ong ba na/ rje'i sku mdun gyi pha tshad de na
gzungs thag gcig 'dug pa de khyer shog nged rang rtsed mo byed pa yin gsungs te/ da khyed gnyis kyis nam mkha' la mthon po gyis la phan tshun du 'then gsungs pa la/ khong
gnyis kyis de bzhin byas pas/ rje nyid rdo rje skyil krung mdzad cing gzungs thag de'i steng du byon nas yun ring po'i bar bzhugs te rdzu 'phrul bstan nas/ de nas khong
gnyis la de bzhin gzhan la ma zer ces gsungs zhes kyang grags so/ /de ltar bla ma dang lhag pa'i lha rnams kyi zhal bstan cing byin gyis brlabs pa dang / mngon shes dang
/ rdzu 'phrul thogs pa med pa la sogs pa thun mong dang thun mong

ma yin pa'i yon tan dpag tu med pa mnga' bas bstan 'gro'i don rgya chen po zhig mdzad nas/ de nas sku mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul ston pa dang nye ba na spyan snga kun dga'
rgyal mtshan pas rje 'di'i zhabs drung du dam pa'i chos kyi bka' mang du nos te zhabs drung nas phyir yong ba'i skabs su spyan snga bas/ da dung zhabs drung du mjal bar
zhus pa na/ rje'i gsung gis/ da rang nyer dgu'i zla ba yin chen po rang e sdod mi shes snga sor lab pa rnams sems la zhog ces gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang gdul bya 'ga' zhig
la na ning shang du phyin dus/ shang phu'i zam 'tsher la kha na 'ja' 'od dpag tu med pa 'khyil zhing 'khrigs pa'i gseb na bud med mang po zhig 'dug pa de rnams kyis nged
la bde ba can du 'gro zer ba sogs kyi cho 'phrul du ma byung / de dus 'dun pa cig byas pas khyed kyis lo brgyad cu thub zer ba'i lung bstan cig byung bas da bar bsdad/
da rang yun ring sdod pa'i nges pa med ces gsung ba sogs zhing khams gzhan du gshegs pa'i gsung 'ba' zhig stsal zhing / de'i skabs su dbus gtsang gi sa phyogs kun tu sgra
dang rol mo la sogs pa ltas mang du byung ba kun gyis mngon sum du mthong zhing thos pa byung zhes kyang grags te/ de dang mthun par bdag nyid chen po 'di nyid 'gyur med
rdo rje'i sku brnyes pas snyung ba mi mnga' yang / gzhan snang du snyung ba'i tshul ston par mdzad pa na sman pa mkhas pa rnams kyis gsol sman zhu ba dang / dge 'dun 'dus
pa rgya mtsho rnams kyis gsung sgrog la sogs pa sku rim rgya chen po bsgrubs/ drung na gnas pa rnams kyis kyang

zhabs tog la rtse gcig tu 'bad kyang / gzhan ngor snang tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa ston pa'i phyir sku khams la skyed du mngon pa cung zad kyang ma byung ba na/ slar yang
sku rim rgya chen po bsgrubs pas/ rje'i zhal nas sngar lung bstan la lo brgyad cu yod pas/ da dung lo 'ga' bsdad kyang btub mod/ 'on kyang rten 'brel 'ga' zhig gi rgyus da
lo cis kyang 'gro bar 'dug pas khyed rang rnams rim gro byas ma byas ni med/ byed na yang khyed rang rnams dbang btsan/ 'o skol tshe dang / tshul khrims/ 'phrin las rnams
mthar phyin pa yin pas sems phral dang mya ngan smre sngags sogs gtan ma byed par dga' spro gyis la gsol ba thob ces gsungs shing / ji srid snyung ba'i bar la yang thugs
dam gyi khrigs rnams gtan nas ma chag par mdzad pa'i ngang nas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing khams ya mtshan can du ma dang / bla ma dang lhag pa'i lha bsam gyis mi khyab pa
dang / dag pa'i zhing du spyan 'dren pa'i lha tshogs mang pos bsu ba'i bkod pa la sogs pa gzigs snang khyad par can du mas dus 'da' bar mdzad cing / de nas rtag 'dzin can
rnams skyo ba bskyed pa dang / le lo can dag dge ba la bskul ba'i phyir dang / zhing khams 'di bas gzhan du 'gro don rgya che ba la dgongs nas chos rje nyid kyis dgung lo
bdun cu rtsa bdun bzhes pa shing mo sbrul gyi lo zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu'i nyi ma rtse shar la/ dkon mchog la mchod pa rgya chen po shoms shig gsungs nas/ zhabs rdo
rje'i skyil mo krung mdzad phyag gnyis rdo rje dril bu thugs kar bsnol

te/ gong du 'pho ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi ngang la mnyam par 'jog pa mdzad de rgyud sde rnams nas bshad pa bzhin/ lha dang rig pa 'dzin pa dang dpa' bo mkha' 'gro'i tshogs kyis
bsus nas/ 'ja' dang / 'od dang / me tog gi char dang / rol mo'i sgra dang lha'i spos kyi dri zhim po la sogs pa kun gyi mthun snang du grub pa'i ltas dpag tu med pa dang
bcas pas/ re zhig gzugs kyi sku chos kyi dbyings su bsdu bar mdzad cing / de'i tshe dbu'i gtsug tor gsal por 'phags pa dang / gsang pa'i gnas bltar mi mngon pa dang /
byang sems gser gyi kha dog lta bu zhal dang shangs nas byon pa la sogs pa ltas khyad par can dpag tu med pa byung zhes grags shing / de ltar sku zhi bar gshegs pa'i tshul
bstan nas kyang yun ring po'i bar du nam mkha' la 'ja' 'od kha dog sna tshogs pa 'khrigs shing me tog kha dog dang dbyibs kyi khyad par mi 'dra ba du ma rgyun ma chad
par babs pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung zhes bshad do/ /dharmA dhwa dzade lta bu'i bdag nyid chen po theg chen kun dga' bkra shis kyi yab
ta dben chos kyi rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba de'i btsun mo gnyis pa yul nyang stod ma/ ming ma gcig sras skyabs bya ba la sras sku mched gnyis 'khrungs pa'i che ba dharmA dhwa
dza zhes bya ba lcags mo yos kyi lo la sku 'khrungs te/ skyes stobs kyi shes rab phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan zhing / bdag chen kun dga' rin chen zhes bya ba gzhi thog
pa mkhas btsun chen po'i sras de nyid dang / ma ti paN chen gnyis kyi drung du rab tu byung nas/ de nas chos rje gzungs pa'i drung du

yab mes kyi chos rnams la legs par sbyangs pas phyin ci ma log par thugs su chud/ gzhan yang slob dpon bsod nams dpal zhes bya ba gus pas bsten nas rigs pa'i gzhung lugs kyi
gtso bo tshad ma rnam 'grel bslabs nas/ bshad pa dang / che 'don mdzad pa la sogs pa bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen po mdzad nas snyan grags gong ma rgyal pos kyang legs par
thos nas/ thog mar gu shrI'i mtshan dang gser dam phul te/ bar skabs su mdo khams su gdan drangs pa na bdag nyid chen po 'dis kyang gnas der chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen
po bskor bas/ de'i ring la me tog gi char chen po phab pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma byung ba la brten rgyal blon 'bangs dang bcas pa thams cad dad pa dang gus
pa chen pos yid rab tu g.yos par gyur te/ zang zing gi dngos po bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul nas de thams cad kyang bdag nyid chen po 'dis dge 'dun dang / bla ma dkon mchog
gi zhabs tog kho na mdzad de/ de yang gdan sa'i tshogs su ja sigs brgya sum cu tsam gyi 'gyed dang / gzhan yang dge 'dun re re la gser rkyang zho re'i 'gyed bzang po
mdzad pa la sogs pa bstan pa rin po che'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad nas/ dgung lo zhe drug pa sa pho byi ba'i lo la dpal sa skya'i gnas mchog bla brang khang gsar zhes bya bar
ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te zhi bar gshegs shing /rdo rje rin chen rgyal mtshan/de'i gcung rdo rje rin chen rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba chu mo sbrul gyi lo sku
'khrungs shing / 'di yang skyes stobs kyi shes rab phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan te/ ta

dben kun dga' rin chen gyi drung du rab byung mdzad/ chos rje gzungs kyi dpal ba'i drung du yab chos la sbyangs pas phyin ci ma log pa mkhyen cing / khyad par chos skyong gi
skor la shin tu mnga' brnyes/ slob dpon dpal ldan chos skyong zhes bya ba la rgyas pa'i bstan bcos tshad ma rnam 'grel gsan sbyong mdzad pas phul du phyin pa mkhyen nas/
bshad gsar dang che 'don gcen dharmA dhwa dza dang mnyam du mdzad cing / gdan sa chen po'i tshogs dbon dang / bstan pa'i bya ba 'chad nyan sogs yun ring po'i bar du mdzad
ces bshad la/ de nas bar skabs su skyid grong phyogs la 'gro ba'i don la phebs te/ mnga' bdag pas gtso byas pa'i mnga' ris kyi sa'i cha la gnas pa'i skye bo kun gyis dam
pa'i chos kyi bka' drin thob nas/ zang zing gi 'bul ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa phul te/ de thams cad kyang dkon mchog gi zhabs tog dang skye bo phal pa rnams kyi don kho
na ma gtogs pa rang don du cung zad kyang mi 'dzin cing / de la sogs pa'i bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen po zhig mdzad de/ de nas dus phyis dben gnas man lung brag dkar zhes
bya bar thugs dam la bzhugs pa'i ring nas dgung lo nga gsum bzhes pa'i tshe sku mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan cing /slob dpon chen po bsod nams bkra shisyang bdag
nyid chen po 'dis yab ta dben chos kyi rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i btsun mo gsum khab tu bzhes pa'i gsum pa/ pha ming lho pa dpon chen 'od zer seng ge'i sras mo/ ming ma
gcig dpal ldan 'bum zhes kyang grags shing / ming gzhan dpon mo sras pa zhes grags pa de la sras slob dpon chen po bsod nams

bkra shis zhes bya ba chu pho 'brug gi lo la sku 'khrungs shing 'di yang gzhi thog pa kun dga' rin chen pa dang / ma ti paN chen la rab byung zhus te/ chos rje bla ma bsod
nams rgyal mtshan sogs dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po gus pas bsten nas yab chos rnams la sbyangs pa rgya chen po dang / khyad par tshad ma rig pa'i gzhung lugs kyi gtso bo
dpal chos kyi grags pa'i rnam 'grel la mkhas pa'i phul du phyin pa mkhyen nas che 'don mdzad cing tshogs chen por tshogs chos kyang mang du gsungs te/ 'chad nyan la sogs
bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen po mdzad pa la brten/ gong nas kyang rgyal po chen pos lung mtshan dam kha dang bcas pa phul zhing / bod du che bar grags shing ngo mtshar ba'i
rgyang gi 'bum mo che bzhengs pa la sogs pa mdzad pa rgya chen po zhig mdzad nas/ dgung lo nga drug pa la lhar rtser ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te bde bar gshegs
so/ /slob dpon chen po bde legs bkra shisde ltar ta dben chos kyi rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba la sras sku mched bzhi 'khrungs pa'i nang nas/ bdag chen bsod nams bkra shis
dpal bzang po zhes bya bas byang pa gu'i gung chos grags dpal gyi lcam mo ma gcig nam pa zhes bya ba khab tu bzhes pa la sras slob dpon chen po bde legs bkra shis zhes
bya ba sa pho byi ba'i lo la 'khrungs te/ grub pa'i mtshan ma brnyes pa zhig byung bar grags shing /mkhas btsun chen po kun dga' bkra shis/'dis btsun mo gcig bzhes pa ni
byang bdag po'i sras mo ste 'di la sras bsod nams rgyal mtshan bya ba dang / shAkya sengge ba/ don grub rgyal mtshan/ bsam 'grub rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba dang sku mched

bzhi 'khrungs/ de'i nang nas shAkya sengge zhes grags pa des btsun mo gnyis khab tu bzhes pa'i dang po gcung pa dpon mo zhes bya ba la sras mkhas btsun chen po kun dga' bkra
shis pa dang / kun dga' rgyal mtshan pa/ gcung kun dga' snying po ste sku mched gsum 'khrungs/ btsun mo gnyis pa ma gcig yum pa zhes bya ba la sras bdag chen rin chen rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po ste gdung sras bzhi tsam byon pa'i nang nas gcen mkhas btsun chen po kun dga' bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba 'di ni gzhon nu nyid
nas dam pa'i spyod pa dang ldan zhing / yab chos rnams la gsan pa rgya chen po mdzad cing / khyad par rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen dang / 'jam dbyangs sa skya lo tsA
ba chen po la sogs pa mkhas pa mang po bsten nas dam pa'i chos spyi dang bye brag ma lus pa la gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son pa dang / lhag par mus chen sangs rgyas
rin chen gyis lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas zhabs tog dbu 'don sogs bla na med pa mdzad cing / rje sangs rin pa nyid dag pa'i zhing du gshegs nas gling dga' bde ba can gyi gdan
sa yang mdzad de/ rje 'dis gling dga' bde ba can gyi gnas mchog der gzhi phab nas skal ldan gyi slob ma brgya phrag mang po la gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang
bcas pa'i gdams pa zab mos thog drangs zab cing rgya che ba'i dam pa'i chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i bka' drin stsal/ de'i skabs shig nas rje 'dis bstan pa dang sems can gyi
don la dgongs nas hor yul du phebs pas/ lam bar du mi grib can 'ga' zhig gi dbang gis sku

grib la brten nas sku mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan nas/ sku gdung rin po che ril po de zhabs 'bring pa rnams kyis spyan drangs te da lta yang gling dga' bde ba can gyi
mchod khang na 'gro ba rnams kyi bsod nams kyi zhing dam par bzhugs shing / de'i gcung bdag chen rin chen rgyal mtshan ni skyes stobs kyi thugs rab phul du phyin pa dang
ldan zhing gzhon nu nas rab tu byung / 'jam pa'i dbyangs sa lo tsA ba chen po gus pa chen pos bsten nas bsnyen par rdzogs pa dge slong gi dngos po dang / gzhan yang bde
kye gsang gsum sogs gsang sngags zab mo'i chos kyi bka' mang du gsan cing thugs su chud par mdzad de/ bstan pa'i bya ba thos bsam sgom gsum rgya cher mdzad/ mdo khams su
phebs nas gdul bya dpag tu med pa smin grol la bkod nas/ dgung lo don gsum pa'i tshe ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas sku mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan zhes grags
so/ /de rnams kyis thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis mdzad pa'i gdung rabs ya rabs kha rgyan las ji ltar 'byung ba'i lha khang bla brang pa'i gdung rabs rin
po che byon tshul rnams legs par bstan zin nas/ da ni de dag gi kha skong cung zad brjod par bya ste/ 'di la yang tshigs su bcad pa'i sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang / de'i
don cung zad phye ba gnyis las/ dang po ni/ kun rgyal btsun mo gling gi dpon chen sras/ /dkar mo'i mtshan la chos kyi rgyal mtshan dang / /gcung po kun dga' legs 'byung rnam
gnyis 'khrungs/ /de rnams lha khang bla brang gdung

brgyud do/ /zhes pa ltar ro/ /gnyis pa de'i don cung zad phye ba ni/ bdag chen shAkya seng ge'i btsun mo dang po la sras sku mched gsum 'khrungs pa'i bar pa kun dga' rgyal
mtshan gyis gling dpon chen gyi sras mo dkar mo'i mtshan dang ldan pa khab tu bzhes pa la sras sku mched gnyis 'khrungs pa'i gcen bdag chen chos kyi rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po ni/ skyes stobs kyi shes rab phun sum tshogs shing / dam pa'i spyod pa dang ldan pa zhig byung yang / dgung lo nyer lnga bzhes pa'i tshe zhi bar gshegs/ de'i gcung
'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' blo gros legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni gzhon nu nyid nas rab tu byung zhing / ku sa la'i brtul zhugs la gnas nas gu ru drag
po la sogs yi dam gyi lha du ma la grangs dang mtshan ma'i bsnyen pa mthar phyin par mdzad cing / byams dang snying rje'i mnga' bdag gtsang sbra shin tu che ba rgyun du
thugs dam 'ba' zhig la bzhugs nas/ mdo khams phyogs kyi rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i gsal byed dam pa zhig byung bar grags shing / khyad par bdag chen des rang gi
rgyal tshab dam par rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rin po che zhig phebs na khams phyogs kyi sa skya pa'i bstan pa rin po che la phan slebs rgya chen po zhig 'byung
ba 'dug snyam du dgongs nas/ bstan pa'i nyi ma sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung du zhu yig
rgyas pa 'bul ba rgya chen po dang bcas te sku tshab mi sna cher gtad gnang ste/ de ltar gnang ba'i zhu don gyi snying po

khams phyogs kyi sa skya pa'i dgon che chung / grwa bu slob yon bdag dang bcas pa 'di rnams bstan pa ji srid gnas kyi bar du nged rang sa skya pa'i grub mtha' 'dres med skyong
ba zhig ma byung na bstan pa mtha' nas 'khum pa zhig byung dogs/ de nyid mi 'byung ba'i phyir 'dab 'dob 'dir sa skya pa'i gdung brgyud rgyun ma chad par 'byon pa zhig
mi dgos kha med yod par brten/ bdag chen kun dga' legs pa rang ni gzhon nu rab byung gtsang ma yin pa nas gdung spel sogs gnang stabs ma bde bas/ des na sngags 'chang chos
kyi rgyal po'i gdung sras sku mched gang rigs shig 'dab 'dob sogs khams kyi sa skya pa'i sde dgon pa bstan pa dang bcas pa'i zhal bdag mdzad par phebs dgos shing / de
bzhin ma gnang na phugs yul rang re sa skya pa'i khams phyogs kyi dgon che chung / grwa pa sbyin bdag sogs thams cad gzhan phyogs kyi grub mtha' 'dzin pa stobs ldan 'ga'
zhig gi rjes su 'brangs nas thams cad 'gyur te/ rang re sa skya pa'i khams phyogs kyi bstan pa ming med du song ba zhig byung dogs 'dug pas/ khyed nyan dgongs pa'i nged 'dab
'dob pa dpon slob thugs rtsa nas ma dor ba zhig cis kyang zhu zhes pa'i lan du/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa de nyid kyis bdag chen
'di pa dpon slob rnams la thugs dam gsung shog ma bu 'di bzhin gnang ba yin te/ slob dpon chen po kun dga' legs pa'i drung khyed sku khams snyoms shing 'gro phan rgya chen
pos rnam dkar gyi mdzad pa gong 'phel gyi ngang

nas/ nged pha bu la phyag rtags bkra shis kha thags kha gang / gan spos brgya bam gcig gos chen gser ma kha dgu pa gcig pho brang gi gos chen bzang kha dang seng rgya ma yug
gcig gos chen lcags kha yug gcig gos chen gyi ring 'gag gser ma gcig na bza' gos ber mtshal kha sprin chen ris gcig bla bre padma stong ldan mtshungs bral gcig gsol ja
tshe ring don ldan spob rtse gcig ser po spob rtse bzhi/ 'u zi ri ho spob rtse gcig nag po spob rtse gcig zi zhing spob rtse gnyis/ 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od 'bar ba'i drung du
'phan bse 'u ma cha gcig pho brang gi stan dmar rnams phyag rgya ma nyams par phebs pas thugs la btags shing yid kyi padmo ches cher bzhad par gyur mchis lags/ slar yang
de tshor sku'i 'tsho skyong bstan 'gro'i don sngar bzhin g.yel ba med pa mdzad dgos/ 'dir yang sku rim srung 'khor 'di phyi'i lam gyi bar chad sel ba'i bsngo ba smon lam
gang drag bgyid pa yod lags/ khong dpon g.yog gsum la gang legs byas tshul sogs ngag nas 'bul/ da lam ri mo gzigs pa'i rten bdud rtsi ril bu stong rdo gcig brgya rdo gcig
bcu rdo gcig dang sil ma'i thum dkar chag dang bcas pa/ sa zhwa/ sku 'gag sku bzan/ sku thabs/ zhabs rog zhabs chag gos spu ma rnams la rgya ldan 'bul/ dus khyad par can
chu stod zla ba'i dpal ldan bla ma'i dus chen nyer lnga la dpal ldan sa skya yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung gnas lha khang chen mo'i yang steng po ta la nas phul zhes
pa'i gsung shog ma mo dang / de'i yig chung du 'di

ltar snang ste/ mdo khams phyogs su sa skya pa'i bstan pa la phan pa zhig byung na dgongs pa'i thugs bsam rnam par dag pa de bzhin ches lhag par ngo mtshar che ba ltar/ nged
rang gi bsam pa la yang shin tu de 'dra zhig yod lags pa nas thabs thob gang shes byas/ tshe 'di'i snyan grags la ma bsams/ phyi ma dang bstan 'gro kho na'i phyir 'di bzhin
byas pa yin kyang / cung phyis pa'i skyon gyis yon tan dang na tshod sogs ma smin pa nas der chag phyi 'grub pa zhig cung ma byung / rtse gdong na na tshod smin kyang
bsam pa ma rdzogs pa sogs nas nged kyi lung 'gro bar ma mchis pas dgongs 'gal mdzad mi nyan/ nged rang gi bsam tshod bla ma gong ma rnams kyi phyag srol ga'u le bzang po
'di ma nyams tsam byung na snyam pa'i bsam pa mi dman tsam yod na'ang / dus bskal gyis ma khyogs pas re ba bzhin ma 'grub pa'i khar/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa la phyi nang
thams cad nas gang gnod rang byed pa cig gda'/ gang ltar de nas nged rang gi bsam pa dang mthun pa'i 'di phyi go ma log pa'i ngos sa skya pa'i bstan pa rang thugs yul du
bcangs pa zhig 'dug ces pa'i snyan grags yang yang thos pa ltar/ da lam thugs bsam rnam dag de bzhin nges shes 'drongs pa'i yid ches pa byung lags pa/ de'i cha thog mar de
kha nas sku ngos 'dir phebs pa'i che 'don dang gtsug lag khang rnams mjal ba cig mi mdzad kha med yin pa yar phebs pa thugs rtsol gyis thon pa rang zhig mdzad dgos/ ngos
kyang na tshod rgan pa sogs sgor ma nas nged rang khu dbon gyi dgongs pa ma

rdzogs pa zhig byung dogs blo mdzangs tsam yong gis 'dug pa/ de ga nas bshom ldan che ba'i thugs 'khos mdzad na sngar bzhin phyag thog mi khel bas/ bya bral 'gros kyi phebs
lugs mdzad na don 'grub pa cig yong bas dgongs zhugs 'tshal/ 'di na yang bya bral lta bu ma gtogs 'khos khyer gang yang med na'ang / nged rang zhal ngo nang gtsang kho na
yin pas mnyam bza' mnyam 'thung ngos re gron med pa'i zhabs tog 'grub pa zhig yong snyam pas ri mo 'di bzhin phyag tu smin 'phral nas grabs chug mdzad pa'i phebs lugs zhu/
'dir bka' bgros gnang long yong ba 'dug na'ang / de ga nas gdung spel zhig gnang na 'phral snang nged bzhin cung mdzes mtshon chung tsam byung rung phugs sku tshe 'di
phyi thams cad du phan yon bsam las 'das pa cig yong snyam pa shes ldan gzur gnas kun la dri ba mdzad cing thugs yul du bzhugs pa zhig zhu/ zhib cha ngos kyi mjal nas 'bul/
der dgon pa tsho'i zhabs tog tu 'gyur ba'i bla ma sogs gang spyi'i gnas tshul mtha' dag kyang dpon gnyer gyi ngag nas 'bul ba ltar yin pa thugs yul du gcags pa zhig zhu
zhes pa'i thugs dam gsung shog ma bu 'di gnyis dang bcas sku tshab mi sna'i ngag tu yang 'das ma 'ongs kyi bslab bya phra rags dpag tu med pa zhig stsol bar mdzad pa yin
la/ 'di lta bu'i sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos bstan pa la dgongs pa'i thugs dam gsung shog nang gi tshig rigs re re la bsams kyang / blo ldan gzur gnas rnams dwang
'dod kyi dad pa dbang med du skye ba'i rgyur 'gyur ba 'dug snyam nas

gsung shog khra gdan rgyal yum bsod nams legs 'dzom dkar mo'i phyag bris ngos ma zhig 'dug pa las ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bkod pa yin la/ de ltar sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal
po'i dgongs pa bzhin/ bdag chen pa nyid gdan sa chen por phebs pa'i khu dbon mjal 'phrad gnang nas che 'don dang rten mjal sogs gnang grub pa zhig bdag chen pa 'di mdzad
pa 'phrin las rgya che bas ma byung yang / sngags 'chang chen po zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i rjes su 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched gnyis kyi drung du bdag chen 'di nyid kyis
slar yang sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal por ji ltar gsol ba btab pa bzhin zhu yig dang mi sna sogs gnang ba la brten nas/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs mched gnyis kyis kyang bdag
chen 'di'i dgongs bzhes ltar/ 'jam dbyangs mthu stobs dbang phyug slob 'khor gyi tshogs dang bcas te mdo khams phyogs su rdzong ltar phun sum tshogs pa mdzad de/ 'dab 'dob
sa dkar gnyis kyis gtsos pa'i dgon che chung grwa bu slob sbyin bdag dang bcas pa'i zhal bdag dang / gdung sras spel ba sogs kyi sgo nas srid pa ji srid gnas kyi bar du
khams phyogs kyi sa skya pa'i bstan pa 'dzin pa'i slad du chibs kyi kha lo sgyur bar mdzad de/ bdag chen 'di dang mjal skabs chos dang mthun pa'i gsung gleng mang du mdzad
pas/ rje 'di thugs shin tu dges pa chen po'i ngang nas 'jam dbyangs mthu stobs dbang phyug la zang zing gi gnang skyel rgya chen po stsal zhing / de nas 'jam dbyangs
mthu stobs mtshan can nyid kyis mdo khams

phyogs su 'phrin las rgya chen po zhig skyong bar mdzad nas/ glang gi lo dbus gtsang du 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched gnyis dang / rgyal yum dam pa lha gcig bsod nams rgyal mo
sogs mjal bar phebs skabs/ yum bka' drin can de nyid glang lo cho 'phrul zla ba'i tshes bco lnga la glo bur du gshegs nas ma mjal kyang / khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po 'jam
mgon mched gnyis sogs zhal ngo bgres gzhon rnams dang dges par mjal nas/ slar yang stag gi lo la khams phyogs su bdag chen 'di'i drung du gdan bteg ste rim gyis phebs
pa na 'jam dbyangs mthu stobs dbang phyug nyid 'phrin las rgya ches pas lam bar rnams su phebs 'gor che ba tsam byung ste/ khams kyi sa'i cha spor yid 'ong bya bar phebs
pa na/ bdag chen 'di sku khams cung ma bde ba'i gnas tshul rnams gsan nas/ myur bar bdag chen pa 'di'i zhabs drung du phebs te/ zhal mjal skabs rje 'di'i gsung gis/ 'jam
dbyangs mthu stobs dbang phyug la/ sngon bdag chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan sku mched kyis bstan pa spyi dang bye brag khyad par rang re sa skya pa'i sde
dgon pa mchod gzhis sogs rgya dpangs mi chung tsam khams phyogs 'dir yod pa rnams 'dzin skyong spel gsum mdzad pa'i rgyun bzang po de/ nged rang ngos nas gong 'phel du spyi
'gro'i thabs 'khos byas pa'i lugs yin/ da phyin chad sa skya pa'i khams phyogs kyi bstan pa sde dgon grwa bu slob dang bcas pa'i 'dzin skyong spel gsum ji ltar yong khyed
mthu stobs pa la rag las pas khyer kha bskyed dgos

shing / khyad par rang re sa skya pa rigs rus kyis bstan pa 'dzin pa yin pas gdung spel mdzod gsung ba sogs 'di phyir phan pa'i bslab bya mang du mdzad pa yin no zhes thos
la/ de ltar mdzad pa 'phrin las rgya chen po zhig mdzad nas/ zhing gzhan du 'byon par nye ba na sa chen po 'di rnam pa drug tu g.yo ba/ nam mkha' nas lha'i rol mo'i sgra
grag pa la sogs pa ltas khyad par ba du ma byung bar grags shing / de nas sku mya ngan las 'da' ba'i dus la babs pa na zhabs rdo rje'i dkyil krung dang / phyag g.yas mnyam
gzhag g.yon gyis phyag phreng bzung nas lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor la thugs dam zab mo mdzad pa'i ngang nas/ dgung lo bdun cu don gnyis pa 'brug lo hor zla bdun pa'i
nyer lnga'i tshe bde bar gshegs shing / de'i dus su sngon dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po sku mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan pa'i rjes
su sku gdung rnams bsam yas nas sa skyar gdan drangs nas gdan sa chen por phebs pa'i nyin lha rnams kyis me tog gi char yu ba can babs pa dang mtshungs par/ lha'i me tog
rgya khyon shin tu che zhing kha dog yid du 'ong ba yu ba can gyi char kha ba ltar mngon sum du babs pa der yod skye bo kun gyis mthong ba dang / gzhan yang dbu'i gtsug tor
gsal por 'phags pa dang / gsang ba'i gnas sbubs su nub pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byung bar yongs su grags so/ /de rnams kyis lha rigs
'khon sa skya pa ste mtshan mchog gsum dang ldan pa'i gdung

rabs byon tshul las/ gdan sa chen po'i bla brang so sor dbang bsgyur ba'i gdung rabs kyi nang nas/ lha khang bla brang pa'i gdung rabs rin po che byon tshul legs par bstan
zin to// //'dir smras pa/ sum rtsen lha khang sa la 'phos 'dra ba'i/ /sprul pa'i lha khang chen po dang nye bar/ /ngo mtshar lha khang gzhal med khang bzang du/ /rim byon
lha khang gdung brgyud che rnams rgyal/ /khyad par sa skyong gtsug rgyan theg chen gyi/ /chos kyi 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po che/ /sa skya pa yi bstan pa'i nyi ma de'i/
/rnam thar bsam gyin gus pas phyag bgyi 'o/ /de sogs mkhas btsun bzang po'i yon tan rnams/ /'bad med lhun gyis grub pa'i skyes bu'i mchog /yongs 'dzin dam pa rnams kyi
gdul bya'i zhing / /dbus gtsang khams 'di bdag gis dbang 'dus shog /bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa'o// //spyi don bzhi pa dus mchod bla brang pa'i gdung rabs bshad pa la
yang / tshigs bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang / de'i don rgyas par bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ sa skya pa'i gdung rabs ya rabs kha rgyan las/ lha khang bla brang
pa'i gdung rabs byon tshul bshad zin ma thag pa'i mjug tu/ bdag nyid chen po'i btsun mo re mda' ma/ /lha gcig nyi ma rin chen zhes bya'i sras/ /gcen po slob dpon chen po
nyi ma dpal/ /chung ba kun dga' legs pa'i rgyal mtshan dbang / /kun legs btsun mo ma gcig khang gsar ma/ /dge 'dun 'bum sras bla chen bsod blo dang / /dbang gi mtshan gsol
grags pa rgyal mtshan gnyis/ /

grags rgyal btsun mo ma gcig lha rin la/ /slob dpon chen po kun dga' legs blo dang / /rnam sras rgyal mtshan dbang zhes grags pa 'khrungs/ /btsun mo gnyis pa stag tshang sras
'dren sras/ /slob dpon chen po 'jam dbyangs chos rgyal yin/ /rnam sras btsun mo rta nag gru gu'i sras/ /slob dpon chen po kun dga' blo gros te/ /btsun mo gnyis pa ma gcig
ya 'brog ma/ /bsod nams 'bum la nam mkha' legs pa 'khrungs/ /nam legs btsun mo ma gcig btsun ma skyid/ /ces bya'i sras ni nam mkha' rgyal mtshan yin/ /nam rgyal btsun
mo shangs pa rgyal mo'i sras/ /slob dpon chen po nam mkha' rin chen no/ /btsun mo gnyis pa dpal 'byor bzang mo'i sras/ /dbang gi mtshan gsol nam mkha' bkra shis yin/ /nam
mkha' bkra shis btsun mo dma' se bza'/ /ma gcig her mo tshe brtan zhes bya'i sras/ /'jam dbyangs sprul pa kun dga' bsod nams dang / /ngag gi dbang phyug dang ni 'jam dpal
grags/ /sangs rgyas tshe brtan bkra shis zhes bya bzhi/ /tshe brtan btsun mo ya 'brog khri lcam sras/ /kun dga' bsam grub ngag dbang kun rin gnyis/ /dus mchod bla brang
gdung brgyud rim pa 'o/ /zhes pa ltar ro/ /gnyis pa de'i don rgyas par bshad pa ni/ bla ma bdag nyid chen po'i btsun mo spyi grangs kyi drug pa/ gdung brgyud spel cig pa'i
lung phud nas khab tu bzhes pa'i btsun mo lnga pa yul re mda' ma/ pha ming re mda' ba'i rtsed po/ ming lha gcig nyi ma rin chen zhes bya ba la sras lcam sring gsum

'khrungs pa de'i nang nas/dus mchod bla brang /nyi ma dpal/gcen slob dpon chen po nyi ma dpal zhes bya ba dus mchod bla brang du sku 'khrungs mod kyang gzhon nu la gshegs nas
bstan pa la phan pa zhig ma byung /slob dpon ma kun dga' 'bum/bar ma slob dpon ma kun dga' 'bum zhes bya ba ste 'di ni khab so bkra shis su 'khrungs nas sku nar son pa
na mnga' ris gung thang du mnga' bdag ta dben sha'i jo mo mdzad cing / sras slob dpon lha btsun phun tshogs dpal dang / mnga' bdag bzang po lde gnyis byung ba'i lha btsun
phun tshogs dpal gyis gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skyar lo mang po'i bar du chos 'chad mdzad ces grags shing / de nas dus phyis slob dpon ma des gdan sa chen por phebs
pa na dpon chen gzhon dbang pa yab sras kyis bla brang seng ge sgang phyag tu phul nas/ gnas der thugs dam zab mo'i ngang nas sku gshegs so/ /dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung
gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/yang lcam sring gsum gyi gcung dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba ni yab bdag nyid chen po dgung
lo zhe bdun pa sa pho spre'u'i lo la gdan sa chen po'i nub phyogs re mda' zhes bya bar sku 'khrungs te/ gzhon nu'i dus su yab chos rnams la sbyangs pa mdzad/ snod ldan
gyi gdul bya rnams la dam pa'i chos kyi dga' ston rgya chen po stsal bas/ rgyal po chen po'i lung gis sa'i len dbang gi mtshan dang / gser gyi dam kha chen mo/ shel gyi
tho shu dang / thong bying dang ging ri'i khrims ra/ rgyal po rang nyid kyi lcam mo khab tu phul zhing / nyi ma nub phyogs bod chol kha gsum la shes su bcug nas khrims
kyi bya ba la mnga' mdzad de/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa dgu pa me pho

byi ba'i lo la srad kyi cha lung du ltas khyad par ba du ma dang bcas te zhi bar gshegs so/ /slob dpon ma bsod nams 'bum/de lta bu'i slob dpon chen po des btsun mo gnyis khab
tu bzhes pa la sras lcam sring bzhi 'khrungs pa yin te/ de yang btsun mo dang po yul dang pha ming gung dang khab pa/ ming lha gcig kun skyong rgyal mo zhes bya ba la
sras slob dpon ma bsod nams 'bum bya ba zhig gdan sa chen po'i gzims khang sengge sgang zhes grags par sku 'khrungs nas/ mnga' bdag bkra shis lde zhes bya ba'i jo mo la byon/
slar gdan sar chag phebs te gnas mchog de nyid du sku gshegs shing /bsod nams blo gros/yang dbang kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas kyi btsun mo gnyis pa yul ta ste ngam
ring ma/ pha ming khang gsar ba/ ming dpon mo dge 'dun 'bum zhes bya ba gzhi thog pa ta dben kun dga' rin chen gyi yum de nyid la sras gsum 'khrungs pa'i gcen bla chen
bsod nams blo gros zhes bya ba chu pho spre'u'i lo la stag tshang rdzong khar sku 'khrungs te/ skyes stobs kyi shes rab phun sum tshogs pa dang ldan pas dgung lo brgyad pa
la rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag gnyis thugs las gsungs/ chos rje bla ma dam pa'i drung du rab byung bsnyen rdzogs mdzad cing / gzhan yang bla ma mkhas btsun chen po/ 'jam dbyangs
don yod rgyal mtshan/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ dpang lo tsA ba/ chos rje brag phug pa/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ rgyal sras thogs med pa/ bla ma dpal ldan sengge sogs
gus pas bsten nas/ mdo rgyud bstan bcos lung man ngag dpag tu med pa la sbyangs pa rgya chen po

mdzad/ chos rje bla mas rin chen sgang sgos kyi gdan sar bskos nas/ gdan sa chen po/ bo dong e/ rta nag ri khung / shangs sreg shing / stag tshang rdzong kha/ bsam yas/ chos
rdzong sogs su mdo sngags kyi 'chad nyan dpag tu med pa mdzad nas skal ldan mang po thar pa'i lam la bkod de/ snyan pa'i grags pas sa chen po khyab pa'i skabs su/ gong
nas rgyal po chen po'i lung gis spyan 'dren gyi gser yig pa mngags nas gdan drangs te gong la phebs/ rgyal po chen po'i ti shrI mdzad cing rgyal blon 'bangs dang bcas pa
thams cad bde ba la bkod/ de ltar mdzad pa rgya chen po zhig mdzad nas/ dgung lo so gcig pa la me tog ra ba'i sde chen por ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te zhi bar
gshegs/bla chen bsod nams blo gros pa sku mched gsum gyi bar pa gzhon nu la gshegs shing /sa'i len dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan/gcung ni sa'i len dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan
zhes bya ba ste/ bdag nyid chen po 'di ni me pho byi ba'i lo la stag tshang rdzong khar sku 'khrungs shing / chos rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa/ gcen bla chen bsod nams
blo gros/ rgyal ba brag phug pa/ mnyam med chen po sogs bla ma dam pa mang du bsten nas yab chos kyis thog drangs chos tshul mang du gsan cing thugs su chud par mdzad/ dpal
ldan bla ma dam pa'i drung du rab tu byung ba mdzad de/ rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa sogs dam chos mang du gsungs pa na/ gong nas sa'i len dbang gi mtshan dang gser
dam tho shu dang bcas pa phul/ rgyal khams 'grims na sdig pa che gsungs nas sa phyogs gzhan du 'gro don

la cher ma phebs par gdan sa chen po dang stag tshang rdzong kha sogs su bzhugs nas/ gtsug lag khang dang dkon mchog gi rten gsum bzhengs pa dang dge 'dun gyi sde'i zhabs tog
mang du mdzad ces grags la/ gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po 'di'i sku smad la stag lpags kyi ri mo'i sha mtshan yod par grags shing / sku lus bying yang rnal 'byor dbang
phyug gi rnam pa 'dra ba yod par bshad de/ sku smad la stag ris kyi rnam pa 'dra ba'i sha mtshan yod pa ni bdag nyid chen po 'di nas bzung ste/ deng sang gi bar gyi dus mchod
bla brang pa'i gdung rigs ma nyams pa phal cher la 'byung ba yin la/ de lta bu'i bdag nyid chen po de bstan pa rin po che'i bya ba rgya chen po zhig mdzad nas dgung
lo zhe gnyis pa la rdzong dkar du sku gshegs pa'i tshul bstan cing /kun dga' legs pa'i blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/bdag nyid chen po 'dis btsun mo gnyis khab tu bzhes
pa'i dang po byang pa dpon nam mkha' tshe brtan pa'i lcam mo ma gcig lha rin bya ba la sras sku mched gnyis 'khrungs te/ de yang gcen po slob dpon chen po kun dga' legs
pa'i blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba ni/ yab grags pa rgyal mtshan dgung lo nyer gnyis pa sa mo bya'i lo gdan sa chen po 'di nyid du sku bltams nas/ gzhon
nu nas bdag chen kun dga' rin chen pa dang ma ti paN chen gyi drung du rab tu byung zhing / chos rje bla ma dam pa dang / bla chen bsod nams blo gros/ bla ma mnyam med
pa sogs gus pas bsten nas yab chos sogs dam pa'i chos la sbyangs pa rgya chen po mdzad de/ tshogs chen por tshogs

chos mang du gsungs/ chos rje bla ma dam pas rin chen sgang bla brang gi gdan sar bsko bzhag mdzad pas/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis kyang gdan sa bzung nas bstan pa'i bya ba rgya
chen po mdzad pa na/ gong nas rgyal pos ta dben gu shrI'i mtshan dang / shel dam chen mo tho shu dang bcas pa stsal zhing / rjes su rta nag skor gyi mchod gzhis rnams kyi
zhal bdag mdzad pa'i ring nas/ /dgung lo nyer brgyad pa la rta nag ri khung gzim khang gser khang bya bar ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas zhi bar gshegs zhes grags
la/dbang rnam sras rgyal mtshan/bdag nyid chen po de'i gcung dbang rnam sras rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba ni/ yab dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan dgung lo nyer lnga pa lcags pho
byi ba'i lo la sku 'khrungs te/ chos rje bla ma dam pa dang / bla chen bsod nams blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan pa rnams la yab chos mang du gsan nas thugs su chud par mdzad
cing / rab tu byung ba'i grabs mdzad skabs/ hor rgyal po tho gan bya bas rang gi sras che ba dang mnyam pa'i las kha/ rwa rtse dbang gi mtshan gser dam/ gser sgor/ dngul
sgor/ khrims ra brgyad/ khrims kyi tha sa pa ping cig pa hu shrI/ nyi ma nub phyogs shes su bcug pa'i lung bzang po dang bcas pa stsal/ lugs gnyis kyi 'phrin las rgya chen
po mdzad de/ de'i bar mkhas grub kyi bla ma mang du bsten cing / /khyad par jo bo chen po dpal ldan a ti sha'i rnam 'phrul lo chen skyabs mchog dpal la sangs rgyas dngos
kyi mos gus mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang gdan sa chen po'i zhabs tog gtsug lag khang dang rten gsum bzhengs

pa/ dge 'dun gyi bsnyen bkur sogs bstan pa rin po che'i bya ba rgya chen po bsgrubs shing / thugs dam la shin tu brtson pa'i ngang nas dgung lo zhe dgu pa sa pho byi ba'i lo
hor zla bzhi pa'i nyer bzhi la ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te smon mkhar rtse gdong lhun po rtse'i gnas mchog tu zhi bar gshegs shing /bdag chen chos kyi rgyal
mtshan/yang dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi btsun mo gnyis pa stag tshang ba'i ma gcig sras 'dren zhes bya ba la sa mo phag gi lo bdag chen chos kyi rgyal mtshan zhes bya
ba 'khrungs nas/ gzhon nu'i dus su yab chos kyi chos rnams dang / gzhan yang phar phyin/ mngon pa/ tshad ma/ gsang sngags gsar rnying / khyad par dus kyi 'khor lo la sogs
mdor na dpal ldan bla ma dam pa nyid la bzhugs pa rnams bum pa gang byo'i tshul du gsan nas thugs su chud pas/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pas kyang bdag nyid chen po 'di la
bla brang rin chen sgang dang / sengge sgang la gtogs pa'i khang zhing dang sa cha thams cad gnang bar grags shing / khyad par du yang gdung brgyud gzhan la med pa'i 'phags
pa'i dbu zhwa/ shel dam gling drug ma/ ti shrI kun blo'i shel dam/ 'gro mgon phyag na'i gser dam 'khor dang bcas pa thams cad bdag nyid chen po 'di la yod par bshad cing
/ gzhan yang bla ma 'di ni 'jig rten gyi bya ba la thugs mi 'jug par thugs dam kho na la thugs gzhol ba dang / khyad par sbyor ba yan lag drug pa la mnga' brnyes pas spos
zhal la phyag phreng gi rjes dod pa la sogs pa grub pa'i rtags mang du bstan cing / gzhan phan dang

thugs dam la rtse gcig pa'i sems dpa' chen por bzhugs pa'i ngang nas dgung lo bdun cu pa sa pho spre'u'i lo hor zla gsum pa'i tshes brgyad la me tog gi char la sogs pa ngo
mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te g.yas ru srin po ri'i rnam rgyal sgang gi gzims khang dmar mor sku mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan to/ /de ltar dbang grags pa rgyal
mtshan gyis btsun mo gnyis khab tu bzhes pa la sras sku mched gsum 'khrungs shing / yang stag tshang gdung rabs las btsun mo gnyis pa ma gcig sras 'dren la lcam sring gnyis
dang / tho ji dpon mo bya ba'i btsun mo gcig bzhes pa la byang sems bsod nams rgyal mo bya ba 'khrungs pas/ dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan la btsun mo gsum byung ba dang
sras lcam sring 'khrungs par yang bshad do/ /gang ltar yang dbang grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi sras dbang rnam sras rgyal mtshan du grags pa des btsun mo gnyis khab tu bzhes
pa la sras lcam sring bdun 'khrungs te/ btsun mo dang po rta nag ba gru gu ma bya ba la slob dpon chen po kun dga' blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba 'khrungs
shing / bla ma chen po 'di ni thugs rab shin tu che ba dang / gzhon nu nyid nas dam chos la mkhas par sbyangs/ khyad par rig gnas lnga'i nang nas tshad ma rig pa'i gzhung
lugs la gsan sbyong rgya chen po mdzad pas mkhas par mkhyen nas/ bo dong er chos rje bla ma dam pa'i gdan sa la phebs te/ tshogs chos su rgyas pa'i bstan bcos tshad
ma rnam 'grel gsungs shing / gzhan yang rta nag phyogs su yang 'gro don dpag med mdzad/ byin

rlabs kyi nus pa shin tu che ba thugs dam la brtson pa'i ring nas gdan sa chen po'i bla brang rin chen sgang du zhi bar gshegs/nam mkha' legs pa'i rgyal mtshan/bdag nyid chen
po 'di'i gcung ni dbang nam mkha' legs pa'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba gzhon nu'i dus su ra khyi phag tu grags pa de nyid de/ 'di ni dbang rnam sras rgyal mtshan gyi btsun
mo gnyis pa ma gcig ya 'brog ma bsod nams 'bum bya ba la/ yab dgung lo bzhi bcu pa sa mo yos kyi lor 'khrungs te/ bdag nyid chen po 'di ni skyes stobs kyi thugs rab phun
sum tshogs pa dang ldan zhing / gzhon nu nas brtag pa gnyis pa sogs la gsan sbyong mthar phyin mdzad de mkhas grub kyi bla ma mang du bsten/ khyad par stag tshang lo tsA
ba shes rab rin chen gyi bsnyen rdzogs kyi mkhan por gyur pa 'brom ston seng ge'i mtshan can la mos gus rtse gcig pa mdzad/ dgung lo bcu drug pa'i dus 'bad rtsol gang
yang ma dgos par theg chen chos rje'i sku ring la gong ma ta ming rgyal pos tu kya ho wang gi mtshan dang / gser dam 'ja' sa bod la shes su bcug pa'i lung bzang po gnang
sbyin rgya chen po dang bcas pa dang / gzhan yang brgya 'bul yod res kyi 'ja' sa gnang sbyin dang bcas pa byung bar grags/ rdzong lha rtse mnga' zhabs dang bcas pa sogs mchod
gzhis kyang shin tu stobs che zhing / ya 'brog him tu chen po/ rin spungs nas nang so nor bu bzang po sogs stobs ldan mang pos bdag nyid chen po 'di'i zhabs pad spyi
bo'i gtsug tu blang ste/ bsnyen bkur zhabs tog phun sum tshogs pa bsgrub pa na/ de rnams smin cing

grol ba'i lam la bkod pa sogs mdzad pa rgya chen po zhig mdzad nas/ dgung lo zhe drug pa shing pho byi ba'i lo hor zla dang po'i nyer gnyis kyi tshe rnam rgyal rtser ngo mtshar
ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas zhi bar gshegs pa'i tshul bstan cing / bla ma 'di la sku'i sring mo lnga byung ba'i dang po ni/ ya 'brog du yar bya ba la khab tu gnang / gnyis
pa slob dpon ma khyed 'dren zhes pa ngam ring du si tu rnam rgyal ba la gnang bar grags la/ gsum pa ni slob dpon ma kun dga' 'bum bya ba/ bzhi pa ni slob dpon ma lha
rin dang / lnga pa slob dpon ma nam mkha' 'bum zhes bya ba rnams te/ de dag ni dbang rnam sras rgyal mtshan gyi sras lcam sring bdun po rnams so/ /de ltar bdun gyi nang
nas dbang nam mkha' legs pa'i rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba des btsun mo gnyis khab tu bzhes pa la sras lcam sring brgyad 'khrungs te/ de yang btsun mo dang po ya 'brog pa dpal
chen bya ba la lcam gnyis 'khrungs pa'i che ba yang 'brog stag lung pa la khab tu gnang / chung ba rgyal mkhar rtser gnang bas chab srid phun sum tshogs par byung bar grags
shing /nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/btsun mo gnyis pa mi nyag ma se he ru ka bya ba'i tsha mo ma gcig btsun ma skyid bya ba la/ sras dbang nam mkha' rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po dang / lcam mo slob dpon ma chos skyong bu 'dren la sogs pa sras mo lnga ste lcam sring drug byung ba'i nang gi sras dbang nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dpal
bzang po ni/ yab dgung lo so bdun pa shing mo yos lo 'khrungs te/ 'di ni sku lha'i cha byad/ gsung ka la ping ka ltar shin tu snyan pa dang / thugs nyi ma'i 'od

ltar rab tu gsal bas chos 'jig rten gang la yang mkhyen pa rgyas shing / sku ni sgyu rtsal mtha' dag la thogs pa mi mnga' ba zhig yin par grags pa dang / gzhan yang bdag nyid
chen po 'di'i ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par thar pa ni/ dgung lo bdun bzhes pa nas rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa 'dzin pa'i dbu btsugs pa'i snga dro me tog gi char chen
po babs shing / de nas bzung rgyud de nyid sogs gzhung lugs du ma la gsan sbyong rgya chen po mdzad de/ dgung lo bco lnga pa'i dus gdan sa chen por bshad pa mdzad pas/ bdag
chen shar pas thog drangs sa skya pa thams cad kyi gtsug gi rgyan du khur te shin tu ngo mtshar du 'dzin pa byung bar grags shing / khyad par bla ma la sri zhu che bas
sku gzhon nu thugs kyis mi dran pa'i dus su yang bla ma'i sku 'dra bzhengs nas gsol ba 'debs pa dang / bla ma'i gzims mal gyi 'og tu dbu btsugs nas byin rlabs zhu ba dang
/ na bza' dbu thog tu 'khur ba dang / rgyang ring por bsu bskyel mdzad pa la sogs pa gus pa'i spyod lam mang du mdzad par bshad la/ dge 'dun la yang thugs shin tu dad
pa'i stobs kyis dge 'dun sde long gi phyag dang ldang ba mi bzhes shing / dge 'dun 'dus pa'i yar khyur phebs nas gus pa'i phyag mdzad pa dang / rje rang nyid kyi gsol ja
bskol ba'i 'phros nas mang ja phongs med du zhu ba dang / gzhan yang mi phal pas bsgrub par mi nus pa'i che 'gying bcag pa'i spyod lam mang du mdzad ces thos la/ de'i stobs
kyis sngar brtsig dbang ye ma byung ba'i lhun po rtse'i rdzong ro yang bdag nyid

chen po 'dis bslangs shing / gzhan yang bla ma 'di la rgya yul du rgyal blon kun rna thos bde mo med skabs kyang / rgyal po chen pos sngar yab la ji ltar gnang ba bzhin gyi
dbang gi mtshan dang / las kha/ lung bzang po dang / gser chas khyad 'phags/ dbang gi skya chas tshang ma 'bul ba stobs che ba dang bcas pa nyes med du phyag tu 'byor ba
dang / mdor na dam pa de nyid sku tshe ring na bstan pa'i zhabs tog dang / 'gro ba mang po'i don rgya chen po mdzad pa'i thugs bzhed dang ldan pa zhig yin na'ang snyigs
ma'i sems can gyi bsod nams kyi khyon du ma shong par/ dgung lo nyi shur phebs tsam chu mo lug gi lo hor zla dang po'i tshes bcu gnyis kyi nub mo bla ma'i phyogs su dbu bsgyur
ba la sogs pa mos gus rtse gcig pa'i ngang nas pho brang chen po lhun po rtser sku zhi bar gshegs pa'i tshul bstan to/ /nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/de ltar dbang nam mkha'
legs pas btsun mo gnyis khab tu bzhes pa la lcam mo bdun dang sras dbang nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po 'di nyid de brgyad byon par stag tshang ba'i gdung rabs las
'byung ba yin la/ gtsang byams pas mdzad pa'i gdung rabs las/ dbang nam mkha' legs pas btsun mo gcig khab tu bzhes zhes dang / de la sras gcig 'khrungs pa zhes sogs gsungs
nas/ dbang nam mkha' legs pas btsun mo gcig las ma bzhes par bshad pa dang / btsun mo de la sras dbang nam mkha' rgyal mtshan ma gtogs lcam rnams byung bar ma bshad
kyang / 'dir ni stag tshang ba ltar bkod pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i dbang nam mkha' rgyal mtshan

dpal bzang po zhes grags pa des btsun mo gsum khab tu bzhes pa las/ shangs mthong smon pa ma gcig bgres gzhon gnyis kyi/ bgres pa la sras mo gcig dang / chung ba ma gcig rgyal
mo bya ba la/ sras nam mkha' rin chen rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba/ yab dgung lo bcu dgu pa chu mo bya'i lo ltas bzang po dang bcas sku bltams te/ skyes stobs
kyi mkhyen rab dang sbyor byung gi brtson 'grus gnyis ka phun sum tshogs pas/ gzhon nu nyid nas kye rdor dang rdo rje phur pa'i thugs dam/ sngags ring mang po'i bzlas
brjod sogs la shin tu brtson zhing / rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa la gsan sbyong phul du phyin pa mdzad de/ byis pa'i spyod pa cung zad kyang mi mnga' bar/ dgung lo
bco lnga'i dus su gcung nam mkha' bkra shis rgyal mtshan dang sku mched lhan cig tu gdan sa chen por nyi ma sum sbrel du bshad pa rgyas pa dga' ston rgya chen po dang bcas
pa mdzad pas/ gdan sa'i skye bo thams cad yi rangs te gdung brgyud kyis chos gsungs pa la 'di las lhag pa dus phyis kyi rgan rnams kyis kyang mi dran zer ba la sogs pa
ngo mtshar mchog tu 'dzin pa byung bar grags pa yin la/nam mkha' bkra shis/bdag nyid chen po 'dis gcung nam mkha' bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba ni/ dbang
nam mkha' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i btsun mo gsum pa rnam rgyal gling pa dpal 'byor bzang mo la/ yab dgung lo nyer bzhi pa sa pho stag gi lo 'khrungs te/ 'khrungs ma
thag nas byis pa'i spyod pa thams cad dang bral zhing thugs la khro ba skad cig

tsam yang mi mnga' ba'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po zhig yin par bshad cing /bdag nyid chen po 'dis btsun mo gcig khab tu bzhes pa ni/ dma' ze bza' ma gcig hor mo tshe brtan
zhes bya ba ste/ 'di la sras sku mched bzhi byung ba'i nang nas gcen bdag nyid chen po sa lo tsA ba 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po zhes bya ba ni/ ji skad du/ dang por zab gsal gnyis med 'jam pa'i dbyangs/ bar du rigs ldan 'jam dpal grags pa'i zhabs/ /mtha' mar gnas lnga rigs pa sa skya pa/ /bdag
nyid chen po'i sngon gyi skyes rabs yin/ /zhes pa ltar dang po bde bar gshegs pa thams cad kyi mkhyen rab thams cad gcig tu bsdus pa'i ngo bo 'phags pa 'jam dpal/ bar
du rigs ldan gyi sa skyong chen po mi'i dbang po 'jam dpal grags pa/ tha mar gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta chen po kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba rnams su
sku'i rnam 'phrul brgyud mar bzhes nas/ slar yang gangs ri'i khrod kyi gdul bya skal ldan rnams kyi smon lam dang legs byas kyis bskul nas/ dbus 'gyur gyi tshal rdo rje'i
gdan nas byang phyogs su dpag tshad brgya tsam bgrod pa'i sa'i cha/ yon tan rin po che du ma'i 'byung khungs/ 'phags pa'i gang zag rnams kyi bsti gnas/ 'gran zla med pa'i
mkhas pa rgyun mi chad par 'byon pa'i mtshan ma dang ldan pa'i gtsang grom pa la stod dpal ldan sa skya zhes grags pa'i dgon pa nas dbang po'i phyogs su ha cang mi ring
ba zhig bgrod pa'i nor 'dzin gyi mthil/ phyi nang gi

dpal 'byor du ma 'byung ba'i bsti gnas dpal rtse gdong gi phun tshogs gling zhes pa'i khang bzang chen po der/ phun tshogs gnas dang skyon med rigs bzang dang / /kha na ma
tho med pa'i yab dang yum/ /skal bar ldan pa'i 'khor tshogs la dgongs nas/ /zas gtsang sras bzhin dge mtshan bcas te bltams/ /zhes pa ltar ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang
bcas legs par 'khrungs pa yin te/ de yang bdag nyid chen po 'di'i yum rtse gdong bla brang du mi phebs tsam gyi nub cig mnal lam du ri gcig la 'dzeg gin 'dug pa na mun pa
che nas lam mi rnyed snyam pa na/ rum nas nyi zla gnyis 'thon nas phyogs thams cad gsal bar byas pa rmis shing / yum gyi lhums su zhugs pa'i tshe rtse gdong gi byang phyogs
na rje btsun sa skya pa'i bla mtsho yin pa'i mtsho zhig yod pa de cher rgyas pa dang / gshin rje gshed kyi rnal 'byor pa 'brom ston ye shes rgyal mtshan gyi mnal lam
du/ rtse gdong bla brang pa'i gsol zhing chen mo la yab gung na bzhugs nas sa bon 'debs shing / skye bo gzhan du ma dang bcas pas phun sum tshogs pa'i bkra shis byed pa
dang / rmis ltas pa gzhan 'ga' zhig gi rmi lam du bla brang la sa dkar gsol ba dang / steng na dar 'phyar ba dang / nyi zla shar ba la sogs pa byung zhing / khyad par du
yum la rmi ltas bzang po du ma dang / nyin bar gyi tshe yang shes pa gsal zhing bde bas brgyan pa dang / lus ldang ba yang zhing zo mdog bde ba la sogs pa'i rtags khyad par
can du ma byung bar grags la/ de ltar ltas du ma dang bcas shing zla grangs

rnams thim pa na/ shing mo sprul gyi lo chu stod zla ba'i nyer brgyad kyi nyin/ bkra shis pa'i dge mtshan du ma dang bcas te bltams shing / de'i skabs su shar mi nyag gi paNDi
ta grags pa rdo rje bas gzhon nu gzugs bzang zhing mdzes la blta na sdug pa des zhal gyi dkyil 'khor gzigs pa na/ a rokSha dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i rtsa ba zin
a gsungs shing sku pang du bzhes nas/ rgyal ba'i thugs sras sngon sbyangs dge ba yis/ /yon tan thams cad 'bad med lhun gyis grub/ /chung ngu nyid nas dam pa'i spyod pa
mdzad/ /bu chung 'phags pa'i sku la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes bstod cing / mtshan rdo rje rgya sogs bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya bar gsol te/ de nas paNDi
ta de'i drung du dam pa'i chos kyang mang du gsan par mdzad ces thos la/ de dag gi skabs su bla ma legs pa bzang po pa byas bas yon tan thams cad kyi phyi mo 'bri klog phul
ba na/ brda bstan pa tsam gyis 'bri klog gnyis ka thog med du mkhyen cing yi ge'i rigs kyang bod yig mi the ba'i rgya gar ba'i yi ge rigs drug tsam dang / mkha' 'gro'i
yi ge dang / hor yig gsar la sogs pa yi ge rigs mang po gzigs pa tsam gyis dgongs te/ mdor na 'dri ba dang klog pa'i tshul thams cad la mkhyen rab phul du byung bas skye
bo thams cad ngo mtshar ba'i gnas su gyur pa yin no/ de nas dgung lo drug bzhes pa na/ bdag chen rgya dkar shes rab rgyal mtshan gyi drung du dges pa rdo rje'i dbang / rdo
rje phur pa'i dbang drag po sgrol ba'i rjes gnang sogs dbang rjes gnang mang du gsan cing / sku

gzhon nu'i skabs der nam mkha' la paNDi ta sngo bsang ma pod ral thogs pa seng ge la chibs pa cig gzigs nas/ 'jam dbyangs ya gi na zhes gsung ba yang byung bar grags te/ de
ni bdag nyid chen po sa paNDi ta nyid mngon sum du gzigs pa ste/ de la sogs pa mdor na bdag nyid chen po 'di ni gzhon nu'i dus nyid nas yon tan gyi tshogs du ma la mnga'
mdzad pa zhig ste/ ji skad du/ sku ni mdzes shing yid 'ong mthong na dga'/ /gsung ni 'jam zhing snyan la 'phrod par smra/ /thugs ni chos kyi bag chags bzang pos bgos/ /gzhon
nur gyur kyang byis pa'i spyod las 'das/ /de tshe nges pa'i don du 'jam dbyangs nyid/ /gdul bya'i snang ngor sa skya paN chen zhes/ /snyan grags kun gyi gtsug la len
pa des/ /rang snang ye shes tshul du gsal ba gzigs/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /de nas bdag nyid chen po 'dis rab tu byung nas bstan pa'i bya ba ji ltar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/
ji skad du/ mgon khyod srid pa'i 'ching bas ma gos shing / /'khor ba'i phun tshogs snying po med gzigs kyang / /mchog gi spyod pas 'gro rnams rjes gzung phyir/ /khyim
gyi 'ching ba dug can zas bzhin spangs/ /slar yang e waM chos kyi 'jug ngogs cher/ /blo gsal chu bya mang pos mdun bsus te/ /mkhan slob ngang pa'i ded dpon bka' drin las/
/bslab gsum 'o ma'i rgya mtshor rim gyis zhugs/ /zhes pa ltar te/ de yang bdag nyid chen po 'di dgung lo bcu gcig bzhes pa shing mo yos bu'i lo smin drug zla ba'i dkar phyogs
la/ mkhan chen

thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams lhun grub legs pa'i 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po pa'i drung du bstan pa'i rtsa ba dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pas thugs rgyud
bltams shing rab tu byung ba'i brtul zhugs la gnas par mdzad/ gzhan yang mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa de la thub pa dgongs gsal gyi bshad bka' sogs chos tshul du ma gsan
te/ de nas lo de nyid kyi rgyal gyi zla ba la ngor e waM chos ldan du phebs te/ zla ba de kha'i yar tshes bcu gnyis kyi tshe rje btsun rdo rje 'chang dkon mchog 'phel
ba'i drung du mkhan po zhus/ chos rje glo bo mkhan chen pas slob dpon mdzad nas dge tshul gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa mnos shing / mtshan yang don dang mthun par 'jam dbyangs
kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya bar gsol te/ bslab bya'i gnas phra zhing phra ba la yang kha na ma tho ba'i dri mas ma gos pa'i btsun
pa'i mchog tu gyur to/ /de nas me pho 'brug lo rje de nyid dgung lo bcu gnyis la nye ba tsam na/ mkhan chen chos kyi rje dang dpon slob lhan cig tu dge ba'i bshes gnyen
sde snod 'dzin pa du ma'i 'khor dang bcas te gdan sa chen po'i phyogs su chibs kyi kha lo sgyur bar mdzad nas rim gyis phebs te/ lo gsar gyi dkar phyogs dga' ba dang po'i
tshes la rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam sprul chos rje sa skya paNDi ta chen po'i chos kyi khri ga la ba der/ rgyal ba'i sras kyi lam po che thub pa'i dgongs pa gsal
ba zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos chen po yongs su rdzogs pa nyi ma gsum gyi bar du legs par bshad

pas/ skye bo'i tshogs thams cad ngo mtshar zhing sku na gzhon nu 'di lta bu la sku gsung thugs kyi yon tan rmad du byung ba 'di 'dra ba 'byung ba ni nges par chos kyi rje sa
skya paNDi ta nyid slar yang gdul bya'i don du sku skye ba bzhes pa yin yang dag go zhes mkhas pa'i skye bo rnams kyis mchog tu bsngags pa'i gnas su gyur ba zhig go zhes
grags te/ ji skad du/ 'dzin ma'i khyon 'dir 'jam dbyangs sprul pa'i sku/ /rim par byon pa'i dpal ldan sa skya zhes/ /grags pa'i rnga chen srid na gsal ba der/ /bcu gnyis
bzhes tshe bshad pa'i dga' ston bsgrub/ /sku ni 'khor tshogs dbus na zla ltar brjid/ /gsung ni tshangs pa'i dbyangs ltar dal dod snyoms/ /thugs ni shes bya'i gnas la gsal
bar 'jug /yon tan skye bo kun gyi kha na rgyu/ /zhes pa ltar ro/ /de nas dgung lo bcu bzhi pa sa pho rta'i lo gzhi thog gi gdan sa mdzad nas bstan pa'i bdag por mnga'
gsol zhing slar yang rtse gdong du phebs nas rwa dpon yon tan 'byung gnas la 'dul ba mdo rtsa ba 'dul ba me tog phreng brgyud/ rgyal ba'i bstan bcos tshad ma rnam 'grel sde
bdun mdo dang bcas pa'i dgongs 'grel gyi bstan bcos rigs pa'i gter/ sdom pa gsum gyi rab tu dbye ba sogs sde snod gtsor gyur pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'ga' zhig lung rigs
kyi mtha' dpyod dang bcas te legs par gsan cing 'bel ba'i gtam gyi sgo nas legs par gtan la phab ste smra ba'i khyu mchog tu gyur la/ de dus snga dro ja sbyor re tsam
gyi bar la shog bu mda' tshad bdun tsam re zin pa yang byas zhes gsungs

pa dang ji snyed thugs su chud pa thams cad kyang bsnyel ba med pa'i spobs pa phun sum tshogs pa mnga' ba ste/ bdag nyid chen po rang gi gsung las/ gsang ston slob dpon yon
tan 'byung gnas la/ /'dul ba mdo rtsa ka ri ka la sogs/ /tshad ma rnam 'grel rigs gter sdom gsum dang / /pha rol phyin pa'i gzhung lugs 'ga' zhig mnos/ /sngags kyi sdebs
sogs lag len phran tshegs bslab/ /de ltar thos pa'i gzhung lugs thams cad la/ /bsam pas sgro 'dogs chod cing bsgoms na yang / /the tshom mi za yid ches cung zad yod/ /ces
gsungs pas so/ /de nas lug gi lo rje nyid dgung lo bco lnga pa'i dus yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba'i gsung gis/ rang gzhan gyi don gnyis bsgrub pa'i phyir gsung bsnyen
mdzad dgos pa'i bka' stsal ba la brten/ dges pa rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi bsnyen pa sbyin sreg dang bcas pa/ rdo rje phur pa'i bsnyen pa/ nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po'i
bsnyen pa rnams mthar phyin pa mdzad pas/ de dag gi skabs su kye rdor dang / rdo rje gzhon nu/ gur mgon rnams zhal gzigs pa la sogs pa grub pa'i mtshan ma mang du byung
bar grags la/ de nas yang rgyal ba'i bstan pa la zhugs la yongs su rdzogs pa ni dge slong nyid yin par dgongs nas/ dgung lo nyi shur phebs pa shing pho byi ba'i lo mkhan
po sngar gyi dge tshul mdzad pa po de nyid dang / las kyi slob dpon 'jam pa'i dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen dpal bzang po dang / gsang ston rwa ston yon tan 'byung gnas
kyis mdzad de/ dge 'dun bcu phrag phyed kyi

dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs par mdzad nas/ 'phags pa rta thul ltar spyod lam shin tu dul ba dang / kA tA ya na'i bu ltar bslab bya rnams la shin tu gus shing / 'od srung bzhin
du sbyangs pa'i yon tan thams cad dang ldan pa ste/ mdor na 'dul ba 'dzin pa rnams kyi gtsug gi rgyan du gyur pa zhig ste/ ji skad du/ zhi dang nyer zhi'i myos bum mtho
ldan zhing / /kun nas dul ba'i gser gyi dra ba can/ /thub bstan skyed tshal mdzes pa'i gnyis 'thung khyod/ /yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i khur chen 'degs par bzod/ /spyod lam
kun nas dul ba rta thul te/ /bslab byar gus pa kA tA ya na'i bu/ /sbyangs pa'i yon tan ldan pa 'od srung bzhin/ /dri zhim blta na sdug la 'od chags 'bar/ /zhes gsungs pa
ltar ro/ /de ltar nges legs kyi lam la gcig tu gzhol zhing / lhag pa'i tshul khrims kyis thugs rgyud phyug par mdzad nas/ slar yang rang gzhan rnam grol thob pa'i thabs kyi
gtso bo dam pa'i chos thos nas nyams su len pa dang / de'i yang rtsa ba dri ma med pa'i gsung rab la thos pa bya ba nyid yin par dgongs nas/ yongs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen
rnams las gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son pa mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ ji skad du/ khyod ni mkhyen pa'i lang tsho cher rgyas kyang / /blo gsal yongs kyi dpyad bya 'di
yin zhes/ /mang du gsan pa'i snyim pa rab brkyangs te/ /mkhas mang zhal gyi bdud rtsi dges par gsol/ /zhes pa ltar/ chos kyi rje yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba'i drung
du dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed/ dbang gi sngon

'gro'i sems bskyed/ de gnyis kyi yig cha'i lung dang bcas pa/ dges pa rdo rje yab yum gyi dbang / gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang sogs dbang gi rnam grangs du ma dang / gsung ngag
lam 'bras kyi khrid dang / 'di dang 'brel ba'i byin rlabs mtha' dag dang / rgyab brten gyi yig cha'i lung / gzhan yang Dombi pa'i lhan cig skyes grub sogs lam skor phyi
ma brgyad du grags pa man ngag yig cha phran tshegs dang bcas pa/ shAnti pa'i mdo rgyud bsre ba sogs sgo drug chos 'brel du grags pa rnams dang / gtso che'i chos sna sum
cu so dgu po sogs dges pa rdo rje'i chos skor mtha' yas pa zhig dang / yang 'khor lo bde mchog skor la/ dpal mngon par rtogs pa sogs lU hi pa'i smad lnga/ bde mchog nag
po pa'i sgrub thabs sogs nag po gzhung drug bde mchog lus dkyil sgrub thabs sogs dril bu skor gsum ste lU nag dril gsum gyi lugs kyi 'khor lo bde mchog gi chos skor phal
mo che dang / gzhan yang sgrub thabs mdo byas/ mdo bsres/ rnam gzhag rim pa sogs pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa'i skor mang po zhig dang / thun mong bsgrubs pas mchog zhar
la 'byung ba dmar po skor gsum gyi byin rlabs man ngag las tshogs dang / de dag gi yig cha'i lung / rje btsun gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/
sems dpa' chen po dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen bsod nams sengge rnams kyi bka' 'bum/ gzhan yang chos skyong skor gyi rjes gnang sogs rjes gnang gi rigs bsam gyis mi
khyab pa dang / khyad par

brgyud pa dri ma med pa las 'ongs pa'i sdom pa gsum gyi bka' drin mnos pa'i bla ma rnams kyi nang nas kyang / 'di nyid la rtsa ba'i bla ma mchog tu 'dzin pa yin te/ nyid kyi
gsung las kyang / khyad par rdo rje 'chang chen ratna'i mtshan/ snyigs dus 'gro ba'i 'dren mchog dam pa las/ /sdom pa gsum gyi bka' drin nyer nos pas/ /bka' drin che zhing
bla ma'i mchog tu bzung / /zhes gsungs pas so/ /yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub las dam pa'i chos gsan pa'i tshul ni/ bdag nyid chen po rang
gi gsung las/ mkhan chen 'jam pa'i dbyangs las ches zab pa'i/ /kye rdor rgyud gsum gsang mtha' gur mgon sogs/ /thun mong ma yin yid ches gnad rnams zhus/ /zhes gsungs pa
ltar/ bya ba spyi rgyud nas bshad pa'i rigs gsum spyi dbang / rnam 'joms ma Ni badzra lugs kyi dbang sogs smin byed dbang gi rnam gzhag bcu phrag gsum du lnga phrag gcig
gis lhag pa rnams dang / dpyal lugs kyi phag mo skor gsum gyi byin rlabs sogs byin rlabs kyi rigs lnga phrag gsum tsam dang / gtsug tor rnam rgyal/ don zhags lha lnga/
gur mgon lha brgyad kyi rjes gnang sogs rjes gnang zur bka' bzhi bcu lhag pa tsam sogs 'di dag kyang rgyab brten gyi yig cha so so'i lung dang / gzhan yang dges pa rdo rje
rgyud gsum gyi bshad bka' bde mchog rtsa rgyud 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i lung bshad sogs dang / chos rje mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa rang nyid kyi bka' 'bum gyi lung sogs
mchog tu

zab pa'i chos kyi bka' drin mang du gsan te thugs su chud par mdzad/ yang rje 'dis 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dang zhal mi gnyis pa'i rje btsun mus pa chen po sangs rgyas rin
chen gyi drung du snga phyir gsan pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs la/ rdo rje phreng ba kri ya sa mutstsha dang bcas pa'i dbang / bde mchog nag po pa'i chos skor yongs rdzogs/
sbyong dkyil bcu gnyis kyi dbang / blo sbyong gi skor/ rje mus chen rang nyid kyi gsung 'bum gyi lung sogs gsan cing / mdor na sngar gsan pa'i gdams ngag mang po yang bskyar
nas gsan par mdzad de/ nyid kyi gsung las/ 'jig rten dbang phyug buddha ratna las/ /sngar gyi gdams ngag phal cher bskyar nas nyan/ /gzhan yang gsang 'dus rigs gsum
blo sbyong spyod/ /kr-i ya sa mutstsha sogs mang du thos/ /zhes sogs gsungs so/ /gzhan yang thams cad mkhyen pa zha lu lo tsA ba rin chen chos skyong bzang po la dus 'khor
sa lugs kyi dbang / sbyor ba yan lag drug pa'i khrid/ tha snyad rigs pa la sgra ka tsan gnyis 'grel pa yan lag dang bcas pa/ sdeb sbyor gyi bstan bcos rin chen 'byung
gnas/ tshig rgyan gyi bstan bcos me long / mngon brjod kyi bstan bcos sna tshogs gsal ba'i nyer mkho bsdus pa sogs mang du gsan cing / gsan pa de dag kyang ming tsam ma yin
par tshig dang don du bcas pa legs par dgongs shing thugs su chud pas phyi nang gi rig gnas gang la yang thogs pa med pa'i paNDi ta chen por gyur pa yin te/ nyid kyi gsung
las/ 'gos lo dharmA pa la'i zhal snga nas/ /dus kyi 'khor

lo'i dbang bskur sa lugs dang / /jo zha lugs kyi sbyor drug la sogs zhus/ /ka la tsandra rin chen 'byung gnas dang / /sna tshogs gsal ba snyan ngag me long dang / /dpag bsam
'khri shing la sogs tha snyad kyi/ /gtsug lag phal cher zhus shing nan tan bgyis/ /rang bzhin rkyen dang rnam 'gyur la sogs pa/ /dus dang don la 'jug tshul cung zad shes/
/saM skr-i ta dang bod kyi klog tshul la/ /snga rabs 'chad tshul rab tu mang na yang / /skyon med 'bri dang brjod pa'i tshul shes pa/ /mkhas pa'i gtsug rgyan 'di nyid
bka' drin las/ /gzhan la 'chad dam rang nyid nyams su len/ /ji ltar byed kyang lag nom mi dgos tsam/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar dang / gzhan yang chag lo tsA ba rin chen chos kyi
rgyal po'i drung du sgrol ma lha bcu bdun ma'i dbang / lus dkyil lha nyer lnga ma'i dbang / mgon po lha bcu gnyis ma dang / brgyad ma'i dbang la sogs pa zab cing dkon
pa'i chos mang du gsan la/ de ltar mkhas shing grub pa'i sa brnyes pa'i bla ma'i tshogs du ma zhig las phyi nang gi chos tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gsan cing thugs
su chud par mdzad pas/ gzhan la 'chad pa dang rang nyid nyams su len pa sogs gang la yang thogs pa med pa'i blo gros mnga' ba zhig ste/ ji skad du/ sgra tshad bzo dang gso
ba nang don rig /sdeb sbyor mngon brjod zlos gar tshig gi rgyan/ /rtsis sogs mkhas pa rnams la yongs grags pa'i/ /rig gnas phal cher gzigs pa tsam gyis dgongs/ /khyad par
nyi zla lta bu'i ka tsan gnyis/ /

phyi nang gzhan gsum dpal ldan dus 'khor lo/ /zab lam rdo rje'i rnal 'byor la sogs pa'i/ /gtsug lag kun la mi 'jigs spobs pa thob/ /ces pa ltar ro/ /de ltar bdag nyid chen
po 'dis yongs 'dzin dam pa rnams las phyi nang gi rig gnas kyis bsdus pa'i zab rgyas dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi rnams phyogs dang ris med pa'i gdul bya blo gsal dad 'dun
can rnams la 'chad pa gtso bor gyur pa'i mkhas pa'i bya ba rnam pa gsum gyis nyin mtshan khor yug tu 'da' bar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ ji skad du/ sngon byon mkhas grub mang
pos nyer bsten pa'i/ /bgrang yas chos kyi khri la mnga' mdzad nas/ /blo gsal mang po'i re ba skong mkhas pa'i/ /mgon khyod gangs can bstan pa'i bdag po nyid/ /blo gros lus
dkar gangs ri'i rjes 'gro zhing / /gzhung mang 'chad rtsod rtsom pa'i gom stabs can/ /stong phrag mkhas btsun bzang po'i khyu mchog de/ /gus pas bsten khyed lnga rig paNDi
ta/ /chos sgo brgyad khri bzhi stong gis mdzes pa'i/ /yongs rdzogs bstan pa'i khang bzang nyams dga' bar/ /bsnyengs bral thos bsam sgom pa'i khrir 'khod nas/ /ston pa'i
rgyal sa 'dzin khyod 'od srung che/ /phyi rig gling chen bzhi la mnga' bsgyur zhing / /nang rig lhun po'i rtse mor bgrod mkhas pa'i/ /rnal 'byor dbang po rnams dang lhan
cig tu/ /zab mo sgrog khyod grub pa'i dbang phyug che/ /yid 'ong mtshan dpe'i ri mo rnam bkra ba'i/ /thub chen rgyal ba'i zhal gyi ltad mo ni/ /skyon bral thugs kyi me
long ngos yangs por/ /nges par gzigs khyod sa thob sems

dpa' che/ /zhes pa ltar te/ de yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i tshul zhib par ni sus kyang brjod par dka' mod/ 'on kyang mdor bsdus pa tsam ni 'di
lta ste/ rje 'dis gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skya/ rtse gdong / ngor e waM chos ldan/ nA lendra/ gling dga' bde ba can/ chos 'khor lha sa/ byang rwa sgreng sogs gnas mang
por chos kyi 'khor lo ji snyed cig bskor ba'i dus rnams su shes bya'i gnas la ma nor bar spyod pa'i mkhyen rab kyi 'jug pa rnon pos/ bshad bya'i chos de tshig rna bar
snyan cing / tshig don go bde zhing chod che la/ dka' ba'i gnas rnams dpyis phyin cing byed pa gsal ba'i sgo nas/ so so'i blo dang 'tshams par bshad pas gdul bya rnams kyi
blo gros kyi padmo rgyas par mdzad pa na/ nyin rang por chos kyi grwar gnas kyang skyo sun sogs gtan mi skye ba zhig yin par yongs su grags shing / ji snyed gsungs pa'i
rnam grangs kyang / rgyud sde rin po che dri ma med pa rnams nas bshad pa'i spyi'i dbang bskur rdo rje phreng ba dkyil 'khor zhe gnyis/ de'i steng du kr-i ya sa mutstsha'i
dge legs su byed pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum ste bzhi bcu zhe lnga'i dbang dang / sbyong rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang rnams dang / bye brag gi dbang la/ kye rdor bka'
babs bzhi'i dbang la sogs pa lnga bcu rtsa gcig ste yongs bsdoms smin byed dbang gi rnam grangs brgya rtsa brgyad dang / gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i
gdams pa la sogs pa grol byed khrid kyi rnam grangs nyi shu rtsa bdun tsam

dang / rdo rje bdag med ma'i byin rlabs la sogs pa snyan brgyud zab mo'i byin rlabs kyi rim pa nyer gsum tsam dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang rgya mtsho ste rjes su gnang
ba'i bka' srol chen po gnyis dang / mi g.yo ba dkar sngon gyi rjes gnang sogs rjes gnang zur bkar grags pa bcu phrag bzhis lhag pa dang / dus 'khor 'grel chen gyi bshad
bka' dang / kye rdor rgyud gsum gyi bshad bka' sogs rgyud dang / rgya bod kyi mkhas grub tshad ldan rnams kyis mdzad pa'i rgyud 'grel zab mo'i bshad bka'i rnam grangs bcu
gsum tsam dang / gzhan yang sor sdom dang / byang sems kyi sdom pa'i bslab bya ston pa'i gsung rab du ma dang / sgra dang / sdeb sbyor snyan ngag skar rtsis la sogs pa
tha snyad kyi rig pa dang / gzhan yang gong du bshad pa'i dbang khrid byin rlabs rnams kyi rgyab rten gyi bka' dang bstan bcos sogs lung gi tshogs rab tu mang po sogs chos
kyi rnam grangs re re nas kyang lan grangs mang po zhig stsol bar mdzad cing / yang bstan pa rin po che yun ring du gnas pa dang / dngos dang brgyud pa'i gdul bya rnams
la phan pa'i slad du legs bshad gsar du mdzad pa yang / rje btsun sa skya pa yab sras rnams la mchod yar gyi tshigs bcad/ rtsa ba'i bla ma bzhi la bstod pa sogs gsol 'debs
dang bstod pa'i skor du ma dang / rje sangs rin dang / glo bo mkhan chen pa gnyis kyi rnam thar/ gzhan yang sgrub thabs/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga khrid yig lha so so'i rjes
gnang gi yi ge chos skyong gi bskang ba bstod pa/ nyid kyi gsan yig padma rA

ga'i phreng ba sogs mdor na sngon med pa'i legs bshad kyi tshogs glegs bam du longs pa mdzad de/ 'di dag kyang ming mngon brjod kyis spras pas bying che/ tshig snyan ngag gis
brgyan pas rna bar snyan/ don brjod bya dang 'brel bas rtogs sla/ gcod mtshams sdeb sbyor dang mthun pas brjod bde ba la sogs pa bstan bcos rtsom pa'i yon tan thams cad
tshang bas mkhas pa rnams kyi yid 'phrog par byed pa kho na ste/ ji skad du/ gzhung brgya 'chad pa'i lce bde blo gsal zhing / /lung rigs 'gal 'brel dpyod pa'i 'dren byed
yang / sdeb legs rtsom pa'i ro 'dzin bsgyur mkhas pa'i/ /gnas lnga rig pa dpal ldan sa skya pa/ /blo bzang khyod kyi mkhyen pa'i ded dpon gyis/ /mkhas grub zhal gyi chu
