gter las blangs pa'i/ /dbang lung man ngag yid bzhin rin chen gyis/ /zab yangs thugs kyi bang mdzod legs bkang nas/ /slar yang skye dgu'i dbul ba sel ba'i phyir/ /rgyud
sde rnam bzhi'i dgongs don rin chen mchog /rdo rje phreng ba kr-i ya sa mutstshar/ /legs par bshad pa'i dkyil 'khor zhe lnga dang / /ngan song sbyong ba'i dkyil 'khor bcu
dang gnyis/ /rnam dag zur bka' lnga bcu rtsa gcig ste/ /smin byed dbang gi rnam grangs brgya dang brgyad/ /grol byed khrid kyi rim pa nyi shu bdun/ /snyan brgyud zab mo'i
byin rlabs nyer gnyis lhag /rjes su gnang ba'i bka' srol chen po gnyis/ /rjes gnang zur bkar grags pa bzhi bcu lhag /rgya bod mkhas pa'i dgongs 'grel dang bcas pa'i/ /zab
rgyas rgyud sde'i bshad bka' bcu

gsum dang / /so thar byang sems sdom pa bslab byar bcas/ /sgra dang snyan ngag sdeb sbyor skar rtsis dang / /bka' dang bstan bcos glegs bam rab 'byams kyi/ /dag gsal lung gi
bka' drin dang bcas pa/ /mtha' yas gdul bya'i bsam pa ji lta bar/ /stsol mdzad chos kyi sbyin bdag che ba po/ /mkhas pa'i mdun sar 'gal 'brel gtam byed tshe/ /lung rigs
rjes su gdams pa'i mche sder gyis/ /ma rtogs log rtog the tshom glang po'i lus/ /'joms mdzad smra ba'i seng ge mtshungs pa med/ /legs sbyar tshig gi srad bu la brgyus pa'i/
/rgyan dang mngon brjod sdeb sbyor nor bu'i phreng / /mkhas pa'i yid 'phrog dbyangs can mgul pa'i rgyan/ /spel mkhas tshig rje tshig bdag smra mkhas po/ /zhes gsungs
pa ltar ro/ /de bas na bdag nyid chen po 'dis mkhas pa'i bya ba rnam pa gsum gyi sgo nas mkhyen brtse nus gsum gyis rgyal ba'i bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal bar mdzad pa'i snyan
grags phyogs kun tu khyab pa la brten/ skal ba dang ldan pa'i gdul bya rnams ma bsdus par yang rang gi ngang gis 'du zhing / khyad par gsung gi bdud rtsi ngoms par gsol
ba dang / chos kyi 'brel pa ci rigs pa thob pa'i bstan 'dzin gyi slob ma yang / bstan pa'i mnga' bdag dam par bzhugs pa rje rang nyid kyi sku'i gcung 'jam pa'i dbyangs
ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po sku mched rnams dang / snyigs dus bstan pa'i nyi ma sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags
pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po dang / bdag chen

kun dga' bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po sku mched rnams dang / rje btsun mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub dang / brag dkar sems dpa' chen po bsod nams rgyal mtshan
dang / mkhan chen dpal ldan pa/ gser gling chos rje kun dga' bkra shis pa dang / gzhi sde chos rje 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' brtan pa dang / thub bstan yangs pa can gyi
chos rje rnam pa gnyis/ chos rje dngos grub dpal 'bar ba yab sras dang / rje lcags thang rab 'byams pa/ lo nas spyan snga rin po che ngag dbang chos grags/ chos rje sku
skye ba ngag dbang grags pa/ lhun sdings lo tsA ba nam mkha' dpal bzang sku mched dang / byang pa dus 'khor ba rin chen bzang po/ sle lung mkhan po dkon mchog rin chen/
rnal 'byor dbang po kun spangs chos kyi nyi ma/ jo nang mkhan chen ngag dbang kun dga' legs pa/ srin po ri'i mkhan chen bsod nams rgyal mchog gro sa mkhan chen nam mkha'
dbang phyug stag lung mkhan po bkra shis dpal 'byor/ gser mdog pa gzhon nu nor bzang / dpal spungs chos rje dge 'dun dpal bzang / skyogs lo tsA ba ngag dbang rin chen bkra
shis dpal bzang po la sogs pa mkhas grub kyi slob ma mtshan nas bgrang du btub pa brgya phrag du ma byon zhing / gzhan yang gdan sa chen po'i brgya dpon dang / zur chos
pa bstan pa'i bya ba mdzad nus pa du ma dang / dbus gtsang khams gsum gyi chos sde chen po'i mkhan po dang / dgon pa so so'i bla ma dang / grwa tshang tha dad kyi slob dpon
dang / blo

gsal du ma'i 'dren pa dang / mi chen mang po'i bla ma la sogs pa mdor na bdag nyid chen po dang yul dang gnas skabs kyis ma bskal zhing / chos lugs gzhan gyi dbang du ma gyur
pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen phal mo che zhig gis rang rang gi skal ba dang 'tshams pa'i gsung gi bdud rtsi thob par byas nas/ dad pa chen pos rigs kyi cod pan dam par 'dzin
cing / sku gsung thugs kyi rnam thar gyi rjes su slob pa bgrang ba las 'das pas kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal bar mdzad cing / de dag gi slob ma dang
yang slob dang / nying slob rnams kyis kyang sa chen po 'di yongs su khyab par gyur pa ste/ ji skad du/ ting 'dzin klu dbang du mas nyer bsten pa'i/ /gting mtha' mi mngon
chos dbyings thugs mtsho las/ /'phrin las rnam bzhi'i chu chen rab phab nas/ /bstan 'dzin rtswa ljang myu gu mang du bskyed/ /e ma 'jam mgon gnyis pa'i zhal gyi lung
/ /rna ba'i kun dgar mi 'dzin mkhas pa su/ /khyod kyi zhabs sen yid 'ong nor bu'i phreng / /spyi bo'i rgyan du mi len chen po gang / /rang gi slob ma rang dang rjes mthun
pa/ /mkhas btsun bzang pos mkhas pa'i bya ba gsum/ /mdzad nus du mas mdzad pa bsam yas kyis/ /blo gsal rnams kyi blo mtsho 'gengs la brtson/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar ro/ /de
ltar bdag nyid chen po 'di ni rang gis thos pa dang / gzhan la bstan pa de dag thams cad kyang zab mo'i ting nge 'dzin la bcud len bya ba'i phyir brtson 'grus drag pos nyin
zhag phrugs re la ji ltar mdzad pa'i nyams len gyi rim pa yang / thog mar

dges pa rdo rje'i phyi nang gi bskyed rim/ lam dus kyi dbang rgyas par blang ba dang bcas pa/ bde mchog dril bu pa'i lus dkyil/ nag po pa'i mngon rtogs/ phur pa'i mngon rtogs/
lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bla ma rin chen 'byung ldan/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug gi srung ba gnyis/ nA ro mkha' spyod kyi nyams len 'chi kha ma'i gdams ngag dang bcas
pa/ bde mchog dkar por nyams len/ rdo rje lha mo'i mngon rtogs/ dmar po skor gsum gyi nyams len/ sgrol dkar gyi mngon rtogs/ thub pa mi ru sbi Sha ra/ rnam rgyal 'joms
gnyis/ mgon po'i srung bzlog rgyas pa sogs lha'i rnal 'byor re re nas kyang sngags kyi bzlas pa grangs mang po dang bcas thun gnyis dang gsum dang bzhi la sogs pa'i nges
pas gtan mi chag pa'i dam bca' brtan po mdzad cing / gtso cher rdzogs rim gyi nyams len lta ba skyong ba dang bcas pa du ma dang / sbyor drug gi nyin mtshan gyi rnal 'byor
dang / rlung dang 'phrul 'khor la sogs pa'i rnal 'byor du mas mtshan mo'i cha phal cher 'da' bar mdzad la/ snga dro thugs dam grol nas rten gsum rnams la phyag dang bcas
pa'i yan lag bdun pa dang / dkar gtor cha bzhi/ nyin bar gyi dus su tshogs chos gsung ba la sogs pa'i lung dang bshad pa la sogs pa'i phyag khrid rnams mdzad/ de lta
bu mi gnang ba'i skabs su phyag dpe'i gzigs rtog kho na mdzad cing / thun mtshams gang rigs la gtor ma brgya rtsa rgyas pa chu sbyin dang bcas pa/ dzam ser nag dbyu gu ma
spun gsum/ dus 'khor gyi

srung ma drug cu/ thugs rje chen po'i brul gtor cha gsum gtor ma rnams mdzad nas/ mthar shes rab snying po saM skr-i ta'i skad du tshar gsum bdud bzlog bsngo ba smon lam dang
bcas pa mdzad/ bar skabs su sku 'chag pa'i zhabs bskor dang bcas te/ rtsa ba'i bla ma rnam bzhi dang / bla ma gong ma rnams kyi bstod pa du ma dang / brgyud pa'i gsol
'debs kha yar/ dpa' bos mdzad pa'i sangs rgyas kyi bstod tshogs 'ga' yar/ dpal ldan chos grags kyis mdzad pa'i bde mchog gi bstod pa rgyun chags/ tsandra go mas mdzad pa'i
'jam dbyangs phyogs bcu ma/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa'i sgrol ma'i bstod pa me tog phreng 'dzin sogs chos spyod kyi rim pa mang du mdzad/ dgongs mo'i
cha la dbang dang byin rlabs dang rjes gnang zab mo rnams so so'i blo dang 'tshams par mdzad/ de nas yang srod thun phal cher rdzogs pa'i mjug tu/ bde dges phur gsum/
mgon po lha brgyad sogs yi dam chos skyong gi gtor bsngo rnams rgyas par mdzad/ de nas srod thun gyi 'phro rnams rdzogs par mdzad pa la sogs pa mdor na bdag nyid chen po
'dis nyin zhag phrugs gcig gi mnyam gzhag gi thugs dam rnams lta zhog chos spyod dang gtor ma'i sgrig chags tsam yang deng sang gi dge ba la rtse gcig tu bzhugs par rlom
pa rnams kyis nyin zhag du mar 'bad kyang grub par dka' bar mthong zhing / de ltar rim gnyis kyi ting nge 'dzin zab mo la g.yel ba med par bzhugs pa'i 'bras bu gnas skabs
su bla ma yi dam sogs kyi zhal bstan cing rjes su

bzung ba'i mtshan ma yang bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' ba yin te/ de yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis dgung lo nyi shu rtsa grangs bzhes pa'i skabs shig rtse gdong gi dgon gzhis
mdo chos gzim khang du sku mtshams mdzad nas rdo rje phur pa gtso bor gyur pa'i thugs dam gnang dus/ sa bir zhal sprod/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu/ dpal ldan bla ma
dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan rnams kyi zhal gzigs pa dang / bdag nyid chen po 'di dgung lo sum cu so gnyis su phebs pa me pho byi ba'i lo nA lendrar gsung ngag rin po che
lam 'bras bu dang bcas pas thog drangs/ khrid/ lung / man ngag dbang byin rlabs rjes gnang sogs zab rgyas kyi dam pa'i chos mang po stsal ba na/ de'i skabs su rje sangs
rgyas rin chen yang phebs te de nas yab sras lhan cig tu gtsang phyogs la gdan bteg ste/ yar lam srin po ri mjal bar phebs pas bde mchog gi sku de bde mchog zhal bzhi phyag
bcu gnyis par gzigs nas sku lus la 'phar g.yo la sogs pa byung ste/ gar stabs sna tshogs mdzad cing / de nas de las sangs pa na khye'u dkar po gcig gis bsu ba byas nas
bskor lam la phebs pas/ de'i dus su rje sangs rgyas rin chen gyis 'khor rnams la/ khong pa la gzigs snang dang nyams rtogs mang po 'khrungs gda'/ mi tsho bde mchog sngon
po yin zer te 'di ni dkar por 'dug gsung ba la sogs pa dang / yang lan cig mus kyi bsam gtan phug tu lo gcig hril po sku mtshams la bzhugs te/ 'khor lo bde mchog gi gsung

bsnyen mthar phyin par mdzad pa'i dus su 'khor lo bde mchog bde chen lha lnga dang / rje btsun rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mus chen sangs rgyas rin chen rnams nam mkhar
zhal gzigs shing / khyad par 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen rje btsun rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug birWa pa'i rnam par gzigs te/ de'i skabs su sku 'khor rnams la gzigs
snang rnams byung tshul dang / nyams rtogs kyang blo kha rdzogs pa tsam byung / rje sangs rgyas rin chen 'di dus kyi min pa/ sems dpa' chen po las 'jigs pa 'dug ces rje
nyid kyis gsungs zhes kyang grags shing / yang chos skyong srung ma rnams kyis zhal bstan te 'phrin las bsgrub pa'i tshul ni/ skabs shig shab dge sdings kyi mgon khang du
rgyun ring bzhugs te thugs dam dang chos skyong gi gtor 'bul dang / bskang ba bstod pa rgya chen po mdzad pas/ de'i dus su kye rdor dang / rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi
mgon po lcam dral dang / khyad par las mkhan pu tra chen po lus kyi stod nyang pa byas pa cig mngon sum du gzigs shing / gzhan yang chos skyong mnyes pa'i rtags/ bud med
rgyan bzang pos brgyan pa dang / 'dzu gi mang po dges pa'i rnam 'gyur ci yang byed pa gzigs te/ de nas chos skyong 'khor bcas la bstod pa dgra bgegs srog gcod kyi 'khor
lo zhes bya ba dang / dpal ldan lha mo'i bskang gso dngos grub rol mtsho zhes bya ba gnyis rtsom par mdzad pa yin zhes thos la/ yang de'i rjes thog sa shig sgo rum du bse
mgon yid bzhin nor bu'i drung du sku mtshams yun ring gnang pa'i skabs su/ rje

btsun birWa pa'i sku'i bkod pa drug dang / sa chen gyi sku'i rnam 'gyur drug gzigs nas birWa pa dang sa skya pa chen po gnyis ngo bo gcig par yang dgongs shing / thugs la nyams
rtogs kyi ting nge 'dzin khyad par ba du ma 'khrungs zhes grags pa dang / gzhan yang skabs shig byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong du tshogs bdag gi sgrub pa mdzad skabs/
gnod sbyin bse'i gdong can gyi 'tshub kyi rnam pas gzims khang gi g.yam gdung gas grum cher byung ba na/ gzim khang la zhig bzos mdzad cing bar chad las grol te/ slar
sku mtshams de ka'i mu mthud nas rgyun ring gnang ba na/ rje btsun rin po che dang rdo rje lha mo sogs bla ma yi dam du ma'i zhal gzigs shing / de skabs dgongs phyogs sku
'chag pa la zhal 'don dang bstun rje btsun rin po che'i zan 'bum la zhabs bskor rgyun du gnang gi yod pa la/ mgo zla ba'i tshes bcu bzhi rje sa paN gyi dus chen gyi nyin/
phyag g.yog pa rab 'byams pa kun tshe bya ba dang dpon slob gnyis kyis zhabs bskor la phebs pas/ rje 'dis nam mkha' la gzigs te zhabs 'bring pa de la khyod kyis e mthong
gsung ba dang / des kyang nam mkha' la bltas pas nam mkha' shin tu dwangs pa la 'ja' 'od zlum po shin tu legs pa gcig 'dug nas/ 'di bzhin 'dug gzhan ni ma mthong zhus
pas/ rje'i zhal nas ya gi na rje sa skya paN chen phebs 'dug 'ja' 'od de tsam mthong ba yang sgrib pa chung ba yin gsungs te/ dpon slob gnyis kas dad pa chen po mdzad pas/
thugs nyams 'phar ba la sogs pa'i rnam

'gyur ci yang mdzad ces grags shing / yang lan cig gi tshe la stod lho'i sa skyong chen pos spyan 'dren gyi gsol ba btab ste zhal gyis bzhes nas/ der phebs pa'i gong rol zhig
tu mkha' spyod gzim chung sbug tu bzhugs pa'i skabs shig mtshan lam du rje sa skya pa chen po dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs yin nam snyam pa'i paNDi ta'i cha lugs byas pa gcig
chos rje sa paN/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug birWa pa/ slob dpon nag po spyod pa ba rnams chos kyi gsung gleng mdzad pa'i drung na bdag nyid chen po 'di phebs te the tshom

la stod lhor phebs te/ der snga dro thugs dam grol mtshams shig rje'i gsung gis/ da nang tho rangs bram ze'i gzugs ral pa'i khrod na seng ldeng gi rdo rje rtse lnga pa
yod pa zhig byung ste/ khyod rang gi mi 'phrod yod do zer nas/ bande char zhags gyon pa gnyis gtad pa'i snang ba byung / phyi na mar ltos shog dang gsungs/ sde pa'i sgo

lo bsgyur te phebs lam shrI rgod tshang du bzhugs nas rgod tshang phug par tshes bcu'i mchod pa mdzad pas/ rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma 'ja' 'od kyi dkyil na bzhugs
pa mngon sum du gzigs/ de nas gdan sar phebs te chos 'chad nyan rgya chen po mdzad pa'i

skabs/ gzhi thog gi gzims chung mkha' spyod sbug tu thugs dam mdzad dus/ 'khor rnams la khyed rnams phyir song / brda ma byung bar la su yang ma btang gsungs nas thugs dam
la sngar bas kyang rgyun ring bar bzhugs pa na/ gzims dpon gyis da nang sku khams nyog pa min lags sam zhus pas/ nyog pa min/ da nang bde ba can yin zer ba'i zhing khams
yid du 'ong ba zhig tu slebs/ rgyal ba 'od dpag med la sangs rgyas byang sems mang pos bskor ba dang / rje sa skya pa yab sras/ rje sangs rgyas rin chen rnams kyang bzhugs
'dug de rnams kyi drung na rin po che'i khri shin tu mdzes pa gnyis 'dug pa'i/ cung mtho ba mtha' skor du mchod pa'i lha mang pos mchod rdzas thogs nas 'khod pa/ steng

ba byung gsungs shing / de nas ha cang rgyun mi ring ba zhig na/ glo bor mkhan chen thams cad mkhyen pa zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i tshul bstan pa na/ de dus bdag nyid chen

bla ma dang yi dam chos skyong

bsam gyis mi khyab pa la mnga' mdzad pa zhig ste/ de yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis lha sar jo bo shAkya mu ne mjal bar phebs pa'i lam du skye chu bya ba'i chu bo de la grur

nas 'jigs pa las grol ba dang / gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis byang rwa sgreng bskor bar phebs te slar yar phebs pa'i lam du bla ma dge dga' ba bya ba dang / mal
gro sgrub chen pa'i slob ma bla ma sbal pa blo gros bya ba sbyor drug gi thugs dam shin tu smin pa gnyis kyi rmis ltas su/ rje 'di 'jam dbyangs dngos yin pa'i mtshan ma

gyi gnod pa mi 'byung ba'i phyir rdo la zhabs kyi rjes shin tu gsal ba 'jog pa mdzad pa na/ de nyid kyi snyan grags la brten sku tshe'i bar chad du song dogs/ /mtho'i 'og

ba'i dus yin yang / brag gseb nas 'jam dbyangs me tog mang po 'khrungs pa sogs mdor na de dag la sogs pa

grub pa brnyes pa'i rtags dang mtshan ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' bas/ 'phags pa sdud pa tshigs su bcad pa sogs shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i gzhung lugs rnams las
byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi phyir mi ldog pa'i rtags su gang bshad pa thams cad bdag nyid chen po 'di la mnga' ba yin la/ de bas na rje btsun sa skya pa zhes snyan pa'i
grags pas rgya mtsho'i gos can yongs su khyab pa'i gdung gi rigs su 'khrungs pa la/ bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan gyi
dge legs tsam gyis kyang skal ldan blo gsal rnams kyi snying gi chu skyes bzhad par nus pa de nyid khu dpon dang / bod yul mun pa'i gling 'dir dam pa'i chos kyi sgron
me chen po legs par spar te/ byang grol thar pa'i lam gyi rgyu'i gtso bo lhag pa tshul khrims kyi bslab pa rin po che'i srol chen kha ba can gyi ljongs 'dir gsar du btod
par mdzad pa'i byang chub sems dpa' chen po zhi ba 'tsho'i rnam par sprul pa'i sku dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes snyan pa'i ba dan dkar
po sa gsum na g.yo ba ste skyes mchog de dag byon pa'i phyi nas bdag nyid chen po 'di bas mkhas pa'i yon tan phul du byung ba gzhan ma byon par sa chen po la gnas pa'i

dag pa'i nam mkhar tshigs gsum gyi/ /tshul khrims yar ngo'i cha shas gong 'phel

zhing / /nges par 'byung ba'i chu shel las grub pa'i/ /gzhan la mi gnod btsun pa'i gos dkar can/ /byams dang snying rje'i dkyil 'khor ches rgyas pa'i/ /sems nyid nyin mor byed
pa'i 'od zer gyis/ /'gro ba'i sdug bsngal mun pa dpyis 'byin pa'i/ /phan bde'i lam bzang gsal mdzad skye dgu'i sgron/ /zab don ljon shing dam tshig rtsa ba brtan/ /rim

por bsgrub min te/ /

phyogs 'di kho nas spu ldang mchi ma g.yo/ /zhes gsungs pa ltar rtogs par bya'o/ /de ltar mkhas btsun bzang gsum dang ldan pa'i bdag nyid chen po de nyid kyis dgung lo bcu
gcig nas brtsams te/ bzhi bcu rtsa brgyad pa chu pho 'brug gi lo ma rdzogs kyi bar du bstan pa'i bya ba thos bsam sgom gsum dang / mkhas pa'i bya ba 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum
spel mar mdzad pas thugs shin tu rangs par gyur cing / snyigs ma'i skye bo ngan pa rnams kyi spyod tshul rnams gzigs pas thugs cung zad gdungs par gyur nas/ zhing khams

kyis kyang da lo rje 'di la sku dog shin tu che zer ba byung ba na/ kun sems yed yed por gyur te de'i skabs su thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyis rje 'di
la deng sang mtshan ltas la sogs pa ji ltar byung / phyi lo 'di dgung steng yin pas sku dog bzhin ni med lags sam zhes zhu ba mdzad pa na/ bdag nyid chen po'i gsung gis/
deng sang rmis ltas la sogs pa gang yang ma byung / kha sing snga gong za zi bzhin kha cig byung ba glo bor mkhan chen chos kyi rje zhing gzhan du gshegs pa la lta ba yin
nam snyam pa gcig byung ste de kha rkyang pa min pa 'dra/ phyi lo 'di la dog cha phran bu yod nyen ka che zhes gsungs/ de la rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyis 'o na de la dmigs
nas sku rim dang / sku mtshams sogs mdzad nas yun ring du zhabs

pad brtan pa'i rten 'brel gnang dgos zhus pas/ rje'i gsung gis/ rim gro sogs sngar yang gang grub byas/ da rung rim pas byed rtsis yin/ mtshams dam pa zhig byed bsams na'ang

sems dpa'i rnam par sprul pa la la bltams pa dang / la la mya ngan las

'da' ba la sogs pa'i tshul ston pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas de kun gyi ltas yin mod gsungs shing / gzhan gyi sems bsrung ba'i phyir du yal yol mdzad/ tshes bcu'i snga gro'i dus
da lta sku khams gso ba'i mnal cung zad cig mdzad na nyin mo sku khams dwangs pa yong lags sam zhus pas/ de tsam 'dug long med ces gsungs shing / zhing khams 'di'i mdzad
pa re zhig rdzogs pa dang / zhing khams gzhan du gdul bya rgya che ba la dgongs nas rtag 'dzin can rnams nges 'byung bskyed pa dang / le lo can rnams brtson 'grus la bskul
ba'i ched du chos kyi rje de nyid dgung lo bzhi bcu rtsa dgur phebs pa chu mo sbrul gyi lo chu stod zla ba'i tshes bcu'i nyi ma dro bar tsam la gdan sa chen po'i bla
brang rin chen sgang nyid du gzugs kyi sku chos kyi dbyings su bsdu bar mdzad cing / de nas phyi dro'i cha la babs pa na thams cad kyis gsan pa'i thag sgra shin tu che ba
dang bcas te dbu'i gtsug gi thod pa sor gang tsam cig gtsug tor gyi tshul du 'phags pa la byang sems kyi zil pa phrom me ba dang bcas par gyur cing / de ma thag nas sngar
su zhig gi sna'i yul du tshor ma myong ba'i lha rdzas kyi spos kyi dri bsung khyad par can gyis gzim khang gi steng 'og thams cad khyab pa dang / kha dog sna tshogs pa'i
'ja' tshon gyi ri mos mdzes pa'i nam mkha' las me tog gi char chen po babs pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te/ rgyud sde rnams nas 'byung ba'i 'da'
kha ma'i rnal 'byor gyis bde ba can gyi zhing khams su dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma rnams kyi bsu ba

dang bcas gshegs par gyur to zhes bshad pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i bdag nyid chen po de'i gcung che ba/ bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ni gzhon
nu nyid nas rab tu byung ste/ slar yang mkhan chen bsod nams lhun grub kyi drung du bsnyen rdzogs mdzad cing / mkhas pa'i bya ba 'chad nyan gyi sgo nas thub bstan rnam
rgyal dang / dpal rnam dga' ba gdong rnams kyi gdan sa mdzad nas bstan pa rin po che dar bar mdzad pa'i ring nas thugs dam zab mo la yang shin tu brtson/ de dag gi skabs
nas gcen sa lo tsA ba 'jam pa'i dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams dang / yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba rje btsun sangs rgyas rin chen sogs mkhas grub mang du bsten nas gsan
pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son pa mdzad cing / bla ma la brtan bzhugs 'bul tshul sogs sngon med pa'i gsung rab kyang 'ga' zhig mdzad/ mdor na sku tshe ril por bstan pa dang
sems can gyi don 'ba' zhig gis dus 'da' bar mdzad nas mthar ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te gzugs kyi sku chos dbyings su bsdu ba'i tshul bstan cing / de'i gcung
'jam dpal grags pa bya ba yang / thugs dam la shin tu brtson zhing khams phyogs la 'gro ba'i don la phebs nas 'phrin las shin tu che ba'i ngang nas mdo khams su ngo mtshar
pa'i rtags du ma dang bcas te zhi bar gshegs/ de'i gcung 'jam dbyangs tshe brtan bkra shis zhes bya ba ni/ spyir thugs dam zab mo'i rim pa la shin tu brtson zhing /
khyad par chos skyong la mnga' brnyes/ de'i nang nas zhing skyong dur khrod

bdag po yab yum bran bzhin du 'khol nus pa sogs nus mthu'i mnga' bdag du grags la/ bstan pa'i bya ba yang gsung ngag bla ma brgyud pa'i bris thang shin tu ngo mtshar ba bzhengs
pa la sogs pa rten gsum mang du bzhengs shing / gzhan yang 'chad nyan sogs kyang ci rigs pa mdzad/ mthar dag pa'i gzigs snang sogs ya mtshan rmad du byung ba'i ltas
du ma dang bcas gdan sa rtse gdong nyid du sku zhi bar gshegs pa'i tshul bstan to/ /bla ma 'dis ya 'brog ma khri lcam khab tu bzhes pa la sras gnyis 'khrungs pa'i che ba
'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsam 'grub ni gzhon nu nyid nas grub pa'i sa brnyes pa'i ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa mang du mdzad cing / sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa sku mched rnams dang
/ yongs 'dzin dkon mchog lhun grub sogs las zab rgyas gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mdzod bzung ste/ thugs dam la brtson pa'i ngang nas spyir grub rtags du ma dang / khyad par chos
skyong gdong bzhi pa la bka' bsgo mdzad pas 'bri mo zhig la be'u rwa lnga byas pa zhig skyes pa'i mgo bo da lta yang rtse gdong na yod ces thos la/ mdor na grub pa'i
mdzad pa ya ma zung gi sgo nas 'os su gyur pa'i gdul bya rnams 'dul bar mdzad de/ mthar gzugs sku bsdu ba'i tshe yang ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te de dag pa'i
zhing du gshegs so/ /de'i gcung 'gran zla dang bral ba'i skyes chen dam pa khams gsum chos kyi rgyal po dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas/ srid pa gsum gyi 'dren mchog dam pa dpal
sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga'

rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan yongs su grags pa'i rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i me ro gso ba la bsams bzhin du sku skye ba bzhes pa
de nyid kyis sku tshe 'di'i sngon rol du thabs la mkhas pa'i sprul pa'i sku du mar bstan te/ mtha' yas pa'i sems can gyi don mdzad pa'i tshul mdo tsam zhig brjod na/ sngags
'chang bla ma bstan pa'i nyi ma grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po 'di nyid ni/ dus gsum rgyun mi 'chad par zhing khams ji snyed par gdul bya so so'i skal ba dang 'tshams
pa'i sku dang mtshan gyi rnam pa tha dad du bstan nas/ gdul bya'i 'gro ba 'khor du ma 'dus pa rnams bsdus/ bsdus pa rnams smin/ smin pa rnams grol/ grol ba rnams mthar phyin
pa'i lam la 'god par mdzad pa yin te/ de yang sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po 'di nyid/ thog mar sngags kyi lam du zhugs pa'i skal ldan rnams kyi ngor gsang sngags kyi
rgyud sde mtha' dag sdud pa'i byed pa po mchog tu gyur pa gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje zhes bya bar grags shing / theg pa chen po'i rigs can rnams kyi ngor theg
pa chen po'i bka' mtha' dag sdud pa po kun tu bzang po zhes bya bar grags la/ gdul bya nyan thos pa rnams kyi ngor mdo sde'i sde snod sdud pa po dgra bcom pa kun dga' bo
zhes bya bar grags shing / yang bod gangs ri'i khrod 'dir mdo rgyud kyi chu gter chen po spel ba la mtshungs pa dang bral ba'i lo tsA ba bai ro tsa na zhes grags shing /
slar yang blang dor gyi rnam gzhag tshul bzhin du ston pa'i rje btsun sa skya paNDi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes

bya bar grags pas rgya bod hor gsum gyi gdul bya skal ldan rnams dam pa'i chos la 'god par mdzad nas shar phyogs mngon par dga' ba'i zhing du de bzhin gshegs pa dri ma med
pa'i dpal zhes bya ba'i mchog gi sprul skur gyur te/ des gdul bya rnams phan bde la 'god par mdzad pa yin la/ de ltar bshad ma thag pa'i sprul pa'i sku'i snang ba ji snyed
pa gcig bstan pa de dag gis ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa bzang po phyogs gcig tu bsdus nas/ gos dkar lcang los mdzes pa'i skur sprul te/ snyigs dus kyi skye bo gdug pa can
rnams zhi rgyas dbang drag gi 'phrin las rnam pa bzhi'i sgo nas rjes su 'dzin par mdzad pa ni/ dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen bkra
shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan yongs su grags pa 'di nyid yin la/ de lta bu'i sprul pa'i sku'i snang ba de dag sangs rgyas kyi ye shes gcig gi ngo
bor grub pa'i tshul sogs rgyal ba'i lung tshad ma dang sbyar na/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal ba'i sras po kun tu bzang po/ nyan thos chen po kun dga' bo ste mdo sngags kyi
bstan pa'i sdud pa po rnams ston pa rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas dang ngo bo dbyer med yin pa'i tshul ni/ gsang ba grub pa'i rgyud las/ 'di yi sdud par byed pa po/ /gzhan dag
yod pa ma yin zhes/ /bdag nyid 'ba' zhig smra bar byed/ /sdud mdzad pa ni thugs rdo rje/ /zhes dang / rtsa rgyud brtag gnyis las kyang / 'chad pa po nga chos kyang nga /
/rang gi tshogs ldan nyan pa nga / /zhes gsungs pa 'dis grub/ khyad

par kun tu bzang po dang kun dga' bo gnyis ngo bo dbyer med yin pa ni/ gnyis med rnam rgyal gyi rgyud las/ de nas thams cad mkhyen pa'i 'khor phun sum tshogs pa bshad par bya'o/
/'di lta ste/ 'jam dpal ni rgyal po zas gtsang mar gyur to/ /'jig rten dbang phyug ni lha mo sgyu 'phrul du gyur to/ /dpal lha mo ni grags 'dzin no/ /rdo rje sems dpa'
ni sgra gcan 'dzin no/ /sgrib pa thams cad rnam par sel ba ni shA ri'i bu'o/ /kun tu bzang po ni kun dga' bor gyur to/ /lha'i dbang po brgya byin ni gnas brtan lha sbyin
no/ /rnam par snang mdzad chen po ni yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub par gyur to zhes gsungs pa 'dis grub/ don de dag la dgongs nas mkhas pa'i dbang
po dkon mchog lhun grub kyis rje btsun sa skya pa'i gsung rabs kyi don bsdus tshul gsum rgyan las/ khyad par 'khor gyi gtso bo sdud pa po/ /ston pa'i gnyis su med pa'i ye
shes las/ /gzhan ngor sprul pa'i byang chub sems dpa' che/ /'og min gnas dang me tog rgyan gyis brgyan/ /mi mjed zhing dang khyad par mi yi ngor/ /rim bzhin rdo rje sems
dpa' kun tu bzang / /gsang ba'i bdag po kun dga' bo zhes grags/ /zhes gsungs pa yin no/ /bai ro tsa na dang kun dga' bo thugs rgyud gcig pa ni/ padma thang yig las/ rgya
gar rdo rje gdan gyi chos grwa nas/ /shAkya thub pa'i nye gnas kun dga' bo/ /tshe 'phos longs sku'i zhing khams mang nyul nas/ /mi lus chos ldan skye ba bdun gyi mtha'/
/gtsang gi snye mo bye mkhar zhes bya yi/ /gnas gzhi gcig

gi brang khang mig dgu na/ /pha ming pa gor he 'dod ces bya dang / /ma ming bran ka bza' sgron skyid kyi bu/ /gan jag thang mtha' zhes bya lo brgyad pa/ /de la bslabs pas lo
tsA rtsod med 'byung / /zhes gsungs pa 'dis grub/ sa skya paN chen dang bai ro tsA na tha dad med pa ni/ gter ston sangs rgyas gling pa'i gter ma kong po pu ri phug mo
che nas spyan drangs pa'i bla ma dgongs pa 'dus pa'i lung bstan bka' rgya'i las can nyi shu rtsa gcig gi lung bstan las/ lo tsA ba gor bai ro tsa na khyod/ /tshe rabs bskal
bzang da dus tshigs la phan/ /de bzhin ma 'ongs dus kyi mthar thug pa/ /rim bzhin 'gro rnams 'dren dang bstan pa skyong / /khyad par dmu rgod 'dul mgo 'chol ba'i tshe/
/sa zhes bya ba shAkya'i zhing khams su/ /sgra bsgyur lo tsA paNDi blo stobs can/ /sa skyong rgyal po'i mchod gnas byed pa ste/ /dmu rgod kha gnon 'gro la phan pa 'byung
/ /rgyud mang rim bzhin de bzhin bsam mi khyab/ /ces lung bstan pa 'dis grub/ de bzhin gshegs pa dri ma med pa'i dpal rje sa paN dang ngo bo gcig pa ni/ sngon rje btsun
rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gzugs sku chos dbyings su bsdus zin pa'i dus re zhig gi tshe na rje sa paN la rje btsun rin po che dang / rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug birWa
pa dang / grub chen nag po pa gsum gyi sku'i snang ba dngos su bstan zhing / rje btsun rin po che'i zhal nas/ khyod skye ba 'di'i 'og rol du mkha' la gnas pa'i rig pa 'dzin
par gyur nas/ sa lam gyi rtogs pa phal cher bgrod de de nas rgya gar shar

phyogs mu mu ne'i zhing khams su rgyal po nyi ma'i stobs 'phel gyi bur gyur te/ 'khor los sgyur ba'i cha byad can gyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnams yongs su sbyong bar byed
cing / de nas skye ba bzhi pa la mngon par dga' ba'i zhing du de bzhin gshegs pa dri ma med pa'i dpal zhes bya bar mngon par rdzogs pa sangs rgyas par 'gyur ro zhes lung
bstan pa 'dis grub/ de ltar na sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa'i sku'i snang ba ji snyed pa de dag bai ro tsA na dang thugs rgyud gcig yin zhing / de dang sngags 'chang
chos kyi rgyal po nyid tha dad med pa ni/ gsang ba'i lung bstan gab rgya can las/ da lta'i lo tsA bai ro tsA na khyod/ /nges don rnam snang gang chen mtsho zhes grags/
/longs sprul byang sems du mas 'gro ba 'dren/ /gsung gi sprul pa drang don bcu gsum gyi/ /tha ma 'khon gyi rigs la grags pa'i mtshan/ /bdud kyi nye mtshams gsang sngags
bstan pa skyong / /byang sems drag gtum ma nges snang tshul can/ /de dang 'brel tshad skye ba gsum nas grol/ /dri snying rta sogs lag gis gang reg pa/ /ngan song skye sgo
chod de nges tshig yin/ /las ldan de la bdud mo'i bar chad dam/ /rgya nag khams nas lha bu'i bdud la gzobs/ /de dus thugs sprul zag med dam pa dang / /'phrad na 'gro la
phan pa dpag med 'byung / /tshe mthar phyin cing bar chad tshogs las rgyal/ /khyad par stod hor bdud sprul zil gyis gnon/ /sprul pas sems can don la sgrib g.yogs med/ /mtha'
yas longs sku chen po'i zhing khams su/ /nges par snying la chongs shig sa ma ya/ /

zhes dang / snang rtse gter ston pas chos 'khor lha sa'i sangs rgyas rabs bdun gyi sku rgyab nas gter nas spyan drangs pa'i thugs rje chen po 'khor ba las grol gyi chos kyi
lo rgyus lung byang gsal ba'i sgron me las/ bai ro'i skye ba 'khon rigs glang lo pa/ /grags pa'i ming can chos bdag skyes bu 'byung / /de la gtad pas sangs rgyas bstan pa
'phel/ /zhes dang / yang sprul sku snang rtse bas khyud tshang brag gi padma bcud phud nas gdan drangs pa'i dam 'dzin lha sras kyi skye rgyud la/ da lta'i lo tsA bai ro
tsA na khyod/ /'khon gyi rigs la grags pa'i ming 'chang ste/ zab chos 'di dang 'phrad na tshe mthar phyin/ /bstan pa dbus khams yongs la spel bar byed/ /ces lung bstan pa
'dis grub pa yin no/ /'di dag ni gang zag 'ga' zhig la skyes bu dam pa 'di zhes bya ba'i rnam par sprul pa'o zhes zog brdzus can dag gi long ba 'khar 'dzugs kyis rang gzhan
gnyis phung gi las la sbyor ba'i tshul dang mi 'dra ba'i dri ma med pa'i lung tshad mas grub pa 'di ni kun dang thun mong ma yin pa'i rnam par thar pa'o/ /'dir smras
pa/ spangs rtogs mthar phyin rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas nyid/ /gzhan ngor sprul sku du ma'i zlos gar gyis/ /mtha' yas 'gro ba'i don mang mdzad pa 'di/ /sngags 'chang bla ma'i
sngon gyi skyes rabs yin/ /da ni da ltar gyi sku'i skye ba bzhes pa'i rnam par thar pa mdo tsam spel ba la don gnyis te/ tshigs bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang / de'i
don mdo tsam bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ dus gsum rgyal ba'i mkhyen zhing

brtse ba las/ /nus mthu gcig bsdus dpal ldan sa skya pa'i/ /dri med rigs su bsams bzhin skur bstan pa/ /snyigs ma'i dus 'dir bstan pa'i gsal byed mchog /ngag dbang kun dga'
rin chen zhes grags pa'i/ /skyes mchog de nyid me mo glang lor bltams/ /bcu bdun bar du sa skya lo tsA che/ /'bral med bsten te dam chos mang du mnos/ /de nas yongs 'dzin
dkon mchog lhun grub dang / /dpal ldan bkra shis ngag dbang chos grags zhabs/ /sangs rgyas seng ge paN chen legs blo sogs/ /gus pas bsten nas dbang khrid man ngag lung
/ /rjes gnang byin rlabs bka' gtad la sogs pa/ /grangs med gsan pa rgya mtsho'i mdzod bzung nas/ /byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong la sogs pa'i/ /gnas mchog du mar dges rdor
bde mchog dang / /rdo rje phur pa chos skyong gur zhal sogs/ /lha mchog zhi khro rab 'byams du ma yi/ /grangs dang mtshan ma'i bsnyen pa mthar phyin nas/ /bka' srung
dam can rgya mtsho bran ltar 'khol/ /de tshe bstan la gnod byed dgra bgegs rnams/ /lo zla ma 'gyangs rnam shes dbyings su bsgral/ /de dag ma 'ongs srid pa'i rgyun kyang bcad/
/gzhan yang rang gi snang ngor dag snang las/ /ma 'das mod kyang gdul bya gzhan gyi ngor/ /dka' spyad drag pos bstan dang 'gro ba'i phyir/ /sku srog nyid kyang gtong
la mi zhum pa'i/ /byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rlabs po ches/ /phyi nang gsang ba'i 'gal rkyen kun bsal nas/ /snang srid lha mi thams cad dbang du bsdus/ /de nas sngon
byon gong ma'i gnas kyi

mchog /gdan sa chen po dpal ldan sa skya yi/ /gtsug lag khang chen nyams pa rnams gsos te/ /sku gsung thugs kyi rten dang mchod chas bkang / /gzhan yang 'gro ba'i bsod nams
'phel ba'i phyir/ /ngo mtshar mchod pa'i rten dang mchod pa'i rdzas/ /yid 'phrog khang bzang du ma'ang gsar du spel/ /khyad par rgyal ba'i bstan pa gsal mdzad pa'i/ /bshes
gnyen brgya phrag mang po 'byung ba'i gzhi/ /chos grwa chen po thub bstan lha chen dang / /gsang sngags 'dzin pa du ma 'du ba'i gnas/ /bde ba chen po'i gling sogs legs
btab nas/ /bstan pa'i bya ba thos bsam sgom gsum dang / /mkhas pa'i bya ba 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyis/ /bde gshegs bstan pa yar ngo'i zla ltar spel/ /gzhan yang rdo rje
'chang dngos sa skya pa'i/ /gong ma dgongs pa chos dbyings mnyam gzhag pa/ /de dag thugs dgongs rdzogs phyir dges rdor dang / /bde mchog gsang 'dus yang phur la sogs pa/
/dri med rgyud nas bshad pa'i dkyil 'khor tshogs/ /sgrub cing mchod dang bdag 'jug len pa dang / /slob ma dbang bskur la sogs lo re bzhin/ /mi nyams dbyar mtsho bzhin du
'phel bar mdzad/ /mdor na zhi rgyas dbang dang drag po yi/ /sna tshogs thabs mkhas du mas gdul bya rnams/ /gang la gang 'dul tshul du legs bskyangs te/ /'dzin ma'i khyon
'di rdzogs ldan bde la bkod/ /sngon tshe chos rgyal mes dbon de dag gis/ /bstan pa rin chen bya ba mdzad pa'i tshul/ /bsam las 'das mod sangs rgyas byang sems

kyi/ /rnam par sprul pa de dag 'das pa'i rjes/ /gangs can khrod 'dir kun mkhyen sangs rgyas kyi/ /bstan pa'i bya ba rlabs chen mdzad pa la/ /sngags 'chang nyid las ngo mtshar
che ba gzhan/ /med ces deng dus dpyod ldan yongs la grags/ /de lta'i bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po de/ /re brgyad bzhes pa shing pho spre'u'i lo/ /gro bzhin zla ba'i yar
ngo'i bcu bzhi la/ /sa skya'i lha chen lhun grub pho brang du/ /dgongs pa chos kyi dbyings su thim tshul bstan/ /de lta'i sprul pa'i skyes mchog de nyid las/ /brgyud 'dzin
slob bu mang du 'phel ba yi/ /kun gyi mchog ni chos dang rigs kyi sras/ /grub pa'i dbang phyug puNya indra dang / /sems dpa' chen po grags pa blo gros mtshan/ /gzhan
yang bstan pa gsal mdzad bshes gnyen tshogs/ /nyi zla bzhin du grags pas yongs khyab cing / /skar phran bzhin du bgrang ba'i yul 'das pas/ /'dzin ma'i khyon 'di yongs su
khyab gyur te/ /spyi dang bye brag bstan pa rin po che/ /dbyar mtsho bzhin du 'phel ba'i dge mtshan 'di/ /sprul pa'i skyes mchog sngags 'chang chos kyi rje/ /kun dga' rin
chen gang gi rnam thar yin/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa de'i don mdo tsam bshad pa ni/ /de lta bu'i bdag nyid chen po de nyid kha ba can 'dir 'gran pa'i zla dang bral ba'i rigs
brgyud 'khon sa skya pa zhes pa'i mtshan gyi dge legs dang ldan pa'i gdung rigs 'dzin pa'i skyes chen dam pa 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' don grub tshe brtan bkra shis rgyal mtshan
dpal bzang po zhes bya ba de nyid kyi btsun mo lha gcig bu 'dren skyid bya ba la me mo

glang gi lo ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas gdan sa chen po rtse gdong bla brang gi gnas mchog tu yum la gnod pa med par bltams pa yin te/ de ltar bltams nas lam thams
cad kyi rtsa ba sdom pa gsum gyis thugs rgyud phyug par mdzad de/ gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son cing / thos bsam mthar phyin par mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ rje 'di dgung
lo dgur phebs pa'i tshe/ gnas lnga rig pa'i paNDi ta chen po 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung du/ so sor thar pa'i bslab bya dge
bsnyen dang dge tshul gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa nos te/ mtshan yang 'jam dbyangs ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes
gsol zhing / yang 'jam dbyangs sa lo tsA ba de nyid kyi drung du theg chen dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed kyang gsan nas/ rgyal ba'i sras po kun gyi gtsug gi nor bur gyur
te/ de nas bdag nyid chen po 'dis sa skya lo tsA chen po de nyid kyi zhabs drung du/ bcom ldan 'das dges pa rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor du smin byed dbang gi chu bo lan grangs
mang po zhig gsan nas rigs 'dzin sngags kyi sdom pas thugs rgyud bltams par mdzad cing / gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa'i drung du bdag med lha mo
bco lnga'i dbang dang / 'khor lo bde mchog lU nag dril gsum gyi dbang sogs smin byed dbang gi rnam grangs nyer bzhi tsam dang grol byed khrid kyi skor la/ gsung ngag rin
po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag

cha lag dang bcas pa dang / de'i rgyab brten gsung ngag glegs bam dkar chag nang bzhin gyi lung dang / pod dmar ma dkar chag nang bzhin gyi lung dang / gtsug tor rnam rgyal
gyi rjes gnang sogs rjes gnang gi rnam grangs bcu phrag gnyis tsam dang / de dag gi rgyab brten gyi lung du rgya bod kyi mkhas pa du mas mdzad pa'i gsung rab dang / gzhan
yang sa lo nyid kyi gsung 'bum/ rdo rje 'chang gi bka' 'bum/ sems dpa' chen po'i bka' 'bum/ kun mkhyen gyi bka' 'bum/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rin gyi bka' 'bum/ glo bo mkhan
chen gyi bka' 'bum rnams kyi lung dang / gzhan yang dag ljon skor gsum gyi lung bshad/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud kyi TI ka mu tig phreng ba'i lung bshad sogs dang / gzhan yang
bla ma'i rnam thar dang / gsol 'debs bstod pa'i lung sogs mdor na zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos tshul rgya mtsho lta bu zhig gsan nas thugs su chud par mdzad cing / rtsa
ba'i bla ma rnams kyi nang nas kyang chos rje 'di nyid la mchog tu 'dzin pa yin te/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ bla ma kun 'dus kun dga' bsod nams dang / /zhes pa
dang / sa lo chen po'i zhabs drung skye phyir bris/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang sa lo nyid dang skad cig kyang 'bral ba med pa'i thugs gdong mthon pa'i ngang nas/
zhi rgyas dbang drag gi 'phrin las ci mdzad kyang de dang de'i don thogs med du 'grub cing / dus phyis kyang dngos dang 'od gsal chen po'i ngang du sa lo nyid byon nas phra
rags kyi lung bstan rnams sgrib med du 'byung ba yin zhes grags

la/ yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis bdag chen ngag gi dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi drung du yang dges pa rdo rje'i dbang sogs dbang gi rnam grangs 'ga' zhig dang / dkar
mo nyi zla lcam dral/ bran bdud gshin rje nag po'i rjes gnang sogs gsan cing / yang sngags 'chang bla ma rang nyid kyi yab 'jam dbyangs nam mkha' don grub tshe brtan bkra
shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhal snga nas la dges pa rdo rje'i dbang sogs dbang gi rnam grangs du ma zhig dang / gshed dmar spros med kyi khrid sogs grol
byed khrid kyi rnam gzhag kha yar dang / gzhan yang rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos dmar po skor gsum sgrub pa'i phyag len/ de'i yig skor sogs mdor na zab mo dam pa'i chos
kyi phyag len phra mo 'ga' zhig gi phyag khrid rnams kyang gsan cing / yang thams cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi drung du gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang
bcas pa'i gdams ngag gi khrid glegs bam gyi lung dang bcas pa dang / gsung ngag bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar thor bu ba rnams kyi lung / gzhan yang gshed dmar lha lnga'i
dbang / rdzogs rim shin tu spros med kyi khrid dang / de'i skor la rnal 'byor dbang phyug gis mdzad pa'i spros med rdo rje'i tshig rkang sogs rgya gzhung tshad ldan du
ma'i lung dang / rje rdo rje 'chang gis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs bdud rtsi'i bum pa/ dkyil chog bdud rtsi'i chu rgyun sogs bod gzhung tshad ldan mang po'i lung sogs mdor
na rje de nyid kyi drung du gshin rje gshed dmar po'i chos skor yongs su rdzogs pa gsan

cing / gzhan yang kye rdor bka' babs phyi ma rnams kyi dbang / rdo rje phreng ba yongs rdzogs kyi dbang / gsang 'dus/ 'jigs byed/ mgon po sogs kyi dbang / kye rdor rgyud gsum
gyi bshad bka'/ rdo rje 'chang gi bka' 'bum pod bzhi ma/ mgon po'i gser pod tshang ma/ rje ngor chen thams cad mkhyen pa rang gi bka' 'bum gyi lung dang / sgrub thabs
rgya mtsho dang brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang dang / de dag gi yig cha'i lung / dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang yig rnying gi lung dang bcas pa sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig
gsan cing thugs su chud par mdzad/ yang chos kyi rje 'phags chen dpal ldan bkra shis kyi drung du/ birWa pa'i srung ba thun mong dang thun mong ma yin pa gnyis dang / brda
chig brgyud sogs gsung ngag gi cha lag rnams dang / rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i byin rlabs dang / 'di'i rnal 'byor bcu gcig gi bshad bka'/ rtsa dbu ma'i khrid/ mgon
po'i rtsa gsum 'khor lo'i khrid sogs khrid bka' mang po zhig dang / rjes gnang zur bka' bcu phrag gnyis kyis lhag pa sogs thun mong ma yin pa'i zab gnad rnams gsan/ yang
chos rje kun dga' grol mchog blo gsal rgya mtsho'i sde'i zhal snga nas la/ 'khor lo sdom chen gyi dbang / dgra nag gi dbang sogs zab chos 'ga' zhig gsan cing / yang lo
nas spyan snga rin po che ngag dbang chos grags kyi drung du/ bka' gdams thig le bcu drug gi dbang / bka' gdams lha bzhi'i khrid/ blo sbyong don bdun ma/ bka' gdams pha
chos bu chos/ bka' gdams gzhung drug sogs

dang / dzam dkar gyi rjes gnang sogs dkon zhing zab pa'i rjes gnang dang / byin rlabs kyi rigs mang po zhig gsan par mdzad/ gzhan yang paN chen legs blo ba/ ngor chen sangs
rgyas seng ge gter ston snang rtse ba/ gter ston shes rab 'od zer ba rnams kyang gus pas bsten nas dbang byin rlabs gter chos sogs mtha' yas pa zhig gsan cing / gsan pa
de rnams kyang tshig don gyi cha la sgro 'dogs mtha' dag chod par mdzad pas mdo rgyud bstan bcos ji snyed pa'i mnga' bdag chen por bzhugs pa yin no zhes grags la/ de ltar
yongs 'dzin dam pa rnams las zab rgyas gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son par mdzad pa'i sngags 'chang bla ma 'di nyid kyis/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i chos kyi khri ga la
ba der zhabs zung bkod cing / bla ma gong ma rnams kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i dgon pa dang / yang dben rnams su sgom sgrub la gzhol ba'i sgo nas yi dam zhi khro rab 'byams
rnams dang / rdo rje'i chos skyong rnams kyi grangs dang mtshan ma'i bsnyen pa mthar phyin pa mdzad de/ bla ma yi dam rnams kyi zhal gzigs shing / bstan srung rnams bran
bzhin du bkol te bstan dgra rnams tshar bcad nas/ spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa 'phel rgyas su mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ bdag nyid chen po 'di dgung lo dgur phebs pa shing
mo bya'i lo/ /sa skya paNDi ta chen po'i chos kyi khri chen por khams gsum chos kyi rgyal por mnga' gsol te/ gdan sa chen po'i bla ma slob dpon dge ba'i bshes gnyen gtso
bor gyur pa'i skye bo'i tshogs stong phrag du ma

la/ thub pa'i dgongs pa gsal ba zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos chen po yongs rdzogs/ dag gsal snyan pa'i gsung gis nyi ma gsum gyi bar du legs par bshad pas/ skye bo mkhas blun thams
cad kyi dad gus chen pos mchog tu bsngags pa'i gnas su gyur cing / de nas bdag nyid chen po 'di'i rtse gdong du phebs nas/ slar yang dgung lo bcu bgrang tsam bzhes pa
na gdan sa chen por phebs te/ de dus gdan sa'i shar phyogs 'phrang ring gi mgor phebs pa na/ chu mig rdzing kha phyogs kyi mchod rten mang po zhig pa'i nag srol le ba de
gzigs pa dang / bdag nyid chen po 'di'i thugs dgongs la/ kye ma bdud sprul rnams kyi byed pas sde mang po zhig ral du song 'dug 'di thams cad zhig gsos byas/ gtsug lag
khang rnams dang / sde 'di tshags su bcug ste khra chem me ba zhig nged la nam yong ngam snyam pa'i nges 'byung dang / lhag bsam yid la nan ltar gcags pa zhig byung zhes
bdag nyid chen po rang gis yang yang gsungs so zhes grags shing / de nas sa lo chen po'i drung du bzhugs te/ de'i skabs nas rje 'di dgung lo bcu bdun bzhes pa tshun chad
du sa lo nyid dang 'bral med du bzhugs nas gong du bstan pa'i zab chos rnams kyang gsan par mdzad cing / sa lo nyid phyogs su 'gro don la phebs pa'i tshe yang zhabs phyir
'brangs te dbang rjes gnang sogs gnang ba'i mchod g.yog rgyun par mdzad/ gdan sa chen por bla ma gong ma'i sgrub mchod dang / gtor bzlog sogs kyi chag phyir yang rgyun par
phebs te dbyangs rol phyag rgya'i gar 'chams sogs

kyi phyag len phra mo rnams kyang shin tu nges par mdzad nas/ dus phyis rjes 'jug rnams kyi don du so so'i yi ge sa lo chen po'i phyag len bzhin bkod par mdzad pa yin la/ de
ltar bdag nyid chen po khu dbon gnyis lhan cig bzhugs pa'i bstan pa rin po che 'phel rgyas su mdzad pa'i skabs nas chu mo sbrul gyi lo/ sa lo 'jam dbyangs chen po nyid/
zhing khams gzhan du 'byon par nye ba na/ bdag nyid chen po 'di la spyan cher gzigs nas/ /ngag gi dbang po byis pa'i snang ba ma byed ang / dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa 'di
chags sam 'jig khyed la rag las pa yod do zhes gsungs pa ltar gyi bka' chem thugs kyi dkyil du bcang ste/ dpal ldan sa skya'i bstan pa rin po che yar ngo'i zla ba ltar
'phel rgyas su mdzad pa yin te/ de nas bdag nyid chen po 'di dgung lo nyi shur ma son tsam gyi skabs su sa lo chen po zhing gzhan du gshegs pas thugs shin tu gdungs par
gyur pa dang / mi srun pa 'ga' zhig gi spyod tshul la thugs 'byung bar gyur nas/ byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong du phebs nas lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor dang / lam gyi
thun bzhi la dbang len pa gtso bor mdzad de/ aShTa 'bum phrag so gnyis sbyin sreg dang bcas pa mdzad pa'i tshe/ lan cig tho rangs kyi tshe byas 'gyur gyi shar phyogs kyi
nam mkha' la 'ja' 'od 'khyil pa'i dbus su sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa nyid zhabs rdo rje skyil krung dang / phyag gnyis rdor dril thugs kar bsnol nas bzung ba zhig gsal
por gzigs te/ dad gus cher g.yos nas/ rgyal ba'i mkhyen brtse ma

bya ba'i sa lo chen po la bstod pa 'di yang de'i skabs su mdzad pa yin zhes grags shing / yang lan cig mnal lam gyi tshul du nam mkhar 'ja' sprin yid du yong ba zhig gi khrod
na rin po che'i khang bzang dang / ljon shing gi tshogs mang po dang bcas pa'i bar mtshams rnams la dar gyi lda ldi dang / rin po ches brgyan pa zhig 'dug pa la/ 'di ci
yin gsungs pa la/ bde ba can yin zer/ zhing khams de nyid du phebs pa'i thugs 'dun mdzad pa na/ sprin gseb nas skas shig skya thal btang byung ba la 'dzegs byon pas/ skas
mgo na sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa nyid zhal bzhugs dus kyi sku 'khor rnams dang bcas gzigs pa na/ thugs dges spro chen pos phyag mang du mdzad pa'i mod la mnal sad byung
bas shin tu phongs pa cig byung zhes zhabs drung na gnas pa rnams la bka' stsal pa dang / mnal lam de nyid kyi bkod pa rnams sgra ji bzhin du bris pa'i 'og thad na/ 'di
ngag gi dbang po'i rmi lam yin ces pa'i zhal byang dang bcas pa yod pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i zhal thang chung ngu grabs gcig yod pa de/ dus phyis bdag gi bla ma sngags 'chang
grags pa blo gros kyi nang rten dngul gdung yid bzhin nor bu bzhengs dus gzungs zhugs su legs par bzhugs so/ /de'i skabs su 'phags chen dpal ldan bkra shis la gong du
bstan pa'i zab chos rnams dang / khyad par 'khor lo bde mchog gi skor rnams gsan nas/ bde mchog nag po pa'i gsung bsnyen dang / rtsa dbu ma'i khrid gsan pa dang mnyam du/
oM gsum ma 'bru 'bum lhag pa tsam gyi gsung bzlas mdzad pa

na/ yi dam gyi rjes su bzung ba'i mtshan ltas bsam gyi mi khyab pa byung ba dang / khyad par de dus sngags 'chang nyid kyi zhabs drung du gtad nas 'ongs pa'i mi rnams skyed
lhas sgrub sde tsam du slebs pa na/ mi rnams kyi dbyibs dang / ming dang / dngos po 'di lta bu khyer 'dug pa sogs 'od gsal gyi ngang nas sgrib med du gzigs pa dang / gzhan
yang gnas der 'phags chen nyid las gur gyi mgon po'i nang khrid gsan nas thugs dam rtse gcig tu mdzad pa na/ gur mgon lha brgyad/ ber nag zangs gri can/ ru 'dren sde bzhi
dregs pa'i 'khor dang bcas pa rnam 'gyur sna tshogs mdzad pa yang nas yang du gzigs shing / gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis rdo rje phur pa la gsung bsnyen thang bzhi'i
bar du mdzad de/ thang cig byas 'gyur du mdzad pa de'i skabs su/ byas 'gyur gyi gzhi bdag klu mo dkar mo dang / bdud kyi rta pa bco brgyad 'khor dang bcas pa snga dro
lung pa'i mdor 'gro ba dang / phyi dro phur 'gro ba nyin re bzhin gzigs snang la byung ba na/ sngar dpal chen pho brang du phur pa'i gsung bsnyen mdzad skabs/ dkar mo nyi
zla dang bdud kyi rgyal po 'khor bcas gzigs snang la byung ba dang cha lugs mthun par 'dug pas thugs rgyud kyang gcig gam snyam du dgongs nas/ byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag
rdzong gi sgrub sde chen po mi nyams shing yun du gnas pa sogs kyi bka' bsgo mdzad pa na/ gzhi bdag rnams kyis kyang de bzhin khas blangs par brten/ de'i gtang rag tu dmigs
nas bsang yig rgyas par/ gzhi bdag klu mo

dkar mo dang / zhes sogs kyi tshigs bcad 'di yang 'jug par mdzad pa yin zhes thos so/ /gzhan yang dpal yang dag he ru ka'i gsung bsnyen yang lan grangs du ma zhig mdzad par
brten/ bla ma dang lhag pa'i lhas byin gyis brlabs pa'i mtshan ma yang mang du brnyes shing / yang dag gi sgrub dkyil ngo mtshar can 'di nyid kyang rtsoms shig pa'i lung
bstan sa lo nyid kyis mdzad par snang ste/ dkyil chog de nyid kyi mjug tu/ sa lo nyid zhal gzigs te/ sngags 'chang rang nyid kyi thugs steng na yod pa'i don 'ga' zhig zhus
pa na rjes su gnang ba'i tshul sogs gsungs pa'i rjes su/ yang dag gi gsung rtsom thor bu 'di rnams sngar phan bdag gis bsgrig ma nus tshul zhib par zhus/ da ni ji lta
bu zhig bgyid lags zhes gsol ba btab pas/ zhal 'dzum pa dang bcas nged rang gi rtsom thor bu de rnams lhan cig bsdebs shing / gong 'og gi mtshams sbyor sogs khyod rang gi
blo la 'dug pa bzhin bsgrigs pas yong ba 'dug phebs pa la brten nas/ mi 'jigs pa'i spobs pa'i gdeng cung zad thob nas bris pa yin pas 'di la byin rlabs dang yid ches gnyis
ka yod do zhes gsungs pas so/ /gzhan yang sngags 'chang bla ma 'di nyid kyis zhing skyong dbang phyug chen po zhal bzhi pa'i gsung bsnyen mthar phyin par mdzad pa'i tshe/
zhing skyong chen po nyid bram ze'i gzugs sku mdog sngon po zhabs gnyis rol pa'i stabs kyis bzhugs pa sku shin tu che bas nam mkha'i khyon gang ba yum bzhi dang bcas
pa zhig gsal bar gzigs pa de'i snang brnyan ji lta ba bzhin 'bri bar

mdzad pa ni/ da lta sngags thang chen mo'i grabs la bzhugs pa 'di yin la/ yang lha khang rtser bzhugs pa'i skabs shig dge slong rin chen rnam grol gyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor
skyed lhas kyi gnas kha'u pa'i gzigs snang ma ltar zhal bzhi pa zhig nyid kyis phyag bris mdzad pa na/ rab gnas kyi tshe sku 'khor rnams kyis a tsa ra mdog sngon po zhig
gzims chung du song ba mngon sum mthun grub tu mthong zhing / sngags 'chang nyid kyi gzigs snang la zhal bzhi pa yum chen bzhi dang bcas pa rngam brjid dang ldan pa zhig
bris sku la mngon sum du thim pa gzigs pa dang / yang lha khang rtse'i po ta la de nyid du bzhugs pa'i skabs shig nub cig thun gtor phul ba'i rjes su grags pa zer ba'i
ban chung zhig yod pa de rje'i zhabs drung du 'ongs pa na/ gzims chung 'gag gi skas mgor/ bud med nag mo ral pas rting pa khebs pa/ lag gnyis spar mo gdengs shing rkang
pa gar stabs kyis 'dug pa zhig dang 'phrad pa na/ ban chung de 'jigs dngangs pas cung zad brgyal zhing / der rjes sngags 'chang nyid la de'i tshul rnams zhus pa na/ de la
skrag par byed mi dgos/ do nub kyi thun gtor len pa la sring mo byon byung ba dang / khyod rang rtsa gsal bas 'phrad pa yin/ nyes skyon gtan med ces kyang gsung bar grags
pa dang / gzhan yang sngags 'chang bla ma 'dis sgo rum ye shes mgon po bzhugs pa'i drung du shA sa na 'bum phrag bzhi dang / gzhan yang sa phyogs gzhan du yi ge bdun ma
bye bsnyen thang gnyis tsam mdzad par brten/ gzhi

thog gi mkha' spyod du bzhugs pa'i skabs shig gzigs snang la/ gur gyi mgon po'i sku shin tu che ba zhig ro gdan dgu brtsegs kyi steng na za 'og gi ber dgu brtsegs gsol te 'gying
ba'i stabs kyis bzhugs pa/ nyi ma 'bum gyi gzi brjid 'bar ba zhig mngon sum du gzigs pa dang / yang dben gnas byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong du sngags 'chang yab
sras sogs dpon slob nyung shas zhig gis mgon po drug cu pa'i gtor bzlog mdzad pa na/ kye bos so'i bskul tshugs pa'i tshe phyag g.yog las dag pa gnyis kyi mthong snang la/
byas 'gyur gyi bla brang nub kyi nam mkhar mi nag dung long can gnyis gros byed pa'i tshul gyis/ nged rang tsho thog mar rin spungs la phyin/ de nas lha sa rdzong la phyin
pa drag pa 'dug zer ba mngon sum du mthong zhing / gzhan yang dur khrod bdag po dang / las mkhan pu tra chen po rnams kyang yang yang zhal gzigs zhing / mdor na sa skya
pa'i bstan srung thams cad bran bzhin du 'khol nus pa'i stobs kyis bstan dgra thams cad gtan rlag tu song ba kun gyis mngon sum du mthong ba 'di yin la/ gzhan yang bdag
nyid chen po 'di nyid kyis yi dam gyi lha'i gzungs sngags bye bsnyen mdzad pa'i rim pa yang kI la ya/ gshed dmar/ mahA kA la/ a ma ra Ni/ 'jigs byed/ oM gsum/ ma Ni/ a ra
pa tsa na/ khyung khra ste 'di rnams la gsung bzlas bye ba mthar phyin pa mdzad par nges te/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi phyag dreg 'byar ba'i deb chung zhig las sngags 'di
rnams la aM gi sogs rtags mang du mdzad nas/ gdan thog gcig tu

ma yin kyang rim pas rgyun 'thud de mthar so so la bye bsnyen song bar gsal bar gsung 'dug pas so/ /de ltar sngags 'chang bla ma 'dis yi dam zhi khro rab 'byams dang chos skyong
srung ma rnams kyi grangs dang mtshan ma'i bsnyen pa mthar phyin mang po mdzad par rten yi dam dang bstan srung dbang po rnams kyi zhal bstan nas byin gyis brlabs shing
bar chad sel ba'i tshul rags rim gong du bstan pa bzhin dang / der yang ma zad bdag nyid chen po 'di ni sngon gyi bag chags bzang po sad pa'i stobs kyis gzhon nu nyid
nas yi dam gyi lhas zhal gzigs shing rjes su bstan pa nos pa zhig yin te/ de yang bdag nyid chen po 'di sku na phra mo'i skabs 'khor 'ga' zhig dang bcas rtse gdong bla
brang du sku rtse zhing bzhugs pa na/ gtsang phung po ri'i yas stong thams cad spyan ras gzigs zhal gcig phyag bzhi pa'i skus go mtshams med par bltams pa dang / mas stong
thams cad spyan ras gzigs phyag stong spyan stong gi sku shin tu che ba dag gis khyab nas 'dug cing / phung po ri bo che'i rtser thar pa'i skas yin zer ba'i skas shin tu
ring ba zhig skya thal le 'dug pa dang / de'i 'gram na rdzing bu shin tu yid du 'ong ba zhig kyang 'dug cing / de nas pha tshad na srid pa'i tsha chu yin zer ba'i chu chen
po skya nyog ge ba zhig gi 'gram na thal tshan gyi chu bo rab med yin zer ba'i thang chen po go thal bkram pa 'dra ba zhig dang / de'i 'khris na ne'u gsing sngo tal pa
zhig 'dug pa spu gris gtams pa'i thang yin la/ de'i 'gram na mi mang po zhig nag phung phung 'dug pa

la/ sngags 'chang nyid kyis mi de rnams phal cher pha rol du bde bar sgrol bar mdzad nas/ de nas rdzing bu de la sku khrus shig mdzad nas/ ri rtse'i skas de la 'dzegs byon
pa na bde ba can yin zer ba'i zhing khams kyi bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa lta bas chog mi shes pa zhig na/ rje btsun gong ma lnga sogs bla ma brgyud pa mang po dang / sangs
rgyas byang sems kha ba bu yug 'tshub pa tsam bzhugs 'dug pa las/ gdams pa dang rjes su bstan pa mang du nos pa'i dag pa'i gzigs snang ngo mtshar can de bzhin byung ba
zhabs drung na gnas pa rnams la de ma thag de'i tshul rnams sgrib med du gsungs pa dang / de dag la sogs pa mdor na ngo mtshar ba'i gzigs snang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig
mnga' ba yin mod kyang / 'dir ni che long tsam zhig brjod pa yin la/ de lta bu'i sngags 'chang bla ma ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen zhes yongs su grags pa de nyid dgung lo
nyi shu rtsa bgrang tsam du phebs nas bzung ste/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' bzhin gdan sa 'di nyid la 'dzin skyong spel gsum gyi sgo nas bstan pa'i me ro gso ba'i
thugs 'dun lhag par yod kyang / der skabs bdud kyi gnas mal snying la bcas pa'i sde pa lha khang pa/ lha sa rdzong pa/ skyed 'phrang pa rnams kyi ngan shed grwa bsgrigs
la brten/ bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes bzhugs pa'i dra sgo la yang khong gsum gyi thel se gsum 'byar byed pa sogs lugs gnyis ka dang mi mthun pa'i srol ngan gyi rgyun ci yang
zhig yod pa la/ sngags 'chang bla ma 'di nyid kyi zhabs tog rin spungs pa dpon blon gyis mdzad

de/ sde pa lha khang pa phyogs gzhan du brdzangs te/ lha khang chen mo phyag tu phul zhing / de nas bdag nyid chen po 'di byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong du thugs dam la rtse
gcig tu bzhugs yod pa'i skabs der/ dbus phyogs kyi sa skyong chen po rnams kyi dad pas spyan 'dren gyi pho nya mngags pa la brten/ dbus phyogs su phebs nas 'gro ba mang
po smin grol la bkod cing / lhag par bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i gnas mchog tu phebs te/ der bsam yas chos skyong chen pos dpe har lha'i pho brang chen po'i lcog tu sngags
'chang nyid gdan drangs te/ lcog gi sgo dmar gyi mdun du bdag nyid chen po la bzhugs gdan stag lpags grwa sder ma nyams pa zhig dang / chos skyong rang la khri'u shing
rnams bshams nas 'dug pa la/ bdag nyid chen pos chos skyong gi khri'u shing de la rje rang gi bzhugs khri yin snyam sku khyel mdzad bzhugs pa na/ bdag nyid chen po'i
sku zil gyis lha mi thams cad kyis gang yang zhu ma nus pa'i tshe/ chos skyong gis ral gri sa la btsugs nas khyel byas pas ral gri zhal ba la 'dred nas chos skyong gan rgyal
du 'gyel ba na/ bsam yas pa rnams kyis sa skya bdag chen gyis chos skyong gi bzhugs khri 'phrogs/ sdigs mdzub mdzad nas chos skyong gan rgyal du sgyel zer ba'i gtam 'brug
ltar sgrogs pa byung bar grags shing / phyis su sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las kyang / dus der de bzhin gyi gnas tshul byung ba cis kyang bden/ khri'u shing nga la
bshams pa yin snyam pa ma gtogs rtog pa gang yang ma shar ba yin

cing / lag pas sdigs mdzub rang byas pa med kyang / pus mo g.yon pa'i steng du lag pa g.yon pa'i mdzub mo ker byas pa'i steng ka zhig byung nyen 'dug ces kyang gsungs zhes
thos la de nas lha mi thams cad kyis zhabs tog bsnyen bkur sogs phun tshogs pa bsgrubs shing / bsam yas lhun gyis grub pa'i chos dang 'jig rten gyi mgon dam pa mdzad par
gsol ba btab ste/ bdag nyid chen pos kyang so so'i bsam pa dang mthun par lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas 'dzin skyong spel gsum dar rgyas su mdzad pa yin no zhes thos shing / de
nas gong dkar sogs su yang bstan pa'i bya ba rgya cher mdzad cing rim gyis gdan sa cher por phebs te/ re zhig nas shab dge sdings su phebs nas sku mtshams bcad rgya dam par
mdzad nas bzhugs pa'i skabs/ dam nyams lha sa rdzong pa dang / gnas pa mgo skya ba gnyis kyi ngan gros kyis/ gnas pas sngags 'chang chen po nyid bkrongs pa byas/ lha sa
pa'i lha khang chen mo bslu bar byas pa la/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi mthu stobs kyis ngan pa de dag gi bsam sbyor ngan pa thog tu ma khel bar lha khang chen mo nyin gcig
gi bslus snga bar byung ste/ sku tshab mdo sngags rab 'byams pa kun dga' tshe brtan bkrong ba dang / 'phan nag mi khur gcig dang / chos dung dkar po rgyang grags kyang khyer
ba sogs/ mdor na bstan pa la gnod pa'i zhabs 'dren dpag tu med pa bsgrubs pa na/ chos dung gi nang 'bus gang ba/ mtshan mo rang skad 'don pa dang / 'phan nag kyang nam
gung sgra dang bcas gdan sa chen po phyogs su 'gro ba sogs rtsub

'gyur sna tshogs byung bar grags shing / dus de nyid kyi tshe sngags 'chang bla ma 'di'i thugs dgongs la/ bod kyi sems can gyi bde skyid kyi rtsa ba dpal sa skya'i sde bstan
pa 'di dar rgyas shig byung na snyam pa yin yang / da dus snyigs pas ngan rgyab byed pa'i bdud sprul stobs ches pa nas/ bstan pa dar rgyas su yong ba dka' ba 'dug pas/
rang nyid kun spangs kyi spyod pas tshe gcig lus gcig la 'tshang rgya ba'i sgrub pa zhig byas na dga' ba 'dug snyam du dgongs nas byang se mo dor phebs par brtsams pa na/
sa skya pa la dad gus che ba'i dgon so so'i bla ma slob dpon rnams kyis kyang bshol 'debs zhus/ khyad par byang nas chos rgyal nam mkha' tshe dbang rdo rje dang / shar kha
sde srid nam mkha' lhun grub pa gnyis kyis bdud sprul lha sa rdzong pa sel 'don byas/ gdan sa chen po chos gzhis dang bcas pa thams cad phyag tu 'bul thub pa'i phyag rtags
phul nas/ chos rgyal gnyis kyis sngags 'chang nyid kyi na bza' la 'jus te spyan chab mang du bsil zhing bshol 'debs drag tu zhus pas/ bdag nyid chen pos sngar bzhin
bstan pa'i 'dzin skyong mdzad par zhal gyis bzhes mod kyang / re zhig dbus phyogs la brdzus stabs kyis phebs nas nA lendra dang / byang rwa sgreng sogs su 'gro ba mang po
smin grol la 'god bzhin pa'i skabs der/ chos kyi rgyal po byang pa dang / rgyal rtse ba gnyis kyi spyan 'dren gyi mi sna slebs pa na/ bdag nyid chen po 'di'i thugs dgongs
la/ sa skya pa'i gong ma lnga dang / sa lo chen po rnams kyi thugs rje

dang / chos skyong rnams kyi mthu rtsal la brten/ da ni sde bstan pa la zhabs tog 'grub pa 'dug snyam du dgongs nas thugs dges pa chen po'i ngang nas/ rgyab brten rdo rje sems
dpa' khyed rang la byas/ /mthu dang nus pa rnal 'byor ljags la tshang / /bdud dang mu stegs btul nas rgyun la ring po song / /da yang ye shes mtsho rgyal dran nas dga'
nas 'ong ngo lags/ /zhes pa'i lam mgur yang mdzad cing gtsang phyogs la chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur te gdan sa chen por phebs nas/ chos rgyal chen po g.yas ru byang pa/ rgyal
rtse ba/ rin spungs pa gsum gyi gdan sa chen po'i mchod gzhis rnying khung gang yod kyi steng du/ lha sa gzhung la gtogs pa rnams dang / mang mkhar gzhung dang / shab
smad du gtogs pa phal che ba rnams/ phu gsum mnga' zhabs su gtogs pa sogs shin tu rgya che ba'i mchod gzhis rnams kyang phyag tu phul nas/ de tsam nas gdan sa chen po 'phel
zhing rgyas pa'i dbu tshugs pa yin la/ de nas sngags 'chang nyid dgung lo sum cu so bgrang tsam du phebs pa nas bzung ste/ gdan sa chen po'i gtsug lag khang rnams kyi
nyams gso dang / gsar bzhengs rnams rim pas mdzad pa gnang ste/ de yang gsar bzhengs ji ltar mdzad pa'i rnam grangs kyang chu mig rdzing khar bde mchog pho brang zhes bya
ba rten gyi gtso bo sa skya pa yab sras gsum dang / sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa rnams la bde mchog bla ma brgyud pas bskor ba'i sku brnyan ngo mtshar can mang du bzhugs pa'i
gtsug lag khang la lcags ris bskor ba'i klu sdings me tog

dang / ljon shing gi rwa bas bskor ba'i rten dang brten par bcas pa 'di nyid gsar du bzhengs shing / yang dus mchod bla brang du grags pa 'di yang gsar bzhengs lta bur mdzad
de/ lhag par gtsug lag khang der bzhugs pa'i 'phags pa'i 'bul thog ma dang / bdag nyid chen po'i sku gnyis ma gtogs gzhan ma rten gtso bdag nyid chen po sa paN gyi sku
brnyan la dus mchod bla brang pa'i gdung rabs rnams kyis bskor ba ngo mtshar can 'di rnams dang / gzhan yang sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku brnyan gnyis dang mkhas pa'i
dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub kyi sku 'dra rnams la lam 'bras brgyud pas bskor ba bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag khang gzhi thog gser khang du grags pa rten dang brten par bcas pa
'di nyid dang / gzhan yang nang so pu tra khang du grags pa 'di nyid kyang gsar bzhengs lta bur mdzad cing / de dag gi lho phyogs sprul pa'i gtsug lag khang lha khang chen
mo'i yang steng du bla ma sa skya pa chen po la lam 'bras brgyud pas bskor ba'i sku brnyan ngo mtshar can blta bas chog mi shes pa 'ba' zhig bzhugs pa'i gtsug lag khang
de nyid dang / de 'og rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po yum chen e ka dza TI/ 'dod khams dbang phyug ma/ zhing skyong chen po bram gzugs/ las mkhan lnga dang bcas
pa bzhugs pa'i mgon khang khyad par du 'phags pa 'di nyid kyang gsar bzhengs mdzad pa yin la/ 'di nyid zhal bkod gnang ba'i tshe/ gong dkar ba sprul sku sbyin pa rnam rgyal
gyis lha khang chen mo'i thigs khang du gur phub nas/ mgon po'i

spen 'dzugs dang ru shing la 'jim pa phal cher g.yogs grub mtshams/ glo bur du rlung dmar chen po zhig langs te/ gur bsgyel zhing las bya byed dang bral bar gyur pa'i tshe/
lha bzo bas sngags 'chang nyid la de'i tshul rnams zhus pa na/ bdag nyid chen po thugs 'ur nyams dang bcas 'phral du phebs te/ gzims chung gi mdo'i g.yabs steng nas dkar
gong zhig bsnams nas/ mgon po'i skya bzo phal cher grub pa de la bsnun pa gnang song bas/ skya bzo'i sku'i nu ma g.yas pa'i 'og tsam du thim song zhing / de mthun gsung
las/ nga sa skya'i sde gog po 'di 'dzin pa dang / gtsug lag khang khyad par can 'di dam nyams tsho'i lag tu mi 'khyar bar bya ba'i phyir mgon khang zhig bzhengs bsams pa
la/ nag bgrad khyod gtor ma bza' yin sdod pa ma gtogs rlung po 'di tsam srung ba'i nus pa yang med pa a yin/ zhes gsung shugs chen po dang bcas gnang ba na/ de ma thag rlung
dmar thams cad rang zhir gyur cing / dus de nas bzung mgon khang nam grub kyi bar la rtsub 'gyur gyi rnam pa cung zad kyang ma byung ba yin no zhes kyang thos so/ /de
lta bu'i sngags 'chang bla ma des gzhan yang sa skya pa chen po la 'jam dbyangs dang mi g.yo ba sgrol ma rnams zhal gzigs pa'i gnas sa chen phug tu grags pa dang / sa chen
gyi dngos slob phag mo grub pa'i gsung ngag gsan nas sgrub pa mdzad pa'i gnas phag mo phug tu grags pa gnyis su yang gtsug lag khang khyad par can so so'i nang du rnam
thar dang mthun pa'i sa 'jam dang / sa chen phag gru rnams kyi sku 'dra yid du 'ong

ba dang bcas pa 'di yang legs par bzhengs te/ 'di dus bdag nyid chen po dam tshig can gyi 'khor nyung shas shig dang bcas bzhugs pa'i tshe/ rje'i gsung las/ sngon gyi dus su
bzhugs khri 'di'i steng nas brtse ba chen po kun dga' snying pos zab chos mang du gsungs shing / slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo bzhugs khri'i g.yas phyogs pha gi der bzhugs/
zhu yas sdod sa sgo 'gram 'di kha yin/ de dus nged rang rgya bo nyis phrag can zhig yin kyang / da lta ni sngags pa rgan po zhig tu 'dug ces rje nyid rje btsun chen po
yin pa zhal gyis bzhes pa sogs ngo mtshar gyi bka' mang du stsal zhing / gzhan yang sngon rdo rje phug pa'i nye logs 'di na sa chen dgung lo bcu gnyis pa'i zhabs rjes shig
yod nges yin kyang / bar skabs sus kyang rtsad ma chod pa zhig byung 'dug pas/ rang re rnams 'tshol ba yin no zhes gsungs pa'i tshe/ gzhan rnams kyis yun ring po btsal
kyang ma rnyed pa la/ sngags 'chang nyid kyis gter ston pa lta bu'i zhabs rjes yod pa'i rdo de phyag tu byung ba na/ rten 'brel bzang gsungs nas dbu thog tu 'jog pa mdzad
cing / sku khrus gsol nas da lta sgo 'gram na bzhugs pa 'di nyid yin la/ de ltar bdag nyid chen po 'dis ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas bris 'bur gyi sku gzhan yang
gsar bzhengs mdzad pa ni/ dbu rtse rnying mar sa skya pa chen po'i sku thog tshad ma/ lha khang bla brang du gong ma lnga/ bla ma dam pa/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa rnams
kyi sku brnyan re re dang / kha'u brang rdzong gi 'du khang na lam zab brgyud

pa/ yang gnas de'i sa chen/ bsod rtse/ 'gro mgon phyag na/ kha'u pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan rnams kyi phug pa so so na yang bla ma so so'i sku 'dra yid du 'ong ba re re sogs
mdor na sngags 'chang nyid kyis gsar du bzhengs pa'i 'bur sku bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gis kha'u skyed lhas dang gdan sa chen po'i gtsug lag khang phal cher ma khyab pa
med pa lta bu zhig bzhugs shing / gzhan yang rigs 'dzin brgyud pa/ bde mchog lam 'bras/ mgon po rnams kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i bris thang mang po dang / sa lo chen po'i rnam
thar thang kha/ yang phur gnyis/ bde kye gsang gsum/ gur zhal gtso bor gyur pa'i sngags thang grabs gcig sogs bris thang che chung bgrang ba las 'das pa zhig gsar du bzhengs
pa mdzad cing / yang gtsug lag khang nyams gso mdzad pa'i rnam grangs ni/ sgo rum gzigs spyil dkar po'i mgon khang mdo phug dpe khang chen mo/ bla ma lha khang / dbu
rtse rnying ma/ 'khon sku 'bum/ g.yu thog 'bum thang / gzhi thog mgon khang / zur khang / rdzong chung / nyi lde/ dge 'phel/ sgrol ma/ bsam gling / lha khang bla brang
/ lha khang chen mo/ mgon khang nub/ rin bzang sku 'bum/ shAka bzang / sgang dkar/ gzhon dbang rnams dang / gzhan yang skyed lhas mgon khang / 'du khang / sa chen phug rtse
mo phug 'phags pa phug phyag na phug pa la sogs pa mdor na gtsug lag khang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig la nyams gso gsar bzhengs dang 'dra ba mdzad cing / gzhan yang gtsug
lag khang dang rten

gsum sogs ngo mtshar yid du 'ong ba ji snyed cig yod pa de dag la yang so so'i drung du ting bdun tshar/ rdo rje dril bu/ rol mo/ sa rgyan/ gnam rgyan/ snyan dar sogs so so
skye bo'i blos dpag par dka' ba zhig 'bul bar mdzad ces yongs su grags shing kun gyi mig gi spyod yul du gyur pa 'di dag go /gzhan yang ngo mtshar bkod pa rmad du byung
zhing yid 'phrog pa'i khang bzang yang lhun grub pho brang sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gsar du 'debs par mdzad cing / de ltar gtsug lag khang gsar bzhengs dang / sngar
yod rnams nyams pa gso ba mdzad pa'i skabs der spyir ngo mtshar gyi mdzad pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dang / khyad par 'bum thang chen mo'i zhig gsos kyi skabs/ nyin
gcig gi tshe/ las mi mang po tsha ba byed skabs spyi khang gi 'gram bcag chen po zhig yod pa glo bur du zhig nas thams cad ci bya gtol med du gyur pa'i tshe/ sngags 'chang
nyid kyi thugs rjes las mi rnams la sa rdo gang gis kyang gnod pa ma byung zhing / de'i rjes su bdag nyid chen po gzigs rtog la phebs pa na/ sa rdo'i gseb na shing leb
gcig la yi ge dbu can khral le ba gsal po rang min pa zhig brkos nas 'dug pa la khrus gsol nas yi ge de nyid bklags pa na/ da lta'i zug rgyab pa 'di ni mahA kA la'o zer ba
'dug pa/ de'i tshul bdag nyid chen po la zhus pas/ he he de nga la zer ba yin pa 'dra zhes gsungs par grags pa dang / gzhan yang sgo rum la nyams gso mdzad skabs kyang
bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes sngags 'chang

nyid kyi drung du phebs pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig byung bar grags so/ /de ltar sngags 'chang bla ma 'dis rten gsum gtsug lag khang dang
bcas pa'i nyams gso dang gsar bzhengs sogs bstan pa'i bya ba rlabs po che du ma mdzad nas/ slar yang sa lo chen po'i bka' chem dang / bstan pa'i rtsa ba dge 'dun gyi sde
la rag las par dgongs nas/ bstan pa'i bya ba thos bsam sgom gsum dang / mkhas pa'i bya ba 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi sgo nas bstan pa rin po che spyi dang bye brag dpal ldan
sa skya pa'i mdo phyogs kyi bstan pa yar ngo'i zla ba ltar 'phel rgyas su 'gyur ba'i gzhi chos grwa chen po thub bstan lha chen zhes snyan pa'i gdugs dkar srid rtse'i
bar du khyab pa'i chos kyi grwa chen po de nyid 'debs par mdzad cing / der bzhugs kyi dge 'dun tshogs pa rnams kyis legs par gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba nas 'byung pa bzhin
gyi spang blang rnams g.yel med du bya dgos tshul dang / chos spyod kyi rim pa sogs ji ltar bya ba'i rnam gzhag ston pa/ mdo rgyud bstan bcos thams cad kyi snying po phyogs
gcig tu bsgrigs pa lta bu'i bca' yig ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba zhig kyang mdzad de/ /de la brten nas lung rigs kyis thugs rgyud phyug pa'i bstan 'dzin bgrang ba las
'das pa zhig byon nas/ spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal bar mdzad pa ni rnam thar rnams kyi nang nas kyang mchog tu shes par bya'o/ /de nas de'i rjes tsam
nas gsang sngags bde chen gling bya ba/ spyir rgyud sde mtha' dag dang / khyad par rje btsun sa skya pa'i

yab chos yang phur gnyis dang / bde kye gsang gsum/ yo ga bya spyod dang bcas pa'i cho ga cha lag dang bcas pa dang / chos skyong gi bskang bzlog gar 'chams/ gdangs dbyangs/
rol mo sogs phyag len phra mo tshun chad kyang ma nyams pa mdzad pa'i sgo nas rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa gong 'phel du mdzad pa'i gzhi dam pa gdan sa dan gyi phyogs su
sngags kyi chos grwa chen po 'di nyid legs par 'debs par mdzad nas dpal ldan sa skya'i sngags phyogs kyi bstan pa gsal bar mdzad pa 'di ni/ bla ma gong ma ye shes kyi spyan
ldan du ma'i thugs dgongs rdzogs byed kyi thabs kyi gtso bo lta bur gyur pa yin te/ rje rdo rje 'chang dag pa'i zhing du gshegs kha'i gsung las/ da 'gro na'ang sems kyi
'khri ba sa skya'i dan stod de la chos khrims gtsang ma cig byung na snyam rtsol ba cher byas pa yin te/ de'i spros pa ni chod 'dug gzhan sems kyi lhag ma cung zad kyang
med ces gsungs pa dang / bdag chen rdo rje 'chang blo gros rgyal mtshan gyi gsung las kyang / nged rang gi bsam pa bzhin byung na sa skya'i skyed 'phrang yan la lam 'bras
sogs sa skya pa'i sngags phyogs kyi chos grwa bzang po zhig ci la thug kyang tshugs par byed snyam pa yod pas/ de dag gi mgo ma la khyed bzhugs dgos zhes paN chen nyi
zla seng ge la gsung bar grags pa sogs bla ma gong ma du ma'i thugs kyi lhag mar lus pa 'di nyid/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis ji lta ba bzhin bde blag tu 'grub par mdzad pa ni
shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i gnas so/ /de ltar gdan sa chen po 'di nyid du mdo

sngags kyi chos grwa ngo mtshar can 'di dag dang / gzhan yang me 'bar gyi gtsug lag khang brgyad kyi nang nas mchog tu gyur pa kha'u skyed lhas bya ba'i sgrub gnas 'di nyid
dang / byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong gnyis kyang nyams gso gsar bzhengs lta bu mdzad cing / rje sa skya pa chen po 'khrungs pa'i gnas phru ma zhes grags par yang shin
tu ngo mtshar ba'i sgrub sde gsar du bzhengs pa 'di nyid dang / shab dge sdings bkra shis bsam 'grub tu 'dra 'dri chos rdzong khams gsum zil gnon zhes bya ba'i sngags dgon
de nyid dang / bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang chen po de nyid du bsam yas rab byung gi sde chen po la sogs pa/ mdor na bdag nyid chen po 'dis mdo
grwa dang sngags grwa sgrub sde sogs dgon che chung du ma zhig gis dbus gtsang gi sa'i cha ma lus pa khyab pa lta bu zhig gsar 'debs mdzad de/ /de dag gi cha rkyen bsnyen
bkur sogs rgya chen po bsgrub pa'i rgyun 'dzugs par mdzad pa 'di ni bdag nyid chen po 'di la/ gangs can khrod kyi bstan 'dzin chen por rlom pa phal cher gyis 'gran zla
dang bral ba'i rnam par thar pa yin no/ /de ltar bdag nyid chen po 'dis mdo sngags kyi chos grwa chen po de dag legs par 'debs par mdzad nas/ de nas bzung nas bla ma gong
ma rnams kyi dus mchod rnams la bde kye gsang gsum/ yang phur gnyis/ gshed dmar/ gur rigs bsdus/ sampu Ta/ kun rig sogs rgyud sde bzhi dang 'brel ba'i dkyil 'khor mang
po'i sgrub mchod dang / rgyud sde zab mo rnams zhal 'don gyi rim pa sogs gsar du 'dzugs

par mdzad nas/ de dag la bsnyen bkur zhabs tog phun sum tshogs pa bsgrub pa sogs mdor na phyag rdzas kyi dngos po ci byung ba thams cad kyang dkon mchog gi zhabs tog kho na
ma gtogs rang don du til 'bru tsam yang mi 'dzin par skye bo mkhas blun thams cad la yongs su grags pa yin cing / gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis mkhas pa'i bya ba rnam
gsum gyi nang nas dngos dang brgyud pa'i gdul bya rnams kyi don du legs bshad kyi tshogs gsar du mdzad pa yang / /sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa/ rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan
snga ngag dbang chos grags rnams kyi bstod pa sogs bstod pa dang gsol 'debs kyi skor mang po dang / bde mchog gsang 'dus/ phur pa sa lugs kyi dkyil chog sogs dkyil chog
du ma dang / bde kye gsang gsum kun rig sogs kyi dbang chog sogs las dang po la mkho zhing / rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa 'grel nges pa'i dbang chog mang po
zhig dang / gzhan yang gsang 'dus dang nA ro mkha' spyod kyi sgrub thabs la sogs pa sgrub thabs kyi rigs mang po zhig dang / khrid yig dang dka' ba'i gnad kyi dris lan gdams
pa dang / springs yig gi skor la sogs pa mdor na kho bo cag gis dpe dang lung rgyun 'tshol ba'i phyir 'bad pa chen pos dus phyis phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i sngags 'chang
nyid kyi bka' 'bum po ti gsum bzhugs pa so so'i dkar chag nang bzhin gyi sngon med pa'i legs bshad bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad pa rnams kyis kyang bstan pa rin po che
ches cher

gsal bar gyur pa lags so/ /de lta bu'i sngags 'chang bla ma bdag nyid chen po des gdan sa chen po'i 'dzin skyong spel gsum rnams dang / dad ldan gyi gdul bya rnams la chos
kyi 'khor lo bskor ba/ skabs 'gar dben gnas rnams su thugs dam zab mo'i rim pa la rtse gcig tu bzhugs pa sogs chos dang mthun pa'i mdzad 'phrin kho na'i ring nas bstan pa'i
rtsa ba gdung sras rgyun ma chad par byon pa nyid yin par dgongs pa'i rgyu dang / bdag nyid chen po'i rigs kyi cod pan dam pa rje dkon mchog lhun grub/ spyan snga ngag
dbang chos grags/ rgyal sras dpal ldan bkra shis/ rje btsun kun dga' grol mchog rnams gtso bor gyur pa'i rje btsun sa skya pa'i bstan pa thugs khongs su bcangs pa'i bla
ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen mang po dang / dbus gtsang gi skyong ba sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i sbyin bdag chen po rnams kyis gdung rigs spel ba mdzad dgos pa'i gsol ba drag tu btab
pa'i rkyen la brten/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis btsun mo gsum tsam zhig khab tu bzhes nas/ rigs kyi gdung sras dam pa gcen 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang po grags pa rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba po de nyid dang / gcung sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba byang chub
sems dpa' chen po zhi ba 'tsho'i rnam par sprul pa de nyid de gdung sras dam pa sku mched gnyis bskrun par mdzad cing / de nas rigs sras dam pa de gnyis la bdag nyid chen
po rang la ji ltar bzhugs pa'i zab chos rnams kyang legs par stsol bar

mdzad pa yin la/ de dag gi skabs shig nas bsam yas kyi sa skyong chen po tshe dbang rdo rje zhing gzhan du gshegs pa la brten/ de'i gshegs rdzong la bdag nyid chen po spyan
'dren gyi pho nya mngags pa na/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis kyang chos rgyal chen po de la thugs brtse bas phebs par zhal gyis bzhes pa gnang nas/ de mthun gdung sras 'jam pa'i
dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can nyid kyang / lo nas spyan snga rin po che'i drung du rab tu byung bar bzhed de/ yab sras lhan cig tu dbus phyogs la chibs kha bsgyur nas
snar thang / ngor e waM chos ldan/ gzhis dga' bsam 'grub rtse/ rin spungs/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan/ bde mchog srin po ri rnams su mar lam phebs nas/ de dag tu gnas pa'i skya
ser rnams la zab rgyas dam pa'i chos kyi bka' drin gzhal du med pa stsal te/ rim gyis bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang chen por phebs nas/ chos rgyal
tshe dbang rdo rje pa'i dgong rdzogs kyi tshogs dbus dang lam ston sogs mdzad skabs/ chos skyong chen po'i lcog lha'i pho brang du bdag nyid chen po spyan drangs te/
chos skyong chen pos sngon slob dpon padma'i zab yangs mthil 'di la sa chog dang rab gnas mdzad pa bzhin/ sa skya pa chen pos kyang gtsug lag khang dang mchod rten rnams
la rab gnas mdzad na bod khams kyi bde skyid la phan pa yod ces zhus pa na/ bdag nyid chen pos kyang yab sras lhan cig tu rdo rje phur pa'i sa chog dang de la brten pa'i
rab gnas rgyas par mdzad de/ de'i dus su tshogs tha ma dgra

bgegs grub kyi 'chams kyi tshe/ skabs shig sngags 'chang nyid kyi drung du chos skyong byon nas/ sa skya pa chen po dang po slob dpon padmas kyang nged zab yangs mthil gyi
lha srin sde brgyad thams cad dam 'og tu bcug bka' nan drag pos bsam yas kyi srung mar bskos pa yin/ de bzhin sa skya pa chen pos kyang nged lha srin sde brgyad la drag po'i
las kyi gnod pa med par so sor sngar bzhin rang gnas su 'jog pa mdzad dgos/ nged lha srin sde brgyad rnams kyis kyang sngon slob dpon rin po che padma'i bka' bzhin dang
/ da lam yang sa skya pa chen pos bka' ji ltar bsgos pa ltar bsgrub cing dam 'og tu 'jug pa byed zer te/ da lta sde brgyad thams cad dbu rtse'i khyams ra chen mo na 'dus
'dug nas gdug 'dre la/ dges bshes su 'phrin skyol zer bar 'dug pas/ sa skya pa chen pos kyang de bzhin du dgongs dgos/ zhes chos skyong chen pos lan gnyis zhus pa na/
rjes ma'i skabs su bdag nyid chen pos chos skyong chen po la spyan cher gzigs nas cang mi gsung bar zhal 'dzum pa zhig mdzad pa na/ chos skyong chen po nyid dges pa chen
po'i ngang nas dbu rtse chen mo'i khyams rar phebs nas sde brgyad rnams kyi ming nas 'bod cing / gdug 'dres dges bshes la 'phrin bskyal ba 'di la khyed zab yangs mthil gyi
sde brgyad thams cad kyi byas pa gzo ba gyis zhes gsung bar grags shing / de nas yang lan cig bdag nyid chen po yab sras gnyis kyi drung du chos skyong chen po glo bur
nyid du byon byung nas maNDal so bdun ma bkod nas/ bsam yas pa'i zhal ngo rnams kyang

bsdus/ lcog pa rnams la maNDal phul zhig par bka' gnang nas/ chos skyong rang gis kyang bse rmog phud cing / ral gri dang zhags pa yang der bzhag nas/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi
drung du thal mo sbyar te sa skya pa chen pos nged zab yangs mthil gyi lha mi 'dir tshogs rnams la bla ma'i rnal 'byor gyi byin rlabs shig gnang ba dgos zhu ba la/ bdag
nyid chen pos kyang thugs dges bzhin du lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor rgyas pa stsal ba'i tshe/ de ma grol gyi bar la bdag nyid chen po'i g.yon phyogs kyi sa dang bar snang
thams cad la sngon slob dpon padmas dam btags kyi gnas kha so so'i srung ma rnams dang / gzhan yang gzugs med kyi rigs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig 'dus nas/ sngags 'chang
nyid la gus 'dud dang bcas 'dug pa mkhan tshang pa bstan pa dar rgyas kyis mngon sum du mthong zhing / de dang dus mnyam du chos skyong chen pos kyang bdag nyid chen
po'i sku'i g.yon phyogs la yang yang gzigs nas brda mang du mdzad cing / phyogs der mi su yang 'gror mi 'jug pa der yod kun gyis mthong bar grags pa dang / de'i tshe bdag
nyid chen po'i gsung las kyang / de ring gi chos nyan pa rnams kyi khrod na sems can mgo lus mi gcig pa mang po 'dus nas bzhed po 'dug pa khyed tshos e mthong zhes zhabs
'bring pa rnams la gsung bar grags la/ de ltar bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang der bod kyi bde skyid la phan pa'i mdzad pa mtha' yas pa zhig mdzad
nas/ de nas lo dgon par

phebs te spyan snga rin po che ngag dbang chos grags kyi drung du thugs sras dam pa dbang po'i zhabs kyis rab tu byung ba dge tshul gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa mnos par mdzad
cing / bdag nyid chen pos kyang spyan snga rin po cher zab chos 'ga' zhig gsan te/ de nas yab sras lhan cig tu lha sar phebs nas der bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa'i
smon lam rgya chen po dang / khyad par jo bo rang byon lnga ldan bcu gcig zhal de nyid la dad ldan rnams kyis gser chab gsol ba stobs ches pa'i zhal dkyil gas pa lta bu'i
