shin tu ma mdzes pa zhig dang / sku de nyid cung zad mdun du bub nas 'dug pa la/ bdag nyid chen pos thabs la mkhas pa'i sgo nas snga mo ltar jo bo'i zhal dkyil shin tu
yid du 'ong ba mdzad cing / mdun du bub pa'i rnam pa yod pa de la yang bdag nyid chen po'i phyag gis sku rgyab tu 'phul ba'i steng ka tsam mdzad pa na/ sku de nyid rang
bzhengs kyi tshul gyis shin tu 'drongs pa byung zhes yongs su grags pa dang / skabs der bdag nyid chen po yab sras rnams skyid shod pas gdan drangs te/ gzhis dga' bde chen
du phebs pa'i skabs su gter ston zhig po gling pa dang mjal nas/ de las bdag nyid chen pos gter chos mang du gsan cing / gzhan la yang rgya cher spel bar mdzad bzhin pa'i
tshe/ bsam yas nas chos skyong chen po sogs lha mi rnams kyis gdan 'dren gyi pho nya mngags pa na slar yang bsam yas su phebs nas/ der chos skyong chen pos/ bdag nyid
chen po rang nyid kyi gcen bdag chen kun dga' bsam grub pa gnyis char gyis bsam

yas kyi gtsug lag khang sogs la rab gnas dang slob dpon la gsol ba btab na bstan 'gro la phan pa rgya chen po 'byung bas de bzhin mdzad dgos tshul zhus pa bzhin/ de 'phral
rtse gdong bdag smyon stag lung nas spyan 'dren par mdzad de/ bdag nyid chen po sku mched khu dbon rnams kyis bsam yas kyi gtsug lag khang dang mchod rten rnams kyi zhig
gsos dang rab gnas rgyas pa mdzad cing / de nas rje btsun gcen gyis stag lung sogs su phebs nas/ bdag nyid chen po yab sras gnyis kyis bsam yas su bzhugs te/ der gter ston
shes rab 'od zer ba dang mjal nas/ de la yang gter chos mang du gsan te/ de'i skabs su nyin gcig gi tshe sngags 'chang sprul pa'i sku nyid kyi dbu rtse chen mo'i bar khang
g.yu zhal mthil nas/ mkha' 'gro ma bde ba'i rdo rje'i dbu thod skye bdun a mas bkang ba dang / slob dpon rin po che'i tshe ril dam rdzas sogs yod pa gter nas 'don par
mdzad cing / skabs der bdag nyid chen po'i chag phyi gter ston shes rab 'od zer bas mdzad nas/ bsam yas mchod rten dkar po nas lcags kyi rdo rje rtse dgu pa zhig dang skye
bdun a ma'i thum bu zhig gter nas spyan drangs te/ de'i dus kyi lcags kyi rdo rje de nyid bdag nyid chen po'i rdo rje phur pa'i dbang bskur gyi dbang rdzas mdzad par grags
shing / bde ba'i rdo rje'i dbu thod de nyid nA ro mkha' spyod sogs kyi byin rlabs mdzad dus dbang rdzas mdzad nas deng sang gi bar du gdan sa chen po nyid na bzhugs
pa 'di nyid do/ /de ltar bdag nyid chen po 'dis bsam

yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gnas mchog de nyid du yang bstan pa'i bya ba rgya chen po zhig mdzad nas/ de nas rim gyis gdan sa chen por phebs te/ sngags 'chang chos kyi
rgyal po nyid dgung lo lnga bcu'i khong tsam du phebs pa'i tshe/ gdung sras sku mched gnyis rang gi rgyal tshab dam par mnga' gsol te spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa rin
po che yar ngo'i zla ba ltar 'phel rgyas su gyur pa yin zhes kyang grags pa yin no/ /de lta'i skabs shig na yar rgyab pa'i sde pa sku 'bring zhing gzhan du gshegs pa'i dgongs
rdzogs la bdag nyid chen po gdan 'dren par byung ba na/ gdung sras sku mched gnyis kyi gcung bdag nyid chen po sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros kyis gdan sa chen po'i
'gan bzhes rnams mdzad cing / gcen 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang po bdag nyid chen po'i zhabs phyir 'brangs te yab sras gnyis kyis slar yang dbus phyogs su phebs te/
zhing gshegs de nyid kyi dgongs rdzogs ma lus pa grub nas lha sar phebs pa'i nub/ bsam yas kyi rgyal po shing bya can bya ba des sngags 'chang nyid kyi drung du lhags nas/
bsam yas dbu rtse chen mo la zhig gsos gnang dgos tshul gyi snyan 'bul du ma zhig zhu ba bzhin/ bdag nyid chen po yab sras rnams kyis kyang bsam yas su phebs pa'i tshe/
sgrags kyi mdo der sa ma sros tsam la phebs pa na/ 'jam dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can nyid la/ khri thog pa dpon slob snga bar la song la gtor ma sogs grabs grub pa gyis
la bar lam la cag gas thon dgos/ 'on kyang lam rgyus la rkang rjes gsum

yong bas/ che ba gnyis la gtad cher med/ chung ba de la gtad nas phyin pas 'khrul pa gtan nas 'ong ba med do gsung ba la/ 'jam dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can dpon slob rnams
kyis/ sa ni sros/ mun 'thibs pas rkang rjes rang yod kyang e mthong na snyam pa'i thugs the tshom cung zad kyi ngang nas phebs pas/ rgyang pa zhig nas sa sros te lam nor
sogs byung ba na/ dpon slob rnams kyis sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung dran nas gsol 'debs mdzad pas/ 'jam dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can gyis gsal po rang min pa'i
rkang rjes gsum gzigs nas/ gsol ba drag tu btab pas rkang rjes gsum gyi chung ba de shin tu gsal bar byung nas/ de'i rjes brtsad nas dpon slob rnams kyis phebs pa'i tshe
lam nor 'khrul sogs gtan ma byung bar bde bar phebs pa na/ de nas mchod g.yog pa zhig gi mthong snang la/ rdo mchod thang kha'i 'og tsam nas mi shin tu che ba gsum song
ba yang mthong bar grags shing / bdag nyid chen po dpon slob rnams la ji srid mun srub pa nas bsam yas su ma phebs bar de srid du sku mdun du me sgron chen po gsum byung
nas nyin mo las kyang gsal ba byung bar grags pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar du ma dang bcas phebs te/ yab sras mjal ba na bdag nyid chen po'i sku 'khor rnams kyis gong gi gnas
tshul de nyid 'jam dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can dpon slob rnams la zhus pa na/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ he he nged rgan po tsho la de 'dra byung / khyed tsho
la ji ltar byung

gsungs pa dang / 'jam pa'i dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can gyis bdag nyid chen po la rkang rjes sogs ji ltar byung ba'i tshul rnams dang / the tshom tsam byung ba la thugs mi
khrel ba zhu zhes zhus pa na/ bdag nyid chen pos rkang rjes de gsum khri thog pa spun rang la byas 'gyur du ngo sprod byas pa'i ming sring gsum po de ka yin/ 'on kyang rkang
rjes de gsum tsam mthong ba la ngo mtshar rgyu med/ nged lo nyi shu rtsa grangs kyi dus ding ri phyogs su phyin pa na/ rtsib ri'i byang ngos de la ltung bshags kyi sangs
rgyas so lnga po khra lam me bzhugs pa mthong zhing / de'i shar gyi phyogs na 'phags pa klu sgrub dang / sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa yin snyam pa'i paNDi ta na bza' ngur
smrig bsnams pa gnyis kyang 'dug cing / yang nged lo bcu gcig tsam gyi dus su phung po ri bo'i byang ngos la gnas brtan bcu drug po sku re re nas rnam 'gyur ya mtshan
sna tshogs mdzad pa dang bcas mthong ba yin no zhes sogs ngo mtshar gyi gsung mang du byon pa dang / de nas bsam yas dbu rtse chen mo la zhig gsos mdzad dgos tshul bsam yas
rgan dmangs la bka' stsal te las brtsams pa na/ glo bur du kha char shin tu che ba zhig byung ba'i tshe/ bdag nyid chen pos rgyal po shing bya can gnas sar phebs te/ de
nyid kyi sgo la phyag 'khar bsnun nas/ nga mi mno ba mnos su bcug da khyod la nus pa med pa e yin/ char pa 'di mi gcod dam zhes gsungs ma thag nam mkha' dwangs par grags
pa dang / de nas sngags 'chang nyid kyi thugs dgongs la chos skyong 'di sngar nas nged la gdug 'dre'i gnas sa da

lta'i 'di ma yin/ byang shar mtshams na pho brang ka gcig sgo gcig bya ba cig yod ces yang yang zer ba zhig byung bas/ de yang da lam rtsad bcad nas lcog gsar bzhengs shig
byas/ sku 'bras yang der bzhugs su gsol/ lcog rnying pa 'di la yang zhig gsos shig byas na legs pa 'dug snyam du dgongs nas/ pho brang ka gcig sgo gcig rtsad gcod par phebs
pa'i tshe/ /pho brang de nyid ni khang brtsegs du ma'i 'og na ra ba lta bu'i mun nag can zhig 'dug pas/ chos skyong chen po la pho brang ka gcig sgo gcig 'di yin nam gsungs
pa la/ chos skyong chen pos de bzhin yin tshul zhus pa na/ bdag nyid chen pos 'o na 'dir khyed rang gnas sa'i lcog cig gsar tu btab/ de mthun lcog rnying pa la yang
zhig gsos shig byed dgos 'dug pas/ sang nyin nga yang slebs yong chos skyong rang yang shog cig gsungs pas/ chos skyong gis sa skya pa chen po gdug 'dre'i gnas khang rnying
pa la zhig gsos dgos pa med zhus pa na/ bdag nyid chen pos 'o na khyod kyis khag theg gam gsungs pa dang / chos skyong gis lo gsum khag theg pa byed zhu ba la/ sngags
'chang nyid thugs 'ur ba'i tshul gyis gdug 'dre tshod med pa lo gsum nas sus 'tsho rgyu yin/ nga sang nyin nas zhig gsos kyi mgo 'dzugs thag chod yin pas/ khyed rang de
bar la gnas khang gzhan zhig tu song zhig ces gsungs pa dang / de nas chos skyong chen po 'khor bcas has po ri'i rgyab kyi thang chen po de la bskyas byas nas bzhugs pa mig
mthong mkhan rnams kyis

mthong bar grags shing / de nas chos skyong chen po snang dus kyi nyin min pa byon ma byung ba na/ sngags 'chang nyid kyis chos skyong la khyed kha rtsang mi yong ba ci yin
gsungs pa la/ chos skyong gis sa skya pa chen po de bden/ gdug 'dres byang shambha lar phyin pas khrag cig la chags nas ma slebs pa yin zhus pas/ sngags 'chang nyid thugs
'khrugs pa'i tshul gyis/ khyed slob dpon padma 'byung gnas kyis li yul lcang ra smug po nas bkug spyir bod kyi gtsug lag khang dang mchod rten bre tsam yan gyi gnyer gtad/
khyad par bsam yas kyi gtsug lag khang dang / sde bstan pa srung bar bka' bsgos pa ltar khas blangs nas/ byang shambha la ru thal ba 'gam du phyin pa yin nam zhes gsungs
pa na/ chos skyong chen po rang yang zhum pa dang bcas bdag nyid chen po'i bka' nyan cing 'dug par grags shing / de nas bdag nyid chen po'i lcog gsar rnying gnyis dang
/ slob dpon gyi phyag bzo sku 'bras chen mo la yang nyams gso mdzad de/ rab gnas dang bkra shis sogs rgyas par gnang nas/ dpal bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug
lag khang na gnas pa'i lha mi thams cad yi rang bar mdzad de bstan pa rin po ches cher gsal bar gyur ces yongs su grags pa yin no/ /de nas bdag nyid chen pos gtsang phyogs
su chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur nas rim gyis gdan sa chen por phebs pa na/ gdung sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched sogs kyis thog drangs gzhir bzhugs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen
mang po dang / phyogs nas byon pa'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen

sogs dad ldan gyi gdul bya mang rab zhig la thog mar sa skya bka' 'bum/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rin gyi bka' 'bum/ glo bo mkhan chen pa'i bka' 'bum/ sa lo chen po'i bka' 'bum/ thams
cad mkhyen pa dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum/ rje nyid kyi bka' 'bum phal cher gyi lung dang / gzhan yang rgyal sras bka' 'bum/ mus chen gyis bsgrigs pa'i blo sbyong
glegs bam yongs rdzogs/ ma Ni bka' 'bum/ bka' gdams pha chos bu chos jo bo'i chos chung brgya rtsa/ bka' gdams gzhung drug bdag chen rgya dkar bas bsgrigs pa'i mgon
pod dang / mgon pod me 'bar ma/ gser pod rnams dang / gzhan yang bde mchog rtsa rgyud/ rnal 'byor ma kun spyod/ kye rdor rgyud gsum/ gsang 'dus rtsa rgyud/ ngan song sbyong
rgyud/ bla ma dam pa'i pod nag ma/ gzhung bshad dmar ma/ sras don ma rnams kyi lung sogs mdor na lung gi rnam grangs blos dpag par dka' ba zhig dang / gzhan yang smin
byed dbang gi rnam grangs la bde kye gsang gsum gyi dbang sogs dbang bskur gyi rigs bcu phrag gnyis tsam dang / bdag med ma'i byin rlabs sogs byin rlabs zab mo'i rim pa bcu
phrag gcig dang phyed kyis lhag pa dang / rjes gnang gi bka' srol zab mo gnyis su grags pa sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang rgya mtsho'i rjes gnang yongs rdzogs dang / rjes
gnang zur bka' bcu phrag bzhi tsam la sogs pa mdor na rjes gnang zab mo'i rim pa yang bsam las 'das pa zhig dang / grol byed khrid kyi rim pa yang

gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa/ lam skor phyi ma brgyad/ nag po rim bzhi/ dril bu rim lnga'i khrid sogs khrid kyi rim pa yang bcu phrag lhag pa sogs mdor na
dbang lung man ngag sogs zab mo dam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rgya chen po bskor te/ skal ldan gyi slob ma'i tshogs kyang bsam gyi mi khyab pa zhig bskrun par mdzad pa yin
no/ /de yang bdag nyid chen po 'di'i drung du snga phyir dam pa'i chos kyi bdud rtsi gsol ba'i bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu ji ltar byon pa'i rnam grangs kyang / nyid kyi thugs
sras rgyal tshab dam pa/ 'jam mgon grub pa'i dbang phyug padma'i rnam 'phrul bsod nams dbang po grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po dang / byang chub sems dpa' bo dhi
satwa'i rnam 'phrul rgyal sras sbas pa'i rnal 'byor sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po ste gdung sras rin po che sku mched gnyis dang / rtse gdong
bdag chen kun dga' legs pa'i 'byung gnas dpal bzang po dang / mnga' ris gung thang gi chos rgyal chen po khri bsam grub sde/ mang yul rgyal brgyud mnga' bdag rgyal por
grags pa/ bsam yas rgyal po btsad po tshe dbang rdo rje sogs bod chos rgyal gyi rigs su 'khrungs pa rnams dang / gzhan yang ngor mkhan chen sangs rgyas sengge/ gling dga'
bde ba can gyi mkhan chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho/ gsang sngags bde chen gling gi mkhan chen dpal ldan bzang po/ chos grwa chen po thub bstan lha chen gyi mkhan chen paN chen
legs blo ba sogs thub bstan lha chen gyi gdan sa pa drug lhag tsam dang / 'dra 'dri chos

rdzong gi mkhan po gdan sa pa dang bcas pa/ gzhan yang ngor chen dkon mchog dpal ldan/ paN chen nam mkha' dpal bzang / shar chen kun dga' bkra shis/ thub bstan rnam rgyal gyi
mkhan chen byams pa rab brtan/ sems dpa' chen po chos 'od zer/ rje bsod nams chos 'phel/ ngam ring mkhan chen sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan dang rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/
thub bstan yangs pa can gyi mkhan chen dbang phyug dpal bzang / 'bras yul skyid tshal gyi mkhan po chos rje gung pa/ chos rje rab brtan dpal 'bar/ gzhan yang jo nang mkhan
chen rje kun dga' grol mchog chos lung tshogs pa'i mkhan po lung rigs rgya mtsho/ dge 'dun sgang pa'i mkhan po shAkya ri dbang / bye rdzing tshogs pa'i mkhan po dang /
gzhan yang byang stag lung mkhan po sku mched gnyis/ gsang phu gling smad mkhan po rin chen 'byor ldan/ bstan 'dzin ngag dbang nyi zla bzang po/ gzhan yang byas 'gyur sgrub
chen dge slong kun dga' don grub dang / kun dga' dpal mgon gnyis/ skyed lhas sgrub chen dpal ldan rdo rje/ nA lendra'i mkhan po stong ra chos rje kun dga' legs grub/ lum
pa chos rje/ lo dgon pa'i gdan sa pa 'jun pa chos rje/ gong dkar rdo rje gdan gyi slob dpon tshe dbang bkra shis/ chos sde chen po de nyid kyi dbu mdzad byang chub dbang
rgyal/ chos rje lha dbang bzang po/ chos rje glu dbang gling pa/ rje gser gling pa/ snyan brgyud gdams pa'i mnga' bdag mkhas pa'i dbang po tshar pa chos rje/ gzhan yang
rje kun dga' lung rig mnga'

ris gzhi sde mkhan po rje mkhas grub pa/ skyid tshal 'og gi mkhan po rje blo gros chos 'phags dang / rje blo gros rnam rgyal/ gser mdog can gyi mkhan po karma bzang po/ bya
rgod gshong gi mkhan po 'ga' rong pa/ gdong dga' slob dpon pa kun dga' mchog ldan/ chos 'khor lhun po'i mkhan po lha btsun grags pa/ shAkya bsam grub/ ngag dbang grags pa
rnams dang / gra thang mkhan po sde bdag chos rje khu dbon gnyis/ paN chen bde ba'i rdo rje/ bsam yas rab byung mkhan po rje gser sku ba/ gter ston zhig po gling pa/ gter
ston shes rab 'od zer/ dpal 'khor chos sde'i mkhan po 'phags pa tshul khrims pa sogs mkhas grub kyi slob ma mtshan grags dang ldan pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / gzhan
yang gdan sa chen po'i brgya dpon/ las chen sogs/ mdor na bstan pa rin po che la bya ba mdzad nus pa'i skyes bu du ma zhig byon nas/ bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa rin po
che ches cher gsal bar gyur pa ni kun gyis mngon du gyur pa 'di yin la/ de ltar 'chad pa nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis gdul bya skal ldan gyi blo gros kyi padmo ches cher bzhad
par mdzad pa'i bdag nyid chen po 'di nyid kyis phyi rol du bstan 'gro'i don rgya chen po mdzad pa'i ring nas nang du ting nge 'dzin bsam gyis mi khyab pa thugs rgyud la 'khrungs
nas grub pa'i rtags mtshan bstan pa'i tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig yod mod/ khyad par dpal gro stag tshang seng ge bsam grub tu phebs nas grub pa'i mtshan ma
brnyes pa'i tshul ni/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis slob dpon chen po padma

'byung gnas kyi sgrub gnas dpal gro stag tshang seng ge bsam grub tu lha dang bla ma'i zhal mngon du gyur te/ gdams pa dang lung bstan khyad par can dngos su nod pa'i dus la
babs par dgongs te/ lho rong phyogs su phebs par brtsams te der chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur ba na/ dpal 'gro'i gzhi bdag lha chen brag skyed dang / has kyi khyung 'dus sogs
lho kha bzhi'i gzhi bdag sogs sngags 'chang nyid kyi zhabs drung du byung nas/ lho rong gi lung pa thams cad zhabs kyis 'chag pa mdzad dgos shing / la chu 'phrang sogs kyi
'phrin las nged rang gzhi bdag rnams kyis bsgrub pa yin no zhes zhus pa dang / sngags 'chang nyid kyis kyang dus der gtor ma rgya chen po gnang zhing / bsang dpe chen
mor yang / dpal gro'i lha chen brag skyed dang / /has kyi khyung 'dus la sogs pa'i/ /lho rong lung pa'i gzhi bdag bsang / /zhes pa 'di yang de'i dus su 'jug par mdzad pa
yin no zhes thos la/ de nas bdag nyid chen pos dpal gro'i sgrub gnas dam pa der phebs par dgongs pa nas/ nags kyi 'phrang dog pa la brten chibs pa'i bgrod ma bde ba la dgongs
nas/ long ra dbon po sogs lho pa gzhon pa mang pos rgyab tu sngags 'chang nyid gdan drangs te/ stag tshang gi 'phrang zin par phebs pa'i tshe/ de'i bar lam zhig tu skye
mthing shwa na ma sogs gzhi bdag 'ga' zhig gi cho 'phrul gyis sems can ma rungs pa zhig gis lam bsgags byung ba la sngags 'chang nyid kyis nged rang rang gnas su 'gro
ba la khyod la khyad ci yod phar song gsung pa

sogs kyi sgo nas bka' bsgo mdzad pas/ sems can gyi gzugs de dngos med la yal song ba der yod kun gyis mthong zhing / de nas dpal gro'i lam 'phrang la phebs pas/ gnas de na
brag ri gzhan las ngam che ba ri gzhan las thog so dgu tsam gyis mtho ba zhig yod pa de'i mgor/ sngon mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal gyi shel phreng brgya rtsa gtor ba'i
chu mig brgya rtsa yod pa'i chu de thams cad brag de'i mdun la dar dkar gyi yol ba bkram pa ltar ngo mtshar che bar 'bab pa zhig yod pa'i brag la chu 'thab de'i dkyil du
glo bur nyid du 'ja' tshon sna lnga'i 'od zer sum sbrag cig byung nas/ de'i dbus nas 'ja' kha dog sngon po zhig rgyang gis byung ba sngags 'chang nyid kyi sku la zug cing
/ zhabs drung na gnas pa'i sku 'khor kun la yang 'ja' de'i 'od kyis khyab pa la brten/ mi'i mdog dang gos bzan sogs kyang sngon po 'ba' zhig tu gyur pa der yod kyi skye
bo kun gyis mthong ba byung zhing / de'i tshe 'phrang de'i g.yas g.yon gyi ljon shing gi tshogs la brten pa'i spra dang spre'u lag na shing gi yal ga thogs pa mang pos/ mi
la mi 'dzem par gral bsgrigs te langs nas sngags 'chang nyid la bsu ba'i tshul du 'dug pa ni/ de dus zhabs drung na 'dug pa kun gyis mthong bar grags la/ de'i tshe sngags
'chang chos kyi rgyal pos sngar gyi brag la chu 'thab nas byung ba'i 'ja' 'od rnams je gsal je gsal du song byung ba la gzigs pas/ de'i dbus 'od dkar po zhig gi khrod
na bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu'i dkyil 'khor la bka' srung dam can rgya mtsho'i tshogs kyis bskor ba

dang / de'i steng na slob dpon padma 'byung gnas gtso 'khor gsum dang / rtsa brgyud kyi bla ma grub thob rigs 'dzin mang po khrom tshogs su bzhugs pa'i mtha' skor du dpa' bo
mkha' 'gro mang pos bskor ba dang / mkha' 'gro sde lnga gar stabs shig shig 'dug pa shin tu gsal bar gzigs nas/ de'i tshe sngags 'chang nyid kyis stag tshang gi phug pa'i
g.yas 'khris na ne'u gsing 'khyil pa zhig yod pa der bzhugs nas lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor thugs nyams su bzhes pas/ sngar gyi gzigs snang la shar ba'i bla ma yi dam
rnams kyi sku las 'od zer kha dog lnga ldan nyi ma bye ba'i gzi 'od tsam dang / bla ma yi dam dpa' bo mkha' 'gro rdul 'khrigs pa lta bu byung nas sngags 'chang nyid kyi
sku la thim par gyur te/ skad cig de nyid la thugs la tha mal gyi rnam rtog gi cha shas cung zad yod pa thams cad khrig 'gags nas/ snang srid thams cad lhag pa lha'i dkyil
'khor gyi 'khor lor khra lam ste shar nas de la thugs zin te bde chen lhan cig skyes pa'i ye shes kyi ngang du lhan gyis gnas byung ba dang / de ma thag dpa' bo mkha'
'gro rigs 'dzin grub thob kyi lha tshogs thams cad 'od sngon po zhig tu gyur nas/ slob dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas la thim zhing / slob dpon yang 'od du zhu la khad 'dug
pa la gzigs pas/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi thugs dgongs la/ da ni tshe tshad kyang nye bar rdzogs 'gro bar 'dug pas 'ja' 'od de'i steng na phar phyin nas slob dpon gyi phyi
la 'brangs na dga' ba 'dug snyam pa thugs la shar ba'i tshe/ yang

de ma thag dpal ldan sa skya'i sde chen po gtsug lag khang dang bcas pa thugs yul du khra lam ste shar zhing / gdung brgyud 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched kyang sku na phra bar
dgongs nas/ sku tshe'i 'du byed byin gyis brlabs pa'i dgongs pa gtad de/ de 'phral du gu ru drag po'i nyams bzhes shar ma zhig gnang ba na/ slob dpon chen po'i sku de sngar
las gsal bar gyur pa'i mod la gdams pa zab mo dang lung bstan rab tu mang po gnang zhing / lhag par da dung lo du ma'i bar du bstan 'gro'i don dpag tu med pa 'grub pa
'dug cing / de nas dag pa'i zhing bde ba can zangs mdog dpal gyi rir padma nga'i drung du byon gsung ba snyam byed pa'i tshe/ slob dpon nyid kyang 'od sngon po zhig tu
zhu nas sngags 'chang nyid kyi sku la thim pa'i thugs nyams shin tu gsal ba byung ba'i mod la rtog pa dang mi rtog pa thams cad las 'das te/ bde gsal mi rtog pa'i ye shes
rgyal ba rnams kyi thugs rgyud la ji ltar mnga' ba bzhin/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi thugs rgyud la 'khrungs par gyur nas re zhig de'i ngang la 'byams te/ de las sad pa na nyi
ma yang phyi mor song 'dug pas myur du bzhengs nas/ de'i nye skor na 'bab chu zhig yod par phebs te/ dpon slob thams cad kyis sku khrus mdzad pa'i tshe/ de'i brag zhig
la sngags 'chang nyid kyi phyag zhabs kyi rjes byung ba da lta yang dad pa can rnams kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du bzhugs par kun la grags pa yin la/ mdor na sngags 'chang
bla ma 'di nyid kyis mdo sngags kyi chos tshul gsan pa rnams la bsams na sku tshe hril por yongs 'dzin dam

pa du ma las dam pa'i chos kho na gsan pa lta bu/ yang dben gnas ri khrod rnams su thugs dam zab mo la gcig tu gzhol bas nyams rtogs bzang po 'khrungs tshul rnams dang / yi
dam zhi khro du ma dang / rdo rje'i chos skyong rnams kyi gsang sngags zab mo mang po'i bye bsnyen mdzad tshul rnams la bsams na sku tshe rang po zab bzhes la chig sgril
kho na mdzad pa lta bu/ yang sa skya pa'i yab chos dri ma med pa rnams gtso bor gyur pa'i dbang khrid lung man ngag rjes gnang bka' gtad sogs zab mo'i chos kyi 'khor lo
bskor tshul rnams la bsams na sku tshe hril po chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba lta bu/ yang bstan pa'i dgra bo lha gnas rnams kyis thog drangs pa'i bdud kyi gnas mal snying la
bcas pa'i stobs ldan gyi gdug pa can mang po/ sa skya pa'i bka' srung khyad par can rnams bran du bskol te drag po mngon spyod kyi las sbyor gyi sgo nas gtan rlag tu btang
ste/ rnam shes chos kyi dbyings su bsgral ba'i tshul rnams bsams na sku tshe rang por las sbyor kho nar mdzad pa lta bu/ yang bsam yas dang sa skya sogs kyi gtsug lag
khang mang po'i zhig gsos mdzad tshul dang / gsar bzhengs bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad pa/ mdo sngags kyi dge 'dun gyi sde gsar 'dzugs gnang ba rnams la bsams na/ sku tshe
ril po gtsug lag khang dang dge 'dun gyi sde'i zhabs tog dang gsar 'dzugs mdzad pa lta bu/ yang lho bod dbus gtsang gi khyon 'di rgyun chad med pa zhabs kyis bcags shing
/ dgon che chung / grwa bu slob/ bstan pa stobs kyis

'dzin pa'i sbyin bdag sa skyong chen po rnams lugs gnyis 'phrin las kyi sgo nas bskyang tshul rnams la bsams na sku tshe ril po de kho na mdzad pa lta bu/ yang bde kye gsang
gsum/ yang phur chos skyong che chung / gzhan yang yi dam zhi khro du ma dang bcas pa'i sgrub dkyil dbang rjes gnang sogs kyi yig cha dang / gsol 'debs nyams mgur zhal
gdams kyi tshogs du ma/ rab gnas sogs dang / gzhan yang gdan sa chen po'i dus ja dkar me sgrub mchod rnams dang / dbyar chos dgun chos/ dus rim che chung sogs 'phral dang
yun gyi dge rgyun gtong dgos kyi deb chen/ zhal ngo che 'don sogs dang / bstan pa'i rnam gzhag mdzad tshul gyi deb chen/ 'bul sdud pa'i deb/ gdan sa mdzod chen gyi deb sogs
dang / gtsug lag khang gi deb chen/ chos sde che chung mang po'i bca' yig sogs bstan pa'i rgyun la phan nges pa'i gsung rab mdzad pa rnams la bsams na sku tshe ril por
bstan bcos rtsom pa kho na mdzad pa lta bu sogs mdor na skyes chen dam pa de nyid kyi ngo mtshar ba'i rnam thar gyi mdzad pa'i cha gang la bsams kyang / sangs rgyas kyi
mdzad pa kho na las ma 'das pa 'di ni grub mtha' ngan pa dang yul dus kyis ma bskal pa'i skyes bu blo gzu bor gnas shing / rnam dpyod dang ldan pa kun la rlung ltar grags
pa yin no/ /de ltar sngags 'chang bla ma bdag nyid chen po de nyid kyis dgung lo dgu bzhes pa nas brtsams te/ drug cu rtsa brgyad du phebs pa shing pho spre'u'i lo ma shar
gyi bar du thabs la mkhas pa sna tshogs kyi sgo nas spyi dang bye brag gi bstan

pa ches cher gsal bar mdzad pa de dag la thugs shin tu rangs par gyur cing / snyigs ma'i dus kyi skye bo rnams kyi spyod tshul ngan pa rnams la gzigs pas thugs cung zad gdungs
par yang gyur nas/ zhing khams gzhan du 'byon pa la mngon du phyogs par gyur te/ de'i snga ltas su sa chen po 'di yang g.yo ba dang / gdan sa chen po'i nye 'khor rnams
su sgra chen po yang mang du grags pa dang / bsam yas chos skyong chen pos kyang / yongs gangs ljongs dpal ldan sa skya yi/ /bstan 'dzin bla ma gzhan don dgongs/ /kye ma
kyi hur ci rang drag /mgo bo gser srang 'bum ri ba/ /de ni myur du 'jig la nye/ /mkha' 'gro'i khyogs la bteg nas song / /khyed zab yangs mthil pas ma tshor ram/ /zhes sogs
mya ngan gyi rnam pa mdzad pa dang / gzhan yang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du mi shis pa'i ltas mang du byung bar grags shing / gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po 'di spyir
phra rags kyi mdzad pa gang bsgrubs kyang thugs rtsol shin tu che ba zhig yin pa la/ dus der ni sngar bas kyang rtsol ba cher mdzad nas/ zhal gyis bzhes pa'i gsung chos
rnams dang gtsug lag khang gi zhig gsos/ gsung rtsom 'phro can sogs ma grub dogs pa lta bu'i sgo nas shin tu myur bar gyis zhes 'khor rnams la yang bka' stsal pa dang
/ lhag par bdag nyid chen po rang gi gsung las/ nang so pu tra khang 'di zhig gsos ma grub na/ de nged kyi sems kyi re ba'i lhag mar yod ces gsungs pa bzhin/ lo de nyid kyi
tshe nang so pu tra khang gi zhig gsos

dang / pu tra chen po dngos su gnas pa'i zangs chen khrag mtsho ma bkra shis 'od 'bar du grags pa 'di nyid kyang mgon khang gi shar nas nub phyogs su spyan 'dren mdzad pa'i
tshe pu tra nyid zangs la dngos su thim pa'i gzigs snang byung bar grags pa sogs ngo mtshar ya mtshan can mang po dang bcas mgon khang gi zhig gsos rnams mdzad de/ de phal
cher grub nas pu tra chen po nyid kyi sku'i skya bzo grub mtshams/ dge sdings phyogs la khor tsam zhig phebs pa'i dgongs gtad shar ba'i tshe/ de'i nub mo gzims chung lhun
grub pho brang gi gzims sgo brdungs nas pu tra nyid drung du byung ste/ nang so'i pu tra'i sku la rtsi tshon rab gnas sogs mi mdzad par 'di khar 'jog pa yin nam zhes
zhu ba zhig byung ba dang / bdag nyid chen pos dge sdings la 'gro ba'i sngon la nang so'i pu tra khang gi rtsi tshon rab gnas sogs mthar phyin grub pa legs pa 'dug snyam
du dgongs shing / sku 'khor rnams la yang bka' stsal te myur bar grub par mdzad de/ /de nas sngags 'chang bla ma yab sras gsum zhabs 'bring pa'i tshogs du ma dang bcas te
dge sdings su phebs/ der bdag chen rgya dkar ba'i thugs dam phyag nas ma'i gur gyi mgon po lcam dral las mkhan dang bcas pa dang / zhing skyong chen po'i sku bram gzugs
rnams la nyams gso dang / dge sdings mthil du mgon khang gsar bzhengs mdzad nas/ der chos skyong che chung gi sku brnyan sogs bzhugs su gsol te rab gnas dang mnga' gsol rgyas
pa mdzad cing / yul khams der lo phyug legs pa'i rten 'brel sogs dang tshe dbang

sogs/ mdor na lugs gnyis kyi sgo nas phyogs de nyid na gnas pa'i skye dgu thams cad kyi bsam pa yongs su rdzogs par mdzad nas/ de nas rim gyis gdan sa chen por chibs kyi kha
lo bsgyur te zhong ngar phebs pa'i tshe/ der yab sras rnams gsol ja zhig mchod pa'i bar la sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ zho nga'i ri 'di thams cad rmugs pa 'ba' zhig
gis gang nas 'dug pa khyed khri thog pa sku mched kyis mthong gi e 'dug gsung ba la/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched kyis bdag rnams kyis de bzhin mi shes pa 'dug lags zhes
zhus pa na/ ci zer gsungs nas cung zad bzhugs pa'i mthar dbu gug pa cig mdzad nas go byung da yong ba 'dug ces gsung bar grags te/ 'di ni mus chen sems dpa' chen po zhi
bar gshegs pa'i gong tsam du skyems dad shin tu che bas gsol ja mang du mchod dgos pa byung ba la rgyu mtshan zhus pas/ nga la kha rin dbyar chos 'chad dus gling dga'i ri
sogs thams cad rmugs pa'i rang bzhin du 'char ba gcig byung ba de sa chu la thim pa'i rtags su 'dug do zhag skom dad shin tu che ba 'di chu me la thim pa'i rtags yin/ rnal
'byor pa lam bsgoms pa'i stobs kyis gzhi dus kyi rtags rnams lam rtags su shar ba yin no zhes gsungs pa dang tshul mtshungs par snang bas shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i rnam
thar yin no/ /de nas gdan sa chen por phebs te de'i nang par nas/ bdag nyid chen po 'dis sngar nas mi mdzad pa'i gdan sa chen po'i gtsug lag khang so so dang / mgon khang
rnams su nyin re bzhin

phebs te dkar me dang snyan dar sogs 'bul ba dang / thugs bskyed dang smon lam rgya chen po 'debs par mdzad cing / so so'i dkon gnyer rnams la yang ma 'ongs pa mkhyen pa'i
bslab bya mang du stsal zhing / khyad par mgon khang rnams su phebs pa'i tshe/ rten rnams la phyag nas gnang ba dang bcas/ spyir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang / bye brag
dpal sa skya pa'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas dar zhing rgyas pa'i 'phrin bcol dang bka' bsgo mang du mdzad cing / khyad par sgo rum/ nang so/ skyed lhas rnams su
'phrin las bcol ba dang bka' bsgo drag tu mdzad pas/ de dus sngags 'chang nyid kyi gzigs snang la chos skyong so so'i gus 'dud dang bcas bka' las mi 'da' ba'i dam bca' phul
bar nges te/ skabs der bdag nyid chen po'i gsung gis/ da res mgon khang so sor 'phrin bcol rnams byas pa'i dus su gang bcol ba bzhin chos skyong so sos bsgrub nges pa'i
yid snang gsal bar byung zhes gsung ba dang / skyed lhas mgon khang du bka' bsgo gnang ba'i dus su brag gi dbus nas Da ma ru dang / dril bu dang / rkang gling gi skad
phra mo zhig dang / lhag par dril bu g.yer kha'i sgra sil chom du byung ba ni der yod kyi sku 'khor kun gyi mthun snang du grub pa thos zhes kyang grags shing / de nas klu
rgyal gtsug na rin chen la chab gtor klu gtor dang bum gter 'jug pa sogs mdzad nas skye dgu rnams la bde skyid bla na med pa 'byung ba'i 'phrin bcol rgya chen po mdzad
de/ de rjes sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa'i dus chen chu stod zla ba'i tshes bcu

dang nye ba rdo rje phur pa'i sgrub mchod tshugs par brtsams pa na/ de nyid kyi gar 'chams/ bris thig dbyangs rol sogs gdung sras sku mched gnyis kyis thog drangs 'dus pa'i
tshogs rnams la sngar las kyang zhib cing mtha' chod par stsal nas/ 'das ma 'ongs kyi bslab bya lung bstan mtha' yas pa zhig mdzad cing / lo de'i phur pa sgrub mchod kyis
'dul gyi gar 'chams kyi rol dpon la yang phebs te/ de dus 'khon rog gi thugs dam ma'i rdo rje phur pa'i sku brnyan nang du bzhugs pa'i bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu'i
sku mi tshad tsam zhig kyang gsar du bzhengs nas sngags 'chang nyid kyis phyag nas dang bkra shis mnga' gsol rgyas par mdzad de ma 'ongs pa'i gdul bya rnams 'phrin las gong
'phel du 'gyur ba'i rten 'brel thams cad sgrig par mdzad pa yin no zhes thos la/ de skabs nas gzhan ngor gsol dwangs zhan pa'i rkyen gyis sku shed je chung je chung la
song ba'i tshul bstan pa na/ bdag nyid chen po dpon slob nyung shas shig gis lhun grub pho brang du sku mtshams ha cang dam pa ma yin pa zhig mdzad nas bzhugs pa'i tshe/
zhabs 'bring pa rnams kyis deng sang mtshan ltas la sogs pa ji ltar byung / sku shed ji chung du 'gro ba 'di la blo bde ba zhig gtan nas mi 'dug pas/ lo 'di la sku dog
bzhin ni med lags sam zhes zhus pa na/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ deng sang rmis ltas la sogs pa gang yang ma byung / kha sing lam 'bras bshad pa'i skabs snga dro khri steng
du lam dus len gyis bsdad pa'i tshe/ nam mkha' nas dar sna lnga ring

po zhig nged kyi mdun du khra tshub kyis skyur byung ba la/ de 'dzin par brtsams pa'i tshe/ yang nam mkha' la khra tshub kyis brdogs 'gro ba de 'dra lam 'bras ma grol bar gyi
snga dro phal che ba la byung zhing / kha rtsang nye stabs sag sar phyin pa'i dus su/ sa skya'i rgyab ri dang gdan sa dan gyi stod phyogs rnams su lha'i rigs mang po phung
phung 'dus nas/ lag na dar lcog dang 'phan gdugs rgyal mtshan sogs dang / rol mo'i rigs mang po khyer zhing de dag gi bar mtshams na nam mkha' 'gro ma yin zer ba'i 'bag
gyon pa 'dra ba mang pos gar byed pa dang / gzhan yang de rnams kyi khrod nas mi nag dung long can dag gis 'o cag la dar dkar gyi g.yab mo ling ling 'debs pa sogs mthong
snang ya mtshan che ba 'ga' re btud nas byung yang / de tsam rang la ni brtag dpyad cher med las che/ gang ltar da lo sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa nyid zhal bzhugs pa'i
dus bzhin sku 'khor mang po dang bcas dus skabs phal che thar rmi lam du 'byon pa zhig 'dug pas/ nged rang 'di phyi bar do gsum du khong rang la gsol ba rtse gcig tu btab
pas chog mod/ gzhan dog cha yod med ci shes zhes gsung bar grags shing / de skabs nas gdan sa chen po dang gtsang phyogs kyi dgon so sor yang sku rim rgya che ba mdzad kyang
/ sku khams la skyed du mngon pa ma byung nas sku mtshams kyang cung zad dam par mdzad cing / byas 'gyur nas sngags 'chang nyid la mi phyed pa'i dad pa dang ldan pa'i
sgrub chen kun dga' don grub kyang zhabs drung du 'bod par mdzad la/ dus der yang thugs dam zab

mo la rtse gcig tu bzhugs shing / skabs shig dge slong kun dga' ba la/ khyod kyis e mthong ba 'dug lha khang chen mo dang phun tshogs gling gi steng 'di thams cad na ga nas
'ong cha med pa'i dar gdugs rgyal mtshan ba dan sogs khyer ba'i lha'i bu mang pos khrig mer gyis gang zhing / rol mo'i sgra chen pos sa skya'i lung pa thams cad bkang nas
'dug pa e ma ya mtshan che zhes gsungs shing / dbu dang phyag gis brda mang po zhig mdzad kyin 'dug pa la/ dge slong pas gang yang zhu ma nus shing / de dang dus mtshungs
su gzim khang gi mdo phug thams cad dri bzang khyad par can zhig gis khyab par byung ba dang / de nas gro bzhin zla ba'i tshes bzhi'i nyin sngags 'chang nyid dge slong
kun dga' don grub dang bcas lhun grub pho brang gi dbang khang gi gdugs la bzhugs pa'i tshe rje nyid phyag thal mo sbyar spyan bar snang la khor mor gzigs shing zhal 'dzum
'dzum mdzad pa dang / de ma thag sngar gyi dri 'dra ba'i dri zhim khyad par can zhig thul gyis byung ba'i tshe/ dge slong pas ci 'dug lags zhus pas/ bdag nyid chen po
thugs dges spro chen po dang bcas a re dga'/ sa lo chen po dang birWa pa slob dpon padma gsum phyag sbrel mdzad nas 'byon pa'i rjes su grub thob rigs 'dzin mang po yang khrom
tshogs su 'byon pa dang / bde kye gsang gsum/ phur pa/ rnal 'byor ma sogs nged rang gis sgrub mchod byas pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi lha tshogs rnams kyang byon 'dug gzhan
yang sangs rgyas byang sems nam mkha' gang bar bzhugs 'dug pa skyabs su

mchi zhes gsungs shing thugs spro ba chen po mdzad kyin 'dug pa na/ dge slong pas kyang spyan chab phyung ste phyag mang du phul ces thos la/ de ltar zla ba phyed gnyis lhag
tsam gyi bar du gzhan ngor gsol dwangs zhan pa'i tshul gyis tshogs 'khor sogs rags pa rnams kyi rgyun snga mo nas gcod par mdzad kyang / rgyal yum dam pa bkra shis dpal
gyi bu khrid kyis nan zhus mdzad pa la brten nas/ mdzo zho la bye kar btab pa gsol dkar chung ngu re tsam zhag 'ga' re'i bar du gsol bar mdzad cing / de rjes de yang gcod
par mdzad de/ gsol ja nag po cung zad re dang / nang mchod cung zad tsam re ma gtogs gzhan gang yang ma gsol bar zhag bcu gnyis tsam gyi bar du bzhugs par grags shing /
de dag gi skabs thams cad du nam mkha' bai DUrYa'i mdog ltar shin tu dwangs pa la nyi ma'i 'od zer sngar bas kyang gsal zhing / 'ja' sna lnga'i ri mo'i dbyibs 'khor lo dang
nor bu sogs ngo mtshar can sna tshogs kyis nam mkha'i khyon thams cad khyab pa dang / lha'i me tog gi char bsam gyis mi khyab pa dus rtag tu 'bab pa sogs ngo mtshar ba'i
ltas dpag tu med pa dang bcas zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu'i nyin mo mchod pa rgya chen po yang shom gsungs shing / zhing gzhan du gshegs par brtsams pa na/ dge slong kun
dga' don grub pas phyag mang du btsal zhing / da dung bstan 'gro'i don du zhabs pad brtan par bzhugs dgos shing / ci ste mi bzhugs na dag pa'i zhing khams gang du gshegs/
gzigs snang ngo mtshar can ci 'dra byung lags zhes zhus pa na/ nyid kyi

gsung las/ ci zer lo drug cu re brgyad tshe ring po min pa e yin/ bstan pa dang sems can gyi don yang rgya chen po grub/ da ni dag pa'i zhing khams bde ba can zhes bya ba'i
ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i zhing khams kyi bkod pa phun sum tshogs pa de nyid kyi dbus na/ sangs rgyas 'od dpag med la sangs rgyas byang sems mang pos bskor ba dang /
slob dpon padma/ sa skya'i rje btsun gong ma lnga/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa rnams kyang bzhugs/ rgyun ring po 'dug long med ces gsungs shing / 'on kyang tshes bcu de nyid
la gshegs na sa lo chen po'i dus dran gyi mchod pa bag la zha bar gyur dogs pa dang / dge slong pas kyang gsol ba btab pa la dgongs nas sku tshe'i 'du byed cung zad bsring
ba mdzad de/ de nas gro bzhin zla ba'i tshes bcu gnyis kyi nyi ma ri rtse la bzhud la nye ba na/ gzugs sku bsdu bar brtsams pa'i tshe da rang gsol ba mi thebs pa 'dra
snyam nas gdung sras sku mched kyang spyan drangs nas zhabs drung du phebs pa na/ thugs sras rgyal tshab dam pa sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can gyi phyag g.yas pa la
bdag nyid chen po'i phyag gis bcang bcangs pa lan gnyis mdzad nas/ sa skya'i sde bstan pa la skyag re ba skyed cig ces nyis btud du bka' stsal nas/ de ma thag sku cung
zad bsrangs te sa lo thams cad mkhyen pas dam rdzas ril bu tshan gcig bzhes par mdzad 'phral zhing khams 'di'i mdzad pa re zhig rdzogs nas/ zhing khams gzhan du gdul bya
rgya che ba la dgongs te/ rtag 'dzin can rnams nges 'byung bskyed pa

dang / le lo can rnams brtson 'grus la bskul ba'i phyir/ sngags 'chang bla ma de nyid dgung lo re brgyad du phebs pa shing pho spre'u'i lo gro bzhin zla ba'i dkar po'i phyogs
kyi tshes bcu gnyis la/ rgyud sde rnams nas 'byung ba'i 'da' kha ma'i rnal 'byor zab mo gsal 'debs par mdzad de/ thun mong du snang ba'i gzugs sku de nyid kyi bkod pa
chos dbyings su bsdu ba'i tshul bstan to/ /de'i dus su bdag nyid chen po la mi phyed pa'i dad pa dang ldan pa rgya mkhar rtse'i chos rgyal chen po bsod nams lhun grub la
mnal ltas dang gzigs snang 'dres pa zhig la sngags 'chang nyid gsal bar byon nas/ deng phyin chad nga dran pa byung na sku 'di la gsol ba thob cig ces gsungs nas/ rgyal rtse
rtse rgyal gyi mgon khang gi mgon po'i sku de la thim pa'i snang ba shin tu gsal bar byung ba dang / yang shab pa rab 'byung pa 'bul dpon shAka blo bar grags pa de nyid
khams kyi lung pa zhig tu yod pa'i dus nyin gcig mthong snang la/ bdag nyid chen po de nyid bzhugs gdan dkar po gru bzhi pa zhig gi steng na bzhugs pa'i zur bzhi bteg
nas nam mkha' la gshegs pa mngon sum du mthong ba sogs 'di dag ni sngon sa skya pa chen po byang gi skya bo kha gdangs su zhing gshegs pa'i tshul bstan pa na/ slob ma rnams
la sku'i bkod pa mi 'dra ba mang du bstan nas dag pa'i zhing du gshegs pa dang tshul mtshungs par shes par bya'o/ /de ltar tshes bcu gnyis kyi nub mo nas bzung ste bcu
bzhi'i bar du 'od gsal ma bu ro gcig tu 'dres pa'i spros pa'i tshogs thams cad nye bar zhi zhing / mtha' dbus

thams cad dang bral ba'i gsal stong zung 'jag gi ngang du mnyam par 'jog pa mdzad nas/ de nas bcu bzhi'i tho rangs su babs pa na sku gdung gi nye skor na bzhugs pa kun gyis
gsan pa'i thag sgra shin tu che ba dang bcas te/ dbu gtsug gi thod pa sor gang tsam zhig gtsug tor gyi tshul du 'phags pa la byang sems kyi zil pa phrom me ba dang bcas
par gyur nas/ de dang dus mnyam du sngar gyi 'od gsal las bzhengs te/ dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs du ma'i bsu ba dang bcas mdo nas bshad pa'i bde ba can nam/ sngags
nas bshad pa'i mkha' spyod dag pa'i zhing du bde bar gshegs pa yin no/ /'dir smras pa/ kye ma kyi hud 'dzam gling ljongs 'dir ni/ /thub dbang skyes mchog lan gnyis 'da'
tshul bstan/ /gdul bya'i yid bde ma lus 'phrog mdzad pa'i/ /brtse ldan khyod las spros pa srid 'dir su/ /dus der 'jig rten stongs so sngags 'chang rje/ /dus der gdul bya'i
yid bzhin nor bu stor/ /dus der dad can thams cad mig dang bral/ /dus der 'jig rten thams cad mun par song / /mkhas btsun bzang po phyogs re'i snang ba can/ /yongs 'dzin
rgyu skar 'char nub mang na yang / /lung rtogs 'od zer bye bas kun gsal ba'i/ /bstan pa'i nyi ma nub bo sngags 'chang rje/ /skal bzang gdul bya rgyu skar phreng ba yis/
/yongs su gang ba'i lha lam gdan sa cher/ /lugs gnyis 'phrin las snang ba mi stsol bar/ /sngags 'chang skye dgu'i zla ba ci slad gshegs/ /thogs med dus nas smon lam mthu
grub pas/ /

dus 'dir ci mdzad bstan 'gro'i don gyur ba'i/ /yid bzhin nor bu lta bu'i sngags 'chang de/ /slob tshogs rnams kyis rnyed nas glo bur stor/ /rigs gzugs phun tshogs mthu stobs
bsam yas shing / /bstan pa 'dzin skyong spel la rab mkhas pa'i/ /'gro ba'i gnyen khyod lo 'ga' mi bzhugs par/ /bstan pa'i bya ba bshol nas gang du gshegs/ /rgyal ba dges
pa'i spyod tshul lhur mdzad pa'i/ /skyes mchog 'di 'dra lha yi bla ma zhes/ /lha bu rnams kyis me tog sil ma dang / /'ja' 'od shing rtas bsus nas yud kyis gshegs/ /dmigs
med thugs rjes rang don kun bor nas/ /rtag tu gzhan don 'ba' zhig bsgrub pa khyod/ /da ni 'gro ba'i don mdzad rdzogs gyur tam/ /min na bu slob 'bor ba 'di phod dam/ /'on
kyang mthong ba don ldan khyod sku yis/ /brtse med zhing 'dir 'dor ba'i tshul ston pa/ /tshad med thugs rje'i skyon du mi 'tshal gyis/ /zhing 'di'i gdul bya'i skal ba'i
skyon du zad/ /sngags 'chang thams cad mkhyen pa khyod gshegs pas/ /dbang bskur rjes gnang bka' gtad su la zhu/ /rgyud dang man ngag zhal shes su yis 'byed/ /phyag len phra
mo'i tshogs rnams su la 'dri/ /mgon khyod bstan pa'i bya bas thugs bskul nas/ /yang yang spyan gyis gzigs shing phyag reg pa'i/ /gtsug lag khang dang rten gsum ngo mtshar
rnams/ /da lta grogs med so sor skye ba 'phel/ /'dren mchog khyed kyi zhabs drung gnas bcas nas/ /'dzum zhal mngon sum mthong ba'i skabs bral ba'i/ /bsod nams dman pa'i
rjes

'jug bdag 'dra la/ /mi mngon dbyings nas gzigs shig sngags 'chang rje/ /dad pas khyod kyi bris 'bur sku brnyan la'ang / /yang yang 'dud cing gus pas gsol btab kyang / /rmi
lam tsam du'ang zhal dkyil mo ston par/ /kye ma bdag gis mtshams med las bsags sam/ /sprul pa'i skyes mchog khyod kyis bstan 'gro phyir/ /sku srog nyid kyang gtong la mi
zhum pa'i/ /rlabs chen mdzad pas bstan pa spel ba'i rgyun/ /'di 'dra mthong bas bdag sems dbang med 'phrogs/ /phyogs 'di'i skye dgu mtha' dag da lta'i bar/ /bde la 'khod
pa khyod kyi drin yin kyang / /kyi hud da ni bu tsha ngan pa yi/ /pha ma'i drin bzhin brjed pa 'di la gzigs/ /da ni khyod kyi rgyal tshab thugs kyi sras/ /bdag gi bla ma
'jam dbyangs sku mched kyang / /kun gyis mi mngon dag pa'i zhing gshegs nas/ /kyi hud bdag cag slob tshogs 'dir lus so/ /mkhyen brtse nus ldan khyod kyi mdzad 'phrin rgyun/
/ngo mtshar mtha' dag bdag gis skyong ngo zhes/ /rlom sems 'di 'dra mi rnams rnam thar la/ /spre 'u dag gis 'gran dang khyad par ci/ /'on kyang lhag bsam dag pas khyed
bskul nas/ /sa skya'i sde dang bstan pa gdung brgyud bcas/ /yar ngo'i zla ltar rgyas par gyur snyam pa'i/ /bsam pa dge 'dis sngags 'chang dges gyur cig /dam pa khyod kyi
ngo mtshar rnam thar cha/ /mtshon pa tsam zhig bdag gis bkod pa 'dis/ /rjes 'jug thams cad dad pa rab g.yos nas/ /kun la bla ma'i byin rlabs 'jug par shog /khyad par thub
dbang

rgyal tshab sa skya pa'i/ /bstan dang bstan 'dzin dgon gnas dang bcas pa/ /skyes chen gang gi drin las byung ba'i tshul/ /shes nas byas shes drin gzo bskyed gyur cig /las ngan
dbang gis dus kyi mthar skyes pa'i/ /rmongs pa bdag dang bdag la ltos bcas rnams/ /'brel tshad don ldan sngags 'chang yab sras kyis/ /'di phyi'i don kun 'grub par byin
gyis rlobs/ /zhes kyang shugs 'byung du gsol ba btab pa'i bar skabs kyi tshigs su bcad pa'o/ /de nas re zhig gi bar du sku gdung rin po che de nyid lhun grub pho brang
de nyid du mchod rten gyi khang bu brtsegs par bzhugs su gsol zhing / de nas rgyun mi ring bar gdung sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched kyis sngags 'chang nyid kyi dgongs pa
rdzogs thabs su nyid kyi sku brnyan gser zangs las grub pa ngo mtshar can thog tshad ma la lam zab bla ma brgyud pas bskor ba dang / khyad par sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal
po nyid kyi sku gdung bzhugs pa'i rnam rgyal mchod rten rgyu rin po che dngul las grub cing bzo khyad rmad du byung ba rin po che bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i phra rgyan gyis
spras shing dpangs shin tu mtho ba/ mthong na mi mthun pa med pa de nyid gsar bzhengs mdzad de/ sku gdung rin po che spyan drangs nas der bzhugs su gsol zhing / mchod
pa'i bye brag bsam gyis mi khyab pa bsham ste/ gdung sras 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched kyis gtso mdzad rdo rje 'dzin pa du mas rab tu gnas pa rgyas par mdzad pa'i tshe/ spyan
dbye'i skabs su rten rnams la nyi ma shar zhing / nam mkha' shin tu dwangs pa la lha rnams kyis me tog

gi char chen po phab pa dang / 'ja' 'od kyi gur phub pa la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas te bkra shis dang byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar bar bzhugs te/ slar yang
srid pa ji srid pa de sring du 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi rnam sprul rim par byon te/ gdul bya gang la ci 'dul gyi rnam par bstan nas phrin las rgyun mi chad cing lhun gyis
grub pa'i rten 'brel phun sum tshogs pa 'grig pa yin no/ /de ltar sku gdung rin po che de nyid mi lo nyi shu'i bar du ril por bzhugs shing / de nas sngon 'jam pa'i dbyangs
sku mched la sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ bla ma dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyi pur ril po yun ring 'jog pa 'di legs rgyu med de/ ma 'ongs pa bstan pa nyams pa'i dus su
bla ma'i pur srang bar gyi khyi sogs kyi zas su 'gro ba yang srid pas/ nged kyi rus bu 'di dang tsho ni myur du bzhu ba gal che'o zhes yang yang gsung ba zhig yod pa gdung
sras sku mched gnyis kyi thugs dkyil du bcangs nas/ shing pho 'brug gi lo shar ba na sku gdung rin po che bzhu la phul te/ gdung tsha rnams dngul gdung rin po che de nyid
du bzhugs su gsol zhing / de dang dus mtshungs par sems dpa' chen po sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos bdag nyid chen po'i dgongs pa rdzogs
thabs su rigs 'dzin bla ma brgyud pa'i gtsug lag khang gsar bzhengs mdzad pa de'i rten gyi gtso bo la sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i nang rten dngul gdung yid bzhin gyi
nor bu de nyid spyan drangs te/ deng sang gi bar du 'gro ba rnams kyi mchod pa'i

gnas su bzhugs pa 'di nyid yin no/ /smras pa/ 'gro la bde skyid ma lus 'byung ba'i gzhi/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa rin chen skyong ba la/ /la la mkhas pa'i sgo nas bstan pa 'dzin/
/'ga' zhig mthu rtsal nus pa'i sgo nas te/ /la la btsun pa'i brtul zhugs kyis 'dzin cing / /kha cig stobs dang chab srid phun tshogs kyis/ /'dzin par bshad kyang sngon
byon bstan 'dzin gyi/ /skyes chen phal la phyogs re ldan mang yang / /gang zag gcig la bstan 'dzin thams cad kyi/ /rnam thar tshang ba sngags 'chang 'di nyid tsam/ /yin
par yongs 'dzin dam pa 'di nyid kyi/ /rnam thar kho bos byas pa'i ngo mtshar rgya mtshor bltas pas shes/ /zhes kyang rang babs su smras so/ /de rnams kyis dus mchod bla
brang pa'i gdung rabs byon tshul mkhas pa'i dbang po dkon mchog lhun grub kyi gdung rabs ya rabs kha rgyan las ji ltar 'byung ba bzhin bstan zin nas/ da ni de nyid kyi kha
skong cung zad brjod par bya ste/ de la yang gnyis te/ rtse gdong pa'i gdung rabs byung tshul bstan pa dang / dpal ldan sa skya nyid du gdung rabs rgyun mi chad par byon
pa'i tshul bshad pa'o/ /dang po la yang tshigs bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang / de'i don cung zad phye ba gnyis las/ /dang po ni/ kun dga' bsam grub btsun mo ma gcig
sras/ /kun dga' bde legs bkra shis zhes bya 'khrungs/ /kun dga' bde legs btsun mo bya bzang ma'i/ /sras la 'jam dbyangs bsod nams lhun grub dang / /tshe dbang hor sogs
bsod nams rgyal mtshan dang / /'jig rten rgya hor zhes bya rnam gsum

byon/ /'jig rten rgya hor btsun mo stag lung mar/ /sras gsum 'khrungs pa da lta bzhugs 'di'o/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa de'i don cung zad bshad pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsam
grub kyis btsun mo zhig khab tu bzhes pa la sras 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bde legs bkra shis 'khrungs pa ni/ gzhon nu nyid nas dam pa'i skyes bu mang po las gsan pa ci rigs
pa mdzad de thugs dam la brtson par bzhugs shing / rnal 'byor dbang phyug gis rjes su bzung bar yang grags la/ mthar dgung lo bzhi bcu bzhes pa'i tshe bde bar gshegs so/
/bdag chen des bya bzang pa'i sras mo dpal bu khrid bya ba btsun mor bzhes pa la/ da lta dgung lo nga dgu'i steng na bzhugs pa'i 'jam dbyangs kun dga' bsod nams lhun grub
dang / gzhon nu la gshegs pa'i tshe dbang hor sog bsod nams rgyal mtshan zhes bya ba dang / 'jig rten rgya hor dang gsum 'khrungs pa de dag gis mdzad pa'i cha rnams ni so
so'i rnam thar du blta'o/ /de gsum gyi nang nas gcung 'jig rten rgya hor gyis stag lung pa'i sras mo khab tu bzhes pa la sras gsum 'khrungs pa ni da lta yod pa'i gdung
sras sku mched 'di dag go /de dag gis rtse gdong pa'i gdung rabs byon tshul bstan zin nas/ da ni dpal ldan sa skya nyid du gdung rabs rgyun ma chad par byon zhing 'byon par
'gyur ba'i tshul bshad par bya ste/ 'di la yang tshigs bcad kyi sgo nas mdor bstan pa dang / de'i don rgyas par bshad pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ ngag dbang kun rin btsun
mo gdong dga'

ma/ /lha gcig dkar mo legs 'dzom zhes bya'i sras/ /grub pa'i dbang phyug bsod nams dbang po dang / /btsun mo gnyis pa slar yang gdong dga' ma/ /bkra shis dpal gyi bu khrid
ces bya'i sras/ /'dzam gling rgyan mchog grags pa'i mtshan can 'khrungs/ /gang de'i btsun mo byang phyogs rgyal po'i lcam/ /lha sras bsod nams rgyal mo zhes bya'i sras/ /'jam
dbyangs sprul pa mthu stobs dbang phyug dang / /rgyal sras ngag dbang kun dga' dbang rgyal mtshan/ /yon tan bral yang dam pa'i rigs skyes pa'i/ /sngags 'chang ngag dbang
kun dga' bsod nams rnams/ /sngon du byon dang da lta rtag bzhugs pa'i/ /dus mchod bla brang gdung brgyud rim pa ste/ /phyis nas 'byon 'gyur bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ /sangs
rgyas bstan pa yar ngo'i zla ba ltar/ /'phel zhing rgyas par 'gyur zhes shes par bya/ /zhes so/ /gnyis pa de'i don rgyas par bshad pa ni/ bstan pa'i nyi ma sngags 'chang
ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba de nyid kyis btsun mo gsum khab tu bzhes pa'i dang po shar gling pa'i bu
sring mo ma gcig bsod nams dpal 'dzom rgyal mo bya ba la lha lcam tshe ring bu khrid dang / lha gcig dpal 'dzom rgyal mo zhes bya ba gnyis 'khrungs pa'i che ba ni/ dge
bsnyen ma sngags kyi nus pa sogs che zhing / 'gro ba nad gdon gyis gzir ba spyi dang / lhag par rims nad sogs la slob dpon ma 'dis srung ba gnang ba tsam gyis gtan mi 'byung
bar grags pa deng sang yang rin chen sgang na bzhugs pa

'di'o/ /yang sngags 'chang bla ma kun dga' rin chen gyi btsun mo gnyis pa gdong dga' ma bsod nams legs 'dzom dkar mo zhes bya ba la/ sras lcam sring bzhi 'khrungs pa'i gcen
po ni bdag la bka' drin che ba'i bla ma gsum gyi nang tshan 'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo padma'i rnam sprul 'jam pa'i dbyangs byams pa dpal ngag dbang bsod nams dbang po
grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan yongs su grags pa de nyid de/ bdag nyid chen po 'di ni yab sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po dgung lo bzhi bcu rtsa gsum du
phebs pa sa mo lug gi lo mchu zla ba'i dkar po'i phyogs kyi tshes gnyis/ res gza' zla ba dang skar ma khrums smad la yod pa'i tho rangs kyi dus su dpal sa skya'i lha khang
chen mo'i yang steng nor rgyas zhes bya ba'i gnas mchog de nyid du ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas 'khrungs pa yin te/ de yang 'di nyid lhums su zhugs nas ma bltams
kyi bar du yum la nyin mtshan kun tu chos skyong rnams 'bral med du gnas pa yin snyam pa'i 'jigs ngam dang dga' ya le ba rgyun du byung bar grags pa dang / bltams nas kyang
sku na shin tu phra ba'i dus su zhabs skyil krung dang / phyag gnyis thugs kar chos 'chad kyi phyag rgya mdzad de bzhugs pa sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal pos gzigs nas/
'jam dbyangs yin zer bar 'dug khyed rnams kyis gtsang sbra dang bca' gas thon par gyis zhes gsungs pa dang / sku lcog la bzhugs thub pa tsam gyi skabs su sku drung na
su yang med pa'i skabs shig tshe/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po

phebs nas zhabs 'bring pa rnams la/ khyed rnams kyis bu tsha la bca' ga cher mi byed 'dug na'ang 'di rang la grogs 'grul btub cig slebs 'dug ces gsungs pa la/ zhabs 'bring
pa rnams kyis grogs de nyid su lags zhus pa na/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung gis/ de pu tra yin pa 'dug ces gsung bar grags pa la sogs pa mdor na gzhon nu'i dus nyid nas
dam can pu tra chen po 'bral ba med pa'i tshul gyis 'phrin las rgya chen po bsgrubs pa zhig yin no zhes thos la/ de nas yon tan gyi phyi mo 'bri klogs la sogs pa rnams ni
gzigs pa tsam gyis thogs med du mkhyen cing mthar phyin nas rim gyis yab rje chos kyi rgyal po nyid kyi drung du/ rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos yang phur rnam gnyis/ bde
kye gsang gsum/ yo ga bya spyod rdo rje'i chos skyong rnams dang bcas pa'i dbang lung man ngag cho ga phyag len dbyangs rol gar 'chams la sogs pa kun la byang chub par
mdzad de/ de nas dgung lo bcu gcig bzhes pa sa mo sbrul gyi lo/ /spyan snga tshul khrims 'bar gyi rnam par sprul pa lo nas spyan snga rin po che ngag dbang chos kyi grags
pa'i drung du dpal lo dgon pa'i gtsug lag khang ga la ba der lam thams cad kyi rtsa ba rab tu byung ba dge tshul gyi sdom pa rnam par dag pa nos shing / de nas brtsams
te lhag pa tshul khrims kyi phung po mig 'bras ltar gces par bzung nas/ bslab bya phra zhing phra ba kun la yang ma nyams par spyod pa zhig yin la/ de nas bdag nyid chen
po 'dis dgung lo bcu phrag gcig dang nyag ma gnyis tsam bzhes pa lcags pho rta'i lo bdag

nyid chen po sa skya paNDi ta chen po'i chos kyi khri ga la ba der bstan pa'i bdag por mnga' gsol te/ de'i skabs su bdag nyid chen po 'dis bstan bcos chen po thub pa'i dgongs
pa gsal ba zhes bya ba/ 'dus pa'i 'khor tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig la/ dag gsal snyan pa'i gsung gis nyi ma gsum gyi bar du bshad pas/ der 'dus kyi skye bo thams
cad yid 'phrog par gyur cing / de nas bdag nyid chen po 'di dgung lo bcu dgur phebs pa'i tshe/ chos kyi rje nam mkha' dbang phyug pas mkhan po dang / las kyi slob dpon
rje mgon po rin chen dang / gsang ston rje byams pa bkra shis pas mdzad cing / gzhan yang grib tshod pa dang grogs dan pa gnyis lo phu nas dge slong bgres pa gnyis kyis mdzad
de/ de ltar gzhi byes kyi dge slong nyer lnga lhag tsam 'dus pa'i dbus su bdag nyid chen po sa skya paN chen gyi bsnyen rdzogs kyi sdom rgyun de nyid bzhes te bsnyen
par rdzogs pa dge slong gi dngos po phyin ci ma log pas thugs rgyud phyug par mdzad do zhes thos la/ de dag gi gnas skabs rnams su bdag nyid chen po 'di nyid kyis mdo phyogs
la gsan sbyong rgya chen po mdzad de/ /rje 'di dgung lo bcu phrag gnyis dang bzhis lhag par phebs pa chu pho rta'i lo gsar du shar ba na tshogs chen por mgon po byams
pa'i mngon rtogs rgyan sogs byams chos sde lnga/ dam pa chos kyi grags pa'i rnam 'grel sogs tshad ma sde bdun/ gzhan yang chos rje sa paN gyi sdom rigs gnyis sogs po ti
brgya dang bcu gcig tsam zhig la sbyor bkod gsung bshad

sogs kyis bstan pa'i rnam gzhag phul du phyin pa mdzad cing / de lta bu'i bdag nyid chen po 'dis yongs 'dzin dam pa rnams las zab rgyas gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol du son
par mdzad pa'i tshul ni/ thog mar yab rje chos kyi rgyal po sngags 'chang kun dga'i mtshan can nyid kyi drung du bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu/ yang dag mar me dgu pa/
bde kye gsang gsum/ bdag med ma rnams kyi dbang sogs smin byed dbang gi rnam grangs du ma zhig dang / gzhan yang rdo rje bdag med ma'i byin rlabs dang / nA ro mkha' spyod
kyi byin rlabs sogs dang / chos skyong che chung / las mkhan pu tra ming sring gi rjes gnang sogs rjes gnang gi rigs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig dang / yang gsung ngag rin
po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa sogs grol byed khrid kyi rnam grangs shin tu zab pa du ma rgyab chos kyi lung dang bcas pa dang / gzhan yang lung gi skor la
rje btsun gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum/ rdo rje'i 'chang kun dga' bzang po'i bka' 'bum/ kun mkhyen bsod nams seng ge'i bka' 'bum/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa'i bka' 'bum/ jo bo'i
chos chung brgya rtsa rnams kyi lung gi rigs bgrang bar dka' ba lta bu zhig gsan cing / mdor na dgung lo nyer drug bzhes pa tshun chad sku dang grib ma'i tshul du 'bral
med du bsten nas/ lugs gnyis kyi bka' drin tshad med pas bskyangs pa la brten/ nyid kyi bla ma rnams kyi nang nas sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po nyid la mchog tu dad
gus che bar mdzad cing / gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis yongs 'dzin dkon

mchog dpal ldan gyi drung du gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang sogs dang / sgrub thabs brgya rtsa'i rjes gnang / dmar po skor gsum gyi rjes gnang / tshe dpag med dkar po'i rjes gnang
sogs dang / gzhan yang bde mchog dkar po'i tshe khrid/ gshed dmar spros med kyi khrid/ rwa lugs kyi rnal 'byor bzhi'i khrid/ rwa rtse sems 'dzin/ rtsa dbu ma'i khrid/
zhen pa bzhi bral gyi khrid sogs zab cing dkon pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs mang du gsan nas thugs su chud par mdzad/ yang spyan snga rin po che 'jam dbyangs dkon mchog rgya
mtsho'i drung du gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa zab mo dang / 'di'i bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar rnams kyi lung / lam 'bras glegs bam dkar
chag nang bzhin gyi lung sogs dang / lam zab sogs cha lag rags rim rjes gnang zur bka'i rigs bgrang ba las 'das pa zhig gsan cing / gzhan yang sems dpa' chen po chos 'od
zer/ rje lung rigs rgya mtsho/ rje gzhon nu blo gros/ mdog lo phu dang dge chu'i gdan sa pa gnyis/ gter ston rin po che sogs grags pa dang ma grags pa'i bla ma du ma zhig
bsten nas bka' gdams/ kye rdor/ chos skyong gur zhal/ gsang sngags snga 'gyur sogs kyis bsdus pa'i dam pa'i chos mu mtha' med pa zhig gsan par mdzad cing / der yang ma zad
bdag gi bla ma dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa'i rgyal ba mus pa chen po sangs rgyal mtshan gyi drung du yang 'khor lo bde mchog gi chos skor yongs rdzogs shig gsan par

bzhed de/ rje mus chen nyid ngam ring rgyal po'i pho brang na bzhugs pa'i skabs shig bdag nyid chen pos thugs dam dang bcas rkang mgyogs shig ched gtad gnang ste/ spyir nged
kyi 'dod chos rnams dbus gtsang gi ljongs 'dir 'tshol lugs byas pas blo kha khengs pa tsam byung yang / bde mchog gi skor 'di sngar yan re ba bzhin ma byung ba khyed mus
pa tsho brgyud pa gtsang zhing bde mchog skor la 'dris pa zhig yin pas/ de skor gyi chos bka' yongs su rdzogs pa zhig ngos la zhu dgos 'dug pas bstan la dgongs pa'i thugs
khur bskyed pa rang gal che che zhes pa'i bka' dam nan chags phebs 'dug pa sogs mdor na zab mo'i chos gsan pa la dus khor yug tu 'bad rtsol gzhan las ches che ba mdzad
de/ gsan pa de dag kyang don dang ldan par bya ba'i phyir rtse gcig tu bsgom sgrub la bzhugs pa'i tshul ni/ de yang gdan sa chen po/ dge sdings bkra shis bsam 'grub/ byas
'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong / phu ri glang brag gi ri khrod sogs su thugs dam zab mo la rtse gcig tu bzhugs nas yi dam zhi khro du ma'i gsung bsnyen dang / lhag par chos
skyong gi rtsa sngags snying po nye snying rnams la bye bsnyen sogs gsung bzlas mang du mdzad pas mthu dang nus pa'i mnga' bdag tu gyur cing / yi dam zhi khro du ma dang
/ rdo rje'i chos skyong du mas zhal gzigs shing byin gyis brlabs pa'i mtshan ma mang du brnyes pa yin te/ de yang byas 'gyur du lo gsum lan gnyis gnang ba'i snga ma'i dus/
shing mgon yid bzhin nor bu'i thugs ka nas 'od sngon po zhig byung ba rje nyid kyi thugs kar thim

pa dang / brag phug me 'bar ba'i khrod na bzhugs pa'i gur gyi mgon po'i sku zil dang ldan pa zhig dngos su gzigs pa dang / gzhan yang bstan srung dbang po rnams kyis dngos
dang rnam 'phrul du mas zhal yang yang bstan pa'i lo rgyus mang du yod kyang 'dir ma spros la/ khyad par pu tra chen po nyid dang 'bral med du bzhugs pa yin te/ nyid kyi
gsung las/ 'dug grogs su pu tra ngo mtshar che/ /zhes gsungs pa dang / kho bo cag gis rje nyid kyi drung du byas 'gyur bla brang nub kyi mgon khang khyad par can der/ gur
mgon lha brgyad/ dpal mgon zhal khra can/ pu tra ming sring gsum gyi rjes gnang rnams zhus pa'i dus/ rje nyid kyi gsung las/ kha rtsang byas 'gyur gyi maNDal na mon pa ming
sring gsum gar byed kyi 'dug pa 'tshub ma zhig tu song nas brag 'di la thim song ba de res rjes gnang 'di byed pa'i rten 'brel du 'dug gsung ba sogs kyis shes so/ /yi
dam zhi khro rnams kyi zhal gzigs pa yang / yang phur/ gur drag bde kye rnams kyi zhal mngon sum du bstan pa'i tshul ngo mtshar can mang du snang zhing / lhag par rdo rje
gzhon nu nyid kyi zhal lan gcig ma yin par yang yang du gzigs shing byin gyis brlabs pa la brten nas rje nyid kyi thugs dam gyi mthil yang lhag pa'i lha 'di kho na la mdzad
pa yin no snyam du kho bo sems shing / de ltar dngos grub kyi mtshan ma brnyes nas grub pa'i rtags mtshan bstan pa'i tshul ni/ spyir bdag nyid chen po 'dis/ zab phu/
rta nag mnga' ris sogs slob dpon rin po che padma'i gnas chen

phal che ba rnams su skam sar chu 'don pa dang / brag la phyag zhabs kyi rjes 'jog par mdzad pa sogs grub pa'i rtags bstan pa'i tshul bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig yod mod kyang
/ 'dir mang du dogs pas ma bris la/ mtshon pa tsam zhig brjod na/ byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong nyid du bla ma lhas rjes su bzung zhing grub pa'i rtags mtshan bstan
pa'i tshul ni/ rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i slob dpon padma'i rnam thar gyi mjug tu 'di ltar 'byung ste/ grub pa'i gnas mchog byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brang rdzong gi rje btsun
rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gyi gzims phug khams gsum zil gnon du spros med kyi dge sbyor ci yang bgyis pa'i tshe/ rgyal gyi zla ba'i nyer lnga'i nub mo rmi lam du sngags
'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung mgur zhig tu/ dben gnas byas 'gyur dpal ri padma 'od/ /sa lo 'jam pa'i rdo rje pad 'byung dngos/ /chu rnams chu mig byang chub bdud
rtsi'i chu/ /za nyal 'chag gi rnal 'byor lus sems bde/ /zhes gsungs pa de dran pas rkyen byas nas/ byas 'gyur gyi ri 'di nyid zangs mdog dpal gyi ri bo dang / gzims phug
de padma 'od kyi gzhal yas khang dngos lta bur gyur pa'i dbus na/ padma'i sdong po yangs shing rgya che ba'i steng du seng ge chen po brgyad kyis bteg pa'i rin po che gser
gyi khri sna tshogs padma dang zla ba'i gdan gyi steng du/ ngo bo rtsa ba'i bla ma yin pa la rnam pa slob dpon rin po che padma 'byung gnas kyi sku blta bas chog mi shes
pa mtshan dang dpe byad kyis brgyan pa'i mtha' skor du/ /rigs 'dzin grub pa'i dbang phyug brgyud pa dang bcas pa bzhugs pa'i

nang nas nam mkha'i snying po dang bdud 'joms rdo rje gnyis gsal zhing / gzhan rnams 'od kyi rnam pa 'dra ba res mthong / res mi mthong ba'i rnam pa can/ yi dam zhi khro rnams
kyi nang nas gur drag dang yang phur gnyis gsal zhing / gzhan rnams gong bzhin/ mkha' 'gro rnams kyi nang nas bde ba'i rdo rje gsal te rigs 'dzin brgyud pa'i zla la 'dug
gzhan rnams gong bzhin/ chos skyong rnams kyi nang nas bram gzugs dang ming don mi 'phrod pa'i khro mo shin tu rngams pa/ phyag g.yas gser gyi spu gri dang / g.yon na
bse'i sgrom bu ser po 'od 'bar ba par bu kha gcod rgyab pa 'dra ba bsnams pa/ dar nag gi gos gser gyi thig le can la sbrul kyi ske rags bcings shing / khram shing sked la
btsugs pa cig 'dug pa de gnyis gsal/ gzhan rnams gong bzhin/ gu ru'i thugs su byon pa'i bud med lnga yang shin tu gsal bar 'dug 'di ni mkha' 'gro sde lnga yin nam snyam/
de la sogs te nyams snang dang 'khrul pa'i bag chags 'dres pa'i snang ba rnam pa sna tshogs snang la rang bzhin med pa me long nang gi gzugs brnyan ltar khra lam me mthong
ba la brten nas/ dad pa'i spu long rab tu g.yos nas mig nas mchi ma lhung zhing lus kyis phyag du ma zhig btsal/ ngag gis spyir gsol 'debs du ma dang / sgos blo chos
su 'gro zhing chos lam du 'gro nges pa de 'khrul pa dang bral ba'am/ ma bral yang ye shes su rtogs pa khyad par skye ba dang tshe rabs thams cad du khyed kyi zhabs drung
du skye ste/ rigs 'dzin bzhi'i go 'phang thob nges

pa zhig khyed mkhyen zhes phur tshugs su gsol ba 'debs kyi 'dug pas/ gu ru rin po che de nyid dges pa'i rnam 'gyur du ma zhig mdzad de/ de nyid kyi thugs ka nas 'od zer sna
lnga 'ja' tshon lta bu zhig bdag gi snying gar thim pa'i snang ba byung bas/ de'i rkyen gyis nyi ma yang shar te byas 'gyur gyi lung pa thams cad 'od kyis gang nas 'dug
pa dang / gnyid sad de shin tu phongs pa cig byung / de ltar rmis pa'i rkyen gyis slob dpon rin po che rje 'bangs nyer lnga rnams la gsol ba 'debs pa'i tshigs bcad gcig kyang
byas yod ces rtsa ba'i bla ma sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen dang dbyer med pa'i slob dpon rin po che dang / gzhan yang rigs 'dzin rig pa'i bla ma
brgyud pa rnams dang / yi dam zhi khro rdo rje'i chos skyong / mkha' 'gro sde lnga sogs zhal gzigs shing / gdams pa dang rjes su bstan pa mang po nod par bdag nyid chen po
rang nyid kyi zhal gyis bzhes pa 'di ni shin tu yid ches pa'i gnas yin zhing / de dus nyin par sku 'chag pa'i slad du byas 'gyur gyi shar gyi mchod rten la zhabs bskor
la phebs pa'i tshe/ dgon pa'i sprin zam gyi 'og tsam gyi brag lam na yod pa'i zhabs rjes 'di dang / da lta mchod khang na bzhugs pa'i rdo skas kyi sen la byung ba'i zhabs
rjes 'di gnyis kyang 'jog par mdzad pa yin no/ /gzhan yang byang pa chos rgyal chen po'i phyag na yod pa'i slob dpon padma'i gter sku tshe chu ma la gsol ba 'debs par mdzad
pa na/ de las tshe chu dngul chu lta bu skya sram gyis rje nyid kyi phyag mtheb kyi steng du dngos su byung ba

dang / mdor na nang du ting nge 'dzin gyi rtogs pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' bas mngon shes dang rdzu 'phrul sogs thogs pa med pa dang ldan pa zhig ste/ dper mtshon na lan
cig kho bo cag gis bdag nyid chen po 'di byas 'gyur rdo rje'i brag rdzong na bzhugs skabs shig zhabs drung du mjal bar phyin pa na/ thugs dges pa'i ngang nas nyin rang
por gsung gleng mang du mdzad de nyi ma phyi mor song ba na gsung las/ do nub 'dir bsdad na snyam pa tsam 'dug ste skyed lhas mgon khang du bskang gso'i grabs byas pa sogs
brel ba'i stabs kyis 'gro ba shar tshe/ lam bar la bca' ga dag po gyis/ lhag par byas 'gyur gyi mdun gyi bla ma do par ma slebs bar rlung 'tshub shin tu che ba byung dogs
yod pas de bar bzabs dgos so/ /de nas rlung po gtan 'ong ba med do zhes gsung byung ba ji ltar bka' stsal pa bzhin kho bo cag 'khor bcas byas 'gyur nas chas tsam nas bzung
glo bur du rlung chen po cher langs nas/ byas 'gyur gyi mdun gyi bla ma do pa zer ba der ma slebs bar du rlung po shin tu che bas mi rta kun la nyen che ba tsam byung
zhing / de nas rlung po rnams nyal gyi zhi ba la sogs bdag nyid chen po ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin byung bas bla ma'i gsung la yid ches kyi dad pa dbang med du skyes shing
/ gzhan yang 'phral gyi mdzad spyod ya ma zung so skye'i blos dpag par dka' ba du ma zhig mdzad pa'i sgo nas kyang sus kyang ma thul ba'i 'jig rten na grags pa can kun kyang
'dar bar mdzad nus pa dang / mdor na gong du bstan pa ltar gyi grub

pa'i mtshan ma bsam gyis mi khyab pas stod mnga' ris skor gsum/ bar dbus gtsang gi sa cha phal cher dang / de'i nang nas kyang zab phu'i gnas chen rnams su yang yang ston par
mdzad pa sogs gang la bsams kyang nges pa'i don du rdo rje'i 'chang chen po nyid las gzhan du ma 'das mod/ gdul bya'i snang ngo tsam du yang slob dpon chen po padma'i
rnam sprul lam/ rjes su bzung nges pa'i mthu stobs nus pa'i mnga' bdag can zhig yin pa la the tshom bya mi dgos pa yin te/ de bzhin gyi zhal bzhes bdag nyid chen po rang
nyid kyis kyang mdzad par snang ste/ dam pa 'di nyid dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim par nye ba'i spre'u'i lo hor zla drug bdun gyi skabs su nged rang dang sa skyar mjal dus
shin tu dges pa'i ngang nas nged rang dpon slob thugs yid gcig tu 'dres pa'i legs lam la brten nas sngar su la yang ma gnang ba'i tshe sgrub chig brgyud ma gnyis dang
/ lam zab bla ma'i rnal 'byor zab khyad can sogs stsal ba'i tshe/ spyir thugs dkyil nas gzhal ba'i 'di phyir phan pa'i bslab bya du ma dang / lhag par bstan pa'i rtsa ba
gdan sa chen po'i lugs gnyis kyi 'dzin skyong spel gsum rnams 'chugs mi 'chugs khyed rang la rag las pas gang spyi'i spang blang 'di bzhin gyis shig pa sogs bka' stsal ba'i
mod la/ nga ni slob dpon padma rang mkhyen bsam pa 'di kho na ma gtogs gzhan nyams len gang yang byed rgyu med ces gsungs pa dang / yang rje 'di'i gsung rtsom rang rig
dbang bskur gyi sgom tshul gcig shes kun grol zhes bya ba'i mjug tu/ padmas rjes bzung

ban rgan mgo dkar ba/ /zhes dang / dris lan bstan pa rgyas byed kyi mjug tu yang / padmas rjes bzung ri khrod pa/ /byas 'gyur sgrub chen zhes byas bris/ /zhes gsungs pa sogs
mang du 'byung bas so/ /gzhan yang bla ma mchog gi lung bstan khyad par can yang brnyes pa'i tshul ni/ rje 'di sku na gzhon nu'i dus su sngags 'chang chen po'i gsung las/
bsod nams dbang po 'di ma 'ongs pa'i dus su dbus gtsang mnga' ris sogs rgyal khams thams cad kyi bla mar gyur nas 'gro ba ma lus pa dbang du 'dus pa'i mthu stobs la kun
gyi 'gran zla dang bral ba zhig 'byung ngo zhes lung bstan pa ltar mthu stobs dang nus pa stobs kyi mgon po birWa pa dang dbyer ma mchis shing / gang gi zhal gyi dkyil
'khor mthong ba tsam gyis kyang gdul bya thams cad dbang du 'du ba zhig yin la/ de lta bu'i grub pa'i dbang phyug chen po de nyid kyi nang du ting nge 'dzin bsam gyis mi
khyab pa las ma g.yos bzhin du mkhas pa'i bya ba rnam gsum gyi nang nas 'chad pa nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis gdul bya'i blo gros kyi padmo rab tu gsal bar mdzad pa'i tshul ni/
bdag nyid chen po 'dis rje btsun sa skya pa'i yab chos thun mong ma yin pa yang phur gnyis dang / bde kye gsang gsum sogs kyi dbang byin rlabs/ rjes gnang lung la sogs pa
du ma zhig stsal ba'i sgo nas skal ldan gyi slob ma'i tshogs kyang bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig bskrun par mdzad cing / dngos dang brgyud pa'i gdul bya rnams kyi don du sngon
med pa'i legs bshad kyi tshogs gsar du mdzad pa yang dges pa rdo

rje'i sgrub thabs kyi rnam bshad/ gsung ngag gi khrid yig slob dpon rin po che padma'i rnam thar sogs dang / gzhan yang gdams pa'i skor du ma dang gnas chen rnams kyi bstod
pa/ rtsa ba'i bla ma sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i bstod pa dang / gsol 'debs kyi skor la sogs pa rtsom pa sdeb legs kyi gsung rab kyang mang du mdzad de rgyal ba'i
bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal bar mdzad pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i grub pa'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i skyes chen de nyid dgung lo drug cu re gsum du phebs par nye ba na/ zhing 'di'i
gdul bya de tsam gyis rdzogs nas zhing khams gzhan du gzhan don rgya che ba la dgongs te/ nyid kyi gsung las/ kho bo ni snga mo nas kyis bsams pa bzhin da myur du rgya
gar la 'gro nges pas de'i phyag g.yog gi 'os rnams kyang gang zag 'di dang 'di zhes bya ba dag mo brtag byas pa'i phyug pa rnams la khrid rtsis yin gsung ba sogs dag pa'i
zhing du myur du phebs pa la thugs rtse gtad kyang bdag cag ltos bcas rnams kyi sems bsrung ba'i phyir yul khams gzhan du nye bar phebs pa'i gsung yang dang yang du 'byon
par mdzad cing / de lta bu'i skabs nas gdan sa chen por rgyun mi thung tsam zhig bzhugs pa'i dgongs pa yod kyang / rtse gdong nas spyan 'dren gyi pho nya nan chen byung
ba la brten nas zhu shin tu dka' yang mthar zhal bzhes gnang nas spre'u lo zla ba bdun pa'i tshes bcu dgu'i tho rangs chibs kyi kha lo sgyur bar mdzad pa'i tshes bco brgyad
dang / khyad par bcu dgu'i chibs thog tu khel bar nye ba'i tshe/ nged rang zhabs drung du yun ring bsdad nas

bslab bya mtha' dag zhus pa'i tshe/ spyir 'das ma 'ongs kyi bka' stsal lung bstan mtha' yas pa zhig gnang nas/ de rnams gsungs pa'i rjes su da ni zhabs dbang bka' bsgo zhig
kyang byed pa yin no gsungs te/ chos skyong rnams la bka' bsgo rgyas par mdzad cing / de nas bzhugs gdan nas bzhengs te/ des na nged rang khu dbon rang 'dod phugs su 'tshab
pa'i bdud sprul tsho'i zer stabs kyi dbang du ma song pa'i bstan pa bsam pa zhig cis kyang dgos pa 'dug pas nged kyis kyang khyed rang dpon slob tshor dbu 'don du gang
'gyur zhu ba 'di ka kha zhe med pas/ nged kyi grogs mchog chos rje la yang mgo 'don du spyan byams pa zhig cis kyang mdzad dgos so zhes gsung byung bas/ rang nyid rtag
'dzin ches pa nas ci gsung ba yin/ sngar nas nged kyi bla ma 'di 'di lta bu'i gsung 'jebs pa che btsun yul gnyan su la yang mi gnang ba la/ da lan nged lta bu'i slob ma'i
tha chung shig la de lta bu gsung ba ci rang yin snyam pa'i sems dga' la skyo ba zhig byung ba phyis bsams pas/ rje nyid myur du dag pa'i zhing du phebs pa'i dgongs pa de
dus nas gtad pa'i gsung du 'dug cing / de nas bdag nyid chen po chibs thog tu 'khyon nas rgyang tsam phebs skyel zhus nas dpon slob gyes kar/ rje nyid kyis chibs pa g.yon
phyogs su bsgor mdzad nas phyag g.yon pa mchog sbyin gyi phyag rgya lta bu zhig mdzad de/ nged rang tsho myur du mjal yong bas de bar thugs bzhugs spro ba mdzod cig gsung
byung bas yid 'phrang ba la tshad med pa zhig byung nas/ da

dung nar tsam phebs skyel la 'gro lags zhus pas/ da ni 'di rang du bzhugs pa legs/ phur sgrub kyi tshogs dpon la 'byon mi dgos pa e yin/ tshogs dung kyang phyis 'gro nyan yod
do zhes gsung byung ba bzhin dgongs pa dang sbyar la tshur log de nas rje nyid kyis rim gyis chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur te rtse gdong bla brang du chag phebs nas bzhugs pa'i
skabs su/ gzhan ngor sku cung zad bsnyung ba'i tshul bstan cing zhing khams gzhan du 'byon par nye ba na/ de'i lnga ltas su 'jig rten gyi khams su rlung 'tshub chen pos
sa gzhi g.yo ba lta bu la sogs pa ltas ngan pa dpag tu med pa yang byung zhing / de'i dus su rje 'dis rgyun du chibs pa mdzad pa'i nor bu 'phur shes bya bde glo bur du
shi ba na/ rje'i gsung gis da mi rgan dang rta rgan mnyam du 'gro ba yin zhes gsungs pa dang / gzhan yang sku 'khor rnams la sngon sngags 'chang chen po zhing gshegs pa'i
tshe sku gdung la zhabs tog mdzad tshul sogs 'phros gtam gyi tshul gyis zhing khams gzhan du gshegs pa'i gsung 'ba' zhig byon pa na/ zhabs 'bring ba rnams mya ngan gyi
khang bur zhugs par gyur te/ sku rim sogs rgya chen po bsgrub cing / gsol sman sogs kyi 'phrod rten gang mang zhig phul kyang sku la skyed du mngon pa zhig ma byung ba na/
de nas bdag nyid chen po 'di gzhan snang du sku dub pa'i tshul bstan kyang / gsung las/ nged rang gi dngos po rgyal rtse dang rtse gdong sogs phyogs na yod pa rnams myur
du dge sdings rang du sgril cig de rnams kyi 'gro sa cig stod phyogs ya gi na yod pa yin no zhes gsungs

pa bzhin/ rje nyid kyi zhabs 'bring pa chen po chos rje kun dga' bkra shis kyis kyang phyag len la thebs par bgyis pa na/ de nas rje btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug bka' drin gzhal
du med pa de nyid kyis gdan sa chen po'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa thugs yul du bcangs pa'i skus mi lcogs bzhin du rtse gdong nas dge sdings bkra shis bsam
'grub tu chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur te/ bya lo hor zla dang po'i yar tshes la dge sdings chos kyi pho brang ga la ba der chag phebs te/ lam bar rnams dang ji srid bsnyung
ba'i bar du thams cad du thugs dam zab mo'i rim pa rnams la rtag 'grus su mdzad pa'i ngang nas/ rgya gar slob dpon shrI sidha byon nas rdzogs chen gyi lta ba'i sgro 'dogs
bcad pa sogs de ltar dag pa'i gzigs snang bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'char bzhin pa dang bcas/ zla ba de ka'i tshes bcu slob dpon chen po padma 'byung gnas nyid bod yul 'dir
dngos su 'byon par nges pa'i dus bzang po de nyid kyi tshe/ nam mkha' la 'ja' 'od dang lha'i me tog gi char sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas/ le lo can rnams brtson
'grus la bskul ba dang / rtag 'dzin can rnams nges 'byung bskyed pa'i phyir/ snyigs dus kyi grub pa mchog gi ded dpon 'khrul zhig yongs kyi gtsug rgyan dam pa de nyid
dgung lo drug cu re gsum du phebs pa'i tshe dge sdings bkra shis bsam 'grub nyid du gzugs kyi sku chos kyi dbyings su bsdu ba'i tshul bstan to/ /de ltar tshes bcu'i snga
dro nas bcu gnyis kyi tho rangs kyi bar du 'od gsal ma bu 'dres pa'i zung

'jug bde ba chen po'i ngang du mnyam par bzhag ste/ de nas tshes bcu gnyis kyi tho rangs kyi cha la babs pa na/ 'od gsal las zung 'jug gi skur bzhengs nas dbu'i gtsug tor mchog
tu 'phags te/ dpa' bo dang rnal 'byor ma'i tshogs bsam gyis mi khyab pas bsu ba dang bcas dag pa'i zhing bde ba can zangs mdog dpal gyi ri ga la ba der/ slob dpon chen
po nyid kyi sprul pa sprul gzhi la thim pa'i tshul gyis gshegs par gyur to/ /de ltar bdag nyid chen po de nyid zhing khams gzhan du gshegs pa'i tshul bstan nas zhag gsum
lon pa'i tshes bcu gnyis kyi nyin kho bo cag dge sdings bkra shis bsam grub tu 'byor skabs/ de'i nyin gang nam mkha' dwangs pa la me tog gi char dang / khyad par 'ja'
'od kyi gur khang sngon chad gangs can gyi khrod du ma byung zhing mi srid pa lta bu'i ri mo ngo mtshar can gyis nam mkha'i khams thams cad khyab pa ni nyi ma ma nub kyi
bar byung bas kun kyang dad gus kyi ba spu ches cher g.yos par gyur cing / de nas ngos cag gis sku gdung rin po che'i drung du dkar me zhal zas yon chab rnams tshar du dngar
ba sogs mchod pa'i bye brag rgya mi chung bar bsham ste/ lam zab bla ma rin 'byung la thun du bcad nas maNDal dang lus kyis phyag bya ba/ ngag gis gsol 'debs dang bshags
pa smon lam la sogs pa grangs med pa zhig nyi ma du ma'i bar du bgyis skabs/ sku gdung rin po che las dri bzang thul ba sogs ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang / khyad par
sdig pa dag pa'i rtags shin tu che ba mngon gyur du byung ste/ de'i dus su kho bo cag gis rje 'di nyid

la gsol 'debs bshags pa dang bcas pa'i tshigs bcad cig kyang brtsams yod do/ /de lta bu'i yongs su 'dzin pa chen po de nyid gzhan ngor gzugs sku chos dbyings su thim pa'i tshul
bstan mod kyang / dad ldan gyi bu slob rnams kyis gsol ba btab na nyams dang rmi lam gyi tshul du zhal gyi dkyil 'khor bstan nas 'bral ba med par byin gyis rlobs par
nges te/ rje nyid kyi slob ma'i tha chung ngos cag lta bu la mtshon na'ang / khyi lo dpal sa skya'i lha khang chen mor gzhi byes kyi chos nyan pa nyis brgya lhag tsam la
gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag nyams myong steng nas 'chad rgyu kho bo la med mod kyang / tshig bshad gang shes kyi ngos zla ba gsum tsam gyi
bar du smin rgyas 'chad skabs tho rangs kyi cha zhig rmi lam du/ lha khang chen mo'i steng gi mgon khang khyad par can de nyid du 'jam mgon grub pa'i dpa' bo dbang po'i
mtshan can de nyid gsal por byon te/ dpal rdo rje nag po chen po gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad/ lha bcu gnyis ma/ lha lnga ma rnams kyi dbang bskur dus gcig la stsal ba snyam
byed pa de'i ngang nas thugs dges pa'i mdangs du ma zhig mdzad de/ khyed la rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal gyis dbang bskur mdzad dus kyi khyor chu'i snod 'khrul
med dung chos ngo mtshar can yod pa de nged la dgos pa 'dug ces gsung byung ba na/ e ma ngo mtshar che/ dung chos de lag na yod pa'i 'phros zur tsam yang rje'i sku 'khor
ba sogs su dang yang 'phros ma byung bar/ 'di bzhin gyi bka' stsal phebs pa ni thugs

mkhyen gyis dgongs pa kho na las gzhan du ma 'das so snyam pa'i dad pa ches cher skyes pa'i mod la gnyid sad byung bas/ rang gi dad mos kyis ma bslus na rje grub thob kyi gtsug
rgyan de nyid kyi thugs rje la nye ring med par 'dug snyam pa'i yid ches dang dga' spro ci yang zhig thob pa lags so/ /de nas bdag nyid chen po'i sku gdung rin po che
de nyid re zhig dge sdings bkra shis bsam 'grub tu mchod rten khang bu brtsegs pa zhig byas nas bzhugs su gsol te/ de'i drung du rdo rje 'dzin pa bcu phrag lhag tsam zhig
gis dus dang rgyun gyi mchod pa rgya chen po rgyun ma chad par phul zhing / de nas rje btsun chos kyi rgyal po de nyid kyi dgongs pa rdzogs thabs su dbus gtsang gi ljongs
kyi dgon gnas nyis brgya lhag tsam zhig tu mang ja 'gyed bcas/ bsdo rten tshan grangs sogs rgya dpangs shin tu che bar bsgrubs shing / de dang dus mtshungs par gdan sa
chen por dge 'dun brgya phrag la nye ba tsam zhig gis rdo rje theg pa bla na med pa'i dkyil 'khor du ma zhal phye ste sgrub mchod yun ring phul zhing / de nas dgongs rdzogs
kyi dngos gzhi la gdan sa chen po'i gtsug lag khang thams cad du dkar me snyan dar sogs mchod pa'i bye brag tshar du dngar ba du ma dang / bla ma slob dpon/ las chen
sogs zur 'bul 'os pa rnams la tshan grangs dpangs mtho ba/ gzhi byes kyi dge 'dun skye bo'i tshogs dang bcas pa khri phrag tu longs pa la mang ja gdan non zab ma'i steng
/ zang zing gi sbyin gtong blo'i ra ba las 'das pa zhig bsgrubs pas/ skya ser tshogs che zhing grangs mang ba la brten sbyin gtong

gi bya ba rnams nyin gang gcig la mi zin pa 'dug go zhes gleng bar byung yang / rje nyid kyi thugs rje'i rgyun gyi nyi ma sngar bas sum cha tsam gyis ring bar gyur te bya ba
phal cher nyi ma bzhud 'phral tshun la grub pas kun kyang ngo mtshar du gyur pa yin la/ de lta bu'i dgongs rdzogs shin tu rgya che ba gzhi byes thams cad du blos mi 'khyud
pa lta bu bsgrubs pa 'di 'dra ba ni rgan rabs sus kyang mi dran pas/ dus phyis byon pa'i rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rigs kyi dgongs pa rdzogs thabs zhig la 'di kho
na dngos po bzang zhing rgya che ba sogs rgyu mtshan du ma'i sgo nas ngo mtshar che ba yin no zhes skye bo thams cad mgrin gcig tu sgrogs par gyur cing / de nas yun mi ring
bar rje btsun grub pa'i dbang phyug nyid kyi nang rten du rin po che dngul las grub pa'i rnam rgyal mchod rten rgya dpangs che zhing bzo khyad phun sum tshogs pa dang
ldan pas blta bas chog mi shes pa kun gyi mig gi bdud rtsir gyur pa zhig dang / rje nyid kyi sku tshab gser zangs las grub pa'i sku tshad ma sogs rten bzhengs rnams gegs
med du grub pa na dge sdings chos kyi pho brang nas rje nyid kyi sku gdung yid bzhin gyi nor bu spyan drangs nas dngul gdung rin po che'i gzungs zhugs kyi gtso bor ji srid
bstan pa nam gnas kyi bar du lhar bcas 'gro ba kun gyi bsod nams kyi zhing dam par bzhugs su gsol zhing / gzhan yang gzungs dang byin rlabs kyi rten grangs dang tshad med
pa zhig gis gdung rten rin po che dang sku tshab sogs rten gsar bzhengs rnams la phyur bur bltams pa'i gzungs rdzong tshul

bzhin du phul te/ kho bo cag rdo rje 'dzin pa bcu phrag lhag tsam gyis yi dam kye rdo rje la brten pa'i rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga smin rgyas su bsgrub ste/ sku brnyan ngo mtshar
