can de nyid dbu rtse rnying mar lam 'bras brgyud pa'i khrod la bzhugs su gsol zhing / dngul gdung yid bzhin gyi nor bu dgos 'dod kun 'byung nyid ni gzhi thog bla brang
gi rigs 'dzin bla ma brgyud pa'i pho brang gi sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gdung rten gyi g.yas su mchod pa'i bye brag dpag tu med pa dang bcas nas skye bo su zhig
gis mthong yang dwang 'dod kyi dad pa bla na med pa skyed pa sogs kun gyis mthong na yid mi mthun pa med par bzhugs pa 'di yin no/ /gzhan yang dus rgyun gyi mchod par dge
'dun brgya phrag la nye bas kye rdo rje'i rtsa rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa'i rgyud 'don/ bla ma mchod chog nar mar 'bul ba sogs dang / lo dus kyi dus dran gyi mchod pa la rje
btsun rdo rje bdag med ma'i sgrub mchod gsar 'dzugs bgyis te/ mdor na rang gi lus longs spyod thams cad rje btsun bla ma de nyid dgongs pa chos kyi dbyings su rdzogs pa'i
thabs su ci 'gyur gyi thabs la rtag 'grus su bgyid pa 'di yin no////'dir smras pa/ dus gsum rgyal ba'i spyi gzugs grub dbang rje/ /mthu rtsal nus pa'i mnga' bdag yongs
'dzin khyed/ /dran pa'i mod la slob bu'i tha chung bdag /gdung ba'i gsol 'debs thal lo snyan gsan cig /gang sku padma rA ga'i lhun po la/ /nyi ma bye ba'i 'od zer mdangs
'phro ba'i/ /dges pa'i 'dzum zhal yang yang ston pa de/ /snying nas dran no gsol 'debs byin gyis

rlobs/ /gang gsung lugs gnyis blang dor ji snyed pa/ /ma 'dres gsal la rdzogs par ston mkhas pa'i/ /zil ldan tshangs pa'i dbyangs ltar yid 'phrog pa/ /rna ba'i bdud rtsi de
yang dran pa'i yul/ /khyod thugs zab gsal ting 'dzin sgo brgya la/ /mnyam par 'jog la skad cig g.yo med pa'i/ /de lta'i ngang nas so so'i skal ba dang / /'tshams par gdul
bya skyong mdzad khyod thugs dran/ /'on kyang thun mong snang ba'i gzugs kyi sku/ /chos kyi dbyings su bsdus kyang las dag pa'i/ /gdul bya rnams la 'bral med skyong mdzad
pa/ /'di la kho bo nges shes rnyed pa'i phyir/ /bdag gis byang chub bar gyi skyabs der 'dud/ /de ltar grub mchog dbang po'i mtshan can nyid/ /dran pa'i yid kyi gdung bas
gsol btab pas/ /bla ma padma 'byung gnas dbyer med pa'i/ /dges pa'i tshul gyis rtag tu rjes 'dzin shog /ces kyang shugs 'byung du gsol ba btab pa'o/ /de lta bu'i grub
pa'i dbang phyug chen po de nyid kyi lcam sring mo che ba ni/ rin chen bsod nams bu khrid ces bya ba 'di mnga' ris btsad po'i khab tu phebs nas sras lcam sring gnyis 'khrungs
shing / sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i bka' 'bum phal cher par du bzhengs pa sogs bstan pa'i bya ba rlabs chen du ma mdzad de mnga' ris nyid du sku gshegs so/ /'bring
po ni lha gcig bkra shis sgrol ma ste 'di nyid kyang bsam yas kyi sa skyong chen po'i khab tu phebs nas sras lcam sku mched gnyis 'khrungs shing / slar gdan sa chen
por phebs nas bla brang shar gyi gzim khang du sku

gshegs shing / chung ba ngag dbang bsod nams chos kyi dpal 'dzom bya ba dge bsnyen ma zhig ste gzhon nu la dge sdings su gshegs so/ /yang sngags 'chang bstan pa'i nyi ma kun
dga'i mtshan can gyi btsun mo slar yang gdong dga' ma bkra shis dpal gyi bu khrid ces bya ba khab tu bzhes pa la sras gcig 'khrungs pa ni/ bdag la bka' drin che ba'i bla
ma gsum gyi nang tshan/ /sngon gyi dus su byang chub sems dpa' mkhan po bo dhi sa twa nyid 'gro ba'i mgon po dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan zhes mtshan
yongs su grags par sku'i skye ba bzhes pa de nyid/ slar yang sa skya pa'i gdung rigs su bsams bzhin du byon pa dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang grags pa blo gros rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po zhes mtshan yongs su grags pa de nyid de/ bdag nyid chen po 'di ni yab sngags 'chang bla ma bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po de ni dgung lo bzhi bcu rtsa
bdun du phebs pa chu mo phag gi lo smal po zla ba'i gnam gang gi nyin gdan sa chen po'i nub phyogs gdong dga' rdzong gi yang rtser ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas
bltams pa yin te/ 'di nyid lhums su zhugs pa'i dus su yang yum la mtshan ltas khyad par can du ma byung zhing / bltams pa'i tshe yang mngal gyi dri mas ma gos pa mtshon
pa'i phyir/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po kun dga' snying po ltar grod gtum gyi tshul du legs par 'khrungs shing / 'khrungs ma thag nas byis pa'i spyod pa las 'das pa skyes
bu chen po'i mtshan dang ldan pa zhig yin no zhes thos la/ de nas yon tan gyi phyi mo 'dri klog la sogs pa rnams ni

gzigs pa tsam gyis phyin ci ma log par dgongs shing / yig rigs kyang war dhu/ lanytsa/ rgya mtsho mtha' yig sogs rgya gar gyi yig rigs du ma dang / bod kyi yi ge'i rigs kyang
mi 'dra ba mang po zhig la bdag nyid chen po 'di'i phyag bris rnams las gzugs mdzes shing brda dag pa ni yi ge la sbyangs shing mkhas par grags pa'i skye bo sus kyang
bskrun par nus pa ma yin la/ gzhan yang sbyang tshul ma bstan kyang bzo'i rig byed phul du phyin pa mkhyen pa'i tshul ni/ chos skyong che chung gi sku brnyan sogs nyid kyi
phyag bris mdzad pa'i bris thang ngo mtshar can rnams mthong ba'i tshe/ dus phyis dbus gtsang gi lha bzo ba mkhas par grags pa sus kyang 'gran zla dang bral zhing yongs
la grags pa 'di yin la/ de lta bu'i ngo mtshar ba'i yon tan du ma dang ldan pa'i bdag nyid chen po 'di nyid kyi rmad du byung ba'i rnam par thar pa'i cha shas 'ga' zhig
rang gis brtsams pa'i rje nyid kyi gsol 'debs dang sbyar nas bshad par bya ste/ de yang gsol 'debs kyi mchod brjod ni/rgya gar saM skr-i ta'i skad la bag chags bzhag pa'i
phyir rgya skad du smos pa yin te/ de yang na mo gu ru kIrti ma ti dhwa dza shrI bha dra ye zhes pa de'i don ni/ na mo phyag 'tshal ba/ gu ru bla ma/ kIrti ma ti grags pa
blo gros/ dhwa dza rgyal mtshan/ shrI dpal/ bha dra bzang po/ ye zhes pa gong gi tshig dang 'brel bas te/ des na bla ma grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po la
phyag 'tshal lo zhes pa'o/ /de ltar mchod par brjod nas gsol 'debs dngos kyi don bshad pa la/ de yang skyes

chen dam pa 'di nyid rigs rus khyad par can gyi brgyud du byon pa'i tshul ni/ legs pa'i 'byung gnas bstan pa rin po che/ /gangs ri'i khrod 'dir 'phel zhing rgyas mdzad pa'i/
/phyogs las rnam rgyal rje btsun sa skya pa/ /dbang po'i grangs ldan brgyud par bcas la 'dud/ /ces pas bstan te/ de yang 'gro ba rnams la dge legs phun sum tshogs pa ma
lus pa'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa'i kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i bstan pa dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i yid bzhin gyi nor bu rin po che dang chos mtshungs pa de nyid/ bod yul gangs ri'i
khrod 'dir rab tu 'phel zhing yun du rgyas par mdzad pa'i skyes chen du ma zhig byon pa rnams kyi gtsug rgyan du gyur pa phyogs thams cad las rnam par rgyal ba'i lha rigs
'khon rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rigs zhes yongs su grags pa rnams kyi nang nas kyang ches mchog tu gyur ba snying po rtse mo rgyal mtshan gyi mtshan gyi mtha' can gsum
dang / chos rje khu dbon gnyis te dbang po'i grangs dang ldan pa'i yab sras brgyud pa dang bcas pa rnams ni sngags 'chang bla ma 'di nyid gang las byon pa'i khyad par du
'phags pa'i gdung rabs te/ skyes bu dam pa thams cad la bdag cag lan gcig ma yin pa yang nas yang du dad pas 'dud do zhes pa ste/ de ltar rigs rus khyad par can las byon
pa'i skyes chen dam pa de nyid mtshan mchog gnyis dang ldan pa ste/ de yang thog ma'i mtshan ni/ rje nyid yum las 'khrungs nas yun ring ma lon par sngags 'chang chos kyi
rgyal pos sku pang du bzhes shing dges dges du ma mdzad de/ byis pa 'di pha shul bus zin pa

zhig 'byung zhes ma 'ongs pa mkhyen pa'i lung bstan dang bcas mtshan grags pa blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya bar gsol ba yin no zhes thos la/ de lta bu'i mtshan
de nyid don dang ldan par nges pa'i phyir 'di skad ces bstod de/ grags pas rgya mtsho'i gos can yongs khyab cing / /blo gros bsam yas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan 'dzin/ /dpal
ldan bla ma'i mdzad pa rnam dag mchog /bzang po'i spyod pas 'gro ba skyong la 'dud/ /ces so/ /de lta bu'i skyes chen dam pa de nyid kyi mtshan gyi rnam grangs gnyis pa
ni/ 'jam dbyangs bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya bar slar yang yab rje chos kyi rgyal po nyid kyis gsol bar mdzad pa yin te/ de'i tshul ni rgyal sras grags
pa'i mtshan can 'di 'khrungs nas dgung lo gsum bzhi tsam bzhes pa'i dus shig na cung zad gsung ngag ma bde ba zhig byung ba'i tshe/ sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal por gter
ston chen po chos kyi 'od zer gyis zhu yig phul ba las 'di ltar 'byung ste/ rgyal ba'i sku gsung thugs yon 'phrin las thams cad gcig tu bsdus pa'i ngo bor gyur pa/ sngags
'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i zhabs drung du zhu ba/ drung rams lags la bka' phebs nang ma'i tshul gnang ba'i skor blo ngor shin tu gcags pa byung lags pa dang / zhabs drung
rgyan rin po che 'di nyid longs sku chen po'i zhing du gsang ba'i bdag po phyag na rdo rje dang / 'phags yul du mkhan chen bo dhi sa twa dang / bod yul du dpal ldan bla
ma dam par grags pa de nyid yin par slob dpon padma saM bha wa'i

phyag bris shog ser la mngon sum 'khrul med du 'dug par brten/ bstan pa dang sems can kho na la phan pa dang bde ba ma lus pa'i 'byung gnas yin 'dug lags/ dus re zhig sku'i
cha lugs sngags 'chang 'di ka gnang tshe gangs nas legs tshogs che ba yong snang lags pa dang / lhag pa'i lha jo bo rje btsun 'jam dbyangs kho na dang / de mthun rdo rje
gzhon nu la gnang tshe bar skabs sku tshe'i bar chad sel ba dang / phyi nang gi dgra 'dre mtha' dag 'dul ba la bsngags pa dang / chos skyong yang mgon po gur zhal gnyis
khyad par med kyi nang nas/ mgon po gnyan mgon gcig nyid du 'brel chags pa gnang ba'i gsang sgrub kyi tshul gnang ba dang / gsung ngag snga sor sku grib la brten pa zhig
byung ba snang tshod du 'dug pa/ thog mar khro bo dme pa brtsegs pa'i bsnyen pa 'bum phrag gsum pa zhig sku mtshams bcad nas gnang ba dang / de mthun thugs dam thams cad
kyi sngon la brgya rtsa re gnang tshe 'phral 'phral dwangs bskyed che ba yong lags pa dang / lhag par dam sel dang sku grib la 'dzem pa gnang tshe/ sku tshe mdzad 'phrin
gnyis ka la yang shin tu phan pa zhig mngon pas dgongs pa'i dbyings kho nar bzhugs pa gnang zhing / don du bstan pa rin po che la phan zhing snyan grags kyang mi chung tsam
yong ba sogs gang spyi'i gnas tshul drung rams pas 'bul ba yod pa dgongs dbyings rin po cher bzhugs pa gnang ba mkhyen mkhyen lags/ tshes bdun la 'bring po gzhis dga'
nas snyel so'i tshul du phul ba'i zhu yig ces pa'i zhu yig ngag ma zhib cha dang bcas sngags 'chang

bstan pa'i mnga' bdag chen po'i zhabs drung du 'byor ma thag gang gi mtshan bsgyur ba dang bstun nas dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i sku 'dra phyag nas ma yar lung pa seng ge rgyal
mtshan gyis bzhengs pa de dang / mgon po'i rdo sku dpal ldan bla ma'i thugs dam ma gnyis rje nyid la stsal te/ rgyan mchog khyod kyis dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i rnam 'phrul
yin pa don dang ldan pa zhig cis kyang bya dgos so zhes gsung bzhin dus rgyun par yang nyams ldan gyi tshul gyis de ltar yang yang du gsung 'byon pa cig yod ces yab
rje chos kyi rgyal po nyid kyi gsung las thos pa lags/ don gyi dbang de nyid kyi phyir 'di skad ces bstod de/ mahA lo tsA bsod nams rgyal mtshan zhes/ /yongs grags dpal ldan
bla ma bzang po de'i/ /rnam par sprul zhes 'gro ba yongs la grags/ /'brel tshad don ldan bla ma'i zhabs la 'dud/ /de ltar don gnyis phun sum tshogs pa'i ston pa rdzogs
pa'i sangs rgyas dang thugs rgyud gcig gis bsdus pa'i sprul pa'i skyes chen dam pa de nyid kyis gdul bya gzhan gyi snang ngor/ yongs 'dzin 'brel tshad don ldan du ma'i
zhabs zung bsten pa sogs kyi sgo nas gsan pa rgya mtsho'i pha rol tu son pa'i tshul ni 'di ltar thos te/ de yang / 'khrul pa kun zhig ngag gi dbang po sogs/ /mkhas grub bla
ma du mas rjes su bzung / /zhes pa ltar/ snyigs dus kyi rgyal ba gnyis pa dpal sa skya pa chen po sngags 'chang ngag gi dbang po kun dga' rin chen bkra shis grags pa rgyal
mtshan dpal bzang po'i drung du dam pa'i chos gsan pa'i rnam grangs

la/ thog mar rje btsun sa skya pa rnams kyi yab chos thun mong ma yin pa bcom ldan 'das rdo rje gzhon nu'i smin byed kyi dbang bskur ba lan grangs du ma zhig dang / gzhan yang
yang dag mar me dgu pa'i dbang / gur drag gi dbang / 'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i dbang / gsang 'dus mi bskyod pa'i dbang / dges pa rdo rje'i rgyu dus kyi dbang dang
/ lam dus kyi dbang / bdag med lha mo bco lnga'i dbang rnams dang / gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i dbang khrid yongs su rdzogs pa cha lag 'ga' zhig dang
/ lam 'bras glegs bam/ gsung ngag bla ma brgyud pa'i rnam thar rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa/ yang rjes gnang gi rnam grangs la/ phur pa drag po sgrol ba'i rjes gnang /
gur mgon lha brgyad/ lcam dral/ zhing skyong chen po/ dur khrod bdag po/ dmag zor rgyal mo/ mon pa ming sring / pu tra'i zur bka'/ dkar bdud rnams kyi rjes gnang sogs rjes
su gnang ba'i rim pa du ma dang / yang lung gi skor la/ rje btsun gong ma lnga'i bka' 'bum/ rdo rje 'chang kun dga' bzang po/ rgyal tshab dam pa kun dga' dbang phyug kun
mkhyen bsod nams seng ge yongs 'dzin dkon mchog 'phel ba/ 'jam dbyangs sangs rgyas rin chen/ sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa rnams kyi bka' 'bum yongs rdzogs kyi lung dang /
gzhan yang rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum po ti dang po'i lung dang / rgyal sras thogs med kyi bka' 'bum thor bu ba rnams kyi lung dang / jo bo'i chos chung brgya
rtsa/ sngags 'chang nyid kyi bka'

'bum sogs zab rgyas lung gi tshogs bgrang ba las 'das pa zhig gsan cing / lugs gnyis kyi bka' drin tshad med pa bskyangs pa la brten bla ma thams cad kyi nang nas kyang mchog
tu 'dzin par mdzad cing / dad gus gdung shugs sogs kyang gzhan las ches che bas/ dgos byed khyad par can gyi dus gsol ba btab pa na/ phra rags kyi bya ba gang la yang
sngags 'chang nyid nyams dang mnal lam gyi tshul gyis gsal bar byon nas lung bstan gyi tshogs rnams 'di dang 'di gyis shig par ston par mdzad pa yin la/ nyid kyis bzhengs
pa'i bla ma brgyud pa'i bris thang ji snyed pa rnams la yang bris thang de nyid kyi grangs dang mnyam pa'i sngags 'chang nyid yab sras 'bral med kyi tshul du bkod pa'i mthong
ba tsam gyis yid 'khul ba'i phyi nang gi rten 'brel zab mo la dgongs pa'i zhal bkod khyad par can du ma mdzad pa dang / khyad par dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung
brgyud dang bcas pa'i 'dzin skyong gi 'khur gyi sku dang thugs yid dub pa sogs ngal ba brgya phrag dang du bzhes pa'i sgo nas mdor na ci mdzad thams cad sngags 'chang chos
kyi rgyal po'i dgongs pa rdzogs thabs kho nar dmigs pa las gzhan du dgongs pa'i thugs cung zad kyang mi mnga' ba ni/ kho bos yang dang yang du nges shes rnyed pa lags pas
sngags 'chang yab sras gnyis ka la bcos ma ma yin pa'i dad pa snying nas skyes pa yin no/ /gzhan yang bdag nyid chen po 'dis mus chen dkon mchog rgya mtsho zhes bya ba
sems dpa' chen po 'phrin las kyi mnga' bdag de nyid kyi drung du

gsung ngag rin po che lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams pa zab mo cha lags yongs rdzogs rgyab chos kyi lung dang bcas pa dang / gzhan yang tshe dpag med dkar po/ mi g.yo ba
dkar sngon gnyis/ sgrol dkar/ rnam rgyal 'joms gnyis/ phyag rdor u tsa/ ri khrod ma/ dzaM ser nag gnyis/ rnam sras rta bdag brgyad/ dmar po skor gsum/ seng ge sgra/ sor
phreng rnams kyi rjes gnang sogs rjes gnang zur bka' du ma dang so so'i yig cha gsar rnying gi lung dang bcas pa rnams gsan/ yang chos kyi rje nam mkha' dpal bzang po'i drung
du rdo rje phreng ba'i dbang / spyod rgyud dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis kyi dbang / gshed dmar lha lnga'i dbang / mgon po lha bcu gnyis kyi dbang / kye rdor bka' babs bzhi'i
dbang sogs smin byed dbang gi rnam grangs bcu phrag gnyis lhag pa dang / rjes gnang gi bka' srol chen po gnyis su grags pa sgrub thabs brgya rtsa dang / rgya mtsho gnyis
kyi rjes gnang yongs su rdzogs pa dang / gzhan yang sher phyin dkar mo'i rjes gnang sogs zur bka' bcu phrag gnyis su bdun gyis lhag pa dang / mgon pod gser pod du grags
pa'i lung / rje dkon mchog lhun grub kyi bka' 'bum po ti phyi ma gnyis dang / rje thar rtse ba rang gi gsung rtsom 'ga' zhig sogs lung gi rigs du ma zhig dang / gzhan yang
khrid dang byin rlabs sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig gsan cing / gzhan yang gcen 'jam pa'i dbyangs bsod nams dbang po'i drung du yang gsung ngag rin po che dang / dbang
lung rjes gnang gi skor sogs

'ga' zhig nod par mdzad la/ mdor na bdag nyid chen po 'di nyid ni rang nyid yon tan kun dang ldan yang rtag tu dman cha 'dzin pa la thugs gcig tu gzhol ba'i gang zag gzhan
gyi skyon nas gsungs pa zhabs drung du yun ring du bsdad pa sus kyang thos ma myong ba yin zhing / mkhas btsun bzang gsum dang ldan pa'i skyes bu dam pa gang na su bzhugs
kyang bla mar bkur ba'i thugs 'dun rgyun chags su mdzad pa yin te/ dus phyis nyid kyi gsung las/ da ni nged kyi bla ma phal cher zhing gzhan du gshegs nas mi bzhugs 'dug
pas/ tshe mjug 'di la nged rang blo gtad thub pa'i bla ma zhal bzhugs shig dgos pa 'dug pa la/ gzhan ni 'os rigs gang nas btsal kyang mi 'dug cing / rin po che mus chen
sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan 'di nged rang yid ches shing gdeng khel ba'i bla ma zhig 'dug pas/ khong gis gnang grogs mdzad na nged rang 'dod chos 'dra zhu ba la brtag pa sogs
byed dgos mi 'dug ces bdag cag zhabs drung na gnas pa kun la yang yang du gsung ba sku 'khor ba kun gyi thugs la gsal ba de yin la/ de ltar bdag nyid chen po 'di nyid sku
gzhon nu nyid nas yon tan mtha' dag ma bslabs pa yang ngang gis rdzogs pa'i tshul gyis/ la la rgyal po'i bu bzhin lhun gyis grub/ /ces gsungs pa'i don dang ldan par gyur
cing / mchod 'os kun la gus pa dang / skye bo gzhan su zhig la'ang khong khro ba tsam yang mi mnga' zhing / kun gyi yid 'dzin pa la mkhas pas 'di ni 'gran zla dang bral
ba'i skyes bu chen po zhig 'byung nges par

snang ngo zhes dus mtshungs pa'i gang zag thams cad rje nyid kyi snyan grags brjod pas dus rtag tu brel bar gyur cing / de de'i skabs nas rje btsun yab kyi chag phyir bkris
te sa skya pa'i yab chos yang phur gnyis/ bde kye gsang gsum/ yo ga bya spyod dang bcas pa/ chos skyong che chung sogs kyis bsdus pa'i dbang khrid lung man ngag rgyud dang
gzhung phran mtha' dag sogs la sbyangs pa mthar phyin pa mdzad cing / tha na de dag gi cho ga'i cha lag phra mo bris thig dbyangs gsum tshun chad la yang rje 'di nyid
las byang chub pa sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i zhal slob kyi khrod du gzhan ma byung bar snang zhing / de nas rje nyid dgung lo brgyad du phebs pa na/ bdag nyid chen
po sa skya paNDi ta chen po'i chos kyi khri ga la ba der rje btsun gcen dang lhan cig tu yab rje chos kyi rgyal po'i rgyal tshab bstan pa'i bdag po chen por mnga' gsol te/
dus de tsam nas bzung ste dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pas thog drangs/ spyi dang bye brag gi bstan pa nyin mo ltar gsal bar gyur pa'i dbu tshugs
pa yin la/ de lta bu'i skabs nas bdag nyid chen po 'di nyid kyis yab rje nyid kyi sku dang grib ma'i tshul du 'bral med du bzhugs bzhin pa'i ring nas/ yang phur bde kye
gsang gsum chos skyong che chung sogs yi dam zhi khro du ma dang / rdo rje'i chos skyong rnams kyi dus dang grangs kyi bsnyen pa mthar phyin par mdzad pa'i mtshan ma khyad
par can brnyes pa'i tshul ni 'og tu 'chad la/ de nas rje nyid dgung lo bcu phrag gnyis tsam du phebs pa na/ mdo phyogs gtso bor gyur pa'i bstan pa'i rnam

gzhag mdzad par bzhed de/ bdag nyid chen po sa skya paNDi ta'i sdom rigs gnyis dang / tshad ma kun btus la sogs pa phyogs glang gis mdzad pa rnams dang / rig pa'i gtsug rgyan
chos kyi grags pa'i rnam 'grel rnam nges rnams te sde bdun sogs gzhung lugs chen po bdun cu rtsa bdun tsam zhig la bshad pa'i dga' ston dang / sbyor bkod sogs kyis bstan
pa'i rnam gzhag ngo mtshar phun sum tshogs pa mdzad/ de ltar rje btsun lung gi chos kyi rgya mtsho chen po nyid kyi sku gsung thugs kyi ngo mtshar ba'i mdzad pa rnams
la sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i yang thugs rangs par gyur te/ rgyan mchog 'di ma 'ongs pa'i dus su dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa gong 'phel du
byas nas/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i srog shing lta bur gyur pa zhig 'byung zhes bstod bkur bsngags gsum du ma mdzad pa ltar ji lta ba bzhin mngon du gyur pa yin te/ de yang
bdag nyid chen po 'di dgung lo nyer bdun du phebs pa nas bzung / lnga bcu rtsa lnga bzhes kyi bar la gdan sa chen po'i bstan pa'i khur mtha' dag bzhes par mdzad de/ dbyar
chos/ dgun chos/ dus rim che chung / dkyil 'khor sgrub mchod so so sogs de thams cad yar ldan du mdzad pa'i ring nas gtsug lag khang gsar bzhengs mdzad pa yang / rdzong
chung bla brang / sgrol ma lha khang / mgon khang nub/ rje btsun gyi sku 'dra mdze thod ma bzhugs pa'i zur khang gtsug lag khang / phru ma'i lha khang / gzhi thog bla
brang gi rigs 'dzin lha khang / dbu rtse'i 'jam dbyangs gzi 'od

'bar ba'i dbu thog gi gser thog chen mo sogs 'di thams cad gsar bzhengs su mdzad de kun gyi mig gi bdud rtsir gyur pa mngon sum du grub pa 'di yin la/ bris 'bur gyi sku ngo
mtshar can gsar du bskrun pa yang / sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gdung rten dngul gdung rin po che/ phyi rten 'bum thang na bzhugs pa/ yum gyi gdung rten/ nyid kyis
yab yum gnyis kyi dgongs pa rdzogs thabs su bzhengs pa'i lam zab brgyud pa'i gser sku che chung gnyis/ phru ma'i gtsug lag khang na bzhugs pa'i sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal
po'i 'dra sku rnams gsar bzhengs su mdzad cing / khyad par mgon khang nub na bzhugs pa'i rdo rje nag po chen po lcam dral gyi 'chams sku chen mo ngo mtshar rmad du byung
ba 'di gnyis bzhengs par mdzad pa na/ thog mar sku rgyu rnams la phyag nas mdzad pa'i nyin/ mgon po'i sku par glo bur du 'bul mi byung ba sogs thog mtha' bar gsum du
rten 'brel phun sum tshogs pa du ma rang 'grig tu byung zhing / mthar phyag nas rgyas par mdzad de mgon khang nub tu bzhugs su gsol ba na/ lo de kho na la sa skya pa'i bstan
dgra la la nang 'dzings/ la la tshe'i dus byas/ kha cig la gnas dbyung phog pa sogs dam nyams bstan pa'i dgra bo rnams la rtags mtshan myur du ston par mdzad pa'i byin
rlabs dang mthu rtsal gyi mnga' bdag de nyid la sogs pa 'bur du bzhengs pa'i sku brnyan kyang bsam gyis mi khyab cing / bris sku la rdzong lugs kyi lam 'bras brgyud pa
gong dkar rdo rje gdan na bzhugs pa'i rgya thang chen mo la 'dra shus gnang ba

dang / gzhan yang gsang 'dus brgyud pa/ rigs 'dzin brgyud pa/ yi dam dang chos skyong gi nag thang che chung grabs gnyis la sogs pa bris thang gi rigs grangs kyis mi chod pa
tsam zhig gsar bzhengs su mdzad pa de thams cad la gos khyad par can gyi gong sham 'ja' ris nyis brtsegs/ zhal khebs lnga sbrag rgyab dar dang bcas pa 'ba' zhig tu mdzad
cing / khyad par sangs rgyas kyi 'khrungs rabs brgya pa ri mo ngo mtshar phul du phyin pa la rin thang gzhal du med pa'i gos gser ma 'ba' zhig gis gong sham 'ja' ris zung
ldan dang bcas pa/ dar chen khyad par du 'phags pa'i zhal khebs lnga sbrag sgril shing gi rtog gser dngul 'jang brdungs las grub pa sogs rgyu dang bzo khyad phun sum tshogs
pas/ mdor na sangs rgyas kyi skyes rabs kyi bris thang cig la 'di nyid las khyad par du 'phags pa ding sang dbus gtsang gi ljongs 'di na med par yongs su grags pa 'di
yin la/ sangs rgyas kyi 'khrungs rabs 'di dang gong gi lam 'bras rgya thang gnyis la phyag nas mdzad dus me tog gi char kha ba ltar babs pa yongs su grags shing / gzhan
yang gdan sa chen po'i gtsug lag khang rnams kyi nyams gso mdzad pa yang / g.yu thog lha khang / shAka bzang sku 'bum/ gzhon dbang sku 'bum/ rigs bzang sku 'bum/ 'khon
sku 'bum sogs gdan sa chen po'i nub phyogs kyi gtsug lag khang rnams dang / gzhan yang bla brang nyi lde/ bla brang dge 'phel sogs lha khang de rnams kyi spang bad spo ba/
gser 'phru 'dzugs pa sogs

nyams gso dgos pa mtha' dag mthar phyin par mdzad cing / de dag gi ring nas 'chad pa nyi ma'i 'od zer gyis gdul bya'i blo gros kyi padmo rgyas par mdzad pa'i tshul yang / bla
ma gong ma'i dus chen gyi dkyil 'khor zab mo'i sgrub mchod rnams dang bstun nas bde kye gsang gsum/ rdo rje phur pa sogs kyi smin byed dbang gi chu rgyun lan mang du stsal
zhing / sgrub thabs kun las btus pa brgya rtsa dang / gzhan yang rjes gnang zur bka'i rigs mang po/ lung gi tshogs du ma dang bcas pas skal ba dang 'tshams pa'i gdul
bya rnams kyi dad pa dang blo gros kyi dbang po rab tu rgyas par mdzad pa yin la/ de dag gi bar mtshams rnams su rtsom pa legs bshad nor bu'i phreng ba gsar du bskrun pa
yang / sngags 'chang chen po la bla ma rgyang 'bod kyi sgo nas gsol ba 'debs pa/ gsung ngag rin po che'i khrid yig ngo mtshar can/ rdo rje phur pa'i sgrub thabs 'bring po/
'khor lo bde mchog nag po pa'i sbyin sreg bse 'bag nag po 'phur shes kyi lo rgyus/ chos dung dkar po rgyang grags kyi dkar chag sogs sngon med pa'i legs bshad du ma yang
gsar du mdzad de/ kun mkhyen rgyal ba'i bstan pa la ma rtogs pa dang / log par rtogs pa dang / the tshom gyi dra ba thams cad bsal bar mdzad pa yin la/ dus dang gnas skabs
thams cad du rje btsun sa skya pa'i chag med rnam pa bzhi dang / chos skyong khyad par can rnams la dus dang rgyun gyi mchod gtor 'bul bsngo la rtag 'grus su mdzad pa'i
ngang nas/ chos dang srid kyi bya ba gang la yang thugs skyel dang thugs ngang shin tu ring

po'i sgo nas gang yang 'jam dar gyi tshul du skyong ba la mchog tu mkhas pas/ dmu rgod su gang gis kyang 'dul bar ma nus pa rnams kyang rang gi ngang gis 'dul bar mdzad cing
/ mdor na sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po ngag dbang kun dga' rin chen gyis dpal sa skya'i sde bstan pa gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i bstan pa'i me ro gso bar mdzad pa'i
rgyun de nyid mi nyams shing yar ldan du skyong ba la/ bdag nyid chen po 'di bas lhag pa gzhan su yang ma byung bas/ des na sngags 'chang bstan pa'i gsal byed chen po de
nyid kyi thugs kyi sras mchog kun gyi gtsug rgyan dam par gyur pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i skyes bu chen po 'di nyid la bla ma dang lhag pa'i lha du mas byin gyis brlabs shing
lung bstan brnyes pa'i tshul sogs ni gong gi rnam thar bstod pa'i tshigs bcad kyi 'phros las/ kye rdo rje yi dkyil 'khor bsgrub pa'i tshe/ /dpal ldan bla mas lung bstan
brnyes la 'dud/ /ces sogs te de yang rje nyid sku phra mo'i dus rje btsun gcen dang lhan cig pas sngags 'chang chen po'i zhabs phyir bzhugs nas/ lha khang chen mo'i yang
steng theg chen pho brang du dges pa rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor rdul tshon ma'i sgrub mchod nyi ma du ma zhig mdzad pa'i tshe/ tho rangs kyi cha zhig la lam 'bras brgyud pa'i
rten gtso rje sa chen gyi sku 'dra rin po che'i zhal dkyil la 'od dkar po zla ba shar ba 'dra ba zhig yun ring po'i bar du byung ba dang / sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po
nyid shin tu dges pa'i gsung gis sa chen gyi sku'i zhal dkyil la 'od dkar po byung ba de rten 'brel

mchog tu bzang / khyed khri thog pa sku mched gnyis po tshe ring po 'ong zhing / 'phrin las kyang shin tu che bas bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa rgya chen po 'byung ba'i
rten 'brel du 'dug pas de'i dga' ston gyis gsungs nas/ sku mched gnyis la gos chen gyi sku bem bzang po re re stsal ba'i rje nyid la gnang ba de ni gos mdog dmar po sprin
ris ma bar mtshams la nor bu cha bdun gyi ri mo byas pa zhig 'dug pa shin tu rnying par song 'dug kyang / dus phyis kyang nyid kyi sku la yang yang bzhes nas gong gi lo
rgyus rnams gsungs te/ gos bem 'di rnying kyang gsar pa brgya bas dga' ba yin zhes gsung ba thos shing / gzhan yang lha dang brgyud pa'i bla ma du mas zhal bstan cing byin
gyis brlabs pa'i tshul sogs ni/ rje nyid kyis bde mchog pho brang du dges pa rdo rje'i gzhi bsnyen la bzhugs pa'i dus su/ tho rangs kyi cha zhig la mnal lam gyi tshul
gyis mdun gyi nam mkhar 'ja' 'od kyi gur khang 'khyil ba'i khrod na/ sa skya pa rje btsun dkar po rnam gsum shin tu gsal bar bzhugs pa'i sku mdun na rin po che'i snod shing
'bras kyis bkang ba zhig dang bcas 'dug pa gzigs pas dad shugs chen pos phyag mang du btsal ba'i snang ba byung gsungs shing / gzhan yang dus der nam mkha' thams cad sprin
dkar po zhig gis khyab pa'i ngos la tshe dpag med dkar po'i sku brnyan shin tu gsal ba zhig kyang mngon sum du mthong ba byung kyang gsungs so/ /de ltar kye rdo rje'i
gsung bsnyen mdzad pa'i rjes de ma thag par/ gur gyi mgon po'i bsgom bzlas zhag bdun pa zhig mdzad pa'i tho rangs

kyi cha mnal lam du/ sa skya'i rgyab ri dpon po ri nas gdong nag gi bar gyi nam mkha' la sprin nag gru gsum 'khrigs pa'i dbus su gur gyi mgon po nyid phyag gnyis kyis gri thod
nyug ge ba dang / de'i steng gi phyogs su khyung chen gsum/ g.yas phyogs su bya nag gsum/ g.yon phyogs su khyi nag gsum/ rgyab phyogs su ce spyang gsum/ mdun phyogs su
mi nag gsum rnams shin tu gsal ba dang / sprin nag gi gseb na me ris shin tu legs pa bzo rigs pa mkhas pa sus kyang bskrun par mi nus pa lta bu 'ur sgra dang bcas 'bar
ba yun ring du gzigs shing / de'i ngang nas gur gyi mgon po'i sku yongs rdzogs je gsal je gsal 'gro ba zhig 'dug pa la/ zhabs 'bring po zhig gis mnal sad byung bas shin tu
phongs pa zhig byung gsungs shing / yang nyid kyis lha khang chen mo'i yang steng du rdo rje phur pa'i gsung bsnyen mdzad pa'i dus tho rangs shig mnal lam du/ gtsug lag
khang chen po de nyid kyi khyams stod na bzhugs pa'i sku rnams la rdul sprugs mdzad kyin 'dug pa na sku de dag gi khrod nas mi dkar po zhig byung nas rje nyid la shog ril
zhig gtad de/ 'di tshe gzungs yin pas rgyun du sgrogs shig zer nas mi snang bar gyur song ste/ shog ril la gzigs pas sngags shig 'dug pa bzung bas/ nang par mnal sad nas
kyang byang bar thugs la bzung 'dug pas re zhig chag med du mdzad cing / dus phyis bsnyel nas med do zhes gsungs kyang / gong gi mi dkar po byung gsungs pa de yang lhag
pa'i lha mchog rdo rje gzhon nus zhal

dngos su bstan par gdon mi za zhing / tshe gzungs bsnyel ba'i tshul de yang / de'i tshul skye bo mang po zhig gis rig na sku tshe'i bar chad du gyur dogs pa la dgongs par mngon
no/ /de dag la 'di skad ces bstod de/ mgon khyod rim gnyis don la gzhol ba'i tshe/ /rje btsun dkar po rnam gsum tshe dpag med/ /nag po chen po 'od gsal ngang nas gzigs/
/lha yis tshe gzungs gtad pa de la 'dud/ /ces so/ /gzhan yang bstan srung dbang po rnams sogs lhag pa'i lha du mas dngos dang rnam 'phrul mtha' yas pa'i sgo nas zhal
bstan cing byin gyis brlabs pa'i tshul 'di ltar yang thos te/ rje nyid dpal mgon zhal bzhi pa'i gsung bsnyen la bzhugs pa'i dus shig gi tshe/ da lta zhing skyong mar grags
pa'i hor sil khyad par can 'di nang par phyag tu 'byor rgyu'i do nub mnal lam du/ mi smug tshon pa zhig gis ras kyis dril ba'i sil snyan zhig rgyab la khyer te shar phyogs
nas byung ba'i rjes su mi skya shar ba zhwa theb gyon pa mang po dang / ban chung mang po lung pa khengs pa tsam slebs byung bas/ de ma thag a tsa ra nag po 'jigs su
rung ba gnyis glo bur du byung nas/ sngar gyi mi skya shar ba dang ban chung thams cad khong gnyis kyis lung pa ma brgal gyi bar du phyir bskrad de/ de'i mod la mi smug tshon
pa de drung du slebs pa dang mnyam du mnal sad byung ba na ci yin nam snyam du dgongs pa'i tshe/ de'i nyin mo hor sil 'di mnal lam du byung ba bzhin ras dril dang bcas
nas zhabs drung du 'byor byung ba'i tshe nyid kyi gsung las/ sil snyan khyad par can 'di chos skyong zhal

bzhi pa rang gis bkug par 'dug cing / 'di la rjes 'brang zhig yod 'dug kyang chos skyong rang gis ring du bskrad nas/ da cha skyon yong ba med pas hor sil 'di'i ming la yang
zhing skyong mar thogs shig gsungs pa bzhin da lta'i bar du yongs su grags pa 'di yin la/ de lta bu ni zhing skyong dbang pos mthun rkyen dngos su bsgrubs pas ngo mtshar
ba'i rnam thar du shes par bya zhing / yang zhal bzhi yongs rdzogs kyi bris sku 'ga' zhig phyag bris mdzad pa'i tshe yang / skyed lhas kyi sgrub sde'i khrod na rje nyid
bzhugs 'dug pa la/ sgrub khang zhig gi nang na a tsa ra gdong ba dmar nyag can 'jigs su rung ba du ma 'dug pa dang / g.yag rgod nag pos lung pa gang ba sogs mnal lam ya
mtshan can mang du byung gsung ba yang chos skyong nyid shin tu 'go zhing mnyes pa'i rtags su mngon zhing / yang byas 'gyur rje btsun gcen gyi drung du bdag med lha mo bco
lnga'i dbang bskur gsan pa'i sta gon gyi nub mo'i mnal lam du/ rang nyid kyi yum bkra shis dpal gyi bu khrid de nyid bzhugs khri mthon po zhig la bzhugs pa'i zhabs drung
na sngags 'chang bla ma nyid la sogs pa slob 'khor mang po 'dus 'dug pa la/ rgyal yum dam pas chos kyi 'khor lo yun ring du bskor ba'i mtshan lam ngo mtshar can byung ba'i
nang bar kho bo cag gis zhabs drung du phyin ma thag thugs dges spro chen po dang bcas nged la mdang nub rmi lam ya mtshan can 'di bzhin byung ba/ sngags 'chang bde bar
gshegs pa de nyid kye rdo rje dang / nged rang gi yum de bdag med ma dngos

yin zer ba'i rtags su 'dug gsungs shing / yang gsung las khyod nged kyi yum de nyid kyi sku skye yin pa'i lugs yin pas/ des na mdang nub khyod la nged kyis chos zhus so zhes
gsung ba sogs nyams ldan gyi gsung mang du 'byon gyin 'dug pa/ 'di lta bu ni rje btsun rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug birWa pa la/ rje btsun rdo rje bdag med mas ye shes kyi
dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur zhing byin gyis brlabs pa'i tshul dang khyad par cung zad kyang ma mchis pas gzhan las rmad du byung ba'i rnam par thar pa shes par bya'o/ /yang
nyid kyi rigs sras sngags 'chang ngag dbang kun dga' dbang rgyal gyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ pu tra chen po'i sku rkyang pa bzhugs pa'i bris thang khyad par can 'di
phyag bris mdzad pa'i tshe mnal lam du/ a tsa ra pho mo gsum byung ba'i gral mgo ma de shin tu dga' ba'i rnam 'gyur ston pa la/ gzhan gnyis po de cung zad khros pa'i tshul
gyis 'dug pas/ de'i nang par rje nyid kyi gsung las/ nged la mdang nub rmi lam 'di bzhin byung ba bris thang 'di la pu tra ming sring gsum ka ma bris pas lan par 'dug ces
gsungs shing / 'di yang 'phral la 'khu ldog ltar snang yang / don la chos skyong nyid shin tu 'go zhing 'ches pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rtags su shes par bya zhing /
gzhan yang dngos cag rnams kyis gsol ba btab nas gur gyi mgon po lha brgyad kyi bris thang khyad par can rnams phyag bris mdzad pa'i dus su/ bris sku rnams kyi sku sked yan
tsam grub nas zhag 'ga' thugs brel gyi dbang gis 'gyangs pa'i tshe/ rje nyid kyi mtshan lam du bya nag

khyi nag sogs ro stod yan chad med pa mang po sku mdun du phung phung byung ba na/ de'i nang par gsung las/ nged kyi rmi lam de bris sku myur du 'dri dgos pa'i rtags su 'dug
gsungs nas thugs rtsol chen pos phyag bris legs par mdzad nas rab gnas dang bskang gso rgyas par mdzad pa'i dus su yang ngo mtshar ba'i rtags du ma byung ba yin la/ gzhan
yang zhing skyong dur khrod bdag po dang / dpal ldan dmag zor rgyal mos kyang zhal dngos su bstan pa'i lo rgyus yod mod kyang yi ges 'jigs nas ma spros la/ yang dkar phyogs
la dga' ba'i lha rnams kyis sri zhu bgyis pa'i tshul ni/ rje nyid lha chen yang rtser thugs dam la bzhugs dus snga dro mnal sad ran pa na nam mkha' nas dril bu skad
bzang po zhig dkrol 'ong ba de'i rkyen gyis gnyid sad 'phral thun la 'jug pa dus rgyun du byas gsung ba dang / yang bde mchog chu mig rdzing khar thugs gnyer mdzad dus bshar
sbyang gi skabs 'gar cung zad mnal ba'i tshe che chung phug ron tsam pa'i bya zhig sku dpung gi steng du babs nas mnal krog pa dus rgyun ldan du byung gsung ba 'di dag
ni dkar phyogs kyi lha gzhi bdag gnyug mar gnas pa rnams kyis go re len gyi zhabs tog pa'i tshul gyis phu dud du bgyis par snang bas shin tu ngo mtshar ba'i gnas so/ /de
ltar nges pa'i don du drug pa rdo rje 'chang chen po nyid gzhan ngor gos dkar lcang los mdzes pa'i sngags 'chang mchog gi skur bstan pa'i skyes bu chen po 'di nyid kyi
zhabs kyis bcags pa tsam gyis kyang sa gzhi'i bcud 'phel ba sogs kyi sgo nas 'gro

ba rnams la bde skyid phun sum tshogs pa stsal ba'i tshul ni/ mtsho sgo rnam rgyal rtag rtse phyogs su lo du ma'i bar du lo nyes brgyud mar byung nas 'gro ba rnams mu ges nyen
pa na/ rje nyid kyi zhabs kyis bcags pa tsam gyis dus de nas bzung ste da lta'i bar du lo legs skya rgyal ba'i ngang du gyur pa dang / de dus mtsho sgo na mtsho zhig
yod pa la/ rje nyid kyi zhabs bskor mdzad pas/ bdag nyid chen po gang du phebs pa'i phyogs su mtsho la gnas pa'i srog chags nya sbrul 'jong mo sogs bsu ba'i tshul gyis mgo
rnams rog rog por bsgrigs nas gus 'dud byed pa yang byung ngo zhes thos shing / gzhan yang gdong dga' gzhis chen phyogs su yang skya mug chen pos 'gro ba rnams nyam thag
pa na/ bdag nyid chen pos sa phyogs der bum gter 'jug pa dang / phyag nas sogs mdzad pa'i legs lam la brten dus rtag tu lo phyugs legs shing bde skyid phun sum tshogs pa
byung ba sogs yongs su grags shing / gdan sa 'dir yang bar skabs shig tu skye bo mi srun pa dag gi bsam sbyor ngan pa'i 'khrul 'khor la brten nas/ lo dgra sad ser ba sogs
dus rgyun du byung ba'i tshe/ slob 'bangs rnams kyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor bdag nyid chen pos bla ma gong ma rnams kyis lo dgra'i gnyen por bzhengs par mdzad pa'i rigs
gsum mgon po'i mchod rten la nyams gso mdzad par bzhed de/ rje nyid dpon slob rnams kyis rim pas chag phebs te/ rigs gsum gyi mchod rten rnying pa'i zhig ro'i dmigs gang
na yod 'tshol bar mdzad pa'i tshe/ sku 'khor rnams kyis yun ring du ma rnyed

pa la dar tsam cig nas/ bya rog cig skad snyan po sgrogs bzhin pa dang bcas da lta mchod rten yod pa'i gdong nag gi ri chung 'di'i khar babs nas brag la mchu yang yang 'dzugs
shing skad du ma sgrog gin 'dug pa la/ bdag nyid chen po'i gsung gis bla ma gong ma rnams kyis lo dgra'i kha gnon du 'debs par mdzad pa'i rigs gsum mchod rten gyi thes
ro de bya rog babs sa ya gi na yod par 'dug pas/ rang re rnams myur du 'gro ba yin gsungs nas chag phebs pa'i tshe/ ji ltar bka' stsal pa bzhin sngar gyi bya rog babs pa'i
shul na mchod rten gsum gyi bum ldir yan zhig pa'i bang rim dang / seng khri man gyi rtsig pa shin tu gsal ba 'dug pa mthong ba'i tshe/ zhabs 'bring ba kun ha las par
gyur cing / de nas sa yul der da lta'i rigs gsum mgon po'i mchod rten 'di legs par bzhengs nas phyag nas bkra shis mnga' gsol mdzad pa nas bzung / da lta'i bar du phyogs
de nyid nas ser ba sogs kyi rgyun 'byung ba gtan med du gyur pa ni/ gdan sar gnas pa'i skye bo kun gyi blo yul du gsal ba 'di yin no/ /don gyi dbang de dag gi phyir 'di skad
ces bstod de/ /dus gcig dpal ldan sa skya'i mdun ri'i sner/ /lo dgra gzhom phyir rigs gsum 'debs bzhed de/ 'das dus gong ma'i btab shul btsal ba'i tshe/ /srung ma'i sprul
pas dngos su bstan la 'dud/ /ces so/ /de ltar sngags 'chang bla ma lung dang rtogs pa'i mnga' bdag chen po 'di nyid ni/ nang du spangs rtogs kyi yon tan ma lus shing
lus pa med

par rdzogs su zin kyang / phyi rol du sbas pa'i rnal 'byor gyi tshul du kho bo ni yon tan thams cad dang bral ba'i za nyal 'chag gi rnal 'byor pa yin no zhes khengs bskyung
ba'i tshig kho na rgyun ldan du gsungs shing / rtag tu rang nyid dman cha bzung nas/ gzhan rnams mchog tu gzigs pa'i sngon gyi skyes bu dam pa rnams kyi rnam thar dang mthun
pa'i mdzad pa kho na phyag bzhes su bstar ba ni bdag nyid chen po 'di'i thun mong ma yin pa'i ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par thar pa yin la/ des na deng sang gi skabs 'dir
dgas po bka' brgyud pa'i bstan 'dzin du rlom pa 'ga' zhig sogs lugs gnyis dang 'gal ba'i gang dran tho cho'i spyod pa 'ba' zhig dus rgyun du byed pa la rang nyid kyang grol
bar rlom zhing / col chung rnams kyang grub thob tu 'dzin pa'i bstan pa dang sems can la phan pa'i gnas skabs dus nam yang cung zad kyang med pa'i mi tshe stong zad mkhan
rnams kyi snang tshul mthong ba'i tshe/ bdag gi bla ma sems dpa' chen po grags pa'i mtshan can de nyid kyi rmad du byung ba'i mdzad ba'i cha shas re re tsam la bsams
na yang / sems yod dag dad pa'i spu long ches cher g.yo bar nges te/ nyid kyis ci mdzad thams cad bstan 'gro'i don du gyur pa kho na las gzhan du cung zad mi snang ba'i
phyir ro/ /de lta bu'i skyes bu chen po de nyid kyis rdo rje theg pa'i nyams len byed pa'i gdul bya rnams la phan par dgongs nas/ dam rdzas 'chi med ril bu'i sgrub pa mdzad
par bzhed de/ sgo rum ye shes mgon po'i drung du de ltar mdzad na legs nyes kyi lung bstan zhu bar mdzad pa'i tshe/ bse mgon

chen po'i phyag gi thod pa'i nang nas dam rdzas brgya rdo rlon pa bdud rtsi'i rgyun 'dzag bzhin pa zhig phyag tu babs byung ba na/ the tshom med pa rje nyid dgung lo nyer lnga
bzhes pa'i dus dam rdzas kyi sgrub pa thog ma mdzad pa na/ nam mkha' shin tu 'jam pa la me tog gi char dang 'ja' 'od kyi gur khang 'khrigs pa/ dri bzang gis sa skya'i
lung pa khyab pa sogs phyi rol du ngo mtshar ba'i rtags du ma byung zhing / nang du yang dam rdzas 'phel stobs che ba sogs gegs med du mthar phyin pa yin no zhes thos la/
de nas bzung ste rang nyid dgung lo nga gsum bzhes pa yan chad du lo gcig gnyis tsam ma gtogs rnal 'byor dbang phyug grub pa brnyes pa'i dus chen sa ga zla ba byung re
bzhin gyi dam rdzas 'chi med ril bu'i sgrub pa rgyun mi chad par mdzad pas 'di nyid kyis 'phrin las kyi sgo nas bstan pa dang sems can gyi don bsgrub pa la bdag nyid chen
po 'di las ngo mtshar che ba sngon chad gangs can gyi khrod 'dir bstan 'dzin gyi skyes bu gzhan su yang ma byung ba yin la/ zang zing gi sbyin gtong rlabs po che'i sgo nas
sems can gyi don mdzad pa yang rje btsun sa skya pa'i gdung rabs dri ma med pa sngon gyi dus su byon pa'i chos kyi rgyal po 'phags pa rin po che dang / dpal ldan bla ma
dam pa sogs kyi rnam thar dang mthun par rang nyid kyi yab yum sogs kyi dgongs rdzogs rgya chen po sgrub par mdzad pa dang / khyad par dga' ston du ming btags pa'i dge
'dun dang skye bo'i tshogs khri phrag tu longs pa la mang ja/ gdan non/ 'bru'i phung po ri bo ltar spungs pa'i

bre 'gyed tshan che ba dang / gzhan yang ja gos dar sogs kyi gral 'gyed blos mi 'khyud pa lta bu sgrub par mdzad cing / de dag dang dus mnyam du gdan sa chen po'i gtsug lag
khang thams cad du snyan dar/ zhal zas mar me'i phreng ba tshar du dngar ba sogs mchod pa'i bye brag du ma 'bul ba dang / gong bzhugs bla ma slob dpon sogs la bsngo rten
'bul tshan grangs kyis mi lang ba lta bu sogs mdor na 'dzam bu gling gi zang zing gi dngos po thams cad phyogs gcig tu spungs nas mchod pa dang sbyin par gtong ba lta bu'i
rnam dkar gyi mdzad pa rlabs po che de 'dra ba lan gsum gyi bar du sgrub par mdzad pa'i sgo nas kyang 'gro ba rnams dbul phongs kyi sdug bsngal las bskyab cing rang nyid
kyi thugs rgyud la bsod nams dang ye shes kyi tshogs rgya cher spel ba dang / rjes 'jug rnams kyang longs spyod don yod pa sogs yang dag pa'i bya ba la 'jug pa'i rnam
dkar gyi dge ba'i shul lam chen po btod par mdzad pa yin no/ /de ltar rje btsun mkhyen brtse'i dbang phyug de nyid kyis gdul bya dus la babs par gzigs nas grub pa brnyes
pa'i rtags mtshan ngo mtshar can bstan pa'i tshul 'di ltar yang thos te/ gong gi rnam thar bstod pa'i tshigs bcad kyi 'phros las/ gzhan yang phyogs mthar 'gro ba'i don mdzad
tshe/ /grang ba'i ngad dang ldan pa'i ri bo la/ /drung na gnas pa'i 'khor tshogs bskyab pa'i phyir/ /'khor yug drod kyis khyab par mdzad la 'dud/ /ces bya ste/ de yang
dus phyis chen po 'ga' zhig gi srog bskyab pa'i slad du rje nyid kyis lho phyogs kyi rgyud du chibs kyi kha lo sgyur

bar mdzad pa na/ phyogs de nyid na g.yag reng rkyang 'khong du grags pa'i la chen po grang ba'i reg cha shin tu che ba zhig yod pa la/ sang nyin dpon slob rnams phebs pa'i
do nub sku 'khor ba rnams nang par grang ba'i ngad pa chen po 'byung ngo zhes 'jigs pas yid ngal bar gyur pa na/ sang nyin bdag nyid chen po dpon slob rnams lhan cig pas
la de la phebs pa'i tshe/ de dus dgun shin tu grang ba'i dus yin kyang dbyar gyi skabs bzhin ri'i ngos thams cad rmugs pa chen pos khyab cing / sngags 'chang bla ma nyid
kyi sku la 'ja' dkar po zhig mdung tshugs kyis zug pa dang / sku'i g.yas g.yon gyi thad la chos skyong gi sprul pa'i bya rog gnyis gshog sgra 'byin bzhin pa dang bcas 'phur
'gro ba dang / rmugs pa de nyid kyi gdugs kyi rnam pas sku 'khor rnams la yang grang ba'i reg byas nyen pa lta ga la zhig ste/ dbyar tsha ba'i dus bzhin tshad pas gdungs
pa'i lus thams cad rngul bun ne ba dang bcas pa la de nyid ma sgrol bar du byung pas/ phyogs der rgyun du 'grul byed pa'i rgan rabs rnams na re/ e ma ya mtshan che/ dbyar
gzhan du tshad pa che ba rang gi dus su yang ri 'di la grang ba'i sdug bsngal kho na dus rtag tu yong ba la/ da lan gcig pu ngo mtshar ba'i rtags 'di bzhin 'byung ba
ni/ sa skya bdag chen gyi byin rlabs las byung ba yin yang dag go zhes kun kyang sgrogs par gyur cing / de lta bu ni rje btsun sngags 'chang bla ma 'di nyid 'byung ba bzhi
la rang dbang brnyes pa'i grub pa'i mtshan ma yang dag par rig par bya ste/ 'ga' zhig rdo brag sogs la

rkang lag gi rjes tsam byung ba la mtshar du 'dzin pa ni ma brtags pa chen po ste/ de lta bu ni rdzas kyi nus pa sogs la brten nas 'byung bar yang yongs su grags pa'i phyir
ro/ /de lta bu'i 'gran zla dang bral ba'i yongs 'dzin dam pa 'di nyid la bdud kyi gnas mal snying la bcas pa'i gang zag 'ga' zhig gis log sgrub brtsams pa de'i tshe/ sa
skya pa'i bstan srung dbang po rnams kyis mngon sum du tshar bcad pa'i tshul ni/ de yang skabs shig gi tshe bstan pa dang rnal 'byor pa la do bdo ba'i gsang ba'i dgra bo
stobs ldan zhig gis log sgrub tshan chen po bsgrub par nye ba na/ bdag nyid chen pos chos skyong rnams la 'phrin bcol drag tu mdzad pa'i tshe/ rje nyid kyi gzims chung gi
gtor khang gi mdun gyi spyan gzigs kyi rgya ral 'khyog po zhig las khrag rlon pa mngon sum du 'dzag pa byung ba dang bstun/ nyid kyi mtshan lam du bande zhag gis rgyu ma
glo snying sogs nang g.yos tshan cig khur byung ba bzhes pas/ nang par yang sku khams log pa'i rnam pa byung ba chos skyong gis sha skal byin par 'dug gsungs shing / de
dag dang dus mtshungs par mig mthong mkhan zhig gi rmi lam du/ bstan dgra dmigs yul gyi mi de nyid kyi phung po khyogs la bteg nas mgon po'i lam mkhan rnams kyis khyer byung
ba rmis pa na/ de nas zhag 'ga' ma lon par stobs ldan gyi bstan dgra de nyid tshe'i dus byas nas log sgrub mtha' dag rang zhir gyur pa yin no/ /gzhan yang 'di 'dra ba'i
rigs can 'ga' zhig yod mod kyang brjod pa'i skabs ma yin pa'i phyir re zhig bzhag go /de lta bu'i skyes bu chen po de nyid

kyi ngo mtshar ba'i rnam par thar pa bsam pa dang brjod pa'i yul las 'das pa rnams don bsdus pa'i tshul gyis 'di skad ces bstod de/ mdor na sngags 'chang rdo rje 'dzin nyid
kyi/ /ngo mtshar rnam thar brjod kyis mi lang zhing / /bdag 'dra'i byis pa'i blo yis rtogs dka' bas/ /yon tan rgya mtsho'i mnga' bdag khyod la 'dud/ /ces so/ /de dag gis
ni bstod pa dngos kyi don rags rim brjod zin nas/ da ni rje btsun sngags 'chang bla ma sems dpa' chen po nyid kyi rnam thar brjod pa po gang gis 'di phyi'i don thams cad
yid bzhin du 'grub par bya ba'i phyir/ dus gsum gyi sdig pa bshags pa dang / yang dag pa'i smon lam btab pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ bla ma'i mdzad pa skyon gyis ma gos kyang
/ /bdag cag las ngan bag chags rab 'thug pas/ /dus gsum log lta byang chub bsgrub pa'i gegs/ /snying nas 'gyod pa chen pos mthol lo bshags/ /zhes pas bstan la/ gnyis
pa smon lam la rang don phun sum tshogs pa dang / gzhan don phun sum tshogs pa'i smon lam btab pa gnyis las/ dang po ni/ bdag kyang skyon bral sum ldan la gnas shing / /thos
bsam sgom pas rang gi rgyud sbyangs nas/ /'chad rtsod rtsom la g.yeng ba'i bdud spangs pas/ /zhes pas bstan/ gnyis pa bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam la/ spyi dang bre brag
gnyis las/ dang po ni/ spyir gyi bstan pa 'phel zhing rgyas gyur cig /ces pas bstan/ gnyis pa bye brag bstan pa rgyas pa'i smon lam ni/ khyad par 'khrul med rje btsun
sa

skya pa'i/ /bstan pa dri med yar ngo'i zla ba ltar/ /'phel zhing rgyas nas 'jig rten khams 'di ru/ /bde skyid ma lus 'byung ba'i rgyur gyur cig /ces pas bstan/ da ni de lta
bu'i yid la re ba'i don thams cad bde blag tu 'grub pa yang / mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i bla ma rdo rje slob dpon gyi byin rlabs rang gi shes rgyud la zhugs pa la rag las
pa'i phyir/ de nyid 'dod gsol gyi sgo nas gsol ba rtse gcig tu btab pa ni/ sems dpa' chen po bla ma'i thugs rje dang / /snying nas dad pas gsol ba btab pa'i mthus/ /'dren
mchog slob bu'i tha chung bdag rgyud la/ /chos kyi rgyal po'i byin rlabs 'jug gyur cig /ces so/ /da ni gsol 'debs kyi sbyar byang bstan pa la/ gang gis brtsams pa'i gang
zag ni/ /tshul 'di sngags 'chang rje nyid kyi/ /rigs dang chos kyi bur gyur pa/ /zas gtsang sras kyi bstan pa yi/ /sgor zhugs skyes stobs blo gros can/ /ngag dbang kun
dga' bsod nams kyis/ /zhes pas bstan la/ gang du brtsams pa'i gnas ni/ gong mas byin rlabs sa skya yi/ /gzhi thog bla brang mkha' spyod du/ /snying nas dad pa thob ste sbyar/
/bla ma so skyer 'dzin pa yi/ /chal chol smra dang 'di mi mtshungs/ /zhes pas bstan/ de ltar brtsams pa'i dge ba rdzogs byang du bsngo ba ni/ 'di las bsod nams gang
thob des/ /'gro kun thar pa'i bde thob phyir/ /bdag cag tshe 'di'am 'chi kha 'am/ /bar dor 'bras bu smin gyur cig /ces pas bstan/ de lta bu'i kho bo cag la mchog dang thun
mong gi dngos grub ma lus pa stsol bar

mdzad pa'i dus gsum rgyal ba kun gyi spyi gzugs chen po sngags 'chang bla ma rgyal sras sbas pa'i rnal 'byor mtshungs pa med pa de nyid kyis zhing 'dir bstan pa dang sems can
gyi don grangs dang tshad med pa zhig mdzad pa rnams la thugs shin tu rangs par gyur cing / dus ngan gyi skye bo khrel med pa dag gi spyod ngan sna tshogs gzigs pas thugs
cung zad gdungs par yang gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan du gdul bya rgya che ba la dgongs pa'i tshe/ de'i snga ltas su sa'i dkyil 'khor 'di yang yang yang du g.yo
zhing / nam mkha' nas lha rnams kyis rol mo'i sgra dbyangs lan mang du sgrogs pa dang / gzhan yang dus mtha'i rlung chen langs pa lta bu'i yid du mi 'ong ba'i rlung dmar
chen pos lung pa thams cad khyab ste/ nyi ma'i 'od zer kyang mog mog por byed pa zla ba du ma'i bar du byung zhing / de lta bu'i skabs shig na dngos cag gzhi thog bla brang
gi mkha' spyod na bsdad pa'i skabs tho rangs shig rmi lam du/ sngags 'chang bla ma nyid sku sham skya 'jol le ba dang bcas rtab pa'i tshul gyis byon byung nas/ nged ni
bde ba can la 'gro khyed rang e 'gro gsung byung ba la/ 'di bzhin gyi rigs sngon gyi bla ma gong ma 'ga' zhig la yang byung 'dug pa la legs rgyu ma byung 'dug pa'i tshul
dran nas/ bdag ni mi 'gro lags zhus pa snyam byed pa dang gnyid sad byung bas yid kyang ma bde zhing / de dus yab rje chos kyi rgyal po nyid 'khor lo bde mchog gi gsung
bsnyen kha gso la bzhugs pa'i dus yin pas/ nyin mo gsol ba tshogs 'khor gyi skabs su rang la rmi

lam byung tshul rnams zhus nas/ deng sang sku dog bzhin ni yod pa min lags sam zhus pas/ he he bde ba can du 'gro na tshang 'dug pa/ gang ltar da nang tho rangs nged kyi rmi
lam na yang lus la ras gos shig min pa gzhan gang yang med pa byas/ bande zhig gi kha la rgya gling gnyis sbyar nas 'bud kyin 'dug pa la mi gnyis kyis bus pa 'dra ba'i
skad tshad ma yong gin 'dug pa de dang bsdebs nas bde mchog chu mig rdzing kha'i ri sul na yar 'dzegs phyin pa'i rmi lam zhig byung gsungs shing / de dag gi rjes tsam bdag
cag ngam ring rgyal po'i pho brang na yod pa'i skabs shig thugs dam gsung shog gnang ba zhig gi nang na yang / ngos ni nyer dgu'i zla bar 'dug sa skya pa'i bstan pa la
gdan sa'i 'dzin skyong 'di las gal che ba mi 'dug pa/ sems khur bskyed pa rang gal che zhes gsung ba 'dug pa de dus ni rang nyid rtag 'dzin ches pas go ba ma byung kyang
/ phyis bsams pas sngags 'chang bla ma nyid myur du dag pa'i zhing du phebs pa'i gsung de dus nas stsal bar 'dug go/de nas rje nyid dgung lo lnga bcu nga lngar phebs pa'i
me mo sbrul gyi lo'i zla ba dang po tsam nas gzhan snang du sku bsnyung ba'i tshul bstan pa na/ spyi sgos tha dad nas sku rim rgya chen po bsgrubs shing / 'tsho byed mkhas
pa rnams kyis kyang 'phrod rten rim par phul kyang sku la gdangs khyad du mngon pa gtan nas ma byung bas/ thams cad sems yed yed por gyur pa'i tshe/ nyid kyi gsung las/
da lo nged la dog cha chen po yod nyen 'dug kha rtsang zla ba bcu gnyis pa'i tho rangs kyi cha zhig la skad

phra mo lhang lhang ba zhig gis khyod la mkha' 'gro'i bsu ma yod do zhes yang yang zer ba zhig byung gsung ba la/ sku 'khor ba rnams kyis des na sku rim rgya chen po mdzad
pa dang / zhabs pad yun ring du brtan pa'i thugs 'dun gnang dgos lags zhus pa na/ yang gsung las/ dus la babs na gang gis kyang mi phan/ lhag par nad kyis khyer ba'i lus
'di bas/ bstan pa la bya ba thub nges kyi lus shig dga' ba 'dug ces sogs myur du gzhan don la phebs par dgongs pa'i gsung mang du byon zhing / de ltar sa ga zla ba ma shar
gyi bar gyi sku bsnyel ba'i dus thams cad du nam mkha' g.ya' dag pa la nyi ma'i 'od zer shin tu gsal zhing / 'ja' 'od kyi ri mo ngo mtshar can gyis nam mkha'i khyon thams
cad gang ba dus 'khor yug tu byung zhing / gzhan yang skabs skabs su me tog gi char 'bab pa sogs skye bo rnams kyis mthong ba'i tshe/ kye ma kyi hud sngags 'chang bla
ma 'di'i sku bsnyel lugs dang / nam mkha' la ngo mtshar ba'i rtags 'di lta bu rtag par yong lugs kyis byang phyogs kyi rgyud 'di mgon dang bral ba zhig myur du mthong bar
'dug go zhes mi bzod pa'i smre sngags drag po dus kun du sgrogs par gyur cing / de nas sa ga zla ba'i tshes bzhi lnga tsam nas gzhan ngor slar yang sku dub bar song ba'i
tshul bstan zhing / gong gi 'ja' 'od la sogs pa ngo mtshar ba'i ltas rnams kyang je gsal je gsal du gyur cing / zla ba de'i tshes bcu gnyis nas bcu drug gi bar la bdag nyid
chen po sku 'khor nyung shas dang bcas gzhi thog bla brang gi tshoms dmar

na gdugs la bzhugs pa'i tshe/ nyin re bzhin nyi ma'i gung tsam la babs pa na/ mgo sil snyan gyi sgra 'dra ba la gsung thag shin tu ring ba'i sgra ya mtshan can zhig thog mar
bla brang shar tsam gyi thad kyi nam mkha' nas byung nas rim gyis lho phyogs su song ste/ mthar bsam gling dgon pa'i thad tsam du yal 'gro ba rgyun chags su byung bas sku
'khor thams cad ya mtshan du gyur cing / lhag par tshes bcu bzhi'i snga dro rje nyid sngags 'chang chen po'i sku bstod shes bya kun la ma gdangs dang bcas pa zhig gsung
shugs chen pos mdzad kyin 'dug pa la/ zhabs 'bring pa rnams kyis rgyu mtshan zhus pas/ gsung las da nang tho rangs rmi lam du sngags 'chang bde bar gshegs pa de nyid sngar
las kyang sku gzi mdangs che ba zhig byas byon pa dang gsal bar mjal nas phyag btsal byin rlabs zhus te nad 'di las grol nas/ shar phyogs su bde phyam phyam phyin pa'i
snang ba zhig byung bas rmi lam de dran nas bla ma la gsol ba btab pa yin gsungs/ 'di ni gsal bar gsung ma byon pa tsam ma gtogs/ don la sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po
dang dngos su mjal ba la the tshom mi dgos shing / yang lan cig gsung las/ da nang tho rangs sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po chibs pa zhig mdzad/ nged rang chibs gdong la
byas nas bla brang zam pa'i steng nas 'byon gyin 'dug pa la/ sngags 'chang chen po'i gsung gis da nged kyis ma yong ba rgyun ring song bas rgyan gyi lam rgyus legs po gyis
shig ces gsung ba'i snang ba zhig byung ba ya mtshan che ci yin nam gsungs/ de dus kyang sngags

'chang nyid dang mjal bar 'dug go /yang tshes bcu bdun gyi snga dro sku 'khor rnams la gzigs nas bzhad mo mdzad cing / nyid kyi gsung las/ dgod bro ba la da nang tho rangs
rgya gar nas thor bshad byas 'ong ba yin zer ba'i khye'u shin tu yid du yong ba gos dkar po gyon pa/ lag na 'be ta'i bum pa thogs pa zhig byung nas khyed spyan 'dren la yong
ba yin zer ba sogs de dang lab mang du byas pa rmis zhes gsung ba sogs ji srid bsnyung ba'i bar thams cad du dag pa'i gzigs snang 'ba' zhig gis dus 'da' ba'i ngang nas/
rgyun gyi thugs dam sogs la yang rtag 'grus su mdzad cing / de nas dgongs pa chos dbyings su thim par nye ba'i tshe/ gzhan las ches ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba'i rtags
mtshan 'di bzhin yang ston par mdzad pa yin te/ de yang tshes bcu drug tsam gyi cha zhig la gdan sa na yod pa'i bud med phun tshogs zer ba zhig la bu mo chung du smra shes
tsam zhig yod pa de bla brang gzhi thog gi ltag sgo na rtse zhing yod pa'i mngon sum gyi mthong snang la/ lhag sgo'i rdo kras kyi mgor bud med rgyan gos zab cing dbu rgyan
dar dpyangs dang bcas pa mang po zhig gis Da ma ru dang dril bu'i sgra drag tu bcam byung bas/ de nas dar tsam zhig nas sngags 'chang bla ma grags pa'i mtshan can nyid
sku gzi 'od 'bar bzhin pa dang bcas gzhi thog bla brang gi ltag sgo brgyud nas phebs byung ste/ bu mo de rang la byin rlabs gnang byung ba'i mod la sngar gyi bud med rnams
kyis bsus te/ Da ma ru dang dril bu'i sgra chen po dang bcas rim bzhin sa dkar logs kyi

ngos la byon te bar snang la yal song ba mthong bas/ de ma thag tu bu mo chung ngu de nyid rang gi ma'i rtsar byung ste sngar gyi lo rgyus rnams sgrib med du smras byung ba
na/ ma yang ha las te da lo gong bzhugs sku shin tu ma bde ba'i tshul gleng ba la/ khyod kyis mthong snang byung tshul de bzhin smras na chad pa yang yong bas su la yang
ma zer cig ces gdams so zhes kyang thos la/ de lta bu ni sngon slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo dag pa mkha' spyod du gshegs pa sa skya'i rgan mo las dag pa zhig gis mngon sum
du mthong ba dang tshul mtshungs pa'i gzhan las ches khyad par du 'phags pa'i rnam par thar pa yin no/ /de nas sa ga zla ba'i tshes bcu bdun la babs pa'i tshe/ de'i mtshan
hril po gsung shugs chen po dang bcas nas thugs dam zab mo 'ba' zhig la bzhugs nas/ tho rangs kyi cha zin pa na lam zab mo bla ma'i rnal 'byor smin rgyas su mdzad cing
/ rten mchod rnams la spyan yang yang du gzigs pa'i ngang nas zhing 'di'i sku dngos kyi gdul bya'i don rnams re zhig mthar phyin nas/ skye bo rtag 'dzin can rnams dge la
bskul ba'i phyir dang / zhing gzhan du gdul bya smin grol la 'god pa'i phyir rgyud sde nas gsungs pa'i 'da' kha ma zab mo la mnyam par bzhag ste bde bar gshegs pa'i tshul
bstan to/ /de nas tshes bco brgyad kyi nyin mtshan gyi bar la 'od gsal ma bu ro gcig tu 'dres pa'i zung 'jug bde ba chen po'i ngang du mnyam par bzhag nas/ bcu dgu'i tho
rangs kyi tshe de nyid las bzhengs te/ sku 'khor ba kun gyis gsan pa'i thag sgra dang bcas dbu gtsug mngon gyur du

'phags pa la byang sems kyi zil pa phrom me bar gyur te/ nyid kyi sku'i skye ba snga mar gyur pa'i sprul pa'i sku dpal ldan bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po zhes bya ba nyid dga' ldan chos kyi pho brang na rgyal ba byams pa'i zhabs drung na bzhugs pa'i gnas der slar yang byon par gyur to/ /de ltar dbu thod 'phags pa dang dus
mnyam du shangs las byang sems dkar dmar gyi rgyun shin tu bungs che ba babs te sku gdung gi mdun gyi na bza' thams cad tshos par gyur cing / 'di ni rnal 'byor pa rang
kha ba zhig yin kyang 'chi khar grub mtha' bsnyogs pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i rtags su bshad de/ rje sa skya pa chen po'i gsung rab 'khor lo bde mchog gi rim bzhi lam bslang
zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos las/ chos kyi sku la chos skur ngo shes pa/ 'chi kha nyid du phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob nas/ rnam shes spyi gtsug tu song ste
longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku'i zhing khams su 'gro bar 'gyur ro/ /de'i rtags pha'i khu ba'i thig le sna bug g.yon na mar 'byung ngo zhes gsungs pas so/ /de nas sku gdung
gi zhabs tog rnams rgyud sde nas bshad pa ltar phul te/ rje btsun gcen gyis yi dam rdo rje phur pa la brten nas bzhu 'bul mdzad pa'i tshe/ nam mkha' la 'ja' 'od kyi phreng
ba rab tu 'khrigs pa dang me tog gi char kha ba ltar bab cing / khyad par gdan sa chen po'i rgyab ri dpon po ri phyogs nas 'ja' 'od sna lnga pa zhig lho phyogs su thal
gyis song nas gzhi thog tshoms dmar gyi sku gdung bzhu la bzhen pa'i bar snang gi thad tsam du

chil gyis 'khyil ba gdung bzhu ba'i dud pa ma yal gyi bar du byung nas/ slar yang dpon po ri phyogs su phyi 'gros kyi tshul gyi rim gyis yal ba kun gyis mthong zhing / gdung
rnams phal cher ring bsrel dang gdung log kho nar gyur cing / de nas bdag nyid chen po'i thugs dam gsal 'debs su dges pa rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor chen po zhal phyes te sgrub
mchod yun ring du phul zhing / dgongs rdzogs dngos gzhi'i dus su skya ser khri phrag tu longs pa la mang ja gdan non/ zang zing gi 'bul 'gyed sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa
bsgrub pa dang / de nas rje nyid kyi sku tshab gser sku thog tshad ma la sngar sngags 'chang chen po'i dgongs rdzogs su bzhengs pa'i lam zab brgyud pa'i kha bskang ste/
lam 'bras bla ma brgyud pa'i sku mi tshad tsam gyis bskor ba gsar bzhengs su mdzad pa'i rten rnams kyi gzungs gzhug gi gtso bo la bdag nyid chen po'i gdung tsha stobs che
bar bzhugs su gsol zhing / gzhan yang gzungs sngags dang byin rlabs kyi rten sogs dpag tu med pa bzhugs pa'i sku brnyan de rnams la 'jam mgon grub pa'i dbang phyug padma
sambha ba'i rnam par sprul pa dbang po'i mtshan can dang / byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'jam dbyangs ngag dbang kun dga' dbang rgyal te khu dbon zhal rnam pa gnyis gtso
bor bzhugs pa la rdo rje 'dzin pa'i 'khor du mas bskor ba dang bcas rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga rgyas par mdzad de byin rlabs kyi gzi 'od 'bar bar bzhugs shing / slar yang ngos
cag gis bdag nyid chen po de nyid kyi dgongs pa rdzogs thabs su nyid kyi nang rten du dmigs

pa'i rnam rgyal mchod rten rgyu rin po che dngul las grub cing bzo khyad dang phra rgyan sogs phun sum tshogs pa kun gyis mthong na yid 'phrog pa ngo mtshar can nyid legs par
bzhengs te/ de'i gzungs zhugs kyi gtso bor sngags 'chang bla ma de nyid kyi gdung ring bsrel dbu lo sogs stobs che ba dang / nyid kyi sku 'dra phyag nas stong tshar ma/
rje nyid zhal bzhugs dus nged rang la gnang ba'i tshems dang zhal rgyan bubs/ gzugs sku bsdu ba'i dus su sku la mchod bzhin pa'i na bza' byang sems dkar dmar gyi rgyun
chen po babs pa de nyid bubs ma nyams pa/ nyid kyis kye rdor gzhi bsnyen mdzad dus kyi dbu skra'i zegs ma la sngags 'chang chen po'i phyag bris 'byar ma/ gzhan yang sa lo
thams cad mkhyen pa'i sku 'dra phyag nas brgya tshar ma/ sngags 'chang chen po'i sku tshe hril por 'bral spangs mdzad pa de nyid dang / yang sa lo'i pur ras la sngags 'chang
chen pos bzhengs pa'i lam 'bras brgyud pa'i bris thang / rje btsun gyi phyag nas bzhugs pa'i bris thang chung ngu / sa lo'i sku 'dra brgya rtsa'i drung du sngags 'chang
chen po re re dang bcas pa yod pa'i bris sku byin rlabs can/ bde kye gsang gsum rnal 'byor ma dang bcas pa'i bris sku bla ma gong ma rnams kyi gsung bsnyen mdzad dus
kyi thugs dam rten 'khrul med re re khyab bdag 'khor lo'i mgon po rgyal ba mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi bris 'bur gyi sku rje nyid kyi phyag
nas brgya rtsa ma/ mus chen gyi gdung tsha gdung rus dbu lo rnams stobs che ba dang / sku chos tshul khrims

kyi dri bsung can bubs ma nyams pa/ theg chen rin po che'i sku 'dra phyag nas ma spyan 'gug tu ring bsrel zhig gsar du byon pa'i byin rlabs yid ches can/ sngags 'chang chen
po'i sku 'gag dri zhim ma khyad par can dang ldan pa bubs ma nyams pa/ slob dpon padma'i gter sku byin rlabs can/ gzhan yang bla ma gong ma na rim bzhin gyi dbu lo na bza'
phyag sen zhabs sen sku sha dam rdzas ril bu sogs byin rlabs kyi phung po bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / stod smad bar gsum du dgos pa'i gzungs sngags zab mo bgrang ba las
'das pa/ mdor na gnod sbyin 'khor lo'i bar gyi rgyud sde nas bshad pa'i gzungs zhugs tshang la ma nor bas gdung rten gyi nang thams cad khyab par phul te/ mchod rdzas
bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas nas gzhi thog bla brang gi nub phyogs rigs 'dzin bla ma brgyud pa'i pho brang gi sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po'i gdung rten rin po che'i
g.yon phyogs su bzhugs su gsol nas/ kho bo cag rdo rje 'dzin pa'i 'khor du ma dang bcas pas rab tu gnas pa smin rgyas su bgyis te/ ji srid bstan pa gnas kyi bar du lhar
bcas 'gro ba rnams kyi bsod nams kyi zhing dam par brtan par bzhugs pa 'di yin la/ gzhan yang yab rje chos kyi rgyal po de nyid kyi dgongs pa chos dbyings su rdzogs pa'i
phyir zla ba byung ngo cog gi dus chen gyi tshes grangs dang bstun nas/ tshogs chen du mang ja/ kye rdo rje'i rtsa rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa'i rgyud 'don/ bla ma mchod chog
rgyas par sgrub pa sogs dang / lo dus kyi dus dran gyi mchod pa 'bul bar zab mo'i yang rtse 'khor lo

bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor rdul tshon ma bzhengs te sgrub mchod yun ring du 'bul ba sogs dang / mdor na rang gi lus longs spyod thams cad rje btsun bla ma thugs rje can de nyid
kyi dgongs pa rdzogs thabs su ci 'gyur gyi thabs la 'bad rtsol bgyid blo mi dman tsam yod pa 'di lags/ de lta bu'i sngags 'chang sprul pa'i skyes mchog mkhyen brtse nus
pa'i mnga' bdag 'brel tshad don dang ldan nges pa de nyid gdul bya gzhan gyi snang ngor thun mong du snang ba'i gzugs sku chos dbyings su bsdus pa'i tshul bstan mod kyang
/ las dag pa'i gdul bya rnams kyis gsol ba btab na rgyun chad med par zhal bstan nas byin gyis rlobs par nges te/ bdag nyid chen po'i slob bu'i tha chung kho bo lta bu
la yang dus phal cher du rmi lam du gsal bar mjal ba dang / lhag par byi lo zla ba bcu pa'i tshes drug gi tho rangs rmi lam du yab rje chos kyi rgyal po de nyid gzhi thog
bla brang gi rab gsal shar ma na bzhugs khri mtho ba zhig gi steng zhal nub tu gzigs nas bzhugs 'dug pa'i sku mdun na rgya ja sogs dngos po mang du 'dug pa la/ nged rang
la spyan gyis gzigs nas dges pa'i mdangs bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig mdzad de/ sku mdun gyi dngos po rnams la 'di rnams la tho rgyab yod do gsungs nas nged rang la stsal
ba snyam byed cing / lhag par sems thog na yod pa'i dogs pa shin tu che ba zhig la 'di ltar gyis shig pa'i bslab bya lhug stsol du gnang byung ba la/ rjes su yi rang ba'i
tshig mang du zhus shing / slar yang dus rtag tu rtse bas skyong bar zhal gyis

bzhes pa snyam byed pa'i mod la gnyid sad byung bas/ yab rje chos kyi rgyal po de nyid la bcos ma ma yin pa'i dad pa snying thag pa nas skyes te/ de'i skabs su gsol 'debs kyi
yi ge bsam pa lhun grub ces bya ba de yang brtsams pa lags so// //'dir smras pa/ phyi ltar sngags 'chang gos dkar lcang lo can/ /nang ltar rgyal ba rab 'byams 'dus pa'i
dngos/ /gsang ba rang sems ye shes ngor bzhugs pa'i/ /yab rje chos kyi rgyal por snying nas dad/ /gang sku gangs ri'i spo ltar lhun chags shing / /zla rgyas bzhin ras 'dzum
pa'i mdangs gsal ba/ /lan gcig min par yang yang yid la gcags/ /de 'dra dran pas snying nas gdung bas 'dud/ /gang gsung mchog dman skye bo'i tshogs kun gyi/ /gang zag
skyon nas gsung ba zhabs drung du/ /rtag tu gnas pa kun gyis ma thos pa'i/ /de 'dra'i gsung gi yon tan dran bzhin 'dud/ /gang thugs dgra gnyen bar ma'i 'gro rnams la/ /byams
sdang khyad med 'byongs pa'i sems dpa' che/ /sa skya'i sde dang bstan pa rgyas pa'i thabs/ /gcig tu dgongs pa'i thugs de bsam gyin dad/ /mgon khyod zhing gzhan gshegs
pa'i tshul bstan kyang / /sras kyi tha chung bdag la thugs brtse bas/ /rmi lam ngang du zhal gyi dkyil 'khor mchog /rgyun chad med par bstan pas spro ba 'phel/ /bdag cag
lugs gnyis blo gros mig bral zhing / /gong ma'i mdzad 'phrin rgyun bzang skyong dka' bas/ /be 'u 'i phrag par glang chen khur bor ltar/ /bstan pa'i khur gyis lus sems
mnar mod kyang / /rgyal ba'i

yab gcig sngags 'chang bla ma khyed/ /mi mngon dbyings nas dgongs pa rdzogs gyur na/ /rang gzhan 'di phyi'i don chen 'grub snyam pa/ /'di tsam kho na sems kyi ngal gso'i gnas/
/sangs rgyas kun las lhag pa'i bka' drin can/ /mkhyen brtse nus ldan rtsa ba'i bla ma rnams/ /gcig tu 'dus pa sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan/ /gsol ba 'debs so don kun
lhun grub stsol/ /zhes pa'ang rang babs su smras shing gsol ba btab pa'o/ /de lta bu'i sngags 'chang bla ma grags pa'i mtshan can de nyid kyis byang phyogs kyi sa skyong
chen po'i lcam mo la sras bsod nams rgyal mo zhes bya ba khab tu bzhes pa la/ sras lcam sring drug 'khrungs pa'i lcam sring gnyis gzhon nu la gshegs shing / sku mched
gsum gegs mang du byung ba'i 'jam dbyangs mthu stobs dbang phyug grags pa rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po zhes bya ba ni/ yab sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can nyid dgung lo
nyer drug bzhes pa sa pho byi ba'i lo la gdan sa chen por sku 'khrungs/ sku gzhon nu nas yon tan gyi rtsa ba 'bri klog sogs tshegs med du mkhyen cing / thugs gsal ba mthar
thug pas kun gyi yid 'dzin pa la mkhas pa zhig yin no zhes thos la/ de de'i skabs nas rje btsun 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched/ thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang sogs las
yab chos mtha' dag gsan cing / dgung lo bcu gsum pa la nged rang sku mched gsum lhan cig tu chos khri chen mor rgyal tshab tu mnga' gsol zhing / rje nyid kyis thub pa'i
dgongs pa

gsal ba'i bstan bcos tshogs chen mor nyi ma gsum gyi bar du gsungs pas kun gyi yid 'phrog par gyur/ de dus dbus gtsang mnga' ris dang bcas pa'i sde dpon rigs rnams kyis khri
ston gyi 'bul nod bsam gyis mi khyab pa nyin re bzhin yang bgrang ba las 'das pa char bzhin du babs pas/ de dus kyi dpal 'byor longs spyod de tsam rgan rabs sus kyang mi
dran par grags/ rje de nyid kyis slar yang rje mus pa chen po rdo rje 'chang sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan gyi drung du rab tu byung zhing zab chos mang du gsan/ de nas khams
phyogs kyi sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i rtsa ba sa dkar 'dab 'dob kyi dgon mchod gzhis dang bcas pa'i zhal bdag mdzad par shar phyogs su chibs kyi kha lo bsgyur te/ bdag chen
kun dga' legs pa dang dges bzhin du mjal/ de nas sga gser kha/ dar rtse mdo sogs su gzhan phan rgya cher mdzad nas/ slar 'jam dbyangs sku mched sogs mjal ba la dbus gtsang
phyogs su chag phebs te/ dpal ldan sa skyar yun mi ring ba zhig bzhugs nas/ slar yang shar phyogs la chibs kha bsgyur te/ bdag chen kun dga' legs pa nyid zhing brje la
khad dang mjal bas skabs zos par byung / de dus bdag chen pa'i gsung gis sngar yan chad nyi ma khams phyogs kyi sa skya pa'i bstan pa nged khu dbon rnams kyis bzung ba
de yin/ da phyin chad khams phyogs 'di'i sa skya pa'i bstan pa'i chags 'jig gdung brgyud mthu stobs pa khyed la rag las pas sems khur che bar byed dgos zhes pa'i bka' stsal
phebs nas de ma thag dag pa'i zhing du gshegs so

zhes thos la/ de nas bdag chen gyis pur gyi chag phyi dang nang rten bzhengs pa sogs mdzad nas sog yul dang / rgya dar rtse mdo sogs su phebs te/ slar sa dkar 'dab 'dob phyogs
su phebs par nye ba na/ skye bo mi srun pa 'ga' zhig gi byed pa sogs rkyen cung zad zhig la brten nas dbus gtsang phyogs su phebs te/ nged rang sku mched dges par mjal
zhing thugs yid gcig tu 'dres pa'i legs lam yar ngo'i zla ba ltar 'phel rgyas su gyur te/ de dus gong nas zang zing gi gnang sbyin rgya che ba stsal zhing / 'di nas kyang
'bul nod bsam gyis mi khyab pa bsgrubs la/ khyad par sa lo thams cad mkhyen pa'i thugs dam ma lam zab brgyud pa sku rgyu li khra las byas pa sngags 'chang chen po yab
sras rnams kyi gzims chung rten gral du rgyun du zhugs pa'i byin rlabs dang bzo khyad khyad par can de nyid rten tshab tu bzhes te/ khams phyogs nas bsnams pa'i sku 'dra
rgya gar ma dang rgya nag ma 'ga' zhig gnang byung ba ni dus phyis kho bo cag gis sngags 'chang chos kyi rgyal po yab sras rnam pa gsum brgyud pa dang bcas pa'i thugs kyi
dgongs pa bskang ba'i phyir/ gdan sa khyad par can 'di nyid du li ma lha khang dang rgya nag lha khang gsar bzhengs su bgyis pa la phan che ba byung ba yin la/ de ltar rje
btsun mthu stobs kyi mtshan can nyid kyi sku gzhon nu'i dus nas yi dam zhi khro rnams dang / rdo rje chos skyong sogs kyi gsung bsnyen rnams mthar phyin par mdzad pas/
so sos zhal bstan cing byin gyis brlabs pa'i mtshan ma brnyes/ mdor na dbus

gtsang khams gsum/ stod mnga' ris dang bcas pa'i gang du phebs pa dang bzhugs pa'i gnas thams cad du grub pa'i mdzad pa ya ma zung kho nas dus 'da' zhing / 'gro ba rnams kyi
mgon skyabs dam pa mdzad bzhin pa da lta dgung lo zhe gnyis pa'i steng na bzhugs pa 'di yin no/ /'di'i gcung zhig gzhon nu la gshegs/ de'i gcung ngag dbang kun dga' dbang
rgyal ni/ yab rje chos kyi rgyal po dgung lo sum cu bzhes pa chu pho 'brug gi lo la dpal sa skya'i bla brang phun tshogs gling du 'khrungs shing / gzhon nu nyid nas yon
tan gyi ma mo 'dri klog sogs la sbyangs/ 'jam pa'i dbyangs sku mched dang / rje thar rtse nas nam mkha' dpal bzang sogs las gsan pa rgya cher mdzad/ bde kye phur pa sogs
kyi dus dang grangs kyi bsnyen pa mthar phyin pas mtshan ma ngo mtshar can mang du brnyes shing / dgung lo nyer brgyad bzhes pa tshun chad du bstan pa dang sems can gyi
don ci rigs pa mdzad nas/ nyer dgu pa sa ga zla ba'i yab rje chos kyi rgyal po'i dus chen thog tu gzhi thog bla brang du ngo mtshar ba'i ltas du ma dang bcas zhi bar gshegs
so/ /de nas nged rang gis kye rdo rje la brten nas sku gdung rin po che'i zhabs tog tshul bzhin du bgyis te/ lo ngo gsum gyi bar du mchod pa rgya chen po dang bcas sku
gdung ril por bzhugs shing / de nas khyi lo bzhu 'bul gyi zhabs tog bgyis nas/ gdung rus rnams 'jam dbyangs/ slob dpon padma/ tshe dpag med/ mchod rten brgya tsam la sogs
pa'i gdung tsha mang du bsgrubs nas sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can gyi sku

brnyan gser zangs las grub pa sogs kyi nang du bzhugs su gsol zhing / gzhan yang nyid kyi sku tshab dbu rtse rnying ma na bzhugs pa'i lam 'bras brgyud pa rnams dang sku tshad
mnyam pa'i gser sku gsar bzhengs su bgyis shing / gzhan yang lo dus zla dus kyi mchod par kye rdo rje'i rtsa rgyud brtag pa gnyis pa'i rgyud 'don/ bla ma mchod pa'i cho
ga 'khor lo bde mchog gi sgrub mchod rdul tshon ma sogs nar mar bsgrub pa 'di legs/ de'i gcung gi tha snyad du gyur pa/ sbas pa'i sangs rgyas mi gzugs can sngags 'chang
grags pa'i mtshan can zhabs kyi sras kyi tha chung kho bo cag ni/ yab rje chos kyi rgyal po dgung lo sum cu rtsa lngar phebs pa me mo bya'i lo dpal sa skya'i lha chen phun
tshogs gling gi bla brang du skyes so/ /skyes sbyang gi blo gros cher dman pas lugs gnyis gang la yang blang dor shes pa'i rnam dpyod dang bral/ chags sdang rmongs gsum
la longs spyod pa'i ngang nas za nyal 'chag gis dus 'da' zhing gnas pa kun gyis gzigs gsal du phebs pa 'di yin la/ 'on kyang nged rang chung ngu nas chos kyi bag chags
ches che ba'i stobs kyis gzhon nu rab byung bstan pa'i sgor zhugs nas mi tshe bshad sgrub kyis 'da' ba zhig 'dod kyang / dus kyi dbang gis bod kyi rdo rje gdan dpal ldan
sa skya'i bstan pa stobs kyis 'dzin pa zhig rang ngos nas ngal ba lhur len ma bgyis na/ spyir bod khams kyi bde skyid dang / bstan pa yongs/ lhag par sa skya'i rtsa ba stong
pa la thug pa nas mi theg bzhin du gdan sa'i lugs gnyis kyi khur 'di bzhin

khyer dgos byung ba/ 'di bzhin dgos pa'i lung bstan bka' chems kyi tshul du bdag gi bla ma rgyal sras sbas pa'i rnal 'byor chen po sngags 'chang grags pa'i mtshan can de nyid
kyis yang yang du bka' stsal pa bzhin thog tu babs pa yin te/ de yang rang lo brgyad gnyis lhag tsam lon pa'i skabs su sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ sa skya pa'i bstan
pa la gdan sa'i 'dzin skyong 'di las gal che ba mi 'dug cing / 'di'i 'dzin skyong yang zhal ngo na rim bzhin gyi bzhon pa la bka' babs shig yod pa dang / lhag par bsam
yas chos skyong chen pos kyang rdo rje gdan gyi 'dzin skyong rigs gsum mgon po'i rnam sprul gyi gzhon pa de la bka' babs yod do zer ba thang gnyis rang nged rang la yi
ge byung ba sogs gang nas bsams kyang khyod kyis gdan sa'i 'dzin skyong spel gsum byas pa'i rab byung gi brtul zhugs 'di dor nas nged rang bzhin bgyis na/ nga yang bsam
pa de gas rdzogs shing nged rang gi gzugs pos nam lcogs bar khur yang len pa dang / de ltar byas na rang re la dgra gnyen grogs gsum sus kyang bsam ngan sbyor rtsub kyis
mi tshugs pa sogs thugs kyi dkyil nas gzhal ba'i lung bstan bslab ston gyi tshogs dran pa tsam gyis mig chu rang dbang med pa 'chor ba du ma lhug stsol du gnang ba dang /
yang dus de'i skabs shig nged rang ngam ring na yod skabs thugs dam phyag bris ma zhig gnang byung ba'i nang na yang / ngos ni nyer dgu'i zla bar 'dug bstan pa la gdan sa'i
'dzin skyong las khag che ba mi 'dug pa sogs zhib cha mtha' dag ngos kyis gleng ba

ltar yin pas sa skya zer ba'i ming yang mang po la rgyas byung ba 'dzin skyong spel gsum la blo khur bskyed pa rang gal che che gsung ba 'dug pa/ de dus ni rang blun pas ma
go yang / phyis bsams pas sngags 'chang nyid rang dag pa'i zhing du myur du phebs pa'i dgongs pa de dus nas gtad pa'i gsung du 'dug cing / yang de'i dus shig gi tshe nged
rang gis rdo rje phur pa'i dbang bskur zhig bgyis skabs/ dbang yon du rgyal ba byams pa'i sku li ma dngos gtsang zhig byung ba sngags 'chang nyid la spyan lam phab pas/
sngags 'chang nyid kyi gsung las/ 'di rten 'brel bzang / byams pa'i bstan pa ma shar bar gdung spel byas nas sdod zer ba'i rten 'brel yin gsung byung ba dang / yang de dus
kyi skabs shig gsung las/ nged kyis kyang sngags 'chang chen po'i bka' chems snying la bcangs nas gdan sa'i 'dzin skyong gi ched du phyi nang gsang gsum nas yid chad gtor
ba mang du byung yang bzod rang bsam pa byas bsran bskyed bas sa skya ming ma stong tsam byung ba 'di yin/ da cha khyod kyis nged la mi nyan pa 'dzin skyong spel gsum
mi byed na nga yang su la bsams nas sdod du 'dug gang na'ang nged kyis sngags 'chang chen po'i bka' chems blos ma thong ba bzhin khyod kyis nged kyi ngag kyang mi gcog pa
byed dgos/ de bzhin ma byas na gong ma ye shes kyi spyan ldan rnams kyang thugs khrel 'gro zhes gsungs shing / yang dus phyis rigs 'dzin brgyud pa'i rten bzhengs gnang
skabs nged kyi rten gsar bzhengs blo la yod pa ltar 'di rnams kyi mjug khyed

la bsgril dgos pa yong zhes yang yang du gsung ba sogs bka' stsal pa thams cad thog tu khel byung bas/ rang ngos nas gdan sa'i khur 'di tsam mi lcogs pa la thug 'dug kyang
'di bzhin gyi khur byas pas/ rgyal sras sbas pa'i rnal 'byor de nyid kyi dgongs pa chos dbyings su rdzogs rgyur 'dug pas gtso bor 'di kho na bsams pa dang / yang grub pa'i
'khor los sgyur ba 'jam dbyangs dbang po'i mtshan can nyid dang / spre'u lo gdan sa chen po nyid du mjal ba'i dus lha khang chen mo'i yang steng po ta lar nged rang la
shin tu dges pa'i gsung mang du byon pa'i mod la/ sngon sngags 'chang chen pos gdan sa chen po'i 'dzin skyong mdzad tshul rnams zhib par gsungs nas/ da ni gdan sa'i khur
khyed rang gis byas na ma byas na rang 'di ka yin tshul sku ngos su yang bka' nan stsal zhing / lhag par zhing mi brje tsam gyi sku bsnyung ba'i skabs shig thugs dam phyag
bris ma zhig phebs byung ba'i nang na/ sa skya pa'i bstan pa 'di rtsa rlag la mi 'gro tsam zhig byed na sgar pa'i khams su bsdad gdung spel byas/ khyed rang gis sa skyar
gdung spel byas nas ma 'chugs pa zhig byas na ma byas na rang du 'dug pa dgongs 'tshal/ deng 'chi kha ma tsho la de'i byus dgos rgyu mi 'dug gsungs pa 'dug pa nas/ rje
'jam pa'i dbyangs de nyid kyis kyang dgongs pa rdzogs pa'i phyir dang / gzhan yang rdo rje 'chang ngur smrig gi bla gos 'chang ba dus gsum sgrib med du gzigs pa'i rgyal ba
mus pa chen po'i gsung las kyang / khyed rang ring por mi thogs pa log sgrub thams cad nam mkha' la

dengs nas/ kun kyang dbang du 'dus pa'i chos dang srid kyi dpal 'byor 'bad med lhun grub kyi sgo nas zang zing gi longs spyod sogs blos mi 'khyud pa tsam yong zhes gsung ba
sogs dang / yang gling dga' chos grwa zur du bde mchog rtsa bshad kyi rgyud rnams gnang skabs/ rgyud zab mo 'di rnams phugs yul sa skya'i sngags dgon bde chen gling du rgyud
'don thabs rgyas pa re khyed rang gis rtsoms la tshugs shig gsung ba dang / yang sa skya pa drag zhan med khyed rang la mgo 'bul lus 'bul byed pa zhig yong ngo zhes
gsungs pa sogs dus phyis 'di bzhin gyi gdan sa'i khur dgos pa'i lung bstan nges shes can mang du yod kyang / 'dir yi ger 'jigs nas ma bris la/ rgyu mtshan des na nged rang
la bka' drin mchog tu che ba'i bla ma rnam gsum gyis gtso mdzad/ rtsa brgyud kyi bla ma gong ma ye shes kyi spyan ldan rnams kyi thugs dgongs rdzogs pa'i phyir dang / spyir
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa/ sems can gyi bde skyid/ lhag par dpal ldan sa skya pa'i bstan pa sde gdung brgyud dang bcas pa snying khong bcangs pa'i rang nyid gcig pu zhi
bde don gnyer gyi blo rgyang ring du spangs nas/ theg chen sems bskyed kyi go cha bzang po gyon te/ lhag bsam bzang pos kun nas blangs pa'i nyan thos 'dul ba nas bshad
pa'i bsnyen par rdzogs pa dang / dge tshul dang tshangs spyod kyi bslab pa ji srid 'tsho'i bar du bsrung bar khas blangs pa de nyid de las nyams pa dang / phyis blang du
med pa sogs kyi nyes pa mi 'byung ba'i phyir/ dam chos 'dul ba rang nas

gsungs pa ltar gyi bslab pa 'bul chog tshul bzhin du bgyis pa'i yongs rdzogs dge bsnyen rdo rje 'dzin pa'i brtul zhugs la gnas par bgyis te/ dpal ldan sa skya'i sde bstan pa
gdung brgyud dang bcas pa'i 'dzin skyong spel gsum gyi khur 'di bzhin khur ba la brten pa'i rnam g.yengs ches pa nas/ rgyun gyi dge sbyor ngag 'don spros med sogs gang
yang mthil phyin rang zhig mi yong 'dug pa sogs lung rtogs kyi yon tan cung zad tsam yang med pa'i yar 'dren gyi gzugs brnyan bdag la rtsa brgyud kyi bla ma ye shes kyi spyan
ldan rnams kyis thugs mi khrel zhing rjes su bzung du gsol/ slar yang rang gi ngang tshul cung zad thol byung du smras pa/ rje lha mchog zur phud lnga pa dang / khong
stobs kyi mgon po bi rU pa'i/ /don brgyud pa min par rjes bzung ba'i/ /dpal sa skya'i bla chen yab sras sogs/ /skyabs kun 'dus bla ma'i zhabs la 'dud/ /bu bdag la re sa
gzhan na med/ /tshe 'di phyi bar dor thugs rjes gzigs/ /dus 'bral ba med par bskyab tu gsol/ /mi chos 'byor bral ba'i sprang po ngas/ /blo bsam mno 'chos pa'i glu chung
'di/ /tshig bsgrigs legs spangs te thol byung smras/ /da mthun rkyen 'dzom na 'dzom ste dga'/ /mi kho bo la mthun rkyen ci byung yang / /ljongs bstan pa'i bdag po sa skya
pa'i/ /bstan bstan 'dzin dgon gnas bcas pa yi/ /don zhabs tog kho na las gzhan gang / /yang mthun rkyen zhan na zhan pas dga'/ /'du 'dzi chung bas g.yeng ba chung / /g.yeng
ba chung bas chos spyod 'phel/ /dpal 'byor che yi sdug bsngal

che/ /kun kyang mi rtag 'jig chos can/ /nga mi tshe ring na ring bas dga'/ /rang gi lus ngag yid gsum gyi/ /spyod lam bya ba che phra kun/ /bstan 'gro yi don las ma 'das shing
/ /rang dang nye gnas kyi grogs kun kyang / /rtag tu chos mthun gyi las spyad nas/ /rang gzhan kun gtan legs kyi 'dun ma byas/ /'dun ma de gegs med 'grub ste mchis/ /mi
kho bo'i nye gnas rnams skal ba bzang / /yang 'chi bar gyur kyang 'gyod pa med/ /bstan 'gro la phan 'dod kyi lhag bsam dang bcas/ /sngar byas kyi sdig pa kun bshags shing
/ 'dir snang gi bya ba snang med po/ /ci byas sdug bsngal gyi rtsa ba la/ don med kyi 'khri ba kun bcad de/ /bla ma dang dkon mchog la blo gtad nas/ /'pho ba dang smon
